B_3_C_1_0
BEGIN_
प्रविश्य तु महारण्यं दण्डकारण्यमात्मवान् |
रामो ददर्श दुर्धर्षस्तापसाश्रममण्डलम् || ३-१-१_END
BEGIN_
On entering the impenetrable Dandaka forest that courageous and unassailable Rama saw a clusters of hermitages of sages. 
[3-1-1]_END

B_3_C_1_1
BEGIN_
कुशचीरपरिक्षिप्तं ब्राह्म्यां लक्ष्यासमावृतम् |
यथा प्रदीप्तं दुर्दर्शं गगने सूर्यमण्डलम् || ३-१-२_END
BEGIN_
Overspread with Darbha, the sacred grass, and jute clothing, well pervaded with Vedic splendour and well glowing like the 
un-seeable solar arena in the sky, with naked eye. [3-1-2]_END

B_3_C_1_2

BEGIN_
On looking at the rising red sun, the devotee is asking "Oh! Pooshan! God Sun, nourisher of the universe, the trueness of 
the Supreme is covered by your golden disk like vessel, [i.e., your Solar disk,] slide it aside, for as a truthful and righteous 
devotee, I visualize [that which is beyond your golden Solar disc.]_END

B_3_C_1_3
BEGIN_
शरण्यं सर्वभूतानां सुसंमृष्टाजिरं सद |
मृगैर्बहुभिराकीर्णं पक्षिसंमैः समातम् || ३-१-३_END
BEGIN_
Those hermitages have well-tidied thresholds on all sides, dense with many deer and teemed with many groups of birds, and 
they are the recourse for all living beings. [3-1-3]_END

B_3_C_1_4
BEGIN_
पूजितं चोपनृत्तं च नित्यमप्सरसाम् गणैः |
विशालैरग्निशरणैः स्रुग्भाण्डैरजिनैः कुशैः || ३-१-४
समिद्भिस्तोयकलशैः फलमूलश्च शोभितम् |
आरण्यैः च महा वृक्षैः पुण्यैः स्वादु फलैर् वृतम् || ३-१-५_END
BEGIN_
Those hermitages are always adored by groups of apsarasa-s with their continued dancing, their Holy Fireplaces are very 
broad, and are with oblation items, vessels, deerskins and sacred grass, and they are beaming forth with gigantic trees 
that yield sacred and palatable fruits, and with ritual fuels, and water vessels, tubers and fruits. [3-1-4, 5]_END

B_3_C_2_0
BEGIN_
 कृत आतिथ्योऽथ रामस्तु सूर्यस्य उदयनम् प्रति |
 
  आमंत्र्य स मुनीम् तत् सर्वान् वनम् एव अन्वगाहत || ३-२-१_END
BEGIN_
 Then, on receiving the hospitality in that hermitage for that day, and on the next
  day before sunrise, Rama bade farewell to all of the sages, and thus entered the deep forests.
  [3-2-1]_END

B_3_C_1_5
BEGIN_
बलिहोमार्चितं पुण्यं ब्रह्मघोषनिनादितम् |
पुष्पैश्चान्यैः परिक्षिप्तं पद्मिन्या च सपद्मया || ३-१-६_END
BEGIN_
Those hermitages are sacrosanct for Ritual fire is being worshiped with fire-oblations and sacrifices to the reverberating 
Vedic sounds, and they are enwrapped with lotus ponds with lotuses, and even with flowers of forest. [3-1-6]_END

B_3_C_2_1
BEGIN_
 नाना मृग गण आकीर्णम् ऋक्ष शार्दूल सेवितम् |
 
  ध्वस्त वृक्ष लता गुल्मम् दुर्दर्श सलिलाशयम् || ३-२-२
  निष्कूजमाना शकुनि झिल्लिका गण नादितम् |
  लक्ष्मण अनुचरोओ रामो वन मध्यम् ददर्श ह || ३-२-३_END
BEGIN_
 Rama followed by Lakshmana has indeed seen that midst of the forest which is
  filled with very many animal herds, where the bears and tigers are frequenting, and whose trees,
  creepers, bushes are ruined, water ponds rendered unsightly, birds song-less, but where the
  swarms of crickets are whistling deafeningly. [3-3-2, 3]_END

B_3_C_1_6
BEGIN_
फलमूलाशनैर्दान्तैस्चीरकृष्णाजिनाम्बरैः |
सूर्यवैश्वानराभश्च पुराणैर्मुनिभिर्युतम् || ३-१-७_END
BEGIN_
They have age-old saints with controlled senses who are clad in jute cloths and deerskin, and who subsist on fruits and 
tubers alone, ye their resplendence is like that that of the Sun-god or the Fire-god. [3-1-7]_END

B_3_C_2_2
BEGIN_
 सीताया सह काकुत्स्थः तस्मिन् घोर मृग आयुते |
 
  ददर्श गिरि शृङ्ग आभम् पुरुषादम् महास्वनम् || ३-२-४_END
BEGIN_
 Therein Rama has seen along with Seetha, a lurid voiced man-eater who is akin to a
  mountain-peak, among horrendous animals. [3-2-4]_END

B_3_C_1_7
BEGIN_
पुण्यैश्च नियताहारैः शोभितं परमर्षिभिः |
तद् ब्रह्मभवनप्रख्यां ब्रह्मघोषनिनादितम् || ३-१-८_END
BEGIN_
Rama has seen such a cluster of hermitages that is glistening forth just by the presence of holy saints whose sustenance 
is constrained, and that hermitage is distinctive like Brahma's abode, reverberating with the sounds of that Brahma's Vedic 
chants alone. [3-1-8]_END

B_3_C_1_8
BEGIN_
ब्रह्मविर्भिर्महाभागैर्ब्राह्मणैरुपशोभितम् |
तद्दृष्ट्वा राघवः श्रीमांस्तापसाश्रममण्डलम् || ३-१-९
अभ्यगच्छन्महातेजा विज्यं कृत्वा महद्धनुः |_END
BEGIN_
That glorious and great resplendent Rama on seeing those precincts of hermitage that is graced with highly blest Brahmans, 
the knowers of Brahma, neared it, unstringing the bowstring of his great bow. [3-1-9-10a]_END

B_3_C_2_3
BEGIN_
 गम्भीर अक्षम् महावक्त्रम् विकटम् विकटोदरम् |
 
  बीभत्सम् विषमम् दीर्घम् विकृतम् घोर दर्शनम् || ३-२-५_END
BEGIN_
 Deep eyed, huge mouthed, horrible with a monstrous belly, hideously misshapen, and
  a very soaring one that demon is, an ugly one with a horrendous look. [3-2-5]_END

B_3_C_1_9
BEGIN_
दिव्यज्ञानोपपन्नास्ते रामं दृष्ःट्वा महर्षयः || ३-१-१०
अभिजग्मुस्तदा प्रीता वैदेहीं च यशस्विनीम् |_END
BEGIN_
Those great sages, the possessors of divine knowledge, are gladdened on seeing Rama and illustrious Seetha, and they moved 
towards them welcomingly. [3-1-10-11a]_END

B_3_C_2_4
BEGIN_
 वसानम् चर्म वैयाघ्रम् वस आर्द्रम् रुधिरोक्षितम् |
 
  त्रासनम् सर्व भूतानाम् व्यादितास्यम् इव अन्तकम् || ३-२-६_END
BEGIN_
 Wearing tiger's skin that is wetted with fat and dampened with blood, he is
  frightening to all beings like the wide-open mouth of Death. [3-2-6]_END

B_3_C_1_10
BEGIN_
ते तु सोममिवोद्यन्तं द्इष्ट्वा वै धर्मचारिणम् || ३-१-११
लक्ष्मणं चैव दृष्ट्वातु वैदेहीं च यशस्विनीम् |
मङ्गलानि प्रयञ्जानाः प्रत्यगृह्णान् दृढव्रताः || ३-१-१२_END
BEGIN_
But those sages who are austerely committed to vows, on their seeing Rama, the treader on the path of rectitude, and who 
is now arising like moon, and at Lakshmana and at glorious Seetha as well, rendered Vedic blessings and welcomed the trio. 
[3-1-11a-12]_END

B_3_C_2_5
BEGIN_
 त्रीन् सिंहान् चतुरो व्याघ्रान् द्वौ वृकौ पृषतान् दश |
 
  सविषाणम् वसादिग्धम् गजस्य च शिरो महत् || ३-२-७
  अवसज्य आअयसे शूले विनदन्तम् महास्वनम् |_END
BEGIN_
 He skewered three lions, four tigers, two wolves, ten spotted deer, and a big head
  of an elephant with tusks and fouled with fat on an iron spear, and he is yelling with his
  deafening voice. [3-2-7-8a]_END

B_3_C_1_11



B_3_C_2_6
BEGIN_
 स रामम् लक्ष्मणम् चैव सीताम् दृष्ट्वा च मैथिलीम् ||
  ३-२-८
  अभ्य धावत् सुसंक्रुद्धो प्रजाः काल इव अन्तकः |_END
BEGIN_
 He that demon on seeing Rama, Lakshmana and Seetha ran towards them very angrily,
  like the Time, the Eliminator of people. [3-2-8b-9a]_END

B_3_C_1_12



B_3_C_2_7
BEGIN_
 स कृत्वा भैरवम् नादम् चालयन् इव मेदिनीम् || ३-२-९
 
  अङ्केन आदाय वैदेहीम् अपक्रंय तदा अब्रवीत् |_END
BEGIN_
 He shouted a tremulous blare, as though to tremor the earth, and seized Vaidehi
  with his arms and gone afar, and then said this way. [9b-10a]_END

B_3_C_3_0
BEGIN_
अथ उवाच पुनर् वाक्यम् विराधः पूरयन् वनम् |
पृच्छतो मम हि ब्रूतम् कौ युवाम् क्व गमिष्यथः || ३-३-१_END
BEGIN_
Then in his turn that demon Viradha said this sentence filling the forest with his gruesome voice, "I am asking you, really... 
tell me who you are and whereto you wish to go? " [3-3-1]_END

B_3_C_1_13



B_3_C_2_8
BEGIN_
 युवाम् जटा चीर धरौ सभार्यौ क्षीण जीवितौ || ३-२-१०
 
  प्रविष्टौ दण्डकारण्यम् शर चाप असि पाणिनौ |_END
BEGIN_
 "You two wear jute cloths like hermits, but handle arrows, bows and swords like
  warriors, yet entered Dandaka forest with your wife... your lives are on the wane...
  [3-2-10b-11a]_END

B_3_C_3_1
BEGIN_
तम् उवाच ततो रामो राक्षसम् ज्वलित आननम् |
पृच्छन्तम् सुमहातेजा इक्ष्वाकु कुलम् आत्मनः || ३-३-२_END
BEGIN_
Then that highly resplendent Rama said about his Ikshvaku dynasty to the blazing faced demon who is insistent. [3-3-2]_END

B_3_C_1_14



B_3_C_2_9
BEGIN_
 कथम् तापसयोः युवाम् च वासः प्रमदया सह || ३-२-११
 
  अधर्म चारिणौ पापौ कौ युवाम् मुनि दूषकौ |_END
BEGIN_
 "How saintly are you while living with your wife? You sinful fellows dishonest are
  you ways... who are you... you insulters of sainthood? [3-2-11b-12a]_END

B_3_C_3_2
BEGIN_
क्षत्रियौ वृत्त संपन्नौ विद्धि नौ वनगोचरौ |
त्वाम् तु वेदितुम् इच्छावः कः त्वम् चरसि दण्डकान् || ३-३-३_END
BEGIN_
"Know us as Kshatriya-s with ennobled bearing, and we are trekking the forest...but we wish to know about you, who are you 
that move about in Dandaka forest? [3-3-3]_END

B_3_C_1_15



B_3_C_2_10
BEGIN_
 अहम् वनम् इदम् दुर्गम् विराघो नाम राक्षसः || ३-२-१२
 
  चरामि सायुधो नित्यम् ऋषि मांसानि भक्षयन् |_END
BEGIN_
 "I am a demon named Viradha and I will be on the rove in this impassable forest
  with weapon, always eating the flesh of sages... [3-2-12b-13a]_END

B_3_C_3_3
BEGIN_
तम् उवाच विराधः तु रामम् सत्य पराक्रमम् |
हन्त वक्ष्यामि ते राजन् निबोध मम राघव || ३-३-४_END
BEGIN_
Viradha said to that truly valiant Rama, "Ah! I'll tell you, oh king, be informed of me, oh Raghava... [3-3-4]_END

B_3_C_1_16



B_3_C_2_11
BEGIN_
 इयम् नारी वरारोहा मम भार्या भविष्यति || ३-२-१३
 
  युवयोः पापयोः च अहम् पास्यामि रुधिरम् मृधे |_END
BEGIN_
 "This best waisted woman will be my wife, and I will drink your blood of you two
  sinful one in a fight with you... [3-2-13b-14a]_END

B_3_C_3_4
BEGIN_
पुत्रः किल जवस्य अहम् माता मम शतह्रदा |
विराध इति माम् आहुः पृथिव्याम् सर्व राक्षसाः || ३-३-५_END
BEGIN_
"I am the son of Java indeed... my mother is Shatahradaa, and all the demons on earth call me Viradha...'[3-3-5]_END

B_3_C_1_17
BEGIN_
रूपसंहननं लक्ष्मीं सौकुमार्यं सुवेषताम् |
ददृशुर्विस्मिताकारा रामस्य वनवासिनः || ३-१-१३_END
BEGIN_
Those forest-dwelling sages saw the physical built, its augustness and gracefulness, and his fine attire remaining in astonished 
postures. [3-1-13]_END

B_3_C_2_12
BEGIN_
 तस्य एवम् ब्रुवतो दुष्टम् विराधस्य दुरात्मनः || ३-२-१४
 
  श्रुत्वा सगर्वितम् वाक्यम् संभ्रान्ता जनकात्मजा |_END
BEGIN_
 On listening those arrogant words spoken in bad intent by that evil minded
  Viradha, Seetha, the daughter of Janaka, is much panicked. [3-2-14b-15a.]_END

B_3_C_3_5
BEGIN_
तपसा च अभि संप्राप्ता ब्रह्मणो हि प्रसादजा |
शस्त्रेण अवध्यता लोके अच्छेद्य अभेद्यत्वम् एव च || ३-३-६_END
BEGIN_
"On my undertaking ascesis I derived a boon from the beneficence of Brahma, by which I will neither be cut, nor slit, nor 
killed with a weapon in this world..."[3-3-6]_END

B_3_C_1_18
BEGIN_
वैदेहीं लक्ष्मणं रामं नेत्रैरनिमिषैरिव |
आश्चरभूतान् ददृशुः सर्वे ते पनवासिनः || ३-१-१४_END
BEGIN_
The forest-dwellers saw Seetha, Lakshmana and Rama, without a wink on their own eyes, as that trio is causing surprise with 
their arrival._END

B_3_C_2_13
BEGIN_
 सीता प्रावेपिता उद्वेगात् प्रवाते कदली यथा || ३-२-१५
 
  ताम् दृष्ट्वा राघवः सीताम् विराध अङ्कगताम् शुभाम् |
  अब्रवीत् लक्ष्मणम् वाक्यम् मुखेन परिशुष्यता || ३-२-१६_END
BEGIN_
 Seetha in fear wiggled like a plantain tree in a whirlwind, and on seeing at the
  auspicious lady gone into the arms of Viradha, Raghava spoke this sentence to Lakshmana, with his
  face fully turning to pale. [3-2-15b-16]_END

B_3_C_3_6
BEGIN_
उत्सृज्य प्रमदाम् एनाम् अनपेक्षौ यथा आगतम् |
त्वरमाणौ पलायेथाम् न वाम् जीवितम् आददे || ३-३-७_END
BEGIN_
"Leave off this lady without any yearning for her, and you expeditiously flee-away as you have come, then your lives will 
not be snatched away... [3-3-7]_END

B_3_C_1_19
BEGIN_
आत्रैनं हि महाभागाः सर्वभूतहिते रताः |
अतिथिं पर्णशालायां राघवं संन्यवेशयन् || ३-१-१५_END
BEGIN_
Those august sages that are interested in the well being of all beings have indeed accommodated Rama in that hermitage, 
as Rama is their guest a priori. [3-1-15]_END

B_3_C_2_14
BEGIN_
 पश्य सौंय नरेन्द्रस्य जनकस्य अत्म संभवाम् |
 
  मम भार्याम् शुभाचाराम् विराधाङ्के प्रवेशिताम् || ३-२-१७
  अत्यन्त सुख संवृद्धाम् राजपुत्रीम् यशस्विनीम् |_END
BEGIN_
 "See! Gentle Lakshmana, see that illustrious princes Seetha, the daughter of
  emperor Janaka, one who is brought up comfortably in immense comfort, and my auspiciously
  traditional wife... now gone into the wretched hands of a demon... [3-2-17-18a]_END

B_3_C_3_7
BEGIN_
तम् रामः प्रति उवाच इदम् कोप संरक्त लोचनः |
राक्षसम् विकृत आकारम् विराधम् पाप चेतसम् || ३-३-८_END
BEGIN_
Rama in reply said this to that ogre Viradha, whose eyes are fully bloodshot in anger, who is monstrous in his body, and 
evil in intent... [3-3-8]_END

B_3_C_1_20
BEGIN_
ततो रामस्य सत्कृत्य विधिना पावकोपमाः |
अजह्रुस्ते महाभागाः सलिलं धर्मचारिणः || ३-१-१६_END
BEGIN_
Then those august sages who are similar to sacred fire in glow have procedurally accorded guestship to Rama, and fetched 
water for him. [3-1-17]_END

B_3_C_2_15
BEGIN_
 यत् अभिप्रेतम् अस्मासु प्रियम् वर वृतम् च यत् || ३-२-१८
 
  कैकेय्यास्तु सुसंवृत्तम् क्षिप्रम् अद्य एव लक्ष्मण |_END
BEGIN_
 "That which is desired to befall on us, and that which is the choicest desire of
  Kaikeyi, and that which is concomitant to her boons, oh, Lakshmana, that has come to pass
  quickly, and today only Lakshmana... [3-2-18b-19a]_END

B_3_C_3_8
BEGIN_
क्षुद्र धिक्त्वाम् तु हीनार्थम् मृत्युम् अन्वेषसे ध्रुवम् |
रणे प्राप्स्यसि संतिष्ठ न मे जीवन् विमोक्ष्यसे || ३-३-९_END
BEGIN_
"You knave, fie upon you... you are in quest of you own death for your meanly measures, and definitely you will get it in 
this confrontation. Stay! I will not let you to live... [3-3-9]_END

B_3_C_1_21
BEGIN_
मङ्गलानि प्रयुञ्जना मुदा परमया युताः |
मूलं पुष्पं फलं सर्वमाश्रमं च महात्मनः || ३-१-१७
निवेदयित्वा ध्र्मज्ञास्ते तु प्राञ्जलयोऽब्रुवन् |_END
BEGIN_
On sounding out Vedic blessings those virtuous sages have offered flowers, fruits and tubers, and even the entire hermitage 
to that great soul Rama, and then with their palms adjoined. [3-1-17-18a]_END

B_3_C_2_16
BEGIN_
 या न तुष्यति राज्येन पुत्रार्थे दीर्घ दर्शिनी || ३-२-१९
 
  ययाऽहम् सर्वभूतानाम् प्रियः प्रस्थापितो वनम् |
  अद्य इदानीम् सकामा सा या माता मम मध्यमा || ३-२-२०_END
BEGIN_
 "She who is a foresighted lady, she who is not happy with the kingdom for her son,
  she by whom I, a dear one to all beings, am sent to forests, and she is my middle mother, her
  desire is fulfilled today, nay now itself... [3-2-19b-20]_END

B_3_C_4_0
BEGIN_
ह्रियमाणौ तु काकुत्स्थौ दृष्ट्वा सीता रघूत्तमौ |
उच्चैः स्वरेण चुक्रोश प्रगृह्य सु महाभुजौ || ३-४-१_END
BEGIN_
On seeing those two very dexterous scions of Kakutstha, and the best ones from Raghu dynasty, namely Rama and Lakshmana, 
grabbed and being carried off, Seetha screamed in a high-pitched voice.[3-4-1]_END

B_3_C_3_9
BEGIN_
ततः सज्यम् धनुः कृत्वा रामः सुनिशितान् शरान् |
सु शीघ्रम् अभिसंधाय राक्षसम् निजघान ह || ३-३-१०_END
BEGIN_
Then, stringing his bow Rama indeed darted very sharp arrows, very quickly and well aiming the demon... [3-3-10]_END

B_3_C_1_22
BEGIN_
धर्मपालो जनस्यास्य शरण्यश्च महायशाः || ३-१-१८
पूजनीयश्च मान्यश्च राजा दण्डधरो गुरुः |_END
BEGIN_
"The king will have great renown for he is the ruler of the righteousness of these people, a protector, a respectable and 
adorable one, and as he wields the sceptre of justice, he is a revered one too... [3-1-18-19a]_END

B_3_C_2_17
BEGIN_
 पर स्पर्शात् तु वैदेह्या न दुःखतरम् अस्ति मे |
 
  पितुर् विनाशात् सौमित्रे स्व राज्य हरणात् तथा || ३-२-२१_END
BEGIN_
 "To me, oh, Soumitri, the grief of others touching Seetha is more, than father's
  demise or grabbing away my kingdom... [3-2-21]_END

B_3_C_3_10
BEGIN_
धनुषा ज्या गुणवता सप्त बाणान् मुमोच ह |
रुक्म पुंखान् महावेगान् सुपर्ण अनिल तुल्य गान् || ३-३-११_END
BEGIN_
Indeed seven arrows are let off with perfectly stringed bow, which have golden vanes, and very fast ones that equal the 
flights of Garuda, the Divine Eagle and the Air-god. [3-3-11]_END

B_3_C_4_1
BEGIN_
एष दाशरथी रामः सत्यवान् शीलवान् शुचिः |
रक्षसा रौद्र रूपेण ह्रियते सह लक्ष्मणः || ३-४-२_END
BEGIN_
"He that truth-abiding, virtuous, and the flawless Rama of Dasharatha is carried off along with Lakshmana by the demon with 
a ferocious look... [3-4-2]_END

B_3_C_1_23
BEGIN_
इन्द्रस्यव चतुर्भागः प्रजा रक्षति राघव || ३-१-१९
राजा तस्माद् वरान् भोगान् रम्यान् भुङ्कै नम |_END
BEGIN_
"The fourth part of Indra is the protector of people, called the king, and hence Oh! Raghava, the king is hailed, and hence 
he enjoys best and delightful fortune... [3-1-19b-20a]_END

B_3_C_2_18
BEGIN_
 इति ब्रुवति काकुत्स्थे बाष्प शोक परिप्लुतः |
 
  अब्रवीत् लक्ष्मणः क्रुद्धो रुद्धो नाग इव श्वसन् || ३-२-२२_END
BEGIN_
 When said thus by Rama, Lakshmana said this with flooding tears of lament, and in
  his anger hissing like a forestalled snake. [3-2-22]_END

B_3_C_3_11
BEGIN_
ते शरीरम् विराधस्य भित्त्वा बर्हिण वाससः |
निपेतुः शोणिता दिग्धा धरण्याम् पावकोपमाः || ३-३-१२_END
BEGIN_
But, they the arrows that are akin to infernos and dressed with peacock feathers as their fins, on piercing the body of 
Viradha they fell onto the ground besmirched with blood. [3-3-12]_END

B_3_C_4_2
BEGIN_
माम् ऋका भक्ष इष्यन्ति शार्दूल द्वीपिनः तथा |
माम् हरः उत्सृज्य काकुत्स्थौ नमस्ते राक्षसोत्तमः || ३-४-३_END
BEGIN_
"Wild bears, tigers and panthers aspire to eat me away... oh, best demon, thieve me instead and release Kakutstha-s... Hail 
to thee..." [Said Seetha.] [3-4-3]_END

B_3_C_1_24
BEGIN_
ते वयं भवता रक्ष्या भवद्विषयवासिनः |
नगरस्थो वनस्थोवा त्वं नो राजा जनेश्वरः || ३-१-२०_END
BEGIN_
"You alone have to protect us as we are the subjects living in your kingdom..May you be in the capital... or in the forest...you 
are our king... [3-1-20b,c]_END

B_3_C_2_19
BEGIN_
 अनाथ इव भूतानाम् नाथः त्वम् वासवोपमः |
 
  मया प्रेष्येण काकुत्स्थः किम् अर्थम् परितप्यसे || ३-२-२३_END
BEGIN_
 "Oh, Rama, you being the Indra like lord of all beings, and while you are being
  attended by an adherent like me, what for you worry yourself like a derelict? [3-2-23]_END

B_3_C_3_12
BEGIN_
स विद्धो न्यस्य वैदेहीम् शूलम् उद्यंय राक्षसः |
अभ्यद्रवत् सुसंक्रुद्धः तदा रामम् स लक्ष्मणम् || ३-३-१३_END
BEGIN_
When that demon is thus struck, then he placed Vaidehi down from his arms, hauled up his spear, and very angrily rushed 
towards Rama and Lakshmana. [3-3-13]_END

B_3_C_4_3
BEGIN_
तस्याः तत् वचनम् श्रुत्वा वैदेह्याः राम लक्ष्मणौ |
वेगम् प्रचक्रतुर् वीरौ वधे तस्य दुरात्मनः || ३-४-४_END
BEGIN_
On hearing Vaidehi's that utterance those valorous ones Rama and Lakshmana speedily busied themselves in eliminating that 
evil-minded demon Viradha. [3-4-4]_END

B_3_C_1_25
BEGIN_
न्यस्तदण्डा वयं राजञ्जितक्रोधा जित्रेन्द्रियाः |
रक्षणीयास्त्वया श्श्वद्गर्भभूतास्तपोधनाः || ३-१-२१_END
BEGIN_
"We gave-up punishments, either physically or by the power of curses, conquered are our anger and senses, and our ascesis 
is the only wealth of ours, thus oh! King, we are to be protected by you, like the foetus inside a womb... [3-1-21]_END

B_3_C_2_20
BEGIN_
 शरेण निहतस्य अद्य मया क्रुद्धेन रक्षसः |
 
  विराधस्य गत असोः हि मही पास्यति शोणितम् || ३-२-२४_END
BEGIN_
 "He will now be felled with my arrow as I am enraged at him, and gone are his
  lives now, and indeed the earth shall drink his blood... [3-2-24]_END

B_3_C_3_13
BEGIN_
स विनद्य महानादम् शूलम् शक्र ध्वज उपमम् |
प्रगृह्य अशोभत तदा व्यात्तानन इव अंतकः || ३-३-१४_END
BEGIN_
And holding fast his spear that is similar to the Indra's Flagstaff he blaringly yelled a ghastly shriek, and thus he shone 
forth like the wide-mouthed Death, ready-to-gulp. [3-3-14]_END

B_3_C_1_26
BEGIN_
एवमुक्त्वा फलैर्मुलैह् पुष्पैरन्यैश्च राघवम् |
वन्यैश्च विविधाहारैः सलक्ष्मणमपूजयन् || ३-१-२२_END
BEGIN_
Thus saying they worshipped Raghava along with Lakshmana, on giving fruits, tubers, flowers and other varieties of forest 
foods. [3-1-22]_END

B_3_C_4_4
BEGIN_
तस्य रौद्रस्य सौमित्रिः सव्यम् बाहुम् बभञ्ज ह |
रामः तु दक्षिणम् बाहुम् तरसा तस्य रक्षसः || ३-४-५_END
BEGIN_
Soumitri indeed severed the left arm of that ferocious one, while Rama rent the right arm of that demon with his might. [3-4-5]_END

B_3_C_2_21
BEGIN_
 राज्य कामे मम क्रोधो भरते यो बभूव ह |
 
  तम् विराधे विमोक्ष्यामि वज्री वज्रम् इव अचले ||३-२-२५_END
BEGIN_
 "Indeed, that which anger was there to me on Bharata when he desired kingdom, that
  anger I will now release on Viradha, as Indra released his Thunderbolt on the mountain...
  [3-2-25]_END

B_3_C_3_14
BEGIN_
अथ तौ भ्रातरौ दीप्तम् शर वर्षम् ववर्षतुः |
विराधे राक्षसे तस्मिन् कालांतक अयम् उपमे || ३-३-१५_END
BEGIN_
Then with an effulgent arrow-rain those two brothers incessantly rained on demon Viradha, who is similar to the terminator 
of lifetime. [3-3-15]_END

B_3_C_1_27
BEGIN_
तथान्ये तापसाः सिद्धा रामं वैश्वानरोपमाः |
न्यायवृत्ता यथान्यायं तर्पयामासुरीश्वरम् || ३-१-२३_END
BEGIN_
Thus other saints and sages who are the followers of the virtue, and similar to the Sacred Fire adored Rama, the king, according 
to the wont of custom. [3-1-23]_END

B_3_C_4_5
BEGIN_
सः भग्न बहुः संविग्नः पपात आशु विमूर्छितः |
धरण्याम् मेघ संकाशो वज्र भिन्न इव अचलः || ३-४-६_END
BEGIN_
When his arms are mutilated that demon similar to a dark-cloud is frustrated, fainted, and fell onto ground, like the mountain 
demolished by the Thunderbolt of Indra. [3-4-6]_END

B_3_C_2_22
BEGIN_
 मम भुज बल वेग वेगितः
 
  पततु शरोऽस्य महान् महोरसि |
  व्यपनयतु तनोः च जीवितम्
  पततु ततः च महीम् विघूर्णितः || ३-२-२६_END
BEGIN_
 "Accelerated by my shoulder strength this ruinous arrow shall fall on his massive
  chest, thus life from his body shall decamp, and then he shall whirlingly fall onto the earth..."
  So said Lakshmana. [3-2-26]_END

B_3_C_3_15
BEGIN_
स प्रहस्य महा रौद्रः स्थित्वा अजृम्भत राक्षसः |
जृंभमाणस्य ते बाणाः कायात् निष्पेतुर् अशुगाः || ३-३-१६_END
BEGIN_
He that highly horrendous demon laughed at that arrow-shower, and standing for a while he yawned, and on his yawning and 
stretching his limbs in fatigue those arrows that earlier have gone speedily, spilled out from his body that speedily. [3-3-16]_END

B_3_C_4_6
BEGIN_
मुष्टिभिर् बाहुभिर् पद्भिः सूदयन्तौ तु राक्षसम् |
उद्यंयोद्यंय च अपि एनम् स्थण्डिले निष्पिपेषतुः || ३-४-७_END
BEGIN_
They battered that demon with their fists, hands and feet, and even by heaving and hurling him again and again they entirely 
pounded on him on the ground. [3-4-7]_END

B_3_C_3_16
BEGIN_
स्पर्शात् तु वर दानेन प्राणान् संरोध्य राक्षसः |
विराधः शूलम् उद्यंय राघवौ अभ्यधावत || ३-३-१७_END
BEGIN_
Demon Viradha held back his lives by the touch of boon, and raising up the spear he ran quickly at Rama and Lakshmana. [3-3-17]_END

B_3_C_4_7
BEGIN_
स विद्धो बहुभिर् बाणैः खड्गाभ्याम् च परिक्षतः |
निष्पिष्टो बहुधा भूमौ न ममार स राक्षसः || ३-४-८_END
BEGIN_
Though that demon is battered with many arrows, even sheared off with two swords, and even though he is entirely pounded 
on the ground he is not killed. [3-4-8]_END

B_3_C_3_17
BEGIN_
तत् शूलम् वज्र संकाशम् गगने ज्वलन उपमम् |
द्वाभ्याम् शराभ्याम् चिच्छेद रामः शस्त्रभृताम् वरः || ३-३-१८_END
BEGIN_
The best wielder of weaponry Rama ripped that spear apart, which is akin to the Thunderbolt of Indra, and that which is 
like a blaze in the sky, with two arrows in the sky itself. [3-3-18]_END

B_3_C_5_0
BEGIN_
हत्वा तु तम् भीम बलम् विराधम् राक्षसम् वने |
ततः सीताम् परिष्वज्य समाश्वास्य च वीर्यवान् || ३-५-१
अब्रवीत् भ्रातरम् रामो लक्ष्मणम् दीप्त तेजसम् |_END
BEGIN_
After killing that stupendously mighty demon Viradha in forest, then Rama comfortingly embraced Seetha, and spoke to his 
brother Lakshmana who is beaming forth with resplendence. [3-5-1]_END

B_3_C_4_8
BEGIN_
तम् प्रेक्ष्य रामः सुभृशम् अवध्यम् अचल उपमम् |
भयेषु अभय दः श्रीमान् इदम् वचनम् अब्रवीत् || ३-४-९_END
BEGIN_
On observing that the mountain-similar demon is ineradicable that easily, then Rama, the sublime one, and the bestower of 
shelter in fear, spoke this sentence to Lakshmana. [3-4-9]_END

B_3_C_5_1
BEGIN_
कष्टम् वनम् इदम् दुर्गम् न च स्मो वन गोचराः || ३-५-२
अभिगच्छामहे शीघ्रम् शरभङ्गम् तपो धनम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Difficult is this impassable forest, nor we are forest inhabitants either... let's go quickly to that ascetically rich 
sage Sharabhanga..." [3-5-2b, 3a]_END

B_3_C_4_9
BEGIN_
तपसा पुरुषव्याघ्र राक्षसोऽयम् न शक्यते |
शस्त्रेण युधि निर्जेतुम् राक्षसम् निखनावहे || ३-४-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Oh! Manly-tiger Lakshmana, it is impossible to overpower this demon with weapons in a confrontation, hence, let's bury 
this demon... [3-4-10]_END

B_3_C_3_18
BEGIN_
तत् राम विशिखैः छिन्नम् शूलम् तस्य आपतत् भुविः |
पपात अशनिना चिन्नम् मेरोर् इव शिला तलम् || ३-३-१९_END
BEGIN_
Shattered by Rama's blazing shafts that spear fallen on ground like the boulder mass of Mt. Meru when it is shattered by 
Indra's Thunderbolt. [3-3-19]_END

B_3_C_3_19
BEGIN_
तौ खड्गौ क्षिप्रम् उद्यंय कृष्ण सर्पौ इव उद्यतौ |
तूर्णम् आपेततुः तस्य तदा प्रहारताम् बलात् || ३-३-२०_END
BEGIN_
They quickly upraised their swords and like a pair of up-swinging black-cobras they rapidly crashed on him, and then battered 
him mightily. [3-3-20]_END

B_3_C_5_2
BEGIN_
आश्रमम् शरभन्गस्य राघवोऽभिजगाम ह || ३-५-३
तस्य देव प्रभावस्य तपसा भावित आत्मनः |
समीपे शरभंगस्य ददर्श महत् अद्भुतम् ||३-५-४_END
BEGIN_
On his approach at the hermitage of Sage Sharabhanga, a sage with a divine effect and the one with a purified soul, saw 
a great wonder at the nearby of that hermitage of Sharabhanga.[3-5-3b, 4]_END

B_3_C_4_10
BEGIN_
कुंजर्स्य इव रौद्रस्य राक्षसस्य अस्य लक्ष्मण! |
वने अस्मिन् सुमहद् श्वभ्रम् खन्यताम् रौद्रवर्चसः || ३-४-११_END
BEGIN_
"Lakshmana, a very deep pit be dug for this furious and ferocious reprobate in this forest, as though for an elephant... 
[3-4-11]_END

B_3_C_5_3
BEGIN_
विभ्राजमानम् वपुषा सूर्य वैश्वानर प्रभम् |
रथ प्रवरम् आरूढम् आकाशे विबुध अनुगम् || ३-५-५
असंस्पृशन्तम् वसुधाम् ददर्श विबुध ईश्वरम् |
संप्रभ आभरणम् देवम् विरजो अंबर धारिणम् || ३-५-६
तत् विधैः एव बहुभिर् पूज्यमानम् महात्मभिः |_END
BEGIN_
Rama has seen Indra, the lord of three worlds, with a radiant body that has the coupled radiance of Sun and Fire, mounted 
on a great chariot that does not touch the earth, wearing greatly brilliant ornaments and attired in spotless dress, while 
the other divinities are attending, and many more selfsame great-souls are worshipping him. [3-5-5, 6, 7a]_END

B_3_C_3_20
BEGIN_
स वध्यमान सुभृशम् भुजाभ्याम् परिगृह्य तौ |
अप्रकंप्यौ नरव्याघ्रौ रौद्रः प्रस्थातुम् ऐच्छत || ३-३-२१_END
BEGIN_
He that demon thus beaten very firmly by Rama and Lakshmana, then on grabbing those unwavering ones and manly tigers with 
his arms, that furious demon wished to carry them away. [3-3-21]_END

B_3_C_4_11
BEGIN_
इति उक्त्वा लक्ष्मणम् रामः प्रदरः खन्यताम् इति |
तस्थौ विराधम् आक्र्ंय कण्ठे पादेन वीर्यवान् || ३-४-१२_END
BEGIN_
On saying to Lakshmana that a trench shall be dug...' then Rama repressively placed his foot on the throat of Viradha, and 
stood by. [3-4-12]_END

B_3_C_3_21
BEGIN_
तस्य अभिप्रायम् अज्ञाय रामो लक्ष्मणम् अब्रवीत् |
वहतु अयम् अलम् तावत् पथानेन तु राक्षसः || ३-३-२२_END
BEGIN_
Knowing the thinking of the demon for sure, Rama spoke to Lakshmana, "Let him easily carry us anywhere on his way... [3-3-22]_END

B_3_C_5_4
BEGIN_
हरितैः वाजिभिर् युक्तम् अंतरिक्ष गतम् रथम् || ३-५-७
ददर्श अदूरतः तस्य तरुण आदित्य संनिभम् |
पाण्डुर अभ्र घन प्रख्यम् चन्द्र मण्डल संनिभम् || ३-५-८_END
BEGIN_
Rama saw at his very nearby a chariot yoked with green horses that traverses in firmament, which in its splendour is either 
like the noontime sun, or a cluster of silver clouds, or like the silvern sphere of the moon. [3-5-7b, 8]_END

B_3_C_4_12
BEGIN_
तत् श्रुत्वा राघवेण उक्तम् राक्षसः प्रश्रितम् वचः |
इदम् प्रोवाच काकुत्स्थम् विराधः पुरुषर्षभम् || ३-४-१३_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that said by Raghava, demon Viradha sincerely spoke these humble words to Rama, the finest one from Kakutstha 
dynasty. [3-4-13]_END

B_3_C_6_0
BEGIN_
 शरभङ्गे दिवम् प्राप्ते मुनि संघाः समागताः |
 
  अभ्यगच्छन्त काकुत्स्थम् रामम् ज्वलित तेजसम् || ३-६-१_END
BEGIN_
 On Sage Sharabhanga attaining heaven, groups of sages assembled and approached
  Rama of Kakutstha dynasty, who is glowing with resplendence. [3-6-1]_END

B_3_C_3_22
BEGIN_
यथा च इच्छति सौमित्रे तथा वहतु राक्षसः |
अयम् एव हि नः पन्था येन याति निशाचरः || ३-३-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Let this demon carry us as he wishes, and Saumitri, by which way this night-walker goes, that alone will be our way... 
[3-3-23]_END

B_3_C_4_13
BEGIN_
हतोऽहम् पुरुषव्याघ्रः शक्र तुल्य बलेन वै |
मया तु पूर्वम् त्वम् मोहान् न ज्ञातः पुरुषर्षभः || ३-४-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Dead I am, oh! Manly-tiger and a coequal of Indra in your strength... I have fallaciously not identified you earlier... 
oh, best one among men... [3-4-14]_END

B_3_C_5_5
BEGIN_
अपश्यत् विमलम् छत्रम् चित्र माल्य उपशोभितम् |
चामर व्यजने च अग्र्ये रुक्म दण्डे महाधने || ३-५-९
गृहीते वर नारीभ्याम् धूयमाने च मूर्धनि |_END
BEGIN_
He saw the stainless parasol of Indra, marvellously garlanded and shining forth, and the exemplary and invaluable royal 
fanning instruments with golden handles, which two best female celestials are handling and fanning at Indra's head sides 
with them. [3-5-9, 10a]_END

B_3_C_6_1
BEGIN_
 वैखानसा वालखिल्याः संप्रक्षाला मरीचिपाः |
 
  अश्म कुट्टाः च बहवः पत्र आहाराः च तापसाः || ३-६-२_END
BEGIN_
 The sages called Vaikahanasa-s, [who are born out of the nails of Prajaapati, the
  first ruler of mankind,] also Vaalakhilyaa-s, [those born from His hair,] and those from the
  water of His feet-wash, and those that thrive on drinking rays of sun and moon alone, and those
  that pound with stones and others who thrive on leaves alone, are those sages... [3-6-2]_END

B_3_C_3_23
BEGIN_
स तु स्व बल वीर्येण समुत्क्षिप्य निशाचरः |
बालाः इव स्कन्ध गतौ चकार अति बलोद्धतः || ३-३-२४_END
BEGIN_
But he that night-walker arrogant as he is by his might has uplifted Rama and Lakshmana like babies by that might and courage 
alone, and placed them on his shoulders as one would place babies. [3-3-24]_END

B_3_C_4_14
BEGIN_
कौसल्या सुप्रजातः तात रामः त्वम् विदितो मया |
वैदेही च महाभागा लक्ष्मणः च महायशाः || ३-४-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, sire, now I have known you to be Rama, the son of Kausalya... and even propitious Seetha and greatly renowned one Lakshmana 
are now known to me... [3-4-15]_END

B_3_C_5_6
BEGIN_
गन्धर्व अमर सिद्धाः च बहवः परम ऋषयः || ३-५-१०
अन्तरिक्ष गतम् देवम् गीर्भिर् अग्र्याभिर् ऐडियन् |_END
BEGIN_
And the celestials like gandharva-s, amara-s, siddhaa-s and very many great sages as well are extolling Indra who is abiding 
in firmament. [3-5-10b, 11a]_END

B_3_C_6_2
BEGIN_
 दन्त उलूखलिनः च एव तथा एव उन्मज्जकाः परे |
 
  गात्र शय्या अशय्याः च तथा एव अनवकाशिकाः || ३-६-३_END
BEGIN_
 Some of them use their own teeth to grid the grain they eat, and some who perform
  ascesis in neck-deep water, and some who sleep with their head resting on their shoulders or on
  chests without using any kind of bed, and some who do not use any kind of beds either, and some
  who meditate without any repose sitting in an enclosure without any leg-space. [3-6-3]_END

B_3_C_3_24
BEGIN_
तौ आरोप्य ततः स्कन्धम् राघवो रजनी चरः |
विराधो विनदन् घोरम् जगाम अभिमुखो वनम् || ३-३-२५_END
BEGIN_
That nightwalker Viradha on placing those two Raghava-s on his shoulders gone towards deeper forest yelling very luridly. 
[3-3-25]_END

B_3_C_4_15
BEGIN_
अभि शापाद् अहम् घोरम् प्रविष्टो राक्ष्सीम् तनुम् |
तुंबुरुः नाम गन्धर्वः शप्तो वैश्रवणेन हि || ४-३-१६_END
BEGIN_
"By curse I had to enter this ghoulish demon's body, but I am a celestial gandharva, named Tumburu and Kubera cursed me... 
[3-4-16]_END

B_3_C_5_7
BEGIN_
सह संभाषमाणे तु शरभंगेन वासवे || ३-५-११
दृष्ट्वा शत क्रतुम् तत्र रामो लक्ष्मणम् अब्रवीत् |_END
BEGIN_
On seeing Indra speaking there to sage Sharabhanga, Rama spoke to Lakshmana. [3-5-11b, 12a]_END

B_3_C_6_3
BEGIN_
 मुनयः सलिल आहारा वायु भक्षाः तथा अपरे |
 
  आकाश निलयाः च एव तथा स्थण्डिल शायिनः || ३-६-४_END
BEGIN_
 And some sages whose food is water alone, or air alone to some, like that some who
  meditate staying in sky and some who sleep on bare ground itself. [3-6-4]_END

B_3_C_3_25
BEGIN_
वनम् महा मेघ निभम् प्रविष्टो
द्रुमैः महद्भिः विविधैः उपेतम् |
नाना विधैः पक्षि कुलैः विचित्रम्
शिव आयुतम् व्याल मृगैः विकीर्णम् || ३-३-२६_END
BEGIN_
That demon entered into a baffling forest that is like a very dark cloud in its sheen, where a variety of massive trees 
are contained in, numerous flocks of vulturine birds are overspreading, and where wild jackals and other predaceous animals 
are sprawling around, along with Rama and Lakshmana. [3-3-26]_END

B_3_C_4_16
BEGIN_
प्रसाद्यमानः च मया सोऽब्रवीत् माम् महायशाः |
यदा दाशरथी रमः त्वाम् वधिष्यति संयुगे || ३-४-१७
तदा प्रकृतिम् आपन्नो भवान् स्वर्गम् गमिष्यति |_END
BEGIN_
"When entreated by me, he that greatly renowned Kubera said to me, 'When Dasharatha's Rama kills you in a fight... then 
you will attain your nature of celestial body and you will go to heavens...' [3-4-17, 18a]_END

B_3_C_5_8
BEGIN_
रामोऽथ रथम् उद्दिश्य भ्रातुर् दर्शयत अद्भुतम् || ३-५-१२
अर्चिष्मन्तम् श्रिया जुष्टम् अद्भुतम् पश्य लक्ष्मण |
प्रतपन्तम् इव आदित्यम् अन्तरिक्ष गतम् रथम् || ३-५-१३_END
BEGIN_
Rama then on pointing out the chariot expressed his own amazement saying, "Lakshmana see this wonderful chariot that includes 
effulgence and auspiciousness as well, and that abides in firmament, and highly luminous like the Sun... [3-5-12b, 13]_END

B_3_C_6_4
BEGIN_
 तथा ऊर्थ्व वासिनः दान्ताः तथा आर्द्र पट वाससः |
 
  स जपाः च तपो नित्याः तथा पंच तपोऽन्विताः || ३-६-५_END
BEGIN_
 Thus some are dwellers on high-peaked places with their senses controlled, and
  some are wearers of wet cloths, always reciting name or hymn japa and like that some who meditate
  with five kinds of fire around them. [3-6-5]_END

B_3_C_4_17
BEGIN_
अनुपस्थीयमानो माम् स क्रुद्धो व्याजहार ह || ३-४-१८
इति वैश्रवणो राजा रंभ आसक्तम् उवाच ह |_END
BEGIN_
" King Kubera thus cursed angrily me for not presenting myself in his service when I was interested in a celestial dancer 
Rambha, and indeed he alone said this curse-clearance to me... [3-4-18b, 19a]_END

B_3_C_5_9
BEGIN_
ये हयाः पुरु हूतस्य पुरा शक्रस्य नः श्रुताः |
अन्तरिक्ष गता दिव्याः ते इमे हरयो ध्रुवम् || ३-५-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Of which horses we have earlier heard from our teachers telling that they belong to Indra, the Chief Invitee in Vedic rituals, 
they are these divinely green horses that now abide in the firmament, and definitely these must be Indra's horses... [3-5-14]_END

B_3_C_6_5
BEGIN_
 सर्वे ब्राह्ंया श्रिया ज्युक्ता दृढ योग समाहिताः |
 
  शरभंग आश्रमे रामम् अभिजग्मुः च तापसाः || ३-६-६_END
BEGIN_
 All have Vedic resplendence and firm yogic control, and they have arrived at the
  hermitage of Sage Sharabhanga for Rama. [3-6-6]_END

B_3_C_4_18
BEGIN_
तव प्रसादान् मुक्तो अहम् अभिशापात् सु दारुणात् || ३-४-१९
भुवनम् स्वम् गमिष्यामि स्वस्ति वोऽस्तु परंतप |_END
BEGIN_
" And by your grace I am released from this utterly hideous cruse, and now I wish to go to my own heavenly abode, oh, firestorm 
of enemies, let safety betide you all... [3-4-19b, 20a]_END

B_3_C_7_0
BEGIN_रामः तु सहितः भ्रात्रा सीतया च परंतपः |सुतीक्ष्णस्य आश्रम पदम् जगाम सह तैः द्विजैः 
|| ३-७-१_END
BEGIN_Rama, the enemy-scorcher, has gone towards the threshold of the hermitage of Sage Suteekshna 
along with his brother Lakshmana and Seetha, also along with those Brahmans who accompanied him all 
the way. [4-7-1]_END

B_3_C_5_10
BEGIN_
इमे च पुरुष व्याघ्र ये तिष्ठन्ति अभितः दिशम् |
शतम् शतम् कुण्डलिनो युवानः खड्ग पाणयः || ३-५-१५
विस्तीर्ण विपुल उरस्काः परिघायत बाहवः |
शोणांशु वसनाः सर्वे व्याघ्र इव दुरासदाः || ३-५-१६
उरो देशेषु सर्वेषाम् हारा ज्वलन संनिभाः |
रूपम् बिभ्रति सौमित्रे पंच विंशति वार्षिकम् || ३-५-१७_END
BEGIN_
"And oh, manly-tiger Lakshmana, those that are there in hundreds and hundreds around Indra, those youthful ones with their 
ear-ornaments and swords in hands, with wide and broad chests, with club shaped arms, and clad in glimmering red garments, 
all are like tigers, all are unapproachable, all of them are wearing ornamental chains on their chest-place that are akin 
to flaring fires, and in their appearance, Soumitri, they always bear a look of twenty-five-year-olds... [3-5-15, 16, 17]_END

B_3_C_6_6
BEGIN_
 अभिगंय च धर्मज्ञा रामम् धर्म भृताम् वरम् |
 
  ऊचुः परम धर्मज्ञम् ऋषि संघाः समागताः || ३-६-७_END
BEGIN_
 Those virtuous sages coming together in groups neared Rama, the best beholder of
  virtue, and said to that supreme one in virtue. [3-6-7]_END

B_3_C_4_19
BEGIN_
इतो वसति धर्मात्मा शरभङ्गः प्रतापवान् || ३-४-२०
अध्यर्थ योजने तातः महर्षिः सूर्य संनिभः |
तम् क्षिप्रम् अभिगच्छ त्वम् स ते श्रेयो अभिधास्यति || ३-४-२१_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Sire, att one and half yojana-s of distance from here Sage Sharabhanga, a great saint of virtue, and an efficacious 
sage with sun-like resplendence dwells, you shall quickly approach him for he advises you opportunely... [3-4-20-21]_END

B_3_C_5_11
BEGIN_
एतद्धि किल देवानाम् वयो भवति नित्यदा |
यथा इमे पुरुष व्याघ्रा दृश्यन्ते प्रिय दर्शनाः || ३-५-१८_END
BEGIN_
"The age factor of gods remains constant at the age that appears for these nice-looking Tigerly-men, so they say... 
for gods are immortals and they will be ever young... [3-5-18]_END

B_3_C_7_1
BEGIN_स गत्वा दीर्घम् अध्वानम् नदीः तीर्त्वा बहु उदकाः |ददर्श विमलम् शैलम् महा मेरुम् 
इव उन्नतम् || ३-७-२_END
BEGIN_He travelling on a long way, and on crossing rivers with plenty of waters has seen a 
tranquil mountain towering like great Mt. Meru. [3-7-2]_END

B_3_C_4_20
BEGIN_
अवटे च अपि माम् राम निक्षिप्य कुशली व्रज |
रक्षसाम् गत सत्त्वानाम् एष धर्मः सनातनः || ३-४-२२
अवटे ये निधीयन्ते तेषाम् लोकाः सनातनाः |_END
BEGIN_
"Rama you go safely on burying me in a pit... this is the age-old custom for those demons that lost vitality... those that 
are inhumed in pit, to them there will be the worlds of manes..." [3-4-22, 23a]_END

B_3_C_6_7
BEGIN_
 त्वम् इक्ष्वाकु कुलस्य अस्य पृथिव्याः च महारथः |
 
  प्रधानः च अपि नाथः च देवानाम् मघवान् इव || ३-६-८_END
BEGIN_
 "You are the supreme charioteer born in Ikshvaku dynasty hence you are the
  protector of earth under your control. As with Indra, the ruler of divinities you are a similar
  ruler for us. [3-6-8]_END

B_3_C_5_12
BEGIN_
इह एव सह वैदेह्या मुहूर्तम् तिष्ठ लक्ष्मण |
यावत् जानामि अहम् व्यक्तम् क एष द्युतिमान् रथे || ३-५-१९_END
BEGIN_
"Stay for a moment Lakshmana along with Vaidehi, until I know clearly about that resplendent one on that chariot... [3-5-19]_END

B_3_C_7_2
BEGIN_ततः तद् इक्ष्वाकु वरौ सततम् विविधैः द्रुमैः |काननम् तौ विविशतुः सीतया सह राघवौ 
|| ३-७-३_END
BEGIN_Then those best ones from Ikshvaku dynasty, those two Raghava-s along with Seetha have 
entered the forest which will always be full with diverse trees. [3-7-3]_END

B_3_C_4_21
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्त्वा तु काकुत्स्थम् विराधः शर पीडितः || ३-४-२३
बभूव स्वर्ग संप्राप्तो न्यस्त देहो महाबलः |_END
BEGIN_
"And on saying thus to Rama that Viradha who is hurt by arrows became heaven-worthy on leaving his body. [3-4-23b, 24a]_END

B_3_C_6_8
BEGIN_
 विश्रुतः त्रिषु लोकेषु यशसा विक्रमेण च |
 
  पितृ व्रतत्वम् सत्यम् च त्वयि धर्मः च पुष्कलः || ३-६-९_END
BEGIN_
 "You are well renowned in all the three worlds by your repute and valour, and in
  you abounding are the virtues like truthfulness and devotion to your father, and even
  righteousness too, is there. [3-6-9]_END

B_3_C_5_13
BEGIN_
तम् एवम् उक्त्वा सौमित्रिम् इह एव स्थीयताम् इति |
अभिचक्राम काकुत्स्थः शरभंग आश्रमम् प्रति || ३-५-२०_END
BEGIN_
On saying to Lakshmana stay there only...' Rama proceeded towards the hermitage of Sage Sharabhanga.. [3-5-20]_END

B_3_C_7_3
BEGIN_प्रविष्टः तु वनम् घोरम् बहु पुष्प फल द्रुमम् |ददर्श आश्रमम् एकान्ते चीर माला 
परिष्कृतम् || ३-७-४_END
BEGIN_Entering that perilous forest with its many a flower and fruit bearing trees, they have 
seen the hermitage in a reclusive place adorned with rows of jute cloths as though garlanding it. [3-7-4]_END

B_3_C_4_22
BEGIN_
तत् श्रुत्वा राघवः वाक्यम् लक्ष्मणम् व्यादिदेश ह || ३-४-२४
कुंजर्स्य इव रौद्रस्य राक्षसस्य अस्य लक्ष्मण! |
वने अस्मिन् सुमहत् श्वभ्रम् खन्यताम् रौद्रकर्मणः|| ३-४-२५
इति उक्त्वा लक्ष्मणम् रामः प्रदरः खन्यताम् इति |
तस्थौ विराधम् आक्रंय कण्ठे पादेन वीर्यवान् || ३-४-२६_END
BEGIN_
And Raghava on hearing those words of the demon ordered Lakshmana, "Lakshmana, a very deep pit be dug for this furious and 
ferocious reprobate in this forest, as though for an elephant..." On saying to Lakshmana that a trench shall be dug...' 
then Rama repressively placed his foot on the throat of Viradha, and stood by. [3-4-24b, 25, 26]_END

B_3_C_6_9
BEGIN_
 त्वाम् आसाद्य महात्मानम् धर्मज्ञम् धर्म वत्सलम् |
 
  अर्थित्वात् नाथ वक्ष्यामः तत् च नः क्षन्तुम् अर्हसि || ३-६-१०_END
BEGIN_
 "You are the great-souled one, knower of righteousness and a patron of virtue...
  such as you are, on approaching you we beg to state something for which we may please be
  excused... [3-6-10]_END

B_3_C_5_14
BEGIN_
ततः समभिगच्छन्तम् प्रेक्ष्य रामम् शची पतिः |
शरभंगम् अनुज्ञाप्य विबुधान् इदम् अब्रवीत् || ३-५-२१_END
BEGIN_
Then, on seeing Rama arriving there, Indra, bade farewell to Sage Sharabhanga and said this to the celestials attending 
him. [3-5-21]_END

B_3_C_7_4
BEGIN_तत्र तापसम् आसीनम् मल पङ्कज धारिणम् |रामः सुतीक्ष्णम् विधिवत् तपोधनम् अभाषत 
|| ३-७-५_END
BEGIN_There on seeing the ascetically rich Sage Suteekshna sitting in yogic posture with his 
body bearing lotus-like blotches of soil, Rama dutifully spoke to him. [3-7-5]_END

B_3_C_4_23
BEGIN_
ततः खनित्रम् आदाय लक्ष्मणः श्वभ्रम् उत्तमम् |
अखनत् पार्श्वतः तस्य विराधस्य महात्मनः || ३-४-२७_END
BEGIN_
Then, on taking a digging tool Lakshmana dug a deep pit beside the great soul Viradha. [3-4-27]_END

B_3_C_6_10
BEGIN_
 अधार्मः सुमहान् नाथ भवेत् तस्य तु भूपतेः |
 
  यो हरेत् बलि षड् भागम् न च रक्षति पुत्रवत् || ३-६-११_END
BEGIN_
 "Oh! , very great a-dharma, wrongness, will occur to that king who takes the sixth
  part of the country's produce as cess, but does not safeguard his subjects like his own sons...
  [3-6-11]_END

B_3_C_5_15
BEGIN_
इह उपयाति असौ रामो यावन् माम् न अभिभाषते |
निष्ठाम् नयत तावत् तु ततो मा द्रष्टुम् अर्हति || ३-५-२२
जितवन्तम् कृतार्थम् हि तदा अहम् अचिराद् इमम् |
कर्म हि अनेन कर्तव्यम् महत् अन्यैः सुदुष्करम् || ३-५-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Here comes that Rama...before he talks to me, you lead him towards his vow, after completing the result of his incarnation, 
then only he is eligible to see me... Let him be a victorious and accomplished one, then I will see him very soon...for 
that will happen very soon... A great deed is to be verily performed by him that is highly impossible for others... [3-5-22, 
23_END

B_3_C_7_5
BEGIN_रामोऽहम् अस्मि भगवन् भवन्तम् द्रष्टुम् आगतः |तत् मा अभिवद धर्मज्ञ महर्षे सत्य 
विक्रम || ३-७-६_END
BEGIN_"Oh! godly sage I am Rama, I have come to see you, hence oh, knower of virtue, oh, great 
sage, oh, one with truthfulness as your courage, please talk to me..." [3-7-6]_END

B_3_C_6_11
BEGIN_
 युंजानः स्वान् इव प्राणान् प्राणैः इष्टान् सुतान् इव |
 
  नित्य युक्तः सदा रक्षन् सर्वान् विषय वासिनः || ३-६-१२
  प्राप्नोति शाश्वतीम् राम कीर्तिम् स बहु वार्षिकीम् |
  ब्रह्मणः स्थानम् आसाद्य तत्र च अपि महीयते || ३-६-१३_END
BEGIN_
 "A king shall treat all the subjects of kingdom as his own sons, and he shall
  protect them as though he is ready to save them at the cost of his own lives, and he who will
  always be endeavouring in that manner will attain permanent renown lasting for many for many
  years to come, and thereby he attains a prosperous place even in Brahma's abode... [3-6-12,
  3]_END

B_3_C_4_24
BEGIN_
तम् मुक्त कण्ठम् उत्क्षिप्य शङ्कु कर्णम् महास्वनम् |
विराधम् प्राक्षिपत् श्वभ्रे नदन्तम् भैरव स्वनम् || ३-४-२८_END
BEGIN_
On releasing his throat from the stamping of Rama, he that long eared, lurid voiced Viradha is ensconced in that pit while 
he is still blaring with his horrific voice. [3-4-28]_END

B_3_C_5_16
BEGIN_
अथ वज्री तम् आमंत्र्य मानयित्वा च तापसम् |
रथेन हय युक्तेन ययौ दिवम् अरिन्दमः || ३-५-२४_END
BEGIN_
Then that Enemy-destroyer Indra adoringly bade farewell to the sage, and travelled to heavens by the chariot with its green 
horses. [3-5-24]_END

B_3_C_7_6
BEGIN_स निरीक्ष्य ततः धीरो रामम् धर्मभृताम् वरम् |समाश्लिष्य च बाहुभ्याम् इदम् वचनम् 
अब्रवीत् || ३-७-७_END
BEGIN_Then that sage having seen that brave and best proponent of virtue, Rama, embraced him 
with both of his hands, and spoke this sentence. [3-7-7]_END

B_3_C_8_0
BEGIN_
रामः तु सह सौमित्रिः सुतीक्ष्णेन अभिपूजितः |परिणांय निशाम् तत्र प्रभाते प्रत्यबुध्यत || ३-८-१_END
BEGIN_
Rama along with Soumitri is well revered by Sage Suteekhsna, spent that night there and awoken in the 
morning. [3-8-1]_END

B_3_C_4_25
BEGIN_
तम् आहवे दारुणम् आशु विक्रमौ
स्थिरौ उभौ संयति राम लक्ष्मणौ |
मुदान्वितौ चिक्षिपतुर् भयावहम्
नदन्तम् उत्क्षिप्य बिलेन राक्ष्सम् || ३-४-२९_END
BEGIN_
Those deftly victorious ones Rama and Lakshmana who compose themselves in a given fight, both have gladly raised that Viradha, 
a ghoulish one in fight, a terrifying demon who is still blaring, with all their might and hurled him into the pit. [3-4-29]_END

B_3_C_6_12
BEGIN_
 यत् करोति परम् धर्मम् मुनिः मूल फल अशनः |
 
  तत्र राज्ञः चतुर् भागः प्रजा धर्मेण रक्षतः || ३-६-१४_END
BEGIN_
 "He who righteously protects his subjects will get one fourth of the merit of
  great duty-bound deeds performed by each individual sage, say yajna-s, ascesis, meditation etc.
  performances. [3-6-14]_END

B_3_C_5_17
BEGIN_
प्रयाते तु सहस्राक्षे राघवः सपरिच्छदः |
अग्नि होत्रम् उपासीनम् शरभंगम् उपागमत् || ३-५-२५_END
BEGIN_
On the transit of that Thousand-eyed Indra, Raghava with his adherents [namely Lakshmana and Seetha,] came nearby the 
Sage Sharabhanga, who is sitting nearby the altar of fire. [3-5-25]_END

B_3_C_7_7
BEGIN_स्वागतम् ते रघु श्रेष्ठ राम सत्यभृताम् वर |आश्रमओ अयम् त्वया आक्रान्तः सनाथ 
इव सांप्रतम् || ३-७-८_END
BEGIN_"Welcome to you Rama, best of Raghu dynasty and the best patron of truth, and when you 
presently caught this hermitage unprepared this has become a well-lorded one... [3-7-8]_END

B_3_C_8_1
BEGIN_
उत्थाय च यथा कालम् राघवः सह सीतया |उपस्पृश्य सु शीतेन तोयेन उत्पल गंधिना || ३-८-२_END
BEGIN_
Rama got up according to time along with Seetha and touched finely cool water with lotus-fragrance for 
morning bath. [3-8-2]_END

B_3_C_6_13
BEGIN_
 सो अयम् ब्राह्मण भूयिष्ठो वानप्रस्थ गणो महान् |
 
  त्वम् नाथो अनाथवत् राम राक्षसैः हन्यते भृशम् || ३-६-१५_END
BEGIN_
 "O, Rama, though you are there as protector for the hermitages, suchlike this one,
  where the most reverent Brahmans are there numerously, they look as though forsaken, for they are
  being demolished by demons, devastatingly... [3-6-15]_END

B_3_C_4_26
BEGIN_
अवध्यताम् प्रेक्ष्य महासुरस्य तौ
शितेन शस्त्रेण तदा नरर्षभौ |
समर्थ्य च अत्यर्थ विशारदौ उभौ
बिले विरधस्य वधम् प्रचक्रतुः || ३-४-३०_END
BEGIN_
On observing the indestructibility of that demon with any weapon, however sharp it might be, those two best ones among men 
that are very expertly skilled have thought over well and undertook the elimination of that great demon in a pit. [3-4-30]_END

B_3_C_5_18
BEGIN_
तस्य पादौ च संगृह्य रामः सीता च लक्ष्मणः |
निषेदुः तद् अनुज्ञाता लब्ध वासा निमंत्रिताः || ३-५-२६_END
BEGIN_
Touching the feet of that Sage Sharabhanga Rama along with Seetha and Lakshmana, and duly permitted and invited by that 
Sage Sharabhanga they sat there, as they obtained a shelter. [3-5-26]_END

B_3_C_7_8
BEGIN_प्रतीक्षमाणः त्वाम् एव न आरोहे अहम् महायशः |देव लोकम् इतो वीर देहम् त्यक्त्वा 
महीतले || ३-७-९चित्रकूटम् उपादाय राज्य भ्रष्टो असि मे श्रुतः |_END
BEGIN_"I am awaiting for you only, oh, greatly renowned one, without my ascent to heavens by 
casting off this body on the earth's plane, oh, brave one, for I have heard that you have arrived at 
Chitrakuta after you are repudiated from your kingdom... [3-7-9]_END

B_3_C_8_2
BEGIN_
अथ ते अग्निम् सुराम् च एव वैदेही राम लक्ष्मणौ |काल्यम् विधिवत् अभ्यर्च्य तपस्वि शरणे वने || ३-८-३
उदयन्तम् दिनकरम् दृष्ट्वा विगत कल्मषाः |सुतीक्ष्णम् अभिगंय इदम् श्लक्ष्णम् वचनम् अब्रुवन् || ३-८-४_END
BEGIN_
Then they all, Vaidehi, Rama and Lakshmana, on worshipping sacred fire and deities dutifully in the 
shelter of the sages in that forest and on seeing the dawning sun, they are reft of their blemishes, 
and then they approached Sage Suteekshna speaking this sentence gently. [3-8-3, 4]_END

B_3_C_6_14
BEGIN_
 एहि पश्य शरीराणि मुनीनाम् भावित आत्मनाम् |
 
  हतानाम् राक्षसैः घोरैः बहूनाम् बहुधा वने || ३-६-१६_END
BEGIN_
 "Come and see many of the bodies of the sages, the contemplative souls, that are
  variously killed by ghastly demons in the forest... [3-6-16]_END

B_3_C_4_27
BEGIN_
स्वयम् विराधेन हि मृत्युम् आत्मनः
प्रसह्य रामेण वधार्थम् ईप्सितः |
निवेदितः कानन चारिणा स्वयम्
न मे वधः शस्त्र कृतो भवेत् इति || ३-४-३१_END
BEGIN_
Viradha himself preferred his death at the hands of Rama and desired for a long to be killed by Rama and that forest walker 
himself appraised that, "Killing me with any weapon is impossible..." [3-4-31]_END

B_3_C_5_19
BEGIN_
ततः शक्र उपयानम् तु पर्यपृच्छत राघवः |
शरभंगः च तत् सर्वम् राघवाय न्यवेदयत् || ३-५-२७_END
BEGIN_
Then, Raghava enquired with sage about the arrival of Indra and Sage Sharabhanga narrated all that to him. [3-5-27]_END

B_3_C_7_9
BEGIN_इह उपयातः काकुत्स्थः देवराजः शततक्रतुः || ३-७-१०उपागंय च मे देवो महादेवः सुर 
ईश्वरः |सर्वान् लोकान् जितान् आह मम पुण्येन कर्मणा || ३-७-११_END
BEGIN_"The king of gods and the chief invitee in hundred sacrifices Indra approached me, and 
that great deity said me that I have conquered all the worlds by my meritorious deeds... [3-7-10, 11]_END

B_3_C_8_3
BEGIN_
सुखोषिताः स्म भगवन् त्वया पूज्येन पूजिताः |आपृच्छामः प्रयास्यामो मुनयः त्वरयन्ति नः || ३-८-५_END
BEGIN_
"We stayed here happily, oh, god, venerated by a venerable one like you, and here we come to ask your 
permission as we wish to journey on, as the sages are hastening us... [3-8-5]_END

B_3_C_6_15
BEGIN_
 पंपा नदी निवासानाम् अनुमन्दाकिनीम् अपि |
 
  चित्रकूट आलयानाम् च क्रियते कदनम् महत् || ३-६-१७_END
BEGIN_
 "At Pampa riverside, and alongside of River Mandakini, and at the surroundings of
  Mt. Chitrakuta also, this hideous warfare is being done... [3-6-17]_END

B_3_C_4_28
BEGIN_
तदेव रामेण निशंय भाषितम्
कृता मतिः तस्य बिल प्रवेशने |
बिलम् च तेन अति बलेन रक्षसा
प्रवेश्यमानेन वनम् विनादितम् || ३-४-३२_END
BEGIN_
On listening to that which is said by Viradha, Rama resolved his mind to cast him into pit, and when that mighty demon is 
being flung into the pit the whole forest blared with that demon's cries. [3-4-32]_END

B_3_C_5_20
BEGIN_
माम् एष वरदो राम ब्रह्म लोकम् निनीषति |
जितम् उग्रेण तपसा दुष्प्रापम् अकृत आत्मभिः || ३-५-२८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh! Rama, that boon-giver Indra wishes to take me to Brahma's abode, which is achieved by me by my arduous ascesis and 
that which is unattainable for them with their souls unconquered... [3-5-28]_END

B_3_C_7_10
BEGIN_तेषु देव ऋषि जुष्टेषु जितेशु तपसा मया |मत् प्रसादात् स भार्यः त्वम् विहरस्व 
स लक्ष्मणः || ३-७-१२_END
BEGIN_"Let me bequeath those worlds that are cherished by gods and sages alike, but which are 
won over by me by my ascesis, and you enjoy in them with your wife and with your brother Lakshmana... 
[3-7-12]_END

B_3_C_6_16
BEGIN_
 एवम् वयम् न मृष्यामो विप्रकारम् तपस्विनाम् |
 
  क्रियमाणम् वने घोरम् रक्षोभिः भीम कर्मभिः || ३-६-१८_END
BEGIN_
 "Thus. we are not able to tolerate this injustice to the sages, being executed in
  this forest by the demons with fiendish deeds, in a ghastly manner... [3-6-18]_END

B_3_C_8_4
BEGIN_
त्वरामहे वयम् द्रष्टुम् कृत्स्नम् आश्रम मण्डलम् |ऋषीणाम् पुण्य शीलानाम् दण्डकारण्य वासिनाम् || ३-८-६_END
BEGIN_
"We make haste to see the habitats of hermitages in their entirety, and even wish to see the sages with 
meritorious selves living in Dandaka forest... [3-8-6]_END

B_3_C_4_29
BEGIN_
प्रहृष्ट रूपौ इव राम लक्ष्मणौ
विराधम् उर्व्याम् प्रदरे निपात्य तम् |
ननन्दतुः वीत भयौ महावने
शिलाभिः अन्तर् दधतुः च राक्षसम् || ३-४-३३_END
BEGIN_
Rama and Lakshmana felt happy by way of their look in burying Viradha in the pit of the earth, and on burying him they two 
felt rejoiced for gone is the fear in that great forest, and within the pit they have also concealed him with boulders in 
order to make it a burial-chamber to the departed soul. [3-4-33]_END

B_3_C_5_21
BEGIN_
अहम् ज्ञात्वा नर व्याघ्र वर्तमानम् अदूरतः |
ब्रह्म लोकम् न गच्छामि त्वाम् अदृष्ट्वा प्रिय अतिथिम् || ३-५-२९_END
BEGIN_
"On knowing that you are course is nearby, oh! Manly-tiger, and without seeing my dear guest I do not wish to go to Brahma's 
abode... [3-5-29]_END

B_3_C_7_11
BEGIN_तम् उग्र तपसम् दीप्तम् महर्षिम् सत्य वादिनम् |प्रत्युवाच आत्मवान् रामो ब्रह्माणम् 
इव वासवः || ३-७-१३_END
BEGIN_That self-respecting Rama replied the radiant sage with intense asceticism, a great soul 
and an advocate of truth by himself, as Indra would reply to Brahma. [3-7-13]_END

B_3_C_6_17
BEGIN_
 ततः त्वाम् शरणार्थम् च शरण्यम् समुपस्थिताः |
 
  परिपालय नः राम वध्यमानान् निशाचरैः || ३-६-१९_END
BEGIN_
 "Therefore we present ourselves before you as you are our protector, for the
  purpose of your protecting us that are being killed by nightwalkers... please safe guard us...
  [3-6-19]_END

B_3_C_8_5
BEGIN_
अभ्यनुज्ञातुम् इच्छामः सह एभिः मुनिपुङ्गवैः |धर्म नित्यैः तपो दान्तैः विशिखैः इव पावकैः || ३-८-७_END
BEGIN_
"We wish to have your permission, and that of these eminent sages, who are ever virtuous, self-controlled 
by their ascesis, and who look like the veritable tongues of sacred fire... [3-8-7]_END

B_3_C_4_30
BEGIN_
ततः तु तौ कांचन चित्र कार्मुकौ
निहत्य रक्षः परिगृह्य मैथिलीम् |
विजह्रतुः तौ मुदितौ महावने
दिवि स्थितौ चन्द्र दिवाकरौ इव || ३-४-३४_END
BEGIN_
Then they two who have dazzling golden bows have eliminated that demon and retrieved Seetha, and they gladly journeyed on 
in that great forest like the two entities abiding on the skies, namely the Sun and Moon. [3-4-34]_END

B_3_C_5_22
BEGIN_
त्वया अहम् पुरुषव्याघ्र धार्मिकेण महत्मनाअ |
समागंय गमिष्यामि त्रिदिवम् च अवरम् परम् || ३-५-३०_END
BEGIN_
" Having met with you, a virtuous one and a great soul as you are, oh, manly-tiger, I wish to go through undesirable lesser 
heavens to Brahma's abode, the highest [3-5-30]_END

B_3_C_7_12
BEGIN_अहम् एव आहरिष्यामि स्वयम् लोकान् महामुने |आवासम् तु अहम् इच्छामि प्रदिष्टम् 
इह कानने || ३-७-१४_END
BEGIN_"I alone can gain all those worlds, oh, great saint, I now seek a place to dwell here 
in this forest as indicated by you... [3-7-14]_END

B_3_C_6_18
BEGIN_
 परा त्वत्तः गतिः वीर पृधिव्यम् न उपपद्यते |
 
  परिपालय नः सर्वान् राक्षसेभ्यो नृपात्मजः || ३-६-२०_END
BEGIN_
 "Other than you, oh, valorous Rama, no way-out is deducible on this earth, hence
  oh, prince, protect all of us from the demons... [3-6-20]_END

B_3_C_8_6
BEGIN_
अविषह्य आतपो यावत् सूर्यो न अति विराजते |अमार्गेण आगताम् लक्ष्मीम् प्राप्य इव अन्वय वर्जितः || ३-८-८
तावत् इच्छामहे गन्तुम् इति उक्त्वा चरणौ मुनेः |ववन्दे सह सौमित्रिः सीतया सह राघवः || ३-८-९_END
BEGIN_
"We wish to proceed before sun attains an intolerable glare, like an unworthy person of unworthy lineage 
attains wealth in an improper way with much glare..." saying so Rama with Seetha and Lakshmana venerated 
at the feet of that sage Suteekshna. [3-8-8, 9]_END

B_3_C_5_23
BEGIN_
अक्षया नर शार्दूल जितालोका मया शुभाः |
ब्राह्ंयाः च नाक पृष्ठ्याः च प्रतिगृह्णीष्व मामकान् || ३-५-३१_END
BEGIN_
"Oh! Tigerly-man, non-diminishing are the abodes achieved by me either in Brahma's abode or yonder than paradise...you take 
them all...that are mine achieved by me ascesis..." So said Sage Sharabhanga to Rama. [3-5-31]_END

B_3_C_7_13
BEGIN_भवान् सर्वत्र कुशलः सर्वभूत हिते रतः |आख्यातः शरभंगेन गौतमेन महात्मना || ३-७-१५_END
BEGIN_"You are an expert in all affairs, and you are interested in the welfare of all the beings, 
so said the great souled Sage Sharabhanga of Sage Gautama's dynasty..." [So said Rama to the sage.] 
[3-7-15]_END

B_3_C_9_0
BEGIN_
सुतीक्ष्णेन अभ्यनुज्ञातम् प्रस्थितम् रघु नन्दनम् |हृद्यया स्निग्धया वाचा भर्तारम् इदम् अब्रवीत् 
|| ३-९-१_END
BEGIN_
To Rama, the scion of Raghu and her husband, who started out when permitted by Sage Suteekshna, Vaidehi 
spoke this with friendly words. [3-9-1]_END

B_3_C_6_19
BEGIN_
 एतत् श्रुत्वा तु काकुत्स्थः तापसानाम् तपस्विनाम् |
 
  इदम् प्रोवाच धर्मात्मा सर्वान् एव तपस्विनः || ३-६-२१_END
BEGIN_
 On hearing all that is said by the sages of great penance, he that virtue souled
  Rama said this unto all of the sages. [3-6-21]_END

B_3_C_8_7
BEGIN_
तौ सम् स्पृशंतौ चरणौ उत्थाप्य मुनिपुंगवः |गाढम् आश्लिष्य सस्नेहम् इदम् वचनम् अब्रवीत् || ३-८-१०_END
BEGIN_
That eminent sage lifted them that are touching his feet, embraced them tightly, and said this sentence 
in all his friendliness. [3-8-10]_END

B_3_C_5_24
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तो नरव्याघ्रः सर्व शास्त्र विशारदः |
ऋषिणा शरभंगेन राघवो वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् || ३-५-३२_END
BEGIN_
Thus said by the Sage Sharabhanga to that Manly-tiger Rama, being the scholar in all the scriptures he spoke this sentence 
to that sage. [3-5-32]_END

B_3_C_7_14
BEGIN_एवम् उक्तः तु रामेण महर्षिः लोक विश्रुतः |अब्रवीत् मधुरम् वाक्यम् हर्षेण महता 
युतः || ३-७-१६_END
BEGIN_When said thus by Rama, that great sage with world renown spoke sweet worded sentence 
with great pleasure. [3-7-16]_END

B_3_C_9_1
BEGIN_
अधर्मम् तु सुसूक्ष्मेण विधिना प्राप्यते महान् |निवृत्तेन च शक्यो अयम् व्यसनात् कामजाद् इह || ३-९-२_END
BEGIN_
"Gross unjust will accrue to any in an abstruse way if his indulgence is enkindled merely by his own 
desire, and in this world it is possible to fend them off, to have a recourse to justness... [3-9-2]_END

B_3_C_6_20
BEGIN_
 न एवम् अर्हथ माम् वक्तुम् आज्ञाप्यः अहम् तपस्विनाम् |
 
  केवलेन स्व कार्येण प्रवेष्टव्यम् वनम् मया || ३-६-२२_END
BEGIN_
 "Unapt is this way of speaking to me...command me, for I am at your behest... just
  for my personal purpose I had to enter the forests.... [3-6-22]_END

B_3_C_8_8
BEGIN_
अरिष्टम् गच्छ पन्थानम् राम सौमित्रिणा सह |सीतया च अनया सार्धम् छाय एव अनुवृत्तया || ३-८-११_END
BEGIN_
"Proceed in an invulnerable way, Rama, along with Lakshmana, and with this Seetha while she follows 
you closely like a shadow... [3-8-11]_END

B_3_C_5_25
BEGIN_
अहम् एव आहरिष्यामि सर्वान् लोकान् महामुने |
आवासम् तु अहम् इच्छामि प्रदिष्टम् इह कानने || ३-५-३३_END
BEGIN_
"I alone can gain all those worlds, oh! Great Saint, I now seek a place to dwell here in this forest as indicated by you... 
[Apparent meaning.] [3-5-33]_END

B_3_C_7_15
BEGIN_अयम् एव आश्रमो राम गुणवान् रंयताम् इति |ऋषि संघ अनुचरितः सदा मूल फलैर् युतः 
|| ३-७-१७_END
BEGIN_"You can take delight in this good featured hermitage alone, for groups of sages will 
always be moving here, and this always contains tubers and fruits..." Thus said Sage Suteekshna. [3-7-17]_END

B_3_C_9_2
BEGIN_
त्रीणि एव व्यसनानि अत्र कामजानि भवन्ति उत |मिथ्या वाक्यम् तु परमम् तस्मात् गुरुतरा उभौ || ३-९-३
पर दार अभिगमनम् विना वैरम् च रौद्रता |_END
BEGIN_
"Only three self-gratifications, the definite products of desire, are there: one is speaking fallacious 
utterances, which itself is worse, and worst than the other two malefic self-gratifications, where the 
other two are the fascination for other's wife, and the cruelness without enmity... [3-9-3, 4a]_END

B_3_C_6_21
BEGIN_
 विप्रकारम् अपाक्रष्टुम् राक्षसैः भवताम् इमम् |
 
  पितुः तु निर्देशकरः प्रविष्टो अहम् इदम् वनम् || ३-६-२३_END
BEGIN_
 "I entered this forest as ordered by my father and even to obliterate the
  unconscionable state of yours owing to the misdeeds of demons. [3-6-23]_END

B_3_C_8_9
BEGIN_
पश्य आश्रम पदम् रंयम् दण्डकारण्य वासिनाम् |एषाम् तपस्विनाम् वीर तपसा भावित आत्मनाम् || ३-८-१२_END
BEGIN_
"See the pleasant thresholds of the hermitages of the dwellers in the forests of Dandaka, oh! Valiant 
one, whose souls are consecrated just by their ascesis... [3-8-2]_END

B_3_C_5_26
BEGIN_
राघवेण एवम् उक्तः तु शक्र तुल्य बलेन वै |
शरभंगो महाप्राज्ञः पुनर् एव अब्रवीत् वचः || ३-५-३४_END
BEGIN_
Thus said by Raghava, who is like Indra in strength, that supremely intellectual Sage Sharabhanga again spoke this sentence 
this way. [3-5-34]_END

B_3_C_7_16
BEGIN_इमम् आश्रमम् आगंय मृग संघा महीयसः |अहत्वा प्रतिगच्छन्ति लोभयित्वा अकुतोभयाः 
|| ३-७-१८_END
BEGIN_"But herds of very large animals will be coming to this hermitage, they return after 
scaring us, of course without killing anyone, and they fear none... [3-7-18]_END

B_3_C_9_3

BEGIN_
Hunting, sleeping in daytime, abusing others, indulgence in women, three artistic impulses namely music, 
dance and drama, wasteful wandering, are the ten desire. Manu smriti._END

B_3_C_6_22
BEGIN_
 भवताम् अर्थ सिद्ध्यर्थम् आगतोऽहम् यदृच्छया |
 
  तस्य मे अयम् वने वासो भविष्यति महाफलः | ३-६-२४_END
BEGIN_
 "Perchance I have come for the achievement of your purpose, such as I am, dwelling
  in this forest will immensely be fruitful to me... [3-6-24]_END

B_3_C_8_10
BEGIN_
सुप्राज्य फल मूलानि पुष्पितानि वनानि च |प्रशस्त मृग यूथानि शान्त पक्षि गणानि च || ३-८-१३फुल्ल 
पंकज खण्डानि प्रसन्न सलिलानि च |कारण्डव विकीर्णानि तटाकानि सरांसि च || ३-८-१४द्रक्ष्यसे दृष्टि 
रंयाणि गिरि प्रस्रवणानि च |रमणीयानि अरण्यानि मयूर अभिरुतानि च || ३-८-१५_END
BEGIN_
"See the well-flowered woodlands with well-grown fruits and tubers, with herds of best animals and 
peaceful bird flocks... tranquil waters with spreading clusters of bloomed lotuses and water-birds in 
the pools and lakes... eye-pleasing rapids from mountains and you can see pleasant forests loaded with 
the hearty screams of precooks... [3-8-13, 14, 15]_END

B_3_C_5_27
BEGIN_
इह राम महातेजाः सुतीक्ष्णो नम धार्मिकः |
वसति अरण्ये नियतः स ते श्रेयो विधास्यति || ३-५-३५_END
BEGIN_
"Here, oh! Rama, a great resplendent sage named Suteekshna, lives in this forest...a virtuous and a self-disciplined one, 
and he will do something benignant to you... [3-5-35]_END

B_3_C_7_17
BEGIN_ना अन्यो दोषो भवेत् अत्र मृगेभ्यः अन्यत्र विद्धि वै |तत् श्रुत्वा वचनम् तस्य 
महर्षेः लक्ष्मणाग्रजः || ३-७-१९उवाच वचनम् धीरो विगृह्य स शरम् धनुः |_END
BEGIN_"Know that no other problem is there other than the animals..." So said the sage. On 
hearing those words of that great sage, that brave elder brother of Lakshmana taking bow and arrow said 
this sentence. [3-7-19, 20a]_END

B_3_C_9_4
BEGIN_
मिथ्या वाक्यम् न ते भूतम् न भविष्यति राघव || ३-९-४कुतो अभिलषणम् स्त्रीणाम् परेषाम् धर्म नाशनम् |_END
BEGIN_
"The habit of telling specious words is not there with you in the past nor it will be there in future, 
oh, Raghava, then wherefrom the virtue-ruining desire for other's women can be there... [3-9-4b, 5a]_END

B_3_C_6_23
BEGIN_
 तपस्विनाम् रणे शत्रून् हन्तुम् इच्छामि राक्षसान् |
 
  पश्यन्तु वीर्यम् ऋषयः सः ब्रातुर् मे तपोधनाः || ३-६-२५_END
BEGIN_
 "I wish to eliminate demons, the enemies of sages, in war... let the sages behold
  my valour, and my brother's valour in doing so..." Thus Rama promised the sages. [3-6-25]_END

B_3_C_5_28
BEGIN_
सुतीक्ष्णम् अभिगच्छ त्वम् शुचौ देशे तपस्विनम् |
रमणीये वनोद्देशे स ते वासम् विधास्यति || ३-५-३६_END
BEGIN_
"You approach Sage Suteekshna and to you he will arrange housing in his auspicious and dpleasant place woods of hermits... 
[3-5-36]_END

B_3_C_8_11
BEGIN_
गंयताम् वत्स सौमित्रे भवान् अपि च गच्छतु |आगन्तव्यम् च ते दृष्ट्वा पुनः एव आश्रमम् प्रति || 
३-८-१६_END
BEGIN_
"My dear Rama, you may go and Soumitri you too also may go... but come again towards this hermitage 
after seeing all of them... [3-8-16]_END

B_3_C_7_18
BEGIN_तान् अहम् सुमहाभाग मृगसंघान् समागतान् || ३-७-२०हन्याम् निशित धारेण शरेण नत पर्वणा 
|_END
BEGIN_"I will eradicate them, oh, greatly blessed one, those animals that will come collectively 
in herds with sharp edged, curve-end arrows... [3-7-20b, 21a]_END

B_3_C_10_0
BEGIN_
वाक्यम् एतत् तु वैदेह्या व्याहृतम् भर्तृ भक्त्या |श्रुत्वा धर्मे स्थितो रामः प्रत्युवाच जानकीम् 
|| ४-१०-१_END
BEGIN_
On hearing all of the words said by Vaidehi, in adoration of her husband, he who abides by virtue alone 
that Rama replied Janaki. [4-10-1]_END

B_3_C_9_5
BEGIN_
तव नास्ति मनुष्येन्द्र न च आभूत् ते कदाचन || ३-९-५मनस्यपि तथा राम न च एतत् विद्यते क्वचित् |
स्व दार निरतः च एव नित्यम् एव नृपात्मज || ३-९-६_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, king, earlier this vile desire for other's women is absent in you, nor it is there now, unobserved 
is such a desire in any corner of your heart oh, prince, for you are always interested in your own wife... 
[3-9-5, 6]_END

B_3_C_6_24
BEGIN_
 दत्त्वा अभयम् च अपि तपो धनानाम्
 
  धर्मे धृइत आत्मा सह लक्ष्मणेन |
  तपो धनैः च अपि सह आर्य दत्तः
  सुतीक्ष्णम् एव अभिजगाम वीरः || ३-६-२६_END
BEGIN_
 Thus giving his aegis to the sages, that valiant Rama who is firmly virtue-souled,
  journeyed towards Sage Suteekshna with Lakshmana and the sages, and along with the one given by
  Honourable Janaka, namely Seetha. [3-6-26]_END

B_3_C_8_12
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तथा इति उक्त्वा काकुत्स्थः सह लक्ष्मणः |प्रदक्षिणम् मुनिम् कृत्वा प्रस्थातुम् उपचक्रमे 
|| ३-८-१७_END
BEGIN_
Thus said by the sage, Rama in his turn said to him, "so be it..." and having performed circumambulations 
around the sage he started to journey on. [3-8-17]_END

B_3_C_5_29
BEGIN_
इमाम् मन्दाकिनीम् राम प्रतिस्रोतम् अनुव्रज |
नदीम् पुष्पोडुप वहाम् ततः तत्र गमिष्यसि || ३-५-३७_END
BEGIN_
" Following opposite to its flow you may follow this River Mandaakini that carries flower-ferries, then you can reach there 
at Sage Suteekshna's hermitage...] [3-5-37]_END

B_3_C_7_19
BEGIN_भवान् तत्र अभिषज्येत किम् स्यात् कृच्छ्र तरम् ततः || ३-७-२१एतस्मिन् आश्रमे वासम् 
चिरम् तु न समर्थये |_END
BEGIN_"But you may be more interested in those animals mercifully, then what will be there 
more painful to you, hence I deem our staying in this hermitage for along will be unbefitting..." So 
said Rama. [3-7-21b, 22a]_END

B_3_C_10_1
BEGIN_
हितम् उक्तम् त्वया देवि स्निग्धया सदृशम् वचः |कुलम् व्यपदिशन्त्या च धर्मज्ञे जनक आत्मजे || ४-१०-२_END
BEGIN_
"You have said beneficial, friendlily words that are seemlier to your disposition, oh, lady, which 
are apt to speak of your familial brought up, for you are the daughter of virtue-knowing Janaka. [4-10-2]_END

B_3_C_9_6
BEGIN_
धर्मिष्टः सत्य सन्धः च पितुः निर्देश कारकः |त्वयि धर्मः च सत्यम् च त्वयि सर्वम् प्रतिष्टितम् ||३-९-७_END
BEGIN_
"You are conscientious, adherent of truth, and obliging father's orders, and in you virtue and truth, 
nay everything is established in you... [3-9-7]_END

B_3_C_8_13
BEGIN_
ततः शुभतरे तूणी धनुषी च आयतेक्षणा |ददौ सीता तयोः भ्रात्रोः खड्गौ च विमलौ ततः || ३-८-१८_END
BEGIN_
Then the broad eyed Seetha gave auspicious quivers and bows to those brothers and then spotless swords 
too. [3-8-18]_END

B_3_C_5_30
BEGIN_
एष पन्था नरव्याघ्र मुहूर्तम् पश्य तात माम् |
यावत् जहामि गात्राणि जीर्णाम् त्वचम् इव उरगः || ३-५-३८_END
BEGIN_
"This is the only way, oh, manly-tiger, and oh, sire, see me for a moment, till I forsake these body parts of mine, like 
a snake casting its withered moult... [3-5-38]_END

B_3_C_7_20
BEGIN_तम् एवम् उक्त्वा उपरमम् रामः संध्याम् उपागमत् || ३-७-२२अन्वास्य पश्चिमाम् संध्याम् 
तत्र वासम् अकल्पयत् |सुतीक्ष्णस्य आश्रमे रंये सीतया लक्ष्मनेन च || ३-७-२३_END
BEGIN_On saying thus to the sage then Rama came by the twilight, and he paused at it. On worshipping 
the westward vesperal time, Rama arranged a stay for himself along with Seetha and Lakshmana, there 
in that delightful hermitage of Sage Suteekshna. [3-7-22b, 23]_END

B_3_C_10_2
BEGIN_
किम् नु वक्ष्यामि अहम् देवि त्वया एव उक्तम् इदम् वचः |क्षत्रियैः धार्यते चापो न आर्त शब्दो भवेद् 
इति || ४-१०-३_END
BEGIN_
"What more shall I say, oh, lady, since it is said that 'a warrior handles a bow so that misery's tears 
cease to flow...' and this saying is iterated even by you... [4-10-3]_END

B_3_C_9_7
BEGIN_
तच्च सर्वम् महाबाहो शक्यम् वोढुम् जितेइन्द्रियैः |तव वश्य इन्द्रियत्वम् च जानामि शुभदर्शन || ३-९-८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, dextrous one, all this can possibly be shouldered by one with controlled senses, and oh, graceful 
one for a gaze, I am also aware of your sense control... [3-9-8]_END

B_3_C_8_14
BEGIN_
आबध्य च शुभे तूणी चापे च आदाय सस्वने |निष्क्रान्तौ आश्रमात् गन्तुम् उभौ तौ राम लक्ष्मणौ || ३-८-१९_END
BEGIN_
Both of those two Rama and Lakshmana tied their beautiful quivers well on their backs, and took the 
twangy bows and exited from that hermitage to go on their way. [3-8-19]_END

B_3_C_5_31
BEGIN_
ततो अग्निम् सु समाधाय हुत्वा च आज्येन मंत्रवित् |
शरभंगो महातेजाः प्रविवेश हुताशनम् || ३-५-३९_END
BEGIN_
Then that hymnist on invoking the sacred fire and offering oblations with clarified butter into it, that radiant sage Sharabhanga 
entered that sacred fire. [3-5-39]_END

B_3_C_7_21
BEGIN_ततः शुभम् तापस अन्नम्स्वयम् सुतीक्ष्णः पुरुषर्षभाभ्याम् |ताभ्याम् सुसत्कृत्य

BEGIN_Then the great soul Sage Suteekshna on completing his evening rituals and on observing 
the fall of night he himself courteously served food that is auspicious and worthy of sages to two of 
the best men, Rama and Lakshmana. [3-7-23]_END

B_3_C_5_32

B_3_C_9_10

B_3_C_11_4

B_3_C_10_18

B_3_C_9_23
BEGIN_
स्नेहात् च बहुमानात् च स्मारये त्वाम् न शिक्षये |न कथंचन सा कार्या गृहीत धनुषा त्वया || ३-९-२४
बुद्धिः वैरम् विना हन्तुम् राक्षसान् दण्डक आश्रितान् |अपराधम् विना हन्तुम् लोको वीर न कामये || ३-९-२५_END
BEGIN_
"In affinity and in respect I am reminding but not tutoring you, and in anyway improper is that thought 
of yours to wield your bow to kill the demons dwelling in Dandaka without any enmity, oh, brave one, 
undesirable is the killing of offenceless... [3-9-24, 25]_END

B_3_C_11_5
BEGIN_
प्रसन्न सलिले रम्ये तस्मिन् सरसि शुश्रुवे |गीत वादित्र निर्घोषो न तु कश्चन दृश्यते || ४-११-७_END
BEGIN_
Out of the tranquil and enchanting waters of that lake audible are the melodies of singing and musical 
instruments, but none is visible. [4-11-7]_END

B_3_C_10_19
BEGIN_
सदृशम् च अनुरूपम् च कुलस्य तव शोभने |सधर्म चारिणी मे त्वम् प्राणेभ्यो अपि गरीयसी || ४-१०-२१_END
BEGIN_
"Appropriate and seemly is your word of caution to your bloodline, oh, graceful Seetha, you are the 
co-pursuer in dharma with me, hence you are loftier to me than my own lives..." So said Rama to Seetha. 
[4-10-21b, c]_END

B_3_C_9_24
BEGIN_
क्षत्रियाणाम् तु वीराणाम् वनेषु नियतात्मनाम् |धनुषा कार्यम् एतावत् आर्तानाम् अभिरक्षणम् || ३-९-२६_END
BEGIN_
"For the valiant Kshatriya-s who are inclined in forests heartily, the purpose of the bow is this much 
'safeguarding the sufferers...' [3-9-26]_END

B_3_C_11_6
BEGIN_
ततः कौतूहलात् रामो लक्ष्मणः च महारथः |मुनिम् धर्मभृतम् नाम प्रष्टुम् समुपचक्रमे || ४-११-८_END
BEGIN_
Then Rama and also Lakshmana, the great charioteer, inquisitively started to ask the Sage named Dharmabhrita 
about it. [4-11-8]_END

B_3_C_10_20
BEGIN_
इति एवम् उक्त्वा वचनम् महात्मासीताम् प्रियाम् मैथिल राज पुत्रीम् |रामो धनुष्मान् सह लक्ष्मणेन
जगाम रम्याणि तपो वनानि || ४-१०-२२_END
BEGIN_
That exalted soul Rama on saying those words to Seetha, his dear wife and the daughter of Janaka, wielding 
his bow proceeded further with Lakshmana to the picturesque woodlands of hermits. [4-10-22]_END

B_3_C_9_25
BEGIN_
क्व च शस्त्रम् क्व च वनम् क्व च क्षात्रम् तपः क्व च |व्याविद्धम् इदम् अस्माभिः देश धर्मः तु पूज्यताम् 
|| ३-९-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Where that weapon? Where this forest? Where the principles of Kshatriya? And where is sageness? All 
this is inconsistent... let us esteem the laws of the land... [3-9-27]_END

B_3_C_11_7
BEGIN_
इदम् अत्यद्भुतम् श्रुत्वा सर्वेषाम् नो महामुने |कौतूहलम् महत् जातम् किम् इदम् साधु कथ्यताम् || ४-११-९_END
BEGIN_
"On hearing this greatly amazing music from lake, oh, great saint, intensive inquisitiveness is created 
in all of us, why this, please tell us clearly about it." Thus Rama asked. [4-11-9]_END

B_3_C_12_0
BEGIN_
स प्रविश्य आश्रम पदम् लक्ष्मणो राघव अनुजः |अगस्त्य शिष्यम् आसाद्य वाक्यम् एतद् उवाच ह || ३-१२-१_END
BEGIN_
On entering the hermitage Lakshmana, the younger brother of Raghava, reached Agastya's disciple and 
spoke this sentence to him. [3-12-1]_END

B_3_C_9_26
BEGIN_
तदार्य कलुषा बुद्धिः जायते शस्त्र सेवनात् |पुनर् गत्वात् तत् अयोध्यायाम् क्षत्र धर्मम् चरिष्यसि 
|| ३-९-२८_END
BEGIN_
"Weapon admiring mind becomes maligned with avariciousness, you may therefore follow the tenet of Kshatriya-s 
on going to Ayodhya again... [3-9-28]_END

B_3_C_11_8
BEGIN_
तेन एवम् उक्तो धर्मात्मा राघवेण मुनिः तदा |प्रभावम् सरसः क्षिप्रम् आख्यातुम् उपचक्रमे || ४-११-१०_END
BEGIN_
Thus said by that Raghava then that virtuous sage quickly started to tell about the efficacy of that 
lake. [4-11-10]_END

B_3_C_12_1
BEGIN_
राजा दशरथो नाम ज्येष्ठः तस्य सुतो बली |रामः प्राप्तो मुनिम् द्रष्टुम् भार्यया सह सीतया || ३-१२-२_END
BEGIN_
"A king named Dasharatha was there, his eldest son and the dynamic one, Rama has arrived along with 
his wife Seetha to see the sage. [3-12-2]_END

B_3_C_9_27
BEGIN_
अक्षया तु भवेत् प्रीतिः श्वश्रू श्वशुरयोः मम |यदि राज्यम् हि संन्यस्य भवेत् त्वम् निरतो मुनिः || 
३-९-२९_END
BEGIN_
"Everlasting satisfaction will be there to my father-in-law and mothers-in-laws, on your becoming a 
devout sage even after forfeiture of kingdom... [3-9-29]_END

B_3_C_11_9
BEGIN_
इदम् पंच अप्सरो नाम तटाकम् सार्व कालिकम् |निर्मितम् तपसा राम मुनिना माण्डकर्णिना || ४-११-११_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama, this is an all-time lake built by the ascetic power of the sage Mandakarni, known as Five 
Apsara Lake. [4-11-11]_END

B_3_C_12_2
BEGIN_
लक्ष्मणो नाम तस्य अहम् भ्राता तु अवरजो हितः |अनुकूलः च भक्तः च यदि ते श्रोत्रम् आगतः || ३-१२-३_END
BEGIN_
"I am his loyal, dedicated, and adherent younger brother named Lakshmana, if ever you have heard of 
us. [3-12-3]_END

B_3_C_9_28
BEGIN_
धर्मात् अर्थः प्रभवति धर्मात् प्रभवते सुखम् |धर्मेण लभते सर्वम् धर्म सारम् इदम् जगत् || ३-९-३०_END
BEGIN_
"From virtuousness prosperity emanates, from righteousness happiness, and by honourableness all are 
achieved, and this universe is the essence of probity... [3-9-30]_END

B_3_C_11_10
BEGIN_
स हि तेपे तपः तीव्रम् माण्डकर्णिः महामुनिः |दश वर्ष सहस्राणि वायु भक्षो जलाशये || ४-११-१२_END
BEGIN_
"He that great saint Mandakarni practiced rigorous ascesis for ten thousand years staying in the waters 
of the lake, and consuming air alone. [4-11-12]_END

B_3_C_12_3
BEGIN_
ते वयम् वनम् अत्युग्रम् प्रविष्टाः पितृ शासनात् |द्रष्टुम् इच्छ्हामहे सर्वे भगवन्तम् निवेद्यताम् 
|| ३-१२-४_END
BEGIN_
"Such as we are, we entered the awful forest at the decree of our father, and we wiush to see the godly 
sage, let this be informed to him." Said Lakshmana to the disciple of Agastya. [3-12-4]_END

B_3_C_9_29
BEGIN_
आत्मानम् नियमैः तैः तैः कर्षयित्वा प्रयत्नतः |प्राप्यते निपुणैः धर्मो न सुखात् लभते सुखम् || ३-९-३१_END
BEGIN_
"Experts will make efforts to exhaust their own selves with those and those principles, thus they realise 
sublimity... unachievable is pleasure by pleasuring alone... [3-9-31]_END

B_3_C_11_11
BEGIN_
ततः प्रव्यथिताः सर्वे देवाः स अग्नि पुरोगमाः |अब्रुवन् वचनम् सर्वे परस्पर समागताः || ४-११-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Then all the gods are worried and met together with Fire-god at the helm of affairs, and they all conversed 
among themselves. [4-11-13]_END

B_3_C_12_4
BEGIN_
तस्य तद् वचनम् श्रुत्वा लक्ष्मणस्य तपोधनः |तथा इति उक्त्वा अग्नि शरणम् प्रविवेश निवेदितुम् || ३-१२-५_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that sentence of Lakshmana that disciple who is ascetically rich replied 'agreed, ' and he 
entered the sanctum of Ritual-fire to submit the same to Agastya. [3-12-5]_END

B_3_C_9_30
BEGIN_
नित्यम् शुचि मतिः सौम्य चर धर्मम् तपो वने |सर्वम् हि विदितम् तुभ्यम् त्रैलोक्यम् अपि तत्त्वतः || 
३-९-३२_END
BEGIN_
"Always tread along the righteousness with a pure mind, oh, gentle one, and specially in these sagely 
forests... you know everything in all the three worlds, in all its nuances... [3-9-32]_END

B_3_C_11_12
BEGIN_
अस्मकम् कस्यचित् स्थानम् एष प्रार्थयते मुनिः |इति संविग्न मनसः सर्वे तत्र दिवौकसः || ४-११-१४_END
BEGIN_
"This sage is praying for someone's place among us," thus all of those heaven-dwellers are perturbed 
at heart. [4-11-14]_END

B_3_C_12_5
BEGIN_
स प्रविश्य मुनिश्रेष्ठम् तपसा दुष्प्रधर्षणम् |कृत अंजलिः उवाच इदम् राम आगमनम् अञ्जसा || ३-१२-६
यथा उक्तम् लक्ष्मणेन एव शिष्यः तस्य अगस्तस्य संमतः |_END
BEGIN_
He that agreeable disciple of sage quickly approached the irrefutable sage by his asceticism, made palm-fold 
and said this to the eminent sage about about the arrival of Rama, exactly as said by Lakshmana. [3-12-6, 
7a]_END

B_3_C_9_31
BEGIN_
स्त्री चापलात् एतत् उदाहृतम् मेधर्मम् च वक्तुम् तव कः समर्थः |विचार्य बुद्ध्या तु सह अनुजेन
यत् रोचते तत् कुरु म अचिरेण || ३-९-३३_END
BEGIN_
"I cite all this with my womanly waver, and who is capable to talk to you about dharma? Ponder mindfully 
along with your brother, and what that is appropriate, you do it...but not belatedly... [3-9-33]_END

B_3_C_11_13
BEGIN_
ततः कर्तुम् तपो विघ्नम् सर्व देवैः नियोजिताः |प्रधान अप्सरसः पंच विद्युत् चलित वर्चसः || ४-११-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Then all gods assigned five important Apsara-s, the celestial courtesans, whose shine is like the sprint 
of the lightning, to effectuate hindrance in that sage's ascesis. [4-11-15]_END

B_3_C_12_6
BEGIN_
पुत्रौ दशरथस्य इमौ रामो लक्ष्मण एव च || ३-१२-७प्रविष्टौ आश्रमपदम् सीतया सह भार्यया |_END
BEGIN_
"Sons of King Dasharatha, Rama and also thus Lakshmana have entered the threshold of hermitage along 
with the wife of Rama, namely Seetha. [3-12-7b, 8a]_END

B_3_C_11_14
BEGIN_
अप्सरोभिः ततः ताभिः मुनिः दृष्ट परावरः |नीतो मदन वश्यत्वम् देवानाम् कार्य सिद्धये || ४-११-१६_END
BEGIN_
Then those five celestial beauties have led that sage astray who discerned the nature of this and the 
other world, or good and bad, or the nature of Absolute-Soul and Body- bound Soul, towards the passional 
restraint by, as though to achieve god's task._END

B_3_C_12_7
BEGIN_
द्रष्टुम् भवन्तम् आयातौ शुश्रूषार्थम् अरिन्दमौ || ३-१२-८यद् अत्र अनंतरम् तत् त्वम् आज्ञापयितुम् 
अर्हसि |_END
BEGIN_
"Those two enemy-destroyers have come cherishing to see and serve you, hence it will be apt of you to 
order what next is to be done in this regard." Said disciple to the sage. [3-12-8b, 9a]_END

B_3_C_11_15
BEGIN_
ताः चैव अप्सरसः पंच मुनेः पत्नीत्वम् आगताः |तटाके निर्मितम् तासाम् तस्मिन् अन्तर्हितम् गृहम् || 
४-११-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Also thus, those five celestial apsara-s attained wifehood of that sage, and for them he built a house 
in there, concealed inside that lake. [4-11-17]_END

B_3_C_12_8
BEGIN_
ततः शिष्यात् उपश्रुत्य प्राप्तम् रामम् स लक्ष्मणम् || ३-१२-९वैदेहीम् च महाभागाम् इदम् वचनम् अब्रवीत् 
|_END
BEGIN_
Having heard from the disciple that Rama has arrived with Lakshmana and with highly fortunate Seetha 
the sage said this to him. [3-12-9b, 10a]_END

B_3_C_11_16
BEGIN_
तत्र एव अप्सरसः पंच निवसन्त्यो यथा सुखम् |रमयन्ति तपोयोगात् मुनिम् यौवनम् आस्थितम् || ४-११-१८_END
BEGIN_
"While those five celestial apsara-s are living in there, they are gratifying that sage according to 
his delight as youthfulness came upon that sage owing to his power of asceticism. [4-11-18]_END

B_3_C_12_9
BEGIN_
दिष्ट्या रामः चिरस्य अद्य द्रष्टुम् माम् समुपागतः || ३-१२-१०मनसा कांक्षितम् हि अस्य मया अपि आगमनम् 
प्रति |_END
BEGIN_
"My heart is indeed yearning for his arrival, and after this long a time Rama providentially came to 
see me." [3-12-10b, 11a]_END

B_3_C_11_17
BEGIN_
तासाम् संक्रीड मानानाम् एष वादित्र निःस्वनः |श्रूयते भूषण उन्मिश्रः गीत शब्दः मनोहरः || ४-११-१९_END
BEGIN_
"These musical sounds we hear are emerging out as played on their instruments, mingled with the tinkling 
of their ornaments, and mixed with their delightful singing of melodies." So said sage Dharmabhrita 
to Rama. [4-11-19]_END

B_3_C_12_10
BEGIN_
गम्यताम् सत्कृतो रामः स भार्यः सह लक्ष्मणः || ३-१२-११प्रवेश्यताम् समीपम् मे किम् असौ न प्रवेशितः 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Go forth and make welcome to Rama, Lakshmana and to Seetha, and they be entered here, why you have 
not invited them as yet? [3-12-11b, 12a]_END

B_3_C_11_18
BEGIN_
आश्चर्यम् इति तस्य एतद् वचनम् भावितात्मनः |राघवः प्रतिजग्राह सह भ्रात्रा महा यशाः || ४-११-२०_END
BEGIN_
That highly renowned Raghava together with his brother acknowledged the sage Dharmabhrita's account, 
exclaiming it as "amazing is this..." [4-11-20]_END

B_3_C_12_11
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु मुनिना धर्मज्ञेन महात्मना || ३-१२-१२अभिवाद्य अब्रवीत् शिष्यः तथा इति नियत अंजलिः |_END
BEGIN_
Thus said by the great-souled sage and the knower of virtue, the disciple adored him with palm-fold 
saying that "as you say." [3-12-12b, 13a]_END

B_3_C_11_19
BEGIN_
एवम् कथयमानः स ददर्श आश्रम मण्डलम् |कुश चीर परिक्षिप्तम् ब्राह्म्या लक्ष्म्या समावृतम् || ४-११-२१
प्रविश्य सह वैदेह्या लक्ष्मणेन च राघवः |_END
BEGIN_
While saying thus Raghava has seen a cluster of hermitages nearby, encircled with sacred grass, jute 
cloths, and even encompassed with Vedic solemness, and he entered that hermitage along with Seetha and 
Lakshmana. [4-11-21, 22a]_END

B_3_C_12_12
BEGIN_
