तदा निष्क्रम्य संभ्रान्तः शिष्यो लक्ष्मणम् अब्रवीत् || ३-१२-१३क्व असौ रामो मुनिम् द्रष्टुम् एतु 
प्रविशतु स्वयम् |_END
BEGIN_
Then that disciple went out with a little perplexity and said this to Lakshmana, "Where is this Rama? 
He may come to see the sage and let him enter hermitage on his own." Said that disciple to Lakshmana. 
[3-12-13b, 14a]_END

B_3_C_11_20
BEGIN_
तदा तस्मिन् स काकुत्स्थः श्रीमति आश्रम मण्डले || ४-११-२२उषित्वा स सुखम् तत्र पूर्ज्यमानो महर्षिभिः 
|जगाम च आश्रमान् तेषाम् पर्यायेण तपस्विनाम् |४-११-२३येषाम् उषितवान् पूर्वम् सकाशे स महास्त्रवित् 
|_END
BEGIN_
Rama happily stayed in that august cluster of hermitages duly venerated by those great saints for sometime, 
and then that expert in great missiles Rama went to the hermitages of those sages with whom he stayed 
earlier, for another round. [4-11-22, 23, 24a]_END

B_3_C_12_13
BEGIN_
ततो गत्वा आश्रम पदम् शिष्येण सह लक्ष्मणः || ३-१२-१४दर्शयामास काकुत्स्थम् सीताम् च जनकात्मजाम् |_END
BEGIN_
Then on going out to the exterior of that hermitage along with that disciple, Lakshmana has shown him 
Rama and Janaka's daughter Seetha. [3-12-14b, 15a]_END

B_3_C_11_21
BEGIN_
क्वचित् परिदशान् मासान् एक संवत्सरम् क्वचित् || ४-११-२४क्वचित् च चतुरो मासान् पंच षट् च परान् क्वचित् 
|अपरत्र अधिकान् मासान् अध्यर्धम् अधिकम् क्वचित् || ४-११-२५त्रीन् मासान् अष्ट मासान् च राघवो 
न्यवसत् सुखम् |_END
BEGIN_
Rama stayed there for nearly ten months at some place, elsewhere for one year, at somewhere else for 
four months, and for five, and six months at elsewhere, even at somewhere else for more than a month, 
and for more than one and half months elsewhere. [4-11-24, 25, 26a]_END

B_3_C_12_14
BEGIN_
तम् शिष्यः प्रश्रितम् वाक्यम् अगस्त्य वचनम् ब्रुवन् || ३-१२-१५प्रावेशयत् यथा न्यायम् सत्कार अर्ह 
सुसत्कृतम् |_END
BEGIN_
While that disciple repeated the obliging words of Agastya entered that reception-worthy Rama into hermitage 
on receiving him well. [3-12-15b, 16a]_END

B_3_C_11_22
BEGIN_
तत्र संवसतः तस्य मुनीनाम् आश्रमेषु वै || ४-११-२६रमतः च आनुकूल्येन ययुः संवत्सरा दश |_END
BEGIN_
While Raghava stayed comfortably taking delight in those hermitages of sages, indeed ten years have 
smoothly elapsed. [4-11-26b, 27a]_END

B_3_C_12_15
BEGIN_
प्रविवेश ततो रामः सीतया सह लक्ष्मणः || ३-१२-१६प्रशान्त हरिण आकीर्णम् आश्रमम् हि अवलोकयन् |_END
BEGIN_
And then Rama entered the hermitage with Seetha and Lakshmana looking over it which is overspread with 
docile deer. [ 3-12-16b, 17a]_END

B_3_C_11_23
BEGIN_
परिसृत्य च धर्मज्ञः राघवः सह सीतया || ४-११-२७सुतीक्ष्णस्य आश्रमम् श्रीमान् पुनर् एव आजगाम ह |_END
BEGIN_
Thus that virtue-knowing glorious Rama on going around those hermitages along with Seetha indeed went 
to the hermitage of Sage Suteekshna again. [4-11-27b, 28a]_END

B_3_C_12_16
BEGIN_
स तत्र ब्रह्मणः स्थानम् अग्नेः स्थानम् तथैव च || ३-१२-१७विष्णोः स्थानम् महेन्द्रस्य स्थानम् 
चैव विवस्वतः |सोम स्थानम् भग स्थानम् स्थानम् कौबेरम् एव च || ३-१२-१८धातुर् विधातुः स्थानम् च 
वायोः स्थानम् तथैव च |स्थानम् च पाश हस्तस्य वारुणस्य महात्मनः || ३-१२-१९स्थानम् तथैव गायत्र्या 
वसूनाम् स्थानम् एव च |स्थानम् च नागराजस्य गरुड स्थानम् एव च || ३-१२-२०कार्तिकेयस्य च स्थानम् 
धर्म स्थानम् च पश्यति |_END
BEGIN_
Rama entered inside the hermitage and saw therein the sanctus of Brahma, Fire-god, Vishnu, Indra, Vivasvat 
- the Sun-god, Soma - the Moon-god, Bhaga - one among the twelve Suns, and the sanctusms of Kubera, 
[Wealth-Management-god, are seen and passed by the three of them, sanctums of Dhaata, Vidhaata - Vedic 
deities created by Brahma to help Svayambhuu Manu, santucm of Vaayu - the Air-god, and also like that 
the sanctum of great-soloed VaruNa - the Rain-god who also wields noose, and the sanctum of Gayatri 
- the presiding deity of gnosis, sanctum of Vasus - eight of them, and the sanctum of cobra's king - 
aadi sheSa, the divine Thousand-headed serpent that bears this globe on its head, and on which Vishnu 
reclines, and even the sanctum of GaruDa - the Divine Eagle and the vehicle of Vishnu, and the half 
brother of aadi sheSa, and the sanctum of Kaartikeya - chief of gods army, second son of Shiva, and 
the sanctum of Dharma - Dharmaraaja, presiding deity of Virtue-Vice-Time of living beings, in-charge 
of the hell. [17b, 18, 19, 20, 21a]_END

B_3_C_11_24
BEGIN_
स तम् आश्रमम् आगम्य मुनिभिः परिपूजितः || ४-११-२८तत्र अपि न्यवसत् रामः कंचित् कालम् अरिन्दमः |_END
BEGIN_
On coming at that hermitage that enemy destroyer is adored by sages, and he resided there for some time. 
[4-11-28b, 29a]_END

B_3_C_12_17
BEGIN_
ततः शिष्यैः परिवृतो मुनिर् अपि अभिनिष्पतत् || ३-१२-२१तम् ददर्श अग्रतो रामो मुनीनाम् दीप्त तेजसम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
Then encircled by disciples the sage Agastya came out quickly, and Rama saw him who is glowing brilliant 
before all the other sages. [3-12-21b, 22a]_END

B_3_C_11_25
BEGIN_
अथ आश्रमस्थो विनयात् कदाचित् तम् महामुनिम् || ४-११-२९उपासीनः स काकुत्स्थः सुतीक्ष्णम् इदम् अब्रवीत् 
|_END
BEGIN_
Then on one day while staying in that hermitage Rama submissively said this to that sage Suteekshna 
who is sitting nearby. [4-11-29b, 30a]_END

B_3_C_12_18
BEGIN_
अब्रवीत् वचनम् वीरो लक्ष्मणम् लक्ष्मिवर्धनम् || ३-१२-२२बहिर् लक्ष्मण निष्क्रामति अगस्त्यो भगवान् 
ऋषिः |औदार्येण अवगच्छ्हामि निधानम् तपसाम् इमम् || ३-१२-२३_END
BEGIN_
On seeing the brilliantly glowing sage among those sages, he that bold Rama said this sentence to Lakshmana, 
the fortifier of fortune, "Here comes the godly sage, Lakshmana, by his eminence I comprehend him as 
a depository of all ascesis." [3-12-22b, 23]_END

B_3_C_11_26
BEGIN_
अस्मिन् अरण्ये भगवन् अगस्त्यो मुनिसत्तमः || ४-११-३०वसति इति मया नित्यम् कथाः कथयताम् श्रुतम् |_END
BEGIN_
"I have always heard through the narratives narrated by other sages that the godly and eminent sage 
Agastya is residing in this forest. [4-11-30b, 31a]_END

B_3_C_12_19
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्त्वा महाबाहुः अगस्त्यम् सूर्य वर्चसम् |जग्राह आपतत् तस्य पादौ च रघुनन्दन || ३-१२-२४_END
BEGIN_
That dexterous Rama on saying about that sun-like radiant sage Agastya, he that descendent of Raghu 
fell on the feet of Agastya touching them reverentially. [3-12-24]_END

B_3_C_11_27
BEGIN_
न तु जानामि तम् देशम् वनस्य अस्य महत्तया || ४-११-३१कुत्र आश्रम पदम् पुण्यम् महर्षेः तस्य धीमतः |_END
BEGIN_
"But due to the vastness of this forest I have not known that place, where is the pious hermitage of 
that astute sage? [4-11-31b, 32a]_END

B_3_C_12_20
BEGIN_
अभिवाद्य तु धर्मात्मा तस्थौ रामः कृतांजलिः |सीतया सह वैदेह्या तदा रामः स लक्ष्मणः || ३-१२-२५_END
BEGIN_
Then he who is a delight to the on lookers that noble-hearted Rama on revering the sage along with Lakshmana 
and Seetha, the princess from Videha, stood aside with his palms adjoined. [3-12-25]_END

B_3_C_11_28
BEGIN_
प्रसाद अर्थम् भगवतः सानुजः सह सीतया || ४-११-३२अगस्त्यम् अभिगच्छ्हेयम् अभिवादयितुम् मुनिम् |_END
BEGIN_
"I wish to approach that sage seeking that godly sage's graciousness, along with my brother and Seetha 
to venerate him. [4-11-32b, 33a]_END

B_3_C_12_21
BEGIN_
प्रतिगृह्य च काकुत्स्थम् अर्चयित्वा आसन उदकैः |कुशल प्रश्नम् उक्त्वा च आस्यताम् इति सोऽब्रवीत् || 
३-१२-२६_END
BEGIN_
Offering seat and water that sage received Rama, and even on exchanging pleasantries that sage said 
to him, "please be seated." [3-12-26]_END

B_3_C_11_29
BEGIN_
मनोरथो महान् एष हृदि परिवर्तते || ४-११-३३यदि अहम् तम् मुनिवरम् शुश्रूषेयम् अपि स्वयम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Can I personally propitiate that supreme sage -- is my high ambition, and it is recurrent in my heart." 
So said Rama to Suteekshna. [4-11-33b, 34a]_END

B_3_C_12_22
BEGIN_
अग्निम् हुत्वा प्रदाय अर्घ्यम् अतिथिन् प्रतिपूज्य च |वानप्रस्थेन धर्मेण स तेषाम् भोजनम् ददौ || ३-१२-२७_END
BEGIN_
Having completed his personal worship to Fire-god, and having offered water and other formalities to 
guest, that sage gave viands to guests according to his hermitic observances. [3-12-27]_END

B_3_C_11_30
BEGIN_
इति रामस्य स मुनिः श्रुत्वा धर्मात्मनो वचः || ४-११-३४सुतीक्ष्णः प्रत्युवाच इदम् प्रीतो दशरथात्मजम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
Sage Suteekshna on hearing that particular request of that virtue-minded Rama is gladdened and said 
this to him. [4-11-34b, 35a]_END

B_3_C_12_23
BEGIN_
प्रथमम् च उपविश्य अथ धर्मज्ञो मुनिपुंगवः |उवाच रामम् आसीनम् प्रांजलिम् धर्मकोविदम् || ३-१२-२८_END
BEGIN_
Then that eminent and shrewd sage Agastya in righteousness took his seat at the outset, and spoke to 
prudent Rama of righteousness itself, and who by now is sitting with his palms adjoined. [3-12-28]_END

B_3_C_11_31
BEGIN_
अहम् अपि एतद् एव त्वाम् वक्तु कामः स लक्ष्मणम् || ४-१-३५अगस्त्यम् अभिगच्छ्ह इति सीतया सह राघव |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Raghava, even I wished to say this to you, that you may approach Agastya along with Lakshmana and 
Seetha. [4-1-35b, 36a]_END

B_3_C_12_24
BEGIN_
अग्निम् हुत्वा प्रदाय अर्घ्यम् अतिथिम् प्रतिपूजयेत् |अन्यथा खलु काकुत्स्थ तपस्वी समुदाचरन् |
दुःसाक्षी इव परे लोके स्वानि मांसानि भक्षयेत् || ३-१२-२९_END
BEGIN_
"Worshipping the fire, giving water and worshipping the guest a hermit should receive a guest and feed 
him, and if a hermit practices contrarily, oh, Rama, he is destined to eat his own flesh like a false 
deponent in other world say, hell. [3-12-29]_END

B_3_C_11_32
BEGIN_
दिष्ट्या तु इदानीम् अर्थे अस्मिन् स्वयम् एव ब्रवीषि माम् || ४-११-३६अयम् आख्यामि ते राम यत्र अगस्त्यो 
महामुनिः |_END
BEGIN_
"But providentially you alone raised this topic with me, Rama, I will tell you where that great sage 
Agastya is. [4-11-36b, 37a]_END

B_3_C_12_25
BEGIN_
राजा सर्वस्य लोकस्य धर्मचारी महारथः |पूजनीयः च मान्यः च भवान् प्राप्तः प्रिय अतिथिः || ३-१२-३०_END
BEGIN_
"You are the king of all the world, the treader in the path of righteousness, great charioteer of probity, 
and you are the venerable and estimable one, and you have arrived as my dear guest. [3-12-30]_END

B_3_C_11_33
BEGIN_
योजनानि आश्रमात् तात याहि चत्वारि वै ततः |दक्षिणेन महान् श्रीमान् अगस्त्य भ्रातुर् आश्रमः || ४-११-३७_END
BEGIN_
"On your going four yojana-s from this hermitage, oh, dear Rama, there is the great and glorious hermitage 
of Agastya's brother on the southern side. [4-11-37b, c]_END

B_3_C_12_26
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्त्वा फलैः मूलैः पुष्पैः च अन्यैः च राघवम् |पूजयित्वा यथा कामम् ततो अगस्त्यः तम् अब्रवीत् 
|| ३-१२-३१_END
BEGIN_
Saying thus, Agastya adored Raghava well with fruits, tubers, flowers and others according to his ardency, 
and then he said this to Rama. [3-12-31]_END

B_3_C_13_0
BEGIN_
राम प्रीतो अस्मि भद्रम् ते परितुष्टो अस्मि लक्ष्मण |
अभिवादयितुम् यन् माम् प्राप्तौ स्थः सह सीतया || ३-१३-१_END
BEGIN_
" I am delighted Rama, safe you be, oh Lakshmana, well-contended I am for you have
come to pay respects to me along with Seetha. [3-13-1]_END

B_3_C_11_34
BEGIN_
स्थली प्राय वनोद्देशे पिप्पली वन शोभिते |बहु पुष्प फले रम्ये नाना विहग नादिते || ४-११-३८_END
BEGIN_
"That hermitage is there on a plateau in a spectacular place of that forest which is adorned with many 
flowers and fruits, thickets of long pepper, and reechoed with the callings of various birds. [4-11-38]_END

B_3_C_12_27
BEGIN_
इदम् दिव्यम् महत् चापम् हेम वज्र विभूषितम् |वैष्णवम् पुरुषव्याघ्र निर्मितम् विश्वकर्मणा || ३-१२-३२
अमोघः सूर्य संकाशो ब्रह्मदत्तः शर उत्तमः |_END
BEGIN_
"This sacred bow that is decorated with gold and diamonds is crafted by the divine architect Vishvakarma 
pertains to Vishnu, and these unwasteful arrows equalling sun in their blaze are the gift of Brahma. 
[3-12-32, 33a]_END

B_3_C_13_1
BEGIN_
अध्व श्रमेण वाम् खेदो बाधते प्रचुर श्रमः |
व्यक्तम् उत्कण्ठते वा अपि मैथिली जनक आत्मजा || ३-१३-२_END
BEGIN_
"The well-worn trail of yours on pathway is strenuousness and painful for you two,
and it is evident from the sweat above your necks, even much more for Janaka's daughter, Maithili.
[3-13-2]_END

B_3_C_11_35
BEGIN_
पद्मिन्यो विविधाः तत्र प्रसन्न सलिल आशयाः |हंस कारण्डव आकीर्णाः चक्रवाक उपशोभिताः || ४-११-३९
तत्र एकाम् रजनीम् व्युष्य प्रभाते राम गम्यताम् |_END
BEGIN_
"There are diverse lakes that are receptacles for tranquil waters, that are teeming with swans and partridges, 
beautified with ruddy geese, and Rama staying there for a night you may proceed in the next morning. 
[4-11-39, 40a]_END

B_3_C_12_28
BEGIN_
दत्तो मम महेन्द्रेण तूणी च अक्षय सायकौ || ३-१२-३३संपूर्णौ निशितैः बाणैः ज्वलद्भिः इव पावकैः |
महा रजत कोशो अयम् असिः हेमविभूषितः || ३-१२-३४_END
BEGIN_
"Also these two inexhaustible quivers packed with arrows that have the blaze of Ritual-fire, and this 
sword decorated in gold together with its sheath made up of excellent golden are once given to me by 
Indra. [3-12-33b, 34]_END

B_3_C_11_36
BEGIN_
दक्षिणाम् दिशम् आस्थाय वन षण्डस्य पार्श्वतः || ४-११-४०तत्र अगस्त्य आश्रम पदम् गत्वा योजनम् अन्तरम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
"On going one yojana beyond, taking the southward course on the side of the forest clump you will find 
Agastya's hermitage. [4-11-40b, 41a]_END

B_3_C_13_2
BEGIN_
एषा च सुकुमारी च खेदैः च न विमानिता |
प्राअज्य दोषम् वनम् प्रप्ता भर्तृ स्नेह प्रचोदिता || ३-१३-३_END
BEGIN_
"She is delicate and not discomforted by such distresses earlier, yet motivated by
her friendship she came to these highly detrimental forests. [3-13-3]_END

B_3_C_12_29
BEGIN_
अनेन धनुषा राम हत्वा संख्ये महासुरान् |आजहार श्रियम् दीप्ताम् पुरा विष्णुर् दिव ओकसाम् || ३-१२-३५_END
BEGIN_
"By this bow, oh, Rama, once Vishnu eliminated horrible demons in war and brought back radiant prosperity 
to the celestials. [3-12-35]_END

B_3_C_11_37
BEGIN_
रमणीये वनोद्देशे बहु पादप शोभिते || ४-११-४१रंस्यते तत्र वैदेही लक्ष्मणः च त्वया सह |स हि रम्यो 
वनौद्देशो बहु पादप संयुतः || ४-११-४२_END
BEGIN_
"Seetha and Lakshmana will enjoy those woodlands adorned with diverse pleasant trees, as the woodlands 
abounding with diverse trees will naturally be delightful, isn't it. [4-11-41b, 42]_END

B_3_C_13_3
BEGIN_
यथा एषा रमते राम इह सीता तथा कुरु |
दुष्करम् कृतवती एषा वने त्वाम् अभिगच्छ्हती || ३-१३-४_END
BEGIN_
"In which way Seetha takes delight in these forests, Rama, that you may ensure
to her, for she has done an impossible deed in following you to forests, an impossible deed for
womenfolk, in general. [3-13-4]_END

B_3_C_12_30
BEGIN_
तत् धनुः तौ च तूणि च शरम् खड्गम् च मानद |जयाय प्रतिगृह्णीष्व वज्रम् वज्रधरो यथा || ३-१२-३६_END
BEGIN_
"The bow, these two quivers, arrows, and the sword, oh, Rama, the endower of grace, receive and wield 
them to triumph over the demons as Indra would wield Thunderbolt. [3-12-36]_END

B_3_C_11_38
BEGIN_
यदि बुद्धिः कृता द्रष्टुम् अगस्त्यम् तम् महामुनिम् |अद्य एव गमने बुद्धिम् रोचयस्व महामते || ४-११-४३_END
BEGIN_
"If your mind is made up to see that great sage Agastya, oh, great ingenious Rama, resolve your thinking 
in going only today." So said Sage Suteekshna to Rama. [4-11-43]_END

B_3_C_13_4
BEGIN_
एषा हि प्रकृतिः स्त्रीणाम् आसृष्टे रघुनंदन |
समस्थम् अनुरंजंते विषमस्थम् त्यजन्ति च || ३-१३-५_END
BEGIN_
"From the beginning of creation the nature of women is this way only, oh scion of
Raghu, they devote themselves to their men in good fortune, but they leave them off in ill fortune.
[3-13-5]_END

B_3_C_12_31
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्त्वा महा तेजाः समस्तम् तत् वर आयुधम् |दत्त्वा रामाय भगवान् अगस्त्यः पुनर् अब्रवीत् || ३-१२-३७_END
BEGIN_
On saying thus that great resplendent and godly sage Agastya, gave all of those best weapons to Rama, 
and again spoke to Rama [3-12-37]_END

B_3_C_13_5
BEGIN_
शत ह्रदानाम् लोलत्वम् शस्त्राणाम् तीक्ष्णताम् तथा |
गरुड अनिलयोः शैघ्र्यम् अनुगच्छ्हन्ति योषितः || ३-१३-६_END
BEGIN_
"With the mercuriality of hundreds of streaks of thunderbolt and with the
incisiveness of a weapon, and with the speediness of an eagle or the gusty wind, the women are
conformable. [3-13-6]_END

B_3_C_11_39
BEGIN_
इति रामो मुनेः श्रुत्वा सह भ्रात्रा अभिवाद्य च |प्रतस्थे अगस्त्यम् उद्दिश्य सानुगः सह सीतया || ४-११-४४_END
BEGIN_
On listening that which is said by the sage, Rama revered that sage along with his brother, and then 
he journeyed with Seetha and his follower Lakshmana aiming to reach Agastya. [4-11-44]_END

B_3_C_13_6
BEGIN_
इयम् तु भवतो भार्या दोषैर् एतैर् विवर्जिताः |
श्लाघ्या च व्यपदेश्या च यथा देवी हि अरुन्धती || ३-१३-७_END
BEGIN_
"But she this wife of yours is devoid of all those stigmas, an exemplary and an
estimable lady, like Lady Arundhati. [3-13-7]_END

B_3_C_14_0
BEGIN_
अथ पंचवटीम् गच्चन्न् अन्तरा रघुनन्दनः |आससाद महाकायम् गृध्रम् भीम पराक्रमम् || ३-१४-१_END
BEGIN_
Then while proceeding to Panchavati that Rahu's descendent came across a mammoth eagle with marvellous 
might in midway. [3-14-1]_END

B_3_C_11_40
BEGIN_
पश्यन् वनानि चित्राणि पर्वतां च अभ्र संनिभान् |सरांसि सरितः चैव पथि मार्ग वश अनुगतान् || ४-११-४५
सुतीक्ष्णेन उपदिष्टेन गत्वा तेन पथा सुखम् |इदम् परम संहृष्टो वाक्यम् लक्ष्मणम् अब्रवीत् || ४-११-४६_END
BEGIN_
While viewing beautiful forests, cloud-like mountains, lakes, and rivers that are flowing following 
the pathways, Rama happily journeyed on the pathway indicated by sage Suteekshna, then he gladly spoke 
this sentence to Lakshmana. [4-11-45, 46]_END

B_3_C_13_7
BEGIN_
अलंकृतो अयम् देशः च यत्र सौमित्रिणा सह |
वैदेह्या च अनया राम वत्स्यसि त्वम् अरिंदम || ३-१३-८_END
BEGIN_
"Where you wish to put up along with Lakshmana and with this Seetha, oh,
enemy-destroyer Rama, that province shall be glorified." So said Sage Agastya to Rama."
[3-13-8]_END

B_3_C_14_1
BEGIN_
तम् दृष्ट्वा तौ महाभागौ वनस्थम् राम लक्ष्मणौ |मेनाते राक्षसम् पक्षिम् ब्रुवाणौ को भवान् इति || ३-१४-२_END
BEGIN_
On seeing such an eagle in the forest those two highly privileged brothers Rama and Lakshmana questioned 
it asking, "Who you are?" presuming it to be a demon. [3-14-2]_END

B_3_C_11_41
BEGIN_
एतद् एव आश्रम पदम् नूनम् तस्य महात्मनः |अगस्त्यस्य मुनेर् भ्रातुर् दृश्यते पुण्य कर्मणः || ४-११-४७_END
BEGIN_
"Definitely this alone appears to be the hermitage of Sage Agastya's brother, one with great soul and 
pious deeds. [4-11-47]_END

B_3_C_13_8
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु मुनिना राघवः संयत अंजलिः |
उवाच प्रश्रितम् वाक्यम् ऋषिम् दीप्तम् इव अनलम् || ३-१३-९_END
BEGIN_
Thus said by the sage, Raghava spoke amiable this sentence adjoining his palms to
the sage who is glowing like a ritual-fire. [3-13-9]_END

B_3_C_14_2
BEGIN_
स तौ मधुरया वाचा सौम्यया प्रीणयन्न् इव |उवाच वत्स माम् विद्धि वयस्यम् पितुर् आत्मनः || ३-१४-३_END
BEGIN_
But that eagle with sweet ad soft words spoke to them as though to please them, "oh boy Rama know me 
as your father's friend." [3-14-3]_END

B_3_C_11_42
BEGIN_
यथा हि इमे वनस्य अस्य ज्ञाताः पथि सहस्रशः |संनताः फल भरेण पुष्प भारेण च द्रुमाः || ४-११-४८_END
BEGIN_
"As how thousands of trees are bowing under the weight of flowers and fruit on the pathway, thereby 
I perceive it to be the hermitage of Agastya's bother. [4-11-48]_END

B_3_C_13_9
BEGIN_
धन्योस्मि अनुगृहीतोस्मि यस्य मे मुनि पुंगवः |
गुणैः सभ्रातृ भार्यस्य गुरुः नः परितुष्यति || ३-१३-१०_END
BEGIN_
"I am privileged and blessed as my mentor and the eminent age is well pleased with
the virtues of my brother and wife which are non-dissimilar to mine. [3-13-10]_END

B_3_C_14_3
BEGIN_
स तम् पितृ सखम् मत्वा पूजयामास राघवः |स तस्य कुलम् अव्यग्रम् अथ पप्रच्छ्ह नाम च || ३-१४-४_END
BEGIN_
Accepting that bird as his father's friend Raghava revered it, and he that Rama then asked for that 
eagle's name and lineage. [3-14-4]_END

B_3_C_11_43
BEGIN_
पिप्पलीनाम् च पक्वानाम् वनाद् अस्माद् उपागतः |गन्धो अयम् पवन उत्क्षिप्तः सहसा कटुकोदयः || ४-११-४९_END
BEGIN_
"Upraised by the wind the sour-smell of pippali fruits is suddenly coming closer from the forest. [4-11-49]_END

B_3_C_13_10
BEGIN_
किन्तु व्यादिश मे देशम् स उदकम् बहु काननम् |
यत्र आश्रम पदम् कृत्वा वसेयम् निरतः सुखम् || ३-१३-११_END
BEGIN_
"But a place with water and many forests may please be shown, where I can reside
happily and self-composedly on erecting a hermitage." Thus Rama asked the Sage Agastya.
[3-13-11]_END

B_3_C_14_4
BEGIN_
रामस्य वचनम् श्रुत्वा कुलम् आत्मानम् एव च |आचचक्षे द्विजः तस्मै सर्वभूत समुद्भवम् || ३-१४-५_END
BEGIN_
On hearing Rama's words that bird said about his ancestry and himself, and in doing so, that eagle also 
narrated the overall genesis of all beings. [3-14-5]_END

B_3_C_11_44
BEGIN_
तत्र तत्र च दृश्यन्ते संक्षिप्ताः काष्ठ संचयाः |लूनाः च परिदृश्यन्ते दर्भा वैदूर्य वर्चसः || ४-११-५०_END
BEGIN_
"Here and there visible are the well heaped heaps of firewood, and all over appearing is the sacred 
grass snipped at its top and gemlike in its tinge. [4-11-50]_END

B_3_C_13_11
BEGIN_
ततो अब्रवीत् मुनि श्रेष्ठः श्रुत्वा रामस्य भाषितम् |
ध्यात्वा मुहूर्तम् धर्मात्मा धीरो धीरतरम् वचः || ३-१३-१२_END
BEGIN_
Then that eminent sage Agastya on contemplating a while about what Rama has said,
that virtuous and confident sage spoke more ideational word to Rama. [3-13-12]_END

B_3_C_14_5
BEGIN_
पूर्वकाले महाबाहो ये प्रजापतयो अभवन् |तान् मे निगदतः सर्वान् आदितः शृणु राघव || ३-१४-६_END
BEGIN_
"Once upon a time there were lords of people, oh dextrous Raghava, and you may listen all about them 
from the beginning, while I narrate [3-14-6]_END

B_3_C_11_45
BEGIN_
एतत् च वन मध्यस्थम् कृष्ण अभ्र शिखर उपमम् |पावकस्य आश्रमस्थस्य धूमाग्रम् संप्रदृश्यते || ४-११-५१_END
BEGIN_
"From inside the hermitage in the midst of this forest the vertex of smoke from ritual fire is clearly 
visible as high as the vertex of a black rainy cloud. [4-11-51]_END

B_3_C_13_12
BEGIN_
इतो द्वि योजने तात बहु मूल फल उदकः |
देशो बहु मृगः श्रीमान् पंचवटि अभिविश्रुतः || ३-१३-१३_END
BEGIN_
"A most prosperous place called Panchavati is there at a distance of two yojana-s
from here, oh, dear Rama, which is abundant with tubers, fruits, water, and many deer." Thus
Agastya started to tell. [3-13-13]_END

B_3_C_14_6
BEGIN_
कर्दमः प्रथमः तेषाम् विकृतः तद् अनन्तरम् |शेषः च संश्रयः चैव बहु पुत्रः च वीर्यवान् || ३-१४-७
स्थाणुर् मरीचिर् अत्रिः च क्रतुः चैव महाबलः |पुलस्त्यः च अ.ंगिराः चैव प्रचेताः पुलहः तथा || ३-१४-८
दक्षो विवस्वान् अपरो अरिष्टनेमिः च राघव |कश्यपः च महातेजाः तेषाम् आसीत् च पश्चिमः || ३-१४-९_END
BEGIN_
"Of them Kardama was there at first, and afterwards Sesha, and later Samshraya was there with many children 
and a vigorous one he was. Then Sthaanu, Mariichi, Atri, the great mighty one Kratu, Pulasthya, Angira, 
Pracheta and Pulah were there. And oh, Raghava, Daksha, Vivaswan were while the other name of Vivasvan 
is Arishtanemi, and lastly the great resplendent Kashyapa, was there as Prajapati. [3-14-9] [3-14-7]_END

B_3_C_11_46
BEGIN_
विविक्तेषु च तीर्थेषु कृत स्नाना द्विजातयः |पुष्प उपहारम् कुर्वन्ति कुसुमैः स्वयम् आर्जितैः || ४-११-५२_END
BEGIN_
"On performing bathing in sacred streams the Brahmans are making flower offerings to gods, called
puSpa bali, with the flowers that are personally collected by them. [4-11-52]_END

B_3_C_13_13
BEGIN_
तत्र गत्वा आश्रम पदम् कृत्वा सौमित्रिणा सह |
रमस्व त्वम् पितुर् वाक्यम् यथा उक्तम् अनुपालयन् || ३-१३-१४_END
BEGIN_
"On your going there along with Saumitri, and on erecting a hermitage you may
take delight in there complying the decreed order of your father. [3-13-14]_END

B_3_C_14_7
BEGIN_
प्रजापतेः तु दक्षस्य बभूवुर् इति विश्रुतम् |षष्टिर् दुहितरो राम यशस्विन्यो महायशः || ३-१४-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Oh glorious Rama, there were sixty highly renowned daughters to Daksha, thus we hear. [3-14-10]_END

B_3_C_11_47
BEGIN_
ततः सुतीक्ष्णस्य वचनम् यथा सौम्य मया श्रुतम् |अगस्त्यस्य आश्रमो भ्रातुर् नूनम् एष भविष्यति || ४-११-५३_END
BEGIN_
"Thus by the words of Sage Suteekshna as I have heard, oh, gentle Lakshmana, this hermitage shall definitely 
be that of Sage Agastya's brother. [4-11-53]_END

B_3_C_13_14
BEGIN_
विदितो हि एष वृत्तांतो मम सर्वः तव अनघ |
तपसः च प्रभावेण स्नेहाद् दशरथस्य च || ३-१३-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Indeed all of this episode of yours is known to me, oh, merited one, by the
ability of my asceticism, and also by my friendship with Dasharatha. [3-13-15]_END

B_3_C_14_8
BEGIN_
कश्यपः प्रतिजग्राह तासाम् अष्टौ सुमध्यमाः |अदितिम् च दितिम् चैव दनूम् अपि च कालकाम् || ३-१४-११
ताम्राम् क्रोध वशाम् चैव मनुम् च अप्य् अनलाम् अपि |_END
BEGIN_
"Of them Kashyapa accepted eight slender-waisted daughters of Daksha Prajapati, namely Aditi, Diti, 
Danu, Kaalakaa and Taamra, Krodhavasha, also thus Manu and even Anala also as wives. [3-14-11, 12a]_END

B_3_C_11_48
BEGIN_
निगृह्य तरसा मृत्युम् लोकानाम् हित काम्यया |यस्य भ्रात्रा कृता इयम् दिक् शरण्या पुण्य कर्मणा || 
४-११-५४_END
BEGIN_
"Whose brother is Sage Agastya with meritorious deeds, who wishing well-being of the world controlled 
death by his efficacy, and who made this southern region a liveable region, this must be the hermitage 
of such a sage, such Agatya's brother. [4-11-54]_END

B_3_C_13_15
BEGIN_
हृदयस्थः च ते छ्हन्दो विज्ञातः तपसा मया |
इह वासम् प्रतिज्ञाय मया सह तपो वने || ३-१३-१६
अतः च त्वाम् अहम् ब्रूमि गच्छ्ह पंचवटीम् इति |_END
BEGIN_
"I am in the know of your heartfelt certitude by my ascesis, thereby I wish to
advise you to go to Panchavati, though I said that you may dwell in these ascetic-woods along with
me. [3-13-16, 17a]_END

B_3_C_14_9
BEGIN_
ताः तु कन्याः ततः प्रीतः कश्यपः पुनर् अब्रवीत् || ३-१४-१२पुत्रामः त्रैलोक्य भर्तॄन् वै जनयिष्यथ 
मत् समान् |_END
BEGIN_
"Then Kashyapa is gladdened and said to those young wives, "You all shall deliver sons similar to me 
and who can sustain the three worlds." [3-14-12b, 13a]_END

B_3_C_11_49
BEGIN_
इह एकदा किल क्रूरो वातापिः अपि च इल्वलः |भ्रातरौ सहितौ आस्ताम् ब्राह्मणघ्नौ महा असुरौ || ४-११-५५_END
BEGIN_
"Once upon a time verily cruel demon brothers Vaataapi and Ilvala were here together, and they the dreadful 
demons, they say, used to be Bhraman-killers. [4-11-55]_END

B_3_C_15_0
BEGIN_
ततः पंचवटीम् गत्वा नाना व्याल मृगायुताम् |उवाच भ्रातरम् रामो लक्ष्मणम् दीप्त तेजसम् || ३-१५-१_END
BEGIN_
Then on going to Panchavati which is full with many serpents and predators, Rama said to splendidly 
brilliant Lakshmana. [3-15-1]_END

B_3_C_13_16
BEGIN_
स हि रम्यो वनोद्देशो मैथिली तत्र रंस्यते || ३-१३-१७
स देशः श्लाघनीयः च न अतिदूरे च राघव |_END
BEGIN_
"That woodland will be delightful, isn't it Raghava, for it is praiseworthy and not
very far off from here, and Seetha can take delight in there. [3-13-17b, 18a]_END

B_3_C_14_10
BEGIN_
अदितिः तन् मना राम दितिः च दनुर् एव च || ३-१४-१३कालका च महाबाहो शेषाः तु अमनसो अभवन् |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, dextrous Rama, Aditi, Diti, Kaalakaa and Danu have agreed for that, but others became unheedful 
of Kashyapa's words. [3-14-13b, 14a]_END

B_3_C_11_50
BEGIN_
धारयन् ब्राह्मणम् रूपम् इल्वलः संस्कृतम् वदन् |आमंत्रयति विप्रान् स श्राद्धम् उद्दिश्य निर्घृणः 
|| ४-११-५६_END
BEGIN_
"Disguising in Bhraman's semblance and speaking sophisticatedly that Ilvala used to invite Brahmans 
for the purpose of obsequial ceremonies, where Brahman are fed after usual ceremony to appeases their 
manes. [4-11-56]_END

B_3_C_15_1
BEGIN_
आगताः स्म यथा उद्दिष्टम् यम् देशम् मुनिः अब्रवीत् |अयम् पंचवटी देशः सौम्य पुष्पित काननः || ३-१५-२_END
BEGIN_
"We arrived at the place as indicated by the sage, oh, gentle Lakshmana, this region with its flowered 
forests is Panchavati." [3-15-2]_END

B_3_C_13_17
BEGIN_
गोदावर्याः समीपे च मैथिली तत्र रंस्यते || ३-१३-१८
प्राज्य मूल फलैः चैव नाना द्विज गणैर् युतः |
विविक्तः च महाबाहो पुण्यो रम्यः तथैव च || ३-१३-१९_END
BEGIN_
"There Maithili will take delight nearby River Godavari, and it is with abundant
tubers, fruits, various are its bird flocks, and it is very reclusive too, oh, great dextrous Rama,
further it is meritorious and appealing. [3-13-18b, 19]_END

B_3_C_14_11
BEGIN_
अदित्याम् जज्ञिरे देवाः त्रयः त्रिंशत् अरिंदम || ३-१४-१४आदित्या वसवो रुद्रा अश्विनौ च परंतप |_END
BEGIN_
"Aditi gave birth to twelve Aditya-s, the Sun-gods, eight Vasu-s, the Terrestrials-gods, eleven Rudraa-s, 
the Fury-gods, and two Ashvinis, the medicine-gods, total thirty-three of them. [3-14-14b, 15a]_END

B_3_C_11_51
BEGIN_
भ्रातरम् संस्कृतम् कृत्वा ततः तम् मेष रूपिणम् |तान् द्विजान् भोजयामास श्राद्ध दृष्टेन कर्मणा || 
४-११-५७_END
BEGIN_
Then Ilvala used to make his brother Vaataapi into a ram, perfect that ram's meat into deliciously cooked 
food, and used to feed Brahmans according to obsequial rites and deeds. [4-11-57]_END

B_3_C_15_2
BEGIN_
सर्वतः चार्यताम् दृष्टिः कानने निपुणो हि असि |आश्रमः कतर अस्मिन् नः देशे भवति सम्मतः || ३-१५-३_END
BEGIN_
"In which place we have to situate our hermitage for our liking, for that cast your sight all over the 
forest, and indeed you are an expert in such matters. [3-15-3]_END

B_3_C_13_18
BEGIN_
भवान् अपि सदाचारः च शक्तः च परिरक्षणे |
अपि च अत्र वसन् राम तापसान् पालयिष्यसि || ३-१३-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Even you, Rama, with your good deportment are capable to safeguard the hermits
while residing there. [3-13-20]_END

B_3_C_14_12
BEGIN_
दितिः तु अजनयत् पुत्रान् दैत्याम् तात यशस्विनः || ३-१४-१५तेषाम् इयम् वसुमती पुरा आसीत् स वन अर्णवा 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, boy Rama, Diti gave birth to well-known Daitya-s, the so-called demons, and earlier this earth 
with forests and oceans belonged to them. [3-14-15b, 16a]_END

B_3_C_11_52
BEGIN_
ततो भुक्तवताम् तेषाम् विप्राणाम् इल्वलो अब्रवीत् |वातापे निष्क्रमस्व इति स्वरेण महता वदन् || ४-११-५८_END
BEGIN_
"When those Brahmans are surfeited with that ram's meat, then Ilvala used to shout loudly, "oh, Vaataapi, 
you may come out." [4-11-58]_END

B_3_C_15_3
BEGIN_
रमते यत्र वैदेही त्वम् अहम् चैव लक्ष्मण |तादृशो दृश्यताम् देशः संनिकृष्ट जलाशयः || ३-१५-४वन 
रामण्यकम् यत्र जल रामण्यकम् तथा |संनिकृष्टम् च यस्मिन् तु समित् पुष्प कुश उदकम् || ३-१५-५_END
BEGIN_
"In which place Vaidehi, likewise you and me too can take delight, where the woodland is scenic and 
the water is pleasurable, and where a water lake, ritual-firewood, flowers, and the sacred grass are 
available in proximity, oh, Lakshmana, such a place may be searched out. [3-15-4, 5]_END

B_3_C_13_19
BEGIN_
एतत् आलक्ष्यते वीर मधूकानाम् महत् वनम् |
उत्तरेण अस्य गंतव्यम् न्यग्रोधम् अपि गच्छ्हता || ३-१३-२१_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, brave one, you see this great forest of flower-liquor trees, you have to
proceed north of it and advance towards a banyan tree. [3-13-21]_END

B_3_C_14_13
BEGIN_
दनुः तु अजनयत् पुत्रम् अश्वग्रीवम् अरिंदम || ३-१४-१६नरकम् कालकम् चैव कालका अपि व्यजायत |_END
BEGIN_
"And oh, enemy-destroyer Rama, Danu gave birth to son Ashvagriiva or also called Hayagriiva, Horse-headed 
god, and Kaalakaa gave birth to Naraka and Kaalaka. [3-14-16b, 17a]_END

B_3_C_11_53
BEGIN_
ततो भ्रातुर् वचः श्रुत्वा वातापिः मेषवत् नदन् |भित्त्वा भित्वा शरीराणि ब्राह्मणानाम् विनिष्पतत् 
|| ४-११-५९_END
BEGIN_
"Then on listening his brother's words Vaataapi used to lunge out bleating like a ram, tearing and rending 
the bodies of those Brahmans. [4-11-59]_END

B_3_C_13_20
BEGIN_
ततः स्थलम् उपारुह्य पर्वतस्य अविदूरतः |
ख्यातः पंचवटी इति एव नित्य पुष्पित काननः || ३-१३-२२_END
BEGIN_
"Then on climbing up an upland a mountain is seen, that which is also not far away,
and that renowned Panchavati is there in an ever-blooming forest in the valley of that mountain."
Said Sage Agastya to Rama. [3-13-22]_END

B_3_C_15_4
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु रामेण लक्मणः संयत अंजलिः |सीता समक्षम् काकुत्स्थम् इदम् वचनम् अब्रवीत् || ३-१५-६_END
BEGIN_
When thus said by Rama, Lakshmana adjoined his palms and said this sentence to Rama in the presence 
of Seetha. [3-15-6]_END

B_3_C_14_14
BEGIN_
क्रौन्चीम् भासीम् तथा श्येनीम् धृतराष्ट्रीम् तथा शुकीम् || ३-१४-१७ताम्रा तु सुषुवे कन्याः पंच एता 
लोकविश्रुताः |_END
BEGIN_
"But Taamraa gave birth to five world renowned girls namely, Krounchi, Bhaasii, Shyenii, Dhritaraashtrii, 
and Shukii. [3-14-17b, 18a]_END

B_3_C_11_54
BEGIN_
ब्राह्मणानाम् सहस्राणि तैः एवम् काम रूपिभिः |विनाशितानि संहत्य नित्यशः पिशित अशनैः || ४-११-६०_END
BEGIN_
"This way they the guise changing demons always ruined thousands of Brahmans together, greedy for raw-flesh 
as they are. [4-11-60]_END

B_3_C_13_21
BEGIN_
अगस्त्येन एवम् उक्तः तु रामः सौमित्रिणा सह |
सत्कृत्य आमंत्रयामास तम् ऋषिम् सत्य वादिनम् || ३-१३-२३_END
BEGIN_
When thus said by Sage Agastya, Rama along with Soumitri venerated and bade farewell
to that truth advocator sage Agastya. [3-13-23]_END

B_3_C_15_5
BEGIN_
परवान् अस्मि काकुत्स्थ त्वयि वर्ष शतम् स्थिते |स्वयम् तु रुचिरे देशे क्रियताम् इति माम् वद || ३-१५-७_END
BEGIN_
"I am but a dependent, as long as you are there, may it be for innumerable years, I am your adherent, 
Rama, therefore you yourself tell me to build hermitage in such and such delightful place. [3-15-7]_END

B_3_C_14_15
BEGIN_
उलूकान् जनयत् क्रौन्ची भासी भासान् व्यजायत || ३-१४-१८श्येनी श्येनाम् च गृध्राम च व्यजायत सुतेजसः 
|धृतराष्ट्री तु हंसाम् च कलहंसाम् च सर्वशः || ३-१४-१९_END
BEGIN_
"And from each of the five daughters of Taamraa in turn emanated are the other avian species, where 
Kraunchii gave birth to Uluuka-s, the owls, Bhasii-s gave birth to Bhaasaa-s, the vultures, and Shyenii 
gave birth to very sharp eagles and falcons, and then Dhritaraashtrii gave birth to swans and all other 
kinds of graceful water-birds. [3-14-18b, 19]_END

B_3_C_11_55
BEGIN_
अगस्त्येन तदा देवैः प्रार्थितेन महर्षिणा |अनुभूय किल श्राद्धे भक्षितः स महा असुरः || ४-११-६१_END
BEGIN_
"Then by Sage Agastya, whom gods have prayed to end this demonic menace, and whom demon Ilvala invited 
to feast during obsequial rites, he that Agastya having relished the fiendish demon in the form of ram, 
they say, had finished him off. [4-11-61]_END

B_3_C_13_22
BEGIN_
तौ तु तेन अभ्यनुज्ञातौ कृत पाद अभिवन्दनौ |
तम् आश्रमम् पंचवटीम् जग्मतुः सह सीतया || ३-१२-२४_END
BEGIN_
Thus well bidden by Sage Agastya those two Rama and Lakshmana have offered their
venerations at the feet of that sage and proceeded to their prospective hermitage at Panchavati
along with Seetha. [3-12-24]_END

B_3_C_15_6
BEGIN_
सुप्रीतः तेन वाक्येन लक्ष्मणस्य महाद्युतिः |विमृशन् रोचयामास देशम् सर्व गुण अन्वितम् || ३-१५-८_END
BEGIN_
Rama is gladdened by those words of that great resplendent Lakshmana, and he selected a place that comprised 
of all the attributes. [3-15-8]_END

B_3_C_14_16
BEGIN_
चक्रवाकाम् च भद्रम् ते विजज्ञे सा अपि भामिनी |शुकी नताम् विजज्ञे तु नताया विनता सुता || ३-१४-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Dhritaraashtrii gave birth even to Chakravaaka water-birds, and Shukii gave birth to a daughter Nata, 
and Nata's daughter is Vinata. [3-14-20]_END

B_3_C_11_56
BEGIN_
ततः संपन्नम् इति उक्त्वा दत्त्वा हस्ते अवनेजनम् |भ्रातरम् निष्क्रमस्व इति च इल्वलः समभाषत || ४-११-६२_END
BEGIN_
"Then Ilvala while giving lateral hand wash into the palms of Agastya entered in the routine conversation 
of obsequies asking, "Is this rite fulfilled..." and he furthered it in calling his brother to come 
out. [4-11-62]_END

B_3_C_13_23
BEGIN_
गृहीत चापौ तु नराधिप आत्मजौ
विषक्त तूणी समरेषु अकातरौ |
यथा उपदिष्टेन पथा महर्षिणा |
प्रजग्मतुः पंचवटीम् समाहितौ || ३-१३-२५_END
BEGIN_
Those princes that are dauntless in war took up their bows and braced up their
quivers, and resolutely proceeded to Panchavati on the route apprised by that great sage Agastya.
[3-13-25]_END

B_3_C_15_7
BEGIN_
स तम् रुचिरम् आक्रम्य देशम् आश्रम कर्मणि |हस्ते गृहीत्वा हस्तेन रामः सौमित्रिम् अब्रवीत् || ३-१५-९_END
BEGIN_
On taking Lakshmana's hand by his hand Rama paced that beautiful place intended for the construction 
of hermitage up and down and spoke to Soumitri this way. [3-15-9]_END

B_3_C_14_17
BEGIN_
दश क्रोधवशा राम विजज्ञे अपि आत्मसंभवाः |मृगीम् च मृगमंदाम् च हरीम् भद्रमदाम् अपि || ३-१४-२१मात.ंगीम् 
अथ शार्दूलीम् श्वेताम् च सुरभीम् तथा |सर्व लक्षण संपन्नाम् सुरसाम् कद्रुकाम् अपि || ३-१४-२२_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama, Krodhavasha gave birth to ten of her self-same daughters namely Mrigi, Mrigamanda, Hari, 
Bhadramanda, Maatangii, Sharduulii, Shweta, Surabhii, and like that to Surasa, who is embodied with 
all giftedness, and even to Kadruva. [3-14-21, 22]_END

B_3_C_11_57
BEGIN_
स तदा भाषमाणम् तु भ्रातरम् विप्र घातिनम् |अब्रवीत् प्रहसन् धीमान् अगस्त्यो मुनि सत्तमः || ४-११-६३_END
BEGIN_
Then that wise and eminent sage Agastya spoke mockingly to Ilvala who is conversing that way to his 
brother to come out. [4-11-63]_END

B_3_C_15_8
BEGIN_
अयम् देशः समः श्रीमान् पुष्पितैर् तरुभिर् वृतः |इह आश्रम पदम् सौम्य यथावत् कर्तुम् अर्हसि || ३-१५-१०_END
BEGIN_
"This is an evenly and propitious place surrounded with flowered trees and it is apt of you to erect 
hermitage here, traditionally. [3-15-10]_END

B_3_C_14_18
BEGIN_
अपत्यम् तु मृगाः सर्वे मृग्या नरवरोत्तम |ऋक्षाः च मृगमंदायाः सृमराः चमराः तथा || ३-१४-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Children Mrigi are all of the the deer, oh best of the best-men, Rama, and Mrigamnda's progeny is Riksha-s, 
Bears, a kind of antelope, and like that the Himalayan yak like species.[3-14-23]_END

B_3_C_16_0
BEGIN_
वसतः तस्य तु सुखम् राघवस्य महात्मनः |शरद् व्यपाये हेमंतऋतुर् इष्टः प्रवर्तत || ४-१६-१_END
BEGIN_
Pleasant hemantha R^itu , pre-winter season has set in after the passage of sharat R^itu, 
post-rainy season at Panchavati where the noble souled Rama is staying comfortably. [4-16-1]_END

B_3_C_11_58
BEGIN_
कुतो निष्क्रमितुम् शक्तिर् मया जीर्णस्य रक्षसः |भ्रातुः ते मेष रूपस्य गतस्य यम सादनम् || ४-११-६४_END
BEGIN_
"Where is the energy for that ram shaped demon brother of yours to come out as I digested and sent him 
to the hellish residence of Terminator. [4-11-64]_END

B_3_C_15_9
BEGIN_
इयम् आदित्य संकाशैः पद्मैः सुरभि गंधिभिः |अदूरे दृश्यते रम्या पद्मिनी पद्म शोभिता || ३-५-११_END
BEGIN_
"This pleasing lake is seen here adjacently, beaming forth with its lotuses that are similar to sun 
in resplendence, and that are scented fragrantly. [3-5-11]_END

B_3_C_14_19
BEGIN_
ततः तु इरावतीम् नाम जज्ञे भद्रमदा सुताम् |तस्याः तु ऐरावतः पुत्रो लोकनाथो महागजः || ३-१४-२४_END
BEGIN_
"Then Bhadramanda gave birth to the girl named Iravati and her son is elephant the great, Airaavata, 
the protector of world. [3-14-24]_END

B_3_C_16_1
BEGIN_
स कदाचित् प्रभातायाम् शर्वर्याम् रघुनंदनः |प्रययाव अभिषेकार्थम् रम्यम् गोदावरीम् नदीम् || ४-१६-२_END
BEGIN_
On some day when night faded into dawn Rama started for the delightful River Godavari for a bath. [4-16-2]_END

B_3_C_11_59
BEGIN_
अथ तस्य वचः श्रुत्वा भ्रातुर् निधन संश्रितम् |प्रधर्षयितुम् आरेभे मुनिम् क्रोधात् निशा चरः || ४-११-६५_END
BEGIN_
"Then on hearing the words of sage Agastya affirming brother's demise, that night-walking demon furiously 
commenced to assault the sage. [4-11-65]_END

B_3_C_15_10
BEGIN_
यथा आख्यातम् अगस्त्येन मुनिना भावितात्मना |इयम् गोदावरी रम्या पुष्पितैः तरुभिर् वृता || ३-१५-१२
हंस कारण्डव आकीर्णा चक्रवाक उपशोभिता |_END
BEGIN_
"This River Godavari is also seen from here, surrounded by blooming trees, spread over with swans, and 
beautified with kaarandava, and chakravaaka birds, as that contemplated soul sage Agastya had said. 
[3-15-12]_END

B_3_C_14_20
BEGIN_
हर्याः च हरयो अपत्यम् वानराः च तपस्विनः |गोला.ंगूलाः च शार्दूली व्याघ्राम् च अजनयत् सुतान् || ३-१४-२५_END
BEGIN_
"And Hari's offspring are lions and sagely/mighty monkeys, while Sharduulii gave birth to baboons and 
tigers. [3-14-25]_END

B_3_C_16_2
BEGIN_
प्रह्वः कलश हसतः तम् सीतया सह वीर्यवान् |पृष्ठतो अनुव्रजन् भ्राता सौमित्रिर् इदम् अब्रवीत् || ४-१६-३_END
BEGIN_
His valorous brother Saumitri following him humbly with a handy vessel, along with Seetha, spoke this 
to Rama. [4-16-3]_END

B_3_C_11_60
BEGIN_
सो अभ्यद्रवत् द्विजेंद्रम् तम् मुनिना दीप्त तेजसा |चक्षुषा अनल कल्पेन निर्दग्धो निधनम् गतः || ४-११-६६_END
BEGIN_
"When that demon rushed towards that best Bhraman to kill, he that sage glowing with his own refulgence 
burnt him down just by his flame-like eyes and doomed him to death. [4-11-66]_END

B_3_C_15_11
BEGIN_
न अतिदूरे न च आसन्ने मृग यूथ निपीडिता || ३-१५-१३मयूर नादिता रम्याः प्रांशवो बहु कंदराः |दृश्यन्ते 
गिरयः सौम्य फुल्लैः तरुभिर् आवृताः || ३-१५-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Those soaring mountains are appearing beautiful with many caves, surrounded by flowered trees, flurried 
by animal herds, sounded by peacocks, and they are neither far-off nor very nearby. [3-15-13, 14]_END

B_3_C_14_21
BEGIN_
मात.ंग्याः तु अथ मातंगाअपत्यम् मनुज ऋषभ |दिशागजम् तु श्वेत काकुत्स्थ श्वेता व्यजनयत् सुतम् || ३-१४-२६_END
BEGIN_
"Then Maatangi's childrenm are elephants, oh, best one among men, Rama, and Shweta gave birth to eight 
elephants that are at eight quarters of world, sustaining the world on their head. [3-14-26]_END

B_3_C_16_3
BEGIN_
अयम् स कालः संप्राप्तः प्रियो यः ते प्रियंवद |अलंकृत इव आभाति येन संवत्सरः शुभः || ४-१६-४_END
BEGIN_
"Adorned by which season the promising year will be bright, oh, pleasant conversationalist, and which 
season will also be pleasant to you, that hemanta season has set in. [4-16-4]_END

B_3_C_11_61
BEGIN_
तस्य अयम् आश्रमो भ्रातुः तटाक वन शोभितः |विप्र अनुकंपया येन कर्म इदम् दुष्करम् कृतम् || ४-११-६७_END
BEGIN_
"This hermitage embellishing with lake and woods belongs to the brother of Sage Agastya who has done 
this impossible deed just by his compassion towards Brahmans." So said Rama to Lakshmana and Seetha 
about Agastya. [4-11-67]_END

B_3_C_15_12
BEGIN_
सौवर्णै राजतैः ताम्रैः देशे देशे च धातुभिः |गवाक्षिता इव आभान्ति गजाः परम भक्तिभिः || ३-१५-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Here and there are the golden, silvery and coppery ores on the mountains, and they are shining forth 
like cow-eye ventilators on walls and also like the superb paintings on elephants. [3-15-15]_END

B_3_C_14_22
BEGIN_
ततो दुहितरौ राम सुरभिर् द्वे वि अजायत |रोहिणीम् नाम भद्रम् ते गन्धर्वीम् च यशस्विनीम् || ३-१४-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Then, oh Rama, Surabhi gave birth to two daughters, one is named as illustrious Rohini, safe you 
be, and the other is Gandharvi. [3-14-27]_END

B_3_C_16_4
BEGIN_
नीहार परुषो लोकः पृथिवी सस्य मालिनी |जलानि अनुपभोग्यानि सुभगो हव्य वाहनः || ४-१६-५_END
BEGIN_
"These days the dew is harsh to the bodies of people, earth is overlaid with crops, water is unenjoyable, 
but fire is delightful. [4-16-5]_END

B_3_C_11_62
BEGIN_
एवम् कथयमानस्य तस्य सौमित्रिणा सह |रामस्य अस्तम् गतः सूर्यः संध्या कालो अभ्यवर्तत || ४-११-६८_END
BEGIN_
While Rama narrated that way to Lakshmana sun went into dusk and the vesperal time came close of him. 
[4-11-68]_END

B_3_C_15_13
BEGIN_
सालैः तालैः तमालैः च खर्जूरैः पनसैः द्रुमैः |नीवारैः तिनिशैः चैव पुन्नागैः च उपशोभिताः || ३-१५-१६
चूतैर् अशोकैः तिलकैः केतकैर् अपि चंपकैः |पुष्प गुल्म लता उपेतैः तैः तैः तरुभिर् आवृताः || ३-१५-१७
स्यन्दनैः चंदनैः नीपैः पर्णासैः लकुचैः अपि |धव अश्वकर्ण खदिरैः शमी किंशुक पाटलैः || ३-१५-१८_END
BEGIN_
"These mountains are brightening with trees of Saala, Palmyra, Tamaala, Date Palms, Jackfruit and also 
thus with Punnaagaa. With Chuuta - Sweet Mango; Ashoka, Tialaka, even with Ketaka, Champaka trees, And 
even with Syandana, Sandalwood, Niipa, Paarnasa, Lakuch, dhava, Ashwakarna, Khadira, Shamii, Kimshuka, 
Paatala trees, and entwined are those and those trees with flowered shrubs, and along with climbers, 
and thus they brighten the mountains. [3-15-16, 17, 18]_END

B_3_C_14_23
BEGIN_
रोहिणि अजनयद् गावो गन्धर्वी वाजिनः सुतान् |सुरसा अजनयन् नागान् राम कद्रूः च पन्नगान् || ३-१२४-२८_END
BEGIN_
"Rohini gave birth to cows and other livestock, while Surasa gave birth to Naagaa-s, viz., many headed 
serpents, while Kadru gave birth to ordinary serpents. [3-124-28]_END

B_3_C_16_5
BEGIN_
नव आग्रयण पूजाभिर् अभ्यर्च्य पितृ देवताः |कृत आग्रयणकाः काले सन्तो विगत कल्मषाः || ४-१६-६_END
BEGIN_
"On appeasing manes with worships during northern solstice and even on performing solstitial rituals 
in time, the righteous people are becoming free from evils. [4-16-6]_END

B_3_C_11_63
BEGIN_
उपास्य पश्चिमाम् संध्याम् सह भ्रात्रा यथा विधि |प्रविवेश आश्रम पदम् तम् ऋषिम् च अभ्यवादयत् || ४-११-६९_END
BEGIN_
Worshipping sunset along with brother as per custom, Rama entered that hermitage and greeted that sage. 
[4-11-69]_END

B_3_C_15_14
BEGIN_
इदम् पुण्यम् इदम् रम्यम् इदम् बहु मृग द्विजम् |इह वत्स्याम सौमित्रे सार्धम् एतेन पक्षिणा || ३-१५-१९_END
BEGIN_
"This place is holy, this is delightful and this is with many animals and birds, hence Soumitri, let 
us reside here along with this bird Jatayu." Thus said Rama to Lakshmana. [3-15-19]_END

B_3_C_14_24
BEGIN_
मनुर् मनुष्यान् जनयत् कश्यपस्य महात्मनः |ब्राह्मणान् क्षत्रियान् वैश्यान् शूद्राम् च मनुजर्षभ || 
३-१४-२९_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, the best among men Rama, the wife of great-soul Kashyapa, lady Manu procreated humans, Brahman--s, 
Kshatriya-s, Vyasya-s, and Shudra-s. [3-14-29]_END

B_3_C_16_6
BEGIN_
प्राज्यकामा जनपदाः संपन्नतर गो रसाः |विचरन्ति महीपाला यात्र अर्थम् विजिगीषवः || ४-१६-७_END
BEGIN_
"Amply fulfilled are the desires of the villagers with the affluence of milch cows and dairy, and the 
vanquishing kings are make moves for the purposes of their further vanquishes. [4-16-7]_END

B_3_C_17_0
BEGIN_
कृत अभिषेको रामः तु सीता सौमित्रिर् एव च |तस्मात् गोदावरी तीरात् ततो जग्मुः स्वम् आश्रमम् || ३-१७-१_END
BEGIN_
On taking bath Rama with Seetha and Soumitri, then went to his own hermitage from that bank of River 
Godavari. [3-17-1]_END

B_3_C_11_64
BEGIN_
सम्यक् प्रतिगृहीतः तु मुनिना तेन राघवः |न्यवसत् ताम् निशाम् एकाम् प्राश्य मूल फलानि च || ४-११-७०_END
BEGIN_
Raghava spent one night there when that sage received him well and when they dined on tubers and fruits. 
[4-11-70]_END

B_3_C_15_15
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु रामेण लक्ष्मणः परवीरहा |अचिरेण आश्रमम् भ्रातुः चकार सुमहाबलः || ३-१५-२०_END
BEGIN_
Thus said by Rama to that remover of foe's valour and one with very great might, namely Lakshmana, he 
briskly erected a hermitage for his brother. [3-15-20]_END

B_3_C_14_25
BEGIN_
मुखतो ब्राह्मणा जाता उरसः क्षत्रियाः तथा |ऊरुभ्याम् जज्ञिरे वैश्याः पद्भ्याम् शूद्रा इति श्रुतिः 
|| ३-१४-३०_END
BEGIN_
"The Brahman-s emerged from face, the Kshatriya-s from chest, the Vyasya-s from two thighs, and the 
Shudra-s from two feet, thus we hear from the scriptures viz., Veda, i.e., Rig Veda Purusha Shuukta. 
[3-14-30]_END

B_3_C_16_7
BEGIN_
सेवमाने दृढम् सूर्ये दिशम् अन्तक सेविताम् |विहीन तिलका इव स्त्री न उत्तरा दिक् प्रकाशते || ४-१६-८_END
BEGIN_
"While the sun is steadfastly attending the direction of Time-god Yama, namely southern horizon, the 
northern direction is not brilliant like a woman who lost the vermilion mark on her forehead. [4-16-8]_END

B_3_C_17_1
BEGIN_
आश्रमम् तम् उपागम्य राघवः सह लक्ष्मणः |कृत्वा पौर्वाह्णिकम् कर्म पर्णशालाम् उपागमत् || ३-१७-२_END
BEGIN_
Nearing that hermitage Raghava along with Lakshmana performed early morning rituals and then reached 
the cottage. [3-17-2]_END

B_3_C_11_65
BEGIN_
तस्याम् रात्र्याम् व्यतीतायाम् उदिते रवि मण्डले |भ्रातरम् तम् अगस्त्यस्य आमंत्रयत राघवः || ४-११-७१_END
BEGIN_
Raghava spent that night there and when sun rose in solar orbit he took leave of the brother of Sage 
Agastya saying the following. [4-11-71]_END

B_3_C_15_16
BEGIN_
पर्णशालाम् सुविपुलाम् तत्र संघात मृत्तिकाम् |सुस्तंभाम् मस्करैर् दीर्घैः कृत वंशाम् सुशोभनाम् || 
३-१५-२१शमी शाखाभिः आस्तीर्य धृढ पाशावपाशितम् |कुश काश शरैः पर्णैः सुपरिच्छ्हादिताम् तथा || ३-१५-२२
समीकृत तलाम् रम्याम् चकार सुमहाबलः |निवासम् राघवस्य अर्थे प्रेक्ष्णीयम् अनुत्तमम् || ३-१५-२३_END
BEGIN_
Lakshmana built a very spacious straw-cottage there levelling and raising the clay for raised floor 
of the cottage, strongly pillared with long bamboos, thereupon on those pillars excellent rafters are 
made, and the branches of Shamii trees are spread out, twined firmly with twines of jute strands, and 
with the cross-laid bamboos for thatching, and over that blades of Kusha grass and leaves of Kaasha 
are spread and well over-covered for the roof, and thus that very great mighty Lakshmana made that best 
and very spacious straw-cottage with a levelled surface for residence of Raghava in the interests of 
Raghava alone, and it resulted as a feast to the eye. [3-15-21, 22, 23]_END

B_3_C_14_26
BEGIN_
सर्वान् पुण्य फलान् वृक्षान् अनला अपि व्यजायत |विनता च शुकी पौत्री कद्रूः च सुरसा स्वसा || ३-१४-३१_END
BEGIN_
"All the merited fruit-bearing trees are given birth by Anala, and now I will narrate about Vinata, 
the daughter's daughter of Shukii, and about Kadru, the sister of Surasa. [3-14-31]_END

B_3_C_16_8
BEGIN_
प्रकृत्या हिम कोश आढ्यो दूर सूर्याः च सांप्रतम् |यथार्थ नामा सुव्यक्तम् हिमवान् हिमवान् गिरिः || 
४-१६-९_END
BEGIN_
"By their very nature Himalayas are the depositories of snow, and presently distanced from the sun they 
are very obviously snowy true to their name. [4-16-9]_END

B_3_C_17_2
BEGIN_
उवास सुखितः तत्र पूज्यमानो महर्षभः|स रामः पर्ण शालायाम् आसीनः सह सीतया || ३-१-७-३विरराज महा 
बाहुः चित्रया चन्द्रमा इव |लक्ष्मणेन सह भ्रात्रा चकार विविधाः कथाः || ३-१७-४_END
BEGIN_
There Rama comfortably spent time while being adored by eminent sages when he is with them, and narrating 
many a narrative while sitting in hermitage along with Seetha and his brother Lakshmana, thus he shone 
forth like the moon when with Chitra constellation. [3-1-7-3, 4]_END

B_3_C_11_66
BEGIN_
अभिवादये त्वाम् भगवन् सुखम् स्म उष्यतो निशाम् |आमंत्रये त्वाम् गच्छ्हामि गुरुम् ते द्रष्टुम् अग्रजम् 
|| ४-११-७२_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, godly sage, we stayed in the night comfortably, I now make an obeisance and bid farewell to you, 
as I wish to proceed to see your mentor and elder brother Agastya. [4-11-72]_END

B_3_C_15_17
BEGIN_
स गत्वा लक्ष्मणः श्रीमान् नदीम् गोदावरीम् तदा |स्नात्वा पद्मानि च आदाय सफलः पुनर् आगतः || ३-१५-२४_END
BEGIN_
On his going to River Godavari that noble Lakshmana bathed and on gathering lotuses and fruits he returned 
to the cottage. [3-15-24]_END

B_3_C_14_27
BEGIN_
कद्रूर् नाग सहस्रम् तु विजज्ञे धरणीधरन् |द्वौ पुत्रौ विनतायाः तु गरुडो अरुण एव च || ३-१४-३२_END
BEGIN_
"Kadru gave birth to a thousand-headed serpent who is the bearer of this earth, and Vinata gave birth 
to two sons namely Garuda and Aruna. [3-14-32]_END

B_3_C_16_9
BEGIN_
अत्यन्त सुख संचारा मध्याह्ने स्पर्शतः सुखाः |दिवसाः सुभग आदित्याअः छ्हाया सलिल दुर्भगाः || ४-१६-१०_END
BEGIN_
"By the way of touch the mid days are comfortable and in these days the daytime is very much comfortable 
for sauntering, thus the sun in daytimes is genial and ungenial are the shades and waters. [4-16-10]_END

B_3_C_17_3
BEGIN_
तदा आसीनस्य रामस्य कथा संसक्त चेतसः |तम् देशम् राक्षसी काचिद् आजगाम यदृच्छ्हया || ३-१७-५_END
BEGIN_
At one time when Rama is sitting in hermitage and heartily absorbed in telling narratives some demoness 
arrived at that place, fortuitously. [3-17-5]_END

B_3_C_11_67
BEGIN_
गम्यताम् इति तेन उक्तो जगाम रघु नन्दनः |यथा उद्दिष्टेन मार्गेण वनम् तत् च अवलोकयन् || ४-११-७३_END
BEGIN_
When the brother of Agastya said, "you may go," Rama the legatee of Raghu journeyed on the pathways 
as directed by Suteekshna, and on observing those woodlands. [4-11-73]_END

B_3_C_15_18
BEGIN_
ततः पुष्प बलिम् कृत्वा शान्तिम् च स यथाविधि |दर्शयामास रामाय तद् आश्रम पदम् कृतम् || ३-१५-२५_END
BEGIN_
Then making flowery offerings and peace-invocations also procedural to gR^iha 
pravesha , entering a new house,] started to show the constructed hermitage to Rama. [3-15-25]_END

B_3_C_14_28
BEGIN_
तस्मात् जातो अहम् अरुणात् संपातिः च मम अग्रजः |जटायुर् इति माम् विद्धि श्येनी पुत्रम् अरिंदम || 
३-१४-३३_END
BEGIN_
"Oh enemy-destroyer Rama, I took birth from that Aruna, the charioteer of Sun, and my elder brother 
Sampati too, hence know me as Jatayu, the son of Shyenii. [3-14-33]_END

B_3_C_16_10
BEGIN_
मृदु सूर्याः सनीहाराः पटु शीताः समारुताः |शून्य अरण्या हिम ध्वस्ता दिवसा भान्ति सांप्रतम् || ४-१६-११_END
BEGIN_
"Overwhelmed by snow presently the noontimes are with soft sun, with bitter cold, with mists and wintry 
breezes, and with them the forests too are bleak in their sheen. [4-16-11]_END

B_3_C_17_4
BEGIN_
सा तु शूर्पणखा नाम दशग्रीवस्य रक्षसः |भगिनी रामम् आसाद्य ददर्श त्रिदश उपमम् || ३-१७-६_END
BEGIN_
She is but the sister of ten-faced demon Ravana, Shuurpanakha by her name and she has seen him on reaching 
the paradisiacal being like Rama. [3-17-6]_END

B_3_C_11_68
BEGIN_
नीवारान् पनसान् सालान् वन्जुलान् तिनिशान् तथा |चिरि बिल्वान् मधूकान् च बिल्वान् अथ च तिन्दुकान् 
|| ४-११-७४_END
BEGIN_
On observing the wild grass that grows on its own giving wild grain, Jack-fruit trees, sala trees, Ashoka 
trees, lemons trees, saplings of bilva trees and also madhuka and bilva trees he journeyed. [4-11-74]_END

B_3_C_14_29
BEGIN_
सो अहम् वास सहायः ते भविष्यामि यदि इच्छ्हसि |इदम् दुर्गम् हि कान्तारम् मृग राक्षस सेवितम्सीताम् 
च तात रक्षिष्ये त्वयि याते सलक्ष्मणे || ३-१४-३४_END
BEGIN_
"Such as I am, I can be your helpmate at your residence if only you wish me to... oh, boy, this impassable 
forest is a beloved one to predators and demons, isn't it... as such I can take care of Seetha if you 
and Lakshmana go out..." Thus Jatayu said to Rama. [3-14-34]_END

B_3_C_15_19
BEGIN_
स तम् दृष्ट्वा कृतम् सौम्यम् आश्रमम् सह सीतया |राघवः पर्णशालायाम् हर्षम् आहारयत् परम् || ३-१५-२६_END
BEGIN_
On seeing the beautifully constructed hermitage along with Seetha, Rama is highly gladdened in respect 
that straw-cottage. [3-15-26]_END

B_3_C_16_11
BEGIN_
निवृत्त आकाश शयनाः पुष्यनीता हिम अरुणाः |शीता वृद्धतर आयामः त्रि यामा यान्ति सांप्रतम् || ४-१६-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Precluded is the reclining under open sky as the nights are led by the Pushya constellation, they will 
now be with brownish-grey fog and chilly, and prolonged are the lengths of nights whereby the three 
watches of night will be quickly slipping away._END

B_3_C_17_5
BEGIN_
दीप्तास्यम् च महाबाहुम् पद्म पत्रायत ईक्षणम् |गज विक्रांत गमनम् जटा मण्दल धारिणम् || ३-१७-७सुकुमारम् 
महा सत्त्वम् पार्थिव व्यंजन अन्वितम् |रामम् इन्दीवर श्यामम् कन्दर्प सदृश प्रभम् || ३-१७-८बभूव 
इन्द्रोपमम् दृष्ट्वा राक्षसी काम मोहिता |_END
BEGIN_
He whose face is radiant, arms lengthy, eyes large like lotus petals, stride like that of an elephant, 
wearing bunches of hair-tufts, delicate yet greatly vigorous, possessor of all kingly aspects, complexion 
deep-blue like blue lotus, similar to Love-god in brilliance and in simile to Indra, the demoness has 
seen such a Rama and became lovesick. [3-17-7, 8, 9a]_END

B_3_C_11_69
BEGIN_
पुष्पितान् पुष्पित अग्राभिर् लताभिर् उपशोभितान् |ददर्श रामः शतशः तत्र कान्तार पादपान् || ४-११-७५
हस्ति हस्तैः विमृदितान् वानरैः उपशोभितान् |मत्तैः शकुनि संघैः च शतशः प्रति नादितान् || ४-११-७६_END
BEGIN_
Rama has seen hundreds of flowered forest trees that are battered by the trunks of elephants, that are 
adorned with monkeys, reverberated by hundreds of lusty bird folks, and that are enriched by the flowered 
climbers whorled around them. [4-11-75, 76]_END

B_3_C_14_30
BEGIN_
जटायुषम् तु प्रतिपूज्य राघवोमुदा परिष्वज्य च सन्नतो अभवत् |पितुर् हि शुश्राव सखित्वम् आत्मवान्
जटायुषा संकथितम् पुनः पुनः || ३-१४-३५_END
BEGIN_
Raghava revered Jatayu in his turn by gladly hugging and stood by him with his head bent, and that kind-natured 
Rama is indeed regardful of the friendship of his father with Jatayu that is repeatedly said by Jatayu. 
[3-14-35]_END

B_3_C_15_20
BEGIN_
सुसंहृष्टः परिष्वज्य बाहुभ्याम् लक्ष्मणम् तदा |अति स्निग्धम् च गाढम् च वचनम् च इदम् अब्रवीत् || 
३-१५-२७_END
BEGIN_
Then Rama very highly gladdened Rama embraced Lakshmana tightly by both of his hands, and spoke these 
friendly words to him. [3-15-27]_END

B_3_C_16_12
BEGIN_
रवि संक्रान्त सौभाग्यः तुषार अरुण मण्डलः |निःश्वास अन्ध इव आदर्शाः चंद्रमा न प्रकाशते || ४-१६-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Transgressed is the destiny of moon by the sun as moon lost the chance of keeping people happy with 
his lustrousness in these days, thus the lustreless moon remained in a blushing sphere with fog, just 
like a mirror blinded by the fog of a suspire. [4-16-13]_END

B_3_C_17_6
BEGIN_
सुमुखम् दुर्मुखी रामम् वृत्त मध्यम् महोदरी || ३-१७-९विशालाक्षम् विरूपाक्षी सुकेशम् ताम्र मूर्धजा 
|प्रियरूपम् विरूपा सा सुस्वरम् भैरव स्वना || ३-१७-१०तरुणम् दारुणा वृद्धा दक्षिणम् वाम भाषिणी 
|न्याय वृत्तम् सुदुर्वृत्ता प्रियम् अप्रिय दर्शना || ३-१७-११शरीरज समाविष्टा राक्षसी रामम् अब्रवीत् 
|_END
BEGIN_
She that demoness who is facially unpleasant one with that pleasant faced one, pot bellied one with 
the slim-waisted one, wry-eyed one with the broad-eyed one, coppery-haired one with the neatly tressed 
one, ugly featured one with the charming featured one, brassy voiced one with the gentle voiced one, 
deplorably oldish one with the youngish one, crooked talker with the pleasant talker, ill-mannered one 
with the well-mannered one, uncouth one with couth, abominable one with amiable Rama spoke, besieged 
by Love-god. [3-17-9b, 11, 12a]_END

B_3_C_11_70
BEGIN_
ततो अब्रवीत् समीपस्थम् रामो राजीव लोचनः |पृष्ठतो अनुगतम् वीरम् लक्ष्मणम् लक्ष्मिवर्धनम् || ४-११-७७_END
BEGIN_
Then the lotus-eyed Rama said this to his follower Lakshmana who is a valiant and glory-enriching one 
and who is near at hand. [4-11-77]_END

B_3_C_14_31
BEGIN_
स तत्र सीताम् परिदाय मैथिलीम्सह एव तेन अतिबलेन पक्षिणा |जगाम ताम् पंचवटीम् सलक्ष्मणोरिपून् 
दिधक्षन् शलभान् इव अनलः || ३-१४-३६_END
BEGIN_
He that Rama took the princess from Mithila Seetha, and proceeded to Panchavati along with that very 
mighty bird and Lakshmana, as though to incinerate enemies, like fire that burns down grasshoppers. 
[3-14-36]_END

B_3_C_15_21
BEGIN_
प्रीतो अस्मि ते महत् कर्म त्वया कृतम् इदम् प्रभो |प्रदेयो यन् निमित्तम् ते परिष्व.ंगो मया कृतः || 
३-१५-२८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, masterful one, I am very happy about you for you have done a great deed, for that reason I am giving 
what I have to give to you a hugging. [3-5-28]_END

B_3_C_16_13
BEGIN_
ज्योत्स्ना तुषार मलिना पौर्णमास्याम् न राजते |सीता इव च आतप श्यामा लक्ष्यते न तु शोभते || ४-१६-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Even on a full moon day the moonlight is unbright blemished by mist, and it is appearing like brightly 
Seetha becoming swarthy by sun's heat, but not brightly. [4-16-14]_END

B_3_C_17_7
BEGIN_
जटी तापस रूपेण सभार्यः शर चाप धृक् || ३-१७-१२आगतः त्वम् इमम् देशम् कथम् राक्षस सेवितम् |किम् 
आगमन कृत्यम् ते तत् त्वम् आख्यातुम् अर्हसि || ३-१७-१३_END
BEGIN_
"You are an ascetic yet with a wife, handling bow and arrows yet in the appearance of a sage  what for 
you have come to this province frequented by demons  it will be apt of you to tell the purpose of your 
coming here, in actuality " [3-17-12b, 13]_END

B_3_C_11_71
BEGIN_
स्निग्ध पत्रा यथा वृक्षा यथा क्षान्ता मृग द्विजाः |आश्रमो न अतिदूरस्थो महर्षेर् भावित आत्मनः || 
४-११-७८_END
BEGIN_
"As to how the trees are appearing with velvety leaves, and as to how the animals and birds appear unwearied, 
thus gauging by this it appears that the hermitage of that contemplative soul Agastya is situated not 
very far from here. [4-11-78]_END

B_3_C_15_22
BEGIN_
भावज्ञेन कृतज्ञेन धर्मज्ञेन च लक्ष्मण |त्वया पुत्रेण धर्मात्मा न संवृत्तः पिता मम || ३-१५-२९_END
BEGIN_
"You are the knower of others feelings, knower of many skills, and the knower of what is right and honest, 
oh, Lakshmana, such as you are, being with you I deem that my virtue-souled father is not gone and forgotten. 
[3-15-29]_END

B_3_C_16_14
BEGIN_
प्रकृत्या शीतल स्पर्शो हिम विद्धाः च सांप्रतम् |प्रवाति पश्चिमो वायुः काले द्वि गुण शीतलः || ४-१६-१५_END
BEGIN_
"The western breeze by itself will be cool to touch, but presently charged with snow it is wafting doubly 
chilly in the early hours. [4-16-15]_END

B_3_C_17_8
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु राक्षस्या शूर्पणख्या परंतपः |ऋजु बुद्धितया सर्वम् आख्यातुम् उपचक्रमे || ३-१७-१४_END
BEGIN_
Thus asked by demoness Shuurpanakha that enemy-scorcher Rama started to inform all about it, straightforwardly. 
[3-17-14]_END

B_3_C_11_72
BEGIN_
अगस्त्य इति विख्यातो लोके स्वेन एव कर्मणा |आश्रमो दृश्यते तस्य परिश्रान्त श्रम अपहः || ४-११-७९_END
BEGIN_
"He who by his own deed is renowned in the world as Agastya, the stopper of mountain, it appears to 
be his hermitage that alleviates the weary of wearied ones. [4-11-79]_END

B_3_C_15_23
BEGIN_
एवम् लक्ष्मणम् उक्त्वा तु राघवो लक्ष्मिवर्धनः |तस्मिन् देशे बहु फले न्यवसत् स सुखम् सुखी || ३-१५-३०_END
BEGIN_
On saying thus to Lakshmana, Raghava, the enhancer of magnificence comfortably resided in that province 
which is with many a fruit. [3-15-30]_END

B_3_C_16_15
BEGIN_
बाष्प च्छ्हन्नानि अरण्यानि यव गोधूमवंति च |शोभन्ते अभ्युदिते सूर्ये नदद्भिः क्रौन्च सारसैः || ४-१६-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Covered with the dew the forests that already covered with crop fields of barley and wheat are beaming 
forth, together with the callings of waterfowls, at the rise of the sun. [4-16-16]_END

B_3_C_17_9
BEGIN_
आसीत् दशरथो नाम राजा त्रिदश विक्रमः |तस्य अहम् अग्रजः पुत्रो रामो नाम जनैः श्रुतः || ३-१७-१५_END
BEGIN_
"A king named Dasharatha was there with his godlike valour, I am his eldest son, and people hear of 
me by name Rama. [3-17-15]_END

B_3_C_11_73
BEGIN_
प्राज्य धूम आकुल वनः चीर माला परिष्कृतः |प्रशान्त मृग यूथः च नाना शकुनि नादितः || ४-११-८०_END
BEGIN_
"The forest nearby this hermitage is overrun by huge smoke from altars of fire, overstuffed with the 
garlands of jute cloth, overcrowded with the herds of peaceful deer, and also overloaded with sonority 
of the birds. [4-11-80]_END

B_3_C_15_24
BEGIN_
कंचित् कालम् स धर्मात्मा सीतया लक्ष्मणेन चअन्वास्यमानो न्यवसत् स्वर्ग लोके यथा अमरः || ३-१५-३१_END
BEGIN_
While Seetha and Lakshmana devoted themselves to that righteous Rama, he resided in Panchavati like 
a Divinity in heavenly world for sometime to come. [3-15-30]_END

B_3_C_16_16
BEGIN_
खर्जूर पुष्प आकृतिभिः शिरोभिः पूर्ण तण्डुलैः |शोभन्ते किंचिद् आलंबाः शालयः कनक प्रभाः || ४-१६-१७_END
BEGIN_
"The paddy crops in fields are gleaming forth with golden lustre, and their heads full with grain and 
a little bent down are shapely like the flowers of date-fruit. [4-16-17]_END

B_3_C_17_10
BEGIN_
भ्राता अयम् लक्ष्मणो नाम यवीयान् माम् अनुव्रतः |इयम् भार्या च वैदेही मम सीतेति विश्रुता || ३-१७-१६_END
BEGIN_
"He is Lakshmana by his name, my younger brother and a devoted follower of mine, and she is my wife, 
daughter of Videha's king, well-known as Seetha. [3-17-16]_END

B_3_C_11_74
BEGIN_
निगृह्य तरसा मृत्युम् लोकानाम् हित काम्यया |दक्षिणा दिक् कृता येन शरण्या पुण्य कर्मणा || ४-११-८१_END
BEGIN_
"He who impeding death by his yogic might and wishing well-being for worlds made this southern extent 
a liveable province by his pious deeds, his hermitage is this. [4-11-81]_END

B_3_C_16_17
BEGIN_
मयूखैः उपसर्पद्भिः हिम नीहार संवृतैः |दूरम् अभ्युदितः सूर्यः शशांक इव लक्ष्यते || ४-१६-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Though he came up long back, and though his beams are spreading around, besieged by snowy mist the 
sun is appearing as moon. [4-16-18]_END

B_3_C_17_11
BEGIN_
नियोगात् तु नरेन्द्रस्य पितुर् मातुः च यंत्रितः |धर्मार्थम् धर्मकांक्षी च वनम् वस्तुम् इह आगतः || 
३-१७-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Desiring to implement the probity in following father's orders and for the sake of establishing probity 
in living an ascetic's life I have come here to forests to dwell, as enjoined by the directives of the 
king and my father, and by my mother, as well. [3-17-17]_END

B_3_C_11_75
BEGIN_
तस्य इदम् आश्रम पदम् प्रभावाद् यस्य राक्षसैः |दिक् इयम् दक्षिणा त्रासाद् दृश्यते न उपभुज्यते || 
४-११-८२_END
BEGIN_
"Under whose influence the demons behold this southern quarter appallingly, and they do not even venture 
to live here, such a sage Agastya's hermitage is this. [4-11-82]_END

B_3_C_16_18
BEGIN_
अग्राह्य वीर्यः पूर्वाह्णे मध्याह्ने स्पर्शतः सुखः |संरक्तः किंचिद् आपाण्डुः आतपः शोभते क्षितौ || 
४-१६-१९_END
BEGIN_
Inappreciable is the warmth of sun in the mornings, but comfortable for touch at noontimes, since the 
reddish but a little palish sunshine is radiating on earth. [4-16-19]_END

B_3_C_17_12
BEGIN_
त्वाम् तु वेदितुम् इच्छ्हामि कस्य त्वम् का असि कस्य वा |त्वम् हि तावन्मनोज्ञा.ंगी राक्षसी प्रतिभासि 
मे || ३-१७-१८_END
BEGIN_
"I too wish to know about you. Whose wife are you? What is your name? Or, whose daughter are you? By 
the way, you are with a most enthralling personality, and then you must be a demoness. [3-17-18]_END

B_3_C_11_76
BEGIN_
यदा प्रभृति च आक्रान्ता दिग् इयम् पुण्य कर्मणा |तदा प्रभृति निर् वैराः प्रशान्ता रजनी चराः || ४-११-८३_END
BEGIN_
"And from when that pious deeded Agastya took possession of this quarter, from then on the night walkers 
are calmed down and remained without feud. [4-11-83]_END

B_3_C_16_19
BEGIN_
अवश्याय निपातेन किंचित् प्रक्लिन्न शाद्वला |वनानाम् शोभते भूमिर् निविष्ट तरुण आतपा || ४-१६-२०_END
BEGIN_
"The pasturelands are a little moistened with the fall of dewdrops, but the fields of forest are enlivened 
by the radiance of tender sun's warmth. [4-16-20]_END

B_3_C_17_13
BEGIN_
इह वा किम् निमित्तम् त्वम् आगता ब्रूहि तत्त्वतः |सा अब्रवीत् वचनम् श्रुत्वा राक्षसी मदन अर्दिता 
|| ३-१७-१९_END
BEGIN_
"What for you have come, either, you tell in actuality..." Thus Rama asked her. On hearing the words 
of Rama she that demoness wetted with love said these words. [3-17-19]_END

B_3_C_11_77
BEGIN_
नाम्ना च इयम् भगवतो दक्षिणा दिक् प्रदक्षिणा |प्रथिता त्रिषु लोकेषु दुर्धर्षा क्रूर कर्मभिः || ४-११-८४_END
BEGIN_
"This very worthy southern quarter is known in the name of that godly saint Agastya and this remained 
unattackable to the demons with cruel deeds. [4-11-84]_END

B_3_C_16_20
BEGIN_
स्पृशन् तु सुविपुलम् शीतम् उदकम् द्विरदः सुखम् |अत्यन्त तृषितो वन्यः प्रतिसंहरते करम् || ४-१६-२१_END
BEGIN_
"On easily touching very clear and cold water with its very broad trunk that intensely thirsty wild 
elephant is backing away its trunk for the water is that cold. [4-16-21]_END

B_3_C_17_14
BEGIN_
श्रूयताम् राम वक्ष्यामि तत्त्वार्थम् वचनम् मम |अहम् शूर्पणखा नाम राक्षसी कामरूपिणी || ३-१७-२०
अरण्यम् विचरामि इदम् एका सर्व भयंकरा |_END
BEGIN_
"I will tell you truth, Rama, nothing but truth, I am a guise-changing demoness named Shuurpanakha, 
and I will be freely moving in this forest in a solitary manner and unnerving all. [3-17-20, 21a]_END

B_3_C_11_78
BEGIN_
मार्गम् निरोद्धुम् सततम् भास्करस्य अचल उत्तमः |संदेशम् पालयन् तस्य विंध्य शैलो न वर्धते || ४-११-८५
अयम् दीर्घ आयुषः तस्य लोके विश्रुत कर्मणः |अगस्त्यस्य आश्रमः श्रीमान् विनीत मृग सेवितः || ४-११-८६_END
BEGIN_
"Complying which sage's directive Mt. Vindhya ceased to heighten in order not to obstruct the path of 
the sun, such sage's hermitage is this who is renowned in the world by his deeds and whose longevity 
is inestimable, hence this glorious hermitage is adored by well-behaved animals and humans as well. 
[4-11-85, 86]_END

B_3_C_16_21
BEGIN_
एते हि समुपासीना विहगा जलचारिणः |न अवगाहन्ति सलिलम् अप्रगल्भा इव आवहम् || ४-१६-२२_END
BEGIN_
"These waterfowls that are sitting nearby are not entering into waters like cowards not entering battlefields. 
[4-16-22]_END

B_3_C_17_15
BEGIN_
रावणो नाम मे भ्राता यदि ते श्रोत्रम् आगतः || ३-१७-२१वीरो विश्रवसः पुत्रो यदि ते श्रोत्रम् आगतः |_END
BEGIN_
"My brother is valorous and mighty Ravana, the king of demons and the son of Vishravasa, if ever you 
have heard of him. [3-17-21b, 22a]_END

B_3_C_11_79
BEGIN_
एष लोक अर्चितः साधुः हिते नित्यम् रतः सताम् |अस्मान् अधिगतान् एष श्रेयसा योजयिष्यति || ४-११-८७_END
BEGIN_
"He that gentle sage who is always interested in the respect of sagacious ones is thus an esteemed one 
in the world, and for us when we approach him he accords beneficence. [4-11-87]_END

B_3_C_16_22
BEGIN_
अवश्याय तमो नद्धा नीहार तमसा आवृताः |प्रसुप्ता इव लक्ष्यन्ते विपुष्पा वन राजयः || ४-१६-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Subdued by snowy darkness, enclosed in misty gloom, and reft of flowers these forest ranges appear 
like those that are asleep. [4-16-23]_END

B_3_C_17_16
BEGIN_
प्रवृद्ध निद्रः च सदा कुंभकर्णो महाबलः || ३-१७-२२विभीषणः तु धर्मात्मा न तु राक्षस चेष्टितः |
प्रख्यात वीर्यौ च रणे भ्रातरौ खर दूषणौ || ३-१७-२३_END
BEGIN_
"And the mighty Kumbhakarna who will always be in profound sleep is my brother, and the virtue-souled 
Vibheeshana too is my brother, but he does not behave like a demon, and two more bothers of mine are 
Khara and Duushana who are renowned for their bravery in war. [3-17-22b, 23_END

B_3_C_11_80
BEGIN_
आराधयिष्यामि अत्र अहम् अगस्त्यम् तम् महामुनिम् |शेषम् च वन वासस्य सौम्य वत्स्यामि अहम् प्रभो || 
४-११-८८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, adept Lakshmana, I wish to worship that great saint Agastya therein that hermitage, and oh, gentle 
one, I think of living the remainder of forest living here only. [4-11-88]_END

B_3_C_16_23
BEGIN_
बाष्प संचन्न सलिला रुत विज्ञेय सारसाः |हिमाअर्द्र वालुकैः तीरैः सरितो भान्ति सांप्रतम् || ४-१६-२४_END
BEGIN_
"Now the rivers are imperceptible as their water is overspread with dewdrops, but their water-birds 
are perceptible only by their callings, thus making that river perceptible, and such rivers are now 
glistening with moist sandbanks and shores. [4-16-24]_END

B_3_C_17_17
BEGIN_
तान् अहम् समतिक्रान्ता राम त्वा पूर्व दर्शनात् |समुपेता अस्मि भावेन भर्तारम् पुरुषोत्तमम् || ३-१७-२४_END
BEGIN_
"I can excel all of them by my bravery, oh, Rama, and on seeing you for the first time I had a notion 
that you being the choicest among men you alone are my husband, hence I neared you. [3-17-24]_END

B_3_C_11_81
BEGIN_
अत्र देवाः सगन्धर्वाः सिद्धाः च परम ऋषयः |अगस्त्यम् नियत आहाराः सततम् पर्युपासते || ४-११-८९_END
BEGIN_
"There gods with gandharva-s, siddha-s, exalted sages will be worshipping Agastya who is self-regulating 
self-disciplinary. [4-11-89]_END

B_3_C_16_24
BEGIN_
तुषार पतनात् चैव मृदुत्वात् भास्करस्य च |शैत्यात् अग अग्रस्थम् अपि प्रायेण रसवत् जलम् || ४-१६-२५_END
BEGIN_
"Owing to the fall of snow, further owing to the softness and coldness of sun, the water deep down the 
wells is generally agreeable for drinking. [4-16-25]_END

B_3_C_17_18
BEGIN_
अहम् प्रभाव संपन्ना स्वच्छ्हंद बल गामिनी |चिराय भव भर्ता मे सीतया किम् करिष्यसि || ३-१७-२५_END
BEGIN_
"I am endowed with such preponderances and I can operate with my independent might, as such you become 
my everlasting husband  by the way, what can you bring off with Seetha. [3-17-25]_END

B_3_C_11_82
BEGIN_
न अत्र जीवेत् मृषावादी क्रूरो वा यदि वा शठः |नृशंसः पाप वृत्तो वा मुनिः एष तथा विधः || ४-११-९०_END
BEGIN_
"There no liar can live, nor a savage, nor even a deceiver, nor a man-torturer, nor one with sinful 
behaviour, for that sage is of that nature. [4-11-90]_END

B_3_C_16_25
BEGIN_
जरा जर्जरितैः पत्रैः शीर्ण केसर कर्णिकैः |नाल शेषा हिम ध्वस्ता न भान्ति कमलाकराः || ४-१६-२६_END
BEGIN_
"Lotus lakes are left alone with stalks of lotuses as their petals are aged and withered, decrepit are 
the fibrils and carpels, thus impaired by cold they are ungracious in look. [4-16-26]_END

B_3_C_17_19
BEGIN_
विकृता च विरूपा च न सा इयम् सदृशी तव |अहम् एव अनुरूपा ते भार्या रूपेण पश्य माम् || ३-१७-२६_END
BEGIN_
"Unlovely and unshapely is this one, such as she is, this Seetha is unworthy to be your wife, and I 
am the lone one worthy to be your wife, hence treat me as your wife. [3-17-26]_END

B_3_C_11_83
BEGIN_
अत्र देवाः च यक्षाः च नागाः च पतगैः सह |वसन्ति नियत आहारा धर्मम् आराधयिष्णवः || ४-११-९१_END
BEGIN_
"There the gods, celestials, reptiles, birds live together wishing to worship the Absolute with self-discipline. 
[4-11-91]_END

B_3_C_16_26
BEGIN_
अस्मिन् तु पुरुषव्याघ्र काले दुःख समन्वितः |तपश्चरति धर्मात्मा त्वत् भक्त्या भरतः पुरे || ४-१६-२७_END
BEGIN_
"But during this time, oh, manly-tiger, ushered by anguish that virtue souled one Bharata must be practising 
ascesis in city with adoration to you. [4-16-27]_END

B_3_C_17_20
BEGIN_
इमाम् विरूपाम् असतीम् करालाम् निर्णत उदरीम् |अनेन सह ते भ्रात्रा भक्षयिष्यामि मानुषीम् || ३-१७-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Shall I eat up this disfigured, dishonest, diabolical human female with a hallow stomach along with 
him, that brother of yours to make you free._END

B_3_C_18_0
BEGIN_
ताम् तु शूर्पणखाम् रामः काम पाश अवपाशिताम् |स्वच्छ्हया श्लक्ष्णया वाचा स्मित पूर्वम् अथ अब्रवीत् 
|| ३-१८-१_END
BEGIN_
Rama then voicing clearly and softly spoke to her, whom the noose of lust has tethered down, with a 
smile preceding his words. [3-18-1]_END

B_3_C_11_84
BEGIN_
अत्र सिद्धा महात्मानो विमानैः सूर्य सन्निभैः |त्यक्त्वा देहान् नवैर् देहैः स्वर् याताः परम ऋषयः 
|| ४-११-९२_END
BEGIN_
"There the blest and great souls of accomplished ascesis rode to heavens by aircrafts similar to sun 
in resplendence, on relinquishing their mortal bodies here and on obtaining new bodies. [4-11-92]_END

B_3_C_16_27
BEGIN_
त्यक्त्वा राज्यम् च मानम् च भोगांश्च विविधान् बहून् |तपस्वी नियताहारः शेते शीते महीतले || ४-१६-२८_END
BEGIN_
"On forsaking kingdom and pride of becoming the king of Ayodhya as well, and varied and various pleasures 
too, he is in self-denial, and with his food regulated he sleeps on chilly surface of earth. [4-16-28]_END

B_3_C_17_21
BEGIN_
ततः पर्वत शृ.ंगाणि वनानि विविधानि च |पश्यन्सहमयाकामीदण्डकान्विचरिष्यसि - यद्वा -पश्यन् सह मया 
कामी दण्डकान् विचरिष्यसि || ३-१७-२८_END
BEGIN_
"Afterwards, you can lustily ramble about Dandaka forest along with me while enjoying yourself on various 
mountaintops in the sky and in forests on the earth." So Shuurpanakha said to Rama. [3-17-28]_END

B_3_C_18_1
BEGIN_
कृत दारो अस्मि भवति भार्या इयम् दयिता मम |त्वत् विधानाम् तु नारीणाम् सुदुःखा ससपत्नता || ३-१८-२_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, honourable one, I am married and this is my dear wife, thus it will be distressing for your sort 
of females to live with a co-wife. [3-18-2]_END

B_3_C_11_85
BEGIN_
यक्षत्वम् अमरत्वम् च राज्यानि विविधानि च |अत्र देवाः प्रयच्छ्हन्ति भूतैः आराधिताः शुभैः || ४-११-९३_END
BEGIN_
"There gods will endow the state of celestials or immortals, or many realms of divine living to those 
auspicious beings that worship them. [4-11-93]_END

B_3_C_16_28
BEGIN_
सोऽपि वेलाम् इमाम् नूनम् अभिषेक अर्थम् उद्यतः |वृतः प्रकृतिभिर् नित्यम् प्रयाति सरयूम् नदीम् || 
४-१६-२९_END
BEGIN_
"Even he might always be getting up at this time of the day and proceeding to River Sarayu for a bath 
surrounded by ministers, definite is that. [4-16-29]_END

B_3_C_17_22
BEGIN_
इति एवम् उक्तः काकुत्स्थः प्रहस्य मदिर ईक्षणाम् |इदम् वचनम् आरेभे वक्तुम् वाक्य विशारदः || ३-१७-२९_END
BEGIN_
When he is said that way Rama chuckled and that wordsmith started to reply her who eyes are besotted 
in lovesickness with this sentence. [3-17-29]_END

B_3_C_18_2
BEGIN_
अनुजः तु एष मे भ्राता शीलवान् प्रिय दर्शनः |श्रीमान् अकृत दारः च लक्ष्मणो नाम वीर्यवान् || ३-१८-३_END
BEGIN_
"He is my younger brother named Lakshmana, he is with a good conduct, good looking, a promising and 
valiant one, and he is without a wife. [3-18-3]_END

B_3_C_11_86
BEGIN_
आगताः स्म आश्रम पदम् सौमित्रे प्रविश अग्रतः |निवेदय इह माम् प्राप्तम् ऋषये सह सीतया || ४-११-९४_END
BEGIN_
"We arrived at the threshold of the hermitage, oh, Soumitri, you enter firstly and submit to Sage Agastya 
about my arrival at this place along with Seetha. [4-11-94]_END

B_3_C_16_29
BEGIN_
अत्यन्त सुख संवृद्धः सुकुमारो हिमार्दितः |कथम् तु अपर रात्रेषु सरयूम् अवगाहते || ४-१६-३०_END
BEGIN_
"But how can he who is brought up in high comfort, a delicate one too, enter the cold-wet waters of 
River Sarayu, in these small hours. [4-16-30]_END

B_3_C_18_3
BEGIN_
अपूर्वी भार्यया च अर्थी तरुणः प्रिय दर्शनः |अनुरूपः च ते भर्ता रूपस्य अस्य भविष्यति || ३-१८-४_END
BEGIN_
"He is without a wife and in need of a wife  he is youthful, good-looking and he can become a fitly 
husband of yours, fit enough to your kind of features. [3-18-4]_END

B_3_C_16_30
BEGIN_
पद्मपत्रेक्षणः श्यामः श्रीमान् निरुदरो महान् |धर्मज्ञः सत्यवादी च ह्री निषेधो जितेन्द्रियः || ४-१६-३१
प्रियाभिभाषी मधुरो दीर्घबाहुः अरिन्दमः |संत्यज्य विविधान् भोगान् आर्यम् सर्वात्मना आश्रितः || ४-१६-३२_END
BEGIN_
"That lotus-petal eyed one with blue-black complexion is an imposing one with lion-like waist, being 
the noblest he is knower of dharma thus an advocate of truth, and thus intolerant of ignominy, and as 
a self-restrained one he talks dearly and sweetly, and he is dextrous and an enemy-destroyer, such as 
he is, that Bharata on forgoing all of his various pleasures he is devoted to you, as you alone are 
his adorable brother. [4-16-31, 32]_END

B_3_C_18_4
BEGIN_
एनम् भज विशालाक्षि भर्तारम् भ्रातरम् मम |असपत्ना वरारोहे मेरुम् अर्क प्रभा यथा || ३-१८-५_END
BEGIN_
"You woo him, oh, board-eyed [bulged-eyed] one, this brother of mine as your husband like sunshine seeking 
the Mt. Meru, then oh, great-waisted [pot-bellied] one, you will be without a co-wife " So said Rama 
to that demoness. [3-18-5]_END

B_3_C_16_31
BEGIN_
जितः स्वर्गः तव भ्रात्रा भरतेन महात्मना |वनस्थम् अपि तापस्ये यः त्वाम् अनुविधीयते || ४-१६-३३_END
BEGIN_
"Even though you are in forests far away from him, he is following you in the practise of austerities, 
and such a brother of yours, that great-souled Bharata has refused ascent to heaven. [4-16-33]_END

B_3_C_18_5
BEGIN_
इति रामेण सा प्रोक्ता राक्षसी काम मोहिता |विसृज्य रामम् सहसा ततो लक्ष्मणम् अब्रवीत् || ३-१८-६_END
BEGIN_
When Rama clearly told that way to that demoness dazed in lust, discarding Rama quickly then she spoke 
to Lakshmana. [3-18-6]_END

B_3_C_19_0
BEGIN_
ताम् तथा पतिताम् दृष्ट्वा विरूपाम् शोणित उक्षिताम् |भगिनीम् क्रोध संतप्तः खरः पप्रच्छ्ह राक्षसः 
|| ३-१९-१_END
BEGIN_
On seeing her who fell before him in a misshapen and blood-soaked condition, demon Khara is all stewed 
up and asked her. [3-19-1]_END

B_3_C_16_32
BEGIN_
न पित्र्यम् अनुवर्न्तन्ते मातृकम् द्विपदा इति |ख्यातो लोक प्रवादो अयम् भरतेन अन्यथा कृतः || ४-१६-३४_END
BEGIN_
"  Humans do not derive father's attitude but they take of their mothers' is the well-know maxim in 
the world, but Bharata rendered it otherwise. [4-16-34]_END

B_3_C_18_6
BEGIN_
अस्य रूपस्य ते युक्ता भार्या अहम् वरवर्णिनी |मया सह सुखम् सर्वान् दण्डकान् विचरिष्यसि || ३-१८-७_END
BEGIN_
"I with my best complexion will be your deserving wife meetly to you charm, you can happily take a jaunt 
all over Dandaka forest along with me." So Shuurpanakha ran after Lakshmana. [3-18-7]_END

B_3_C_19_1
BEGIN_
उत्तिष्ठ तावत् आख्याहि प्रमोहम् जहि संभ्रमम् |व्यक्तम् आख्याहि केन त्वम् एवम् रूपा विरूपिता || ३-१९-२_END
BEGIN_
"Rise up, first tell me clearly putting away your flurry and fluster, who disfigured your form in this 
way. [3-19-2]_END

B_3_C_16_33
BEGIN_
भर्ता दशरथो यस्याः साधुः च भरतः सुतः |कथम् नु सा अम्बा कैकेयी तादृशी क्रूरदर्शिनी || ४-१६-३५_END
BEGIN_
"Whose husband is Dasharatha and whose son is gentle Bharata, how then can she, our mother Kaikeyi, 
is with this sort of cruel disposition, indeed " Thus Lakshmana spoke to Rama on their way to River 
Godavari. [4-16-35]_END

B_3_C_18_7
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु सौमित्री राक्षस्या वाक्य कोविदः |ततः शूर्पणखीम् स्मित्वा लक्ष्मणो युक्तम् अब्रवीत् 
|| ३-१८-८_END
BEGIN_
Thus said by the demoness that meaningful sentence maker Lakshmana, the son of Sumitra, then smiled 
and appropriately replied Shuurpanakha. [3-18-8]_END

B_3_C_19_2
BEGIN_
कः कृष्ण सर्पम् असीनम् आशी विषम नागसम् |तुदति अभिसमापन्नम् अ.ंगुलि अग्रेण लीलया || ३-१९-३_END
BEGIN_
"Who for sport is poking his fingertip at a venomously fanged black-cobra that has chanced in his close 
proximity but slouching down inoffensively. [3-19-3]_END

B_3_C_16_34
BEGIN_
इति एवम् लक्ष्मणे वाक्यम् स्नेहात् वदति धर्मिके |परिवादम् जनन्यः तम् असहन् राघवो अब्रवीत् || ४-१६-३६_END
BEGIN_
When that upright Lakshmana is speaking those words that way out of his fondness towards Rama, Raghava 
spoke to Lakshmana, intolerant of that slanderous talk about their mother. [4-16-36]_END

B_3_C_18_8
BEGIN_
कथम् दासस्य मे दासी भार्या भवितुम् इच्छ्हसि |सो अहम् आर्येण परवान् भ्रात्रा कमल वर्णिनी || ३-१८-९_END
BEGIN_
"How you wish to become a female servant, oh, [black] lotus-coloured one, by becoming the wife of a 
servant like me? I am just a vassal of my adorable brother. [3-18-9]_END

B_3_C_19_3
BEGIN_
काल पाशम् समासज्य कण्ठे मोहात् न जानते |यः त्वाम् अद्य समासाद्य पीतवान् विषम् उत्तमम् || ३-१९-४_END
BEGIN_
"Who on harrowing you is now heedless about his gulping a deadly poison, or about his foolish bracing 
the noose of Time around his own neck. [3-19-4]_END

B_3_C_16_35
BEGIN_
न ते अम्बा मध्यमा तात गर्हितव्या कथंचन |ताम् एव इक्ष्वाकु नाथस्य भरतस्य कथाम् कुरु || ४-१६-३७_END
BEGIN_
"In any way, dear Lakshmana, you are not supposed to deplore another mother of ours, but you go on telling 
the topics of Bharata, the king of Ikshvaku-s. [4-16-37]_END

B_3_C_18_9
BEGIN_
समृद्ध अर्थस्य सिद्धार्था मुदित अमल वर्णिनी |आर्यस्य त्वम् विशालाक्षि भार्या भव यवीयसी || ३-१८--१०_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, goggle eyed one, befitting to your complexion that is un-stainable further you better become the 
wife of my brother Rama who is abounding in means, and on becoming the younger wife of that adorable 
one, you too will achieve your means and thus you will be happy. [3-18-10]_END

B_3_C_19_4
BEGIN_
बल विक्रम संपन्ना कामगा काम रूपिणी |इमाम् अवस्थाम् नीता त्वम् केन अंतक समा गता || ३-१९-५_END
BEGIN_
"You are gifted with boldness and braveness, a whimsical rover, a guise changer by your wish, a coequal 
of Terminator, but to whom you have gone and by whom you are led into this kind of plight. [3-19-5]_END

B_3_C_16_36
BEGIN_
