निश्चिता एव हि मे बुद्धिः वन वासे दृढ व्रता |भरत स्नेह संतप्ता बालिशी क्रियते पुनः || ४-१६-३८_END
BEGIN_
"My mind is indeed set to dwell only in forest, and it is firmly avowed, but while yearning for Bharata's 
fellowship my fascination to reunite with him is recurring again. [4-16-38]_END

B_3_C_18_10
BEGIN_
एनाम् विरूपाम् असतीम् करालाम् निर्णत उदरीम् |भार्याम् वृद्धाम् परित्यज्य त्वाम् एव एष भजिष्यति || 
३-१८-११_END
BEGIN_
"On discarding her who is disfigured, dishonest, diabolically deleterious old wife with a hallow stomach 
that Rama will adore you alone. [3-18-11]_END

B_3_C_19_5
BEGIN_
देव गन्धर्व भूतानाम् ऋषीणाम् च महात्मनाम् |को अयम् एवम् महावीर्यः त्वाम् विरूपाम् चकार ह || ३-१९-६_END
BEGIN_
"Who is that kind of highly intrepid warper, either from gods, or from celestials or from high-souled 
sages who indeed rendered you shapeless. [3-19-6]_END

B_3_C_16_37
BEGIN_
संस्मरामि अस्य वाक्यानि प्रियाणि मधुराणि च |हृद्यानि अमृत कल्पानि मनः प्रह्लादानि च || ४-१६-३९_END
BEGIN_
"I reminisce his words well, that are genial, sweet, heartily, ambrosial and that will gladden the heart. 
[4-16-39]_END

B_3_C_19_6
BEGIN_
न हि पश्यामि अहम् लोके यः कुर्यात् मम विप्रियम् |अमरेषु सहस्राक्षम् महएन्द्रम् पाकशासनम् || ३-१९-७_END
BEGIN_
"Indeed, I do not find anyone who causes displeasure to me in this world, even among divinities including 
the thousand eyed Indra, the controller of demon Paaka. [3-19-7]_END

B_3_C_18_11
BEGIN_
को हि रूपम् इदम् श्रेष्ठम् संत्यज्य वरवर्णिनि |मानुषेषु वरारोहे कुर्यात् भावम् विचक्षणः || ३-१८-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, best complexioned one with best waist, is there any wiseacre to simply discard your kind of best 
personality, indeed, in preference to human females?" Lakshmana said so to Shuurpanakha. [3-18-12]_END

B_3_C_20_0
BEGIN_
ततः शूर्पणखा घोरा राघव आश्रमम् आगता |रक्षसान् आचचक्षे तौ भ्रातरौ सह सीतया || ३-२०-१_END
BEGIN_
Then on arriving at Raghava's hermitage that ghastly Shuurpanakha has shown the brothers, Rama and Lakshmana, 
along with Seetha to the fourteen demons. [3-20-1]_END

B_3_C_16_38
BEGIN_
कदा हि अहम् समेष्यामि भरतेन महात्मना |शत्रुघ्नेन च वीरेण त्वया च रघुनंदन || ४-१६-४०_END
BEGIN_
"When can I really reunite, oh, Lakshmana, with great-souled Bharata, valorous Shatrughna, and with 
you and Seetha." Thus said Rama to Lakshmana. [4-16-40]_END

B_3_C_19_7
BEGIN_
अद्य अहम् मार्गणैः प्राणान् आदास्ये जीवितांतगैः |सलिले क्षीरम् आसक्तम् निष्पिबन् इव सारसः || ३-१९-८_END
BEGIN_
"Now, I will take away the lives of that miscreant with my arrows that are terminators of lives, as 
a swan would drink milk to dregs even if it is mingled in water, duly separating milk from water. [3-19-8]_END

B_3_C_18_12
BEGIN_
इति सा लक्ष्मणेन उक्ता कराला निर्णतोदरी |मन्यते तत् वचः सत्यम् परिहास अविचक्षणा || ३-१८-१३_END
BEGIN_
Thus said by Lakshmana that despicable one with slouching stomach Shuurpanakha presumed those words 
to be truthful, for she is equivocal of that equivoque. [3-18-13]_END

B_3_C_20_1
BEGIN_
ते रामम् पर्ण शालायाम् उपविष्टम् महाबलम् |ददृशुः सीतया सार्धम् लक्ष्मणेन अपि सेवितम् || ३-२०-२_END
BEGIN_
They have seen the great-mighty Rama seated in the thatched cottage along with Seetha and Lakshmana 
attending to him. [3-20-2]_END

B_3_C_16_39
BEGIN_
इति एवम् विलपन् तत्र प्राप्य गोदावरीम् नदीम् |चक्रे अभिषेकम् काकुत्स्थः सानुजः सह सीतया || ४-१६-४१_END
BEGIN_
Thus worrying that way while proceeding, there Rama reached River Godavari and performed bathing with 
his younger brother Lakshmana and along with Seetha. [4-16-41]_END

B_3_C_19_8
BEGIN_
निहतस्य मया संख्ये शर संकृत्त मर्मणः |सफेनम् रुधिरम् कस्य मेदिनी पातुम् इच्छ्हसि || ३-१९-९_END
BEGIN_
"Whose frothy blood is it that the earth wishes to quaff when I cut off his crucial organs by my arrows 
and drop him dead in a combat. [3-19-9]_END

B_3_C_18_13
BEGIN_
सा रामम् पर्णशालायाम् उपविष्टम् परंतपम् |सीतया सह दुर्धर्षम् अब्रवीत् काम मोहिता || ३-१८-१४_END
BEGIN_
She who is fuddle by lust said to that unassailable enemy scorcher Rama who is sitting in the cottage 
along with Seetha. [3-18-14]_END

B_3_C_20_2
BEGIN_
ताम् दृष्ट्वा राघवः श्रीमान् आगताम् ताम् च राक्षसीम् |अब्रवीत् भ्रातरम् रामो लक्ष्मणम् दीप्त तेजसम् 
|| ३-२०-३_END
BEGIN_
On seeing the arrival of the demons, and the demoness Shuurpanakha too, that magnificent Rama of Raghava 
dynasty said to the radiantly brilliant Lakshmana. [3-20-3]_END

B_3_C_16_40
BEGIN_
तर्पयित्वा अथ सलिलैः तैः पितॄन् दैवतानि च |स्तुवन्ति स्म उदितम् सूर्यम् देवताअः च तथा अनघाः|| ४-१६-४२_END
BEGIN_
Then on offering water oblations to manes and gods that impeccant trinity extolled the rising sun and 
gods likewise. [4-16-42]_END

B_3_C_19_9
BEGIN_
कस्य पत्ररथाः कायात् मांसम् उत्कृत्य संगताः |प्रहृष्टा भक्षयिष्यन्ति निहतस्य मया रणे || ३-१९-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Whose body is it from which birds pressing round gladly wish to wring flesh to pieces for eating when 
I slay him in war. [3-19-10]_END

B_3_C_18_14
BEGIN_
इमाम् विरूपाम् असतीम् करालाम् निर्णतोदरीम् |वृद्धाम् भार्याम् अवष्टभ्य न माम् त्वम् बहु मन्यसे 
|| ३-१८-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Tenacious of her who is disfigured, dishonest, diabolical, hallow-stomached old wife of yours you are 
not regarding me high. [3-18-15]_END

B_3_C_20_3
BEGIN_
मुहूर्तम् भव सौमित्रे सीतायाः प्रत्यनंतरः |इमान् अस्या वधिष्यामि पदवीम् आगतान् इह || ३-२०-४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Soumitri, briefly tarry at the close of Seetha as I wish to eliminate these demons who have trailed 
the path of that demoness to here. [3-20-4]_END

B_3_C_16_41
BEGIN_
कृताभिषेकः स रराज रामःसीता द्वितीयः सह लक्ष्मणेन |कृत अभिषेको तु अग राज पुत्र्यारुद्रः स 
नन्दिः भगवान् इव ईशः || ४-१६-४३_END
BEGIN_
On taking bath in the river along with Seetha and Lakshmana, Rama shone forth like All-controlling god 
Rudra, who will be radiant on taking bath along with his consort Paarvati and with his follower Nandi, 
the Holy Bull. [4-16-43]_END

B_3_C_19_10
BEGIN_
तम् न देवा न गंधर्वा न पिशाचा न राक्षसाः |मया अपकृष्टम् कृपणम् शक्ताः त्रातुम् इह आहवे || ३-१९-११_END
BEGIN_
"Now, when I haul him easily on the ground in a battle that villain will be unredeemable either by gods, 
celestials, evil spirits, or by demons. [3-19-11]_END

B_3_C_18_15
BEGIN_
अद्य इमाम् भक्षयिष्यामि पश्यतः तव मानुषीम् |त्वया सह चरिष्यामि निःसपत्ना यथा सुखम् || ३-१८-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Now I wish to eat up this human female right before your very eyes, and then I can blithely make merry 
along with you, without the botheration of a co-wife." Said Shuurpanakha to Rama. [3-18-16]_END

B_3_C_20_4
BEGIN_
वाक्यम् एतत् ततः श्रुत्वा रामस्य विदित आत्मनः |तथा इति लक्ष्मणो वाक्यम् रामस्य प्रत्यपूजयत् || ३-२०-५_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that word of Rama, then the nimble-souled Lakshmana honoured the word of Rama saying "so 
be it." [3-20-5]_END

B_3_C_21_0
BEGIN_
स पुनः पतिताम् दृष्ट्वा क्रोधात् शूर्पणखाम् खरः |उवाच व्यक्तता वाचा ताम् अनर्थ अर्थम् आगताम् || 
३-२१-१_END
BEGIN_
On seeing Shuurpanakha who came back only to wreck havoc on demonic race and again fell before him as 
before, Khara spoke this sentence to her in clear terms in all his fury. [3-21-1]_END

B_3_C_19_11
BEGIN_
उपलभ्य शनैः संज्ञाम् तम् मे शंसितुम् अर्हसि |येन त्वम् दुर्विनीतेन वने विक्रम्य निर्जिता || ३-१९-१२_END
BEGIN_
"It will be apt of you to gather your sensitivity slowly and tell me as to which miscreant attacked 
and worsted you in the forest." Thus Khara spoke to Shuurpanakha. [3-19-12]_END

B_3_C_18_16
BEGIN_
इति उक्त्वा मृगशावाक्षीम् अलात सदृश ईक्षणा |अभ्यधावत् सुसंक्रुद्धा महा उल्का रोहिणीम् इव || ३-१८-१७_END
BEGIN_
Speaking that way she that torch-eyed Shuurpanakha dashed towards the deer-eyed Seetha in high exasperation 
as a great meteor would dash towards Rohini, the brightest star in the sky. [3-18-17]_END

B_3_C_20_5
BEGIN_
राघवो अपि महत् चापम् चामीकर विभूषितम् |चकार सज्यम् धर्मात्मा तानि रक्षांसि च अब्रवीत् || ३-२०-६_END
BEGIN_
On taking up his awful bow that is decorated with gold Raghava stringed it with bowstring and even spoke 
the demons as a forewarning. [3-20-6]_END

B_3_C_21_1
BEGIN_
मया तु इदानीम् शूराः ते राक्षसा पिशित अशनाः |त्वत् प्रियार्थम् विनिर्दिष्टाः किम् अर्थम् रुद्यते 
पुनः || ३-२१-२_END
BEGIN_
"What for your are howling again when I have just now commanded those fearless flesh eating demons in 
order to fulfill your wish? [3-21-2]_END

B_3_C_19_12
BEGIN_
इति भ्रातुर् वचः श्रुत्वा क्रुद्धस्य च विशेषतः |ततः शूर्पणखा वाक्यम् सबाष्पम् इदम् अब्रवीत् || ३-१९-१३_END
BEGIN_
On hearing this kind of words of her brother, especially who is rancorous, then Shuurpanakha spoke these 
words, tearfully. [3-19-13]_END

B_3_C_18_17
BEGIN_
ताम् मृत्यु पाश प्रतिमाम् आपतंतीम् महाबलः |विगृह्य रामः कुपितः ततो लक्ष्मणम् अब्रवीत् || ३-१८-१८_END
BEGIN_
By that the great-energetic Rama took umbrage and checking her who is like the noose of death swooping 
down on Seetha said to Lakshmana. [3-18-18]_END

B_3_C_20_6
BEGIN_
पुत्रौ दशरथस्य आवाम् भ्रातरौ राम लक्ष्मणौ |प्रविष्टौ सीतया सार्धम् दुश्चरम् दण्डका वनम् || ३-२०-७_END
BEGIN_
"We the sons of Dasharatha are brothers named Rama and Lakshmana, and we entered the impenetrable forests 
Dandaka along with Seetha. [3-20-7]_END

B_3_C_21_2
BEGIN_
भक्ताः चैव अनुरक्ताः च हिताः च मम नित्यशः |हन्यमाना अपि न हन्यन्ते न न कुर्युः वचो मम || ३-२१-३_END
BEGIN_
"Those demons are my admirers, adherers and they always remained my well-wishers, hence there is no 
question of their non-accomplishment of my orders. [3-21-3]_END

B_3_C_19_13
BEGIN_
तरुणौ रूप संपन्नौ सुकूमारौ महाबलौ |पुण्डरीक विशालाक्षौ चीर कृष्ण अजिन अंबरौ || ३-१९-१४फल मूल 
अशिनौ दान्तौ तापसौ ब्रह्मचारिणौ |पुत्रौ दशरथस्य आस्ताम् भ्रातरौ राम लक्ष्मनौ || ३-१९-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Those two are in adulthood, good-looking, gentle yet greatly mighty, eyes broad like lotuses, dressed 
in jute-cloths and deerskin, subsistent on fruits and tubers, composed, sagacious and celibate, and 
they are the sons of Dasharatha, namely Rama and Lakshmana. [3-19-14,15]_END

B_3_C_18_18
BEGIN_
क्रूरैः अनार्यैः सौमित्रे परिहासः कथंचन |न कार्यः पश्य वैदेहीम् कथंचित् सौम्य जीवतीम् || ३-१८-१९_END
BEGIN_
"Punning in any way with the base and brutish is inapposite, oh, gentle Saumitri, mark note of Vaidehi, 
somehow surviving  [3-18-19]_END

B_3_C_20_7
BEGIN_
फल मूल अशनौ दांतौ तापसौ धर्म चारिणौ |वसन्तौ दण्डकारण्ये किम् अर्थम् उपहिंसथ || ३-२०-८_END
BEGIN_
"We the dispassionate subsist on fruits and tubers treading in the path of virtue, and we being the 
sages resident in Dandaka forest what for you outrage us. [3-20-8]_END

B_3_C_19_14
BEGIN_

गन्धर्व राज प्रतिमौ पार्थिव 
व्यन्जन अन्वितौ |देवौ वा दानवौ - मानुषौ - वा तौ न तर्कयितुम् उत्सहे || ३-१९-१६_END
BEGIN_

"Having all the aspects 
of kings they equal the kings of gandharva celestials, and I am ill-disposed to differentiate whether 
they two are gods or demons. [3-19-16]_END

B_3_C_21_3
BEGIN_
किम् एतत् श्रोतुम् इच्छ्हामि कारणम् यत् कृते पुनः |हा नाथ इति विनर्दन्ती सर्पवत् चेष्टसे क्षितौ 
|| ३-२१-४_END
BEGIN_
"Owing to what you are highly bawling by saying, 'haa, lord' and wriggle on the ground like a snake? 
I would like to know the reason for all this, what is it? [3-21-4]_END

B_3_C_18_19
BEGIN_
इमाम् विरूपाम् असतीम् अतिमत्ताम् महोदरीम् |राक्षसीम् पुरुषव्याघ्र विरूपयितुम् अर्हसि || ३-१८-२०_END
BEGIN_
"She is freakish, knavish and overtly ruttish, oh, tigerly man, it will be apt of you to deface this 
paunchy demoness " Thus Rama said to Lakshmana. [3-18-20]_END

B_3_C_20_8
BEGIN_
युष्मान् पाप आत्मकान् हंतुम् विप्रकारान् महाहवे |ऋषीणाम् तु नियोगेन प्राप्तो अहम् सशर आसनः || ३-२०-९_END
BEGIN_
"As assigned by the sages I chanced here with bow and arrows to decimate you evil-souled and unrighteous 
beings in a crucial clash. [3-20-9]_END

B_3_C_19_15
BEGIN_

तरुणी रूपसंपन्ना सर्वाअभरण 
भूषिता |दृष्टा तत्र मया नारी तयोर् मध्ये सुमध्यमा || ३-१९-१७_END
BEGIN_

" I have seen a curvaceous 
lady between those two, a ripely beauty, rich in comeliness, adorned with lots of ornaments. [3-19-17]_END

B_3_C_21_4
BEGIN_
अनाथ वत् विलपसि किम् नु नाथे मयि स्थिते |उत्तिष्ठोत्तिष्ठ मा मैवम् वैक्लव्यम् त्यज्यताम् इति || 
३-२१-५_END
BEGIN_
"I am here to take care of you, then why should you really cry out like an uncared-for being, get up...get 
up, and ward off this sort of perplexity." Thus Khara said to Shuurpanakha. [3-21-5]_END

B_3_C_18_20
BEGIN_
इति उक्तो लक्ष्मणः तस्याः क्रुद्धो रामस्य पश्यतः |उद्धृत्य खड्गम् चिच्छ्हेद कर्ण नासम् महाबलः || 
३-१८-२१_END
BEGIN_
Thus said to that mighty Lakshmana he infuriately drew sword and chopped off her ears and nose before 
the very eyes of Rama. [3-18-21]_END

B_3_C_20_9
BEGIN_
तिष्ठत एव अत्र संतुष्टा न उपवरितितुम् अर्हथ |यदि प्राणैः इह अर्थो वो निवर्तध्वम् निशा चराः || ३-२०-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Stay there obligingly or you should not be able to return, else if you desire your lives, oh, nightwalkers, 
you may return now. [3-20-10]_END

B_3_C_21_5
BEGIN_
इति एवम् उक्ता दुर्धर्षा खरेण परिसान्त्विता |विमृज्य नयने स अस्रे खरम् भ्रातरम् अब्रवीत् || ३-२१-६_END
BEGIN_
She that Shuurpanakha who is otherwise an unassuageable one is wholly pacified when Khara spoke to her 
thus that way, and she on dabbing her tearful eyes then spoke to her brother Khara. [3-21-6]_END

B_3_C_19_16
BEGIN_

ताभ्याम् उभाभ्याम् संभूय 
प्रमदाम् अधिकृत्य ताम् |इमाम् अवस्थाम् नीता अहम् यथा अनाथा सती तथा || ३-१९-१८_END
BEGIN_

"Owing to that woman I am 
led into this sort of situation, together by those two, as with an insecure female. [3-19-18]_END

B_3_C_18_21
BEGIN_
निकृत्त कर्ण नासा तु विस्वरम् सा विनद्य च |यथा आगतम् प्रदुद्राव घोरा शूर्पणखा वनम् || ३-१८-२२_END
BEGIN_
On hewing off her ears and nose she that ghastly Shuurpanakha blared highly and discordantly, and very 
speedily fled into forest as she came. [3-18-22]_END

B_3_C_20_10
BEGIN_
तस्य तद् वचनम् श्रुत्वा राक्षसाः ते चतुर्दश |ऊचुर् वाचम् सुसंक्रुद्धा ब्रह्मघ्नः शूल पाणयः || ३-२०-११
संरक्त नयना घोरा रामम् रक्तांत लोचनम् |परुषा मधुर आभाषम् हृष्टाः अदृष्ट पराक्रमम् || ३-२०-१२_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that sentence of Rama they the fourteen ghoulish demons who are the slayers of Brahmans and 
handlers of spears have become highly infuriated, and they with their bloodshot eyes and with harsh 
words said these words to Rama, whose eyes are with blood streaks at their ends, and who also is a sweet 
talker, and whose valour is yet unseen by those fourteen demons. [3-20-11, 12]_END

B_3_C_19_17
BEGIN_

तस्याः च अनृजु वृत्तायाः 
तयोः च हतयोर् अहम् |सफेनम् पातुम् इच्छ्हामि रुधिरम् रण मूर्धनि || ३-१९-१९_END
BEGIN_

"Staying in the van of war 
I wish to drink the frothy blood of that guileful Seetha along with that of those two, Rama and Lakshmana, 
when they are killed in war. [3-19-19]_END

B_3_C_21_6
BEGIN_
अस्मि इदानीम् अहम् प्रप्ता हत श्रवण नासिका |शोणित ओघ परिक्लिन्ना त्वया च परिसमन्विता || ३-२१-७_END
BEGIN_
"I came to you just a while back with my ears and nose chopped off and wet with gushes of blood, and 
you too have comforted me, isn't it. [3-21-7]_END

B_3_C_18_22
BEGIN_
सा विरूपा महाघोरा राक्षसी शोणित उक्षिता |ननाद विविधान् नादान् यथा प्रावृषि तोयदः || ३-१८-२३_END
BEGIN_
She that very ghastly demoness when defaced is wetted by blood and blared many a blare like a cloud 
in cloudburst. [3-18-23]_END

B_3_C_20_11
BEGIN_
क्रोधम् उत्पाद्य नो भर्तुः खरस्य सुमहात्मनः |त्वम् एव हास्यसे प्राणान् अद्य अस्माभिर् हतो युधि || 
३-२०-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Killed in conflict by us you alone will set your lives loose as an inciter of fury in our highly great 
souled lord Khara. [3-20-13]_END

B_3_C_21_7
BEGIN_
प्रेषिताः च त्वया शूरा राक्षसाः ते चतुर् दश |निहन्तुम् राघवम् घोराम् मत् प्रियार्थम् स लक्ष्मणम् 
|| ३-२१-८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, valiant brother, for my delight you too have sent fourteen demons to eliminate that atrocious Rama 
along with Lakshmana, isn't it? [3-21-8]_END

B_3_C_19_18
BEGIN_

एष मे प्रथमः कामः कृतः तत्र 
त्वया भवेत् |तस्याः तयोः च रुधिरम् पिबेयम् अहम् आहवे || ३-१९-२०_END
BEGIN_

"I shall drink her blood 
and also that of those two in war, this being my prime longing let it be fulfilled by you." Thus wailed 
Shuurpanakha before her brother Khara. [3-19-20]_END

B_3_C_18_23
BEGIN_
सा विक्षरंती रुधिरम् बहुधा घोर दर्शना |प्रगृह्य बाहू गर्जन्ती प्रविवेश महावनम् || ३-१८-२४_END
BEGIN_
She that gruesome one in her appearance clasped herself and thunderously entered similarly gruesome 
forest while her blood fountained and profusely exuded. [3-18-24]_END

B_3_C_20_12
BEGIN_
का हि ते शक्तिर् एकस्य बहूनाम् रण मूर्धनि |अस्माकम् अग्रतः स्थातुम् किम् पुनर् योद्धुम् आहवे || 
३-२०-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Indeed, what capability you have as a lone one to stand against many of us in the forefront of war, 
and why tell again about your battling ability in a given battle. [3-20-14]_END

B_3_C_22_0
BEGIN_
एवम् आधर्षितः शूरः शूर्पणख्या खरः ततः |उवाच रक्षसाम् मध्ये खरः खरतरम् वचः || ३-२२-१_END
BEGIN_
Thus when Shuurpanakha disparaged that valiant Khara amidst demons he is infuriated and spoke these 
highly hurtful words. [3-22-1]_END

B_3_C_19_19
BEGIN_

इति तस्याम् ब्रुवाणायाम् 
चतुर् दश महाबलान् |व्यादिदेश खरः क्रुद्धो राक्षसान् अंतकोपमान् || ३-१९-२१_END
BEGIN_

While she is saying like 
that Khara vengefully summoned fourteen great mighty demons that are similar to the Terminator. [3-19-21]_END

B_3_C_21_8
BEGIN_
ते तु रामेण सामर्षाः शूल पट्टिस पाणयः |समरे निहताः सर्वे सायकैः मर्म भेदिभिः || ३-२१-९_END
BEGIN_
"But they all who handled their spears and bolts along with an envious anger are killed in a fight with 
Rama by his arrows that cleave the crucial parts of his opponents. [3-21-9]_END

B_3_C_18_24
BEGIN_
ततः तु सा राक्षस संघ सम्वृतम्खरम् जन स्थान गतम् विरूपिता |उपेत्य तम् भ्रातरम् उग्र तेजसम्
पपात भूमौ गगनाद् यथा अशनिः || ३-१८-२५_END
BEGIN_
Then she who is deformed neared her brother Khara who possess violent vigour, who is abiding in Janasthaana 
and who is presently surrounded by his band of his hench-demons, and before him she that Shuurpanakha 
fell onto ground like a thunderbolt from the sky. [3-18-25]_END

B_3_C_20_13
BEGIN_
एभिः बाहु प्रयुक्तैः नः परिघैः शूल पट्टिशैः |प्राणाम् त्यक्ष्यसि वीर्यम् च धनुः च कर पीडितम् || 
३-२०-१५_END
BEGIN_
"When we launch maces, spears and swords by our might you will forgo your lives, mettle, and even the 
bow now clasped in your hand." So said the demons to Rama. [3-20-15]_END

B_3_C_22_1
BEGIN_
तव अपमान प्रभवः क्रोधो अयम् अतुलो मम |न शक्यते धारयितुम् लवण अंभ इव उल्बणम् || ३-२२-२_END
BEGIN_
"This fury of mine originating from the disgrace brought on you is like the highly bitter salt water 
that is impossible to contain when ingested. [3-22-2]_END

B_3_C_19_20
BEGIN_

मानुषौ शस्त्र संपन्नौ चीर 
कृष्ण अजिन अंबरौ |प्रविष्टौ दण्डकारण्यम् घोरम् प्रमदया सह || ३-१९-२२_END
BEGIN_

"Wielding weapons and wearing 
jute-cloths and deerskin two humans have got into ghastly forest of Dandaka along with a woman of age." 
Thus Khara is ordering the fourteen demons. [3-19-22]_END

B_3_C_18_25
BEGIN_
ततः सभार्यम् भय मोह मूर्चितासलक्ष्मणम् राघवम् आगतम् वनम् |विरूपणम् च आत्मनि शोणित उक्षिता
शशंस सर्वम् भगिनी खरस्य सा || ३-१८-२६_END
BEGIN_
Then that sister of Khara who is convulsed in the fluster of fear and her body wetted with blood reported 
to her brother Khara, all about Rama's arrival in forest with his wife and Lakshmana, and even about 
his misshaping her. [3-18-26]_END

B_3_C_21_9
BEGIN_
तान् भूमौ पतितान् दृष्ट्वा क्षणेन एव महाजवान् |रामस्य च महत् कर्म महान् त्रासो अभवन् मम || ३-२१-१०_END
BEGIN_
"On seeing those highly impetuous demons falling to earth in a trice, and even on seeing the unusual 
deed of Rama in felling them, I am highly alarmed. [3-21-10]_END

B_3_C_20_14
BEGIN_
इति एवम् उक्त्वा संरब्धा राक्षसाः ते चतुर्दश |उद्यत आयुध निस्त्रिंशा रामम् एव अभिदुद्रुवुः || ३-२०-१६
चिक्षिपुः तानि शूलानि राघवम् प्रति दुर्जयम् |_END
BEGIN_
Thus saying that way clamorously they the fourteen demons, upraising their weapons they unhesitatingly 
rushed towards Rama alone, and they hurled lances towards that unconquerable Raghava. [3-20-16, 17a]_END

B_3_C_22_2
BEGIN_
न रामम् गणये वीर्यान् मानुषम् क्षीण जीवितम् |आत्म दुश्चरितैः प्राणान् हतो यो अद्य विमोक्ष्यति || 
३-२२-३_END
BEGIN_
"I do not care the valour of that Rama for he is a human with dwindled lifetime, now going to give up 
his life slain by his own misdoings. [3-22-3]_END

B_3_C_19_21
BEGIN_

तौ हत्वा ताम् च दुर्वृत्ताम् 
उपावर्तितुम् अर्हथ |इयम् च रुधिरम् तेषाम् भगिनी मम पास्यति || ३-१९-२३_END
BEGIN_

"You shall return to me only on killing those two and also that 
treacherous woman, and their blood this sister of mine will drink. [3-19-23]_END

B_3_C_21_10
BEGIN_
सा अस्मि भीता समुद्विग्ना विषण्णा च निशाचर |शरणम् त्वाम् पुनः प्राप्ता सर्वतो भय दर्शिनी || ३-२१-११_END
BEGIN_
"Oh me! I am alarmed, fully frenzied, and even despaired, oh, nightwalker Khara, and beholding dread 
everywhere again I have come seeking your refuge. [3-21-11]_END

B_3_C_20_15
BEGIN_
तानि शूलानि काकुत्स्थः समस्तानि चतुर्दश || ३-२०-१७तावद्भिः एव चिच्छ्हेद शरैः कांचन भूषितैः |_END
BEGIN_
Rama in turn shredded all of those fourteen lances only with as many arrows that are adorned in gold. 
[3-20-17b, 18a]_END

B_3_C_22_3
BEGIN_
बाष्पः संधार्यताम् एष संभ्रमः च विमुच्यताम् |अहम् रामम् सह भ्रात्रा नयामि यम सादनम् || ३-२२-४_END
BEGIN_
"Control your tears and cast off your despair too, for I will send Rama to the abode of the Terminator 
along with his brother. [3-22-4]_END

B_3_C_19_22
BEGIN_

मनोरथो अयम् इष्टो अस्या भगिन्या मम राक्षसाः |शीघ्रम् संपद्यताम् 
गत्वा तौ प्रमथ्य स्व तेजसा || ३-१९-२४_END
BEGIN_

"Oh, demons, on going there swiftly stamp them out by you own 
vigour, thus let the fanciful hearty desire of my sister be achieved. [3-19-24]_END

B_3_C_21_11
BEGIN_
विषाद नक्र अध्युषिते परित्रास ऊर्मि मालिनि |किम् माम् न त्रायसे मग्नाम् विपुले शोक सागरे || ३-२१-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Why do not you rescue me when I am drowned in a vast ocean called grief, wherein each pervasive crocodile 
is despair and each swelling wave is fright. [3-21-12]_END

B_3_C_20_16
BEGIN_
ततः पश्चात् महातेजा नाराचान् सूर्य संनिभान् || ३-२०-१८जग्राह परम क्रुद्धः चतुर्दश शिल अशितान् |_END
BEGIN_
Next that great resplendent Rama in high wrath took up fourteen iron bolt like arrows that are whetted 
on whetstone and equalling the sun in their dazzle. [3-20-18b, 19a]_END

B_3_C_22_4
BEGIN_
परश्वध हतस्य अद्य मन्द प्राणस्य भू तले |रामस्य रुधिरम् रक्तम् उष्णम् पास्यसि राक्षसि || ३-२२-५_END
BEGIN_
"Now, you demoness, you will swill that Rama's red hot blood when that short-lived one is hewed down 
to earth with an axe." So Khara assured Shuurpanakha. [3-22-5]_END

B_3_C_19_23
BEGIN_

युष्माबिः निर्हतो दृष्ट्वा तौ उभौ भ्रातौ रणे |इयम् प्रहृष्टा 
मुदिता रुधिरम् युधि पास्यति || ३-१९-२५_END
BEGIN_

"On seeing your finishing those two brothers flatly in a war she 
this sister of mine will be gladdened, and then she drinks their blood in war, amusingly. [3-19-25]_END

B_3_C_21_12
BEGIN_
एते च निहता भूमौ रामेण निशितैः शरैः |ये च मे पदवीम् प्राप्ता राक्षसाः पिशित अशनाः || ३-२१-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Besides, those flesh-eating demons that have followed me are also felled by Rama with his sharp arrows, 
for whom I have a contrite heart. [3-21-13]_END

B_3_C_20_17
BEGIN_
गृहीत्वा धनुः आयम्य लक्ष्यान् उद्दिश्य राक्षसान् || ३-२०-१९मुमोच राघवो बाणान् वज्रान् इव शतक्रतुः 
|_END
BEGIN_
Then Raghava took up his bow, arched it, and aiming at the targeted demons released arrows as Indra 
would release his Thunderbolts. [3-20-19b, 20a]_END

B_3_C_22_5
BEGIN_
सा प्रहृष्ट्वा वचः श्रुत्वा खरस्य वदनात् च्युतम् |प्रशशंस पुनर् मौर्ख्यात् भ्रातरम् रक्षसाम् वरम् 
|| ३-२२-६_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words plunged from the mouth of Khara she is very much gladdened and in all her stupidity 
she further praised her brother highly saying, "you are the best among all the demons..." [3-22-6]_END

B_3_C_19_24
BEGIN_

इति प्रतिसमादिष्टा राक्षसाः ते चतुर् दश |तत्र जग्मुः तया सार्धम् 
घना वातेरिताः यथा || ३-१९-२६_END
BEGIN_

In this way when Khara ordered those fourteen demons, they have 
gone to Panchavati along with Shuurpanakha like black-clouds glided by gales. [3-19-26]_END

B_3_C_21_13
BEGIN_
मयि ते यदि अनुक्रोशो यदि रक्षःसु तेषु च |रामेण यदि शक्तिः ते तेजो वा अस्ति निशा चर || ३-२१-१४
दण्डकारण्य निलयम् जहि राक्षस कण्टकम् |_END
BEGIN_
"If you have mercy on me, and even on those dead demons, and if ability and animation are still left 
in you to cope with Rama, oh, nightwalker, kill that Rama who is a thorn in the side of demons dwelling 
in Dandaka forest. [3-21-14, 15a]_END

B_3_C_20_18
BEGIN_
ते भित्त्वा रक्षसाम् वेगात् वक्षांसि रुधिर आप्लुताः || ३-२०-२०विनिष्पेतुः तदा भूमौ वल्मीकात् इव 
पन्नगाः |_END
BEGIN_
And by the force of their speed those arrows gored the chests of those demons, and then on coming out 
bedaubed with blood they swiftly penetrated into earth like snakes into snake pit. [3-20-20b, 21a]_END

B_3_C_23_0
BEGIN_
तत् प्रयातम् बलम् घोरम् अशिवम् शोणित उदकम् |अभ्यवर्षत् महा मेघः तुमुलो गर्दभ अरुणः || ३-२३-१_END
BEGIN_
A massy and tumultuous ass-coloured cloud rained ill-omened bloody water while that fiendish force is 
advancing. [3-23-1]_END

B_3_C_22_6
BEGIN_
तया परुषितः पूर्वम् पुनर् एव प्रशंसितः |अब्रवीत् दूषणम् नाम खरः सेना पतिम् तदा || ३-२२-७_END
BEGIN_
Though she denounced him earlier she alone praised him now for which Khara is overjoyed, and then he 
ordered his army commander, namely Duushana. [3-22-7]_END

B_3_C_19_25
BEGIN_

ततस्तु ते तम् समुदर्ग तेजसम्तथापि तीक्ष्ण प्रदरा निशाचरा |
न शेकुर् एनम् सहसा प्रमर्दितुम्वनद्विपा दीप्त्वम् इव अग्निम् उथितम् || ३-१९-२७_END
BEGIN_

But then, though the nightwalker wielding sharp arrows have become 
ineffectual to trounce Rama like the wild elephants which will become ineffectual to overcome the blazingly 
uprising wildfire. [3-19-27]_END

B_3_C_21_14
BEGIN_
यदि रामम् अमित्रघ्नम् न त्वम् अद्य वधिष्यसि || ३-२१-१५तव चैव अग्रतः प्राणान् त्यक्ष्यामि निरपत्रपा 
|_END
BEGIN_
"If you are not going to kill that enemy destroyer Rama now itself, I will give up my life unhesitatingly, 
that too in your fore, that too now itself._END

B_3_C_20_19
BEGIN_
तैः भग्न हृदया बूमौ छ्हिन्न मूला इव द्रुमाः || ३-२०-२१निपेतुः शोणित स्नाता विकृता विगत असवः |_END
BEGIN_
Those arrows bursting their hearts they are blood bathed, mangled, and utterly dead, and like the uprooted 
trees they fell onto the ground. [3-20-21b, 22a]_END

B_3_C_23_1
BEGIN_
निपेतुः तुरगाः तस्य रथ युक्ता महाजवाः |समे पुष्पचिते देशे राजमार्गे यदृच्छ्हया || ३-२३-२_END
BEGIN_
The highly speedy horses paired to Khara's chariot have tottered in a trice, even though that place 
on the highway is with even surface and spread with flowers. [3-23-2]_END

B_3_C_22_7
BEGIN_
चतुर्दश सहस्राणि मम चित्त अनुवर्तिनाम् |रक्षसाम् भीम वेगानाम् समरेषु अनिवर्तिनाम् || ३-२२-८_END
BEGIN_
"Those who are the followers of my will, whose hustle will be frightful and who will be unretreating 
in combats, such of those demons are there in fourteen thousand numbers, aren't they. [3-22-8]_END

B_3_C_21_15
BEGIN_
बुद्ध्या अहम् अनुपश्यामि न त्वम् रामस्य संयुगे || ३-२१-१६स्थातुम् प्रति मुखे शक्तः स बलो अपि महा 
रणे |शूरमानी न शूरः त्वम् मिथ्या आरोपित विक्रमः || ३-२१-१७_END
BEGIN_
"I can perceive instinctually that you are incapable of affronting Rama in a given crucial battle, even 
if your are with all your forces on the battlefield, and you assert yourself a valiant, but you are 
just vainglorious. [3-21-16b, 17]_END

B_3_C_20_20
BEGIN_
तान् भूमौ पतितान् दृष्ट्वा राक्षसी क्रोध मूर्च्छ्हिता || ३-२०-२२उपगम्य खरम् सा तु किंचित् संशुष्क 
शोणिता |पपात पुनः एव आर्ता सनिर्यासा इव वल्लरी || ३-२०-२३_END
BEGIN_
On seeing the demons falling onto ground that demoness Shuurpanakha is convulsed in rage, and she with 
a blanched aspect returned to the near of Khara in an agonising manner like a creeper exuding resin 
on incision, and fell before him as before. [3-20-22b, 23]_END

B_3_C_23_2
BEGIN_
श्यामम् रुधिर पर्यन्तम् बभूव परिवेषणम् |अलात चक्र प्रतिमम् प्रतिगृह्य दिवाकरम् || ३-२३-३_END
BEGIN_
Capturing the sun a blackish corona with blood-red outer circle has formed and nested around it 
like the fiery ring formed by circling a fireball. [3-23-3]_END

B_3_C_22_8
BEGIN_
नील जीमूत वर्णानाम् लोक हिंसा विहाराणाम् |सर्व उद्योगम् उदीर्णानाम् रक्षसाम् सौम्य कारय || ३-२२-९_END
BEGIN_
"And oh, gentle Duushana, those domineering demons are with dark-clouds like complexions, and they are 
the pamperers of genocide, as such, cause them for a belligerency, all at once. [3-22-9]_END

B_3_C_21_16
BEGIN_
अपयाहि जन स्थानात् त्वरितः सह बान्धवः |जहि त्वम् समरे मूढान् यथा तु कुलपांसन || ३-२१-१८मानुषौ 
तौ न शक्नोषि हन्तुम् वै राम लक्ष्मणौ |निःसत्त्वस्य अल्प वीर्यस्य वासः ते कीदृशः तु इह || ३-२१-१९_END
BEGIN_
"Kill those two, Rama and Lakshmana, as they are just humans, or else, if you are incapable of doing 
so, really what for is your stay here in Janasthaana with your trivial stamina and trifling sinews like 
a stupid blemishing his clan, then get out of this Janasthaana at once along with your hench-demons. 
[3-21-18, 19]_END

B_3_C_20_21
BEGIN_
भ्रातुः समीपे शोक आर्ता ससर्ज निनदम् महत् |सस्वरम् मुमोच बाष्पम् विवर्ण वदना तदा || ३-२०-२४_END
BEGIN_
Then she in the presence of her brother Khara discharged a great outcry, and with a bloodless face she 
spilled tears attuning the strains of a whiner. [3-20-24]_END

B_3_C_23_3
BEGIN_
ततो ध्वजम् उपागम्य हेम दण्डम् समुच्छ्ह्रितम् |समाक्रम्य महाकायः तस्थौ गृध्रः सुदारुणः || ३-२३-४_END
BEGIN_
Then, nearing the golden shaft of the flag of the chariot with a very lofty flagstaff, an awful eagle 
with massive body occupied and perched atop of that golden shaft. [3-23-4]_END

B_3_C_22_9
BEGIN_
उपस्थापय मे क्षिप्रम् रथम् सौम्य धनूंषि च |शरान् च चित्रान् खड्गां च शक्ती च विविधाः शिताः || ३-२२-१०_END
BEGIN_
"For me, oh, gentle one, promptly position my chariot before me along with bows and arrows, amazing 
swords and diverse sharp power bolts. [3-22-10]_END

B_3_C_21_17
BEGIN_
राम तेजो अभिभूतो हि त्वम् क्षिप्रम् विनशिष्यसि |स हि तेजः समायुक्तो रामो दशरथात्मजः || ३-२१-२०_END
BEGIN_
"You will completely and quickly evanish, indeed, subjugated by resplendence of Rama, for that Dasharatha's 
son Rama possess that kind of resplendence, in effect. [3-21-20]_END

B_3_C_20_22
BEGIN_
निपातितान् प्रेक्ष्य रणे तु राक्षसान्प्रधाविता शूर्पणखा पुनः ततः |वधम् च तेषाम् निखिलेन रक्षसाम्
शशंस सर्वम् भगिनी खरस्य सा || ३-२०-२५_END
BEGIN_
Shuurpanakha having seen the fall of demons quickly fled from Panchavati of Rama to trikanTaka, the 
capital of Khara, and she being the sister of Khara she reported to Khara all about the destruction 
of those demons, in its entirety. [3-20-25]_END

B_3_C_23_4
BEGIN_
जनस्थान समीपे च समाक्रम्य खर स्वनाः |विस्वरान् विविधान् च चक्रुः मांस आदा मृग पक्षिणः || ३-२३-५_END
BEGIN_
Cacophonous and carnivorous predators and vultures took over the nearby places of Janasthaana and they 
made raucous sounds of many kinds. [3-23-5]_END

B_3_C_22_10
BEGIN_
अग्रे निर्यातुम् इच्छ्हामि पौलस्त्यानाम् महात्मनाम् |वधार्थम् दुर्विनीतस्य रामस्य रण कोविद || ३-२२-११_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, war pert Duushana, I wish to start ahead of all the demons of ours, who are the clans-demons of 
the great souled Paulastya, for the purpose of elimination of that evil-minded Rama." So said Khara 
to Duushana. [3-22-11]_END

B_3_C_21_18
BEGIN_
भ्राता च अस्य महा वीर्यो येन च अस्मि विरूपिता |एवम् विलाप्य बहुशो राक्ष्सी प्रदरोदरी || ३-२१-२१
भ्रातुः समीपे शोक आर्ता नष्ट संज्ञा बभूव ह |कराभ्याम् उदरम् हत्वा रुरोद भृश दुःखिता || ३-२१-२२_END
BEGIN_
"And, by whom I am misshapen that brother of Rama too is a highly vigorous one..." in this way on saying 
Shuurpanakha bawled variously in the presence of her brother, Khara, and then anguished by her own affliction 
that demoness with a cave like belly started hitting her paunch with both of her hands, and what is 
more, she swooned. [3-21-21, 22]_END

B_3_C_23_5
BEGIN_
व्याजह्रुः च पदीप्तायाम् दिशि वै भैरव स्वनम् |अशिवा यातुधानानाम् शिवा घोरा महास्वनाः || ३-२३-६_END
BEGIN_
Turning towards the stretch scorched by the sun, fearsome and loud noised jackals have howled emitting 
awful sounds, that which is inauspicious to the demons. [3-23-6]_END

B_3_C_22_11
BEGIN_
इति तस्य ब्रुवाणस्य सूर्य वर्णम् महारथम् |सत् अश्वैः शबलैः युक्तम् आचचक्षे अथ दूषणः || ३-२२-१२_END
BEGIN_
While Khara is saying thus Duushana heralded saying, "Here comes the great chariot with sun's dazzle, 
yoked with very good horses of variegated colours." [3-22-12]_END

B_3_C_24_0
BEGIN_
आश्रमम् प्रति याते तु खरे खर पराक्रमे |तान् एव औत्पातिकान् रामः सह भ्रात्रा ददर्श ह || ३-२४-१_END
BEGIN_
While fiercely valorous Khara proceeded towards Rama's hermitage, Rama along with his brother Lakshmana 
has indeed seen the very same auguries which have earlier appeared to Khara. [3-24-1]_END

B_3_C_23_6
BEGIN_
प्रभिन्नगजसंकाशतोयशोणितधारिणः | - यद्वा -प्रभिन्न गज संकाश तोय शोणित धारिणः |आकाशम् तत् अनाकाशम् 
चक्रुः भीम अंबु वाहकाः|| ३-२३-७_END
BEGIN_
Then frightening clouds similar to bursting mountains carrying bloodlike water have rendered the firmament 
less of leeway. [3-23-7]_END

B_3_C_22_12
BEGIN_
तम् मेरु शिखर आकारम् तप्त कांचन भूषणम् |हेम चक्रम् असंबाधम् वैदूर्यमय कूबरम् || ३-२२-१३मत्स्यैः 
पुष्पैः द्रुमैः शैलैः चन्द्र सूर्यैः च कांचनैः |मा.ंगल्यैः पक्षि सम्घैः च ताराभिः च समावृतम् || 
३-२२-१४ध्वज निस्त्रिंश संपन्नम् किंकिणी वर भूषितम् |सत् अश्व युक्तम् सः अमर्षात् आरुरोह खरः 
तदा || ३-२२-१५_END
BEGIN_
That chariot which has a roomy cabin with its rooftop like that of the ridge of Mt. Meru, body embellished 
in gold, wheels golden, gem-studded yoke-to-carriage shaft, all around encompassed with golden artefacts 
like fishes, flowers, trees, mountains, sun, moon, and auspicious birds flocks and stars, and even decorated 
with jingle-bells, endowed with flags, swords, and best horses, and such as it is, Khara embarked on 
it with all his rancour. [3-22-13, 14, 15]_END

B_3_C_24_1
BEGIN_
तान् उत्पातान् महाघोरान् रामो दृष्ट्वा अति अमर्षण |प्रजानाम् अहितान् दृष्ट्वा वाक्यम् लक्ष्मणम् 
अब्रवीत् || ३-२४-२_END
BEGIN_
On looking at those very gruesomely bad omens, and perceiving them to be unpropitious to people, Rama 
spoke this sentence to Lakshmana. [3-24-2]_END

B_3_C_22_13
BEGIN_
खरः तु तान् महत् सैन्याम् रथ चर्म आयुध ध्वजान् |निर्यात इति अब्रवीत् प्रेक्ष्य दूषणः सर्व राक्षसान् 
|| ३-२२-१६_END
BEGIN_
On overseeing that great army with chariots, skins shields, weaponry and flags, and even at Duushana 
too, Khara charged all those demons saying "proceed." [3-22-16]_END

B_3_C_23_7
BEGIN_
बभूव तिमिरम् घोरम् उद्धतम् रोम हर्षणम् |दिशो वा प्रदिशो वा अपि सुव्यक्तम् न चकाशिरे || ३-२३-८_END
BEGIN_
There chanced an abominable, cataclysmic, hair-raising darkness whereby the milieus or inter-milieus 
are not very clearly brightened. [3-23-8]_END

B_3_C_24_2
BEGIN_
इमान् पश्य महाबाहो सर्व भूत अपहारिणः |समुत्थितान् महा उत्पातान् संहर्तुम् सर्व राक्षसान् || ३-२४-३_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, dextrous Lakshmana, for the complete elimination of all the demons these great indications have 
arisen, as though betokening the annihilation of all beings. See them. [3-24-3]_END

B_3_C_22_14
BEGIN_
ततः तद् राक्षसम् सैन्यम् घोर चर्म आयुध ध्वजम् |निर्जगाम जन स्थानात् महानादम् महाजवम् || ३-२२-१७_END
BEGIN_
Then that demonic force with their ghoulish skin shields, weaponry and flags, issued forth from Janasthaana, 
blaring blatantly and foraying dashingly. [3-22-17]_END

B_3_C_23_8
BEGIN_
क्षतज आर्द्र सवर्णाभा संध्या कालम् विना बभौ |खरम् च अभिमुखम् नेदुः तदा घोरा मृगाः खगाः || ३-२३-९
कंक गोमायु गृध्राः च चुक्रुशुः भय संशिनः |_END
BEGIN_
An untimely eventide glistened with a colour similar to the one drenched in blood, and then horrendous 
brutes and birds have clamoured facing Khara directly, and the vultures, jackals and eagles too have 
screamed portending danger. [3-23-9, 10a]_END

B_3_C_24_3
BEGIN_
अमी रुधिर धाराः तु विसृजंतो खर स्वनाः |व्योम्नि मेघा निवर्तन्ते परुषा गर्दभ अरुणाः || ३-२४-४_END
BEGIN_
"On their part these clouds are hovering on the sky with stark reddish-grey tint, thunderously braying 
and copiously showering streams of blood. [3-24-4]_END

B_3_C_23_9
BEGIN_
नित्या अशिव करा युद्धे शिवा घोर निदर्शनाः || ३-२३-१०नेदुः बलस्य अभिमुखम् ज्वाल उद्गारिभिः आननैः 
|_END
BEGIN_
Jackals, that too female jackals, are always the agents of inauspiciousness in wars with demonstrable 
calamities brought forth by their portending howling, and such jackals have now howled in front of Khara's 
army with their snouts spewing blazes. [3-23-10]_END

B_3_C_22_15
BEGIN_
मुद्गरैः पट्टिशैः शूलैः सुतीक्ष्णैः च परश्वधैः |खड्गैः चक्रैः च हस्तस्थैः भ्राजमानैः स तोमरैः || 
३-२२-१८शक्तिभिः परिघैः घोरैः अतिमात्रैः च कार्मुकैः |गदा असि मुसलैः वज्रैः गृहीतैः भीम दर्शनैः 
|| ३-२२-१९राक्षसानाम् सुघोराणाम् सहस्राणि चतुर्दश |निर्यातानि जन स्थानात् खर चित्त अनुवर्तिनाम् 
|| ३-२२-२०_END
BEGIN_
Wielding maces, dart-bolts, and spears, and also razor-sharp axes, swords and discs, and dreadful power-darts 
and power-bolts that are flashing, iron maces, unusual bows, clubs, scimitars and pounding-shafts, and 
even thunderbolt like weapons that are calamitous in look, that army which comprises fourteen thousand 
fiendish demons that are the followers of Khara's whim, has started from Janasthaana. [3-22-18, 19, 
20]_END

B_3_C_24_4
BEGIN_
स धूमाः च शराः सर्वे मम युद्ध अभिनन्दिताः |रुक्म पृष्ठानि चापानि विचेष्टन्ते विचक्षण || ३-२४-५_END
BEGIN_
"All my arrows too are incensed to fuming in an ecstasy towards a war, and dorsally gold-plated bows 
of mine are incessantly spurring to hook up those arrows, telling apart the impeding conflict. [3-24-5]_END

B_3_C_23_10
BEGIN_
कबन्धः परिघ आभासो दृश्यते भास्कर अंतिके || ३-२३-११जग्राह सूर्यम् स्वर्भानुः अपर्वणि महाग्रहः |
प्रवाति मारुतः शीघ्रम् निष्प्रभो अभूत् दिवाकरः || ३-२३-१२_END
BEGIN_
A spherical object like that of a human trunk is revealed near at the sun, while the sun is rendered 
shineless as though Rahu, the great eclipsing-planet, has eclipsed him inopportunely, and the wind too 
whirled frantically. [3-23-11b, 12]_END

B_3_C_22_16
BEGIN_
तान् तु निर्धावतो दृष्ट्वा राक्षसान् भीम दर्शनम् |खरस्य अथ रथः किंचित् जगाम तत् अनन्तरम् || ३-२२-२१_END
BEGIN_
On seeing the outrush of those demons of diabolic appearance, then Khara's chariot also proceeded a 
little later at their behind. [3-22-21]_END

B_3_C_24_5
BEGIN_
यादृशा इह कूजन्ति पक्षिणो वन चारिणः |अग्रतो नः भयम् प्राप्तम् संशयो जीवितस्य च || ३-२४-६_END
BEGIN_
"Judging by the kind of wild birds that are shrieking here, danger is up ahead and coming upon us, along 
with uncertainty of our lives. [3-24-6]_END

B_3_C_23_11
BEGIN_
उत्पेतुः च विना रात्रिम् ताराः खद्योतन प्रभाः |संलीन मीन विहगा नलिन्यः शुष्क पंकजाः || ३-२३-१३
तस्मिन् क्षणे बभूवुः च विना पुष्प फलैः द्रुमाः |_END
BEGIN_
Stars sprang up with the brilliance of fireflies though it is not night, and at that moment fishes and 
waterfowls stood still in lakes, lotuses have dried up, flowers and fruits have dropped from trees as 
though it is night. [3-23-13, 14a]_END

B_3_C_22_17
BEGIN_
ततः तान् शबलान् अश्वान् तप्त कांचन भूषितान् |खरस्य मतम् आज्ञाय सारथिः पर्यचोदयत् || ३-२२-२२_END
BEGIN_
Then the charioteer set spurs on those colourful horses that are adorned in polished gold according 
to the notions of Khara. [3-22-22]_END

B_3_C_24_6
BEGIN_
संप्रहारः तु सुमहान् भविष्यति न संशयः |अयम् आख्याति मे बाहुः स्फुरमाणो मुहुर् मुहुः || ३-२४-७
संनिकर्षे तु नः शूर जयम् शत्रोः पराजयम् |सुप्रभम् च प्रसन्नम् च तव वक्त्रम् हि लक्ष्यते || ३-२४-८_END
BEGIN_
"This right hand of mine is indicating by its repeated throbbing that a critical and riotous conflict 
is going to occur, no doubt, but oh brave one, our victory and defeat to the enemies are also in vicinity, 
and for sure, your face is also appearing brightish and aglow, which itself is a good omen. [3-24-8] 
[3-24-7, 8]_END

B_3_C_23_12
BEGIN_
उद्धूतः च विना वातम् रेणुः जलधर अरुणः || ३-२३-१४चीची कूचि इति वाश्यन्तो बभूवुः तत्र सारिकाः |_END
BEGIN_
Without any puffing of wind dust in brownish-red colour is heaved up, and there the songbirds like Maina 
started to twitter as 'cii cii kuu cii'. [3-23-14b, 15a]_END

B_3_C_22_18
BEGIN_
संचोदितो रथः शीघ्रम् खरस्य रिपु घातिनः |शब्देन आपूरयामास दिशः स प्रदिशः तथा || ३-२२-२३_END
BEGIN_
When the chariot of enemy destroyer Khara is driven that impetuously, it has started to swell earth's 
four cardinal quarters and inter-quarters with turbulence. [3-22-23]_END

B_3_C_24_7
BEGIN_
उद्यतानाम् हि युद्धार्थम् येषाम् भवति लक्ष्मणः |निष्प्रभम् वदनम् तेषाम् भवति आयुः परिक्षयः || ३-२४-९_END
BEGIN_
"If the faces of those that are poised for a conflict loose lustre, deem that the death is looming large 
on their longevity too. [3-24-9]_END

B_3_C_25_0
BEGIN_
अवष्टब्ध धनुम् रामम् क्रुद्धम् च रिपु घातिनम् |ददर्श आश्रमम् आगम्य खरः सह पुरःसरैः || ३-२५-१_END
BEGIN_
Khara on arriving at the hermitage along with forerunning soldiers saw the enemy-eliminator and wrathful 
Rama holding fast to his bow. [3-25-1]_END

B_3_C_23_13
BEGIN_
उल्काः च अपि स निर्घोषा निपेतुः घोर दर्शनाः || ३-२३-१५प्रचचाल मही च अपि स शैल वन कानना |_END
BEGIN_
Meteors horrible in their look have fallen down thunderously, and even the earth together with its mountains, 
woods and forests quaked shakily. [3-23-15b, 16a]_END

B_3_C_22_19
BEGIN_
प्रवृद्ध मन्युः तु खरः खर स्वरेरिपोः वध अर्थम् त्वरितो यथा अंतकः |अचूचुदत् सारथिम् उन्नदन् पुनर्
महाबलो मेघ इव अश्म वर्षवान् || ३-२२-२४_END
BEGIN_
He whose voice is thunderous and whose rancour escalated speedily, and who is hastening forward like 
the Terminator intending to destroy his enemy, that Khara repeatedly hurried the charioteer shouting 
at him loudly like a overwhelming cloud that is going to storm stones. [3-22-24]_END

B_3_C_24_8
BEGIN_
रक्षसाम् नर्दताम् घोरः श्रूयते अयम् महाध्वनिः |आहतानाम् च भेरीणाम् राक्षसैः क्रूर कर्मभिः || ३-२४-१०_END
BEGIN_
"This nasty noise which we hear pertains to the uproar of demons, and even to the drumming of war drums 
by the demons of fiendish activities, and this is ear-splitting. [3-24-10]_END

B_3_C_25_1
BEGIN_
तम् दृष्ट्वा सगुणम् चापम् उद्यम्य खर निःस्वनम् |रामस्य अभिमुखम् सूतम् चोद्यताम् इति अचोदयत् || ३-२५-२_END
BEGIN_
On seeing Rama that bawling Khara raised his string-taut bow that makes an ass-like braying twang, drove 
his charioteer crazy saying, "drive to the fore of that Rama..." [3-25-2]_END

B_3_C_23_14
BEGIN_
खरस्य च रथस्थस्य नर्दमानस्य धीमतः || ३-२३-१६प्राकंपत भुजः सव्यः स्वरः च अस्य अवसज्जत |_END
BEGIN_
He who is raving while sitting in his chariot that clever Khara's left shoulder thrilled excessively, 
and his voice too quavered. [3-23-16b, 17a]_END

B_3_C_24_9
BEGIN_
अनागत विधानम् तु कर्तव्यम् शुभम् इच्छ्हता |आपदम् शंकमानेन पुरुषेण विपश्चिता || ३-२४-११_END
BEGIN_
"Preventive measures are to be effectuated for any imminent situation by any well-wishing person, or 
by a person with misgivings about a danger, or by a person of talent. [3-24-11]_END

B_3_C_25_2
BEGIN_
स खरस्य आज्ञया सूतः तुरगान् समचोदयत् |यत्र रामो महाबाहुः एको धुन्वन् धनुः स्थितः || ३-२५-३_END
BEGIN_
On the orders of Khara the charioteer drove the horses to there where the mighty armed Rama is standing 
single-handedly while swaying his bow. [3-25-3]_END

B_3_C_23_15
BEGIN_
स अस्रा संपद्यते दृष्टिः पश्यमानस्य सर्वतः || ३-२३-१७ललाटे च रुजो जाता न च मोहात् न्यवर्तत |_END
BEGIN_
While he is seeing everywhere his eyes spawned tears for no good reason, his forehead ached, but he 
did not retrace his steps owing to his own vanity. [3-23-17b, 18a]_END

B_3_C_24_10
BEGIN_
तस्मात् गृहीत्वा वैदेहीम् शर पाणिः धनुर् धरः |गुहाम् आश्रय शैलस्य दुर्गाम् पादप संकुलाम् || ३-२४-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Hence, wield your bow, keep arrows ready at hand, and taking Vaidehi with you seek shelter in a impassable 
cave of a mountain overgrown with trees. [3-24-12]_END

B_3_C_25_3
BEGIN_
तम् तु निष्पतितम् दृष्ट्वा सर्वे ते रजनी चराः |मुंचमाना महानादम् सचिवाः पर्यवारयन् || ३-२५-४_END
BEGIN_
On seeing Khara descending on Rama then all those nightwalkers who are the deputies of Khara encircled 
Khara venting out loud battle cries. [3-25-4]_END

B_3_C_23_16
BEGIN_
तान् समीक्ष्य महोत्पातान् उत्थितान् रोम हर्षणान् || ३-२३-१८अब्रवीत् राक्षसान् सर्वान् प्रहसन् स 
खरः तदा |_END
BEGIN_
On observing those worst auguries stemming up at that moment with hair-raising nature, Khara laughed 
them off and said this to all of the demons. [3-23-18b, 19a]_END

B_3_C_24_11
BEGIN_
प्रतिकूलितुम् इच्छ्हामि न हि वाक्यम् इदम् त्वया |शापितो मम पादाभ्याम् गम्यताम् वत्स मा चिरम् || 
३-२४-१३_END
BEGIN_
"I wish you to gainsay me for this word of mine, my boy, have honour on my feet and be gone not before 
long. [3-24-13]_END

B_3_C_25_4
BEGIN_
स तेषाम् यातुधानानाम् मध्ये रथः गतः खरः |बभूव मध्ये ताराणाम् लोहिता.ंग इव उदितः || ३-२५-५_END
BEGIN_
Khara staying on his chariot in the thick of those demons appeared to be like coppery-red planet Mars 
up-shot in the thick of stars. [3-25-5]_END

B_3_C_23_17
BEGIN_
महा उत्पातान् इमान् सर्वान् उत्थितान् घोर दर्शनान् || ३-२३-१९न चिंतयामि अहम् वीर्यात् बलवान् दुर्बलान् 
इव |_END
BEGIN_
"These awful auguries with their horrible nature have arisen, but owing to my own valour I am unbothered 
about all of them as with a mighty one unworried of the mightless. [3-23-19b, 20a]_END

B_3_C_24_12
BEGIN_
त्वम् हि शूरः च बलवान् हन्या एतान् न संशयः |स्वयम् निहन्तुम् इच्छ्हमि सर्वान् एव निशाचरान् || ३-२४-१४_END
BEGIN_
"You are a stalwart, a forceful one, and for sure you can eliminate them all, it is doubtless, but I 
long to eliminate all of the nightwalkers, personally" Rama said thus to Lakshmana. [3-24-14]_END

B_3_C_23_18
BEGIN_
तारा अपि शरैः तीक्ष्णैः पातयेयम् नभः तलात् || ३-२३-२०मृत्युम् मरण धर्मेण संक्रुद्धो योजयामि अहम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
"With the excruciating arrows of mine I can hurtle stars from the face of sky, and if highly infuriated, 
I can even enjoin mortality to Death himself. [3-23-20b, 21a]_END

B_3_C_25_5
BEGIN_
ततः शर सहस्रेन रामम् अप्रतिम ओजसम् |अर्दयित्वाअ महानादम् ननाद समरे खरः || ३-२५-६_END
BEGIN_
In his proneness to war then Khara assaulted that uniquely forceful Rama with a thousand arrows and 
blared a roaring battle cry. [3-25-6]_END

B_3_C_24_13
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु रामेण लक्ष्मणः सह सीतया |शरान् आदाय चापम् च गुहाम् दुर्गाम् समाश्रयत् || ३-२४-१५_END
BEGIN_
When Rama said to him that way, Lakshmana picked up his bow and arrows, and together with Seetha he 
took shelter in an unreachable cave. [3-24-15]_END

B_3_C_25_6
BEGIN_
ततः तम् भीम धन्वानम् क्रुद्धाः सर्वे निशाचराः |रामम् नाना विधैः शस्त्रैः अभ्यवर्षन्त दुर्जयम् || 
३-२५-७_END
BEGIN_
All of those infuriated nightwalkers then incessantly rained diverse weapons on that invincibleRama 
who is handling a horrific bow. [3-25-7]_END

B_3_C_23_19
BEGIN_
राघवम् तम् बल उत्सिक्तम् भ्रातरम् च अस्य लक्ष्मणम् || ३-२३-२१अहत्वा सायकैः तीक्ष्णैः न उपावर्तितुम् 
उत्सहे |_END
BEGIN_
"I am reluctant to return without killing that Rama, a haughty one by his might, together with his brother 
Lakshmana, with my incisive arrows. [3-23-21b, 22a]_END

B_3_C_24_14
BEGIN_
तस्मिन् प्रविष्टे तु गुहाम् लक्ष्मणे सह सीतया |हन्त निर्युक्तम् इति उक्त्वा रामः कवचम् आविशत् || 
३-२४-१६_END
BEGIN_
On Lakshmana's entering into cave along with Seetha, Rama said to himself, "thank goodness, it is a 
good-idea!" and thus saying he donned his shield. [3-24-16]_END

B_3_C_25_7
BEGIN_
मुद्गरैः आयसैः शूलैः प्रासैः खड्गैः परश्वधैः |राक्षसाः समरे रामम् निजघ्नू रोष तत्पराः || ३-२५-८_END
BEGIN_
Those demons that are already caught up with rancour bombarded Rama with bludgeons, lances, tridents, 
darts and hatchets. [3-25-8]_END

B_3_C_23_20
BEGIN_
यन् निमित्तम् तु रामस्य लक्ष्मणस्य विपर्ययः || ३-२३-२२सकामा भगिनी मे अस्तु पीत्वा तु रुधिरम् तयोः 
|_END
BEGIN_
"In whose respect both Rama and Lakshmana behaved perversely, let that sister of mine be contented in 
drinking the blood of those two. [3-23-22b, 23a]_END

B_3_C_26_0
BEGIN_
दूषणः तु स्वकम् सैन्यम् हन्यमानम् विलोक्य च |संदिदेश महाबाहुः भीम वेगान् निशाचरान् || ३-२६-१
राक्षसान् पंच साहस्रान् समरेषु अनिवर्तिनः |_END
BEGIN_
On seeing the shattering of his own forces, Duushana bid five thousand mighty-armed nightwalkers of 
monstrous impetus, and who knew no retreat in war, to attack Rama. [3-26-1]_END

B_3_C_24_15
BEGIN_
स तेन अग्नि निकाशेन कवचेन विभूषितः |बभूव रामः तिमिरे महान् अग्निर् इव उत्थितः || ३-२४-१७_END
BEGIN_
Well bedecked in a shield that has fire-like brilliance that Rama shone forth like a fumeless conflagration 
up-shot in utter darkness. [3-24-17]_END

B_3_C_25_8
BEGIN_
ते वलाहक संकाशा महाकाया महाबलाः |अभ्यधावन्त काकुत्स्थम् रथैः वाजिभिः एव च || ३-२५-९गजैः पर्वत 
कूट अभैः रामम् युद्धे जिंघासवः |_END
BEGIN_
Those massive bodied and exceptionally mighty demons came jostling like immense clouds in their eagerness 
to kill Rama in that war, while some mounted on chariots and horsebacks, and some more riding mountain-ridges 
like elephants rushed in on Rama. [3-25-9,10a]_END

B_3_C_23_21
BEGIN_
न क्वचित् प्राप्त पूर्वो मे संयुगेषु पराजयः || ३-२३-२३युष्माकम् एतत् प्रत्यक्षम् न अनृतम् कथयामि 
अहम् |_END
BEGIN_
"No defeat has chanced on me in combats at anytime and anywhere, that to you all is obvious and I tell 
no untruth. [3-23-23b, 24a]_END

B_3_C_26_1
BEGIN_
ते शूलैः पट्टिशैः कदगैः शिला वरषैः द्रुमैः || ३-२६-२शर वर्षैः विच्छ्हिन्नम् ववर्षुः तम् समन्ततः 
|_END
BEGIN_
And they with spears, scimitars, swords, and with the rains of boulders, trees and arrows rained incessantly 
and inordinately upon Rama from all over. [3-26-2b, 3a]_END

B_3_C_24_16
BEGIN_
स चापम् उद्यम्य महत् शरान् आदाय वीर्यवान् |संबभूव अवस्थितः तत्र ज्या स्वनैः पूरयन् दिशः || ३-२४-१८_END
BEGIN_
On raising his imposing bow and drawing arrows, that valorous Rama firmed up and stood there, filling 
all the directions with the tinny sounds of bowstring. [3-24-18]_END

B_3_C_23_22
BEGIN_
देव राजम् अपि क्रुद्धो मत्त ऐरावत गामिनम् || ३-२३-२४वज्र हस्तम् रणे हन्याम् किम् पुनः तौ च मानुषौ 
|_END
BEGIN_
"If I am infuriated I can eliminate even the king of gods, wielder of Thunderbolt and a trekker on ruttish 
elephant Iravata, namely Indra in a war, then why talk about these two humans." Thus Khara addressed 
his troops. [3-23-24b, 25a]_END

B_3_C_25_9
BEGIN_
ते रामे शर वर्षाणि व्यसृजन् रक्षसाम् गणाः || ३-२५-१०शैलेन्द्रम् इव धाराभिर् वर्षमाणा महाधनाः |_END
BEGIN_
And those bands of demons have outpoured arrows on Rama, as with enormous black-clouds disemboguing 
torrents on a lofty mountain. [3-25-10b, 11a]_END

B_3_C_26_2
BEGIN_
तत् द्रुमाणाम् शिलानाम् च वर्षम् प्राण हरम् महत् || ३-२६-३प्रतिजग्राह धर्मात्मा राघवः तीक्ष्ण सायकैः 
|_END
BEGIN_
Raghava, the virtue-souled, in his turn has neutralised that ghastly and life-taking storm of boulders 
and trees with his fierce arrows. [3-26-3b, 4a]_END

B_3_C_24_17
BEGIN_
ततो देवाः सगन्धर्वाः सिद्धाः च सह चारणैः |समेयुः च महात्मनो युद्ध दर्शन कांक्षया || ३-२४-१९_END
BEGIN_
Gods with gandharva-s and great-souled siddha-s along with carana-s have then met one another and came 
there aspiring to see the war. [3-24-19]_END

B_3_C_23_23
BEGIN_
सा तस्य गर्जितम् श्रुत्वा राक्षसाअनाम् महा चमूः || ३-२३-२५प्रहर्षम् अतुलम् लेभे मृत्यु पाश अवपाशिता 
|_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that thundering speech of Khara that sizeable army of demons which is tied down by the noose 
of death obtained an incomparable rejoice. [3-23-25b, 26a]_END

B_3_C_25_10
BEGIN_
सर्वैः परिवृतो रामो राक्षसैः कॄरदर्शिनैः || ३-२५-११तिथिषु इव महादेवो वृतः पारिषदाम् गणैः |_END
BEGIN_
When hemmed in with those grisly-looking demons Rama appeared like Rudra surrounded by his divine retinue 
called prathama gaNa-s, on certain days, whereupon he starts his all-destructive 
cosmic-dance. [3-25-11b, 12a]_END

B_3_C_26_3
BEGIN_
प्रतिगृह्य च तद् वर्षम् निमीलित इव ऋषभः || ३-२६-४रामः क्रोधम् परम् लेभे वध अर्थम् सर्व रक्षसाम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
Like a bull receiving rain with closed eyes Rama assimilated that storming and then evoked an inordinate 
infuriation for eliminating all of the demons. [3-26-4b, 5a]_END

B_3_C_23_24
BEGIN_
समेयुः च महात्मानो युद्ध दर्शन कांक्षिणः || ३-२३-२६ऋषयो देव गन्धर्वाः सिद्धाः च सह चारणैः |_END
BEGIN_
Then desiring to see the war of Khara with Rama, great-souls like sages, gods, gandharva-s along with 
carana-s and siddha-s have come together in firmament. [3-23-26b, 27a]_END

B_3_C_24_18
BEGIN_
ऋषयः च महात्मनो लोके ब्रह्मर्षि सत्तमाः |समेत्य च ऊचुः सहिताः ते अन्योन्यम् पुण्य कर्मणः || ३-२४-२०_END
BEGIN_
The great-souled sages and those that are known in worlds as eminent Brahma-sages, on their coming together 
those beings of pious exploits spoke to one another, among themselves. [3-24-20]_END

B_3_C_25_11
BEGIN_
तानि मुक्तानि शस्त्राणि यातुधानैः स राघवः || ३-२५-१२प्रतिजग्राह विशिखैः नदि ओघान् इव सागरः |_END
BEGIN_
That Raghava has pre-empted those arrows discharged by the demons with his excruciatingly pointed arrows 
as an ocean would do with the river's onrush. [3-25-12b, 13a]_END

B_3_C_26_4
BEGIN_
ततः क्रोध समाविष्टः प्रदीप्त इव तेजसा || ३-२६-५शरैः अभ्यकिरत् सैन्यम् सर्वतः सह दूषणम् |_END
BEGIN_
Exasperation prevailing on him who appeared to be highly blazing with the blaze of his own virtue, he 
then diffused Duushana and his army with arrows from all over. [3-26-5b, 6a]_END

B_3_C_23_25
BEGIN_
समेत्य च ऊचुः सहिताः ते अन्यायम् पुण्यकर्मणः || ३-२३-२७स्वस्ति गो ब्राह्मणेभ्यो अस्तु लोकानाम् ये 
च सम्मताः |_END
BEGIN_
On gathering at a place those great souls met one another and said, "let good betide cows, Brahmans 
and those that are held respectful by the people at large." [3-23-27b, 28a]_END

B_3_C_24_19
BEGIN_
स्वस्ति गो ब्राह्मणानाम् च लोकानाम् च इति संस्थिताः |जयताम् राघवो युद्धे पौलस्त्यान् रजनी चरान् 
|| ३-२४-२१चक्र हस्तो यथा युद्धे सर्वान् असुर पु.ंगवान् |_END
BEGIN_
"Let good betide cows, Brahmans and those people that are abiding in all the worlds. Raghava shall be 
victorious in the war over the clansmen of Sage Paulastya, the nightwalkers." Thus they talked among 
themselves. [3-24-21]_END

B_3_C_25_12
BEGIN_
स तैः प्रहरणैः घोरैः भिन्न गात्रो न विव्यथे || ३-२५-१३रामः प्रदीप्तैर् बहुभिर् वज्रैर् इव महा अचलः 
|_END
BEGIN_
Even if his body is gashed with those gruesome assault weapons Rama is not enfeebled, as with the enormous 
Mt. Meru that can withstand even if battered by very many highly blazing thunderbolts of Indra. [3-25-13, 
14a]_END

B_3_C_26_5
BEGIN_
ततः सेना पतिः क्रुद्धो दूषणः शत्रु दूषणः || ३-२६-६शरैः अशनि कल्पैः तम् राघवम् समवारयत् |_END
BEGIN_
And on becoming enraged Duushana, the railer of his rivals and the commander of that army, then virtually 
forestalled Raghava's onslaught with his arrows that are simulative of thunderbolts. [3-26-6b, 7a]_END

B_3_C_23_26
BEGIN_
जयताम् राघवो युद्धे पौलस्त्यान् रजनी चरान् || ३-२३-२८चक्रहस्तो यथा विष्णुः सर्वान् असुर सत्तमान् 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Let Raghava triumph over these mighty night walkers from the lineage of Pulastya, as with Vishnu who 
once conquered all the mighty demons in war." So said celestials to one another. [3-23-28]_END

B_3_C_24_20
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्त्वा पुनः प्र ऊचुः आलोक्य च परस्परम् || ३-२४-२२चतुर्दश सहस्राणि रक्षसाम् भीम कर्मणाम् |
एकः च रामो धर्मात्मा कथम् युद्धम् भविष्यति || ३-२४-२३_END
BEGIN_
Thus speaking they also well-said again, looking at each other "the demons of fiendish deeds are fourteen 
thousand in number and this virtue-souled Rama is solitary... what would be the result of this war!" 
Thus the sages discussed among themselves. [3-24-22b, 23]_END

B_3_C_25_13
BEGIN_
स विद्धः क्षतज दिग्धः सर्व गात्रेषु राघवः || ३-२५-१४बभूव रामः सन्ध्य अभ्रैः दिवाकर इव आवृतः |_END
BEGIN_
Bruised and bedaubed with blood on all his limbs that Rama of Raghu's dynasty took shape of the sun 
enshrouded by cloudscapes at eventide. [3-25-14b, 15a]_END

B_3_C_26_6
BEGIN_
ततो रामः संक्रुद्धः क्षुरेण अस्य महत् धनुः || ३-२६-७चिच्छ्हेद समरे वीरः चतुर्भिः चतुरो हयान् |_END
BEGIN_
That valiant one in warring Rama is then infuriated and with his crescent-barbed arrow shivered the 
sturdy bow of Duushana, shredding four of his horses with four more arrows. [3-26-7b, 8a]_END

B_3_C_27_0
BEGIN_
खरम् तु राम अभिमुखम् प्रयांतम् वाहिनी पतिः |राक्षसः त्रिशिरा नाम संनिपत्य इदम् अब्रवीत् || ३-२७-१_END
BEGIN_
But when Khara is about to lunge to the forefront of Rama, nearing him the commander of demonic forces 
named Trishira spoke this to him. [3-27-1]_END

B_3_C_23_27
BEGIN_
एतत् च अन्यत् च बहुशो ब्रुवाणाः परम ऋषयः || ३-२३-२९जात कौतूहलात् तत्र विमानस्थाः च देवताः |ददृशुर् 
वाहिनीम् तेषाम् राक्षसानाम् गत आयुषाम् || ३-२३-३०_END
BEGIN_
While the great sages are speaking about this and many other topics, they and the gods abiding in their 
aircrafts have inquisitively seen the flow of army of demons, whose longevity is now beyond hope. [3-23-29, 
30]_END

B_3_C_25_14
BEGIN_
विषेदुर् देव गन्धर्वाः सिद्धाः च परम ऋषयः || ३-२५-१५एकम् सहस्रैः बहुभिः तदा दृष्ट्वा समावृतम् |_END
BEGIN_
On seeing lone Rama beset by many demons, then the gods, celestials, saints and sublime-sages are dispirited. 
[3-25-15b, 16a]_END

B_3_C_24_21
BEGIN_
इति राजर्षयः सिद्धाः स गणाः च द्विजर्षभाः |जात कौतूहलात् तस्थुर् विमानस्थाः च देवता || ३-२४-२४_END
BEGIN_
Thus the assemblages of kingly-sages, siddha-s and the eminent Brahmans, along with gods that are staying 
in their aircrafts, tarried there in the firmament peering inquisitively at Rama. [3-24-24]_END

B_3_C_26_7
BEGIN_
हत्वा च अश्वान् शरैः तीक्ष्णैः अर्थ चन्द्रेण सारथे || ३-२६-८शिरो जहार तद् रक्षः त्रिभिर् विव्याध 
वक्षसि |_END
BEGIN_
On destructing the horses with excruciating arrows, he even fragmented the head of the charioteer with 
a crescent-barbed arrow, and even impaled the chest of demon Duushana with some more arrows. [3-26-8b, 
9a]_END

B_3_C_27_1
BEGIN_
माम् नियोजय विक्रांतम् त्वम् निवर्तस्व साहसात् |पश्य रामम् महाबाहुम् संयुगे विनिपातितम् || ३-२७-२_END
BEGIN_
"Desisting from your personal adventure you enjoin me for I am an invader, and then you are certain 
to see me felling that mighty-armed Rama in combat. [3-27-2]_END

B_3_C_23_28
BEGIN_
रथेन तु खरो वेगात् सैन्यस्य अग्रात् विनिःसृतः |श्येनगामी पृथुग्रीवो यज्ञशत्रुः विहंगमः || ३-२३-३१
दुर्जयः करवीराक्षः परुषः कालकार्मुकः |हेममाली महामाली सर्पाअस्यो रुधिराशनः || ३-२३-३२द्वादश 
एते महावीर्याः प्रतस्थुः अभितः खरम् |_END
BEGIN_
Khara speedily bolted in his chariot to the van of his legions, and on seeing that demon Khara going 
in front other important demons too rushed to fore. They are Shyenagaami, Prithugviira, Yajnashatru, 
Vihamgama and also Durjaya, Karaviiraaksha, Parusha, Kaalakaarmuka, Hemamaali, Mahaamaali, Sarpaasya, 
Rudhiraaksha. These twelve highly valorous demons cruised in a semicircle around Khara. [3-23-31]_END

B_3_C_24_22
BEGIN_
आविष्टम् तेजसा रामम् स.ंग्राम शिरसि स्थितम् |दृष्ट्वा सर्वाणि भूतानि भयात् विव्यथिरे तदा || ३-२४-२५_END
BEGIN_
Immured in an aura of invincibility Rama is standing up to the war in its vanguard, and then on seeing 
at him all beings went into the throes of dread. [3-24-25]_END

B_3_C_25_15
BEGIN_
ततो रामः तु सुसंक्रुद्धो मण्डली कृत कार्मुकः || ३-२५-१६ससर्ज निशितान् बाणान् शतशः अथ सहस्रशः |_END
BEGIN_
But Rama on becoming highly infuriated curved his bow to a full circularity on stretching the bowstring 
up to his ear, and then jetted out trenchant arrows in hundreds. Why hundreds? He surged them in thousands. 
[3-25-16b, 17a]_END

B_3_C_26_8
BEGIN_
स च्छ्हिन्न धन्वा विरथो हत अश्वो हत सारथिः || ३-२६-९जग्राह गिरि शृंग आभम् परिघम् रोम हर्षणम् |
वेष्टितम् कांचनैः पट्टैः देव सैन्य अभिमर्दनम् || ३-२६-१०आयसैः शंकुभिः तीक्ष्णैः कीर्णम् पर वसा उक्षिताम् 
|वज्र अशनि सम स्पर्शम् पर गोपुर दारणम् || ३-२६-११_END
BEGIN_
With his bow fractured and chariot shredded, and with horses and charioteer killed, he that Duushana 
grabbed a mace which outranks a peak of mountain and a hair-thriller at its sight, and which girt with 
golden girths once gritted the armies of gods, the head of which is studded with incisive iron spikes 
and saturated with the fat of foes, a coequal of a diamond and a thunderbolt in its hardiness and flashiness, 
and a ransacker of the archways of fortresses of his adversaries. [3-26-9b, 10, 11]_END

B_3_C_27_2
BEGIN_
प्रतिजानामि ते सत्यम् आयुधम् च अहम् आलभे |यथा रामम् वधिष्यामि वधार्हम् सर्व रक्षसाम् || ३-२७-३_END
BEGIN_
"Taking oath on my weapon I promise to you that I truly wish to kill this Rama, as he deserves ill of 
all the demons by killing. [3-27-3]_END

B_3_C_23_29
BEGIN_
महाकपालः स्थूलाक्षः प्रमाथी त्रिशिराः तथा |चत्वार एते सेना अग्रे दूषणम् पृष्ठतो अन्वयुः || ३-२३-३३_END
BEGIN_
Likewsie Mahakapaala, Stuulaaksha, Pramaathii, Trishira are the four commanders of demonic forces and 
they followed Duushana marching at his behind. [3-23-33]_END

B_3_C_25_16
BEGIN_
दुरवारान् दुर्विषहान् कालपाश उपमान् रणे || ३-२५-१७मुमोच लीलया रामः कंकपत्रान् कांचन भूषणान् |_END
BEGIN_
In that war Rama sportily discharged eagle-feathered arrows adorned in gold which are unstoppable and 
intolerable, and which in simile are the leads of Time-god. [3-25-17b, 18a]_END

B_3_C_24_23
BEGIN_
रूपम् अप्रतिमम् तस्य रामस्य अक्लिष्ट कर्मणः |बभूव रूपम् क्रुद्धस्य रुद्रस्य इव महात्मनः || ३-२४-२६_END
BEGIN_
That nonesuch aspect of Rama whose deeds are unharmful to any, has become the aspect of wrathful supreme-souled 
Rudra. [3-24-26]_END

B_3_C_26_9
BEGIN_
तम् महा उरग संकाशम् प्रगृह्य परिघम् रणे |दूषणो अभ्यपतत् रामम् क्रूर कर्मा निशाचरः || ३-२६-१२_END
BEGIN_
On firmly gripping that mace which in war is akin to an infernal serpent, and the touch of which tantamount 
to snakebite, rushed that nightwalker Duushana with infernal exerts rushed towards Rama. [3-26-12]_END

B_3_C_27_3
BEGIN_
अहम् वा अस्य रणे मृत्युः एष वा समरे मम |विनिवर्त्य रण उत्साहम् मुहूर्तम् प्राश्निको भव || ३-२७-४_END
BEGIN_
"Hold back your combative-adventurism and become an examiner to decide whether I am going to become 
his god of death in this combat, or he becomes mine. [3-27-4]_END

B_3_C_23_30
BEGIN_
सा भीम वेगा समर अभिकांक्षिणीसुदारुणा राक्षस वीर सेना |तौ राज पुत्रौ सहसा अभ्युपेतामाला ग्रहाणाम् 
इव चन्द्र सूर्यौ || ३-२३-३४_END
BEGIN_
That army of valiant demons which is highly execrable, infernally speedy, and readily inspirited for 
a battle quickly rushed towards those two princes, Rama and Lakshmana, as though a festoon of planets 
would rush towards the Moon and Sun so as to put them to rout. [3-23-34]_END

B_3_C_25_17
BEGIN_
ते शराः शत्रु सैन्येषु मुक्ता रामेण लीलया || ३-२५-१८आददू रक्षसाम् प्राणान् पाशाः कालकृता इव |_END
BEGIN_
Those arrows that are playfully discharged on the army of enemy have grabbed the lives of demons like 
the tethers flung by the Time-god. [3-25-18b, 19a]_END

B_3_C_24_24
BEGIN_
इति संभाष्यमाणो तु देव गंधर्व चारणैः |ततो गंभीर निर्ह्रादम् घोर चर्म आयुध ध्वजम् ||३-२४-२७अनीकम् 
यातुधानानाम् समन्तात् प्रत्यदृश्यत |वीर आलापान् विसृजताम् अन्योन्यम् अभिगच्छ्हताम् || ३-२४-२८
चापानि विस्फरयताम् जृंभताम् च अपि अभीक्ष्णशः |विप्रघुष्ट स्वनानाम् च दुंदुभीम् च अपि निघ्नताम् || 
३-२४-२९_END
BEGIN_
While gods, gandharva-s, carana-s are conversing thus, then they have seen there the legions of the 
demons arriving from all over with boisterous noises, spouting cries of bravo, handling their grisly 
skins, shields, weaponry and war-flags, and onrushing at each other in disarray. With brassy twanging 
of bows, with the drumming of war drums, and even by their jumping, leaping and bouncing that area is 
filled with very loud and clamorous noise. [3-24-27, 28, 29]_END

B_3_C_26_10
BEGIN_
तस्य अभिपतमानस्य दूषणस्य स राघवः |द्वाभ्याम् शराभ्याम् चिच्छ्हेद स हस्त आभरणौ भुजौ || ३-२६-१३_END
BEGIN_
While Duushana came falling on, he that Raghava sheared off his shoulders that have wrist-ornaments 
on his arms with two arrows. [3-26-13]_END

B_3_C_27_4
BEGIN_
प्रहृष्टो वा हते रामे जनस्थानम् प्रयास्यसि |मयि वा निहते रामम् संयुगाय प्रयास्यसि || ३-२७-५_END
BEGIN_
"If I were to kill Rama you may gladly proceed to Janasthaana, else if Rama kills me then you can adventurously 
proceed against him for a combat." Thus Trishira spoke to Khara. [3-27-5]_END

B_3_C_25_18
BEGIN_
भित्त्वा राक्षस देहान् ताम् ते शरा रुधिर आप्लुताः || ३-२५-१९अंतरिक्ष गता रेजुः दीप्त अग्नि सम तेजसः 
|_END
BEGIN_
On impaling the bodies demons, the arrows swamped in blood have gone into welkin, where they are aglow 
with flares equalling inflamed flames. [3-25-19b, 20a]_END

B_3_C_24_25
BEGIN_
तेषाम् सुतुमुलः शब्दः पूरयामास तद् वनम् |तेन शब्देन वित्रस्ताः श्वापदा वन चारिणः || ३-२४-३०दुद्रुवुः 
यत्र निःशब्दम् पृष्ठतो न अवलोकयन् |_END
BEGIN_
When highly brutish cacophony of demons started to fill the forest, that jangling even panicked the 
brutes ranging in that forest, and those beasts dashed off to other places where silence prevailed, 
without looking back. [3-24-30, 31a]_END

B_3_C_26_11
BEGIN_
भ्रष्टः तस्य महाकायः पपात रण मूर्धनि |परिघः छ्हिन्न हस्तस्य शक्र ध्वज इव अग्रतः || ३-२६-१४_END
BEGIN_
When Duushana's arms are thus sheared in the van of war, his gigantic mace slipped and spun in his own 
front, like the flagstaff with flag raised in honour of Indra, and collapsed . [3-26-14]_END

B_3_C_27_5
BEGIN_
खरः त्रिशिरसा तेन मृत्यु लोभात् प्रसादितः |गच्छ्ह युध्य इति अनुज्ञातो राघव अभिमुखो ययौ || ३-२७-६_END
BEGIN_
By that death-greedy demon Trishira, Khara is manoeuvred and Khara to him said 'begone... combat...' 
and thus permitted, Trishira proceeded to the forefront of Rama. [3-27-6]_END

B_3_C_25_19
BEGIN_
असंख्येयाः तु रामस्य सायकाः चाप मण्डलात् || ३-२५-२०विनिष्पेतुः अतीव उग्रा रक्षः प्राण अपहारिणः |_END
BEGIN_
Innumerable and highly frightening arrows fusilladed from the nimbus of the bow of Rama that resulted 
as the filchers of the lives of demons. [3-25-20b, 21a]_END

B_3_C_24_26
BEGIN_
तत् च अनीकम् महावेगम् रामम् समनुवर्तत || ३-२४-३१घृत नाना प्रहरणम् गंभीरम् सागरोपमम् |_END
BEGIN_
And that foolhardy army of demons which in simile is like an unnavigable ocean steered towards Rama 
handling many assault weapons. [3-24-31b, 32a]_END

B_3_C_26_12
BEGIN_
कराभ्याम् च विकीर्णाभ्याम् पपात भुवि दूषणः |विषाणाभ्याम् विशीर्णाभ्याम् मनस्वी इव महागजः || ३-२६-१५_END
BEGIN_
With both of his arms strewn around Duushana fell down onto earth like a haughty and gigantic elephant 
when both of its tusks are broken down. [3-26-15]_END

B_3_C_27_6
BEGIN_
त्रिशिराः तु रथेन एव वाजि युक्तेन भास्वता |अभ्यद्रवत् रणे रामम् त्रि शृंग इव पर्वतः || ३-२७-७_END
BEGIN_
Trishira with a lustrous chariot that is yoked with equally lustrous horses hurried towards Rama in 
that war, like a tri-peaked mountain, for they say, he is a tri-headed demon. [3-27-7]_END

B_3_C_25_20
BEGIN_
तैः धनूंषि ध्वज अग्राणि चर्माणि च शिरांसि च || ३-२५-२१बहून् स हस्त आभरणान् ऊरून् करि कर उपमान् |
चिछ्हेद रामः समरे शतशः अथ सहस्रशः || ३-२५-२२_END
BEGIN_
In that war, shooting now with hundreds, and now with thousands of such arrows, Rama shredded those 
many bows, pinnacles of war-flags, armours and the like. And even shred are the heads of demons, along 
with their ornamented arms and thighs similar to the trunks of elephants. [3-25-21b, 22]_END

B_3_C_24_27
BEGIN_
रामो अपि चारयन् चक्षुः सर्वतो रण पण्डितः || ३-२४-३२ददर्श खर सैन्यम् तत् युद्ध अभिमुखो गतः |_END
BEGIN_
Casting his sight all-over even that war-expert Rama has seen that army of Khara lunging at a conflict. 
[3-24-32b, 33a]_END

B_3_C_26_13
BEGIN_
दृष्ट्वा तम् पतितम् भूमौ दूषणम् निहतम् रणे |साधु साधु इति काकुत्स्थम् सर्व भूतानि अपूजयन् || ३-२६-१६_END
BEGIN_
On seeing Duushana eliminated and fallen to ground, all the beings have applauded Rama saying, 'good, 
good...' [3-26-16]_END

B_3_C_27_7
BEGIN_
शर धारा समूहान् स महामेघ इव उत्सृजन् |व्यसृजत् सदृशम् नादम् जल आर्द्रस्य इव दुन्दुभेः || ३-२७-८_END
BEGIN_
Discharging hosts of arrow-torrents like a hefty-arrow-cloud, he readily discharged a noise similar 
to the thudding drumbeat when a water-wet war-drum is beaten, rather than a blast from a heated drum. 
[3-27-8]_END

B_3_C_25_21
BEGIN_
हयान् कांचन सन्नाहान् रथ युक्तान् स सारथीन् |गजाम् च स गज आरोहान् स हयान् सारधिनः तदा || ३-२५-२३
चिछ्हिदुः बिभिदुः च एव राम बाणा गुण च्युताः |पदातीन् समरे हत्वा हि अनयत् यम सदनम् || ३-२५-२४_END
BEGIN_
With the arrows flung from the bow-bowstring-nimbus of Rama, he indeed shredded and scraped the horses 
hitched with golden harnesses, and the chariots to which they are yoked, and even their charioteers. 
Likewise, he even ripped off the elephants along with their riders, and the horses along with their 
cavaliers. And on eliminating infantrymen in that war Rama led them to the abode of Yama, the Time-god. 
[3-25-23, 24] [3-25-23]_END

B_3_C_24_28
BEGIN_
वितत्य च धनुर् भीमम् तूण्याः च उद्धृत्य सायकान् || ३-२४-३३क्रोधम् आहारयत् तीव्रम् वधार्थम् सर्व 
रक्षसाम् |_END
BEGIN_
Rama stretched his awesome bow to examine the taut of bowstring, and even whipped arrows out of quiver, 
and then adopted a mask of extreme wrath to eliminate all the demons. [3-24-33]_END

B_3_C_27_8
BEGIN_
आगच्छ्हंतम् त्रिशिरसम् राक्षसम् प्रेक्ष्य राघवः |धनुषा प्रतिजग्राह विधुन्वन् सायकान् शितान् || ३-२७-९_END
BEGIN_
On seeing the oncoming of that demon Trishira, Raghava welcomed him by speedily winnowing smarting arrows 
from his bow. [3-27-9]_END

B_3_C_26_14
BEGIN_
एतस्मिन् अन्तरे क्रुद्धाः त्रयः सेना अग्र यायिनः |संहत्य अभ्यद्रवन् रामम् मृत्यु पाश अवपाशिताः || 
३-२६-१७महाकपालः स्थूलाक्षः प्रमाथी च महाबलः |_END
BEGIN_
In the meantime infuriated are the three leading commanders of that army, namely Mahakapaala, Sthulaaksha 
and great mighty Pramaathii, and they collectively ran towards Rama, bound by the rein of death. [3-26-17, 
18a]_END

B_3_C_25_22
BEGIN_
ततो नालीक नाराचैः तीक्ष्ण अग्रैः विकर्णिभिः |भीमम् आर्त स्वरम् चक्रुः छ्हिद्यमाना निशाचराः || ३-२५-२५_END
BEGIN_
While ripped to pieces with tubular arrows, with arrows made of iron, and with sharp-edged and crescent-tipped 
arrows those demons have let out disgusting cries of anguish. [3-25-25]_END

B_3_C_24_29
BEGIN_
दुष्प्रेक्ष्यश्चाभवत्क्रुद्धोयुगान्ताग्निरिवज्वलन् - यद्वा -दुष्प्रेक्ष्यः च अभवत् क्रुद्धो युगान्त 
अग्निः इव ज्वलन् || ३-२४-३४तम् दृष्ट्वा तेजसा आविष्टम् प्राव्यथन् वन देवताः |_END
BEGIN_
And when he is enraged and blazing he became frightful-looking like the blazing Fire at the end of era, 
and on seeing such a Rama when he is pervaded with conflagration like anger, the pastoral deities are 
very much annoyed. [3-24-34]_END

B_3_C_27_9
BEGIN_
स संप्रहारः तुमुलो राम त्रिशिरसोः तदा |संबभूव अतीव बलिनोः सिंह कुं~जरयोः इव || ३-२७-१०_END
BEGIN_
That grave and tumultuous encounter chanced between Rama and Trishira is like the extremely forceful 
encounter between a loin and an elephant. [3-27-10]_END

B_3_C_26_15
BEGIN_
महाकपालो विपुलम् शूलम् उद्यम्य राक्षसः || ३-२६-१८स्थूलाक्षः पट्टिशम् गृह्य प्रमाथी च परश्वधम् |_END
BEGIN_
Mahakapaala raising a broad trident, Sthulaaksha handling a scimitar, Pramaathi handling an axe rushed 
towards Rama. [3-26-18b, 19a]_END

B_3_C_25_23
BEGIN_
तत् सैन्यम् निशितैः बाणैः अर्दितम् मर्म भेदिभिः |न रामेण सुखम् लेभे शुष्कम् वनम् इव अग्निना || ३-२५-२६_END
BEGIN_
When those arrows that gore the critical parts are thus harrowing, that army is discomposed like a forest 
burnt to a cinder by wild-fire. [3-25-26]_END

B_3_C_24_30
BEGIN_
तस्य रुष्ट्स्य रूपम् तु रामस्य ददृशे तदा |दक्षस्य इव क्रतुम् हन्तुम् उद्यतस्य पिनाकिनी || ३-२४-३५_END
BEGIN_
The all-pacific aspect of that Rama then in his exasperation appeared to be like that of the all-ruinous 
Rudra, the wielder of bow called Pinaki, namely peaceful Shiva when enraged, at the time of Rudra's 
embarking on to ruin the Vedic ritual of Daksha Prajaapati. [3-24-35]_END

B_3_C_27_10
BEGIN_
ततः त्रिशिरसा बाणैः ललाटे ताडितः त्रिभिः |अमर्षी कुपितो रामः संरब्धम् इदम् अब्रवीत् || ३-२७-११_END
BEGIN_
Later when Trishira smote on the forehead of highly enraged Rama with three arrows, Rama's ire is intensified 
and he franticly said this to that demon. [3-27-11]_END

B_3_C_26_16
BEGIN_
दृष्ट्वा एव आपततः ताम् तु राघवः सायकैः शितैः || ३-२६-१९तीक्ष्ण अग्रैः प्रतिजग्राह संप्राप्तान् अतिथीन् 
इव |_END
BEGIN_
As one would receive guests meeting his basic needs, Raghava too took on these untimely guests of war, 
rather the insurgents, meeting their basic needs which now are no more than highly sharpened acute edged 
arrows, when he saw them coming and falling upon him, inopportunely. [3-26-19b, 20a]_END

B_3_C_25_24
BEGIN_
केचिद् भीम बलाः शूराः प्रासान् शूलान् परश्वधान् |चिक्षिपुः परम क्रुद्धा रामाय रजनीचराः || ३-२५-२७_END
BEGIN_
Some of the grotesquely sinewy and braving nightwalkers are highly enraged and dashed their darts, tridents, 
and hatchets towards Rama. [3-25-27]_END

B_3_C_24_31
BEGIN_
तत् कार्मुकैः आभरणैः रथैः चतत् वर्माभिः च अग्नि समान वर्णैः |बभूव सैन्यम् पिशित अशनिनाम्
सूर्य उदये नीलम् इव अभ्र जालम् || ३-२४-३६_END
BEGIN_
That army of raw-flesh eaters with their bows, embellishments, and chariots, and also with their armours, 
all glittering with the dazzle of flaming fire, varied into a sky-blue coloured cluster of clouds on 
which the dazzling sunrays will be glittering at the dawning of the sun. [3-24-36]_END

B_3_C_27_11
BEGIN_
अहो विक्रम शूरस्य राक्षसस्य ईदृशम् बलम् |पुष्पैः इव शरैः यस्य ललाटे अस्मि परिक्षतः || ३-२७-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Oho! What an energy of a triumphing adventurer is this! A demon with this sort of energy is adventuring 
me, whose arrows rap my forehead peripherally, like flowers! [3-27-12]_END

B_3_C_26_17
BEGIN_
महाकपालस्य शिरः चिच्छ्हेद रघुनंदनः || ३-२६-२०असंख्येयैः तु बाण ओघैः प्रममाथ प्रमाथिनम् |स्थूलाक्षस्य 
अक्षिणी स्थूले पूरयामास सायकैः || ३-२६-२१स पपात हतो भूमौ विटपी इव महाद्रुमः |दूषणस्य अनुगान् 
पंच सहस्रान् कुपितः क्षणात् || ३-२६-२२हत्वा तु पंच सहस्रान् अनयत् यम सदनम् |_END
BEGIN_
Rama, the legatee of Raghu, chopped off the head of Mahakapaala, with incalculable spates of arrows 
he eliminated Pramaathi, and filled the bulging eyes of Sthulaaksha with arrows by which Sthulaaksha 
is killed and fell down onto ground like a burly tree with its broad branches. Then still infuriated 
Rama forthwith eliminated the five thousand hench-demons of Duushana with five thousand arrows, and 
thus he led them to the residence of Time-god, namely the hell. [3-26-20b, 21, 22, 23a]_END

B_3_C_25_25
BEGIN_
तेषाम् बाणैः महाबाहुः शस्त्राणि आवार्य वीर्यवान् |जहार समरे प्राणान् चिच्छ्हेद च शिरो धरान् || ३-२५-२८_END
BEGIN_
On fending off those weapons with his arrows that mighty armed and valorous Rama filched away their 
lives by shearing off their necks in that war. [3-25-28]_END

B_3_C_27_12
BEGIN_
मम अपि प्रतिगृह्णीष्व शरान् चाप गुण च्युतान् |एवम् उक्त्वा सुसंरब्धः शरान् आशीविष उपमान् || ३-२७-१३
त्रिशिरो वक्षसि क्रुद्धो निजघान चतुर् दश |_END
BEGIN_
"Now you accept arrows plunging from the string of my bow..." saying thus, that infuriated Rama with 
his alacritous swiftness hit the chest of Trishira with fourteen arrows similar to venomous snakes. 
[3-27-13, 14a]_END

B_3_C_26_18
BEGIN_
दूषणम् निहतम् श्रुत्वा तस्य च एव पदानुगान् || ३-२६-२३व्यादिदेश खरः क्रुद्धो सेन अध्यक्षान् महाबलान् 
|_END
BEGIN_
On hearing about the killing of Duushana and also thus of the followers of Duushana, Khara irately ordered 
his army captains, under whose captaincy mighty forces are there. [3-26-23b, 24a]_END

B_3_C_25_26
BEGIN_
ते छ्हिन्न शिरसः पेतुः छ्हिन्न चर्म शरासनाः |सुपर्ण वात विक्षिप्ता जगत्याम् पादपा यथा || ३-२५-२९_END
BEGIN_
Those demons crashed down to earth with their heads severed and shields and bows wrecked, like the trees 
strewn around on earth owing to the gust raised by Garuda, the Divine Eagle, when he takes a sudden 
flight in heavens. [3-25-29]_END

B_3_C_27_13
BEGIN_
चतुर्भिः तुरगान् अस्य शरैः संनत पर्वाभिः || ३-२७-१४न्यपातयत तेजस्वी चतुरः तस्य वाजिनः |_END
BEGIN_
With four of his straight shooting arrows that have hook-like barbs, that resplendent Rama hewed down 
four of the speedy horses of Trishira's chariot. [3-27-14b, 15a]_END

B_3_C_26_19
BEGIN_
अयम् विनिहतः संख्ये दूषणः स पदानुगाः || ३-२६-२४महत्या सेनया सार्धम् युद्ध्वा रामम् कुमानुषम् |
शस्त्रैः नाना विध अकारैः हनध्वम् सर्व राक्षसाः || ३-२६-२५_END
BEGIN_
"Duushana is killed in war along with his followers, hence all you demons, take formidable army, take 
weapons of diverse designs, combat and kill that evil-human Rama..." Thus Khara ordered the remaining 
demons. [3-26-24b, 25]_END

B_3_C_25_27
BEGIN_
अवशिष्टाः च ये तत्र विषण्णाः ते निशाचराः |खरम् एव अभ्यधावन्त शरणार्थम् शर आहताः || ३-२५-३०_END
BEGIN_
Those nightwalkers that are battered by those arrows and remaining there, they desperately rushed towards 
Khara alone seeking shelter. [3-25-30]_END

B_3_C_27_14
BEGIN_
अष्टभिः सायकैः सूतम् रथ उपस्थे न्यपातयत् || ३-२७-१५रामः चिच्छ्हेद बाणेन ध्वजम् च अस्य समुच्छ्ह्रितम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
With eight arrows Rama felled the charioteer from his settle on the chariot, and with one arrow ripped 
off the high flying flag on that chariot. [3-27-15b, 16a]_END

B_3_C_26_20
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्त्वा खरः क्रुद्धो रामम् एव अभि दुद्रुवे |श्येनगामी पृथुग्रीवो यज्ञशत्रुर् विहंगमः || ३-२६-२६
दुर्जयः करवीराक्षः परुषः कालकार्मुकः |हेममाली महामाली सर्पस्यो रुधिराशनः || ३-२६-२७द्वादश एते 
महावीर्या बल अध्यक्षाः स सैनिकाःरमम् एव अभ्यधावंत विसृजंतः शरोत्तमान् || ३-२६-२८_END
BEGIN_
Saying so Khara himself rushed towards Rama in rage, and Shyenagaami, Prithugriiva, Yajnashatru, Vihangama 
Durjaya, Karaviiraaksha, Parusha, Kaalakaarmuka, Hemamaali, Mahaamaali, Sarpaasya, and Rudhiraaksha 
are the twelve fiendishly atrocious troop leaders of demonic forces, and they too rushed towards Rama 
launching their atrocious arrows. [3-26-26, 27, 28]_END

B_3_C_25_28
BEGIN_
तान् सर्वान् धनुर् आदाय समाश्वास्य च दूषणः |अभ्यधावत सुसंक्रुद्धः क्रुद्धः [रुद्रम्] क्रुद्ध इव 
अन्तकः || ३-२५-३१_END
BEGIN_
Comforting all of them and taking his bow, very highly infuriated Duushana rushed towards that infuriated 
Rama like the furious Eliminator Yama._END

B_3_C_27_15
BEGIN_
ततो हत रथात् तस्मात् उत्पतंतम् निशाचरम् || ३-२७-१६चिच्छ्हेद रामः तम् बाणैः हृदये सो अभवत् जडः |_END
BEGIN_
When that nightwalker is vaulting from that smashed chariot Rama with his arrows tore his chest to shreds 
and he that Trishira became inert. [3-27-16b, 17a]_END

B_3_C_26_21
BEGIN_
ततः पावक संकाशैः हेम वज्र विभूषितैः |जघन शेषम् तेजस्वी तस्य सैन्यस्य सायकैः || ३-२६-२९_END
BEGIN_
He who is resplendent that Rama then annihilated the remaining demons of that army with his arrows that 
are embellished with gold and diamonds, and that are blazing like ritual-fires. [3-26-29]_END

B_3_C_25_29
BEGIN_
निवृत्ताः तु पुनः सर्वे दूषण आश्रय निर्भयाः |रामम् एव अभ्यधावन्त साल ताल शिल आयुधाः || ३-२५-३२_END
BEGIN_
Coming under the shelter of Duushana all of those demons are but emboldened and returned, and they once 
again rushed towards Rama with saala trees, palm trees and boulders as their weapons. [3-25-32]_END

B_3_C_27_16
BEGIN_
सायकैः च अप्रमेय आत्मा सामर्षः तस्य रक्षसः || ३-२७-१७शिरांसि अपातयत् त्रीणि वेगवद्भिः त्रिभिः शतैः 
|_END
BEGIN_
And with three sharp and rapid arrows, and even with his own exasperation, Rama of inestimable aptitude 
rolled the three heads that demon. [3-27-17b, 18a]_END

B_3_C_26_22
BEGIN_
ते रुक्म पुंखा विशिखाः स धूमा इव पावकाः |निजघ्नुः तानि रक्षांसि वज्रा इव महाद्रुमान् || ३-२६-३०_END
BEGIN_
With those arrows that have golden tailpieces and sharp barbs, and that are dazzling like fuming ritual 
fires Rama felled the demons, as Thunderbolts of Indra will be felling gigantic trees. [3-26-30]_END

B_3_C_25_30
BEGIN_
शूल मुद्गर हस्ताः च पाश हस्ता महाबलाः |सृजन्तः शर वर्षाणि शस्त्र वर्षाणि संयुगे|| ३-२५-३३द्रुम 
वर्षाणि मुंचन्तः शिला वर्षाणि राक्षसाः |_END
BEGIN_
Handling tridents, maces, and leashes those great-mighty demons have created torrents of arrows, missiles, 
trees and boulders, and inundated Rama in that war. [3-25-33, 34a]_END

B_3_C_27_17
BEGIN_
स धूम शोणित उद्गारी राम बाण अभिपीडितः || ३-२७-१८न्यपतत् पतितैः पूर्वम् समरस्थो निशाचरः |_END
BEGIN_
When that nightwalker is highly tortured with Rama's arrows he collapsed spewing blood with fumes, whereat 
he is standing in war, at where his three heads rolled just now. [3-27-18b, 19a]_END

B_3_C_26_23
BEGIN_
रक्षसाम् तु शतम् रामः शतेन एकेन कर्णिना |सहस्रम् तु सहस्रेण जघान रण मूर्धनि || ३-२६-३१_END
BEGIN_
With a hundred rudder like arrows Rama hit down a hundred demons, and with a thousand more, thousand 
more demons are hit in the forefront of that war. [3-26-31]_END

B_3_C_25_31
BEGIN_
तद् बभूव अद्भुतम् युद्धम् तुमुलम् रोम हर्षणम् || ३-२५-३४रामस्य अस्य महाघोरम् पुनः तेषाम् च रक्षसाम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
Again there chanced a highly gruesome war between Rama and those demons that is tumultuous, stunning, 
and a hair-raising. [3-25-34b, 35a]_END

B_3_C_27_18
BEGIN_
