हत शेषाः ततो भग्ना राक्षसाः खर संश्रयाः || ३-२७-१९द्रवन्ति स्म न तिष्ठन्ति व्याघ्र त्रस्ता मृगा 
इव |_END
BEGIN_
As with the fleeing of deer alarmed by a tiger, the demons remaining after liquidation, whom Khara has 
protected so far and whose confidence is now shattered, are running away, and they gave Khara the run-around. 
[3-27-19b, 20a]_END

B_3_C_26_24
BEGIN_
तैः भिन्न वर्म आभरणाः छ्हिन्न भिन्न शर आसनाः |निपेतुः शोणित आदिग्धा धरण्याम् रजनीचराः || ३-२६-३२_END
BEGIN_
Ripped are their shields and armorial-ornaments, ruined and rickety are their bows, and they the nightwalkers 
fell flat on ground, bodies wholly smudged with blood. [3-26-32]_END

B_3_C_25_32
BEGIN_
ते समन्तात् अभिक्रुद्धा राघवम् पुनर् आर्दयन् || ३-२५-३५ततः सर्वा दिशो दृष्ट्वा प्रदिशाः च समावृताः 
|राक्षसैः सर्वतः प्राप्तैः शर वर्षाभिः आवृतः || ३-२५-३६स कृत्वा भैरवम् नादम् अस्त्रम् परम भास्वरम्|
समयोजयत् गान्धर्वम् राक्षसेषु महाबलः || ३-२५-३७_END
BEGIN_
Those demons have resurfaced from all around pressurising Raghava in high dudgeon. On seeing the reappearance 
of demons from everywhere, with whom all the directions and inter-directions are fully filled, and who 
are storming torrents of arrows, then that exceptionally forceful Rama made a thunderous sound and launched 
an extremely blazing missile among the gather of demons, called gandharva missile. [3-25-35b, 36, 37]_END

B_3_C_27_19
BEGIN_
तान् खरो द्रवतो दृष्ट्वा निवर्त्य रुषितः त्वरन् |रामम् एव अभिदुद्राव राहुः चन्द्रमसम् यथा || ३-२७-२०_END
BEGIN_
On seeing at those deserters Khara is piqued and quickly brought them back to his control, and then 
as with the scampering of eclipsing planet Rahu towards moon during lunar-eclipse, he scurried towards 
Rama alone. [3-27-20b, c]_END

B_3_C_26_25
BEGIN_
तैः मुक्त केशैः समरे पतितैः शोणित उक्षितैः |विस्तीर्णा वसुधा कृत्स्ना महावेदिः कुशैः इव || ३-२६-३३_END
BEGIN_
With those demons that have fallen down in war, whose hair is tousled and who are drenched in blood, 
entire earth looked like a vast altar of fire overspread with holy grass. [3-26-33]_END

B_3_C_25_33
BEGIN_
ततः शर सहस्राणि निर्ययुः चाप मण्डलात् |सर्वा दश दिशो बानैः आपूर्यन्त समागतैः || ३-२५-३८_END
BEGIN_
Then from the nimbus of his bow, arrows in thousand have scurried out, and with them thus arrived all 
the ten sides are cramped up. [3-25-38]_END

B_3_C_26_26
BEGIN_
तत् क्षणे तु महा घोरम् वनम् निहत राक्षसम् |बभूव निरय प्रख्यम् मांस शोणित कर्दमम् || ३-२६-३४_END
BEGIN_
That forest which became sludgy with the flesh and blood of killed demons and very disgusting, in a 
moment it became identical with hell. [3-26-34]_END

B_3_C_25_34
BEGIN_
न आददानाम् शरान् घोरान् विमुंचंतम् शर उत्तमान् |विकर्षमाणम् पश्यन्ति राक्षसाः ते शर आर्दिताः || 
३-२५-३९_END
BEGIN_
Either the drawing of those supreme arrows from the quiver, or the traction of bowstring on placing 
them, or unloosing them from the bow is unperceived by those demons that are harrowing under those arrows. 
[3-25-39]_END

B_3_C_26_27
BEGIN_
चतुर्दश सहस्राणि रक्षसाम् भीम कर्मणाम् |हतानि एकेन रामेण मानुषेण पदातिना || ३-२६-३५_END
BEGIN_
Thus that Rama, a lone one, that too a foot-soldier, has eliminated fourteen thousand demons of frightening 
exploits. [3-26-35]_END

B_3_C_25_35
BEGIN_
शर अन्धकारम् आकाशम् आवृणोत् स दिवाकरम् |बभूव अवस्थितो रामः प्रक्षिपन् इव तान् शरान् || ३-२५-४०_END
BEGIN_
Darkness caused by the thick of the arrows overspread the sky including its sun, while Rama happened 
to persevere spewing forth his arrows. [3-25-40]_END

B_3_C_26_28
BEGIN_
तस्य सैन्यस्य सर्वस्य खरः शेषो महारथः |राक्षसः त्रिशिराः चैव रामः च रिपुसूदनः || ३-२६-३६_END
BEGIN_
Of his entire army great-charioteer Khara and Trishira are the remaining nightwalkers, and Rama, the 
enemy destroyer, naturally on the other side. [3-26-36]_END

B_3_C_25_36
BEGIN_
युगपत् पतमानैः च युगपच्च हतैः भ्रिशम् |युगपत् पतितैः चैव विकीर्णा वसुधा अभवत् || ३-२५-४१_END
BEGIN_
Far and wide the earth is scattered with herds that are falling instantaneously, hosts that have fallen 
instantly, and huddles that are already felled with an instantaneity. [3-25-41]_END

B_3_C_26_29
BEGIN_
शेषा हता महावीर्या राक्षसा रण मूर्धनि |घोरा दुर्विषहाः सर्वे लक्ष्मणस्य अग्रजेन || ३-२६-३७_END
BEGIN_
Lakshmana's elder brother Rama eliminated all of the remaining demons in the forefront of war who are 
highly valorous, ghastly and unbearable. [3-26-37]_END

B_3_C_25_37
BEGIN_
निहताः पतिताः क्षीणा च्छ्हिन्न भिन्न विदारिताः |तत्र तत्र स्म दृश्यन्ते राक्षसाः ते सहस्रशः || ३-२५-४२_END
BEGIN_
Thousands of demons are noticeable hither and yon, killed, fallen and enfeebled, and slashed, gashed 
and ripped. [3-25-42]_END

B_3_C_26_30
BEGIN_
ततः तु तद् भीम बलम् महा आहवेसमीक्ष्य रामेण हतम् बलीयसा |रथेन रामम् महता खरः ततःसमाससाद इन्द्र 
इव उद्यत अशनिः || ३-२६-३८_END
BEGIN_
Then on surveying that great demonic force which is eliminated by Rama in that staggering war, Khara 
then marched on to reach Rama in a huge chariot, as with Indra who will march upraising his Thunderbolt. 
[3-26-38]_END

B_3_C_25_38
BEGIN_
स उष्णीषैः उत्तम अंगैः च स अ.ंगदैः बाहुभिः तथा |ऊरुभिः बाहुभिः च्छ्हिन्नैः नाना रूपैः विभूषणैः || 
३-२५-४३हयैः च द्विप मुख्यैः च रथैः भिन्नैः अनेकशः |चामर व्यजनैः छ्हत्रैः ध्वजैः नाना विधैः अपि 
|| ३-२५-४४रामेण बाण अभिहतैः विच्छ्हिन्नैः शूल पट्टिशैः |खड्गैः खण्डीकृतैः प्रासैः विकीर्णैः 
च पश्वधैः || ३-२५-४५चूणिताभिः शिलाभिः च शरैः चित्रैः अनेकशः |विच्छ्हिन्नैः समरे भूमिः विस्तीर्णा 
आभूत् भयंकरा || ३-२५-४६_END
BEGIN_
Some severed heads still have their headgears and some bare, some arms are with armlets and some bare, 
while some with their arms cut off, some with their thighs cut off, some with their divers patterns 
of ornaments on their bodies have fallen on ground. Numerous horses and elephants are felled. Chariots, 
royal-fans, royal-parasols, war-flags of very many kinds are ravaged in many ways. Hit down by Rama's 
arrows spears and tridents are variously splintered, swords broken to pieces, darts and hatchets shattered 
and strewn around. Also the boulders are pulverised, various amazing arrows have gone to rack and ruin 
in many ways. Spread with such wreckage the earth has become horrifying for a glance. [3-25-43, 44, 
45, 46]_END

B_3_C_25_39
BEGIN_
तान् दृष्ट्वा निहतान् सर्वे रक्षसाः परम आतुराः |न तत्र चलितुम् शक्ता रामम् पर पुरंजयम् || ३-२५-४७_END
BEGIN_
On seeing the killed demons all the surviving demons have become enervated and they are rendered incapable 
to make a move towards Rama, the conqueror of enemy's capitals. [3-25-47]_END

B_3_C_28_0
BEGIN_
निहतम् दूषणम् दृष्ट्वा रणे त्रिशिरसा सह |खरस्य अपि अभवत् त्रासो दृष्ट्वा रामस्य विक्रमम् || ४-२८-१_END
BEGIN_
Khara is intimidated on seeing the elimination of Duushana along with Trishira inasmuch as the intrepidity 
of Rama is concerned. [4-28-1]_END

B_3_C_28_1
BEGIN_
स दृष्ट्वा राक्षसम् सैन्यम् अविषह्यम् महाबलम् |हतम् एकेन रामेण दूषणः त्रिशिरा अपि || ४-२८-२तद् 
बलम् हत भूयिष्ठम् विमनाः प्रेक्ष्य राक्षसः |आससाद खरो रामम् नमुचिर् वासवम् यथा || ४-२८-३_END
BEGIN_
On seeing the annihilation of the insufferable and mighty force of demons, even that of Duushana and 
Trishira by lone Rama, and thus to apprehend that the demonic force is wholly destructed, that demon 
Khara became apprehensive, and then he lunged at Rama, as with demon Namuchi who once lunged at Indra. 
[4-28-2, 3]_END

B_3_C_28_2
BEGIN_
विकृष्य बलवत् चापम् नाराचान् रक्त भोजनान् |खरः चिक्षेप रामाय क्रुद्धान् आशी विषान् इव || ४-२८-४_END
BEGIN_
Forcefully drawing the bowstring fitted with iron-arrows, which looked like furious serpents of venom 
ingesting only blood, Khara discharged them on Rama. [4-28-4]_END

B_3_C_28_3
BEGIN_
ज्याम् विधुन्वन् सुबहुशः शिक्षया अस्त्राणि दर्शयन् |चचार समरे मार्गान् शरै रथ गतः खरः || ४-२८-५_END
BEGIN_
Fidgeting with bowstring in many a way, brandishing missiles with many a skill, Khara moved about the 
battleground in many a manner, seated on chariot and showing his expertise with arrows. [4-28-5]_END

B_3_C_28_4
BEGIN_
स सर्वाः च दिशो बाणैः प्रदिशः च महारथः |पूरयामास तम् दृष्ट्वा रामो अपि सुमहत् धनुः || ४-२८-६
स सायकैः दुर्विषहैः स स्फुलिन्गैः इव अग्निभिः |नभः चकार अविवरम् पर्जन्य इव वृष्टिभिः || ४-२८-७_END
BEGIN_
That great chariot-fighter Khara then started to fill all the stretches and inter-stretches with arrows, 
seeing that even Rama reciprocally started to take aim with his bow Rama, and then filled and made the 
sky less of leeway with verily unendurable arrows that are like tongues of fire emitting sparks, as 
with Rain-god chocking the sky with torrents, less of latitude. [4-28-6, 7]_END

B_3_C_28_5
BEGIN_
तद् बभूव शितैः बाणैः खर राम विसर्जितैः |परि आकाशम् अनाकाशम् सर्वतः शर संकुलम् || ४-२८-८_END
BEGIN_
No empty space is left out in the space around since it has become riotous with the sharp arrows discharged 
by Rama and Khara from everywhere. [4-28-8]_END

B_3_C_28_6
BEGIN_
शर जाल आवृतः सूर्यो न तदा स्म प्रकाशते |अन्योन्य वध संरम्भात् उभयोः संप्रयुध्यतोः || ४-२८-९_END
BEGIN_
While both of them are warring with excitement to slay one another, then the sun obscured with the mesh 
of arrows has not shined. [4-28-9]_END

B_3_C_29_0
BEGIN_
खरम् तु विरथम् रामो गदा पाणिम् अवस्थितम् |मृदु पूर्वम् महातेजाः परुषम् वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् || ३-२९-१_END
BEGIN_
Rama, the great-resplendent, spoke these words forbiddingly albeit softly to Khara who lost his chariot 
but staying his course wielding a mace. [3-29-1]_END

B_3_C_28_7
BEGIN_
ततो नालीक नाराचैः तीक्ष्ण अग्रैः च विकर्णिभिः |आजघान रणे रामम् तोत्रैर् इव महा द्विपम् || ४-२८-१०_END
BEGIN_
Then with acutely edged tubular, iron, and crescent-edged arrows Khara swatted Rama in that combat, 
as a great elephant will be swatted with a goad. [4-28-10]_END

B_3_C_29_1
BEGIN_
गज अश्व रथ संबाधे बले महति तिष्ठता |कृतम् सुदारुणम् कर्म सर्व लोक जुगुप्सितम् || ३-२९-२_END
BEGIN_
"Although you hold sway over a gigantic force abounding with elephants horses and chariots, you have 
perpetrated heinous deeds in Dandaka forests that are loathsome to all the worlds, that is unseemliest 
to this soldiery. [3-29-2]_END

B_3_C_28_8
BEGIN_
तम् रथस्थम् धनुष् पाणिम् राक्षसम् पर्यवस्थितम् |ददृशुः सर्व भूतानि पाश हस्तम् इव अंतकम् || ४-२८-११_END
BEGIN_
When charioted Khara came to the presence of Rama with bow in hand and ready for a close combat, that 
demon appeared to all beings as the Terminator handling his noose. [4-28-11]_END

B_3_C_29_2
BEGIN_
उद्वेजनीयो भूतानाम् नृशंसः पाप कर्मकृत् |त्रयाणाम् अपि लोकानाम् ईश्वरो अपि न तिष्ठति || ३-२९-३_END
BEGIN_
"One who causes suffering to living beings, besides being a transgressor and completely ruthless, he 
does not stand up for himself even if he were to be the lord of all the three worlds. [3-29-3]_END

B_3_C_28_9
BEGIN_
हन्तारम् सर्व सैन्यस्य पौरुषे पर्यवस्थितम् |परिश्रन्तम् महासत्त्वम् मेने रामम् खरः तदा || ४-२८-१२_END
BEGIN_
Khara presumed that greatly indefatigable Rama is wholly fatigued by now, though he has shown his mettle 
of boldness in eliminating all of the demonic forces, all the while. [4-28-12]_END

B_3_C_29_3
BEGIN_
कर्म लोक विरुद्धम् तु कुर्वाणम् क्षणदा चर |तीक्ष्णम् सर्व जनो हन्ति सर्पम् दुष्टम् इव आगतम् || ३-२९-४_END
BEGIN_
"All people will eliminate him, oh, nightwalker, who is imperious and an infringer of worldly routine, 
as they would eradicate a vicious serpent, in the event of its running across them. [3-29-4]_END

B_3_C_28_10
BEGIN_
तम् सिंहम् इव विक्रान्तम् सिंह विक्रान्त गामिनम् |दृष्ट्वा न उद्विजते रामः सिंहः क्षुद्र मृगम् यथा 
|| ४-२८-१३_END
BEGIN_
On seeing Khara who is prancing like a lion with a gait of a lion, Rama is unruffled like a lion that 
sees a least beast. [4-28-13]_END

B_3_C_29_4
BEGIN_
लोभात् पापानि कुर्वाणः कामात् वा यो न बुध्यते |हृष्टः पश्यति तस्य अन्तम् ब्राह्मणी करकात् इव || 
३-२९-५_END
BEGIN_
"He who goes on performing evils selfishly, obsessively, heedlessly, more so delightedly, he will see 
the results of his own doings, like red-tailed-lizard on its eating self-destructive hailstones, obsessively 
and delightedly. [3-29-5]_END

B_3_C_28_11
BEGIN_
ततः सूर्य निकाशेन रथेन महता खरः |आससाद अथ तम् रामम् पतंग इव पावकम् || ४-२८-१४_END
BEGIN_
In a chariot that equals the sun in its radiance then Khara reached Rama as a moth reaches fire. [4-28-14]_END

B_3_C_29_5
BEGIN_
वसतो दण्डकारण्ये तापसान् धर्म चारिणः |किम् नु हत्वा महाभागान् फलम् प्राप्स्यसि राक्षस || ३-२९-६_END
BEGIN_
"The residents of Dandaka forest are the highly-propitious sages that tread the path of virtue, and 
oh, demon, what benefit you gain in killing them, really? [3-29-6]_END

B_3_C_28_12
BEGIN_
ततो अस्य सशरम् चापम् मुष्टि देशे महात्मनः |खरः चिच्छ्हेद रामस्य दर्शयन् हस्त लाघवम् || ४-२८-१५_END
BEGIN_
Showing sleight of hand Khara then broke the handgrip of the bow of that great-souled Rama along with 
an arrow fitted on it. [4-28-15]_END

B_3_C_29_6
BEGIN_
न चिरम् पाप कर्माणः क्रूरा लोक जुगुप्सिताः |ऐश्वर्यम् प्राप्य तिष्ठन्ति शीर्ण मूला इव द्रुमाः || 
३-२९-७_END
BEGIN_
"Even if a fortune is made for a lavish living with an iota of merit, the evildoers, that too reprobates, 
further more those that are abominated by world will not last long, no more that petrified tree trunks. 
[3-29-7]_END

B_3_C_28_13
BEGIN_
स पुनः तु अपरान् सप्त शरान् आदाय वर्मणि |निजघान रणे क्रुद्धः शक्र अशनि सम प्रभान् || ४-२८-१६_END
BEGIN_
Still infuriated Khara has drawn seven more arrows that equal the radiance of Indra's thunderbolts and 
hit Rama's armour in that war. [4-28-16]_END

B_3_C_29_7
BEGIN_
अवश्यम् लभते कर्ता फलम् पापस्य कर्मणः |घोरम् पर्यागते काले द्रुमः पुष्पम् इव आर्तवम् || ३-२९-८_END
BEGIN_
"One who undertakes evildoings will definitely and seasonably reap their fruits, which in his case will 
be ghoulish, as with the flowering of trees according to season. [3-29-8]_END

B_3_C_28_14
BEGIN_
ततः शर सहस्रेण रामम् अप्रतिम ओजसम् |अर्दयित्वा महानादम् ननाद समेरे खरः || ४-२८-१७_END
BEGIN_
Then, on distressing Rama of unequalled vitality with a thousand arrows in that combat Khara blared 
a loud blare. [4-28-17]_END

B_3_C_29_8
BEGIN_
न चिरात् प्राप्यते लोके पापानाम् कर्मणाम् फलम् |स विषाणाम् इव अन्नानाम् भुक्तानाम् क्षणदाचर || ३-२९-९_END
BEGIN_
"In the world one acquires the fruit of profane acts not before long, oh, nightwalker, and it will be 
like venomous food devoured. [3-29-9]_END

B_3_C_30_0
BEGIN_
भित्त्वा तु ताम् गदाम् बाणैः राघवो धर्म वत्सलः |स्मयमानः खरम् वाक्यम् संरब्धम् इदम् अब्रवीत् || 
३-३०-१_END
BEGIN_
On smashing the mace with arrows Raghava spoke this sentence to Khara smiling him out of temper, without 
assaulting weaponless and flustering Khara, because Rama is the patron of virtue following the protocol 
of righteous war. [3-30-1]_END

B_3_C_28_15
BEGIN_
ततः तत् प्रहतम् बाणैः खर मुक्तैः सुपर्वभिः |पपात कवचम् भूमौ रामस्य आदित्य वर्चसः || ४-२८-१८_END
BEGIN_
With the arrows released by Khara that have a great egress, then that armour of Rama that has a sun-like 
resplendence is completely destroyed and fell on the field. [4-28-18]_END

B_3_C_29_9
BEGIN_
पापम् आचरताम् घोरम् लोकस्य अप्रियम् इच्छ्हताम् |अहम् आसादितो राज्ञा प्राणान् हन्तुम् निशाचर || ३-२९-१०_END
BEGIN_
"I am the king who arrived to exterminate the lives of those that perpetrate hideous sins, and even 
of those that wish to do evils to the disapprobation of world._END

B_3_C_30_1
BEGIN_
एतत् ते बल सर्वस्वम् दर्शितम् राक्षसाधम |शक्ति हीनतरो मत्तो वृथा त्वम् उपगर्जसि || ३-३०-२_END
BEGIN_
"So, this is all the strength of yours and your army that is displayed and nothing more to display, 
is it! You wretched demon, it is paltriest compared to my strength, yet you vaunt aloud futilely! [3-30-2]_END

B_3_C_28_16
BEGIN_
स शरैः अर्पितः क्रुद्धः सर्व गात्रेषु राघवः |रराज समरे रामो विधूमो अग्निर् इव ज्वलन् || ४-२८-१९_END
BEGIN_
When all his limbs are hit with arrows Rama is enraged and in that war Rama flared up like a fumeless 
flaring fire. [4-28-19]_END

B_3_C_29_10
BEGIN_
अद्य भित्वा मया मुक्ताः शराः कांचन भूषणाः |विदार्य अतिपतिष्यन्ति वल्मीकम् इव पन्नगाः || ३-२९-११_END
BEGIN_
"Now, my arrows that are decorated in gold will be released on you like snakes rebounding from a snake-pit, 
and they will tear you asunder, and on riving you they will bounce back into my quivers. [3-29-11]_END

B_3_C_30_2
BEGIN_
एषा बाण विनिर्भिन्ना गदा भूमि तलम् गता |अभिधान प्रगल्भस्य तव प्रत्यय घातिनी || ३-३०-३_END
BEGIN_
"This mace of yours in which you repose your bombastic aplomb, now completely battered with my arrows 
has gone onto the surface of earth, so also is your vanity. [3-30-3]_END

B_3_C_28_17
BEGIN_
ततो गंभीर निर्ह्रादम् रामः शत्रु निबर्हणः |चकार अंताय स रिपोः सज्यम् अन्यन् महत् धनुः || ४-२८-२०_END
BEGIN_
Then Rama, the blaster of enemies, strung bowstring to another thunderously blasting bow, to end the 
enemy. [4-28-20]_END

B_3_C_29_11
BEGIN_
ये त्वया दण्डकारण्ये भक्षिता धर्म चारिणः |तान् अद्य निहतः संख्ये स सैन्यो अनुगमिष्यसि || ३-२९-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Now eliminated in war, you along with your army will tread behind those sages that were treading the 
path of virtue, on whom you have so far feasted in Dandaka forest. [3-29-12]_END

B_3_C_30_3
BEGIN_
यत् त्वया उक्तम् विनष्टानाम् इदम् अश्रु प्रमार्जनम् |राक्षसानाम् करोमि इति मिथ्या तत् अपि ते वचः 
|| ३-३०-४_END
BEGIN_
"What that is said by you, 'I will dab the tears of the demons whose kinfolk are dead here...' even 
this word of yours is a fake. [3-30-4]_END

B_3_C_28_18
BEGIN_
सुमहत् वैष्णवम् यत् तत् अतिसृष्टम् महर्षिणा |वरम् तत् धनुः उद्यम्य खरम् समभिधावत || ४-२८-२१_END
BEGIN_
That which is a very admirable bow of Vishnu and that which is awarded by great-sage Agastya, upraising 
that choicest bow Rama rushed towards Khara. [4-28-21]_END

B_3_C_29_12
BEGIN_
अद्य त्वाम् निहतम् बाणैः पश्यन्तु परमर्षयः |निरयस्थम् विमानस्था ये त्वया निहता पुरा || ३-२९-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Let the supreme sages who were earlier slain by you may now see abiding on their aircrafts, your abidance 
in hellish death pangs when assaulted with my arrows. [3-29-13]_END

B_3_C_30_4
BEGIN_
नीचस्य क्षुद्र शीलस्य मिथ्या वृत्तस्य रक्षसः |प्राणान् अपहरिष्यामि गरुत्मान् अमृतम् यथा || ३-३०-५_END
BEGIN_
"In boasting you are knavish, in character roguish, and in behaviour ghoulish, such a demon as you are, 
I will take your life away as the Divine Eagle Garuda took away Ambrosia. [3-30-5]_END

B_3_C_28_19
BEGIN_
ततः कनक पुंखैः तु शरैः संनत पर्वभिः |चिच्छ्हेद रामः संक्रुद्धः खरस्य समरे ध्वजम् || ४-२८-२२_END
BEGIN_
With arrows that have golden fins and curved barbs that highly infuriated Rama then fragmented Khara's 
flagstaff with flag in that war. [4-28-22]_END

B_3_C_29_13
BEGIN_
प्रहरस्व यथा कामम् कुरु यत्नम् कुलाधम |अद्य ते पातयिष्यामि शिरः ताल फलम् यथा || ३-२९-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Attack me as you wish... make an effort... you the knave of your clan... now I am going to toss your 
head down like a palm-fruit..." Thus Rama addressed Khara. [3-29-14]_END

B_3_C_30_5
BEGIN_
अद्य ते भिन्न कण्ठस्य फेन बुद्बुद भूषितम् |विदारितस्य मत् बाणैः मही पास्यति शोणितम् || ३-३०-६_END
BEGIN_
"Now, my arrows will rip and chop off your throat, and then the earth will guzzle the blood gushed therefrom 
garnished with froth and foam. [3-30-6]_END

B_3_C_29_14
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु रामेण क्रुद्धः संरक्त लोचनः |प्रति उवाच ततो रामम् प्रहसन् क्रोध मूर्चितः || ३-२९-१५_END
BEGIN_
But when Rama said thus, Khara is infuriated and convulsed in anger, and he replied Rama with bloodshot 
eyes, laughing boisterously. [3-29-15]_END

B_3_C_28_20
BEGIN_
स दर्शनीयो बहुधा विच्छ्हिन्नः कांचनो ध्वजः |जगाम धरणीम् सूर्यो देवतानाम् इव आज्ञया || ४-२८-२३_END
BEGIN_
That eye-pleasing golden flagstaff with flag is severally shattered and fell onto ground as if it is 
god-damned sun fallen on earth. [4-28-23]_END

B_3_C_30_6
BEGIN_
पांसु रूषित सर्वान्गः स्रस्त न्यस्त भुज द्वयः |स्वप्स्यसे गाम् समाश्लिष्य दुर्लभाम् प्रमदाम् इव 
|| ३-३०-७_END
BEGIN_
"You will go to eternal sleep embracing the earth as you embrace an un-gainable lady, when both of your 
arms are knocked down to slide on earth, and limbs smeared with dirt. [3-30-7]_END

B_3_C_29_15
BEGIN_
प्राकृतान् राक्षसान् हत्वा युद्धे दशरथ आत्मज |आत्मना कथम् आत्मानम् अप्रशस्यम् प्रशंससि || ३-२९-१६_END
BEGIN_
"On killing average demons in war, oh, son of Dasharatha, how you praise yourself when you yourself 
are un-praiseworthy?" Thus Khara started to speak to Rama. [3-29-16]_END

B_3_C_28_21
BEGIN_
तम् चतुर्भिः खरः क्रुद्धो रामम् गात्रेषु मार्गणैः |विव्याध हृदि मर्मज्ञो मातंगम् इव तोमरैः || ४-२८-२४_END
BEGIN_
By that Khara is enraged, and as one who is aware of striking crucial parts/war tactics assaulted on 
the chest of Rama with four arrows, and even on other limbs, as one would prod an elephant with lancets. 
[4-28-24]_END

B_3_C_30_7
BEGIN_
प्रवृद्ध निद्रे शयिते त्वयि राक्षस पांसने |भविष्यन्ति अशरण्यानाम् शरण्या दण्डका इमे || ३-३०-८_END
BEGIN_
"While you are in profound sleep, oh, notorious demon, this Dandaka forest becomes a shelter to the 
shelter-worthy sages and saints. [3-30-8]_END

B_3_C_29_16
BEGIN_
विक्रान्ता बलवन्तो वा ये भवन्ति नरर्षभाः |कथयन्ति न ते किंचित् तेजसा स्वेन गर्विताः || ३-२९-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Those best of men that are victorious and mighty will not boast anything, for they will be really proud 
of their own valour. [3-29-17]_END

B_3_C_28_22
BEGIN_
स रामो बहुभिः बाणैः खर कार्मुक निःसृतैः |विद्धो रुधिर सिक्तांगो बभूव रुषितो भृशम् || ४-२८-२५_END
BEGIN_
Impacted with various arrows unloosened from the bow of Khara, limbs of Rama are drenched in blood and 
he became highly indignant. [4-28-25]_END

B_3_C_30_8
BEGIN_
जनस्थाने हत स्थाने तव राक्षस मत् शरैः |निर्भया विचरिष्यन्ति सर्वतो मुनयो वने || ३-३०-९_END
BEGIN_
"When the strongholds of demons in your Janasthaana are ruined with my arrows, the sages in this forest 
will move about everywhere, fearlessly. [3-30-9]_END

B_3_C_28_23
BEGIN_
स धनुर् धन्विनाम् श्रेष्ठः प्रगृह्य परम आहवे |मुमोच परम इष्वासः षट् शरान् अभिलक्षितान् || ४-२८-२६_END
BEGIN_
On aiming his great bow that ablest one among archers, namely Rama, then in that war released six arrows 
targeting pointedly. [4-28-26]_END

B_3_C_29_17
BEGIN_
प्राकृताः तु अकृत आत्मानो लोके क्षत्रिय पांसनाः |निरर्थकम् विकत्थन्ते यथा राम विकत्थसे || ३-२९-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama, as to how undignified Kshatriya-s that are frivolous and irresolute in self-confidence will 
boast in the world, likewise you too are boasting in a meaningless manner. [3-29-18]_END

B_3_C_30_9
BEGIN_
अद्य विप्रसरिष्यन्ति राक्षस्यो हत बान्धवाः |बाष्प आर्द्र वदना दीना भयात् अन्य भयावहाः || ३-३०-१०_END
BEGIN_
"The demonesses who terrorized others so far will be pitiably terrorised now, and they flee away very 
quickly with tear-wet faces as their kinsmen are killed. [3-30-10]_END

B_3_C_28_24
BEGIN_
शिरसि एकेन बाणेन द्वाभ्याम् बाह्वोर् अथ आर्पयत् |त्रिभिः चन्द्र अर्ध वक्त्रैः च वक्षसि अभिजघान ह 
|| ४-२८-२७_END
BEGIN_
Rama indeed hit Khara's head with one arrow, with two his hands, and next with three crescent shaped 
arrows he hit his chest. [4-28-27]_END

B_3_C_29_18
BEGIN_
कुलम् व्यपदिशन् वीरः समरे को अभिधास्यति |मृत्यु काले हि संप्राप्ते स्वयम् अप्रस्तवे स्तवम् || ३-२९-१९_END
BEGIN_
"Who will be that valiant that speaks about his lineage at wartime, that too, when the death-time is 
looming large! And, there will there be someone who broaches his self-extols in such an inopportune 
situation, is it! [3-29-19]_END

B_3_C_30_10
BEGIN_
अद्य शोक रसज्ञाः ताः भविष्यन्ति निरर्थकाः |अनुरूप कुलाः पत्न्यो यासाम् त्वम् पतिः ईदृशः || ३-३०-११_END
BEGIN_
"To which demonesses your kind of grievous demon is the husband, they must have taken birth in a befittingly 
grievous family like that of yours, and must be well-matched to you in grievous atrocities, and though 
they might not have tasted a grievous situation so far, since their lives have become meaningless, now 
they will become the enjoyers of the empathy of grief. [3-30-11]_END

B_3_C_28_25
BEGIN_
ततः पश्चात् महातेजा नाराचान् भास्कर उपमान् |जघान राक्षसम् क्रुद्धः त्रयोदश शिला अशितान् || ४-२८-२८_END
BEGIN_
Then afterwards that great-resplendent Rama wishing to eliminate the demon, infuriately launched 
thirteen iron arrows that are sharply whetted and similar to the dazzle of sun. [4-28-28]_END

B_3_C_29_19
BEGIN_
सर्वथा तु लघुत्वम् ते कत्थनेन विदर्शितम् |सुवर्ण प्रतिरूपेण तप्तेन इव कुश अग्निना || ३-२९-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Howsoever your ignominy is well shown by your self-praise, like the manifestation of gold on the tip 
of grass-blade burnt by fire, where the fire on grass-blade is no fire, and the bulb of fire appearing 
at the tip of grass-blade as a bulb of gold, is no gold. [3-29-20]_END

B_3_C_30_11
BEGIN_
नृशंस शील क्षुद्र आत्मन् नित्यम् ब्राह्मण कण्टक |त्वत् कृते शन्कितैः अग्नौ मुनिभिः पात्यते हविः 
|| ३-३०-१२_END
BEGIN_
"You are atrocious in conduct because you countervail against Veda-s, debased by conscience because 
you counteract to Vedic rituals, and you are countermanding Vedic procedures because you have always 
been bothersome to Brahmans, and those Brahmans becoming sceptical of your deeds of hindrance, they 
are hesitatingly consigning oblations into Ritual-Fire, which are to be swiftly dropped into fire to 
the chants of hymns and even on time, hence you are countervailing against Veda-s and counteracting 
to their rituals, and countermanding their procedures." Thus Rama spoke to Khara irefully. [3-30-12]_END

B_3_C_28_26
BEGIN_
रथस्य युगम् एकेन चतुर्भिः शबलान् हयान् |षष्ठेन च शिरः संख्ये चिच्छ्हेद खर सारथेः || ४-२८-२९
त्रिभिः त्रिवेणून् बलवान् द्वाभ्याम् अक्षम् महाबलः |द्वादशेन तु बाणेन खरस्य स शरम् धनुः || ४-२८-३०
छ्हित्त्वा वज्र निकाशेन राघवः प्रहसन् इव |त्रयोदशेन इन्द्र समो बिभेद समरे खरम् || ४-२८-३१_END
BEGIN_
That mighty Raghava who equals Indra in combats, smiling at the warfare of Khara, smashed the yoke of 
the chariot with one arrow; with four, four of the dappled horses; with the sixth, the head of the charioteer 
of Khara; with three, the three-pronged shaft from yoke to the base of chariot; with two the axels, 
thus that chariot is fragmented. Then, on wrecking Khara's bow on which an arrow is placed with the 
twelfth, that mighty one Rama impaled Khara with the thirteenth arrow that is similar to a thunderbolt. 
[4-28-29, 30, 31]_END

B_3_C_29_20
BEGIN_
न तु माम् इह तिष्ठंतम् पश्यसि त्वम् गदा धरम् |धराधरम् इव अकंप्यम् पर्वतम् धातुभिः चितम् || ३-२९-२१_END
BEGIN_
"But you are seeing me wielding a mace and standing before you like an unshakable and jagged mountain 
laden with ores, isn't it! [3-29-21]_END

B_3_C_30_12
BEGIN_
तम् एवम् अभिसंरब्धम् ब्रुवाणम् राघवम् रणे |खरो निर्भर्त्सयामास रोषात् खरतर स्वरः || ३-३०-१३_END
BEGIN_
While Raghava is speaking that way with such an impetuosity in that forest, Khara started to intimidate 
him rancorously in a voice stridulous than braying. [3-30-13]_END

B_3_C_28_27
BEGIN_
प्रभग्न धन्वा विरथो हत अश्वो हत सारथिः |गदा पाणिः अवप्लुत्य तस्थौ भूमौ खरः तदा || ४-२८-३२_END
BEGIN_
With his bow utterly shattered, chariot fragmented, horses killed, and charioteer felled, that Khara 
then hopped down to ground from the dilapidated chariot wielding a mace, and stood fast. [4-28-32]_END

B_3_C_30_13
BEGIN_
दृढम् खलु अवलिप्तो असि भयेषु अपि च निर्भयः |वाच्य अवाच्यम् ततो हि त्वम् मृत्यु वश्यो न बुध्यसे || 
३-३०-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Priding yourself resolutely you are unfearing even in a fearful situation, thereby you have indeed 
gone into the control of death, and for sure you are unmindful of what is speakable and what is not." 
Thus, Khara started his tongue-lashing. [3-30-14]_END

B_3_C_29_21
BEGIN_
पर्याप्तो अहम् गदा पाणिर् हन्तुम् प्राणान् रणे तव |त्रयाणाम् अपि लोकानाम् पाश हस्त इव अंतकः || ३-२९-२२_END
BEGIN_
"As to how the Terminator wielding noose is enough to take away all the lives in all the three worlds, 
handling my mace I am enough for detracting your life from you. [3-29-22]_END

B_3_C_28_28
BEGIN_
तत् कर्म रामस्य महारथस्यसमेत्य देवाः च महर्षयः च |अपूजयन् प्रांजलयः प्रहृष्टाःतदा विमान 
अग्र गताः समेताः || ४-२८-३३_END
BEGIN_
The gods as well as great-sages have then came together and assembled in heavens, and those assemblies 
that are aboard their aircrafts are highly gladdened at the exploit of the great chariot-fighter Rama, 
and they worshipped him with their adjoined palms. [4-28-33]_END

B_3_C_30_14
BEGIN_
काल पाश परिक्षिप्ता भवंति पुरुषा हि ये |कार्य अकार्यम् न जानन्ति ते निरस्त षड् इन्द्रियाः || ३-३०-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Such of those men on whom the Lead of the Time verily closes in, they will not know what is to be done 
and what not, for all of their six senses will be rendered insensible." Thus Khara intimidated Rama. 
[3-30-15]_END

B_3_C_29_22
BEGIN_
कामम् बहु अपि वक्तव्यम् त्वयि वक्ष्यामि न तु अहम् |अस्तम् प्राप्नोति सविता युद्ध विघ्नः ततो भवेत् 
|| ३-२९-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Even though much is to be said in your respect I will not continue to say, for the sun is getting at 
the dusk thereby disruption to war occurs. [3-29-23]_END

B_3_C_30_15
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्त्वा ततो रामम् संरुध्य भृकुटिम् ततः |स ददर्श महा सालम् अविदूरे निशाचरः || ३-३०-१६रणे 
प्रहरणस्य अर्थे सर्वतो हि अवलोकयन् |_END
BEGIN_
Saying so to Rama that nightwalker Khara then knitting his brows tightly saw everywhere for an assault 
weapon for use in that combat, and then he indeed found one not far away from him, namely a huge saala 
tree. [3-30-16, 17a]_END

B_3_C_29_23
BEGIN_
चतुर्दश सहस्राणि राक्षसानाम् हतानि ते |त्वत् विनाशात् करोमि अद्य तेषाम् अश्रु प्रमार्जनम् || ३-२९-२४_END
BEGIN_
"You have killed fourteen thousand demons and on killing you I will wipe the tears of the wives of those 
dead demons today itself." Khara said so to Rama. [3-29-24]_END

B_3_C_30_16
BEGIN_
स तम् उत्पाटयामास संदष्ट दशन च्छ्हदम् || ३-३०-१७तम् समुत्क्षिप्य बाहुभ्याम् विनर्दित्वा महाबलः |
रामम् उद्दिश्य चिक्षेप हतः त्वम् इति च अब्रवीत् || ३-३०-१८_END
BEGIN_
He curled his lips in frown and started to extricate that Saala tree, and that great-mighty Khara on 
forcefully uprooting that tree with both of hands hurled it aiming at Rama, braying loudly and shouting 
at him 'you are dead...' [3-30-17b, 18]_END

B_3_C_29_24
BEGIN_
इति उक्त्वा परम क्रुद्धः ताम् गदाम् परम अन्गदाम् |खरः चिक्षेप रामाय प्रदीप्ताम् अशनिम् यथा || ३-२९-२५_END
BEGIN_
Saying thus that highly infuriated Khara hurled his mace towards Rama, around which there are superb 
golden cinctures, and which is extremely glaring like a thunderbolt. [3-29-25]_END

B_3_C_30_17
BEGIN_
तम् आपतन्तम् बाण ओघैः च्छ्हित्त्वा रामः प्रतापवान् |रोषम् आहारयत् तीव्रम् निहंतुम् समरे खरम् || 
३-३०-१९_END
BEGIN_
But that adventurous Rama on shredding that tree which is swooping down with a torrent of arrows, and 
deciding to eliminate that Khara in that war evoked an unusual rancour, which rancour is equally an 
unusual facet of Rama. [3-30-19]_END

B_3_C_29_25
BEGIN_
खर बाहु प्रमुक्ता सा प्रदीप्ता महती गदा |भस्म वृक्षाम् च गुल्माम् च कृत्वा अगात् तत् समीपतः || ३-२९-२६_END
BEGIN_
Forcefully discharged from Khara's hands that highly fiery and stupendous mace rendering trees and shrubs 
down to ashes darted towards Rama. [3-29-26]_END

B_3_C_30_18
BEGIN_
जात स्वेदः ततो रामो रोषात् रक्त अन्त लोचनः |निर्बिभेद सहस्रेण बाणानाम् समरे खरम् || ३-३०-२०_END
BEGIN_
Rama whose body is perspiring and whose eyes are acrimoniously bloodshot at ends, he utterly shredded 
Khara with a thousand arrows in that war. [3-30-20]_END

B_3_C_29_26
BEGIN_
ताम् आपतन्तीम् महतीम् मृत्यु पाश उपमाम् गदाम् |अंतरिक्ष गताम् रामः चिच्छ्हेद बहुधा शरैः || ३-२९-२७_END
BEGIN_
When that monstrous mace similar to the halter of the Terminator is swooping down, Rama smashed it to 
smithereens with his arrows while it is still sky rocketing. [3-29-27]_END

B_3_C_30_19
BEGIN_
तस्य बाण अंतरात् रक्तम् बहु सुस्राव फेनिलम् |गिरेः प्रस्रवणस्य इव धाराणाम् च परिस्रवः || ३-३०-२१_END
BEGIN_
Copious frothy blood gushed out from the gashes of arrows on the mountainous body of Khara, like the 
rapids on Mt. Prasavana, and it overflowed on earth too. [3-30-21]_END

B_3_C_29_27
BEGIN_
सा विशीर्णा शरैः भिन्ना पपात धरणी तले |गदा मंत्र औषधि बलैर् व्याली इव विनिपातिता || ३-२९-२८_END
BEGIN_
That mace splintered with arrows of Rama fell crumbling onto the surface of earth as a springing female 
snake would fall down by the strength of spells and nostrums. [3-29-28]_END

B_3_C_30_20
BEGIN_
विकल स कृतो बाणैः खरो रामेण संयुगे |मत्तो रुधिर गन्धेन तम् एव अभ्यद्रवत् द्रुतम् || ३-३०-२२_END
BEGIN_
When Khara is tormented with the arrows of Rama in that conflict he is bedevilled and with his blood 
stinking body he quickly bolted towards that Rama alone. [3-30-22]_END

B_3_C_30_21
BEGIN_
तम् आपतंतम् संरब्धम् कृत अस्त्रो रुधिर आप्लुतम् |अपसर्पत् द्वि त्रि पदम् किंचित् त्वरित विक्रमः 
|| ३-३०-२३_END
BEGIN_
When Khara is descending on boisterously with his body bathed in blood, that adept one in the Science 
of Archery, dhanur veda , the scripture on archery, and that valorous Rama, 
in swiftness lurched a little...say, two or three steps... [3-30-23]_END

B_3_C_30_22
BEGIN_
ततः पावक संकाशम् वधाय समरे शरम् |खरस्य रामो जग्राह ब्रह्म दण्डम् इव अपरम् || ३-३०-२४_END
BEGIN_
Then, Rama snatched an arrow which is similar to the Ritual-fire, and secondary only to the ultimate 
missile, namely the Brahma-missile, for the elimination of Khara in war. [3-30-24]_END

B_3_C_30_23
BEGIN_
स तत् दत्तम् मघवता सुर राजेन धीमता |संदधे च स धर्मात्मा मुमोच च खरम् प्रति || ३-३०-२५_END
BEGIN_
That particular arrow is made available to Rama through Sage Agastya by the king of gods, namely Indra, 
because Indra is a sensible one about the future course of events, and he is also prosperous in securing 
impossible weaponry, and now Rama fitted such an arrow on his bow and released it towards Khara. [3-30-25]_END

B_3_C_30_24
BEGIN_
स विमुक्तो महाबाणो निर्घात सम निःस्वनः |रामेण धनुरायम्य खरस्य उरसि च आपतत् || ३-३०-२६_END
BEGIN_
That formidable arrow is promptly released on Rama's stretching the bowstring up to his ear, bending 
bow almost to a circularity, and which arrow is thunderous while in egress like the thunder of a thunderbolt, 
and that has come and plunged inthe chest of Khara. [3-30-26]_END

B_3_C_30_25
BEGIN_
स पपात खरो भूमौ दह्यमानः शर अग्निना |रुद्रेण एव विनिर्दग्धः श्वेत अरण्ये यथा अन्धकः || ३-३०-२७_END
BEGIN_
Khara fell down on to earth and on being burnt by the radiation of that arrow he is like demon Andhaka, 
who once was very completely burnt by Rudra in Shveta-araNya, the White-forest. [3-30-27]_END

B_3_C_30_26
BEGIN_
स वृत्र इव वज्रेण फेनेन नमुचिर् यथाअ |बलो वा इन्द्र अशनि हतो निपपात हतः खरः || ३-३०-२८_END
BEGIN_
As with fall of demon Vritta or fall of demon Bala who are eliminated by Indra with his Thunderbolt, 
or as with the collapse of demon Namuchi who is eliminated by the same Indra just with forth or foam, 
Khara too is brought down. [3-30-28]_END

B_3_C_30_27
BEGIN_
एतस्मिन् अंतरे देवाः चारणयोः सह संगताः |दुन्दुभिः च अभिनिघ्नंतः पुष्प वर्ष समंततः || ३-३०-२९
रामस्य उपरि संहृष्टा ववर्षुः विस्मिताः तदा |_END
BEGIN_
In this meantime gods gathering along with carana-s drummed celestial drums from all over and showered 
flowers on Rama from all over. [3-30-29, 30a]_END

B_3_C_30_28
BEGIN_
अर्थ अधिक मुहूर्तेन रामेण निशितैः शरैः || ३-३०-३०चतुर् दश सहस्राणि रक्ष्साम् काम रूपिणाम् |खर 
दूषण मुख्यानाम् निहतानि महामृधे || ३-३०-३१_END
BEGIN_
And those gods and other celestials in their amazement said among themselves that 'in one and half hours, 
say seventy two minutes of this extreme crack-down Rama with his sharp arrows has eradicated fourteen 
thousand guise changing demons, including their chieftains Khara and Duushana. [3-30-30b, 31]_END

B_3_C_30_29
BEGIN_
अहो बत महत् कर्म रामस्य विदित आत्मनः |अहो वीर्यम् अहो दार्ढ्यम् विष्णोः इव हि दृश्यते || ३-३०-३२
इति एवम् उक्त्वा ते सर्वे ययुः देवा यथा आगतम्|_END
BEGIN_
"Aha! Surprising is this great deed of Rama, the shrewd-soul, what a valour, what a fortitude, really, 
his valour and fortitude are like those of Vishnu..." Thus saying that way all of those gods have gone 
away as the have come. [3-30-32, 33a]_END

B_3_C_30_30
BEGIN_
ततो राज ऋषयः सर्वे सम्गताः परम ऋषयः || ३-३०-३३सभाज्य मुदिता रामम् स अगस्त्या इदम् अब्रुवन् |_END
BEGIN_
All the kingly-sages and elite-sages along with Sage Agastya, who as incidentally came here to witness 
the victory of Rama, then on foregathering near at Rama delightedly said this on adoring him. [3-30-33b, 
34a]_END

B_3_C_30_31
BEGIN_
एतत् अर्थम् महातेजा महेन्द्रः पाक शासनः || ३-३०-३४शरभंग आश्रमम् पुण्यम् आजगाम पुरंदरः |_END
BEGIN_
"He that great-resplendent one, the controller of demon Paka, and the destroyer of enemy's cities, namely 
Indra, once came to the meritorious hermitage of Sage Sharabhanga only for the purpose such an elimination 
of demons. [3-30-34b, 35a]_END

B_3_C_30_32
BEGIN_
आनीतः त्वम् इमम् देशम् उपायेन महर्षिभिः || ३-३०-३५एषाम् वध अर्थम् शत्रूणाम् रक्षसाम् पाप कर्मणाम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
"For the purpose of eradicating these demons who are the evildoers by nature and the natural enemies 
to saintly people you are led to this countryside by the great sages with an ideation. [3-30-35b, 36a]_END

B_3_C_30_33
BEGIN_
तत् इदम् नः कृतम् कार्यम् त्वया दशरथ आत्मज || ३-३०-३६स्व धर्मम् प्रचरिष्यन्ति दण्डकेषु महर्षयः |_END
BEGIN_
"That which is the task of ours it is accomplished by you, oh, son of Dasharatha, now that Dandaka is 
unimpeded these great-sages will be practising their respective sacred devoirs in it." Thus, the sages 
expressed their thanksgiving. [3-30-36b, 37a]_END

B_3_C_30_34
BEGIN_
एतस्मिन् अनंतरे वीरो लक्ष्मणः सह सीतया || ३-३०-३७गिरि दुर्गात् विनिष्क्रम्य संविवेश आश्रमम् सुखी 
|_END
BEGIN_
In the meanwhile the brave Lakshmana exiting from the mountain cave came along with Seetha to their 
hermitage, and he is charmed at the victory of his brother Rama. [3-30-37b, 38a]_END

B_3_C_30_35
BEGIN_
ततो रामः तु विजयी पूज्यमानो महर्षिभिः || ३-३०-३८प्रविवेश आश्रमम् वीरो लक्ष्मणेन अभिपूजितः |_END
BEGIN_
And then that brave and victories Rama too came towards hermitage while great-sages reverenced him, 
and he entered the hermitage while Lakshmana came forward to greet him. [3-30-38b, 39a]_END

B_3_C_30_36
BEGIN_
तम् दृष्ट्वा शत्रु हंतारम् महर्षीणाम् सुख आवहम् || ३-३०-३९बभूव हृष्टा वैदेही भर्तारम् परिष्वजे |_END
BEGIN_
And Seetha on seeing her husband, the eliminator of enemies and accorder of happiness to sages, embraced 
her husband Rama, rejoicingly. [3-30-39b, 40a]_END

B_3_C_30_37
BEGIN_
मुदा परमया युक्ता दृष्ट्वा रक्षो गणान् हतान् |रामम् च एव अव्ययम् दृष्टा तुतोष जनक आत्मजा || ३-३०-४०_END
BEGIN_
Janaka's daughter Seetha on seeing the hordes of demons eliminated, and even on observing her husband 
is also scatheless, she is all-smiles for him smiling sniggeringly. [3-30-40]_END

B_3_C_30_38
BEGIN_
ततः तु तम् राक्षस संघ मर्दनम्स पूज्यमानम् मुदितैः महात्मभिः |पुनः परिष्वज्य मुदा अन्वित आनना
बभूव हृष्टा जनक आत्मजा तदा || ३-३०-४१_END
BEGIN_
She whose face is beaming with delight that Seetha, the daughter Janaka, on seeing Rama who has eliminated 
demonic troops, and whom great-sages are worshipping, again embraced him and became rapturous. [3-30-41]_END

B_3_C_31_0
BEGIN_
त्वरमणः ततो गत्वा जनस्थानात् अकंपनः |प्रविश्य लंकाम् वेगेन रावणम् वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् || ३-३१-१_END
BEGIN_
Then on going hurriedly from Janasthaana and on speedily entering Lanka Akampana spoke these words to 
Ravana. [3-31-1]_END

B_3_C_31_1
BEGIN_
जनस्थान स्थिता राजन् रक्षसा बहवो हताः |खरः च निहतः संख्ये क्थंचित् अहम् आगतः || ३-३१-२_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, king, many demons positioned in Janasthaana are killed, Khara is also killed in war, and somehow 
I have come here. [3-31-2]_END

B_3_C_31_2
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तो दशग्रीवः क्रुद्धः सम्‌रक्त लोचनः |अकंपनम् उवाच इदम् निर्दहन् इव तेजसा || ३-३१-३_END
BEGIN_
Thus said, then that ten-faced Ravana is infuriated with bloodshot eyes, and as though to burn down 
whole world with his radiance he spoke this to Akampana. [3-31-3]_END

B_3_C_31_3
BEGIN_
केन भीमम् जनस्थानम् हतम् मम परासुना |को हि सर्वेषु लोकेषु गतिम् न अधिगमिष्यति || ३-३१-४_END
BEGIN_
"Who is that dead-and-gone that has destroyed my indomitable Janasthaana? Who is it that has indeed 
opted for no recourse in all of the worlds? [3-31-4]_END

B_3_C_31_4
BEGIN_
न हि मे विप्रियम् कृता शक्यम् मघवता सुखम् |प्रप्तुम् वैश्रवणेन अपि न यमेन च विष्णुना || ३-३१-५_END
BEGIN_
"Evoking indignation in me it is really impossible for Indra to be happy; even for Kubera - no; for 
Yama - no; why them, even Vishnu cannot be happy. [3-31-5]_END

B_3_C_31_5
BEGIN_
कालस्य च अपि अहम् कलो दहेयम् अपि पावकम् |मृत्युम् मरण धर्मेण संयोजयितुम् उत्सहे || ३-३१-६_END
BEGIN_
"I am the End-Time for the Time-god himself, I will burn down the Fire-god, and I am capable of conjoining 
Death with the virtue of deathliness. [3-31-6]_END

B_3_C_32_0
BEGIN_
ततः शूर्पणखा दृष्ट्वा सहस्राणि चतुर्दश |हतानि एकेन रामेण रक्षसाम् भीम कर्मणाम् || ३-३२-१दूषणम् 
च खरम् चैव हतम् त्रिशिरसम् रणे |दृष्ट्वा पुनर् महानादम् ननाद जलद उपमा || ३-३२-२_END
BEGIN_
On seeing the fourteen thousands demons of heinous crimes, and even on seeing Trishira, Duushana, and 
even Khara, who are all exterminated by lone Rama, then Shuurpanakha emitted a thunderous blare like 
a thundercloud. [3-32-1, 2]_END

B_3_C_31_6
BEGIN_
वातस्य तरसा वेगम् निहन्तुम् अपि च उत्सहे |दहेयम् अपि संक्रुद्धः तेजसा आदित्य पावकौ || ३-३१-७_END
BEGIN_
"If I am enraged I will incinerate Sun-god or Fire-god just with my radiance, I will halt even the impetuosity 
of Wind-god with that of mine." Thus Ravana said about himself. [3-31-7]_END

B_3_C_32_1
BEGIN_
सा दृष्ट्वा कर्म रामस्य कृतम् अन्यैः सुदुष्करम् |जगाम परम उद्विग्ना लंकाम् रावण पालिताम् || ३-३२-३_END
BEGIN_
Highly agitated to witness the deed done by Rama, which deed is highly impossible for others, she hurried 
Lanka ruled by Ravana. [3-32-3]_END

B_3_C_31_7
BEGIN_
तथा क्रुद्धम् दशग्रीवम् कृतांजलिः अकंपनः |भयात् संदिग्धया वचा रावणम् याचते अभयम् || ३-३१-८_END
BEGIN_
Akampana with his palms adjoined and voice hesitant with fear sought for the clemency of that decahedral 
demon Ravana who is enraged in that way. [3-31-8]_END

B_3_C_32_2
BEGIN_
सा ददर्श विमान अग्रे रावणम् दीप्त तेजसम् |उपोपविष्टम् सचिवैः मरुद्भिः इव वासवम् || ३-३२-४_END
BEGIN_
She saw Ravana who is fulgent with his own radiance, seated with ministers at his nearby in the midst 
of the divine aircraft Pushpaka, as with Indra who will be sitting amidst wind-gods. [3-32-4]_END

B_3_C_31_8
BEGIN_
दशग्रीवो अभयम् तस्मै प्रददौ रक्षसाम् वरः |स विस्रब्धो अब्रवीत् वाक्यम् असंदिग्धम् अकंपनः || ३-३१-९_END
BEGIN_
When the supremo of demons Dasha-griiva pardoned him then that Akampana spoke these words, unfalteringly 
and trustfully. [3-31-9]_END

B_3_C_32_3
BEGIN_
आसीनम् सूर्य संकाशे कांचने परमासने |रुक्म वेदि गतम् प्राज्यम् ज्वलंतम् इव पावकम् || ३-३२-५_END
BEGIN_
Seated similar to the Sun in firmament on a supreme golden throne, which resembles a golden Altar of 
Fire, and he himself resembling the blazing Ritual-fire spurting out of it when that Golden-Fire-Altar 
is drenched with plentiful ghee, she saw such a Ravana. [3-32-5]_END

B_3_C_31_9
BEGIN_
पुत्रो दशरथः ते सिंह संहननो युवा |रामो नाम महास्कंधो वृत्त आयत महाभुजः || ३-३१-१०_END
BEGIN_
"He is a youth whose shoulders are mighty, arms round and lengthy, built like that a lion, who is the 
son of Dasharatha and known as Rama. [3-31-10]_END

B_3_C_32_4
BEGIN_
देव गन्धर्व भूतानाम् ऋषीणाम् च महात्मनाम् |अजेयम् समरे घोरम् व्यात्त आननम् इव अन्तकम् || ३-३२-६_END
BEGIN_
An invincible one either for gods or gandharva-s, or to sages with exalted souls, or even to any other 
entity worth its name, whose appearance itself is catastrophic, and who is sitting identical to the 
Terminator, as though that Terminator himself is sitting with a wide gaped mouth, at such a Ravana Shuurpanakha 
saw. [3-32-6]_END

B_3_C_31_10
BEGIN_
श्यामः पृथुयशाः श्रीमान् अतुल्य बल विक्रमः |हतः तेन जनस्थाने खरः च सह दूषणः || ३-३१-११_END
BEGIN_
"He is blue-black in complexion, a highly renowned one with matchless might and valour, a magnificent 
one such as he is he slew Duushana along with Khara in Janasthaana." [3-31-11]_END

B_3_C_33_0
BEGIN_
ततः शूर्पणखा दीना रावणम् लोक रावणम् |अमात्य मध्ये संक्रुद्धा परुषम् वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् || ३-३३-१_END
BEGIN_
Then that doleful Shuurpanakha spoke these scornful words to Ravana who makes the world to wail in the 
presence of his ministers. [3-33-1]_END

B_3_C_32_5
BEGIN_
देव असुर विमर्देषु वज्र अशनि कृत व्रणम् |ऐरावत विषाण अग्रैः उत्कृष्ट किण वक्षसम् || ३-३२-७_END
BEGIN_
One who is severally bruised in several combats of gods and demons with the thunderbolts from the Vajra 
weapon of Indra, and one who is severally blotched on his chest when the prongs of the tusks of Airavata, 
the lordly elephant of Indra, gored his chest, at such a Ravana Shuurpanakha saw. [3-32-7]_END

B_3_C_31_11
BEGIN_
अकंपन वचः श्रुत्वा रावणो राक्षसाधिप |नागेन्द्र इव निःश्वस्य इदम् वचनम् अब्रवीत् || ३-३१-१२_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of Akampana, the chief of demons Ravana, spoke these words hissing like a kingly 
serpent. [3-31-12]_END

B_3_C_33_1
BEGIN_
प्रमत्तः काम भोगेषु स्वैर वृत्तो निरंकुशः |समुत्पन्नम् भयम् घोरम् बोद्धव्यम् न अवबुध्यसे || ३-३३-२_END
BEGIN_
"Highly infatuated with lustful gratifications you are incontinent and unchecked, thus you are unobservant 
of a calamitous jeopardy that has surfaced, though you ought to be observant of it as a king. [3-33-2]_END

B_3_C_32_6
BEGIN_
विंशत् भुजम् दश ग्रीवम् दर्शनीय परिच्छदम् |विशाल वक्षसम् वीरम् राज लक्ष्मण लक्षितम् || ३-३२-८_END
BEGIN_
One who has twenty arms, ten faces and a broad chest, and a possessor of all regalia of Indra like white 
parasol, white fanning instruments, colours and the like insigne, and at that brave one who is attributed 
with all of the kingly attributes, Shuurpanakha saw. [3-32-8]_END

B_3_C_31_12
BEGIN_
स सुरेन्द्रेण संयुक्तो रामः सर्व अमरैः सह |उपयातो जनस्थानम् ब्रूहि कच्चित् अकंपन || ३-३१-१३_END
BEGIN_
"The question is whether that Rama arrived at Janasthaana associated with Indra and along with all of 
the immortal gods? Oh, Akampana, speak about it. [3-31-13]_END

B_3_C_33_2
BEGIN_
सक्तम् ग्राम्येषु भोगेषु काम वृत्तम् महीपतिम् |लुब्धम् न बहु मन्यन्ते श्मशान अग्निम् इव प्रजाः || 
३-३३-३_END
BEGIN_
"If a king deports himself in an overly self-assured manner, that too with self-serving motives, and 
clings only to dirty pleasures, he will be unhonoured by people as with a crematory fire. [3-33-3]_END

B_3_C_32_7
BEGIN_
नद्ध वैदूर्य संकाशम् तप्त कान्चन कुण्डलम् |सुभुजम् शुक्ल दशनम् महा आस्यम् पर्वतोपमम् || ३-३२-९_END
BEGIN_
Blent with the gleam of Lapis gems studded in his ornaments his glisten is alike that gem, while 
his ear-knobs are made out of refined gold, and his arms strongish, teeth whitish, mouth widish and 
he is mountainous, and Shuurpanakha saw such a Ravana. [3-32-9]_END

B_3_C_31_13
BEGIN_
रावणस्य पुनर् वाक्यम् निशम्य तद् अकंपनः |आचचक्षे बलम् तस्य विक्रमम् च महात्मनः || ३-३१-१४_END
BEGIN_
Akampana again detailed about the might and valour of that great souled Rama on hearing that sentence 
of Ravana. [3-31-14]_END

B_3_C_33_3
BEGIN_
स्वयम् कार्याणि यः काले न अनुतिष्ठति पार्थिवः |स तु वै सह राज्येन तैः च कार्यैः विनश्यति || ३-३३-४_END
BEGIN_
"The king who will not deal with the concerns of kingdom, in person and on time, he and his kingdom 
and even those concerns of his kingdom will get ruined. [3-33-4]_END

B_3_C_32_8
BEGIN_
विष्णु चक्र निपातैः च शतशो देव संयुगे |अन्यैः शस्त्रैः प्रहारैः च महायुद्धेषु ताडितम् || ३-३२-१०_END
BEGIN_
His body bears hundreds of welts caused when assaulted with Vishnu-disc for hundreds of times in wars 
with gods, and when assaulted for hundreds of times with the other assaults-missiles in other gruesome 
wars as well, and Shuurpanakha saw at such a Ravana. [3-32-10]_END

B_3_C_31_14
BEGIN_
रामो नाम महातेजाः श्रेष्टः सर्व धनुष्मताम् |दिव्य अस्त्र गुण संपन्नः परंधर्म गतो युधि || ३-३१-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Rama means someone who is highly resplendent, an ablest archer among all archers, one who is endowed 
with divine missiles and divine attributes, and he is the one who conducts warfare with a supreme conduct. 
[3-31-15]_END

B_3_C_33_4
BEGIN_
अयुक्त चारम् दुर्दर्शम् अस्वाधीनम् नराधिपम् |वर्जयन्ति नरा दूरात् नदी पंकम् इव द्विपाः || ३-३३-५_END
BEGIN_
"If a king is inaccessible to spies for exchange of information, unavailable for subjects for an audience 
for a similar appraisal, more so if he is intemperately not able to impose self-discipline, people will 
eschew such a king from a distance as elephants will refrain themselves from the mud of river from a 
distance. [3-33-5]_END

B_3_C_32_9
BEGIN_
आहत अंगम् समस्तैः च देव प्रहरणैः तथा |अक्षोभ्याणाम् समुद्राणाम् क्षोभणम् क्षिप्र कारिणम् || ३-३२-११_END
BEGIN_
Likewise, whose limbs are thrashed with thrashing missilery of all gods, whereby his body and soul have 
become harsh, thus he can perpetrate anything swiftly at his will, and he who can capably roil an un-perturbable 
ocean at his wish, at such Ravana Shuurpanakha saw. [3-32-11]_END

B_3_C_31_15
BEGIN_
तस्य अनुरूपो बलब्वान् रक्ताक्षो दुन्दुभि स्वनः |कनीयान् लक्ष्मणो भ्राता राका शशि निभ आननः || ३-३१-१६_END
BEGIN_
"And a mighty one with redly eyes and drumbeat like voice, and whose face is shiny like the full-moon 
is Rama's selfsame younger brother known as Lakshmana. [3-31-16]_END

B_3_C_33_5
BEGIN_
ये न रक्षन्ति विषयम् अस्वाधीना नराधिपः |ते न वृद्ध्या प्रकाशन्ते गिरयः सागरे यथा || ३-३३-६_END
BEGIN_
"Which of those kings that will not safeguard their kingdoms by remaining in a self-restrained manner, 
they will not outshine advantageously, like mountains submerged under ocean. [3-33-6]_END

B_3_C_32_10
BEGIN_
क्षेप्तारम् पर्वत अग्राणाम् सुराणाम् च प्रमर्दनम् |उच्छेत्तारम् च धर्माणाम् पर दार अभिमर्शनम् || 
३-३२-१२_END
BEGIN_
At him who is a volleyer of mountain peaks, a represser of gods, an extirpator of ethical values, and 
a molester of others wives, Shuurpanakha saw. [3-32-12]_END

B_3_C_34_0
BEGIN_
ततः शूर्पणखाम् दृष्ट्वा ब्रुवन्तीम् परुषम् वचः |अमात्य मध्ये संकृउद्धः परिपप्रच्छ रावणः || ३-३४-१_END
BEGIN_
On observing Shuurpanakha who is speaking bitter words against him in the presence of ministers then 
Ravana is highly infuriated and queried her. [1-34-1]_END

B_3_C_31_16
BEGIN_
स तेन सह संयुक्तः पावकेन अनिलो यथा |श्रीमान् राज वरः तेन जनस्थानम् निपातितम् || ३-३१-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Alike the wind associating with fire this Lakshmana is associated with that glorious and nonpareil 
prince Rama, and that firestorm, namely Rama, destroyed Janasthaana. [3-31-17]_END

B_3_C_33_6
BEGIN_
आत्मवद्भिः विगृह्य त्वम् देव गंधर्व दानवैः |अयुक्त चारः चपलः कथम् राजा भविष्यसि || ३-३३-७_END
BEGIN_
"Externally you are belligerent with sensible gods, gandharva-s and other demons, and internally you 
are needful of intelligence agents, and such as you are, you are an erratic even, then how can you thrive 
as a king! [3-33-7]_END

B_3_C_32_11
BEGIN_
सर्व दिव्य अस्त्र योक्तारम् यज्ञ विघ्न करम् सदा |पुरीम् भोगवतीम् गत्वा पराजित्य च वासुकिम् || ३-३२-१३
तक्षकस्य प्रियाम् भार्याम् पराजित्य जहार यः |_END
BEGIN_
He who is a marksman of every divine missile, and an ever interdictor of Vedic-rituals, and who on going 
to the city named Bhogavati, the capital of Naga-s, and on defeating Vaasuki, the King of Serpents, 
has abducted the dear wife of Taksha on molesting her, and Shuurpanakha saw such a molester of others 
wives. [3-32-13, 14a]_END

B_3_C_34_1
BEGIN_
कः च रामः कथम् वीर्यः किम् रूपः किम् पराक्रमः |किम् अर्थम् दण्डकारण्यम् प्रविष्टः च सुदुस्तरम् || 
३-३४-२_END
BEGIN_
"Who is Rama? How brave he is? Of what mien and what calibre he is? And for what reason he entered the 
highly inscrutable Dandaka forest? [1-34-2]_END

B_3_C_31_17
BEGIN_
न एव देवा महत्मनो न अत्र कार्या विचारणा |शरा रामेण तु उत्सृष्टा रुक्मपुंखाः पतत्रिणः || ३-३१-१८
सर्पाः पंचानना भूत्वा भक्षयन्ति स्म राक्षसान् |_END
BEGIN_
"They are not any great souled gods or any heavenly beings as such, hence there is no need to doubt 
about it. Rama unloosened his gold-finned and feather-winged arrows, which on becoming five-faced serpents 
started consuming the demons. [3-31-18]_END

B_3_C_33_7
BEGIN_
त्वम् तु बाल स्वभावत् च बुद्धि हीनः च राक्षस |ज्ञातव्यम् तु न जानीषि कथम् राजा भविष्यसि || ३-३३-८_END
BEGIN_
"Your bent is boyish and you are mindless, oh, demon, you are not able to know the knowable danger because 
you are carefree, and how do you thrive as a king! [3-33-8]_END

B_3_C_32_12
BEGIN_
कैलासम् पर्वतम् गत्वा विजित्य नर वाहनम् || ३-३२-१४विमानम् पुष्पकम् तस्य कामगम् वै जहार यः |_END
BEGIN_
On going to Mt. Kailash he who has defeated the god who uses humans as his vehicle, namely Kubera, and 
snatched away his aircraft, namely Pushpaka, which aircraft transits at the wish of its steersman, and 
Shuurpanakha saw such a grabber of others possessions. [3-32-14b, 15a]_END

B_3_C_34_2
BEGIN_
आयुधम् किम् च रामस्य येन ते राक्षसाः हता |खरः च निहतः संख्ये दूषणः त्रिशिराः तथा || ३-३४-३तत् 
त्वम् ब्रूहि मनोज्ञान्गी केन त्वम् च विरूपिता |_END
BEGIN_
"What is the weapon of that Rama by whom these many demons are killed in war, likewise Duushana and 
Trishira are killed, and even the unkillable Khara is killed? Oh, lady with fascinating limbs, who disfigured 
you? That you tell. [1-34-3, 4a]_END

B_3_C_31_18
BEGIN_
येन येन च गच्छन्ति राक्षसा भय कर्शिताः || ३-३१-१९तेन तेन स्म पश्यन्ति रामम् एव अग्रतः स्थितम् |
इत्थम् विनाशितम् जनस्थानम् तेन तव अनघ || ३-३१-२०_END
BEGIN_
"To whichever nook those demons smitten by fear of those serpent-like are fleeing, they have seeing 
Rama alone standing afore them in that corner, and oh, merited king Ravana, in this way your Janasthaana 
is totally ruined by that Rama. [3-31-19b, 20] [3-31-19]_END

B_3_C_33_8
BEGIN_
येषाम् चारः च कोशः च नयः च जयताम् वर |अस्वाधीना नरेन्द्राणाम् प्राकृतैः ते जनैः समाः || ३-३३-९_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, so-called best one among triumphant kings, those kings that do not retain spies, treasuries and 
strategies under their control, but vouchsafe them to others, they are of a piece with the peasantry. 
[3-33-9]_END

B_3_C_32_13
BEGIN_
वनम् चैत्ररथम् दिव्यम् नलिनीम् नंदनम् वनम् || ३-३२-१५विनाशयति यः क्रोधात् देव उद्यानानि वीर्यवान् 
|_END
BEGIN_
He who enviously devastated the divine gardens of Kubera, called Caitraratha, along with a divine Lake 
of Lotuses pertaining to the same Kubera, called Pushkarini, and the gardens of Indra, called Nandana, 
along with other paradisiacal gardens of gods, Shuurpanakha saw such an envious demon. [3-32-15b, 16a]_END

B_3_C_34_3
BEGIN_
इति उक्ता राक्षस इन्द्रेण राक्षसी क्रोध मूर्च्छिता || ३-३४-४ततो रामम् यथा न्यायम् आख्यातुम् उपचक्रमे 
|_END
BEGIN_
When the king of demons has asked her thus, she that demoness Shuurpanakha who is in a fit of fury then 
commenced to describe Rama in the point of fact. [3-34-4b, 5a]_END

B_3_C_31_19
BEGIN_
अकंपन अचः श्रुत्वा रावणो वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् |गमिष्यामि जनस्थनम् रामम् हन्तुम् स लक्ष्मणम् || ३-३१-२१_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of Akampana Ravana said these words, "I will to go to Janasthaana to kill Rama 
along with Lakshmana." [3-31-21]_END

B_3_C_33_9
BEGIN_
यस्मात् पश्यन्ति दूरस्थान् सर्वान् अर्थान् नराधिपाः |चारेण तस्मात् उच्यन्ते राजानो दीर्घ चक्षुषः 
|| ३-३३-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, titular overlord of humans, only some can be called prescient kings because they see all the situations 
happening distantly through their spies. [3-33-10]_END

B_3_C_32_14
BEGIN_
चन्द्र सूर्यौ महा भागौ उत्तिष्ठन्तौ परंतपौ || ३-३२-१६निवारयति बाहुभ्याम् यः शैल शिखरोपमः |_END
BEGIN_
Shuurpanakha saw him who is similar to the pinnacle of a mountain, and who with his two hands 
forestalls the highly propitious ones that are the stiflers of their enemies, namely the Sun and Moon, when they tend to 
rise. [3-32-16b, 17a]_END

B_3_C_34_4
BEGIN_
दीर्घबाहुः विशालाक्षः चीर कृष्ण अजिन अम्बरः || ३-३४-५कन्दर्प सम रूपः च रामो दशरथ आत्मजः |_END
BEGIN_
"Dasharatha's son Rama is the one with inescapable arms and keen-eyed, but has jute-cloths and skin 
of black-deer for his dress, yet in semblance he is similar to the Love-god. [3-34-5b, 6a]_END

B_3_C_31_20
BEGIN_
अथ एवम् उक्ते वचने प्रोवाच इदम् अकंपनः |श्रुणु राजन् यथा वृत्तम् रामस्य बल पौरुषम् || ३-३१-२२_END
BEGIN_
When Ravana said so then Akampana said these words in reply, " listen, oh, king, what all has happened, 
and of what in actuality is Rama's spirit and grit. [3-31-22]_END

B_3_C_33_10
BEGIN_
अयुक्त चारम् मन्ये त्वाम् प्राकृतैः सचिवैः युतः |स्व जनम् च जनस्थानम् निहतम् न अवबुध्यसे || ३-३३-११_END
BEGIN_
"I believe that you have no spies worth their profession, yet you are associated with artless ministers 
worthy to worship you, hence you are incognisant of the ruination of all of your subjects in Janasthaana, 
including Janasthaana. [3-33-11]_END

B_3_C_32_15
BEGIN_
दश वर्ष सहस्राणि तपः तप्त्वा महावने || ३-३२-१७पुरा स्वयंभुवे धीरः शिरांसि उपजहार यः |_END
BEGIN_
That courageous one who in early times has practised ascesis for ten thousand years in a great-forest, 
and who on accomplishing it has dedicated ten of his heads to the Self-Created Brahma, she saw such 
a Ravana with such ten heads. [3-32-17b, 18a]_END

B_3_C_34_5
BEGIN_
शक्र चाप निभम् चापम् विकृष्य कनकांगदम् || ३-३४-६दीप्तान् क्षिपति नाराचान् सर्पान् इव महा विषान् 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Yanking out a bow with golden fillets, and that is similar to the bow of Indra in its shine, he strews 
candent iron-arrows that simulate snakes with deadly poison. [3-34-6b, 7a]_END

B_3_C_31_21
BEGIN_
असाध्यः कुपितो रामो विक्रमेण महायशाः |आप गायाः तु पूर्णाया वेगम् परिहरेत् शरैः || ३-३१-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Rama, the highly renolwned, is invincible just by braving against him, for that Rama in fury can stall 
the onrush of a plethoric river with his arrows. [3-31-23]_END

B_3_C_33_11
BEGIN_
चतुर्दश सहस्राणि रक्षसाम् भीम कर्मणाम् |हतानि एकेन रामेण खरः च सह दूषणः || ३-३३-१२_END
BEGIN_
"A single soul called Rama has eliminated fourteen thousand demons of dreadful deeds in Janasthaana, 
even Duushana is killed, even Khara is also killed. [3-33-12]_END

B_3_C_32_16
BEGIN_
देव दानव गधर्व पिशाच पतग उरगैः || ३-३२-१८अभयम् यस्य संग्रामे मृत्युतो मानुषाद् ऋते |_END
BEGIN_
Whereby, to whom there is an indemnity against death in war at the hand of gods, demons, gandharva-s, 
devils, birds, or reptiles, excepting humans, and Shuurpanakha saw such an unimperilled Ravana. [3-32-18b, 
19a]_END

B_3_C_34_6
BEGIN_
न आददानम् शरान् घोरान् न मुंचंतम् महाबलम् || ३-३४-७न कार्मुकम् विकर्षन्तम् रामम् पश्यामि संयुगे 
|_END
BEGIN_
"It has become imperceivable for me to me to see when and how he drew his ghastly arrows from quiver 
on the battleground; or, stretching his bow admitting those arrows on bowstring - no; or, his releasing 
those sharp edged arrows from the bow - no; why them, that great mighty Rama himself has become imperceptible 
in the fastness of his action. [3-34-7b, 8a]_END

B_3_C_31_22
BEGIN_
स तारा ग्रह नक्षत्रम् नभः च अपि अवसादयेत् |असौ रामः तु सीदन्तीम् श्रीमान् अभ्युद्धरेत् महीम् || 
३-३१-२४_END
BEGIN_
"That magnificent Rama can collapse even the firmament along with its starlets, stars and planets, and 
he even can elevate the earth if it were to collapse. [3-31-24]_END

B_3_C_33_12
BEGIN_
ऋषीणाम् अभयम् दत्तम् कृत क्षेमाः च दण्डकाः |धर्षितम् च जनस्थानम् रामेण अक्लिष्ट कारिणा || ३-३३-१३_END
BEGIN_
"That indefatigable champion Rama gave security to the sages, rendered Dandaka forest safeguarded, and 
he put Janasthaana to rout. [3-33-13]_END

B_3_C_35_0
BEGIN_
ततः शूर्पणखा वाक्यम् तत् श्रुत्वा रोम हर्षणम् |सचिवान् अभ्यनुज्ञाय कार्यम् बुद्ध्वा जगाम ह || ३-३५-१_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the exciting advise of Shuurpanakha then Ravana bade adieu to ministers, and indeed on resolving 
his further task he proceeded to his personal palace chambers. [3-35-1]_END

B_3_C_32_17
BEGIN_
मन्त्रैः अभितुष्टम् पुण्यम् अध्वरेषु द्विजातिभिः || ३-३२-१९हविर्धानेषु यः सोमम् उपहन्ति महाबलः |_END
BEGIN_
He who is an extreme-ultraist that expropriates the Soma-juice-oblation form the vessels of oblation 
in Vedic-rituals, which Soma juice-oblation is blest with Vedic-hymns and kept separately by Vedic Brahmans, 
since it is intended and shall belong to Indra and other divinities, and she saw such a plunderer. [3-32-19b, 
20a]_END

B_3_C_31_23
BEGIN_
भित्वा वेलाम् समुद्रस्य लोकान् आप्लावयेत् विभुः |वेगम् वा अपि समुद्रस्य वाअयुम् वा विधमेत् शरैः 
|| ३-३१-२५_END
BEGIN_
"On breaching the shoreline of the ocean with his arrows that lord Rama can deluge worlds, and he can 
stem the tide of turbulent ocean, or can even stall the agent of that turbulence, namely the wind. [3-31-25]_END

B_3_C_34_7
BEGIN_
हन्यमानम् तु तत् सैन्यम् पश्यामि शर वृष्टिभिः || ३-३४-८इन्द्रेण इव उत्तमम् सस्यम् आहतम् तु अश्म 
वृष्टिभिः |_END
BEGIN_
"As with a crop of grain devastated by a hailstorm of Indra, I could only see that best army while it 
is being annihilated with a downpour of arrows. [3-34-8b, 9a]_END

B_3_C_33_13
BEGIN_
त्वम् तु लुब्धः प्रमत्तः च पराधीनः च रावण |विषये स्वे समुत्पन्नम् यो भयम् न अवबुध्यसे || ३-३३-१४_END
BEGIN_
"On your part you are but selfish, hotheaded, and others like the appeasers of your lust, or these artless 
ministers, or those underpaid unfaithful spies hold you down, and such as you are, you are unperceptive 
of the calamity rising up against you in your own kingdom. [3-33-14]_END

B_3_C_35_1
BEGIN_
तत् कार्यम् अनुगम्यांतर् यथावत् उपलभ्य च |दोषाणाम् च गुणानाम् च सम्प्रधार्य बल अबलम् || ३-३५-२
इति कर्तव्यम् इति एव कृत्वा निश्चयम् आत्मनः |स्थिर बुद्धिः ततो रम्याम् यान शालाम् जगाम ह || ३-३५-३_END
BEGIN_
While following up his thinking about that task he got a pertinent thought, and on deliberating about 
the credits and discredits, strengths and weaknesses of that thought he decided that 'this is to be 
done in this method only.' On taking a decision in that way and with a firm mind he indeed proceeded 
to his excellent vehicle-garage. [3-35-2, 3]_END

B_3_C_32_18
BEGIN_
प्राप्त यज्ञ हरम् दुष्टम् ब्रह्म घ्नम् क्रूर कारिणम् || ३-३२-२०कर्कशम् निरनुक्रोशम् प्रजानाम् अहिते 
रतम् |_END
BEGIN_
He who is such an embezzler of the Vedic-rituals at the time of their culmination, a malicious one, 
and one with cruel acts, a hinderer of Vedic-rituals, or, the slayer of those Brahmans that conduct 
Vedic-rituals contrary to his wishes, and one who is heartless and a rampant demon, who is a delighter 
in the iniquity to the people, at him Shuurpanakha saw. [3-32-20b, 21a]_END

B_3_C_31_24
BEGIN_
संहृत्य वा पुनर् लोकान् विक्रमेण महायशाः |शकतः श्रेष्ठः स पुरुषः स्रष्टुम् पुनर् अपि प्रजाः || ३-३१-२६_END
BEGIN_
"That great valorous and the ablest among humans is capable to destroy all the worlds with his valour, 
and even capable of creating the people again._END

B_3_C_34_8
BEGIN_
रक्षसाम् भीम वीर्याणाम् सहस्राणि चतुर्दश || ३-३४-९निहतानि शरैः तीक्ष्णैः तेन एकेन पदातिना |अर्धाधिक 
मुहूर्तेन खरः च सह दूषणः || ३-३४-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Thus a lone foot-soldier with his excruciating arrows has exterminated fourteen thousand demons with 
fiendish might, including Duushana, and along withKhara, say, within one and half hours. [3-34-9b,10]_END

B_3_C_33_14
BEGIN_
तीक्ष्णम् अल्प प्रदातारम् प्रमत्तम् गर्वितम् शठम् |व्यसने सर्व भूतानि न अभिधावन्ति पार्थिवम् || 
३-३३-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Should a king be overweening, an under-payer, an improvident, self-conceited, and dubious, all his 
subjects bid goodbye to such a king when he is in strife. [3-33-15]_END

B_3_C_35_2
BEGIN_
यान शालाम् ततो गत्वा प्रच्छन्नम् राक्षस अधिपः |सूतम् संचोदयामास रथः संयुज्यताम् इति || ३-३५-४_END
BEGIN_
That lordly demon then has gone to the vehicle garage in secrecy, and directed the charioteer thus as, 
'let the chariot be harnessed.' [3-35-4]_END

B_3_C_32_19
BEGIN_
रावणम् सर्व भूतानाम् सर्व लोक भयावहम् || ३-३२-२१राक्षसी भ्रातरम् क्रूरम् सा ददर्श महाबलम् |_END
BEGIN_
She that demoness Shuurpanakha saw her brother who makes all beings to wail, an alarming one to all 
the worlds, an atrocious one and highly formidable Ravana. [3-32-21b, 22a]_END

B_3_C_34_9
BEGIN_
ऋषीणाम् अभयम् दत्तम् कृत क्षेमाः च दण्डकाः || ३-३४-११एका कथंचित् मुक्ता अहम् परिभूय महात्मना |
स्त्री वधम् शंकमानेन रामेण विदितात्मना || ३-३४-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Accorded is the protection to the sages, and Dandaka is made as a snuggest place for them. I am the 
lone one somehow let off by such a high-minded Rama, of course, on humiliating me by cutting my nose 
and ears. Maybe, it is because he is hesitant of woman-slaughter for he is a well-versed soul. [1-34-11, 
12]_END

B_3_C_31_25
BEGIN_
न हि रामो दशग्रीव शक्यो जेतुम् रणे त्वया |रक्षसाम् वा अपि लोकेन स्वर्गः पाप जनैः इव || ३-३१-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Dashagriiva, it is impossible to conquer that Rama in war for your, either singly or along with 
the hosts of the demon-supporters of yours, as one heaven cannot be won by many sinners. [3-31-27]_END

B_3_C_33_15
BEGIN_
अतिमानिनम् अग्राह्यम् आत्म संभावितम् नरम् |क्रोधिनम् व्यसने हन्ति स्व जनो अपि नराधिपम् || ३-३३-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Should a ruler be unduly self-conceited, self-centred, self-adulating and a spitfire too, his own kith 
and kin will ruin him when he is in distress. [3-33-16]_END

B_3_C_35_3
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः क्षणेन एव सारथिः लघु विक्रमः |रथम् संयोजयामास तस्य अभिमतम् उत्तमम् || ३-३५-५_END
BEGIN_
When that brisk-paced charioteer is said in this way he instantly harnessed the favourite and choicest 
chariot of Ravana with horses and got it ready. [3-35-5]_END

B_3_C_32_20
BEGIN_
तम् दिव्य वस्त्र आभरणम् दिव्य माल्य उपशोभितम् || ३-३२-२२आसने सूपविष्टम् तम् काले कालम् इव उद्यतम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
And at him who is conspicuously sitting on a throne, attired and bejewelled in excellent apparels and 
jewels, shining forth with marvellous garlands, and who is like the Ultimate-Time on the rise destined 
for the Eventual-Time. [3-32-22b, 23a]_END

B_3_C_34_10
BEGIN_
भ्राता च अस्य महातेजा गुणतः तुल्य विक्रमः |अनुरक्तः च भक्तः च लक्ष्मणो नाम वीर्यवान् || ३-३४-१३_END
BEGIN_
"A highly resplendent one who by his trait matches his brother in bravery, an adherent and a devotee 
of his brother, such a stout-hearted one is Rama's brother known as Lakshmana. [1-34-13]_END

B_3_C_31_26
BEGIN_
न तम् वध्यम् अहम् मन्ये सर्वैः देव असुरैः अपि |अयम् अस्य वध उपाय तत् एकमनाः शृउणु || ३-३१-२८_END
BEGIN_
"I do not think that he is killable even for all god and demons, and this is the idea to kill him, and 
to this you may listen attentively. [3-31-28]_END

B_3_C_33_16
BEGIN_
न अनुतिष्ठति कार्याणि भयेषु न बिभेति च |क्षिप्रम् राज्यात् च्युतो दीनः तृणैः तुल्यो भवेत् इह || 
३-३३-१७_END
BEGIN_
"That king who does not officiate his good offices, nor un-panicked into panicky situations, he will 
be quickly overthrown from his kingdom, and on becoming a debased individual he will be equated with 
a piece of straw in this world. [3-33-17]_END

B_3_C_32_21
BEGIN_
राक्षसेन्द्रम् महाभागम् पौलस्त्य कुल नन्दनम् || ३-३२-२३उपगम्य अब्रवीत् वाक्यम् राक्षसी भय विह्वला 
|रावणम् शत्रु हन्तारम् मंत्रिभिः परिवारितम् || ३-३२-२४_END
BEGIN_
Demoness Shuurpanakha nearing Ravana, who is the highly fortunate king of demons, an enemy-destroyer 
and a felicity of the dynasty of Sage Pulasta, and who is now surrounded by his ministers, she spoke 
this sentence. [3-32-23b, 24]_END

B_3_C_35_4
BEGIN_
कांचनम् रथम् आस्थाय कामगम् रत्न भूषितम् |पिशाच वदनैः युक्तम् खरैः कनक भूषणैः || ३-३५-६मेघ प्रतिम 
नादेन स तेन धनद अनुजः |राक्षसाधिपतिः श्रीमान् ययौ नद नदी पतिम् || ३-३५-७_END
BEGIN_
That chariot which is decorated with golden ornaments, yoked with monster-faced mules that have gem 
studded trappings is rideable by the wish of the rider, and sitting in such a chariot which is wholly 
golden and which rides with a sound like the pealing of thunder, that celebrated Ravana, the brother 
of Kubera and the lord of demons, travelled towards the lord of rivers and rivulets, namely the ocean. 
[3-35-6,7]_END

B_3_C_34_11
BEGIN_
अमर्षी दुर्जयो जेता विक्रान्तो बुद्धिमान् बली |रामस्य दक्षिणे बाहुः नित्यम् प्राणो बहिः चरः || ३-३४-१४_END
BEGIN_
"That Lakshmana is an easily irritable one, he is not that easily invincible, an easy victor, but not 
an easygoing valiant, yet he is an intellectual at ease, and a mighty one who does not ease off, such 
a Lakshmana is the perpetual right-hand and the peripherally moving life of Rama. [1-34-14]_END

B_3_C_31_27
BEGIN_
भार्या तस्य उत्तमा लोके सीता नाम सुमध्यमा |श्यामा सम विभक्त अंगी स्त्री रत्नम् रत्न बूषिता || ३-३१-२९_END
BEGIN_
"An excellent woman in the world is there, a youthful one with symmetrical limbs, a jewel-like lady 
adorned with jewellery, that slender-waisted one who is known as Seetha is his wife. [3-31-29]_END

B_3_C_33_17
BEGIN_
शुष्क काष्ठैः भवेत् कार्यम् लोष्टैः अपि च पांसुभिः |न तु स्थानात् परिभ्रष्टैः कार्यम् स्यात् वसुधाधिपैः 
|| ३-३३-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Dried sticks, globs or the particles of dust are of some avail, but kings fallen from their position 
are of no avail. [3-33-18]_END

B_3_C_35_5
BEGIN_
स श्वेत वाल व्यजनः श्वेतः छत्रो दशाननः |स्निग्ध वैदूर्य संकाश तप्त कान्चन भूषणः || ३-३५-८दशग्रीवो 
विंशति भुजो दर्शनीय परिच्छदः |त्रिदश अरिः मुनीन्द्र घ्नो दश शीर्ष इव अद्रि राट् || ३-३५-९कामगम् 
रथम् आस्थाय शुशुभे राक्षसाधिपः |विद्युन् मण्डलवान् मेघः स बलाक इव अंबरे || ३-३५-१०_END
BEGIN_
Dasha-aanana, the decahedral demon, whose complexion like the smoothened Lapis-gem is lustrous, whose 
regalia that comprise white long-furred fans, white parasol and the like is spectacular, whose ornaments 
made out of refined gold are glittering, who similar to a kingly mountain with ten pinnacles and crags 
by way of his ten heads and twenty arms is gorgeous, and such a chief of demons who by that way is an 
adversary of gods and cutthroat of eminent-sages, seated in a nitid golden chariot that is rideable 
by the wish of its steersman, he shone forth like a black-cloud fringed with the streaks of lightning 
and rimmed with flights of cranes. [3-35-8, 9, 10]_END

B_3_C_32_22
BEGIN_
तम् अब्रवीत् दीप्त विशाल लोचनम्प्रदर्शयित्वा भय लोभ मोहिता |सुदारुणम् वाक्यम् अभीत चारिणी
महात्मना शूर्पणखा विरूपिता || ३-३२-२५_END
BEGIN_
She who is disfigured by the high souled Lakshmana, and who is still perplexed with the fear of Lakshmana 
and her own craving for Rama as well, on displaying her misfortune to everybody that fearless rover 
Shuurpanakha spoke this very caustic sentence to Ravana, whose eyes are broad and burning. [3-32-25]_END

B_3_C_34_12
BEGIN_
रामस्य तु विशालाक्षी पूर्णेन्दु सदृश आनना |धर्म पत्नी प्रिया नित्यम् भर्तृः प्रिय हिते रता || ३-३४-१५_END
BEGIN_
"But, one with her broad-eyes, face similar to the full-moon is the dear and wedded wife of Rama, and 
she always takes delight in the well-being of her dear one, namely Rama. [1-34-15]_END

B_3_C_36_0
BEGIN_
मारीच श्रूयताम् तात वचनम् मम भाषतः |
आर्तो अस्मि मम च आर्तस्य भवान् हि परमा गतिः || ३-३६-१_END
BEGIN_
"Give attention to my words as I speak, oh, sire, Maareecha, I am an anguished one,
and when I am in such an anguish you are the ultimate course to me, isn't so." Thus Ravana started
addressing Maareecha. [3-36-1]_END

B_3_C_31_28
BEGIN_
न एव देवी न गन्धर्वी न अप्सरा न च पन्नगी |तुल्या सीमन्तिनी तस्या मानुषी तु कुतो भवेत् || ३-३१-३०_END
BEGIN_
"No goddess can be likened to that mature lady; a gandharva female - no; a apsara female - no; a pannaga 
female -no, then how can there be a woman of her like? [3-31-30]_END

B_3_C_33_18
BEGIN_
उपभुक्तम् यथा वासः स्रजो वा मृदिता यथा |एवम् राज्यात् परिभ्रष्टः समर्थो अपि निरर्थकः || ३-३३-१९_END
BEGIN_
"As to how a used up raiment or a crumpled flower-tassel is meaningless, likewise a king derelict from 
his kingdom, though functional, is meaningless. [3-33-19]_END

B_3_C_35_6
BEGIN_
स शैलम् सागर अनूपम् वीर्यवान् अवलोकयन् |नाना पुष्प फलैर् वृक्षैर् अनुकीर्णम् सहस्रशः || ३-३५-११_END
BEGIN_
That dauntless Ravana forged ahead while viewing the area along the coastline which is interspersed 
with thousands of mountains and which is with variously flowered and fruited trees. [3-35-11]_END

B_3_C_34_13
BEGIN_
सा सुकेशी सुनासोरुः सुरूपा च यशस्विनी |देवत इव वनस्थ अस्यराजते श्रीर् इव अपरा || ३-३४-१६_END
BEGIN_
"She is the one with lengthy hairdo, her nose and thighs are fine, and that glorious one with fine looks 
is the wife of Rama, and she is beaming forth like a sylvan deity situated in that woodland, who in 
turn is like Goddess Lakshmi in a temporal form. [1-34-16]_END

B_3_C_36_1
BEGIN_
जानीषे त्वम् जनस्थाने भ्राता यत्र खरो मम |
दूषणः च महाबाहुः स्वसा शूर्पणखा च मे || ३-३६-२
त्रिशिराः च महातेजा राक्षसः पिशित अशनः |
अन्ये च बहवः शूरा लब्ध लक्षा निशाचराः || ३-३६-३
वसन्ति मत् नियोगेन अधिवासम् च राक्षसः |
बाधमाना महारण्ये मुनीन् ये धर्म चारिणः || ३-३६-४_END
BEGIN_
"You are aware as to how my brother Khara, and the mighty armed Duushana, also my
sister Shuurpanakha, and even the highly fiery demon and devourer of raw-flesh Trishira, and even
numerous other night-walking demons who are cocksure of hitting their targets have made Janasthaana
as their residency, and while residing there they put the sages of that great forest that tread a
righteous path to torture, of course, all this as assigned by me. [3-36-2, 3, 4]_END

B_3_C_31_29
BEGIN_
तस्य अपहर भार्याम् त्वम् तम् प्रमथ्य महावने |सीताया रहितो रामो न च एव हि भविष्यति || ३-३१-३१_END
BEGIN_
"You forcefully abduct his wife when she is in solitude, and indeed Rama will not exist reft of Seetha." 
Akampana advised Ravana in this way. [3-31-31]_END

B_3_C_33_19
BEGIN_
अप्रमत्तः च यो राजा सर्वज्ञो विजितेन्द्रियः |कृतज्ञो धर्म शीलः च स राजा तिष्ठते चिरम् || ३-३३-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Which king will be cautious, clever, conscientious, with his controlled senses, and thankful, that 
king survives for a long time. [3-33-20]_END

B_3_C_35_7
BEGIN_
शीत मंगल तोयाभिः पद्मिनीभिः समंततः |विशालैः आश्रम पदैः वेदिमद्भिः अलंकृतम् || ३-३५-१२_END
BEGIN_
Everywhere the coastland is bedecked with lotus-lakes containing clean and cool waters, and with extensive 
thresholds of hermitages containing Fire-altars. [3-35-12]_END

B_3_C_36_2
BEGIN_
चतुर्दश सहस्राणि रक्षसाम् भीम कर्मणाम् |
शूराणाम् लब्ध लक्षाणाम् खर चित्त अनुवर्तिनाम् || ३-३६-५
ते तु इदानीम् जनस्थाने वसमाना महाबलाः |_END
BEGIN_
"You are equally aware of the stationing fourteen thousand braving demons in
Janasthaana, who are the followers of the wish of Khara, who are with fiendish exploits, and who
are the troublemakers to the sages of Dandaka forest or to the intruders therein, aren't you.
[3-36-5]_END

B_3_C_34_14
BEGIN_
तप्त कांचन वर्ण आभा रक्त तुंग नखी शुभा |सीता नाम वरारोहा वैदेही तनु मध्यमा || ३-३४-१७_END
BEGIN_
"She has a complexion mathing the shade of refined gold, her nails are rosy and jutting, and she with 
her curvaceous hips and slim waist is the daughter of King of Videha, and known as Seetha. [1-34-17]_END

B_3_C_31_30
BEGIN_
अरोचयत् तद् वाक्यम् रावणो राक्षस अधिपः |चिंतयित्वा महाबाहुः अकंपनम् उवाच || ३-३१-३२_END
BEGIN_
The chief of demons Ravana favouring that idea thought of it and that mighty armed Ravana then spoke 
to Akampana. [3-31-32]_END

B_3_C_33_20
BEGIN_
नयनाभ्याम् प्रसुप्तो वा जागर्ति नय चक्षुषा |व्यक्त क्रोध प्रसादः च स राजा पूज्यते जनैः || ३-३३-२१_END
BEGIN_
"He who keeps his mental eyes of wariness will be wakeful even though he slept well closing his physical 
eyes and he who will make his fury and favour evident to people without any concealment or cunningness, 
people will highly revere him as a king._END

B_3_C_35_8
BEGIN_
कदल्य अटवि संशोभम् नालिकेर उपशोभितम् |सालैः तालैः तमालैः च तरुभिः च सुपुष्पितैः || ३-३५-१३_END
BEGIN_
Entire coast is gleaming with banana plantation and glistening with coconut trees, and the saala, palm, 
and tamaala trees are also in full blossom. [3-35-13]_END

B_3_C_34_15
BEGIN_
न एव देवी न गंधर्वा न यक्षी न च किंनरी |तथा रूपा मया नारी दृष्ट पूर्वा महीतले || ३-३४-१८_END
BEGIN_
"So far I have not seen any goddess with such a comeliness; a gandharva female - no; a yaksha female 
- no; a kinnara female - no; and a woman, no, not on the face of earth! [1-34-18]_END

B_3_C_36_3
BEGIN_
संगताः परम आयत्ता रामेण सह संयुगे || ३-३६-६
नाना शस्त्र प्रहरणाः खर प्रमुख राक्षसः |_END
BEGIN_
"But recently those great mighty demons that are the residents of Janasthaana,
namely Khara and others, preparing themselves inordinately and wielding diverse weapons and
assaulters, for their part had an encounter with Rama in a combat. [3-36-6, 7a]_END

B_3_C_31_31
BEGIN_
बाढम् कल्यम् गमिष्यामि हि एकः सारथिना सह |आनेष्यामि च वैदेहीम् इमाम् हृष्टो महा पुरीम् || ३-३१-३३_END
BEGIN_
"Agreed! I wish to go alone early in the morning with a charioteer and I delightfully wish to lead Vaidehi 
into the elegant city Lanka." Ravana declared that way. [3-31-33]_END

B_3_C_33_21
BEGIN_
त्वम् तु रावण दुर्बुद्धिः गुणैः एतैः विवर्जितः |यस्य ते अविदितः चारैः रक्षसाम् सुमहान् वधः || ३-३३-२२_END
BEGIN_
"But, oh, Ravana, because you are imprudent you are bereft of these merits, and such as you are, unknown 
is the very great massacre of demons to you, though not personally, but at least through your spies. 
[3-33-22]_END

B_3_C_35_9
BEGIN_
अत्यन्त नियत आहारैः शोभितम् परम ऋषिभिः |नागैः सुपर्णैः गंधर्वैः किंनरैः च सहस्रशः || ३-३५-१४
जित कामैः च सिद्धैः च चारणैः च उपशोभितम् |आजैः वैखानसैः माषैः वालखिल्यैः मरीचिपैः || ३-३५-१५_END
BEGIN_
It is brightened up with thousands of reptiles and birds, with those many celestial beings that frequent 
the earth like gandharva-s, kinnaraa-s. And with eminent sages who have highly controlled food-habits, 
as well. It is also refulgent with the self-denying Siddha-s, Carana-s, and with sages that are the 
brainchildren of Brahma, namely Vaikhanasa-s, Maasha-s, Vaalakhilya-s, Mariicipa-s. [3-35-14, 15]_END

B_3_C_34_16
BEGIN_
यस्य सीता भवेत् भार्या यम् च हृष्टा परिष्वजेत् |अति जीवेत् स सर्वेषु लोकेषु अपि पुरंदरात् || ३-३४-१९_END
BEGIN_
"To whom Seetha becomes a wife and around whom she gladly throws her arms after such a marriage, he 
lives more grandly than Indra in all the worlds. [1-34-19]_END

B_3_C_36_4
BEGIN_
तेन संजात रोषेण रामेण रण मूर्धनि || ३-३६-७
अनुक्त्वा परुषम् किंचित् शरैर् व्यापारितम् धनुः |_END
BEGIN_
"With rancour tiding in him, and without making any scathing remark in the least,
that Rama brought his bow into play with arrows in the van of the combat. [3-36-7b, 8a]_END

B_3_C_33_22
BEGIN_
पर अवमंता विषयेषु संगवान्न देश काल प्रविभाग तत्त्व वित् |अयुक्त बुद्धिः गुण दोष निश्चयेविपन्न 
राज्यो न चिरात् विपत्स्यते || ३-३३-२३_END
BEGIN_
"You are the humiliator of others, you hobnob only with your ravishes, and incognisant of the object 
for apportionment of time and place for your activities, as to when and where and how the things are 
to be dealt with. And, as you are not attending any kingly activity, or do not focus your mind in deciding 
rights and wrongs, thereby your kingdom will get ruined and you will be imperilled, not before long." 
Thus Shuurpanakha declaimed Ravana about his worthlessness as a king. [3-33-23]_END

B_3_C_31_32
BEGIN_
तत् एवम् उक्त्वा प्रययौ खर युक्तेन रावणः |रथेन आदित्य वर्णेन दिशः सर्वाः प्रकाशयन् || ३-३१-३४_END
BEGIN_
Saying so Ravana journeyed in a chariot that is yoked with mule-like horses, and that has the dazzling 
of the sun, whereby all the directions are made to glitter. [3-31-34]_END

B_3_C_35_10
BEGIN_
दिव्य आभरण माल्याभिः दिव्य रूपाभिः आवृतम् |क्रीडा रति विधिज्ञाभिः अप्सरोभिः सहस्रशः || ३-३५-१६_END
BEGIN_
With thousands of celestial maidens divine in their mien, namely apsara-s, who are prettified with divine 
ornaments and garlands, and who are also the experts in the methodical sex-games that seaside is pervaded. 
[3-35-16]_END

B_3_C_34_17
BEGIN_
सा सुशीला वपुः श्लाघ्या रूपेण अप्रतिमा भुवि |तव अनुरूपा भार्या सा त्वम् च तस्याः पतिः वरः || ३-३४-२०_END
BEGIN_
"She is a highly gracious lady, laudable by her bodily structure, incomparable by her appearance, and 
she will become a seemly wife of yours, and you too will become a best husband of hers. [1-34-20]_END

B_3_C_36_5
BEGIN_
चतुर्दश सहस्राणि रक्षसाम् उग्र तेजसाम् || ३-३६-८
निहतानि शरैः दीप्तैः मानुषेण पदातिना |_END
BEGIN_
"But that foot-soldier, that too, a human, has completely wiped out those
fourteen-thousand demons with flaring fieriness with his fierce arrows. [3-36-8b, 9a]_END

B_3_C_33_23
BEGIN_
इति स्व दोषान् परिकीर्तिताम् तयासमीक्ष्य बुद्ध्या क्षणदा चरेश्वरः |धनेन दर्पेण बलेन च अन्वितो
विचिन्तयामास चिरम् स रावणः || ३-३३-२४_END
BEGIN_
In this way when Shuurpanakha extolled only his negative traits, he that lord of night-walkers Ravana, 
who holds only his pride, power and prosperity dear to him, pored them over in his mind and contemplated 
over a time. [3-33-24]_END

B_3_C_31_33
