BEGIN_
स रथो राक्षस इंद्रस्य नक्षत्र पथगो महान् |चंचूर्यमानः शुशुभे जलदे चंद्रमा इव || ३-३१-३५_END
BEGIN_
That opalescent chariot of the lord of demons while speedily progressing through starry way shone forth 
as if it is the moon in clouds. [3-31-35]_END

B_3_C_35_11
BEGIN_
सेवितम् देव पत्नीभिः श्रीमतीभिः उपासितम् |देव दानव सन्घैः च चरितम् तु अमृत अशिभिः || ३-३५-१७_END
BEGIN_
That seacoast is adored by the propitious wives of gods and frequented by the assemblages of gods who 
thrive upon ambrosia, and even patronised by demons that strive for ambrosia. [3-35-17]_END

B_3_C_34_18
BEGIN_
ताम् तु विस्तीर्ण जघनाम् पीन उत्तुंग पयो धराम् |भार्या अर्थे तु तव आनेतुम् उद्यता अहम् वर आननाम् 
|| ३-३४-२१विरूपिता अस्मि क्रूरेण लक्ष्मणेन महाभुज_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, mighty shouldered brother, but when I ventured to bring her as your wife, whose hips are broad, 
bosom fat and bulgy, face excellent, that cruel Lakshmana disfigured me. [1-34-21, 22a]_END

B_3_C_36_6
BEGIN_
खरः च निहतः संख्ये दूषणः च निपातितः || ३-३६-९
हत्वा त्रिशिरसम् च अपि निर्भया दण्डकाः कृताः |_END
BEGIN_
"Khara is hewed down, Duushana is mowed down, and even Trishira is hacked down,
thereof that Dandaka forest is rendered free from the fear of demons. [3-36-9b, 10a]_END

B_3_C_31_34
BEGIN_
स दूरे च आश्रमम् गत्वा ताटकेयम् उपागतम् |मारीचेन अर्चितो राजा भक्ष्य भोज्यैः अमानुषैः || ३-३१-३६_END
BEGIN_
On going to the hermitage of Maareecha which is at a distant place Maareecha the son of Tataka received 
Ravana and venerated that king of demons with sweetmeats and savouries that are unavailable to humans. 
[3-31-36]_END

B_3_C_35_12
BEGIN_
हंस क्रौन्च प्लव आकीर्णम् सारसैः संप्रणादितम् |वैदूर्य प्रस्तरम् स्निग्धम् सांद्रम् सागर तेजसा || 
३-३५-१८_END
BEGIN_
It is spread with swans, ruddy-gees and frogs, and there the waterfowls are very noisy, and stones overlain 
on the coast are like lapis-gems, and with the ambience of ocean that whole delta is appearing smooth 
and sludgy. [3-35-18]_END

B_3_C_34_19
BEGIN_
ताम् तु दृष्ट्वा अद्य वैदेहीम् पूर्ण चन्द्र निभ आननाम् || ३-३४-२२मन्मथस्य शराणाम् च त्वम् विधेयो 
भविष्यसि |_END
BEGIN_
"You too will become a groveller at the arrows Lover-god in case you now see Vaidehi with a face shining 
like full-moon. [1-34-22, 23a]_END

B_3_C_36_7
BEGIN_
पित्रा निरस्तः क्रुद्धेन स भार्यः क्षीण जीवितः || ३-३६-१०
स हन्ता तस्य सैन्यस्य रामः क्षत्रिय पांसनः |_END
BEGIN_
"He who is put to flight by his infuriated father, and who came to Dandaka forest
along with his wife, that ignoble Kshatriya is the slaughterer of that demonic army of mine, as his
lifespan is diminished. [3-36-10b, 11a]_END

B_3_C_31_35
BEGIN_
तम् स्वयम् पूजयित्वा तु आसनेन उदकेन च |अर्थ उपहितया वाचा मारीचो वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् || ३-३१-३७_END
BEGIN_
Offering proper seat and water for washing feet and hands Maareecha personally attended Ravana and spoke 
to him this sentence that is worded meaningfully. [3-31-37]_END

B_3_C_35_13
BEGIN_
पाण्डुराणि विशालानि दिव्य माल्य युतानि च |तूर्य गीत अभिजुष्टानि विमानानि समंततः || ३-३५-१९तपसा 
जित लोकानाम् कामगान् अभिसंपतन् |गन्धर्व अप्सरसः चैव ददर्श धनदानुजः || ३-३५-२०_END
BEGIN_
While Ravana, the brother of Kubera, is quickly transiting he saw everywhere the whitish and widish 
aircrafts belonging to the deified souls who acquired higher worlds, and from those aircrafts adorned 
with divine flowery tassels and piloted by the wish of their steersmen, instrumental and vocal music 
is resonating, and gandharva-s are singing and apsara-s are dancing in them. [3-35-19, 20]_END

B_3_C_36_8
BEGIN_
अशीलः कर्कशः तीक्ष्णो मूर्खो लुब्धो अजित इन्द्रियः || ३-३६-११
त्यक्त धर्मः तु अधर्म आत्मा भूतानाम् अहिते रतः |_END
BEGIN_
"He is out of character, brutal, firestorm, senseless, selfish, one with his senses
unconquered and righteousness discarded, and he is an unrighteous soul just delighting in the
disservice of all beings. [3-36-11b, 12a]_END

B_3_C_34_20
BEGIN_
यदि तस्याम् अभिप्रायो भार्या अर्थे तव जायते |शीघ्रम् उद् ध्रियताम् पादो जयार्थम् इह दक्षिणः || ३-३४-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Hence, if you hatch an opinion to make her as your wife, and if you aspire success, now itself quickly 
put your best foot, namely your right foot, forward. [1-34-23]_END

B_3_C_31_36
BEGIN_
कश्चित् सुकुशलम् राजन् लोकानाम् राक्षसाधिप |आशंके न अथ जाने त्वम् यतः तूर्णम् उपागतम् || ३-३१-३८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, king and supremo of demons, I am anxious to know whether everything safe and secure to the inhabitants 
of your kingdom, for I am not in the know of the reason by which now you have come here rushingly. [3-31-38]_END

B_3_C_35_14
BEGIN_
निर्यास रस मूलानाम् चंदनानाम् सहस्रशः |वनानि पश्यन् सौम्यानि घ्राण तृप्ति कराणि च || ३-३५-२१_END
BEGIN_
Ravana proceeded while observing thousands of woodlands with sandalwood trees that are soothing and 
satisfying the sense of smell, and that oozed sweet-smelling resin at their bases. [3-35-21]_END

B_3_C_37_0
BEGIN_
तत् श्रुत्वा राक्षसेन्द्रस्य वाक्यम् वाक्य विशारदः |
प्रत्युवाच महाप्राज्ञो मारीचो राक्षसेश्वरम् || ३-३७-१_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that idea of the chief of demons Ravana in abducting Seetha, Maareecha, a
well-informed one and an articulator spoke to the lord of demons in reply. [3-37-1]_END

B_3_C_34_21
BEGIN_
रोचते यदि ते वाक्यम् मम एतत् राक्षसेश्वर |क्रियताम् निर्विशंकेन वचनम् मम रावण || ३-३४-२४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, the king of demons Ravana, if this advise of mine is pleasing to you, let this idea be actualised 
without any shilly-shallying in your mind. [1-34-24]_END

B_3_C_36_9
BEGIN_
येन वैरम् विना अरण्ये सत्त्वम् आश्रित्य केवलम् || ३-३६-१२
कर्ण नास अपहारेण भगिनी मे विरूपिता |
तस्य भार्याम् जनस्थानात् सीताम् सुर सुत उपमाम् || ३-३६-१३
आनयिष्यामि विक्रम्य सहायः तत्र मे भव |_END
BEGIN_
"By whom my sister is disfigured stripping off her nose and ears, that too, without
any enmity but just depending upon his own brawn, I would like to inveigle such a man's nymphean
wife Seetha holding sway on her in Janasthaana, and in that matter I want you to be my aide in
Dandaka forest. [3-36-12b, 13, 14a]_END

B_3_C_31_37
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तो महातेजा मारीचेन स रावण |ततः पश्चात् इदम् वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् वाक्य कोविदः || ३-३१-३९_END
BEGIN_
When Maareecha said so to him that greatly radiant one who is a sententious speaker that Ravana thereafter 
spoke this sentence. [3-31-39]_END

B_3_C_35_15
BEGIN_
अगुरूणाम् च मुख्यानाम् वनानि उपवनानि च |तक्कोलानाम् च जात्यानाम् फलानाम् च सुगन्धिनाम् || ३-३५-२२_END
BEGIN_
He also observed on his way the forests and woodlands containing the noteworthy aloe plants, Takkola 
trees, and the nutmeg trees that are with fruits and aromatic, as well. [3-35-22]_END

B_3_C_37_1
BEGIN_
सुलभाः पुरुषा राजन् सततम् प्रिय वादिनः |
अप्रियस्य च पथ्यस्य वक्ता श्रोता च दुर्लभः || ३-३७-२_END
BEGIN_
"It will always be easy to get people who talk pleasantly, oh, king, but it is
impossible to get them who talk judgementally and give suggestions that may be apparently insipid,
but that are recuperative, more so, it is impossible to get listeners of such advises. [3-37-2]_END

B_3_C_34_22
BEGIN_
विज्ञाय इह आत्म शक्तिम् च क्रियताम् च महाबल |सीता तव अनवद्यांगी भार्यत्वे राक्षसेश्वर || ३-३४-२५_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, king of the demons, realise your stout-heartedness, and oh, great mighty one, let that immaculately 
limbed Seetha be abducted to become your wife. [1-34-25]_END

B_3_C_31_38
BEGIN_
आरक्षो मे हतः तात रामेण अक्लिष्ट कारिणा |जनस्थानम् अवध्यम् तत् सर्वम् युधि निपातितम् || ३-३१-४०
तस्य मे कुरु साचिव्यम् तस्य भार्य अपहरणे |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, sire, Rama who is indefatigable in warring has ruined my security stationed at Janasthaana, and 
in war he even brought down all of Janasthaana which is undefeatable so far, such as I am, to me you 
have to render friendly help in kidnapping Rama's wife." [3-31-40]_END

B_3_C_36_10
BEGIN_
त्वया हि अहम् सहायेन पार्श्वस्थेन महाबल || ३-३६-१४
भ्रातृभिः च सुरान् युद्धे समग्रान् न अभिचिंतये |
तत् सहायो भव त्वम् मे समर्थो हि असि राक्षस || ३-३६-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, highly powerful Maareecha, with you and with my brothers standing by my side as
my associates, I indeed care a damn for all of the gods if they are going to wage a war against me,
therefore, oh, demon Maareecha, as you are capable of rendering aid you should indeed become my
aide in this venture. [3-36-14b, 15]_END

B_3_C_35_16
BEGIN_
पुष्पाणि च तमालस्य गुल्मानि मरिचस्य च |मुक्तानाम् च समूहानि शुष्यमाणानि तीरतः || ३-३५-२३_END
BEGIN_
Also seen are the flowers of Tamaala trees, shrubberies of pepper, and heaps of desiccating pearl-oysters 
along the seashore. [3-35-23]_END

B_3_C_37_2
BEGIN_
न नूनम् बुध्यसे रामम् महावीर्यम् गुण उन्नतम् |
अयुक्त चारः चपलो महेन्द्र वरुण उपमम् || ३-३७-३_END
BEGIN_
"Definitely you do not apperceive Rama who is decidedly dynamic and exaltedly adept,
for you are impetuous and desultory in dealing with your spies, but that Rama is identical to the
thunderous Mahendra and tempestuous Varuna, the Rain-god. [3-37-3]_END

B_3_C_34_23
BEGIN_
निशम्य रामेण शरैः अजिह्मगैःहतान् जनस्थान गतान् निशाचरान् |खरम् च दृष्ट्वा निहतम् च दूषणम्
त्वम् अद्य कृत्यम् प्रतिपत्तुम् अर्हसि || ३-३४-२६_END
BEGIN_
"On recognising that Rama with his straight shooting arrows destroyed the night-walkers positioned at 
Janasthaana, and further on distinguishing that Duushana, and even Khara, is dispatched, it is apt of 
you to awake to a workable action." Thus Shuurpanakha has earbashed Ravana. [1-34-26]_END

B_3_C_31_39
BEGIN_
राक्षसेन्द्र वचः श्रुत्वा मारीचो वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् || ३-३१-४१आख्याता केन वा सीता मित्र रूपेण शत्रुणा 
|त्वया राक्षस शार्दूल को न नंदति नंदितः || ३-३१-४२_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of that chief of demons, Maareecha spoke these words, "who broached the subject 
of Seetha with you, an enemy in the fakery of a friend? Oh, tigerly demon, who is that censurable one 
that is unhappy with you, since he is giving such a self-ruinous advise? [3-31-42]_END

B_3_C_36_11
BEGIN_
वीर्ये युद्धे च दर्पे च न हि अस्ति सदृशः तव |
उपायतो महान् शूरो महा माय विशारदः || ३-३६-१६_END
BEGIN_
"In valour, war and verve there is none similar to you, you are a topmost stalwart
in trickery, and a matchless expert in illusive-tricks. [3-36-16]_END

B_3_C_35_17
BEGIN_
शैलानि प्रवरान् चैव प्रवाल निचयान् तथा |कांचनानि च शृंगाणि राजतानि तथैव च || ३-३५-२४_END
BEGIN_
Thus, he saw the peaking boulders, like that the reefs of corals, and like that also at the mountains 
that have golden and silvern crests. [3-35-24]_END

B_3_C_37_3
BEGIN_
अपि स्वस्ति भवेत् तात सर्वेषाम् भुवि रक्षसाम् |
अपि रामो न संक्रुद्धः कुर्यात् लोकम् अराक्षसम् || ३-३७-४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, boy, will there be safety to all demons on earth? Or, that highly enraged Rama
will render this world de-demonised! [3-37-4]_END

B_3_C_31_40
BEGIN_
सीताम् इह आनस्व इति को ब्रवीति ब्रवीहि मे |रक्षो लोकस्य सर्वस्य कः शृंगम् च्छेत्तुम् इच्छति || ३-३१-४३_END
BEGIN_
" 'Seetha may be brought to Lanka...' who said it, say him to me, who is that one desiring to cut off 
the prominence of all the demons in all worlds in saying so?_END

B_3_C_36_12
BEGIN_
एतत् अर्थम् अहम् प्राप्तः त्वत् समीपम् निशाचर |
शृणु तत् कर्म साहाय्ये यत् कार्यम् वचनात् मम || ३-३६-१७_END
BEGIN_
"I have come nigh of you only for that reason, oh, nightwalker, and listen to that
deed which you have to do in the course of helping me as I detail you. [3-36-17]_END

B_3_C_35_18
BEGIN_
प्रस्रवाणि मनोज्ञानि प्रसन्नानि अद्भुतानि च |धन धान्य उपपन्नानि स्त्री रत्नैः आवृतानि च || ३-३५-२५
हस्ति अश्व रथ गाढानि नगराणि विलोकयन् |_END
BEGIN_
On seeing the delightful, serene, and marvellous cascades, and cities that are abundant in wealth and 
agricultural produce, and abundant with gemlike womenfolk, and that are replete with elephants, horses, 
and chariots, Ravana proceeded further. [3-35-25, 26a]_END

B_3_C_37_4
BEGIN_
अपि ते जीवित अंताय न उत्पन्ना जनकात्मजा |
अपि सीता निमित्तम् च न भवेत् व्यसनम् महत् || ३-३७-५_END
BEGIN_
"Has this Seetha, the daughter of Janaka, taken birth to end your life, or what! And
because of this Seetha will there be a great disaster, so to speak! [3-37-5]_END

B_3_C_36_13
BEGIN_
सौवर्णः त्वम् मृगो भूत्वा चित्रो रजत बिन्दुभिः |
आश्रमे तस्य रामस्य सीतायाः प्रमुखे चर || ३-३६-१८_END
BEGIN_
"On becoming an astounding golden deer with silver dots, you move in front of Seetha
in the hermitage of that Rama. [3-36-18]_END

B_3_C_31_41
BEGIN_
प्रोत्साहयति यः च त्वम् स च शत्रुः असंशयम् |आशी मुखात् दंष्ट्राम् उद्धर्तुम् च इच्छति त्वया || ३-३१-४४_END
BEGIN_
"Also, he who has motivated you in this way is an undoubted enemy of yours, for he wanted to extricate 
the fangs of a snake from its mouth, of course, through you. [3-31-44]_END

B_3_C_35_19
BEGIN_
तम् समम् सर्वतः स्निग्धम् मृदु संस्पर्श मारुतम् || ३-३५-२६अनूपे सिन्धु राजस्य ददर्श त्रिदिव उपमम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
Ravana observed the delta adjacent to seacoast of that kingly ocean to be uniform and smooth, while 
the light air breezing in there is soft for touch, thus it looked heavenly. [3-35-26b, 27a]_END

B_3_C_37_5
BEGIN_
अपि त्वाम् ईश्वरम् प्राप्य काम वृत्तम् निरंकुशम् |
न विनश्येत् पुरी लंका त्वया सह स राक्षसा || ३-३७-६_END
BEGIN_
"Egocentric and rampant, such as you are, on acquiring you as her lord, will the
City of Lanka be doomed along with her demons, and you put together, or what! [3-37-6]_END

B_3_C_36_14
BEGIN_
त्वाम् तु निःसंशयम् सीता दृष्ट्वा तु मृग रूपिणम् |
गृह्यताम् इति भर्तारम् लक्ष्मणम् च अभिधास्यति || | ३-३६-१९_END
BEGIN_
"On seeing you in the shape of a deer, Seetha undoubtedly bids her husband
forthwith, and even Lakshmana, saying, 'lay hold of it.' [3-36-19]_END

B_3_C_31_42
BEGIN_
कर्मणा अनेन केन असि कापथम् प्रतिपादितः |सुख सुप्तस्य ते राजन् प्रहृतम् केन मूर्धनि || ३-३१-४५_END
BEGIN_
"By whom and by which purpose of his you are made to blunder upon this awry path, oh, king, it is as 
good as his hitting hard on your head while you are fast asleep. [3-31-45]_END

B_3_C_35_20
BEGIN_
तत्र अपश्यत् स मेघ आभम् न्यग्रोधम् मुनिभिर् वृतम् || ३-३५-२७समंतात् यस्य ताः शाखाः शत योजनम् आयताः 
|_END
BEGIN_
There Ravana also saw a banyan tree which in sheen is like a black-cloud, and the branches of which 
are stretching all over for a hundred yojana-s in length, and on which sages made their abode for practising 
ascesis. [3-35-27b, 28a]_END

B_3_C_37_6
BEGIN_
त्वत् विधः काम वृत्तो हि दुःशीलः पाप मंत्रितः |
आत्मानम् स्व जनम् राष्ट्रम् स राजा हन्ति दुर्मतिः || ३-३७-७_END
BEGIN_
"Any king of your like who is with a self-will, ill-will, ensorcelled by evil, and
malicious in intent, that king alone ruins his own city-state, his own people, even himself, as a
matter of actual fact. [3-37-7]_END

B_3_C_38_0
BEGIN_
कदाचित् अपि अहम् वीर्यात् पर्यटन् पृथिवीम् इमाम् |
बलम् नाग सहस्रस्य धारयन् पर्वतोपमः || ३-३८-१
नील जीमूत संकाशः तप्त कांचन कुण्डलः |
भयम् लोकस्य जनयन् किरीटी परिघ आयुधः || ३-३८-२
व्यचरम् दण्डक अरण्यम् ऋषि मांसानि भक्षयन् |_END
BEGIN_
"At one time even I was on the rove around this earth, taking pride in my valour,
bearing the strength of a thousand elephants, mountainous in my size and black-cloudlike in my
sheen, wearing ear-knobs and a crown made out of refined gold, with a bludgeon as my weapon, and
such as I was, I rambled Dandaka forest causing terror to the world, and eating the fleshes of
sages." Thus Maareecha started to narrate his experience with Rama. [3-38-1, 2]_END

B_3_C_31_43
BEGIN_
विशुद्ध वंश अभिजना अग्र हस्तःतेजो मदः संस्थित दोर् विषाणः |उदीक्षितुम् रावण न इह युक्तः
स संयुगे राघव गन्धि हस्ती || ३-३१-४६_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Ravana, it will be unbefitting to raise an eye to see Rama in war, who will be then like a majestic 
elephant that has an impeccable dynasty and bloodline as its mammoth trunk, personal radiance as its 
indomitable might, very firm pair of arms as its pernicious tusks, more so, who will be with the redolence 
of the irrepressible lineage of Raghava-s. [3-31-46]_END

B_3_C_36_15
BEGIN_
ततः तयोः अपाये तु शून्ये सीताम् यथा सुखम् |
निराबाधो हरिष्यामि राहुः चन्द्र प्रभाम् इव || | ३-३६-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Then on the diversion of those two, Rama and Lakshmana, I will comfortably and
unimpededly abduct Seetha in that lonely place, as planet Rahu abducts the shine of moon.
[3-36-20]_END

B_3_C_35_21
BEGIN_
यस्य हस्तिनम् आदाय महा कायम् च कच्छपम् || ३-३५-२८भक्षार्थम् गरुडः शाखाम् आजगाम महाबलः |_END
BEGIN_
This is the tree on the branch of which once highly mighty Divine Eagle Garuda swooped to perch, clawing 
an elephant and a mammoth tortoise, for the purpose of dining them out on that tree-branch. [3-35-28b, 
29a]_END

B_3_C_37_7
BEGIN_
न च पित्रा परित्यक्तो न अमर्यादः कथंचन |
न लुब्धो न च दुःशीलो न च क्षत्रिय पांसनः || ३-३७-८
न च धर्म गुणैर् हीनैः कौसल्या आनंद वर्धनः |
न च तीक्ष्णो हि भूतानाम् सर्व भूत हिते रतः || ३-३७-९_END
BEGIN_
"Rama the enhancer of his mother Kausalya's happiness is completely forsaken by his
father - no, he is not; there is unseemliness in him - no, not in the least; he is out of character
- no; he is selfish - no; he is an ignoble Kshatriya - no, not at all; and he is neither a debased
one insofar as the merits of righteousness are concerned, nor he is atrocious towards living
beings, for he takes delight in the welfare of all beings. [3-37-8, 9]_END

B_3_C_38_1
BEGIN_
विश्वामित्रो अथ धर्मात्मा मत् वित्रस्तो महामुनिः || ३-३८-३
स्वयम् गत्वा दशरथम् नरेन्द्रम् इदम् अब्रवीत् |_END
BEGIN_
"The virtue-souled great-saint Vishvamitra who was highly scared of me, then on
going to Dasharatha in person that great-saint spoke this to that lord of people. [3-38-3b, 4a]_END

B_3_C_31_44
BEGIN_
असौ रण अन्तः स्थिति संधि वालःविदग्ध रक्षो मृग हा नृसिंहः |सुप्तः त्वया बोधयितुम् न शक्यः
शारांग पूणो निशित असि दम्ष्ट्रः || ३-३१-४७_END
BEGIN_
"To be in the midst of war itself is the fury of that lion called Rama, by which that lion raises its 
tail touching the back of its trunk, that lion is all-inclusive with forelegs, paws, and claws that 
are included in arrows, while its fangs are swords, and it is the killer of the deer called the expert 
killer-demons, and mind you, do not dare to rouse that sleeping man-lion. [3-31-47]_END

B_3_C_36_16
BEGIN_
ततः पश्चात् सुखम् रामे भार्या आहरण कर्शिते |
विस्रब्धम् प्रहरिष्यामि कृत अर्थेन अन्तर् आत्मना || ३-३६-२१_END
BEGIN_
"Thereafter Rama will be enervated by the abduction of his wife, and then surely and
conveniently I wish to retaliate him if he is going to come up against me, for my inner-soul will
be firstly gratified with its volition, namely possessing Seetha." Thus Ravana requested Maareecha.
[3-36-21]_END

B_3_C_35_22
BEGIN_
तस्य ताम् सहसा शाखाम् भारेण पतगोत्तमः || ३-३५-२९सुपर्णः पर्ण बहुलाम् बभंज अथ महाबलः |_END
BEGIN_
While descending rapidly then that best bird among birds Garuda suddenly broke that tree's branch which 
is full with leaves, owing to the impact of his high impetuosity. [3-35-29b, 30a]_END

B_3_C_37_8
BEGIN_
वंचितम् पितरम् दृष्ट्वा कैकेय्या सत्य वादिनम् |
करिष्यामि इति धर्मात्मा ततः प्रव्रजितो वनम् || ३-३७-१०_END
BEGIN_
"On seeing his father who is a proponent of truth, and whom Kaikeyi has outwitted,
that virtue-souled Rama neatly decamped from Ayodhya saying that 'I will prove my father to be a
real proponent of truth.' [3-37-10]_END

B_3_C_38_2
BEGIN_
अयम् रक्षतु माम् रामः पर्व काले समाहितः || ३-३८-४
मारीचात् मे भयम् घोरम् समुत्पन्नम् नरेश्वर |_END
BEGIN_
" 'An awesome dismay has befallen owing to this Maareecha, oh, lord of people
Dasharatha, let Rama safeguard me becoming alert at the opportune time of the Vedic-ritual.
[3-38-4b 5a]_END

B_3_C_31_45
BEGIN_
चापापहारे भुज वेग पंकेशर ऊर्मिमाले सु महा आहव ओघे |न राम पाताल मुखे अति घोरेप्रस्कन्दितुम् 
राक्षस राज युक्तम् || ३-३१-४८_END


B_3_C_36_17
BEGIN_
तस्य राम कथाम् श्रुत्वा मारीचस्य महात्मनः |
शुष्कम् समभवत् वक्त्रम् परित्रस्तो बभूव च || ३-३६-२२_END
BEGIN_
On listening the very word of Rama that honest-souled Maareecha's mouth is
completely dried up, and he is fully frightened. [3-36-22]_END

B_3_C_35_23
BEGIN_
तत्र वैखानसा माषा वालखिल्या मरीचिपाः || ३-३५-३०अजा बभूवुः धूम्राः च संगताः परमर्षयः |_END
BEGIN_
Adhering to that tree-branch there are eminent sages like, Vaikhanasa-s, Maasha-s, Vaalakhilya-s, Mariicipa-s, 
Aja-s, and even sages like Dhuumraa-s that thrive on fumes and smokes are there, and there they are 
collectively practising asceticism upside down while clasping branches with their legs. [3-35-30b, 31a]_END

B_3_C_37_9
BEGIN_
कैकेय्याः प्रिय कामार्थम् पितुर् दशरथस्य च |
हित्वा राज्यम् च भोगान् च प्रविष्टो दण्डका वनम् || ३-३७-११_END
BEGIN_
"Discarding the kingdom and even royal-comforts Rama entered Dandaka forest only to
fulfil the cherish of Kaikeyi, viz., kingdom for her son Bharata, and even that of Dasharatha,
viz., to remain loyal to his promise to Kaikeyi. [3-37-11]_END

B_3_C_38_3
BEGIN_
इति एवम् उक्तो धर्मात्मा राजा दशरथः तदा || ३-३८-५
प्रत्युवाच महाभागम् विश्वामित्रम् महामुनिम् |_END
BEGIN_
"When he is spoken in that way, then that virtue-souled king Dasharatha replied that
great-fortunate and great-saint Vishvamitra in this way. [3-38-5b, 6a]_END

B_3_C_31_46

BEGIN_
"His bow is crocodilian, his shoulder-speed is quagmire, his arrows are tidal, and the great immensity 
of his war itself is a tideland, and oh, king of demons, it is inapt of you to slide down into the much-ghoulish 
mouth of that abyssal ocean, called Rama. [3-31-48]_END

B_3_C_36_18
BEGIN_
ओष्टौ परिलिहन् शुष्कौ नेत्रैः अनिमिषैः इव |
मृत भूत इव आर्तः तु रावणम् समुत् ईक्षतः || ३-३६-२३_END
BEGIN_
Wetting dried up lips with his tongue he has become goggle-eyed almost like an
about-to-die animal, and he agonisingly looked up at Ravana with winkless eyes. [3-36-23]_END

B_3_C_35_24
BEGIN_
तेषाम् दयाअर्थम् गरुडः ताम् शाखाम् शत योजनाम् || ३-३५-३१भग्नम् आदाय वेगेन तौ च उभौ गज कच्छपौ |_END
BEGIN_
For the sake of the grace of those sages Garuda took flight from that tree, grasping that broken tree-branch 
of a hundred yojana length along with those pendulous sages with his beak, and both of the elephant 
and tortoise with both of his claws. [3-35-31b, 32a]_END

B_3_C_37_10
BEGIN_
न रामः कर्कशः तात न अविद्वान् न अजित इन्द्रियः |
अनृतम् न श्रुतम् चैव नैव त्वम् वक्तुम् अर्हसि || ३-३७-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Rama is ruthless - no; an unscholarly one - no; unconquered are his senses - no;
and oh, boy, it is unapt of you to speak of impalpable and unheard-of topics in this way.
[3-37-12]_END

B_3_C_38_4
BEGIN_
ऊन द्वादश वर्षो अयम् अकृत अस्त्रः च राघवः || ३-३८-६
कामम् तु मम यत् सैन्यम् मया सह गमिष्यति |_END
BEGIN_
" 'This boy Rama is less than twelve years in his age, unproficient in the use of
weapons, and if need be, whatever army of mine is there it will march on along with me instead of
Rama. [3-38-6b, 7a]_END

B_3_C_31_47
BEGIN_
प्रसीद लंकेश्वर राक्षसेन्द्रलंकाम् प्रसन्नो भव साधु गच्छ |त्वम् स्वेषु दारेषु रमस्व नित्यम्
रामः स भार्यो रमताम् वनेषु || ३-३१-४९_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, lord of Lanka, be appeased towards Rama, be quietened and gently proceed to Lanka. You take delight 
in your wives, and let Rama be delighting with wife in forests." Thus Mareecha spoke to Ravana. [3-31-49]_END

B_3_C_36_19
BEGIN_
स रावणम् त्रस्त विषण्ण चेता
महावने राम पराक्रमज्ञः |
कृत अंजलिः तत्त्वम् उवाच वाक्यम्
हितम् च तस्मै हितम् आत्मनः च || ३-३६-२४_END
BEGIN_
Maareecha's heart sank with scare as he is aware of Rama's valour when he was in the
great forest of Tataka, thus suppliantly making palm-fold he started telling about factuality of
Rama to Ravana, which is beneficial both to Ravana and to himself, as well, if only Ravana is
heedful of it. [3-36-24]_END

B_3_C_35_25
BEGIN_
एक पादेन धर्म आत्मा भक्षयित्वा तत् आमिषम् || ३-३५-३२निषाद विषयम् हत्वा शाखया पतगोत्तमः |प्रहर्षम् 
अतुलम् लेभे मोक्षयित्वा महामुनीन् || ३-३५-३३_END
BEGIN_
That virtue-souled Garuda consumed the meat of his prays, namely the elephant and the giant tortoise 
with a single foot, and destroyed the province of tribesmen with the same broken tree branch, and thus 
that supreme bird Garuda gained an incomparable happiness in rescuing those great-sages. [3-35-32b, 
33]_END

B_3_C_37_11
BEGIN_
रामो विग्रहवान् धर्मः साधुः सत्य पराक्रमः |
राजा सर्वस्य लोकस्य देवानाम् इव वासवः || ३-३७-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Rama is the embodiment of righteousness, he is an equable person with truthfulness
as his valour, and as with Indra to all gods he is the king of entire world. [3-37-13]_END

B_3_C_38_5
BEGIN_
बलेन चतुरंगेण स्वयम् एत्य निशाचरम् || ३-३८-७
वधिष्यामि मुनिश्रेष्ठ शत्रुम् तव यथा ईप्सितम् |_END
BEGIN_
" 'And having come in person with fourfold forces, oh eminent sage, I myself will
eradicate that nightwalker whomever you indicate as an enemy of yours." So said Dasharatga to
Vishvamitra. [3-38-7b, 8a]_END

B_3_C_31_48
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तो दशग्रीवो मारीचेन स रावणः |न्यवर्तत पुरीम् लंकाम् विवेश च गृह उत्तमम् || ३-३१-५०_END
BEGIN_
When thus said by Maareecha that ten faced Ravana returned to his city Lanka and entered his best house 
and home. [3-31-50]_END

B_3_C_35_26
BEGIN_
स तेन तु प्रहर्षेण द्विगुणी कृत विक्रमः |अमृत आनयनार्थम् वै चकार मतिमान् मतिम् || ३-३५-३४_END
BEGIN_
When his valour has become twice as much with that happiness that heedful Garuda indeed resolved to 
bring ambrosia from heaven. [3-35-34]_END

B_3_C_37_12
BEGIN_
कथम् नु तस्य वैदेहीम् रक्षिताम् स्वेन तेजसा |
इच्छसे प्रसभम् हर्तुम् प्रभाम् इव विवस्वतः || ३-३७-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Rama's proper resplendence is protecting Vaidehi. How then you really wish to
forcibly rob her off from Rama, as though wishing to rob the Sun of his resplendence. [3-37-14]_END

B_3_C_38_6
BEGIN_
] एवम् उक्तः स तु मुनी राजानम् इदम् अब्रवीत् || ३-३८-८
रामात् न अन्यत् बलम् लोके पर्याप्तम् तस्य रक्षसः |_END
BEGIN_
"When the sage Vishvamitra is spoken thus, then he said to the king, 'No other force
in the world than Rama can counterbalance that demon. [3-38-8b, 9a]_END

B_3_C_35_27
BEGIN_
अयो जालानि निर्मथ्य भित्त्वा रत्न गृहम् वरम् |महेन्द्र भवनात् गुप्तम् आजहार अमृतम् ततः || ३-३५-३५_END
BEGIN_
Smashing the guard of iron-grid completely and crashing the unbreakable diamond -like strongroom in 
which the ambrosia is safeguarded, then Garuda carried off ambrosia from the palace of Indra. [3-35-35]_END

B_3_C_37_13
BEGIN_
शर अर्चिषम् अनाधृष्यम् चाप खड्ग इन्धनम् रणे |
राम अग्निम् सहसा दीप्तम् न प्रवेष्टुम् त्वम् अर्हसि || ३-३७-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Arrows as it jets of fire, bow and sword as it firewood that fire called Rama will
be blazing in war, and it will be inapt of you to enter into such an uninfringeable fire,
recklessly. [3-37-15]_END

B_3_C_38_7
BEGIN_
देवतानाम् अपि भवान् समरेषु अभिपालकः || ३-३८-९
आसीत् तव कृते कर्म त्रिलोक विदितम् नृप |_END
BEGIN_
" 'No doubt, you are a defender of gods in wars, and oh, king, the exploits you have
undertaken on behalf of gods are well-known in the triad of worlds. [3-38-9b, 10a]_END

B_3_C_35_28
BEGIN_
तम् महर्षि गणैः जुष्टम् सुपर्ण कृत लक्षणम् |नाम्ना सुभद्रम् न्यग्रोधम् ददर्श धनद अनुजः || ३-३५-३६_END
BEGIN_
Ravana on his way saw such a banyan tree named as Subhadra which is a much sought after tree for assemblages 
of great sages, and which betokens the deeds of that best-winged Garuda. [3-35-36]_END

B_3_C_37_14
BEGIN_
धनुर् व्यादित दीप्त आस्यम् शर अर्चिषम् अमर्षणम् |
चाप बाण धरम् तीक्ष्णम् शत्रु सेना अपहारिणम् || ३-३७-१६
राज्यम् सुखम् च संत्यज्य जीवितम् च इष्टम् आत्मनः |
न अति आसादयितुम् तात राम अंतकम् इह अर्हसि || ३-३७-१७_END
BEGIN_
"With the bow stretched to his ear becoming a gaping mouth spouting flames, arrows
becoming tongues of fire spewed forth from that flaming mouth, he that Rama the reified Terminator
will become fierce and insufferable when he wields bow and arrows, and oh, dear boy Ravana, it will
be inapt of you to at once draw pretty nigh of such an annihilator of the armies of enemies, on
discarding your kingdom, comforts and even the dear life of yours. [3-37-16, 17]_END

B_3_C_39_0
BEGIN_
एवम् अस्मि तदा मुक्तः कथंचित् तेन संयुगे |
इदानीम् अपि यत् वृत्तम् तत् शृउणुष्व यत् उत्तरम् || ४-३९-१_END
BEGIN_
"Thus I was somehow released by him in a confrontation then in his teens. Now you
may also listen to what has happened later in his adulthood." Thus Maareecha continued his advise
to Ravana. [4-39-1]_END

B_3_C_38_8
BEGIN_
कामम् अस्ति महत् सैन्यम् तिष्टतु इह परंतप || ३-३८-१०
बालो अपि एष महातेजाः समर्थः तस्य निग्रहे |
गमिष्ये रामम् आदाय स्वस्ति ते अस्तु परंतपः || ३-३८-११_END
BEGIN_
" 'Maybe your army is a remarkable one, oh, enemy-inflamer, let it sit tight here
alone, and even if this great resplendent one is still a boy he alone is competent to forestall
that Maareecha, hence oh, enemy-subjugator, let good betide you, I wish to take him alone along
with me.' [3-38-10b, 11]_END

B_3_C_35_29
BEGIN_
तम् तु गत्वा परम् पारम् समुद्रस्य नदी पतेः |ददर्श आश्रमम् एकांते पुण्ये रम्ये वनांतरे || ३-३५-३७_END
BEGIN_
On going to the other side of the lord of rivers, namely ocean, Ravana saw a pleasing hermitage in the 
sacred and scenic interior of the forest. [3-35-37]_END

B_3_C_37_15
BEGIN_
अप्रमेयम् हि तत् तेजो यस्य सा जनकात्मजा |
न त्वम् समर्थः ताम् हर्तुम् राम चाप आश्रयाम् वने || ३-३७-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Which Rama's wife is Janaka's daughter that Rama is indeed with an inestimable
resplendence, and it will be incapable of you to steal Seetha while such a Rama's bow safeguards
her in the forest, besides the firewall called his resplendence. [3-37-18]_END

B_3_C_39_1
BEGIN_
राक्षाभ्याम् अहम् द्वाभ्याम् अनिर्विण्णः तथा कृतः |
सहितो मृग रूपाभ्याम् प्रविष्टो दँडका वने || ४-३९-२_END
BEGIN_
"Though Rama hit me previously in such a way, I unabashedly entered Dandaka forest
together with two more demons who were in the guise of animals. [4-39-2]_END

B_3_C_38_9
BEGIN_
इति एवम् उक्त्वा स मुनिः तम् आदाय नृपात्मजम् |
जगाम परम प्रीतो विश्वामित्रः स्वम् आश्रमम् || ३-३८-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Thus that way on saying he that sage Vishvamitra returned to his own hermitage
highly gladdening to take the prince Rama along with him. [3-38-12]_END

B_3_C_35_30
BEGIN_
तत्र कृष्ण अजिन धरम् जटा वल्कल धारिणम् |ददर्श नियत आहारम् मारीचम् नाम राक्षसम् || ३-३५-३८_END
BEGIN_
At that place Ravana saw the demon named Maareecha, wearing jute-clothes and black deerskin and tufts 
of hairs, and the one with regulated diet. [3-35-38]_END

B_3_C_39_2
BEGIN_
दीप्त जिह्वो महादंष्ट्रः तीक्ष्ण शृंगो महाबलः |
व्यचरन् दँडाकारण्यम् मांस भक्षो महामृगः || ४-३९-३_END
BEGIN_
"On becoming a gigantic carnivorous animal with a torching tongue, incisive teeth
and excruciating horns, and with an extraordinary energy, I was on the rove in Dandaka forest while
getting at Rama. [4-39-3]_END

B_3_C_37_16
BEGIN_
तस्य वै नर सिंहस्य सिंह उरस्कस्य भामिनी |
प्राणेभ्यो अपि प्रियतरा भार्या नित्यम् अनुव्रता || ३-३७-१९_END
BEGIN_
"That lady Seetha is his wife, dearest than the lives of that lion-chested lion-man
Rama, and in truth, she is avowed to follow him alone, in perpetuity. [3-37-19]_END

B_3_C_38_10
BEGIN_
तम् तदा दण्डकारण्ये यज्ञम् उद्दिश्य दीक्षितम् |
बभूव उपस्थितो रामः चित्रम् विस्फारयन् धनुः || ३-३८-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Then in Dandaka forest Rama twingeing his amazing bow stayed nearby the sage
Vishvamitra who entered the vow of Vedic-ritual. [3-38-13]_END

B_3_C_35_31
BEGIN_
स रावणः समागम्य विधिवत् तेन रक्षसा |मारीचेन अर्चितो राजा सर्व कामैः अमानुषैः || ३-३५-३९_END
BEGIN_
That demon Maareecha welcomed the king Ravana and customarily entertained him catering all the offerings 
that are beyond the scope of humans. [3-35-39]_END

B_3_C_39_3
BEGIN_
अग्निहोत्रेषु तीर्थेषु चैत्य वृक्षेषु रावण |
अत्यन्त घोरो व्यचरन् तापसान् संप्रधर्षयन् || ४-३९-४_END
BEGIN_
"I moved about Dandaka forest, oh, Ravana, in an extremely horrible aspect of
animal, utterly brutalising the sages at ritual-altars, holy bathing places and under the trees of
religious sanctuaries while reaching Rama. [4-39-4]_END

B_3_C_37_17
BEGIN_
न सा धर्षयितुम् शक्या मैथिली ओजस्विनः प्रिया |
दीप्तस्य इव हुत आशस्य शिखा सीता सुमध्यमा || ३-३७-२०_END
BEGIN_
"As the spire of blazing ritual fire cannot be abused, so also, she that curvaceous
Maithili, the cherished wife of that dynamic Rama, is an impossibility for any abuse. [3-37-20]_END

B_3_C_38_11
BEGIN_
अजात व्यंजनः श्रीमान् बालः श्यामः शुभेक्षणः |
एक वस्त्र धरो धन्वी शिखी कनक मालया || ३-३८-१४
शोभयन् दण्डकारण्यम् दीप्तेन स्वेन तेजसा |
अदृश्यत तदा रामो बाल चन्द्र इव उदितः || ३-३८-१५_END
BEGIN_
"At that time, yet unborn are the identities of adulthood like moustache on his
face, and that providential one was magnificent in looks with a peacock-blue complexion, wearing a
single cloth, locks of hair, and golden locket, and wielding a bow, and he was irradiating the
Dandaka forest with a radiating radiance of his own, and then he appeared like the just risen
baby-moon. [3-38-14, 15]_END

B_3_C_35_32
BEGIN_
तम् स्वयम् पूजयित्वा च भोजनेन उदकेन च |अर्थोपहितया वाचा मारीचो वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् || ३-३५-४०_END
BEGIN_
On personally offering meals and drinking water, and venerating him properly Maareecha spoke this sentence 
to Ravana which is connotative of significance. [3-35-40]_END

B_3_C_39_4
BEGIN_
निहत्य दँडकारण्ये तापसान् धर्मचरिणः |
रुधिराणि पिबन्तः तेषाम् तन् मांसानि च भक्षयन् || ४-३९-५_END
BEGIN_
"I have proceeded to Rama killing saints in Dandaka forest who are the treaders in
saintliness, and drinking off their blood and feasting on their flesh. [4-39-5]_END

B_3_C_37_18
BEGIN_
किम् उद्यमम् व्यर्थम् इमम् कृत्वा ते राक्षसाधिप |
दृष्टः चेत् त्वम् रणे तेन तत् अंतम् तव जीवितम् || ३-३७-२१_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, king of demons, What is the result in making such a futile effort? If that Rama
glances at you in a given war that alone ends your life. [3-37-21]_END

B_3_C_38_12
BEGIN_
ततो अहम् मेघ संकाशः तप्त कांचन कुण्डलः |
बली दत्त वरो दर्पात् आजगाम आश्रम अंतरम् || ३-३८-१६_END
BEGIN_
"And I who was like a massive black-cloud, wearing golden ear-knobs, already a
forceful one further reinforced with the boon of Brahma, I pridefully entered into the interior of
Vishwamitra's hermitage. [3-38-16]_END

B_3_C_35_33
BEGIN_
कच्चित् ते कुशलम् राजन् लंकायाम् राक्षसेश्वर |केन अर्थेन् पुनः त्वम् वै तूर्णम् एव इह आगतः || ३-३५-४१_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, king of the demons, is everything well with your Lanka? Oh, king, for what reason you have put 
in an appearance again, that too in a trice? [3-35-41]_END

B_3_C_39_5
BEGIN_
ऋषि माअंस अशनः क्रूरः त्रासयन् वनगोचरान् |
तदा रुधिर मत्तो अहम् व्यचरन् दँडका वनम् || ४-३९-६_END
BEGIN_
"On becoming such a brutal animal I have been eating the flesh of sages, frightening
the forest dwellers, and in that way I rambled in Dandaka forest besotted with blood-drinking while
reaching Rama. [4-39-6]_END

B_3_C_37_19
BEGIN_
जीवितम् च सुखम् चैव राज्यम् चैव सुदुर्लभम् |
यत् इच्छसि चिरम् भोक्तुम् मा कृथा राम विप्रियम् || ३-३७-२२_END
BEGIN_
"If you cherish to take pleasure for a long time in your life, in your comforts and
also thus in your kingdom, which kingdom is highly impossible to achieve, do not do anything
unpleasant to Rama. [3-37-22]_END

B_3_C_38_13
BEGIN_
तेन दृष्टः प्रविष्टो अहम् सहसा एव उद्यत आयुधः |
माम् तु दृष्ट्वा धनुः सज्यम् असम्भ्रान्तः चकार ह || ३-३८-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Rama quickly noticed me on my very entry with an uplifted weapon, and on seeing me
he unexcitedly strung bowstring to his bow. [3-38-17]_END

B_3_C_35_34
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तो महातेजा मारीचेन स रावण |ततः पश्चात् इदम् वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् वाक्य कोविदः || ३-३५-४२_END
BEGIN_
When Maareecha spoke to him thus, that highly radiant and eloquent Ravana then afterwards spoke this 
sentence to Maareecha. [3-35-42]_END

B_3_C_39_6
BEGIN_
तदा अहम् दँडकारण्ये विचरन् धर्म दूषकः |
आसादयम् तदा रामम् तापसम् धर्मम् आश्रितम् || ४-३९-७
वैदेहि च महाभागाम् लक्ष्मणम् च महरथम् |_END
BEGIN_
"While I was wandering in Dandaka forest as an abuser of virtue, then I reached Rama
who by then has assumed the rectitude befitting to a saint, and I even reached the great-fortunate
Vaidehi and top-speeded-chariot-rider Lakshmana. [4-39-7, 8a]_END

B_3_C_37_20
BEGIN_
स सर्वैः सचिवैः सार्धम् विभीषण पुरस्कृतैः |
मंत्रयित्वा तु धर्मिष्ठैः कृत्वा निश्चयम् आत्मनः |
दोषाणाम् च गुणानाम् च संप्रधार्य बल अबलम् || ३-३७-२३
आत्मनः च बलम् ज्ञात्वा राघवस्य च तत्त्वतः |
हितम् हि तव निश्चित्य क्षमम् त्वम् कर्तुम् अर्हसि || ३-३७-२४_END
BEGIN_
"Such as you are, you should firstly deliberate with all of your ministers that have
a righteous bearing, duly keeping your brother Vibheeshana at the helm of affairs, and then you
take a decision on your own considering rights and wrongs of the case, and bearing in mind about
your own strengths and weakness, and even on making sure of Raghava's capability in its reality,
and then it will be apt of you to take up befitting action that will be conducive to your
interests. [3-37-24,25]_END

B_3_C_38_14
BEGIN_
अवजानन् अहम् मोहात् बालो अयम् इति राघवम् |
विश्वामित्रस्य ताम् वेदिम् अभ्यधावम् कृत त्वरः || ३-३८-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Unmindfully trivialising him as, 'this Raghava is just a boy,' I made haste and ran
towards that Fire-altar of Vishvamitra. [3-38-18]_END

B_3_C_39_7
BEGIN_
तापसम् नियत आहारम् सर्व बूत हिते रतम् || ४-३९-८
सः अहम् वन गतम् रामम् परिभूय महाबलम् |
तापसो अयम् इति ज्ञात्वा पूर्व वैरम् अनुस्मरन् || ४-३९-९
अभ्यधावम् सुसंक्रुद्धः तीक्ष्ण शृंगो मृग आकृतिः |
जिघांसुः अकृतप्रज्ञः तम् प्रहारम् अनुस्मरन् || ४-३९-१०_END
BEGIN_
"I was in the shape of an animal with incisive horns. Such as I was I recollected my
earlier grudge against that great mighty Rama who takes delight in the welfare of all being, who by
then was santlike on a regulated diet and abiding in the forest, whereby I presumed him to be mere
hermit. In that way, I was very extremely infuriated to recollect his earlier assault on me, and I
indiscriminately dashed towards him, only to kill him, completely disregarding his other faculties.
[4-39-8b, 9, 10]_END

B_3_C_37_21
BEGIN_
अहम् तु मन्ये तव न क्षमम् रणे
समागमम् कोसल राज सूनुना |
इदम् हि भूयः शृणु वाक्यम् उत्तमम्
क्षमम् च युक्तम् च निशाचर अधिप || ३-३७-२५_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, king of nightwalkers Ravana, I for myself deem that your confrontation with
Rama, the prince of Kosala, in a war is improper, and a better, befitting, and a reasonable one is
this advise of mine, to which you may listen further. [3-37-25]_END

B_3_C_38_15
BEGIN_
तेन मुक्तः ततो बाणः शितः शत्रु निबर्हणः |
तेन अहम् ताडितः क्षिप्तः समुद्रे शत योजने || ३-३८-१९_END
BEGIN_
"He then released an acute arrow that eliminates the enemy, and hit by it I am
plunged into the ocean which was a hundred yojana-s off. [3-38-19]_END

B_3_C_39_8
BEGIN_
तेन त्यक्ताः त्रयो बाणाः शिताः शत्रु निबर्हणाः |
विकृष्य सुमहत् चापम् सुपर्ण अनिल तुल्य गाः || ४-३९-११_END
BEGIN_
"Stringing out his highly magnificent bow Rama then released three excruciating and
enemy eliminating arrows which in their egress match the Air-god and the Divine-Eagle Garuda.
[4-39-11]_END

B_3_C_40_0
BEGIN_
मारीचस्य तु तत् वाक्यम् क्षमम् युक्तम् च रावणः |
उक्तो न प्रतिजग्राह मर्तु काम इव औषधम् || ३-४०-१_END
BEGIN_
When Maareecha spoke those acceptable and equitable words, Ravana rejected them like
a person with a death wish rejects medicament. [3-40-1]_END

B_3_C_38_16
BEGIN_
न इच्छता तात माम् हन्तुम् तदा वीरेण रक्षितः |
रामस्य शर वेगेन निरस्तो भ्रान्त चेतनः || ३-३८-२०_END
BEGIN_
"That Rama did not wish to kill me then, and I am thus saved by that valiant one,
oh, dear boy Ravana, but the thrust of Rama's arrow bewildered my animation and I was on my last
legs. [3-38-20]_END

B_3_C_39_9
BEGIN_
ते बाणा वज्र संकाशाः सुघोरा रक्त भोजनाः |
आजग्मुः सहिताः सर्वे त्रयः संनतपर्वणः || ४-३९-१२_END
BEGIN_
"All those three thunderbolt like arrows that have only blood for their board,
acutely bent at barbs, and that are highly horrendous have come at us in a coordinated manner.
[4-39-12]_END

B_3_C_40_1
BEGIN_
तम् पथ्य हित वक्तारम् मारीचम् राक्षसाधिपः |
अब्रवीत् परुषम् वाक्यम् अयुक्तम् काल चोदितः || ३-४०-२_END
BEGIN_
Ushered by the Terminator the king of demons Ravana, uncouthly spoke these
unbefitting words to Maareecha who had been speaking conducive and beneficial words of advise.
[3-40-2]_END

B_3_C_38_17
BEGIN_
पातितो अहम् तदा तेन गंभीरे सागर अंभसि |
प्राप्य संज्ञाम् चिरात् तात लंकाम् प्रति गतः पुरीम् || ३-३८-२१_END
BEGIN_
"That way I who had been flung into the abyssal water of the ocean by him gained
consciousness after a long time and proceeded towards the city of Lanka. [3-38-21]_END

B_3_C_39_10
BEGIN_
पराक्रमज्ञो रामस्य शठो दृष्ट भयः पुरा |
समुत्क्रांतः ततः मुक्तः तौ उभौ राक्षसौ हतौ || ४-३९-१३_END
BEGIN_
"As I have earlier seen the fear caused by his arrow I am in the know of Rama's
valour, hence I retreated from there trickily and gingerly, but the other two demons were killed.
[4-39-13]_END

B_3_C_40_2
BEGIN_
यत् किल एतत् अयुक्तार्थम् मारीच मयि कथ्यते |
वाक्यम् निष्फलम् अत्यर्थम् बीजम् उप्तम् इव ऊषरे || ३-४०-३_END
BEGIN_
"All these meaningless words that are being said to me are decidedly worthless, in
effect, like the seeds seeded in wastelands. [3-40-3]_END

B_3_C_38_18
BEGIN_
एवम् अस्मि तदा मुक्तः सहायाः ते - शायास्तु - निपातिताः |
अकृत अस्त्रेण रामेण बालेन अक्लिष्ट कर्मणा || ३-३८-२२_END
BEGIN_
"At that time, that one with elementary knowledge in the use of weaponry, but who
can undertake deeds in an effortless manner, such a boy, such a Rama spared me, albeit killing them
that were my helpmates in that escapade. [3-38-22]_END

B_3_C_39_11
BEGIN_
शरेण मुक्तो रामस्य कथंचित् प्राप्यजीवितम् |
इह प्रव्राजितो युक्तः तापसो अहम् समाहितः || ४-३९-१४_END
BEGIN_
"When I was somehow exempted by the arrow of Rama I regained lifespan, and when that
arrow made me to renounce everything like a monk and fled me to this place, the other side of ocean
to where you came by your aircraft, here I am living here in a yogic way, self-collectedly like an
ascetic. [4-39-14]_END

B_3_C_40_3
BEGIN_
त्वत् वाक्यैः न तु माम् शक्यम् - भेतुम् - भेत्तुम् रामस्य संयुगे |
पाप शीलस्य मूर्खस्य मानुषस्य विशेषतः || ३-४०-४_END
BEGIN_
"But it is impossible to scare me away from a war with that iniquitous and imprudent
Rama, that too, from a human being, with these words of yours. [3-40-4]_END

B_3_C_38_19
BEGIN_
तत् मया वार्यमाणः त्वम् यदि रामेण विग्रहम् |
करिष्यसि आपदम् घोराम् क्षिप्रम् प्राप्य न शिष्यसि || ३-३८-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Thereby, if you wish to make for any confrontation with Rama, despite of my
proscribing you, you will ruin yourself on getting a disastrous calamity. [3-38-23]_END

B_3_C_39_12
BEGIN_
वृक्षे वृक्षे हि पश्यामि चीर कृष्ण अजिन अंबरम् |
गृहीत धनुषम् रामम् पाश हस्तम् इव अंतकम् || ४-३९-१५_END
BEGIN_
"From then on wards, I am indeed descrying Rama at this tree and at that tree,
dressed in jute-cloths and black deerskin, and handling his bow like the Terminator handling a
tether. [4-39-15]_END

B_3_C_40_4
BEGIN_
यः त्यक्त्वा सुहृदो राज्यम् मातरम् पितरम् तथा |
स्त्री वाक्यम् प्राकृतम् श्रुत्वा वनम् एक पदे गतः || ३-४०-५_END
BEGIN_
"He who bolted off to forest in a single-foot on hearing the artless words of a
woman, forfeiting his kingdom, friends and relatives, and even his mother, likewise his father too,
you cannot scare me away from such a Rama. [3-40-5]_END

B_3_C_38_20
BEGIN_
क्रीडा रति विधिज्ञानाम् समाज उत्सव शालिनाम् |
रक्षसाम् चैव संतापम् अनर्थम् च आहरिष्यसि || ३-३८-२४_END
BEGIN_
"The demons are methodical in sporting and flirting, thus by their own conduct they
are also socialising and frolicking, and to them you derive distress and disaster. [3-38-24]_END

B_3_C_39_13
BEGIN_
अपि राम सहस्राणि भीतः पश्यामि रावण |
राम भूतम् इदम् सर्वम् अरण्यम् प्रतिभाति मे || ४-३९-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Given to fright I even visualise thousands Rama-s, and whole this forest is
reflecting to me as one entity of Rama. [4-39-16]_END

B_3_C_40_5
BEGIN_
अवश्यम् तु मया तस्य संयुगे खर घातिनः |
प्राणैः प्रियतरा सीता हर्तव्या तव संनिधौ || ३-४०-६_END
BEGIN_
"But his wife Seetha who is dearer to him more than his lives is certainly seizable
by me in association with you, as that Rama had purposelessly killed Khara in a war. [3-40-6]_END

B_3_C_38_21
BEGIN_
हर्म्य प्रासाद संबाधाम् नाना रत्न विभूउषिताम् |
द्रक्ष्यसि त्वम् पुरीम् लंकाम् विनष्टाम् मैथिली कृते || ३-३८-२५_END
BEGIN_
"Dense with skyscrapers and palaces, and decorated with many a gemstone is that city
Lanka, but you will see it completely shattered down, for the sake of that Maithili. [3-38-25]_END

B_3_C_39_14
BEGIN_
रामम् एव हि पश्यामि रहिते राक्षसेश्वर |
दृष्ट्वा स्वप्न गतम् रामम् उद् भ्रमामि विचेतनः || ४-३९-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Even at a place void of people I am envisaging Rama alone, and oh, king of demons,
even if he enters my dream, in fact, I am jolting up and swooning. [4-39-17]_END

B_3_C_40_6
BEGIN_
एवम् मे निश्चिता बुद्धिः हृदि मारीच विद्यते |
न व्यावर्तयितुम् शक्या स इन्द्रैः अपि सुर असुरैः || ३-४०-७_END
BEGIN_
"In this way my thinking is decided and it is lingering on in my heart, and it is
impossible to roll back my mind or heart even for Indra coming along with gods and demons.
[3-40-7]_END

B_3_C_38_22
BEGIN_
अकुर्वन्तो अपि पापानि शुचयः पाप संश्रयात् |
पर पापैः विनश्यन्ति मत्स्या नाग ह्रदे यथा || ३-३८-२६_END
BEGIN_
"Even if with uncommitted sins, the sinless will get ruined owing to their
interdependence with other sinners, like the fish in a lake with snakes. [3-38-26]_END

B_3_C_39_15
BEGIN_
र कार अदीनि नामानि राम त्रस्तस्य रवण |
रत्नानि च रथाः च एव वित्रासम् जनयन्ति मे || ४-३९-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Ravana, appalled of Rama the names starting with the syllable 'ra' like
ratna-s, ratha-s, viz., gemstones, chariots are appalling to me, including your name, that starts
with a 'ra....' [4-39-18]_END

B_3_C_40_7
BEGIN_
दोषम् गुणम् वा संपृष्टः त्वम् एवम् वक्तुम् अर्हसि |
अपायम् वा अपि उपायम् वा कार्यस्य अस्य विनिश्चये || ३-४०-८_END
BEGIN_
"If you are asked about the credits or discredits, or either of the danger or
ideation of the deed for determining its modus operandi, it will be apt of you to talk like this,
but I did not seek any viewpoints of yours. [3-40-8]_END

B_3_C_38_23
BEGIN_
दिव्यचंदनदिग्धांगान्दिव्याअभरणभूषितान् -यद्वा-
दिव्य चंदन दिग्ध अंगान् दिव्य आभरण भूषितान् |
द्रक्ष्यसि अभिहतान् भूमौ तव दोषात् तु राक्षसान् || ३-३८-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Bedaubed with divine sandal-paste, beautified with divine ornaments are the limbs
of the demons now, perchance you will be seeing them trampled out on ground for the blunder of
yours. [3-38-27]_END

B_3_C_39_16
BEGIN_
अहम् तस्य प्रभावज्ञो न युद्धम् तेन ते क्षमम् |
बलिम् वा नमुचिं वा अपि हन्यद्धि रघुन्ंअंदन || ४-३९-१९_END
BEGIN_
"I am well-acquainted with his efficacy, and a war with him will be an unfair thing
for you, for that Raghu's descendant can in fact kill either Emperor Bali or Namuchi, the demon.
[4-39-19]_END

B_3_C_40_8
BEGIN_
संपृष्टेन तु वक्तव्यम् सचिवेन विपश्चिता |
उद्यत अंजलिना राज्ञे य इच्छेत् भूतिम् आत्मनः || ३-४०-९_END
BEGIN_
"Even if someone is asked, and if he desires his own welfare, then he has to submit
his opinion to the king suppliantly upraising his palm-fold, may he be an intellectual, or an
astute adviser. [3-40-9]_END

B_3_C_41_0
BEGIN_
आज्ञप्तो रावणेन इत्थम् प्रतिकूलम् च राजवत् |
अब्रवीत् परुषम् वाक्यम् निःशन्को राक्षसाधिपम् || ३-४१-१_END
BEGIN_
When Ravana perversely ordered that way in all his kingliness, Maareecha spoke these
words caustically and frankly to that king of demons. [3-41-1]_END

B_3_C_38_24
BEGIN_
हृत दारान् स दारान् च दश विद्रवतो दिशः |
हत शेषान् अशरणान् द्रक्ष्यसि त्वम् निशाचरान् || ३-३८-२८_END
BEGIN_
"Maybe, you will have to see the fleeing of the nightwalkers surviving after the
carnage in all ten directions, some abandoning their wives and some along with their wives, only
for lack of a protector. [3-38-28]_END

B_3_C_39_17
BEGIN_
रणे रामेण युद्ध्स्व क्षमाम् वा कुरु रावण |
न ते राम कथा कार्या यदि माम् द्रष्टुम् इच्छसि || ४-३९-२०_END
BEGIN_
"You may either wage a war with Rama if you wish to avenge the killings of Khara and
others, or forgive and forget that Rama agreeing to my suggestions, but do not broach the topic of
Rama with me if you wish to see me alive. [4-39-20]_END

B_3_C_40_9
BEGIN_
वाक्यम् अप्रतिकूलम् तु मृदु पूर्वम् शुभम् हितम् |
उपचारेण युक्तम् च वक्तव्यो वसुधा अधिपः || ३-४०-१०_END
BEGIN_
"The king being lord of the land is to be addressed preceded with gentility, with
auspicious and beneficial words that do not contradict the interests of that lord, more so, they
shall be inclusive of etiquette. [3-40-10]_END

B_3_C_41_1
BEGIN_
केन अयम् उपदिष्टः ते विनाशः पाप कर्मणा |
स पुत्रस्य स राज्यस्य स अमात्यस्य निशाचर || ३-४१-२_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, night-walker, by which evildoer this thought, which is self-ruinous to you,
along with your progeny, kingdom and ministers put together, is taught to you? [3-41-2]_END

B_3_C_38_25
BEGIN_
शर जाल परिक्षिप्ताम् अग्नि ज्वाला समावृताम् |
प्रदग्ध भवनाम् लंकाम् द्रक्ष्यसि त्वम् असंशयम् || ३-३८-२९_END
BEGIN_
"Without a doubt you will be seeing Lanka encircled with an enmesh of arrows,
enfolded in the tongues of torches, while her buildings are utterly gutting down. [3-38-29]_END

B_3_C_39_18
BEGIN_
बहवः साधवो लोके युक्ता धर्मम् अनुष्टिताः |
परेषाम् अपराधेन विनष्टाः स परिच्छदाः || ४-३९-२१_END
BEGIN_
"In the world many of the sagacious and reasonable people that are the practisers of
righteousness are utterly ruined along with their kith and kin, just by the misdeeds of others.
[4-39-21]_END

B_3_C_40_10
BEGIN_
स अवमर्दम् तु यत् वाक्यम् अथवा मारीच हितम् उच्यते |
न अभिनंदति तत् राजा मानार्थी मान वर्जितम् || ३-४०-११_END
BEGIN_
"Or else, oh, Maareecha, even if a beneficial word is said, but if it is said with
reprehension it will not gladden that king who insists upon honour, for that said word is
dishonourable, let alone reprehension. [3-40-11]_END

B_3_C_41_2
BEGIN_
कः त्वया सुखिना राजन् न अभिनन्दति पापकृत् |
केन इदम् उपदिष्टम् ते मृत्यु द्वारम् उपायतः || ३-४१-३_END
BEGIN_
"Who is that reprobate unhappy with such a happy one like you, and oh, king, by whom
this door of demise is ingeniously shown to you? [3-41-3]_END

B_3_C_38_26
BEGIN_
पर दार अभिमर्षात् तु न अनयत् पाप तरम् महत् |
प्रमदानाम् सहस्राणि तव राजन् परिग्रहे || ३-३८-३०_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, king, there is no other sin that is outrageous and gravest than the dalliance
with another's wife and, besides, you already have a thousand wives, isn't so! [3-38-30]_END

B_3_C_39_19
BEGIN_
सः अहम् पर अपराधेन विनाशेयम् निशाचर |
कुरु यत् ते क्षमम् तत् त्वम् अहम् त्वाम् न अनुयामि वै || ४-३९-२२_END
BEGIN_
"Such a saintly one as I am, I am bound to ruin by other's misdeeds, hence you do
whatever that is fair to you, but I am not the one to simply take after you. [4-39-22]_END

B_3_C_40_11
BEGIN_
पंच रूपाणि राजानो धारयन्ति अमित ओजसः |
अग्नेः इन्द्रस्य सोमस्य यमस्य वरुणस्य च || ३-४०-१२_END
BEGIN_
"The kings with infinite vigour embody five constituents forces of Fire, Moon, Rain,
Terminator, and that of Indra, the Administrator of Natural Forces. [3-40-12]_END

B_3_C_41_3
BEGIN_
शत्रवः तव सुव्यक्तम् हीन वीर्या निशा चर |
इच्छन्ति त्वाम् विनश्यन्तम् उपरुद्धम् बलीयसा || ३-४१-४_END
BEGIN_
"It is very clear, oh, night-walker, that your rivals with skimpy might are aspiring
that you should be completely ruined coming into conflict with more mighty Rama. [3-41-4]_END

B_3_C_38_27
BEGIN_
भव स्व दार निरतः स्व कुलम् रक्ष राक्षस |
मानम् वृद्धिम् च राज्यम् च जीवितम् च इष्टम् आत्मनः || ३-३८-३१_END
BEGIN_
"Abide by your own wife and be delighted with her, oh, demon, safeguard your own
ethnos, thus safeguard dignity, affluence, and kingdom of demons, thereby safeguard even your own
dear life. [3-38-31]_END

B_3_C_39_20
BEGIN_
रामः च हि महातेजा महासत्त्वो महाबलः |
अपि राक्षस लोकस्य भवेत् अन्तकरो अपि हि || ४-३९-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Definitely Rama is the one with exceptional resplendence, exemplary courage and
extraordinary power, and for sure, he becomes an eradicator of the world of demons. [4-39-23]_END

B_3_C_40_12
BEGIN_
औष्ण्यम् तथा विक्रमम् च सौम्यम् दण्डम् प्रसन्नताम् |
धारयन्ति महाताम्नो राजानः क्षणदाचर || ३-४०-१३
तस्मात् सर्वासु अवस्थासु मान्याः पूज्याः च पार्थिवाः |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, nightwalker, thus the kings being great-souls personify the sultriness of Fire,
sternness of Indra, softness of Moon, suppleness of Rain, and harshness of Terminator, and
therefore in all situations they are respectable and reverential. [3-40-13, 14a]_END

B_3_C_41_4
BEGIN_
केन इदम् उपदिष्टम् ते क्षुद्रेण अहित बुद्धिना |
यः त्वाम् इच्छति नश्यन्तम् स्व कृतेन निशाचर || ३-४१-५_END
BEGIN_
"He who wishes you to get ruined by your undertaking a self-made destruction is a
scoundrel with a pernicious intent, as such, by whom you are counselled to do this? [3-41-5]_END

B_3_C_38_28
BEGIN_
कलत्राणि च सौम्यानि मित्र वर्गम् तथैव च |
यदि इच्छसि चिरम् भोक्तुम् मा कृथा राम विप्रियम् || ३-३८-३२_END
BEGIN_
"If you desire to take pleasure with your beautiful wives and with your friend's
circles for a long time, do not do anything undesirable to Rama. [3-38-32]_END

B_3_C_39_21
BEGIN_
यदि शूर्पणखा हेतोः जनस्थान गत खरः |
अति वृत्तो हतः पूर्वम् रामेण अक्लिष्ट कर्मणा |
अत्र ब्रूहि यथावत् त्वम् को रामस्य व्यतिक्रमः || ४-३९-२४_END
BEGIN_
"If Khara positioned in Janasthaana has firstly overstepped his bounds and attacked
Rama, that too owing to Shuurpanakha, and if Rama of uncomplicated actions has eliminated Khara in
self-defence, what really is the transgression of Rama in that matter, you tell of that in the
final analysis. [4-39-24]_END

B_3_C_40_13
BEGIN_
त्वम् तु धर्मम् अविज्ञाय केवलम् मोहम् आश्रितः || ३-४०-१४
अभ्यागतम् माम् दौरात्म्यात् परुषम् वदसि ईदृशम् |_END
BEGIN_
"But you are ill-advisedly babbling with me in this way, incognizant of rectitude
and holding on to your obsession, and wishing ill of me, as I am on your doorstep. [3-40-14b,
15a]_END

B_3_C_41_5
BEGIN_
वध्याः खलु न वध्यन्ते सचिवाः तव रावण |
ये त्वाम् उत्पथम् आरूढम् न निगृह्णन्ति सर्वशः || ३-४१-६_END
BEGIN_
"Your ministers are not curbing you anywise when you scramble on a high road to
self-ruination, hence they are indeed to be sentenced to death, but they are not being executed for
their dereliction. [3-41-6]_END

B_3_C_38_29
BEGIN_
निवार्यमाणः सुहृदा मया भृशम्
प्रसह्य सीताम् यदि धर्षयिष्यसि |
गमिष्यसि क्षीण बलः स बान्धवो
यम क्षयम् राम शर आत्त जीवितः || ३-३८-३३_END
BEGIN_
"If you wish to intimidate Seetha aggressively despite of my considerable preventing
in all my good-heartedness towards you, then your army will fade away, and you with your kinsfolk
will emigrate to the world of Yama, the Terminator, for your life will be taken away by the arrow
of Rama." Thus, Maareecha spoke to Ravana. [3-38-33]_END

B_3_C_39_22
BEGIN_
इदम् वचो बन्धु हित अर्थिना मया
यथा उच्यमानम् यदि न अभिपत्स्यसे |
स बान्धवः त्यक्ष्यसि जीवितम् रणे
हतो अद्य रामेण शरैः जिह्मगैः || ४-३९-२५_END
BEGIN_
"I am saying this word of advise as I am ambitious of the wellbeing of my kinsmen
through you, and if this is disagreeable to you, you will have to deliver up your life in a
confrontation with Rama along with the lives of your kinsmen, perishing at the linearly
accelerating arrows of Rama. [4-39-25]_END

B_3_C_42_0
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्त्वा तु परुषम् मारीचो रावणम् ततः |
गच्छावः इति अब्रवीत् दीनो भयात् रात्रिम् चर प्रभोः || ३-४२-१_END
BEGIN_
Maareecha though curtly said in that way, then afraid of the king of night-walkers
he became self-pitying, and said to Ravana, 'let us go.' [3-42-1]_END

B_3_C_40_14
BEGIN_
गुण दोषौ न पृच्छामि क्षमम् च आत्मनि राक्षस || ३-४०-१५
मया उक्तम् अपि च एतावत् त्वाम् प्रति अमितविक्रम |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, demon, I did not ask the rights and wrongs concerning me, nor that which is
expedient for me, but oh, demon of untold bravery, I have said this much to you. [3-40-15]_END

B_3_C_41_6
BEGIN_
अमात्यैः काम वृत्तो हि राजा कापथम् आश्रितः |
निग्राह्यः सर्वथा सद्भिः न निग्राह्यो निगृह्यसे || ३-४१-७_END
BEGIN_
"Veracious ministers have to restrain a self-willed king when he relies on a
wrong-route, isn't it. But you are unrestrained by your ministers though you are self-willed and
though you are taking a wrong-route. [3-41-7]_END

B_3_C_42_1
BEGIN_
दृष्टाः च अहम् पुनः तेन शर चाप असि धारिणा |
मद्वधो उद्यत शस्त्रेण विनष्टम् जीवितम् च मे || ३-४२-२_END
BEGIN_
"If he who wields a bow, arrows and a sword, and who brandishes a weapon to only
kill me happens to see me again, deem my life is verily lost, without his shooting any arrow.
[3-42-2]_END

B_3_C_40_15
BEGIN_
अस्मिन् तु स भवान् कृत्ये साहाय्यम् कर्तुम् अर्हसि || ३-४०-१६
श्रुणु तत् कर्म साहाय्ये यत् कार्यम् वचनात् मम |_END
BEGIN_
" 'It will be apt of you to proffer a helping hand in this deed.' This much I said
to you. And such as you are you may now listen to that task which you have to undertake during the
course of your assistance as I detail it to you. [3-40-16]_END

B_3_C_41_7
BEGIN_
धर्मम् अर्थम् च कामम् च यशः च जयताम् वर |
स्वामि प्रसादात् सचिवाः प्राप्नुवन्ति निशाचर || ३-४१-८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, best conqueror Ravana, probity, prosperity and pleasures, and even the
popularity of the ministers, oh, night-walker, are achieved at the beneficence of their master.
[3-41-8]_END

B_3_C_42_2
BEGIN_
न हि रामम् पराक्रम्य जीवन् प्रति निवर्तते |
वर्तते प्रति रूपो असौ यम दण्ड हतस्य ते || ३-४२-३_END
BEGIN_
"None can really make so bold at Rama to reappear with life, isn't it. What is
appearing before you is the reflected image of mine, as I am already slain by the wand of Yama, the
Terminator, the moment I conceded to your demand._END

B_3_C_40_16
BEGIN_
सौवर्णः त्वम् मृगो भूत्वा चित्रो रजत बिन्दुभिः || ३-४०-१७
आश्रमे तस्य रामस्य सीतायाः प्रमुखे चर |
प्रलोभयित्वा वैदेहीम् यथा इष्टम् गन्तुम् अर्हसि || ३-४०-१८_END
BEGIN_
"On becoming an amazing silver-potted golden deer you move in front of Seetha in the
hermitage of Rama, and on verily alluring Vaidehi you can go away as you like. [3-40-17, 18 ]_END

B_3_C_41_8
BEGIN_
विपर्यये तु तत् सर्वम् व्यर्थम् भवति रावण |
व्यसनम् स्वामि वैगुण्यात् प्राप्नुवन्ति इतरे जनाः || ३-४१-९_END
BEGIN_
"Contrariwise, oh, Ravana, all that beneficence of the king to ministers becomes
futile when the king behaves perversely, and even the others, namely the subjects of kingdom, will
derive distress by the negative virtue of their master. [3-41-9]_END

B_3_C_42_3
BEGIN_
किम् नु कर्तुम् मया शक्यम् एवम् त्वयि दुरात्मनि |
एष गच्छामि अहम् तात स्वस्ति ते अस्तु निशाचरः || ३-४२-४_END
BEGIN_
"When you are spiteful, oh, boy, indeed what can I possibly do otherwise, oh,
night-walker, thither I go, may good betide you." So said Maareecha to Ravana. [3-42-4]_END

B_3_C_40_17
BEGIN_
त्वाम् हि माया मयम् दृष्ट्वा कांचनम् जात विस्मया |
आनय एनम् इति क्षिप्रम् रामम् वक्ष्यति मैथिली || ३-४०-१९_END
BEGIN_
"On seeing you as a wholly illusory golden deer curiosity arises in Vaidehi, and
indeed she tells Rama, 'bring that one quickly.' [3-40-19]_END

B_3_C_41_9
BEGIN_
राज मूलो हि धर्मः च जयः च जयताम् वर |
तस्मात् सर्वासु अवस्थासु रक्षितव्यो नराधिपाः || ३-४१-१०_END
BEGIN_
"The king alone is the root cause for probity and prosperity, isn't it. Therefore,
oh, best prosperous one, in all situations the kings are to be safeguarded from the ill effects of
influences. [3-41-10]_END

B_3_C_42_4
BEGIN_
प्रहृष्टः तु अभवत् तेन वचनेन स राक्षसः |
परिष्वज्य सुसंश्लिष्टम् इदम् वचनम् अब्रवीत् || ३-४२-५_END
BEGIN_
By that word of Maareecha demon Ravana is very much gladdened and he spoke this
sentence tightly hugging him. [3-42-5]_END

B_3_C_40_18
BEGIN_
अपक्रान्ते च काकुत्स्थे दूरम् च यात्वा अपि उदाहर |
हा सीते लक्ष्मणे इति एवम् राम वाक्य अनुरूपकम् || ३-४०-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Further, on Rama's coming out of his hermitage you go distantly and blurt out in
this way, 'ha Seetha' and even as, 'ha, Lakshmana,' mimicking Rama's voice. [3-40-20]_END

B_3_C_41_10
BEGIN_
राज्यम् पालयितुम् शक्यम् न तीक्ष्णेन निशाचर |
न च अपि प्रतिकूलेन न अविनीतेन राक्षस || ३-४१-११_END
BEGIN_
"It is impossible to govern kingdom, oh, demon, the night-walker, for a king with
acridity, with hostility, or with immorality. [3-41-11]_END

B_3_C_40_19
BEGIN_
तत् श्रुत्वा राम पदवीम् सीताया च प्रचोदितः |
अनुगच्छति संभ्रांतम् सौमित्रिः अपि सौहृदात् || ३-४०-२१_END
BEGIN_
"On hearing that, and further hastened by Seetha, even Soumitri apprehensively
follows the path of Rama in all his fondness for Rama. [3-40-21]_END

B_3_C_42_5
BEGIN_
एतत् शौण्डीर्य - चौत्तिर्य -न्युक्तम् ते मत् च्छंद वश वर्तिनः |
इदानीम् असि मारीचः पूर्वम् अन्यो निशाचरः || ३-४२-६_END
BEGIN_
"This word of yours shows your obduracy for you are abiding under the control of my
dictate, and though you were a different night-walker earlier, henceforth you are really the good
old Maareecha. [3-42-6]_END

B_3_C_41_11
BEGIN_
ये तीक्ष्ण मंत्राः सचिवा भज्यन्ते सह तेन वै |
विषमे तुरगाः शीघ्रा मन्द सारथयो यथा || ३-४१-१२_END
BEGIN_
"The ministers with drastic notions will indeed fall apart together with their king,
like a chariot that gets ramshackled together with it charioteer on a rough road, though it is
hieing with galloping horses but badly controlled by that slothful charioteer. [3-41-12]_END

B_3_C_40_20
BEGIN_
अपक्रान्ते च काकुत्स्थे लक्ष्मण च यथा सुखम् |
आहरिष्यामि वैदेहीम् सहस्राक्षः शचीम् इव || ३-४०-२२_END
BEGIN_
"When Rama is diverted from hermitage, Lakshmana as well, I will carry off Vaidehi
effortlessly like the Thousand-eyed Indra who once carried off Sachi Devi. [3-40-22]_END

B_3_C_42_6
BEGIN_
आरुह्यताम् शीघ्रम् खगो रत्न विभूषितः |
मया सह रथो युक्तः पिशाच वदनैः खरैः || ३-४२-७_END
BEGIN_
"Then you promptly emplane this sky-flying chariot which is yoked with ghost-faced
mules and adorned with gems along with me. [3-42-7]_END

B_3_C_41_12
BEGIN_
बहवः साधवो लोके युक्त धर्मम् अनुष्ठिताः |
परेषाम् अपराधेन विनष्टाः स परिच्छदाः || ३-४१-१३_END
BEGIN_
"In the world many saintly beings that are high-minded and pursuers of ethicality
are completely ruined together with their kinsmen owing to the misdeeds of others. [3-41-13]_END

B_3_C_40_21
BEGIN_
एवम् कृत्वा तु इदम् कार्यम् यथा इष्टम् गच्छ राक्षस |
राज्यस्य अर्धम् प्रदास्यामि मारीच तव सुव्रत || ३-४०-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, demon, on carrying out this stint in this manner you may go as you like, and to
you oh, Maareecha with solemn vows, I will grant half of my kingdom. [3-40-23]_END

B_3_C_42_7
BEGIN_
प्रलोभयित्वा वैदेहीम् यथा इष्टम् गन्तुम् अर्हसि |
ताम् शून्ये प्रसभम् सीताम् आनयिष्यामि मैथिलीम् || ३-४२-८_END
BEGIN_
"On deluding Vaidehi it is apt of you to go as you please, and I will bring that
Seetha of Mithila, however defiant it might be." Thus Ravana said to Maareecha. [3-42-8]_END

B_3_C_41_13
BEGIN_
स्वामिना प्रतिकूलेन प्रजाः तीक्ष्णेन रावण |
रक्ष्यमाणा न वर्धन्ते मेषा गोमायुना यथा || ३-४१-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Ravana, the subjects do not flourish while a lord with contrariety and
coerciveness safeguards them, just like goats guarded by a fox. [3-41-14]_END

B_3_C_40_22
BEGIN_
गच्छ सौम्य शिवम् मार्गम् कार्यस्य अस्य विवृद्धये |
अहम् तु अनुगमिष्यामि स रथो दण्डका वनम् || ३-४०-२४_END
BEGIN_
"Hence, oh, gentle one, get going on a trouble-free path for the easy achievement of
the task, and I for myself will follow you to Dandaka forest along with the chariot. [3-40-24]_END

B_3_C_42_8
BEGIN_
तथा इति उवाच एनम् रावणम् ताटका सुतः |
ततो रावण मारीचौ विमानम् इव तम् रथम् || ३-४२-९
आरुह्य ययतुः शीघ्रम् तस्मात् आश्रम मण्डलात् |_END
BEGIN_
Tataka's son Maareecha said "All right" to Ravana, and then both Ravana and
Maareecha mounted the chariot as they would emplane an aircraft and swiftly journeyed from the
surroundings of Maareecha's hermitage. [3-42-9, 10a]_END

B_3_C_41_14
BEGIN_
अवश्यम् विनशिष्यन्ति सर्वे रावण राक्षसाः |
येषाम् त्वम् कर्कशो राजा दुर्बुद्धिः अजित इन्द्रियः || ३-४१-१५_END
BEGIN_
"All those demons will definitely ruin, oh, Ravana, to whom you are the acrimonious
and malicious king with unconquered senses, though you have conquered the heaven. [3-41-15]_END

B_3_C_40_23
BEGIN_
प्राप्य सीताम् अयुद्धेन वंचयित्वा तु राघवम् |
लंकाम् प्रति गमिष्यामि कृत कार्यः सह त्वया || ३-४०-२५_END
BEGIN_
"My goal will be achieved just by misleading Raghava, and by gaining Seetha without
a conflict, then I will proceed to Lanka along with you. [3-40-25]_END

B_3_C_42_9
BEGIN_
तथैव तत्र पश्यन्तौ पत्तनानि वनानि च || ३-४२-१०
गिरीम् च सरिताः सर्वा राष्ट्राणि नगराणि च |_END
BEGIN_
While looking at the seaports and forests, also at all the mountains and rivers,
even at the cities and provinces en route they proceeded. [3-42-10b, 11a]_END

B_3_C_41_15
BEGIN_
तद् इदम् काक तालीयम् घोरम् आसादितम् मया |
अत्र त्वम् शोचनीयो असि स सैन्यो विनशिष्यसि || ३-४१-१६_END
BEGIN_
"What is the use of laming for myself as I foregathered this ghastly situation as in
crow-palm-tree syndrome, but in this issue you alone are regrettable, for you are gong to
completely ruin along with your military. [3-41-16]_END

B_3_C_40_24
BEGIN_
नो चेत् करोषि मारीच हन्मि त्वाम् अहम् अद्य वै |
एतत् कार्यम् अवश्यम् मे बलाद् अपि करिष्यसि |
राज्ञो हि प्रतिकूलस्थो न जातु सुखम् एधते || ३-४०-२६_END
BEGIN_
"If you are not going to do so, oh, Maareecha, for sure I will kill you now itself.
I will get my work done through you even under duress, and indeed, any subject setting against his
king will never succeed safely. [3-40-26]_END

B_3_C_42_10
BEGIN_
समेत्य दण्डक अरण्यम् राघवस्य आश्रमम् ततः || ३-४२-११
ददर्श सह मरीचो रावणो राक्षसाधिपः |_END
BEGIN_
On reaching Dandaka forest along with Maareecha the king of demons Ravana has then
seen the hermitage of Raghava. [3-42-11b, 12a]_END

B_3_C_41_16
BEGIN_
माम् निहत्य तु रामो असौ अचिरात् त्वाम् वधिष्यति |
अनेन कृत कृत्यो अस्मि म्रिये च अपि अरिणा हतः || ३-४१-१७_END
BEGIN_
"That Rama will soon kill you after killing me, and I will be dying at the hand of
my enemy rather than at the hand of my own clansman like you, whereby the purpose of my life will
be brought to an end. [3-41-17]_END

B_3_C_43_0
BEGIN_
सा तम् संप्रेक्ष्य सुश्रोणी कुसुमानि विचिन्वती |हेम राजत वर्णाभ्याम् पार्श्वाभ्याम् उपशोभितम् || 
३-४३-१प्रहृष्टा च अनवद्यान्गी मृष्ट हाटक वर्णिनी |भर्तारम् अपि च आक्रन्द लक्ष्मणम् चैव सायुधम् 
|| ३-४३-२_END
BEGIN_
That slender-waisted Seetha whose limbs are flawless, whose complexion is like purified gold, and who 
is presently culling flowers is highly gladdened to observe the Golden Deer that is brightened in one 
flank with the colour of gold and the other is silvery, and she shouted for attention of her husband, 
and even that of Lakshmana who is presently weaponed. [3-43-1, 2]_END

B_3_C_42_11
BEGIN_
अवतीर्य रथात् तस्मात् ततः कांचन भूषणात् || ३-४२-१२
हस्ते गृहीत्वा मारीचम् रावणो वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् |_END
BEGIN_
Alighting the chariot that is decorated with golden ornaments Ravana then spoke this
sentence to Maareecha taking his hand into his. [3-42-12b, 13a]_END

B_3_C_40_25
BEGIN_
आसाद्या तम् जीवित संशयः ते
मृत्युर् ध्रुवो हि अद्य मया विरुध्यतः |
एतत् यथावत् परिगृह्य बुद्ध्या
यत् अत्र पथ्यम् कुरु तत् तथा त्वम् || ३-४०-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Your life may be indefinite on reaching Rama, but your death is surely definite now
as you are conflicting with me. Hence, keeping all this in view you come to a conclusion that would
be conducive to your interests, and whatever desirable to you let it be done in that way. " Thus
Ravana spoke to Maareecha. [3-40-27]_END

B_3_C_41_17
BEGIN_
दर्शनात् एव रामस्य हतम् माम् अवधारय |
आत्मानम् च हतम् विद्धि हृत्वा सीताम् स बान्धवम् || ३-४१-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Know that I am killed just when Rama notices me, and know that you are also killed
along with your kinsmen just when you steal Seetha. [3-41-18]_END

B_3_C_43_1
BEGIN_
आहूय आहूय च पुनः तम् मृगम् साधु वीक्षते |आगच्छ आगच्छ शीघ्रम् वै आर्यपुत्र सह अनुज || ३-४३-३_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, noble prince, come here," thus she called her husband and peered at the deer, and again she called, 
"really come with your younger brother quickly," and again gazed at the deer, and thus she oftentimes 
called and oftentimes saw the deer fondly. [3-43-3]_END

B_3_C_42_12
BEGIN_
एतत् राम आश्रम पदम् दृश्यते कदली वृतम् || ३-४२-१३
क्रियताम् तत् सखे शीघ्रम् यत् अर्थम् वयम् आगताः |_END
BEGIN_
"This one which we are seeing and which is surrounded with banana plants is the
threshold of Rama's hermitage, and -`----oh, friend, the purpose for which we came here let it be
effectuated promptly." Thus Ravana hastened Maareecha. [3-42-13b, 14a]_END

B_3_C_41_18
BEGIN_
आनयिष्यसि चेत् सीताम् आश्रमात् सहितो मया |
न एव त्वम् असि न एव अहम् न एव लंका न राक्षसाः || ३-४१-१९_END
BEGIN_
"If you are going to bring Seetha from their hermitage on going there with me, then
you will not be there, I will not be there, Lanka will not be there, the demons will not be there.
[3-41-19]_END

B_3_C_43_2
BEGIN_
तया आहूतौ नरव्याघ्रौ वैदेह्या राम लक्ष्मणौ |वीक्षमाणौ तु तम् देशम् तदा ददृशतुः मृगम् || ३-४३-४_END
BEGIN_
Those manly lions Rama and Lakshmana thus bidden by Vaidehi came there exploring that place and then 
they saw that Golden Deer. [3-43-4]_END

B_3_C_42_13
BEGIN_
स रावण वचः श्रुत्वा मारीचो राक्षसः तदा || ३-४२-१४
मृगो भूत्वा आश्रम द्वारि रामस्य विचचार ह |_END
BEGIN_
"And on hearing Ravana's words demon Maareecha then became a deer and indeed ambled
freely in the frontage of Rama's hermitage. [3-42-14b, 15a]_END

B_3_C_41_19
BEGIN_
निवार्यमाणः तु मया हित एषिणा
न मृष्यसे वाक्यम् इदम् निशाचर |
परेत कल्पा हि गत आयुषो नरा
हितम् न गृह्णन्ति सुहृद्भिः ईरितम् || ३-४१-२०_END
BEGIN_
"As a desirer of your welfare I am dissuading you, oh, night-walker, but you may
feel that this word of mine is unpleasant to you. People on diminishing lifetime will be similar to
corpses and a corpse cannot take in the expedient spoken by considerate confidants, isn't so.
[3-41-20]_END

B_3_C_43_3
BEGIN_
शंकमानः तु तम् दृष्ट्वा लक्ष्मणो रामम् अब्रवीत् |तम् एव एनम् अहम् मन्ये मारीचम् राक्षसम् मृगम् || 
३-४३-५_END
BEGIN_
But Lakshmana became incredulous on seeing it and said to Rama, "I believe this deer to be that Maareecha, 
the demon." [3-43-5]_END

B_3_C_42_14
BEGIN_
स तु रूपम् समास्थाय महत् अद्भुत दर्शनम् || ३-४२-१५
मणिप्रवर शृंगाग्रः सित असित मुखाकृतिः |_END
BEGIN_
Adopting the form of a gorgeous deer which is superbly amazing just by its
appearance, whose tips of antlers are in the hue of best sapphires, and whose face is whitish at
some places and not so whitish at other in its look, he became a Golden Deer and moved thereabout.
[3-42-15b, 16a]_END

B_3_C_43_4
BEGIN_
चरन्तो मृगयाम् हृष्टाः पापेन उपाधिना वने |अनेन निहता राम राजानः काम रूपिणा || ३-४३-६_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama, when kings engaged in hunting games were delightedly moving in the forest, this Maareecha 
killed many of them resorting to many disguises, for he is a guise-changer by his wish. [3-43-6]_END

B_3_C_42_15
BEGIN_
रक्तपद्मोत्पल मुख इन्द्रनीलोत्पल श्रवाः || ३-४२-१६
किंचित् अभ्युन्नत ग्रीव इन्द्रनील निभ उदरः |_END
BEGIN_
One of its cheeks in the shade of a reddish-lotus while the other in the hue of a
bluish-lotus, one of its ears is in the hue of bloomed blue-lotus while the other is in the shade
of a sapphire, while the shine of its stomach is like that of a best blue-diamond,
Indra-niila-maNi, and with a little upraised neck that deer has moved about there. [3-42-16b,
17a]_END

B_3_C_43_5
BEGIN_
अस्य मायाविदो माया मृग रूपम् इदम् कृतम् |भानुमत् पुरुषव्याघ्र गन्धर्व पुर संनिभम् || ३-४३-७_END
BEGIN_
"Maareecha is an expert in many wiles and he has now assumed the form of this Golden-Deer, oh, manly 
lion, which is not more than the scintillating city of Gandharva-s, a city of wiles, which any trickster 
can create to make-believe. [3-43-7]_END

B_3_C_42_16
BEGIN_
मधूक निभ पार्श्वः च कंज किंजल्क सम्निभः || ३-४२-१७
वैदूर्य संकाश खुरः तनु जंघः सुसंहतः |_END
BEGIN_
One flank is shining whitish like Madhuka flowers and the other is similar to the
roseate fibrils of lotuses, while its hooves are similar to the gemstone lapis, calves thin, and
thus with very well cohered limbs that deer moved about there. [3-42-17b, 18a]_END

B_3_C_43_6
BEGIN_
मृगो हि एवम् विधो रत्न विचित्रो न अस्ति राघव |जगत्याम् जगतीनाथ माया एषा हि न संशयः || ३-४३-८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Raghava, this kind of amazing animal with gemlike dapples is nonexistent in the world, isn't it. 
Hence, oh, lord of the world, this is truly a phantasm. No doubt about it." So said Lakshmana to Rama. 
[3-43-8]_END

B_3_C_44_0
BEGIN_
तथा तु तम् समादिश्य भ्रातरम् रघुनंदनः |
बबन्ध असिम् महातेजा जांबूनदमयः त्सरुम् || ३-४४-१_END
BEGIN_
Rama, the great-resplendent scion of Raghu, on instructing his brother Lakshmana in
that way securely fastened his sword with golden handle to his waist. [3-44-1]_END

B_3_C_42_17
BEGIN_
इन्द्र आयुध सवर्णेन पुच्छेन ऊर्ध्वम् विराजितः || ३-४२-१८
मनोहर स्निग्ध वर्णो रत्नैः नाना विधैः वृतः |_END
BEGIN_
With an upraised tail that shone forth in a tinge equal to the weapon of Indra,
namely Rainbow, and with a complexion that is lustrous and dappled with many diverse gemlike
dapples, that deer moved thereabout with a heart-stealing aura. [3-42-18b, 19a]_END

B_3_C_43_7
BEGIN_
एवम् ब्रुवाणम् काकुत्स्थम् प्रतिवार्य शुचि स्मिता |उवाच सीता संहृष्टा चद्मना हृत चेतना || ३-४३-९_END
BEGIN_
While Lakshmana of Kakutstha-s is speaking thus, she who is self-satisfied as her heart is conjured 
by the cozenage, such a Seetha of a toothy smile deterred him and spoke. [3-43-9]_END

B_3_C_44_1
BEGIN_
ततः त्रि विनतम् चापम् आदाय आत्म विभूषणम् |
आबध्य च कलापौ द्वौ जगाम उदग्र विक्रमः || ३-४४-२_END
BEGIN_
Rama whose valour is escalating then took his own insignia, the three-way arched bow
called kodanDa, and fastened two quivers and proceeded. [3-44-2]_END

B_3_C_42_18
BEGIN_
क्षणेन राक्षसो जातो मृगः परम शोभनः || ३-४२-१९
वनम् प्रज्वलयन् रम्यम् राम आश्रम पदम् च तत् |_END
BEGIN_
Thus that demon Maareecha emerged like a highly splendorous and fascinating deer in
a wink highly irradiating those woodlands, and the threshold of Rama's hermitage in particular.
[3-42-19b, 20a]_END

B_3_C_44_2
BEGIN_
तम् वंचयानो राजेन्द्रम् आपतन्तम् निरीक्ष्य वै |
बभूव अंतर्हितः त्रासात् पुनः संदर्शने अभवत् || ३-४४-३
बद्ध असिः धनुः आदाय प्रदुद्राव यतो मृगः |_END
BEGIN_
On peering at the peerless one among kings, namely Rama, who is indeed coming down
on him, that Golden Deer disappeared as if with fear and even to beguile him, and again it came
into clear visibility. And Rama speedily spurted to that place from where the Golden Deer has
firstly disappeared with securely grit sword and firmly handled bow. [3-44-3]_END

B_3_C_43_8
BEGIN_
आर्यपुत्र अभिरामो असौ मृगो हरति मे मनः |आनय एनम् महाबाहो क्रीडार्थम् नः भविष्यति || ३-४३-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, nobleman's son, that delightful deer is stealing my heart, oh, dextrous one, bring it round, it 
will be our plaything. [3-43-10]_END

B_3_C_42_19
BEGIN_
मनोहरम् दर्शनीयम् रूपम् कृत्वा स राक्षसः || ३-४२-२०
प्रलोभनार्थम् वैदेह्या नाना धातु विचित्रितम् |
विचरन् गच्छते सम्यक् शाद्वलानि समंततः || ३-४२-२१_END
BEGIN_
Adopting such an exquisite and heart-stealing form which is amazingly dappled with
the colours of diverse ores, that demon ambled all over there freely with the bearing of a real
deer in order that Vaidehi might be deluded, and he moved forward onto the pastures. [3-42-2b,
21]_END

B_3_C_43_9
BEGIN_
इह आश्रम पदे अस्माकम् बहवः पुण्य दर्शनाः |मृगाः चरन्ति सहिताः चमराः सृमराः तथा || ३-४३-११_END
BEGIN_
"Here in the threshold of our hermitage many animals with adorable manifestation are moving about in 
flocks and herds, say Caamara deer, like that Srimara deer. [3-43-11]_END

B_3_C_44_3
BEGIN_
तम् स्म पश्यति रूपेण द्योतमानम् इव अग्रतः || ३-४४-४
अवेक्ष्य अवेक्ष्य धावन्तम् धनुष् पाणिः महावने |
अतिवृत्तम् इषोः पातात् लोभयानम् कदाचन || ३-४४-५
शंकितम् तु समुद् भ्रान्तम् उत्पतन्तम् इव अंबरे |
दृअश्यमानम् अदृश्यम् च वन उद्देशेषु केषुचित् || ३-४४-६
चिन्न अभ्रैः इव संवीतम् शारदम् चन्द्र मण्डलम् |_END
BEGIN_
Rama the wielder of bow kept on beholding that Golden Deer which is observing him
over and over and running away into deep of the forest. In the next moment he has seen it right in
front of him as though effulgent with its marvellous form. At times he has seen it running away as
though to circumvent the fall of arrow, and at times stopping only to tantalise him. Sometimes it
appeared to be springing as though to skies in very highly perplexity of wariness. It is
disappearing somewhere in the thickets of forest, and it is putting in an appearance elsewhere in
those thickets, like the autumnal orb of the moon under the fly front of splintered clouds.
[3-44-4b, 5, 6, 7a]_END

B_3_C_42_20
BEGIN_
रोप्यैः बिन्दु शतैः चित्रो भूत्वा च प्रिय दर्शनः |
विटपीनाम् किसलयान् भक्षयन् विचचार ह || ३-४२-२२_END
BEGIN_
And with hundreds of silvery stipples of body he became an astonishing deer with
pleasant looks and indeed moved chewing new grass-blades of trees. [3-42-22]_END

B_3_C_44_4
BEGIN_
मुहूर्तात् एव ददृशे मुहुर् दूरात् प्रकाशते || ३-४४-७
दर्शन अदर्शनेन एव सः अपाकर्षत राघवम् |
सुदूरम् आश्रमस्य अस्य मारिचो मृगताम् गतः || ३-४४-८_END
BEGIN_
In a wink Rama could proximately see that Maareecha who transformed himself into the
Golden Deer, and again in a flash he appeared distantly. Thus that deer/demon has drawn off Raghava
very far from his hermitage in this hide and seek game. [3-44-7b, 8]_END

B_3_C_43_10
BEGIN_
ऋक्षाः पृषत संघाः च वानराः किनराः तथा |विचरन्ति महाबाहो रूप श्रेष्ठा महाबलाः || ३-४३-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Also the animals that are excellent in their form, say monkeys, are moving here. Likewise herds of 
Kinnara deer, spotted-deer, and even bears of great-might are freely moving here. [3-43-12]_END

B_3_C_42_21
BEGIN_
कदली गृहकम् गत्वा कर्णिकारानि ततः ततः |
समाश्रयन् मंदगतिः सीता संदर्शनम् ततः || ३-४२-२३_END
BEGIN_
That Golden Deer has gone into the boscages of banana plants, and moved here and
there around Karnikara trees, and then resorted to a place which is within the eyeshot of Seetha.
[3-42-23]_END

B_3_C_43_11
BEGIN_
न च अस्य सदृशो राजन् दृष्ट पूर्वो मृगः मया |तेजसा क्षमया दीप्त्या यथा अयम् मृग सत्तमः || ३-४३-१३_END
BEGIN_
"As to how this extraordinary deer is appearing, oh, king, by way of its brilliance, tameness, or by 
the lustre of its skin, I have not so far seen any coequal to this. [3-43-13]_END

B_3_C_44_5
BEGIN_
आसीत् क्रुद्धः तु काकुत्स्थो विवशः तेन मोहितः |
अथ अवतस्थे सुश्रान्तः च्छायाम् आश्रित्य शाद्वले || ३-४४-९_END
BEGIN_
Rama of Kakutstha is incensed as its form is spellbinding but its capture slippery,
and then verily tired as he is he stayed on a pasture taking shelter of a tree shade. [3-44-9]_END

B_3_C_42_22
BEGIN_
राजीव चित्र पृष्ठः स विरराज महामृगः |
राम आश्रम पद अभ्याशे विचचार यथा सुखम् || ३-४२-२४_END
BEGIN_
With an odd lotus like hind-side that astounding deer is verily scintillating, and
it milled around the surroundings in the threshold of Rama's hermitage according to its own
delight. [3-42-24]_END

B_3_C_43_12
BEGIN_
नाना वर्ण विचित्र अंगो रत्न भूतो मम अग्रतः |द्योतयन् वनम् अव्यग्रम् शोभते शशि संनिभः || ३-४३-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Diversely coloured, amazingly limbed, and spotted with gemlike dapples it is shining forth like a deer 
that is completely gemmy, and while nonchalantly moving before me it is enlivening the forest like the 
moon. [3-43-14]_END

B_3_C_44_6
BEGIN_
स तम् उन्मादयामास मृगरूपो निशाचर |
मृगैः परिवृतो अथ वन्यैः अदूरात् प्रत्यदृश्यत || ३-४४-१०_END
BEGIN_
Nightwalker Maareecha has further maddened Rama in the guise of Golden Deer by
reappearing in his close-by, surrounded with other animals of the forest. [3-44-10]_END

B_3_C_42_23
BEGIN_
पुनर् गत्वा निवृत्तः च विचचार मृगोत्तमः |
गत्वा मुहूर्तम् त्वरया पुनः प्रति निवर्तते || ३-४२-२५_END
BEGIN_
That excellent deer beats a retreat and again returns, and meanders thus time and
again, and turns its tail for sometime only to return once again very playfully. [3-42-25]_END

B_3_C_43_13
BEGIN_
अहो रूपम् अहो लक्ष्मीः स्वर संपत् च शोभना |मृगो अद्भुतो विचित्रांगो हृदयम् हरति इव मे || ३-४३-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Ah, what a form, ah, what a brilliance, what a beautiful bleat! This amazingly limbed deer is wonderful, 
and this is stealing my heart, as it were. [3-43-15]_END

B_3_C_44_7
BEGIN_
ग्रहीतु कामम् दृष्ट्वा तम् पुनः एव अभ्यधावत |
तत् क्षणात् एव संत्रासात् पुनर् अंतर्हितो अभवत् || ३-४४-११_END
BEGIN_
Again on seeing Rama who is stalking his catch that deer ran towards him as though
to impress with its guilelessness, and just at that moment it vanished again as if with extreme
fear. [3-44-11]_END

B_3_C_42_24
BEGIN_
विक्रीडन् च पुनर् भूमौ पुनर् एव निषीदति |
आश्रम द्वारम् आगम्य मृग यूथानि गच्छति || ३-४२-२६_END
BEGIN_
Again gambolling everywhere it sits somewhere on the ground, then, on coming to the
threshold of hermitage it goes towards herds of deer. [3-42-26]_END

B_3_C_43_14
BEGIN_
यदि ग्रहणम् अभ्येति जीवन् एव मृगः तव |आश्चर्य भूतम् भवति विस्मयम् जनयिष्यति || ३-४३-१६_END
BEGIN_
"It will be surprising if this deer draws into your capture alive and well, as it creates astonishment 
to one and all. [3-43-16]_END

B_3_C_44_8
BEGIN_
पुनर् एव ततो दूरात् वृक्ष खण्डात् विनिःसृतः |
दृष्ट्वा रामो महातेजाः तम् हन्तुम् कृत निश्चयः || ३-४४-१२_END
BEGIN_
