Then that deer has again emerged out of the thick of trees, and on spotting it the
great-resplendent Rama has firmed up his decision to fell it. [3-44-12]_END

B_3_C_42_25
BEGIN_
मृग यूथैः अनुगतः पुनर् एव निवर्तते |
सीता दर्शनम् आकांक्षन् राक्षसो मृगताम् गतः || ३-४२-२७
परिभ्रमति चित्राणि मण्डलानि विनिष्पतन् |_END
BEGIN_
That demon who has gone into the deer-hood has gone after some herd of deer. But he
returned again though that herd followed him wanting to fraternise, in order that he shall remain
perceptible to Seetha, and he whirligiged in amusing circles while leaping and bounding to and from
that herd of deer. [3-42-27, 28a]_END

B_3_C_43_15
BEGIN_
समाप्त वन वासानाम् राज्य स्थानाम् च नः पुनः |अंतःपुरे विभूषार्थो मृग एष भविष्यति || ३-४३-१७_END
BEGIN_
"When we return to kingdom on completing our dwelling in forest this deer becomes a masterpiece in palace-chambers 
for us. [3-43-17]_END

B_3_C_44_9
BEGIN_
भूयः तु शरम् उद्धृत्य कुपितः तत्र राघवः |
सूर्य रश्मि प्रतीकाशम् ज्वलंतम् अरि मर्दनम् || ३-४४-१३
संधाय सुदृढे चापे विकृष्य बलवत् बली |
तम् एव मृगम् उद्दिश्य श्वसंतम् इव पन्नगम् || ३-४४-१४
मुमोच ज्वलितम् दीप्तम् अस्त्रम् ब्रह्म विनिर्मितम् |_END
BEGIN_
At that instant Raghava became highly infuriated and unholstered a holocaustic,
enemy-subjugating arrow that is similar to the flare of the sun, tautening it on his very sturdy
bow that forceful Rama forcefully outstretched the bowstring with arrow targeting the Golden Deer
alone, and released that fierily blazing arrow-missile which is carefully created by Brahma and
which is hissing like a snake. [3-44-13, 14, 15a]_END

B_3_C_42_26
BEGIN_
समुद्वीक्ष्य च सर्वे तम् मृगा ये अन्ये वनेचराः || ३-४२-२८
उपगम्य समाघ्राय विद्रवन्ति दिशो दश |_END
BEGIN_
All the other animals moving in that forest on seeing this demon-deer with their
necks up have come close to it, and on smelling it well they are running away to all the ten
directions noticing it as a demon turned into a deer. [3-42-28b, 29a]_END

B_3_C_43_16
BEGIN_
भरतस्य आर्यपुत्रस्य श्वश्रूणाम् मम च प्रभो |मृग रूपम् इदम् दिव्यम् विस्मयम् जनयिष्यति || ३-४३-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, lord, the form of this deer creates an excellent jubilation to Bharata, to you the son of the nobleman, 
to my mothers-in-law, and also to me in palace-chambers. [3-43-18]_END

B_3_C_44_10
BEGIN_
शरीरम् मृग रूपस्य विनिर्भिद्य शरोत्तमः || ३-४४-१५
मारीचस्य एव हृदयम् विभेद अशनि संनिभः |_END
BEGIN_
On very profoundly impaling the body of deer's form that superb arrow which is
similar to a thunderbolt has severed the heart of Maareecha in the core of deer's body. [3-44-15b,
16a]_END

B_3_C_42_27
BEGIN_
राक्षसः सो अपि तान् वन्यान् मृगान् मृगवधे रतः || ३-४२-२९
प्रच्छादनार्थम् भावस्य न भक्षयति संस्पृशन् |_END
BEGIN_
Even that demon in the deer's semblance Maareecha, though indulged in killing those
forest animals, and though the other animals are touching him, he is not killing and eating them
indulgently, only for the reason of camouflaging his present nature of demon-hood. [3-42-29b,
30a]_END

B_3_C_43_17
BEGIN_
जीवन् न यदि ते अभ्येति ग्रहणम् मृग सत्तमः |अजिनम् नरशार्दूल रुचिरम् तु भविष्यति || ३-४३-१९_END
BEGIN_
"Else if that best deer does not come into you capture while alive, oh tigerly-man, at the least its 
gorgeous deerskin will be remnant of it. [3-43-19]_END

B_3_C_44_11
BEGIN_
ताल मात्रम् अथ उत्प्लुत्य न्यपतत् स भृश आतुरः || ३-४४-१६
व्यनदत् भैरवम् नादम् धरण्याम् अल्प जीवितः |_END
BEGIN_
Then Maareecha is highly frenzied as his lifespan is minimised, blared a blaring
shriek, vaulted up to a height of palm-tree, and fell down onto the ground. [3-44-16b, 17a]_END

B_3_C_45_0
BEGIN_
आर्तस्वरम् तु तम् भर्तुः विज्ञाय सदृशम् वने |उवाच लक्ष्मणम् सीता गच्छ जानीहि राघवम् || ३-४५-१_END
BEGIN_
On identifying the grievous voice that is identifiable with her husband's voice, Seetha spoke to Lakshmana, 
"you go at once, and check up on Raghava.' [3-45-1]_END

B_3_C_42_28
BEGIN_
तस्मिन् एव ततः काले वैदेही शुभलोचना || ३-४२-३०
कुसुम अपचये व्यग्रा पादपान् अभ्यवर्तत |_END
BEGIN_
What is more, Vaidehi with her felicitous eyes came towards trees yearning for
plucking the flowers in the same instant. [3-42-30b, 31a]_END

B_3_C_43_18
BEGIN_
निहतस्य अस्य सत्त्वस्य जांबूनदमय त्वचि |शष्प बृस्याम् विनीतायाम् इच्छामि अहम् उपासितुम् || ३-४३-२०_END
BEGIN_
"I wish to sit along with you on its golden deerskin, overlaying it on a seat of tender darbha grass-blades, 
in case the deer is felled. [3-43-20]_END

B_3_C_44_12
BEGIN_
म्रियमाणः तु मारीचो जहौ ताम् कृत्रिमाम् तनुम् || ३-४४-१७
स्मृत्वा तत् वचनम् रक्षो दध्यौ केन तु लक्ष्मणम् |
इह प्रस्थापयेत् सीता ताम् शून्ये रावणे हरेत् || ३-४४-१८_END
BEGIN_
Maareecha on his part abandoned the body of Golden Deer when he is dying. But
remembering the words of Ravana that demon gave a thought, 'how best will Seetha hasten Lakshmana
to this place, and how best Ravana can abduct Seetha in a place void of people.' [3-44-17b, 18]_END

B_3_C_45_1
BEGIN_
न हि मे जीवितम् स्थाने हृदयम् वा अवतिष्ठते |क्रोशतः परम आर्तस्य श्रुतः शब्दो मया भृशम् || ३-४५-२
आक्रन्दमानम् तु वने भ्रातरम् त्रातुम् अर्हसि |_END
BEGIN_
"I have heard the loud yelling voice of highly fretful Rama whereby my heart, or my very entity, is 
not abiding in its place, and it will be apt of you to protect such a brother of yours who is screaming 
in the forest. [3-45-2, 3a]_END

B_3_C_42_29
BEGIN_
कर्णिकारान् अशोकान् च चूताम् च मदिरेक्षणा || ३-४२-३१
कुसुमानि अपचिन्वन्ती चचार रुचिरानना |_END
BEGIN_
And she with her inebriating glances and delightful visage moved there about while
plucking flowers of Karnikaara, Ashoka, and of Mango trees. [3-42-31b, 32a]_END

B_3_C_43_19
BEGIN_
कामवृत्तम् इदम् रौद्रम् स्त्रीणाम् असदृशम् मतम् |वपुषा तु अस्य सत्त्वस्य विस्मयो जनितो मम || ३-४३-२१_END
BEGIN_
"Tradition says that this sort of unruly self-seeking is unbefitting to women, yet that deer's beautiful 
body is inducing curiosity in me." Seetha said so to Rama and remained waiting for his reply. [3-43-21]_END

B_3_C_44_13
BEGIN_
स प्राप्त कालम् अज्ञाय चकार च ततः स्वरम् |
सदृशम् राघवस्य एव हा सीते लक्ष्मण इति च || ३-४४-१९_END
BEGIN_
Perceptive of the time that chanced bearing his death, and wishful of the death of
Ravana too, then made a voice that is a soundalike to Raghava's voice and yelled 'ha, Seetha...'
also thus 'ha Lakshmana...' [3-44-19]_END

B_3_C_45_2
BEGIN_
तम् क्षिप्रम् अभिधाव त्वम् भ्रातरम् शरण एषिणम् || ३-४५-३रक्षसाम् वशम् आपन्नम् सिंहानाम् इव गोवृषम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
"He might have come under the subjugation of demons as with a bull coming under the seize of lions, 
hence, you hurry up so as to near such a brother of yours who is seeking protection." So said Seetha 
toi Lakshmana. [3-45-3b, 4a]_END

B_3_C_42_30
BEGIN_
अनर्हा अरण्य वासस्य सा तम् रत्नमयम् मृगम् || ३-४२-३२
मुक्ता मणि विचित्र अंगम् ददर्श परम अंगना |_END
BEGIN_
That select lady who is unmeet for forest life beheld that deer which is completely
gemlike and whose limbs are surprising as though studded with pearls and gems. [3-42-32b, 33a]_END

B_3_C_43_20
BEGIN_
तेन कांचन रोम्णा तु मणि प्रवर शृंगिणा |तरुण आदित्य वर्णेन नक्षत्र पथ वर्चसा || ३-४३-२२बभूव राघवस्य 
अपि मनो विस्मयम् आगतम् |_END
BEGIN_
As for that deer's horns they vie with excellent sapphires, its golden coat with the glitter of tender 
sun, and its ambience with silver spots on coat with a milk way containing twinkling stars, and by that 
reason even Raghava's heart is awestruck when he saw it. [3-43-22, 23a]_END

B_3_C_44_14
BEGIN_
तेन मर्मणि निर्विद्धम् शरेण अनुपमेन हि |
मृग रूपम् तु तत् त्यक्त्वा राक्षसम् रूपम् आस्थितः || ३-४४-२०
चक्रे स सुमहा कायम् मारीचो जीवितम् त्यजन् |_END
BEGIN_
When Rama's incomparable arrow has indeed shattered his crucial organ, namely the
heart, in a downright manner, then Maareecha assumed a very massive physique of a demon, abandoning
the form of Golden Deer. [3-44-20, 21a]_END

B_3_C_45_3
BEGIN_
न जगाम तथा उक्तः तु भ्रातुः आज्ञाय शासनम् || ३-४५-४तम् उवाच ततः तत्र क्षुभिता जनक आत्मजा |_END
BEGIN_
Although she spoke a lot to him in this way, Lakshmana on his part has not moved out remembering his 
brother's order to stay guard to Seetha, and hence that Janaki, the daughter of Janaka, who is already 
agitated for Rama further spoke to him in the paradox of his not going out of hermitage. [3-45-4b, 5a]_END

B_3_C_42_31
BEGIN_
तम् वै रुचिर दंत ओष्ठम् रूप्य धातु तनू रुहम् || ३-४२-३३
विस्मयात् उत्फुल्ल नयना स स्नेहम् समुदैक्षत |_END
BEGIN_
And she that Seetha goggled the Golden Deer with a wide-eyed astonishment, which
deer has pretty lips and teeth, hair resembling silver and copper ores, and she indeed gazed at it
with an affinity for wildlife. [3-42-33b, 34a]_END

B_3_C_43_21
BEGIN_
एवम् सीता वचः श्रुत्वा दृष्ट्वा च मृगम् अद्भुतम् || ३-४३-२३लोबितः तेन रूपेण सीताया च प्रचोदितः |
उवाच राघवो हृष्टो भ्रातरम् लक्ष्मणम् वचः || ३-४३-२४_END
BEGIN_
In this way, hearing the words of Seetha and observing that wondrous deer Raghava is also amused by 
its form, and even motivated by Seetha in fetching it, he delightedly spoke this word to his brother 
Lakshmana. [3-43-23b, 24]_END

B_3_C_44_15
BEGIN_
तम् दृष्ट्वा पतितम् भूमौ राक्षसम् भीम दर्शनम् || ३-४४-२१
रामो रुधिर सिक्त अंगम् चेष्टमानम् महीतले |
जगाम मनसा सीताम् लक्ष्मणस्य वचः स्मरन् || ३-४४-२२_END
BEGIN_
On seeing that demon with a fiendish look, who has fallen to earth with limbs
steeped in blood, and who is weltering on the surface of earth, Rama emotionally took flight to
Seetha reminiscing Lakshmana's words. [3-44-21b, 22]_END

B_3_C_42_32
BEGIN_
स च ताम् राम दयिताम् पश्यन् मायामयो मृगः || ३-४२-३४
विचचार ततः तत्र दीपयन् इव तत् वनम् |_END
BEGIN_
On seeing Rama's wife Seetha that highly phantasmal deer too then moved there about
as though to scintillate that woodland. [3-42-34b, 35a]_END

B_3_C_45_4
BEGIN_
सौमित्रे मित्र रूपेण भ्रातुः त्वम् असि शत्रुवत् || ३-४५-५यः त्वम् अस्याम् अवस्थायाम् भ्रातरम् न 
अभिपद्यसे |_END
BEGIN_
"You are like a foe of your brother in friend's mien, Soumitri, as you are not making a move towards 
a brother even if he is in an emergency. [3-45-5b, 6a]_END

B_3_C_43_22
BEGIN_
पश्य लक्ष्मण वैदेह्याः स्पृहाम् उल्लसिताम् इमाम् |रूप श्रेष्ठतया हि एष मृगो अद्य न भविष्यति || ३-४३-२५
न वने नंदनोद्देशे न चैत्ररथ संश्रये |कुतः पृथिव्याम् सौमित्रे यो अस्य कश्चित् समो मृगः || ३-४३-२६_END
BEGIN_
"Lakshmana, behold this enthusiastic delight of Vaidehi. Oh, Soumitri, presently no other deer indeed 
with such an excellent form exists in this forest. Or else, does it exist in Nandana Gardens of Indra 
- no, it cannot be there; in the adjoins of Caitraratha Gardens of Kubera - no, it will not be there, 
then how can there be some deer on earth which is similar to this! [3-43-25, 26]_END

B_3_C_44_16
BEGIN_
मारीचस्य तु माय एषा पूर्व उक्तम् लक्ष्मणेन तु |
तत् तदा हि अभवत् च अद्य मारीचो अयम् मया हतः || ३-४४-२३_END
BEGIN_
"This is the trickery of Maareecha which Lakshmana vouchsafed earlier, that has
indeed happened in that way alone, and the one whom I have killed now is none other than Maareecha.
[3-44-23]_END

B_3_C_42_33
BEGIN_
अदृष्ट पूर्वम् दृष्ट्वा तम् नाना रत्नमयम् मृगम् |
विस्मयम् परमम् सीता जगाम जनक आत्मजा || ३-४२-३५_END
BEGIN_
To see such a deer which is hitherto unseen, and which is as though studded with
numerous gems, the daughter of Janaka, Seetha, went in to an intense wonderment. [3-42-35b, c]_END

B_3_C_45_5
BEGIN_
इच्छसि त्वम् विनश्यन्तम् रामम् लक्ष्मण मत् कृते || ३-४५-६लोभात् तु मत् कृतम् नूनम् न अनुगच्छसि राघवम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Because of me you wish Rama to be completely destroyed, and only because of your cupidity for me you 
are not following up on Raghava. It is definite. [3-45-6b, 7a]_END

B_3_C_43_23
BEGIN_
प्रतिलोम अनुलोमाः च रुचिरा रोम राजयः |शोभन्ते मृगम् आश्रित्य चित्राः कनक बिन्दुभिः || ३-४३-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Amazing are its hairlines with hair upturned at some places and down-turned at other, and the golden 
spots embedded on the coat of the deer are glittery. [3-43-27]_END

B_3_C_44_17
BEGIN_
हा सीते लक्ष्मण इति एवम् आक्रुश्य तु महा स्वनम् |
ममार राक्षसः सो अयम् श्रुत्वा सीता कथम् भवेत् || ३-४४-२४
लक्ष्मणः च महाबाहुः काम् अवस्थाम् गमिष्यति |
इति संचिन्त्य धर्माअत्मा रामो हृष्ट तनू रुहः || ३-४४-२५_END
BEGIN_
"This demon died while crying out with a blatant voice 'ha, Seetha... ha,
Lakshmana...' And on hearing this how Seetha will be? And what will be the plight of dextrous
Lakshmana?" Thus on thinking over them that righteous-souled Rama remained in a hair-raising
predicament. [3-44-24]_END

B_3_C_45_6
BEGIN_
व्यसनम् ते प्रियम् मन्ये स्नेहो भ्रातरि न अस्ति ते || ३-४५-७तेन तिष्ठसि विस्रब्धः तम् अपश्यन् महाद्युतिम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
" 'Raghava in direst strait' is the most liked thing to you, thus I deem, as you have no heart for that 
brother, and as you complacently stay behind even when that great-resplendent Rama is unseen. [3-45-7b, 
8a]_END

B_3_C_43_24
BEGIN_
पश्य अस्य जृंभमाणस्य दीप्ताम् अग्नि शिखोपमाम् |जिह्वाम् मुखात् निःसरंतीम् मेघात् इव शत ह्रदाम् || 
३-४३-२८_END
BEGIN_
"See at its tongue that is exserting from its mouth while it is yawning, which is similar to the flaring 
tongue of fire and to the lightning from a cloud. [3-43-28]_END

B_3_C_44_18
BEGIN_
तत्र रामम् भयम् तीव्रम् आविवेश विषादजम् |
राक्षसम् मृग रूपम् तम् हत्वा श्रुत्वा च तत् स्वनम् || ३-४४-२६_END
BEGIN_
On killing that demon in the form of Golden Deer, and also on hearing his yelling,
Rama is ensorcelled with a frantic fear caused by his own gloom. [3-44-26]_END

B_3_C_45_7
BEGIN_
किम् हि संशयम् आपन्ने तस्मिन् इह मया भवेत् || ३-४५-८कर्तव्यम् इह तिष्ठन्त्या यत् प्रधानः त्वम् आगतः 
|_END
BEGIN_
"After which helmsman you have come here that Rama is undergoing an uncertainty of life-and-death, as 
such I indeed wonder what business you have here now in staying with me at this hermitage?" Seetha spoke 
so to Lakshmana. [3-45-8, 9a]_END

B_3_C_43_25
BEGIN_
मसार गल्वर्क मुखः शंख मुक्ता निभ उदरः |कस्य नाम अनिरूप्यः असौ न मनो लोभयेत् मृगः || ३-४३-२९_END
BEGIN_
"Its face is like a mug made up of sapphires, its paunch is pearly and conchoidal, and whose heart is 
it that will not lured for this deer with an inexplicable beauty. [3-43-29]_END

B_3_C_46_0
BEGIN_
तया परुषम् उक्तः तु कुपितो राघव अनुजः |स विकांक्षन् भृशम् रामम् प्रतस्थे न चिरात् इव || ३-४६-१_END
BEGIN_
Raghava's younger brother Lakshmana is very much infuriated at Seetha who spoke to him rudely, as such 
he journeyed towards Rama at once as though he is yearning to see Rama immediately, albeit his heart 
wanted him to stand guard to Seetha. [3-46-1]_END

B_3_C_44_19
BEGIN_
निहत्य पृषतम् च अन्यम् मांसम् आदाय राघवः |
त्वरमाणो जनस्थानम् ससार अभिमुखः तदा || ३-४४-२७_END
BEGIN_
Raghava then on killing another spotted deer and on taking its flesh, he hurried
himself towards Janasthaana. [3-44-27]_END

B_3_C_45_8
BEGIN_
एवम् ब्रुवाणम् वैदेहीम् बाष्प शोक समन्वितम् || ३-४५-९अब्रवीत् लक्ष्मणः त्रस्ताम् सीताम् मृग वधूम् 
इव |_END
BEGIN_
Lakshmana spoke to Seetha, the princess from Videha kingdom, who is talking deluged under tears and 
anguish in that way, as she is fretful like a she-deer. [3-45-9a, 10b]_END

B_3_C_43_26
BEGIN_
कस्य रूपम् इदम् दृष्ट्वा जांबूनदमय प्रभम् |नाना रत्नमयम् दिव्यम् न मनो विस्मयम् व्रजेत् || ३-४३-३०_END
BEGIN_
"On seeing at this astounding look of the deer which is golden in glitter and bejewelled numerously 
as it were, whose heart is it that will not be transported into astonishment. [3-43-30]_END

B_3_C_46_1
BEGIN_
तदा आसाद्य दशग्रीवः क्षिप्रम् अंतरम् आस्थितः |अभिचक्राम वैदेहीम् परिव्राजक रूप धृक् || ३-४६-२_END
BEGIN_
Quickly taking hold of intervallic time then the ten-headed Ravana approached Vaidehi adopting an aspect 
of a sanyaasi, a meandering Brahman friar. [3-46-2]_END

B_3_C_45_9
BEGIN_
पन्नग असुर गन्धर्व देव दानव राक्षसैः || ३-४५-१०अशक्यः तव वैदेही भर्ता जेतुम् न संशयः |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Vaidehi, your husband is an impossible one for vincibility by serpents, asura-s, gandharva-s, gods, 
fiends, demons, no doubt about it._END

B_3_C_43_27
BEGIN_
मांस हेतोः अपि मृगान् विहारार्थम् च धन्विनः |घ्नन्ति लक्ष्मण राजानो मृगयायाम् महावने || ३-४३-३१_END
BEGIN_
"Kings pursuing games of hunting in great forests, oh, Lakshmana, will be felling deer either for the 
sake of flesh, or just for the purpose of sporting archery. [3-43-31]_END

B_3_C_46_2
BEGIN_
श्लक्ष्ण काषाय संवीतः शिखी चत्री उपानही |वामे च अंसे अवसज्य अथ शुभे यष्टि कमण्डलू || ३-४६-३परिव्राजक 
रूपेण वैदेहीम् अन्ववर्तत |_END
BEGIN_
That sanyaasi is now cloaked in smooth silky saffron, his head-hair is neatly tufted, sandals are wooden, 
umbrella is on right shoulder, and on his left shoulder a shaft of sanyaasi is shouldered, onto which 
his handy water vessel is hooked, and he proceeded towards Vaidehi in a mien of meandering sanyaasi. 
[3-46-3, 4a]_END

B_3_C_45_10
BEGIN_
देवि देव मनुष्येषु गन्धर्वेषु पतत्रिषु || ३-४५-११राक्षसेषु पिशाचेषु किन्नरेषु मृगेषु च |दानवेषु 
च घोरेषु न स विद्येत शोभने || ३-४५-१२यो रामम् प्रतियुध्येत समरे वासव उपमम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, auspicious one, unmarked is some combatant who can counterattack Rama from among gods, humans, 
gandharva-s, birds, ogres, kinnaraa-s, beasts, or oh, lady, even from horrendous demons, as Rama vies 
with Indra in any given war. [3-45-11b, 12, 13a]_END

B_3_C_43_28
BEGIN_
धनानि व्यवसायेन विचीयन्ते महावने |धातवो विविधाः च अपि मणि रत्न सुवर्णिनः || ३-४३-३२_END
BEGIN_
"And exerting themselves in great forests they by far amass forest produce, ores, jewels, gemstones 
and the gravel of gold. [3-43-32]_END

B_3_C_46_3
BEGIN_
ताम् आससाद अतिबलो भ्रातृभ्याम् रहिताम् वने || ३-४६-४रहिताम् सूर्य चन्द्राभ्याम् संध्याम् इव महत् 
तमः |_END
BEGIN_
As with a pitchiest gloom overcoming the sunless and moonless lively eventide, that great-mighty Ravana 
came over to Vaidehi in that forest, when she is without two of the brothers, namely Rama and Lakshmana. 
[3-46-4b, 5a]_END

B_3_C_45_11
BEGIN_
अवध्यः समरे रामो न एवम् त्वम् वक्तुम् अर्हसि || ३-४५-१३न त्वाम् अस्मिन् वने हातुम् उत्सहे राघवम् 
विना |_END
BEGIN_
"It is inapt of you to talk that way as Rama is inextirpable in a given war, and as for me, I do not 
venture to abandon you in this forest in the absence of Raghava. [3-45-13b, 14a]_END

B_3_C_43_29
BEGIN_
तत् सारम् अखिलम् नॄणाम् धनम् निचय वर्धनम् |मनसा चिन्तितम् सर्वम् यथा शुक्रस्य लक्ष्मण || ३-४३-३३_END
BEGIN_
"Everything of that wealth from forest produce will be filling the treasuries of kings, like the speculated 
objects filling the entire treasury of Shukra just by his thinking of them in his mind. [3-43-33]_END

B_3_C_46_4
BEGIN_
ताम् अपश्यत् ततो बालाम् राज पुत्रीम् यशस्विनीम् || ३-४६-५रोहिणीम् शशिना हीनाम् ग्रहवत् भृश दारुणः 
|_END
BEGIN_
As a sinister planet looks over Star Rohini when she is devoid of Moon, that extremely sinister Ravana 
then looked over the glorious and youthful princess Seetha. [3-46-5b, 6a]_END

B_3_C_45_12
BEGIN_
अनिवार्यम् बलम् तस्य बलैः बलवताम् अपि || ३-४५-१४त्रिभिः लोकैः समुदितैः स ईश्वरैः स अमरैः अपि |_END
BEGIN_
"Let the most forceful Crowns with all their military forces, or, all of the gods together with their 
heads, why they, let all the three worlds put together come mutinously, whether jointly or severally, 
Rama's prowess is irrestrainable. [3-45, 14b, 15a]_END

B_3_C_43_30
BEGIN_
अर्थी येन अर्थ कृत्येन संव्रजति अविचारयन् |तम् अर्थम् अर्थ शास्त्रज्ञः प्राहुः अर्थ्याः च लक्ष्मण 
|| ३-४३-३४_END
BEGIN_
"The financial experts and the other financially well-off people say that with which aspirational activity 
an aspirant unhesitatingly scurries and achieves it, that achieved target alone is lauded to be worthwhile, 
or, as real wealth. [3-43-34]_END

B_3_C_46_5
BEGIN_
तम् उग्रम् पाप कर्माणम् जनस्थान गता द्रुमाः || ३-४६-६संदृश्य न प्रकंपन्ते न प्रवाति च मारुतः |_END
BEGIN_
On observing ferocious Ravana whose activities are iniquitous, the trees of Janasthaana are not in full 
sway, nor the wind is in full swing. [3-46-6b, 7a]_END

B_3_C_45_13
BEGIN_
हृदयम् निर्वृतम् ते अस्तु संतापः त्यज्यताम् तव || ३-४५-१५आगमिष्यति ते भर्ता शीघ्रम् हत्वा मृगोत्तमम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Hence, let your heart be diverted and anxiety divested, as your husband will be returning soon on killing 
that extraordinary deer. [3-45-15b, 16a]_END

B_3_C_43_31
BEGIN_
एतस्य मृग रत्नस्य परार्ध्ये कांचन त्वचि |उपवेक्ष्यति वैदेही मया सह सुमध्यमा || ३-४३-३५_END
BEGIN_
"This comely Vaidehi will be sitting on that invaluable golden skin of that gem of a deer along with 
me. [3-43-35]_END

B_3_C_46_6
BEGIN_
शीघ्र स्रोताः च तम् दृष्ट्वा वीक्षंतम् रक्त लोचनम् || ३-४६-७स्तिमितम् गंतुम् आरेभे भयात् गोदावरी 
नदी |_END
BEGIN_
On seeing him who is seeing with his bloodshot eyes, River Godavari too is frightened and started to 
rush off quietly, whose onrush will be rapid otherwise. [3-46-7b, 8a]_END

B_3_C_45_14
BEGIN_
न सस् तस्य स्वरो व्यक्तम् न कश्चित् अपि दैवतः || ३-४५-१६गन्धर्व नगर प्रख्या माया तस्य च रक्षसः |_END
BEGIN_
"Evidently it is not the voice of Rama, nor that of any other god, but someone mimicked that voice for 
chicanery, and that must be the illusory voice of that demon Maareecha, similar in effect to the magical 
city of gandharva-s usually created by magicians in general. [3-45-15b, 16]_END

B_3_C_43_32
BEGIN_
न कादली न प्रियकी न प्रवेणी न च अविकी |भवेत् एतस्य सदृशी स्पर्शनेन इति मे मतिः || ३-४३-३६_END
BEGIN_
"I think the skin of Kadali deer, or of Priyaki deer, or of Praveni deer, or as a matter of fact the 
skins of best breed of deer or sheep will not be match to the deerskin of this deer, insofar as the 
soft-touch is concerned. [3-43-36]_END

B_3_C_46_7
BEGIN_
रामस्य तु अंतरम् प्रेप्सुः दशग्रीवः तत् अंतरे || ३-४६-८उपतस्थे च वैदेहीम् भिक्षु रूपेण रावणः |_END
BEGIN_
In the meanwhile the Decahedron demon Ravana, who is all the while waiting for some lapse of Rama, neared 
Vaidehi in the getup of a sanyaasi. [3-46-8b, 9a]_END

B_3_C_45_15
BEGIN_
न्यास भूता असि वैदेहि न्यस्ता मयि महात्मना || ३-४५-१७रामेण त्वम् वरारोहे न त्वाम् त्यक्तुम् इह उत्सहे 
|_END
BEGIN_
"And you are an entrustment, oh, best lady Vaidehi, as the great-souled Rama has entrusted you in my 
security, as such I do not dare to leave you off now. [3-45-17, 18a]_END

B_3_C_43_33
BEGIN_
एष चैव मृगः श्रीमान् यः च दिव्यो नभः चरः |उभौ एतौ मृगौ दिव्यौ तारामृग महीमृगौ || ३-४३-३७_END
BEGIN_
"Only two divine deer are there, this magnificent deer on earth, and the other that moves in skies remaining 
in stellar region. [3-43-37]_END

B_3_C_46_8
BEGIN_
अभव्यो भव्य रूपेण भर्तारम् अनुशोचतीम् || ३-४६-९अभ्यवर्तत वैदेहीम् चित्राम् इव शनैश्चरः |_END
BEGIN_
That disgraceful Ravana made advances in a graceful mien of Brahman almsman to Vaidehi who is thinking 
over her husband, like the slow moving Saturn making advance to Star Citra which will be ominous. [3-46-9b, 
10a]_END

B_3_C_45_16
BEGIN_
कृत वैराः च कल्याणि वयम् एतैः निशाचरैः || ३-४५-१८खरस्य निधने देवि जनस्थान वधम् प्रति |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, gracious lady, we have become the adversaries of these night-walkers insofar as the elimination 
of Khara and others, and concerning the eradication of Janasthaana. [3-45-18b, 19a]_END

B_3_C_43_34
BEGIN_
यदि वा अयम् तथा यत् माम् भवेत् वदसि लक्ष्मण |माया एषा राक्षसस्य इति कर्तव्यो अस्य वधो मया || ३-४३-३८_END
BEGIN_
"You are telling me that 'this is the wizardry of the demon.' Even then, Lakshmana, if this results 
in that way as a demon's wizardry, my duty also results in the elimination of that deer. [3-43-38]_END

B_3_C_46_9
BEGIN_
सहसा भव्य रूपेण तृणैः कूप इव आवृतः || ३-४६-१०अतिष्ठत् प्रेक्ष्य वैदेहीम् राम पत्नीम् यशस्विनीम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
Like a wellspring shrouded by grass, enshrouded in a decent getup of a Brahman friar, in a trice Ravana 
leeringly stood before of Vaidehi, the admirable wife of Rama. [3-46-10b, 11a]_END

B_3_C_45_17
BEGIN_
राक्षसा विविधा वाचो व्यवहरन्ति महावने || ३-४५-१९हिंसा विहारा वैदेहि न चिन्तयितुम् अर्हसि |_END
BEGIN_
"The demons are the swaggerers in violence in great forests and they will be employing various voices. 
Therefore Vaidehi, just do not bother about it." Thus Lakshmana advised Seetha. [3-45-18b, 19, 20a]_END

B_3_C_43_35
BEGIN_
एतेन हि नृशंसेन मारीचेन अकृत आत्मना |वने विचरता पूर्वम् हिंसिता मुनि पुंगवाः || ३-४३-३९_END
BEGIN_
"If this deer is Maareecha, this heinous and vicious-souled demon has indeed tortured many eminent sages 
earlier when was on the prowl in the forests, thus he is eliminable. [3-43-39]_END

B_3_C_46_10
BEGIN_
तिष्टन् संप्रेक्ष्य च तदा पत्नीम् रामस्य रावण || ३-४६-११शुभाम् रुचिर दन्त ओष्ठीम् पूर्ण चन्द्र निभ 
आननाम् |आसीनाम् पर्णशालायाम् बाष्प शोक अभिपीडिताम् || ३-४६-१२स ताम् पद्म पलाश अक्षीम् पीत कौशेय 
वासिनीम् |अभ्यगच्छत वैदेहीम् हृष्ट चेता निशा चरः || ३-४६-१३_END
BEGIN_
While standing before her then Ravana eyed at the auspicious wife of Rama, whose lips and teeth are 
fine, visage is shiny like a full moon, and who is presently tortured by her tearful lamentation and 
sitting in the straw-cottage, and he approached that lotus-petal eyed Vaidehi who is dressed in ochry 
silks, as that night-walker is gladdened at his heart for her solitude. [3-46-11b, 12,13]_END

B_3_C_45_18
BEGIN_
लक्ष्मणेन एवम् उक्ता तु क्रुद्धा संरक्त लोचना || ३-४५-२०अब्रवीत् परुषम् वाक्यम् लक्ष्मणम् सत्य वादिनम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
As for Seetha, she became furious on hearing Lakshmana's words of advice, and while her eyes are becoming 
bloodshot she spoke these rude sentences to that veracious Lakshmana. [3-45-20b, 21a]_END

B_3_C_43_36
BEGIN_
उत्थाय बहवो अनेन मृगयायाम् जनाधिपाः |निहताः परम इष्वासाः तस्मात् वध्यः तु अयम् मृगः || ३-४३-४०_END
BEGIN_
"He rebelliously killed many kings who are excellent archers while they were in hunting games, at least 
for that reason this bestial monster is eradicable. [3-43-40]_END

B_3_C_46_11
BEGIN_
दृष्ट्वा काम शर आविद्धो ब्रह्म घोषम् उदीरयन् |अब्रवीत् प्रश्रितम् वाक्यम् रहिते राक्षस अधिपः || 
३-४६-१४_END
BEGIN_
He who is hit by the arrows of Love-god that king of demons Ravana, on seeing Seetha entered resonating 
the resonances of Vedic-hymns as precursory in seeking alms, and spoke these well-mannered sentences 
to her who is in solitariness. [3-46-14]_END

B_3_C_45_19
BEGIN_
अनार्य करुणारंभ नृशंस कुल पांसन || ३-४५-२१अहम् तव प्रियम् मन्ये रामस्य व्यसनम् महत् |_END
BEGIN_
"You are a debased one devoid of mercy, thus a dreadful one, and a degrader of your dynasty, and I deem 
that you derive pleasure from fatal hardship to Rama. [3-45-21b, 22a]_END

B_3_C_46_12
BEGIN_
ताम् उत्तमाम् त्रिलोकानाम् पद्म हीनाम् इव श्रियम् |विभ्राजमानाम् वपुषा रावणः प्रशशंस ह || ३-४६-१५_END
BEGIN_
Ravana really acclaimed her who is an excellent one in all the three worlds, beaming forth with the 
beauty of her body, and who is like Goddess Lakshmi but for Divine-lotus as Her settle, for Seetha is 
devoid of her settling, namely Rama. [3-46-15]_END

B_3_C_43_37
BEGIN_
पुरस्तात् इह वातापिः परिभूय तपस्विनः |उदरस्थो द्विजान् हन्ति स्व गर्भो अश्वतरीम् इव || ३-४३-४१_END
BEGIN_
"Demon Vaataapi who held ascetics in contempt was here earlier, and staying in the stomachs of Brahmans 
he used to come out by ripping their stomachs open and thus he was killing Brahmans, like a mare-calf 
killing its own mother at its time of birth by ripping the womb of its own mother. [3-43-41]_END

B_3_C_45_20
BEGIN_
रामस्य व्यसन्म् दृष्ट्वा तेन एतानि प्रभाषसे || ३-४५-२२न एव चित्रम् सपत्नेषु पापम् लक्ष्मण यत् भवेत् 
|त्वत् विधेषु नृशंसेषु नित्यम् प्रच्छन्न चारिषु || ३-४५-२३_END
BEGIN_
"You are haranguing all these sermons only on noticing hardship to Rama. It is unsurprising that the 
pitiless ones and rivals of your kind, who always behave in a cloak-and dagger way, will tend to commit 
deadly sins, Lakshmana, and it is not uncommon. [3-45-22b, 23]_END

B_3_C_46_13
BEGIN_
का त्वम् कांचन वर्ण आभे पीत कौशेय वासिनि |कमलानाम् शुभाम् मालाम् पद्मिनी इव च बिभ्रती || ३-४६-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Glittering like the glitter of gold, silkened in ochry silks, you are like a lotus-tendril garlanded 
with divine lotuses as your ensemble, who are you?" Thus Ravanan started addressing Seetha [3-46-16]_END

B_3_C_43_38
BEGIN_
स कदाचित् चिरात् लोभात् आससाद महामुनिम् |अगस्त्यम् तेजसा युक्तम् भक्ष्यः तस्य बभूव ह || ३-४३-४२_END
BEGIN_
"On one occasion after some time, that Vaataapi avariciously obtained that great-saint and the one who 
is endowed with effulgent, namely Agastya, as an eatable, but actually that demon has became an eatable 
to the sage. [3-43-42]_END

B_3_C_47_0
BEGIN_
रावणेन तु वैदेही तदा पृष्टा जिहीर्षुणा |परिव्राजक रूपेण शशंस आत्मानम् आत्मना || ३-४७-१_END
BEGIN_
When Ravana whose intention is to abduct her has enquired thus, then on the basis of his Brahman friar's 
mien Seetha informed about herself on her own. [3-47-1]_END

B_3_C_45_21
BEGIN_
सुदुष्टः त्वम् वने रामम् एकम् एको अनुगच्छसि |मम हेतोः प्रतिच्छन्नः प्रयुक्तो भरतेन वा || ३-४५-२४_END
BEGIN_
"You are verily maleficent for you have singly and covertly followed Rama, who started to forests all 
alone, or instigated by Bharata, only because of me. [3-45-24]_END

B_3_C_46_14
BEGIN_
ह्रीः श्रीः कीर्तिः शुभा लक्ष्मीः अप्सरा वा शुभ आनने |भूतिर् वा त्वम् वराअरोहे रतिर् वा स्वैर चारिणी 
|| ३-४६-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, rosy faced one, are you the personified numen of Respect, Renown or Resplendence, or the Felicitous 
Lakshmi herself, or oh, curvaceous one, are you a nymphal Apsara, or the numen of Benefactress, or a 
self-motivated woman, or Rati Devi, the consort of Manmatha, the Love God. [3-46-17]_END

B_3_C_43_39
BEGIN_
समुत्थाने च तत् रूपम् कर्तु कामम् समीक्ष्य तम् |उत्स्मयित्वा तु भगवान् वातापिम् इदम् अब्रवीत् || 
३-४३-४३_END
BEGIN_
"On observing the demon Vaataapi who is trying to assume his original form of demon in order to come 
out of his stomach, that godly saint Agastya spoke this to Vaataapi with a scornful smile. [3-43-43]_END

B_3_C_47_1
BEGIN_
ब्राह्मणः च अतिथिः च एष अनुक्तो हि शपेत माम् |इति ध्यात्वा मुहूर्तम् तु सीता वचनम् अब्रवीत् || ३-४७-२_END
BEGIN_
Thinking briefly that, 'he is a Brahman and an untimely guest, he will indeed curse me if he is not 
replied,' Seetha spoke this sentence. [3-47-2]_END

B_3_C_45_22
BEGIN_
तत् न सिद्ध्यति सौमित्रे तव अपि भरतस्य वा |कथम् इंदीवर श्यामम् रामम् पद्म निभेक्षणम् || ३-४५-२५
उपसंश्रित्य भर्तारम् कामयेयम् पृथक् जनम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Whether this is an intrigue of yours or that of Bharata it is unachievable, Saumitri. How can I long 
for another commoner when I have put my faith only in the lotus-blue-complexioned and lotus-bright-eyed 
husband of mine, Rama? [3-45-25, 26a]_END

B_3_C_46_15
BEGIN_
समाः शिखरिणः स्निग्धाः पाण्डुरा दशनाः तव |विशाले विमले नेत्रे रक्तान्ते कृष्ण तारके || ३-४६-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Your teeth are evenly, smooth and their tips are like jasmine buds, and your whitish broad eyes are 
spotless, reddish at ends, and pupils are black. [3-46-18]_END

B_3_C_43_40
BEGIN_
त्वया अविगण्य वातापे परिभूताः च तेजसा |जीव लोके द्विज श्रेष्ठाः तस्मात् असि जराम् गतः || ३-४३-४४_END
BEGIN_
" 'Oh, Vaataapi, you have irreverently eradicated the best Brahmans in this world owing to your might, 
therefore I have assimilated you.' So said sage Agastya to Vaataapi. [3-43-44]_END

B_3_C_47_2
BEGIN_
दुहिता जनकस्य अहम् मैथिलस्य महात्मनः |सीता नाम्ना अस्मि भद्रम् ते रामस्य महिषी प्रिया || ३-४७-३_END
BEGIN_
"I am the daughter of noble-souled Janaka, the king of Mithila, by name I am Seetha, and the dear wife 
and queen of Rama, let safety betide you. [3-47-3]_END

B_3_C_45_23
BEGIN_
समक्षम् तव सौमित्रे प्राणान् त्यक्ष्यामि असंशयम् || ४-५-२६रामम् विना क्षणम् अपि न एव जीवामि भू तले 
|_END
BEGIN_
"If that comes to that, I will just discard my life in your presence, Soumitri do not mistake it. I 
do not eke out an existence on this earth even for a moment without Rama." Thus Seetha threatened Lakshmana. 
[3-45-26b, 27a]_END

B_3_C_46_16
BEGIN_
विशालम् जघनम् पीनम् ऊरू करि कर उपमौ |एतौ उपचितौ वृत्तौ संहतौ संप्रगल्भितौ || ३-४६-१९पीन उन्नत 
मुखौ कान्तौ स्निग्ध ताल फल उपमौ |मणि प्रवेक आभरणौ रुचिरौ ते पयो धरौ || ३-४६-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Your hips are beamy, thighs burly akin to elephant's trunks, and these two breasts of yours that are 
ornamented with best jewellery are rotund, rubbing and bumping each other, and they are swinging up 
and up, their nipples are brawny and jutting out, and they are smoothish like palm-fruits, thus they 
are covetable for they are beautiful. [3-46-19, 20]_END

B_3_C_43_41
BEGIN_
तत् एतत् न भवेत् रक्षो वातापिः इव लक्ष्मण |मत् विधम् यो अतिमन्येत धर्म नित्यम् जितेन्द्रियम् || 
३-४३-४५भवेत् हतो अयम् वातापिः अगस्त्येन इव मा गतः |_END
BEGIN_
"Lakshmana, such a demon who is like Vaataapi will not be there any more. He who disregards someone 
of my kind, who always abides in righteousness and who is self-controlled, such a demon will be eliminated 
as sage Agastya has eliminated demon Vaataapi, if that demon happens to get at me. [3-43-45, 46a]_END

B_3_C_47_3
BEGIN_
उषित्वा द्वा दश समाः इक्ष्वाकूणाम् निवेशने |भुंजाना मानुषान् भोगान् सर्व काम समृद्धिनी || ३-४७-४_END
BEGIN_
"On residing in the residence of Ikshvaku-s in Ayodhya for twelve years, I was in sumptuosity of all 
cherishes while relishing all humanly prosperities. [3-47-4]_END

B_3_C_45_24
BEGIN_
इति उक्तः परुषम् वाक्यम् सीतया रोमहर्षणम् || ३-४५-२७अब्रवीत् लक्ष्मणः सीताम् प्रांजलिः विजितेन्द्रियः 
|_END
BEGIN_
When that self-mortified Lakshmana is addressed in this way with hair-raising and acerbic words by Seetha, 
he spoke to her suppliantly adjoining his palm-fold. [3-45-27b, 28a]_END

B_3_C_46_17
BEGIN_
चारु स्मिते चारु दति चारु नेत्रे विलासिनि |मनो हरसि मे रामे नदी कूलम् इव अंभसा || ३-४६-२१करान्तमित 
मध्या असि सुकेशी संहत स्तनी |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, allurer, your smile is alluring, teeth are alluring, and your eyes allure, oh, beauty, your waist 
is palmful, your hair velvety, your breasts are jostling, and you rob my soul as a spate robs riverbank. 
[3-46-21, 22a]_END

B_3_C_43_42
BEGIN_
इह त्वम् भव संनद्धो यंत्रितो रक्ष मैथिलीम् || ३-४३-४६अस्याम् आयत्तम् अस्माकम् यत् कृत्यम् रघुनंदन 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Lakshmana, the descendent of Raghu, you stay here in all preparedness and guard Maithili steadfastly, 
whatever enterprise of ours is there that is founded in her. [3-43-46b, 47a]_END

B_3_C_47_4
BEGIN_
तत्र त्रयो दशे वर्षे राज अमंत्र्यत प्रभुः |अभिषेचयितुम् रामम् समेतो राज मन्त्रिभिः || ३-४७-५_END
BEGIN_
"In the thirteenth year the lordly king Dasharatha deliberated together with his imperial ministers 
to anoint Rama as Crown Prince of Ayodhya. [3-47-5]_END

B_3_C_45_25
BEGIN_
उत्तरम् न उत्सहे वक्तुम् दैवतम् भवती मम || ३-४५-२८वाक्यम् अप्रतिरूपम् तु न चित्रम् स्त्रीषु मैथिलि 
|स्वभावः तु एष नारीणाम् एषु लोकेषु दृश्यते || ३-४५-२९_END
BEGIN_
"I do not venture to reply you Maithili, as you are like a deity to me. Women using words that are in 
a class by themselves is not at all surprising. This sort of bringing stilted words into play is the 
nature of women and it is obvious in the world. [3-45-28b, 29]_END

B_3_C_46_18
BEGIN_
न एव देवी न गन्धर्वी न यक्षी न च किंनरी || ३-४६-२२न एवम् रूपा मया नारी दृष्ट पूर्वा मही तले |_END
BEGIN_
"I have not hitherto seen any earthly female with this kind of features on the face of earth; or, a 
goddess - no; a gandharva female - no; yaksha female - no; kinnaraa female - no, none whosoever! [3-46-22b, 
23a]_END

B_3_C_43_43
BEGIN_
अहम् एनम् वधिष्यामि ग्रहीष्यामि अथवा मृगम् || ३-४३-४७यावत् गच्छामि सौमित्रे मृगम् आनयितुम् द्रुतम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
"I wish to catch this deer, Soumitri, if not I will kill it, and I will be going forthwith to fetch 
the deer. [3-43-47b, 48a]_END

B_3_C_47_5
BEGIN_
तस्मिन् संभ्रियमाणे तु राघवस्य अभिषेचने |कैकेयी नाम भर्तारम् मम आर्या याचते वरम् || ३-४७-६_END
BEGIN_
"When Raghava's anointment was being organised my venerable mother-in-law known as Kaikeyi begged her 
husband Dasharatha for a boon. [3-47-6]_END

B_3_C_48_0
BEGIN_
एवम् ब्रुवत्याम् सीतायाम् संरब्धः परुष अक्षरम् |ललाटे भ्रुकुटीम् कृत्वा रावणः प्रति उवाच ह || ३-४८-१_END
BEGIN_
When Seetha spoke thus Ravana is embittered, and knitting his eyebrows he indeed spoke these rudish 
words to Seetha. [3-48-1]_END

B_3_C_45_26
BEGIN_
विमुक्त धर्माः चपलाः तीक्ष्णा भेदकराः स्त्रियः |न सहे हि ईदृशम् वाक्यम् वैदेही जनक आत्मजे || ३-४५-३०
श्रोत्रयोः उभयोः मध्ये तप्त नाराच सन्निभम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Women by their nature are unbound by the etiquette of decency, whimsical, cantankerous and they tend 
to become the artificers of vicissitudes, and oh, Vaidehi, the daughter of Janaka, indeed unbearable 
are this kind of words that are much the same as burnt iron arrows thrust in between my two ears. [3-45-30, 
31a]_END

B_3_C_46_19
BEGIN_
रूपम् अग्र्यम् च लोकेषु सौकुमार्यम् वयः च ते || ३-४६-२३इह वासः च कांतारे चित्तम् उन्मथयन्ति मे |_END
BEGIN_
"I marvel why an excellent one in all the three worlds by her features, more so, fragile and youthful 
as yourself should be living here in the thick of forest. [3-46-23b, 24, 25a]_END

B_3_C_43_44
BEGIN_
पश्य लक्ष्मण वैदेहीम् मृग त्वचि गताम् स्पृहाम् || ३-४३-४८त्वचा प्रधानया हि एष मृगो अद्य न भविष्यति 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Lakshmana, see how Vaidehi's percept is overtaken by deerskin. Indeed by the strangeness of its skin 
that deer must be a mysterious being, hence, it will not survive now. [3-43-48]_END

B_3_C_47_6
BEGIN_
प्रतिगृह्य तु कैकेयी श्वशुरम् सुकृतेन मे |मम प्रव्राजनम् भर्तुर् भरतस्य अभिषेचनम् || ३-४७-७द्वौ 
अयाचत भर्तारम् सत्यसंधम् नृपोत्तमम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Restraining my veracious father-in-law by a good deed once done by her in his respect, Kaikeyi besought 
two boons from him, namely expatriation of my husband, and anointment of her son Bharata. [3-47-7, 8a]_END

B_3_C_48_1
BEGIN_
भ्राता वैश्रवणस्य अहम् सापत्नो वरवर्णिनि |रावणो नाम भद्रम् ते दशग्रीवः प्रतापवान् || ३-४८-२_END
BEGIN_
"I am known as Ravana, oh, lady with superb complexion, let safety betide you, the highly valorous and 
ten-headed stepbrother of Kubera. [3-48-2]_END

B_3_C_45_27
BEGIN_
उपशृण्वंतु मे सर्वे साक्षिनो हि वनेचराः || ३-४५-३१न्याय वादी यथा वाक्यम् उक्तो अहम् परुषम् त्वया 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Let all of the forest-itinerants indeed listen as to how you are addressing me with bitter words, though 
I am reasoning with you conscientiously, and let them become my corroborators for the sake of justice. 
[3-45-31b, 32a]_END

B_3_C_46_20
BEGIN_
सा प्रतिक्राम भद्रम् ते न त्वम् वस्तुम् इह अर्हसि || ३-४६-२४राक्षसानाम् अयम् वासो घोराणाम् काम रूपिणाम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
Such as you are you go back, let safety betide you, as you are unsuited to live in here, for this forest 
is the dwelling for ghastly demons who by their wish will be changing their guise. [3-46-24b, 25a]_END

B_3_C_43_45
BEGIN_
अप्रमत्तेन ते भाव्यम् आश्रमस्थेन सीतया || ३-४३-४९यावत् पृषतम् एकेन सायकेन निहन्मि अहम् |हत्वा 
एतत् चर्म च आदाय शीघ्रम् एष्यामि लक्ष्मण || ३-४३-५०_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Lakshmana, apply yourself vigilantly while staying in hermitage along with Seetha. So soon as I 
go I will be felling that spotted deer with one arrow and returning quickly. [3-43-49b, 50]_END

B_3_C_47_7
BEGIN_
न अद्य भोक्ष्ये न च स्वप्स्ये न पास्ये कदाचन || ३-४७-८एष मे जीवितस्य अन्तो रामो यदि अभिषिच्यते |
इति ब्रुवाणाम् कैकेयीम् श्वशुरो मे स पार्थिवः || ३-४७-९अयाचत अर्थैः अन्वर्थैः न च यांचाम् चकार सा 
|_END
BEGIN_
" 'If Rama is anointed now, come what may I will not eat, sleep, or drink, and my life ends this way,' 
thus Kaikeyi was adamantine, and the king and my father-in-law entreated her who is nagging with meaningful 
riches, but she did not make good on that entreaty. [3-47-8b, 9, 10a]_END

B_3_C_48_2
BEGIN_
यस्य देवाः स गंधर्वाः पिशाच पतग उरगाः |विद्रवन्ति भयात् भीता मृत्योः इव सदा प्रजाः || ३-४८-३_END
BEGIN_
"I am that Ravana at whose sight all the gods together with gandharva-s, evil-spirits, birds and snakes 
will always be frightened and fleeing, as with the people frightened and fleeing from death. [3-48-3]_END

B_3_C_45_28
BEGIN_
धिक् त्वाम् अद्य प्रणश्यन्तीम् यन् माम् एवम् विशंकसे || ३-४५-३२स्त्रीत्वात् दुष्ट स्वभावेन गुरु 
वाक्ये व्यवस्थितम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Fie upon you, you are acrimoniously tempered owing to your faminality, and by which impulsive reason 
you mistrust me who am presently abiding in my brother's order, may God damn you for that crotchety. 
[3-45-32b, 33a]_END

B_3_C_46_21
BEGIN_
प्रासाद अग्राणि रम्याणि नगर उपवनानि च || ३-४६-२५संपन्नानि सुगन्धीनि युक्तानि आचरितुम् त्वया |_END
BEGIN_
"Delightful rooftops of skyscrapers, flourishing and richly fragranced pleasure-gardens of cities alone 
are meetly to you to saunter. [3-46-25b, 26a]_END

B_3_C_47_8
BEGIN_
मम भर्ता महातेजा वयसा पंच विंशकः || ३-४७-१०अष्टा दश हि वर्षाणि मम जन्मनि गण्यते |_END
BEGIN_
"My great-resplendent husband was of twenty-five years of age at that time, and to me eighteen years 
are reckoned up from my birth. [3-47-10b, 11a]_END

B_3_C_43_46
BEGIN_
प्रदक्षिणेन अतिबलेन पक्षिणाजटायुषा बुद्धिमता च लक्ष्मण |भव अप्रमत्तः प्रतिगृह्य मैथिलीम्
प्रति क्षणम् सर्वत एव शन्कितः || ३-४३-५१_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Lakshmana, you be here taking care of Maithili along with the forthright, formidable and fatherly 
bird Jatayu, and be watchful and suspicious from everywhere and every split-second." Thus Rama spoke 
to Lakshmana and started to go after the deer [3-43-51]_END

B_3_C_48_3
BEGIN_
येन वैश्रवणो भ्राता वैमात्रः कारणांतरे |द्वन्द्वम् आसादितः क्रोधात् रणे विक्रम्य निर्जितः || ३-४८-४_END
BEGIN_
"I am that Ravana who when infuriated for some other reason took up a duel with Kubera, his brother 
from stepparent, wherein that Kubera is set up against and completely trounced in a combat. [3-48-4]_END

B_3_C_45_29
BEGIN_
गमिष्ये यत्र काकुत्स्थः स्वस्ति ते अस्तु वरानने || ३-४५-३३रक्षन्तु त्वाम् विशालाक्षि समग्रा वन देवताः 
|_END
BEGIN_
"I am going there where Rama is, oh, lady with best visage, you be blest, and oh, broad-eyed one, let 
all of the forest deities protect you. [3-45-33b, 34a]_END

B_3_C_46_22
BEGIN_
वरम् माल्यम् वरम् गंधम् वरम् वस्त्रम् च शोभने || ३-४६-२६भर्तारम् च वरम् मन्ये त्वत् युक्तम् असितेक्षणे 
|_END
BEGIN_
Oh, beauteous lady, I opine that only best garlands, best scents, best foodstuffs, best clothing are 
meetly to you, oh, lady with black pupils, hence it is meet and right to you to have a best husband._END

B_3_C_47_9
BEGIN_
राम इति प्रथितो लोके सत्यवान् शीलवान् शुचिः || ३-४७-११विशालाक्षो महाबाहुः सर्व भूत हिते रतः |_END
BEGIN_
"Rama - thus he is exalted in the world, an unambiguous, unblemished, unsullied one, and a broad-eyed 
ambidextrous one, who delights in bringing universal welfare, is my husband. [3-47-11b, 12a]_END

B_3_C_48_4
BEGIN_
मत् भय आर्तः परित्यज्य स्वम् अधिष्ठानम् ऋद्धिमत् |कैलासम् पर्वत श्रेष्ठम् अध्यास्ते नर वाहनः || 
३-४८-५_END
BEGIN_
"I am that Ravana by whom Kubera, the god for Wealth-Management whose vehicular transport is handled 
by humans, is tormented fearfully and made to completely abandon his wealthiest place which is presided 
over by him till then, and I am the one who made that Kubera to flee to the excellent Mt. Kailash where 
he is somehow living, because I will not cause any harm on Mt. Kailash as I hold it sacred. [3-48-5]_END

B_3_C_45_30
BEGIN_
निमित्तानि हि घोराणि यानि प्रादुर्भवन्ति मे |अपि त्वाम् सह रामेण पश्येयम् पुनरागतः || ३-४५-३४_END
BEGIN_
"Gauging by those dangerous forebodings that are now bidding fair, can I to see you again along with 
Rama on my return, or not? That I do not know." Thus Lakshmana spoke to Seetha. [3-45-34b, c]_END

B_3_C_46_23
BEGIN_
का त्वम् भवसि रुद्राणाम् मरुताम् वा शुचिस्मिते || ३-४६-२७वसूनाम् वा वराअरोहे देवता प्रतिभासि मे 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, curvaceous lady, who are you? Oh, one with an impeccable smile, do you belong to Rudraa-gods, or 
Marut-gods, or to Vasu-s? To me you are beaming forth like a goddess. [3-46-27b, 28a]_END

B_3_C_47_10
BEGIN_
कामार्तः च महाराजः पिता दशरथः स्वयम् || ३-४७-१२कैकेय्याः प्रिय कामार्थम् तम् रामम् न अभिषेचयत् |_END
BEGIN_
"But Rama's father Dasharatha was lovesick for Kaikeyi and to fulfil her desired aspiration that great 
king did not anoint Rama. [3-47-12b, 13a]_END

B_3_C_48_5
BEGIN_
यस्य तत् पुष्पकम् नाम विमानम् कामगम् शुभम् |वीर्याद् आवर्जितम् भद्रे येन यामि विहायसम् || ३-४८-६_END
BEGIN_
"I am that Ravana, oh, auspicious lady, who just by his valour acquired Kubera's auspicious aircraft 
known as Pushpaka, whose pilotage is just by the wish of its aviator, with which I will be travelling 
in skies. [3-48-6]_END

B_3_C_45_31
BEGIN_
लक्ष्मणेन एवम् उक्ता तु रुदती जनकाअत्मजा |प्रत्युवाच ततो वाक्यम् तीव्रम् बाष्प परिप्लुता || ३-४५-३५_END
BEGIN_
When Lakshmana spoke to that wailful daughter of Janaka, she on her part spoke this curt sentence to 
him, while tears whelmed her to a fault. [3-45-35]_END

B_3_C_46_24
BEGIN_
न इह गच्छंति गंधर्वा न देवा न च किन्नराः || ३-४६-२८राक्षसानाम् अयम् वासः कथम् तु त्वम् इह आगता |_END
BEGIN_
"This is the dwelling-place of demons, and no goddess, nor a gandharva, nor a kinnara can arrive here, 
but how you have come here? [3-46-28b, 29a]_END

B_3_C_47_11
BEGIN_
अभिषेकाय तु पितुः समीपम् रामम् आगतम् || ३-४७-१३कैकेयी मम भर्तारम् इति उवाच द्रुतम् वचः |_END
BEGIN_
"When Rama arrived in the presence of his father, Kaikeyi readily and decidedly spoke these words to 
my husband. [3-47-b, 14a]_END

B_3_C_48_6
BEGIN_
मम संजात रोषस्य मुखम् दृष्ट्वा एव मैथिलि |विद्रवन्ति परित्रस्ताः सुराः शक्र पुरोगमाः || ३-४८-७_END
BEGIN_
"Just by seeing rancour-shot face of mine, oh, Maithili, all the gods will quickly shoot off, even if 
Indra is leading them, then where is the question of their confronting me. [3-48-7]_END

B_3_C_45_32
BEGIN_
गोदावरीम् प्रवेक्ष्यामि हीना रामेण लक्ष्मण |आबन्धिष्ये अथवा त्यक्ष्ये विषमे देहम् आत्मनः || ३-४५-३६_END
BEGIN_
"Without Rama I plunge myself in River Godavari, or else I string up myself, or discard this body of 
mine from heights..." Thus Seetha started to vent out her feelings. [3-45-36]_END

B_3_C_47_12
BEGIN_
तव पित्रा समाज्ञप्तम् मम इदम् शृणु राघव || ३-४७-१४भरताय प्रदातव्यम् इदम् राज्यम् अकण्टकम् |_END
BEGIN_
" 'What your father has proclaimed, oh, Raghava, that may be heard from me. He said, 'let this thornless 
kingdom be accorded to Bharata.' [3-47-14b, 15a]_END

B_3_C_46_25
BEGIN_
इह शाखामृगाः सिंहा द्वीपि व्याघ्र मृगाः तथा || ३-४६-२९ऋक्षाः तरक्षवः कंकाः कथम् तेभ्यो न बिभ्यसे 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Here, simians, lions, leopards, tigers, likewise other predators, bears, tigers, vultures will be moving. 
How you are not frightened from them? [3-46-29b, 30a]_END

B_3_C_48_7
BEGIN_
यत्र तिष्ठामि अहम् तत्र मारुतो वाति शन्कितः |तीव्र अंशुः शिशिर अंशुः च भयात् संपद्यते रविः || ३-४८-८_END
BEGIN_
"Where I will be staying there the Air-god wafts doubtfully, lest his gusts and blasts may hurt me, 
and the Sun also effectuates his singeing sunbeams as cooling moonbeams, lest I may abduct his wife 
Prabha, the Sunshine. [3-48-8]_END

B_3_C_45_33
BEGIN_
पिबामि वा विषम् तीक्ष्णम् प्रवेक्ष्यामि हुताशनम् |न तु अहम् राघवात् अन्यम् कदाअपि पुरुषम् स्पृशे 
|| ३-४५-३७_END
BEGIN_
"I drink deadly poison, or I enter a flaring fire, but I will never touch another man other than Raghava. 
[3-45-37]_END

B_3_C_47_13
BEGIN_
त्वया तु खलु वस्तव्यम् नव वर्षाणि पंच च || ३-४७-१५वने प्रव्रज काकुत्स्थ पितरम् मोचय अनृतात् |_END
BEGIN_
"And you, oh, Kakutstha Rama, indeed have to inhabit the forests for nine plus five years, hence you 
repair to forests and redeem your father from the remorse of perjury.' [3-47-15b, 16a]_END

B_3_C_46_26
BEGIN_
मद अन्वितानाम् घोराणाम् कुंजराणाम् तरस्विनाम् || ३-४६-३०कथम् एका महारण्ये न बिभेषि वराअनने |_END
BEGIN_
"Being alone in this forest, oh, lady with a lovely face, how you are unafraid of horrendous and mighty 
elephants possessed of rut? [3-46-30b, 31a]_END

B_3_C_48_8
BEGIN_
निष्कंप पत्राः तरवो नद्यः च स्तिमित उदकाः |भवन्ति यत्र तत्र अहम् तिष्ठामि च चरामि च || ३-४८-९_END
BEGIN_
"At places where I will be staying or freely moving there the leaves of trees will be less of rustle, 
lest I may wilt them up, and there the gush of water of rivers too will quieten, lest I may dry them 
up. [3-48-9]_END

B_3_C_49_0
BEGIN_
सीताया वचनम् श्रुत्वा दशग्रीवः प्रतापवान् |हस्ते हस्तम् समाहत्य चकार सुमहत् वपुः || ३-४९-१_END
BEGIN_
On hearing Seetha's words that valorous ten-headed Ravana loudly clapped in dissent for once and divulged 
his very mighty body. [3-49-1]_END

B_3_C_47_14
BEGIN_
तथा इति उवाच ताम् रामः कैकेयीम् अकुतो भयः || ३-४७-१६चकार तत् वचः तस्या मम भर्ता दृढ व्रतः |_END
BEGIN_
" 'As an unfearing one from any quarter and as a resolute one in his pledge my husband Rama said 'so 
be it' to Kaikeyi and followed her dictate. [3-47-16b, 17a]_END

B_3_C_45_34
BEGIN_
इति लक्ष्मणम् आश्रुत्य सीता दुह्ख समन्विता |पाणिभ्याम् रुदती दुह्खाद् उदरम् प्रजघान ह || ३-४५-३८_END
BEGIN_
Seetha on declaring to Lakshmana in this way, she who is anguished and weeping bitterly, then started 
to smite her belly with both of her palms in a heightened agony. [3-45-38]_END

B_3_C_46_27
BEGIN_
का असि कस्य कुतः च त्वम् किम् निमित्तम् च दण्डकान् || ३-४६-३१एका चरसि कल्याणि घोरान् राक्षस सेवितान् 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, auspicious lady, who are you? Whose are you? Also from where are you? And being lonely, what for 
you are moving in dreadful Dandaka forest that is adored by demons?" Thus Ravana spoke to Seetha. [3-46-31, 
32b]_END

B_3_C_49_1
BEGIN_
स मैथिलीम् पुनः वाक्यम् बभाषे वाक्य कोविदः |न उन्मत्तया श्रुतौ मन्ये मम वीर्य पराक्रमौ || ३-४९-२_END
BEGIN_
That wordsmith Ravana again spoke these words to Maithili, "Perhaps you have not heard about my valour 
and vanquishes in all your madness for Rama. [3-49-2]_END

B_3_C_48_9
BEGIN_
मम पारे समुद्रस्य लंका नाम पुरी शुभा |संपूर्णा राक्षसैः घोरैः यथा इन्द्रस्य अमरावती || ३-४८-१०_END
BEGIN_
"My magnificent city known as Lanka is there on the other shore of the ocean, plethoric with all kinds 
of amenities, as well as with ghastly demons, which city will be on par with Indra's Amaravati, but 
for meekly gods and meaningless souls. [3-48-10]_END

B_3_C_47_15
BEGIN_
दद्यात् न प्रतिगृह्णीयात् सत्यम् ब्रूयात् न च अनृतम् || ३-४७-१७एतत् ब्राह्मण रामस्य व्रतम् ध्रुवम् 
अनुत्तमम् |_END
BEGIN_
"My husband is evermore a renderer but not a recipient, and forever he speaks truth, and not the untruth, 
least of all. Oh, Brahman, this is the unalterable and unsurpassable vow of Rama. [3-47-17b, 18a]_END

B_3_C_45_35
BEGIN_
ताम् आर्त रूपाम् विमना रुदन्तीम्सौमित्रिः आलोक्य विशाल नेत्राम् |आश्वासयामास न चैव भर्तुः
तम् भ्रातरम् किंचित् उवाच सीता || ३-४५-३९_END
BEGIN_
Observing the agonised aspect of Seetha that cheerless Saumitri started to cheer her up by repeatedly 
informing that her husband Rama will come soon. Even then Seetha has not spoken in the least to the 
brother of her husband, and maintained a silence of antipathy. [3-45-39]_END

B_3_C_46_28
BEGIN_
इति प्रशस्ता वैदेही रावणेन दुरात्मना - महात्मना- || ३-४६-३२द्विजाति वेषेण हि तम् दृष्ट्वा रावणम् 
आगतम् |सर्वैः अतिथि सत्कारैः पूजयामास मैथिली || ३-४६-३३_END
BEGIN_
When the wicked minded Ravana praised her in this way, Vaidehi the princess from Mithila has seen him 
who has arrived in the getup of Brahman and started to revere him with all the respects affordable to 
a casual guest. [3-46-32b, 33]_END

B_3_C_49_2
BEGIN_
उद् वहेयम् भुजाभ्याम् तु मेदिनीम् अंबरे स्थितः |आपिबेयम् समुद्रम् च मृत्युम् हन्याम् रणे स्थितः 
|| ३-४९-३_END
BEGIN_
"Standing on the sky I can lift up the earth with two of my arms, I can completely gulp down any ocean, 
standing in war I can even put the Death to death. [3-49-3]_END

B_3_C_48_10
BEGIN_
प्राकारेण परिक्षिप्ता पाण्डुरेण विराजिता |हेम कक्ष्या पुरी रम्या वैदूर्यमय तोरणा || ३-४८-११_END
BEGIN_
"That gorgeous city is completely walled in with compound walls that are adorned with whitish silver, 
and its palace-chambers are golden, and its archways are fully jewelled with lapis jewels. [3-48-11]_END

B_3_C_47_16
BEGIN_
तस्य भ्राता तु वैमात्रो लक्ष्मणो नाम वीर्यवान् || ३-४७-१८रामस्य पुरुषव्याघ्रः सहायः समरे अरिहा |_END
BEGIN_
"One known as Lakshmana is such a Rama's brother from another mother, and he is a valorous one, tigerly-man, 
and an eliminator of enemies in war. [3-47-18b, 19a]_END

B_3_C_45_36
BEGIN_
ततः तु सीताम् अभिवाद्य लक्ष्मणःकृत अन्जलिः किंचिद् अभिप्रणम्य |अवेक्षमाणो बहुशः स मैथिलीम्
जगाम रामस्य समीपम् आत्मवान् || ३-४५-४०_END
BEGIN_
But then, holding Seetha in usual reverence that self-respectful Lakshmana briefly came to her fore 
making a reverential palm-fold that briefly, and then he proceeded to the proximity of Rama, while repeatedly 
looking back at that lonely lady in the thick of forest. [3-45-40]_END

B_3_C_46_29
BEGIN_
उपानीय आसनम् पूर्वम् पाद्येन अभिनिमंत्र्य च |अब्रवीत् सिद्धम् इति एव तदा तम् सौम्य दर्शनम् || ३-४६-३४_END
BEGIN_
She firstly fetched a seat him, then invited him with water for feet-wash, and then said to him who 
looked gracious in his bearing, 'alms are ready.' [3-46-34]_END

B_3_C_49_3
BEGIN_
अर्कम् तुंद्याम् शरैः तीक्ष्णैर् विभिंद्याम् हि महीतलम् |काम रूपिणम् उन्मत्ते पश्य माम् कामदम् पतिम् 
|| ३-४९-४_END
BEGIN_
"Indeed, I can split the Sun and splinter the earth with my splitting arrows, oh, mad woman, I can assume 
any form as I wish, and endow any wish you wish, such as I am, I must be your husband, behold me." So 
said Ravana when revealing his real nature. [3-49-4]_END

B_3_C_48_11
BEGIN_
हस्ति अश्व रथ संभाधा तूर्य नाद विनादिता |सर्व काम फलैः वृक्षैः संकुल उद्यान भूषिता || ३-४८-१२_END
BEGIN_
"It is encumbered with elephants, horses and chariots, well sounded by the sounds of trumpets, and with 
trees which yield fruits that fulfil all the savours, and it is bedecked with chirrupy pleasure-gardens. 
[3-48-12]_END

B_3_C_47_17
BEGIN_
स भ्राता लक्ष्मणो नाम धर्म चारी दृढ व्रतः || ३-४७-१९अन्वगच्छत् धनुष् पाणिः प्रव्रजंतम् मया सह |_END
BEGIN_
"He who is known as Lakshmana, a follower of virtue and steadfast in his commitment, followed Rama handling 
his bow as a helpmate, when Rama was proceeding to forests along with me. [3-47-19b, 20a]_END

B_3_C_46_30
BEGIN_
द्विजाति वेषेण समीक्ष्य मैथिलीतम् आगतम् पात्र कुसुंभ धारिणम् |अशक्यम् उद्द्वेष्टुम् उपाय दर्शनान्
न्यमंत्रयत् ब्राह्मणवत् यथा आगतम् || ३-४६-३५_END
BEGIN_
Maithili explored him who arrived with the features of a Brahman, with a saffron-robe and alms-bowl, 
and finding no reason to refute him flatly, as he has come like a Brahman, she invited him as a Brahman._END

B_3_C_49_4
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तवतः तस्य रावणस्य शिखि प्रभे |क्रुद्धस्य हरि पर्यन्ते रक्ते नेत्रे बभूवतुः || ३-४९-५_END
BEGIN_
While the infuriated Ravana is saying in that way his eyes which by themselves are torchlit in their 
shine have became further bloodshot and blackened at their edges. [3-49-5]_END

B_3_C_48_12
BEGIN_
तत्र त्वम् वस हे सीते राजपुत्रि मया सह |न स्मरिष्यसि नारीणाम् मानुषीणाम् मनस्विनि || ३-४८-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, princess, oh, self-respectful lady, if you reside there together with me, hè, Seetha, then you 
will not think of yourself as one from among human females. [3-48-13]_END

B_3_C_47_18
BEGIN_
जटी तापस रूपेण मया सह सह अनुजः || ३-४७-२०प्रविष्टो दँडकारण्यम् धर्म नित्यो धृढ व्रतः |_END
BEGIN_
"Because Rama always abides in probity and resolutely vowed to it, he entered Dandaka forest in the 
aspect of a tufty haired saint along with me and his brother. [3-47-20b, 21a]_END

B_3_C_46_31
BEGIN_
इयम् बृसी ब्राह्मण कामम् आस्यताम्इदम् च पाद्यम् प्रतिगृह्यताम् इति |इदम् च सिद्धम् वन जातम् 
उत्तमम्त्वत् अर्थम् अव्यग्रम् इह उपभुज्यताम् ३-४६-३६_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Brahman, this is the Darbha-grass-seat and you be seated comfortably, here is water, receive it 
for hand and feet wash, here is the forest grown victuals for your sake... dine on them relaxedly..." 
Thus Seetha said to Ravana. [3-46-36]_END

B_3_C_49_5
BEGIN_
सद्यः सौम्यम् परित्यज्य तीक्ष्ण रूपम् स रावणः |स्वम् रूपम् काल रूप आभम् भेजे वैश्रवण अनुजः || ३-४९-६_END
BEGIN_
Immediately discarding the gentle form of a Brahman friar, that younger brother of Kubera, Ravana, assumed 
his own ferocious form which is similar to the form of Terminator. [3-49-6]_END

B_3_C_48_13
BEGIN_
भुंजाना मानुषान् भोगान् दिव्यान् च वरवर्णिनि |न स्मरिष्यसि रामस्य मानुषस्य गत आयुषः || ३-४८-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Revelling in humanly luxuries, over and beyond in heavenly luxuries also, you will not recollect humanly 
Rama, whose longevity is lessened. [3-48-14]_END

B_3_C_47_19
BEGIN_
ते वयम् प्रच्युता राज्यात् कैकेय्याः तु कृते त्रयः || ३-४७-२१विचराम द्विज श्रेष्ठ वनम् गंभीरम् ओजसा 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Such as we are, oh, eminent Brahman, we three are moving about the impenetrable Dandaka forest just 
by our own mettle as we fell down from kingdom owing to Kaikeyi. [3-47-21b, 22a]_END

B_3_C_46_32
BEGIN_
निमंत्र्यमाणः प्रतिपूर्ण भाषिणीम्नरेन्द्र पत्नीम् प्रसमीक्ष्य मैथिलीम् |प्रसह्य तस्या हरणे धृढम् 
मनःसमर्पयामास आत्म वधाय रावणः || ३-४६-३७_END
BEGIN_
Ravana thoroughly observed that wife of the king, Maithili, when she invited him talking civilities 
contextual in inviting a guest, that too Brahman sanyasi, and he firmed up his mind to abduct her even 
forcibly, and started to dedicate himself for destruction. [3-46-37]_END

B_3_C_49_6
BEGIN_
संरक्त नयनः श्रीमान् तप्त कांचन भूषणः |क्रोधेन महता आविष्टो नील जीमूत सन्निभः || ३-४९-७दश आस्यो 
विंशति भुजो बभूव क्षणदा चरः |_END
BEGIN_
That celebrated Ravana whose eyes are bloodshot as he is ensorcelled by desperate fury transmuted his 
form into a tend-faced, twenty-armed night-walker wearing golden ornaments of purified gold and appearing 
as a black tempestuous cloud. [3-49-7, 8a]_END

B_3_C_48_14
BEGIN_
स्थापयित्वा प्रियम् पुत्रम् राज्ञा दशरथेन यः |मन्द वीर्यः सुतो ज्येष्ठः ततः प्रस्थापितो वनम् || 
३-४८-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Though Rama is the eldest son, king Dasharatha established his dear son Bharata as king, and because 
Rama is spineless he is put to flight to forests, and now, what is he and what am I, in matter of sovereignty. 
[3-48-15]_END

B_3_C_47_20
BEGIN_
समाश्वस मुहूर्तम् तु शक्यम् वस्तुम् इह त्वया || ३-४७-२२आगमिष्यति मे भर्ता वन्यम् आदाय पुष्कलम् |
रुरून् गोधान् वराहान् च हत्वा आदाय अमिषान् बहु || ३-४७-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Be comfortable for a moment, here it is possible for you to make a sojourn, and soon my husband will 
be coming on taking plentiful forest produce, and on killing stags, mongooses, wild boars he fetches 
meat, aplenty. [3-47-22b, 23]_END

B_3_C_46_33
BEGIN_
ततः सुवेषम् मृगया गतम् पतिम्प्रतीक्षमाणा सह लक्ष्मणम् तदा |निरीक्षमाणा हरितम् ददर्श तत्महद् 
वनम् न एव तु राम लक्ष्मणौ || ३-४६-३८_END
BEGIN_
Then she looked forward for her shapely husband who has gone on a hunting game, and who must be returning 
along with Lakshmana, and though she looked intently she could only see the green backdrop of that great 
forest, but not Rama or Lakshmana. [3-46-38]_END

B_3_C_49_7
BEGIN_
स परिव्राजक च्छद्म महाकायो विहाय तत् || ३-४९-८प्रतिपेदे स्वकम् रूपम् रावणो राक्षस अधिपः |रक्त 
अंबर धरः तस्थौ स्त्री रत्नम् प्रेक्ष्य मैथिलीम् || ३-४९-९_END
BEGIN_
On discarding that guise of a Brahman friar that sovereign of demons Ravana educed his own physique 
and then that mighty bodied one attired in reddish clothing stood before Maithili observing that gem 
of a lady. [3-49-8b, 9]_END

B_3_C_48_15
BEGIN_
तेन किम् भ्रष्ट राज्येन रामेण गत चेतसा |करिष्यसि विशालाक्षि तापसेन तपस्विना || ३-४८-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Rama is subverted from kingdom, thus dwindled is valour, thus winded down is his anima, thus he has 
become a pitiable one, thus he became an ascetic as nothing else is there for him to undertake, oh, 
broad-eyed lady, what do you aspire to do with such a Rama? [3-48-16]_END

B_3_C_47_21
BEGIN_
सः त्वम् नाम च गोत्रम् च कुलम् आचक्ष्व तत्त्वतः |एकः च दण्डकारण्ये किम् अर्थम् चरसि द्विज || ३-४७-२४_END
BEGIN_
"Such as you are, oh, Brahman, you may make mention of your name, parentage and caste, in their actuality. 
For what reason you are wandering in Dandaka forest lonesomely?" Thus Seetha questioned Ravana. [3-47-24]_END

B_3_C_49_8
BEGIN_
स ताम् असित केश अन्ताम् भास्करस्य प्रभाम् इव |वसन आभरण उपेताम् मैथिलीम् रावणो अब्रवीत् || ३-४९-१०_END
BEGIN_
She whose tresses are glossily blackish until their ends, and who has on her glittering jewellery and 
silken-ochry-sari, whereby who is imperceivable like sun's glaring shine, to such Maithili Ravana spoke. 
[3-49-10]_END

B_3_C_48_16
BEGIN_
सर्व राक्षस भर्तारम् कामय - कामात् - स्वयम् आगतम् |न मन्मथ शर आविष्टम् प्रति आख्यातुम् त्वम् अर्हसि 
|| ३-४८-१७_END
BEGIN_
"I, the king of all the demons, am hit by the arrows of Love-god and came to you in love, and instead 
of beseeching me to love you, your rejection and speaking this way, is unapt of you._END

B_3_C_47_22
BEGIN_
एवम् ब्रुवत्याम् सीतायाम् राम पत्नीआम् महाबलः |प्रत्युवाच उत्तरम् तीव्रम् रावणो राक्षसाधिपः || ३-४७-२५_END
BEGIN_
Ravana, the great-mighty king of demons, brusquely replied Seetha, the wife of Rama, while she is still 
speaking in this way. [3-47-25]_END

B_3_C_48_17
BEGIN_
प्रति आख्याय हि माम् भीरु परितापम् गमिष्यसि |चरणेन अभिहत्य इव पुरूरवसम् ऊर्वशी || ३-४८-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, modest lady, on refusing me you surely become remorseful like Uurvashi who once kicked Puruurava 
with her feet. [3-48-18]_END

B_3_C_49_9
BEGIN_
त्रिषु लोकेषु विख्यातम् यदि भर्तारम् इच्छसि |माम् आश्रय वरारोहे तव अहम् सदृशः पतिः || ३-४९-११_END
BEGIN_
"If you wish to have a husband of well-renown in three worlds you seek shelter in me, oh, high-hipped 
lady, I alone will match up to you as husband. [3-49-11]_END

B_3_C_47_23
BEGIN_
येन वित्रासिता लोकाः स देव असुर मानुषा |अहम् सः रावणो नाम सीते रक्षो गण ईश्वरः || ३-४७-२६_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Seetha, of whom all the worlds composed of gods, demons and humans are highly startled, I am that 
sovereign of hosts of demons, known as Ravana. [3-47-26]_END

B_3_C_48_18
BEGIN_
अंगुल्या न समो रामो मम युद्धे स मानुषः |तव भाग्येन् संप्राप्तम् भजस्व वरवर्णिनि || ३-४८-१९_END
BEGIN_
"He that Rama is merely a human, and in war he equals me not by my finger, oh, richly colourful lady, 
and I chanced here merely by your serendipity, thus you honour me and my desire to possess you..." Thus 
Ravana spoke to Seetha. [3-48-19]_END

B_3_C_49_10
BEGIN_
माम् भजस्व चिराय त्वम् अहम् श्लाघ्यः पतिः तव |न एव च अहम् क्वचित् भद्रे करिष्ये तव विप्रियम् || 
३-४९-१२त्यज्यताम् मानुषो भावो मयि भावः प्रणीयताम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Ultimately you have a much-lauded husband in me, as such you oblige me, and I will not cause any displeasure 
to you at any point of time. Let your heart refrain from that humanly Rama and you start bringing round 
your heart towards me. [3-49-12, 13a]_END

B_3_C_47_24
BEGIN_
त्वाम् तु कांचन वर्ण आभाम् दृष्ट्वा कौशेय वासिनीम् |रतिम् स्वकेषु दारेषु न अधिगच्छामि अनिन्दिते 
|| ३-४७-२७_END
BEGIN_
"On seeing you, oh, impeccable one, glittering with golden complexion and attired in ochry-silks, I 
derive no pleasure in my wives. [3-47-27]_END

B_3_C_48_19
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्ता तु वैदेही क्रुद्धा संरक्त लोचना |अब्रवीत् परुषम् वाक्यम् रहिते राक्षस अधिपम् || ३-४८-२०_END
BEGIN_
Vaidehi who is spoken thus is infuriated on her part and with her eyes bloodshot spoke these bitter 
words to the king of demons in that lonely lace. [3-48-20]_END

B_3_C_49_11
BEGIN_
राज्यात् च्युतम् असिद्ध अर्थम् रामम् परिमित आयुषम् || ३-४९-१३कैः गुणैः अनुरक्ता असि मूढे पण्डित 
मानिनि |यः स्त्रिया वचनात् राज्यम् विहाय ससुहृत् जनम् || ३-४९-१४अस्मिन् व्याल अनुचरिते वने वसति 
दुर्मतिः |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, halfwitted lady, you who deem yourself a highly intellectual lady, listen, that mindless Rama who 
just by a word of a woman forebode kingdom along with all of his amiable people, and lives in this forest 
where the predators are on the prowl, thus he who is spurned off from kingdom, ungainful are his purposes, 
and who is even a short-lived human, I wonder by what merits you are impassioned for such a Rama?" Thus 
Ravana spoke to Seetha. [3-49-13b, 14, 15a]_END

B_3_C_47_25
BEGIN_
बह्वीनाम् उत्तम स्त्रीणाम् आहृतानाम् इतः ततः |सर्वासाम् एव भद्रम् ते मम अग्र महिषी भव || ३-४७-२८_END
BEGIN_
"You become my prime queen above all the choicest women with superior status, whom I have appropriated 
from here and there. [3-47-28]_END

B_3_C_48_20
BEGIN_
कथम् वैश्रवणम् देवम् सर्व देव नमस्कृतम् |भ्रातरम् व्यपदिश्य त्वम् अशुभम् कर्तुम् इच्छसि || ३-४८-२१_END
BEGIN_
"How you wish to commit sins although saying that Kubera, a god reverenced by all of the gods, is your 
brother? [3-48-21]_END

B_3_C_49_12
BEGIN_
इति उक्त्वा मैथिलीम् वाक्यम् प्रिय अर्हाम् प्रिय वादिनीम् || ३-४९-१५अभिगम्य सुदुष्ट आत्मा राक्षसः 
काम मोहितः |जग्राह रावणः सीताम् बुधः खे रोहिणीम् इव || ३-४९-१६_END
BEGIN_
On saying that sentence to Maithili, who by herself is a nice talker and who is a proper one for addressing 
with nice words, that verily evil-minded demon Ravana maddened by lust drew nigh of Seetha and grabbed 
her, as Budha, the Jupiter grabs the Star Rohini in firmament. [3-49-15b, 16]_END

B_3_C_47_26
BEGIN_
लंका नाम समुद्रस्य मध्ये मम महापुरी |सागरेण परिक्षिप्ता निविष्टा गिरि मूर्धनि || ३-४७-२९_END
BEGIN_
"Nestled on a mountaintop my great city known as Lanka is there in the midst of an ocean and all over 
encompassed by an ocean. [3-47-29]_END

B_3_C_48_21
BEGIN_
अवश्यम् विनशिष्यन्ति सर्वे रावण राक्षसाः |येषाम् त्वम् कर्कशो राजा दुर्बुद्धिः अजित इन्द्रियः || 
३-४८-२२_END
BEGIN_
"All the demons will perforce get completely destroyed, oh, Ravana, for whom you the cruel and culpable 
one with uncontrolled senses is the king, and you will be blameworthy for the elimination of righteous 
demons like Vibheeshana, et al. [3-48-22]_END

B_3_C_49_13
BEGIN_
वामेन सीताम् पद्माक्षीम् मूर्धजेषु करेण सः |ऊर्वोः तु दक्षिणेन एव परिजग्राह पाणिना || ३-४९-१७_END
BEGIN_
He that Ravana grabbed the lotus-eyed Seetha on lifting her up with his left hand at her plait of hair 
at nape, and with his right hand at her thighs. [3-49-17]_END

B_3_C_47_27
BEGIN_
तत्र सीते मया सार्धम् वनेषु विचरिष्यसि |न च अस्य वन वासस्य स्पृहयिष्यसि भामिनि || ३-४७-३०_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Seetha, there you can saunter in pleasure-gardens along with me, and oh, lady with resentment, 
you will not think back to this forest-living, at all events. [3-47-30]_END

B_3_C_50_0
BEGIN_
तम् शब्दम् अवसुप्तस्य जटायुः अथ शुश्रुवे |निरैक्षत् रावणम् क्षिप्रम् वैदेहीम् च ददर्श सः || ३-५०-१_END
BEGIN_
Jataayu who is slumbering away craned and stared on hearing the voicing of Seetha and then he saw Ravana 
and even Vaidehi. [3-50-1]_END

B_3_C_48_22
BEGIN_
अपहृत्य शचीम् भार्याम् शक्यम् इन्द्रस्य जीवितुम् |न हि रामस्य भार्याम् माम् अपनीय अस्ति जीवितम् 
|| ३-४८-२३_END
BEGIN_
"It may be possible to live after abducting Shaci Devi, the wife of Indra, somehow and anyhow there 
will be no liveability after abducting me, the wife of Rama. [3-48-23]_END

B_3_C_49_14
BEGIN_
तम् दृष्ट्वा गिरि शृंग आभम् तीक्ष्ण दंष्ट्रम् महा भुजम् |प्राद्रवन् मृत्यु संकाशम् भय आर्ता वन देवताः 
|| ३-४९-१८_END
BEGIN_
On seeing him who grabbed Seetha, who has incisive fangs, mightily armed and who is shining forth like 
a mountain crest and similar to Death, the forest deities quickly fled away terrorised by his terrorism. 
[3-49-18]_END

B_3_C_47_28
BEGIN_
पंच दास्यः सहस्राणि सर्व आभरण भूषिताः |सीते परिचरिष्यन्ति भार्या भवसि मे यदि || ३-४७-३१_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Seetha, if you become my wife five thousand handmaidens adorned with ornaments of every description 
will be in your attendance." Thus Ravana said to Seetha. [3-47-31]_END

B_3_C_50_1
BEGIN_
ततः पर्वत शृंग आभः तीक्ष्ण तुण्डः खग उत्तमः |वनस्पति गतः श्रीमान् व्याजहार शुभाम् गिरम् || ३-५०-२_END
BEGIN_
That best bird majestic Jataayu with a very sharp beak and appearing like a mountain peak, then uttered 
these words of expediency still perching on a tree. [3-50-2]_END

B_3_C_48_23
BEGIN_
जीवेत् चिरम् वज्र धरस्य हस्तात्शचीम् प्रधृष्य अप्रतिरूप रूपाम् |न मा दृशीम् राक्षस धर्षयित्वा
पीत अमृतस्य अपि तव अस्ति मोक्षः || ३-४८-२४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, demon, un-mirrored is the prettiness of prettyish Shaci Devi, and one may live long on forcibly 
snatching her away from the hands of the wielder of Thunderbolt, Indra, but to him who intimidates or 
abuses me or women like me, there will be no moksha, release from the cycle of rebirth, 
even if he has consumed amR^ita ambrosia." Thus Seetha spoke to Ravana. [3-48-24]_END

B_3_C_47_29
BEGIN_
रावणेन एवम् उक्ता तु कुपिता जनक आत्मजा |प्रत्युवाच अनवद्यांगी तम् अनादृत्य राक्षसम् || ३-४७-३२_END
BEGIN_
When Ravana said in this way, Seetha the daughter of Janaka, a flawless one by her physique, dishonoured 
and replied that demon. [3-47-32]_END

B_3_C_49_15
BEGIN_
स च मायामयो दिव्यः खर युक्तः खर स्वनः |प्रत्यदृश्यत हेमांगो रावणस्य महारथः || ३-४९-१९_END
BEGIN_
Then the miracle-air-chariot of Ravana which is miraculously designed to appear and disappear at the 
wish of its master, yoked with miraculous mules, and built with its golden wheels and parts, appeared 
afore Ravana braying noisily. [3-49-19]_END

B_3_C_50_2
BEGIN_
दशग्रीव स्थितो धर्मे पुराणे सत्य संश्रयः |भ्रातः सः त्वम् निन्दितम् कर्म कर्तुम् न अर्हसि संप्रताम् 
||३-५०-३जटायुः नाम नाम्ना अहम् गृध्र राजो महाबलः |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, brother, now it is inapt of you to undertake a deplorable deed. I am one of those who abide by 
perpetual probity and avowed to truthfulness. Such as I am, oh, Decahedral-demon Ravana, I am the mightiest 
king of eagles known by the name Jataayu. [3-50-3, 4a]_END

B_3_C_47_30
BEGIN_
महा गिरिम् इव अकंप्यम् महेन्द्र सदृशम् पतिम् |महा उदधिम् इव अक्षोभ्यम् अहम् रामम् अनुव्रता || ३-४७-३३_END
BEGIN_
"I have avowed to adhere to such a husband Rama, who is inflexible like a sturdy mountain, comparable 
to lordly Indra, unshakable like a vast ocean. [3-47-33]_END

B_3_C_49_16
BEGIN_
ततः ताम् परुषैः वाक्यैः अभितर्ज्य महास्वनः |अंकेन आदाय वैदेहीम् रथम् आरोपयत् तदा || ३-४९-२०_END
BEGIN_
Then he whose voice is strident that Ravana lifted her up by her waist and got Vaidehi up on the air-chariot 
intimidating her with bitter words. [3-49-20]_END

B_3_C_50_3
BEGIN_
राजा सर्वस्य लोकस्य महेन्द्र वरुण उपमः || ३-५०-४लोकानाम् च हिते युक्तो रामो दशरथ आत्मजः |_END
BEGIN_
"Rama, the son of Dasharatha, is the master of all the world, one similar to Mahendra and Varuna, the 
Rain-god, and the one who is connected with the well-being of all the world. [3-50-4b, 5a]_END

B_3_C_47_31
BEGIN_
सर्व लक्षण संपन्नम् न्यग्रोध परि मण्डलम् |सत्य संधम् महाभागम् रामम् अनुव्रता || ३-४७-३४_END
BEGIN_
"He who is enriched with all endowments, and who is like a banyan tree with its surmounted orbicularity, 
the high-minded one with truthfulness alone is his target, and I am avowed to adhere to such a Rama. 
[3-47-34]_END

B_3_C_49_17
BEGIN_
सा गृहीता अतिचुक्रोश रावणेन यशस्विनी |रामा इति सीता दुःख आर्ता रामम् दूरम् गतम् वने || ३-४९-२१_END
BEGIN_
Agonised with anguish when gone into the captivity of Ravana, she that glorious Seetha wailed loudly 
for Rama saying 'oh, Rama,' which Rama has gone deep into the forest by then. [3-49-21]_END

B_3_C_50_4
BEGIN_
तस्य एषा लोक नाथस्य धर्म पत्नी यशस्विनी || ३-५०-५सीता नाम वरारोहा याम् त्वम् हर्तुम् इह इच्छसि |_END
BEGIN_
"Whom you desire to abduct now, that best lady is Seetha by her name, and this glorious one is the legitimate 
wife of that preserver of all the worlds, namely Rama. [3-50-5b, 6a]_END

B_3_C_47_32
BEGIN_
महाबाहुम् महोरस्कम् सिंह विक्रांत गामिनम् |नृसिंहम् सिंह संकाशम् अहम् रामम् अनुव्रता || ३-४७-३५_END
BEGIN_
"He who is ambidextrous, broad-chested, supreme among men, and a lion-like person with the strides of 
prancing lion, and I am avowed to adhere to such a Rama. [3-47-35]_END

B_3_C_49_18
BEGIN_
ताम् अकामाम् स काम आर्तः पन्नग इन्द्र वधूम् इव |विवेष्टमानाम् आदाय उत्पपात अथ रावणः || ३-४९-२२_END
BEGIN_
Ravana who is infatuated with lust picked her up, which lady is disinclined for any kind of sensuality 
and who is verily writhing like the wife of King Cobra, and then he surged skyward and flew off with 
her in his air-chariot. [3-49-22]_END

B_3_C_50_5
BEGIN_
कथम् राजा स्थितो धर्मे पर दारान् परामृशेत् || ३-५०-६रक्षणीया विशेषेण राज दारा महाबलः |_END
BEGIN_
"How a king adhering to probity can lay his hands on the wives of others? If it is a king's wife, oh, 
great-mighty Ravana, she is to be safeguarded particularly. [3-50-6b, 7a]_END

B_3_C_47_33
BEGIN_
पूर्ण चन्द्र आननम् वीरम् राज वत्सम् जितेन्द्रियम् |पृथु कीर्तिम् महाबाहुम् अहम् रामम् अनुव्रता || 
३-४७-३६_END
BEGIN_
"He who is a valiant one with a face like that of full-moon, a prince with his self-conquered, and he 
who is expressly acclaimed and effectively armed, and I am avowed to adhere to such a Rama. [3-47-36]_END

B_3_C_49_19
BEGIN_
ततः सा राक्षसेन्द्रेण ह्रियमाणा विहायसा |भृशम् चुक्रोश मत्ता इव भ्रांत चित्ता यथा आतुरा || ३-४९-२३_END
BEGIN_
While that lord of demons is abducting her in the skyway, Seetha became frenzied with bewildered faculties 
and then bawled stridently like a hysterical person. [3-49-23]_END

B_3_C_50_6
BEGIN_
निवर्तय गतिम् नीचाम् पर दार अभिमर्शनात् || ३-५०-७न तत् समाचरेत् धीरो यत् परो अस्य विगर्हयेत् |
यथा आत्मनः तथा अन्येषाम् दारा रक्ष्या विमर्शनात् || ३-५०-८_END
BEGIN_
"Reverse your filthy course, or fortuity, or mind form laying your hands on other's wives. A sagacious 
person does not undertake that deed by which others deplore him. As with the protection of one's own 
wife from somebody's laying hands on her, other person's wife is also to be protected in that way. [3-50-8 
[3-50-7b, 8]_END

B_3_C_47_34
BEGIN_
त्वम् पुनः जंबुकः सिंहीम् माम् इह इच्छसि दुर्लभाम् |न अहम् शक्या त्वया स्प्रष्टुम् आदित्यस्य प्रभा 
यथा || ३-४७-३७_END
BEGIN_
"You being a fox you woo me who am an absolutely inaccessible lioness? Why wooing, it is impossible 
for you to touch me as with the untouchable Shine of the Sun. [3-47-37]_END

B_3_C_49_20
BEGIN_
हा लक्ष्मण महाबाहो गुरु चित्त प्रसादक |ह्रियमाणाम् न जानीषे रक्षसा काम रूपिणा || ३-४९-२४_END
BEGIN_
"Haa, greatly dextrous Lakshmana... oh, rejoicer of your mentor... you are incognisant of me who am 
being abducted by this demon who is a dissembler. [3-49-24]_END

B_3_C_50_7
BEGIN_
अर्थम् वा यदि वा कामम् शिष्टाः शास्त्रेषु अनागतम् |व्यवस्यन्ति अनु राजानम् धर्मम् पौलस्त्य नंदन 
|| ३-५०-९_END
BEGIN_
"If the means to gain probity, or prosperities, or even pleasures are inconspicuous in scriptures, oh, 
the scion of Paulastya, then even the erudite scholars will conduct themselves following the king and 
his demeanour. [3-50-9]_END

B_3_C_47_35
BEGIN_
पादपान् कांचनान् नूनम् बहून् पश्यसि मंदभाक् |राघवस्य प्रियाम् भार्याम् यः त्वम् इच्छसि राक्षस || 
३-४७-३८_END
BEGIN_
"You who are an ill-fated demon, oh, demon, by your wooing the dear wife of Raghava, thus you must be 
visualising many golden trees, undeniably. [3-47-38]_END

B_3_C_49_21
BEGIN_
जीवितम् सुखम् अर्थाम् च धर्म हेतोः परित्यजन् |ह्रियमाणाम् अधर्मेण माम् राघव न पश्यसि || ३-४९-२५_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Raghava, you have relinquished your high-life, happiness, and riches for the sake of righteousness, 
and though you avowed to protect your observants, you are unobservant of me who am being abducted by 
the unrighteousness itself. [3-49-5]_END

B_3_C_50_8
BEGIN_
राजा धर्मः च कामः च द्रव्याणाम् च उत्तमो निधिः |धर्मः शुभम् वा पापम् वा राज मूलम् प्रवर्तते || ३-५०-१०_END
BEGIN_
"A king is the best repository for probity, prosperities, and pleasures, and whether it is probity or 
felicity or even iniquity that will emerge from the fount called king. [3-50-10]_END

B_3_C_47_36
BEGIN_
क्षुधितस्य च सिंहस्य मृग शत्रोः तरस्विनः |आशी विषस्य वदनात् दम्ष्ट्राम् आदातुम् इच्छसि || ३-४७-३९_END
BEGIN_
"Do you wish to twitch fangs from the mouth of a ravenous lion, the expeditious challenger of animals, 
and from the mouth of a rebounding venomous serpent. [3-47-39]_END

B_3_C_49_22
BEGIN_
ननु नाम अविनीतानाम् विनेता असि परंतप |कथम् एवम् विधम् पापम् न त्वम् शास्सि हि रावणम् || ३-४९-२६_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, enemy-inflamer Rama, I reckon that you are an absolute controller of uncontrollable beings, I wonder 
why you are not controlling this kind of sinner, Ravana, indeed?" This is how Seetha started her cry 
in wilderness. [3-49-26]_END

B_3_C_50_9
BEGIN_
पाप स्वभावः चपलः कथम् त्वम् रक्षसाम् वर |ऐश्वर्यम् अभिसंप्राप्तो विमानम् इव दुष्कृती || ३-५०-११_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, prominent one among demons, deviltry and mercuriality are but natural for you demons, but how you 
have amassed affluence, as with an evildoer attaining an aircraft that puts him to flight to heaven._END

B_3_C_49_23
BEGIN_
ननु सद्यो अविनीतस्य दृश्यते कर्मणः फलम् |कालो अपि अंगी भवति अत्र सस्यानाम् इव पक्तये || ३-४९-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Indeed, the result for an evil act will not be apparent instantaneously. Even the time becomes a factor 
in the matter of cause and effect, as with the crops becoming cookable after certain time lag." Thus, 
she is addressing Ravana now. [3-49-27]_END

B_3_C_47_37
BEGIN_
मंदरम् पर्वत श्रेष्ठम् पाणिना हर्तुम् इच्छसि |काल कूटम् विषम् पीत्वा स्वस्तिमान् गंतुम् इच्छसि || 
३-४७-४०_END
BEGIN_
"Do you wish to steal away the massive Mandara Mountain by the sleight of your hand, but how do you 
wish to decamp healthily without consuming lethal poison? [3-47-40]_END

B_3_C_50_10
BEGIN_
काम स्वभावो यः सः असौ न शक्यः तम् प्रमार्जितुम् |न हि दुष्ट आत्मनाम् आर्यम् आवसति आलये चिरम् || 
३-५०-१२_END
BEGIN_
"He whose nature is such, that nature is perhaps impossible to efface, a sermon does not dwell in the 
heart of an evil-minded one for a long time, indeed._END

B_3_C_47_38
BEGIN_
अक्षि सूच्या प्रमृजसि जिह्वया लेढि च क्षुरम् |राघवस्य प्रियाम् भार्याम् अधिगंतुम् त्वम् इच्छसि || 
३-४७-४१_END
BEGIN_
"If you wish to override the dear wife of Raghava, then it is as good as wishing to deeply scrape your 
eyes with needlepoint, and licking the razorblade with your tongue. [3-47-41]_END

B_3_C_49_24
BEGIN_
त्वम् कर्म कृतवान् एतत् काल उपहत चेतनः |जीवित अंतकरम् घोरम् रामात् व्यसनम् आप्नुहि || ३-४९-२८_END
BEGIN_
"The Time has battered your brains and as an infringer you have undertaken this particular exploit, 
whereby you will get a devastating and life-ending tribulation from Rama." Thus, she upbraided Ravana. 
[3-49-28]_END

B_3_C_50_11
BEGIN_
विषये वा पुरे वा ते यदा रामो महाबलः |न अपराध्यति धर्मात्मा कथम् तस्य अपराध्यसि || ३-५०-१३_END
BEGIN_
"When that great-mighty Rama has not transgressed either in your country or in your city Lanka, then 
how you become a transgressor in respect of that noble-souled Rama? [3-50-13]_END

B_3_C_49_25
BEGIN_
हन्त इदानीम् सकामा तु कैकेयी बान्धवैः सह |ह्रियेयम् धर्म कामस्य धर्म पत्नी यशस्विनः || ३-४९-२९_END
BEGIN_
"An honest wife of a glorious one who aspires nothing but honesty, such a wife of Rama as I am, I am 
being abducted, thus the aspiration of Kaikeyi and her kinfolk has now come true. Oh, god!" Thus, she 
soliloquised. [3-49-29]_END

B_3_C_47_39
BEGIN_
अवसज्य शिलाम् कण्ठे समुद्रम् तर्तुम् इच्छसि |सूर्या चन्द्रमसौ च उभौ प्राणिभ्याम् हर्तुम् इच्छसि 
|| ३-४७-४२यो रामस्य प्रियाम् भार्याम् प्रधर्षयितुम् इच्छसि |_END
BEGIN_
"You who wish to bitterly intimidate the dear wife of Rama are as good as the one who wish to swim an 
ocean arraying a boulder around his neck, and with a pair of hands you wish to steal away both the Sun 
and Moon? [3-47-42, 43a]_END

B_3_C_50_12
BEGIN_
यदि शूर्पणखा हेतोः जनस्थान गतः खरः |अतिवृत्तो हतः पूर्वम् रामेण अक्लिष्ट कर्मणा || ३-५०-१४अत्र 
ब्रूहि यथा तत्त्वम् को रामस्य व्यतिक्रमः |यस्य त्वम् लोक नाथस्य हृत्वा भार्याम् गमिष्यसि || ३-५०-१५_END
BEGIN_
"If Rama of indefatigable deeds firstly eliminated Khara who is stationed at Janasthaana, and who transgressed 
for the sake of Shuurpanakha, tell me what in actuality is the highly overstepping behaviour of Rama 
in that matter, whereupon you are stealing off with the wife of such a lord of world? [3-50-14, 15]_END

B_3_C_47_40
BEGIN_
अग्निम् प्रज्वलितम् दृष्ट्वा वस्त्रेण आहर्तुम् इच्छसि || ३-४७-४३कल्याण वृत्ताम् यो भार्याम् रामस्य 
हर्तुम् इच्छसि |_END
BEGIN_
"You who wish to abduct me with an auspicious legend as the wife of Rama, thus you wish to steal away 
a glowing fire in a cloth-bundle, though evincing it to be highly flaming? [3-47-43b, 44a]_END

B_3_C_49_26
BEGIN_
आमंत्रये जनस्थानम् कर्णिकारान् च पुष्पितान् |क्षिप्रम् रामाय शंसध्वम् सीताम् हरति रावणः || ३-४९-३०_END
BEGIN_
"I call the attention of the flowered Karnikaara trees of Janasthaana, you inform Rama that Ravana is 
thieving Seetha." Thus, she is addressing the woods and others on the ground from air-chariot. [3-49-30]_END

B_3_C_50_13
BEGIN_
क्षिप्रम् विसृज वैदेहीम् मा त्वा घोरेण चक्षुषा |दहेत् दहनभूतेन वृत्रम् इन्द्र अशनिः यथा || ३-५०-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Instantly deliver up Vaidehi. Let not the disastrous and glowing fire-like eyes of Rama, which transmogrify 
so when he assumes fury, burn you down as the Thunderbolt of Indra once burnt the demon Vritta. [3-50-16]_END

B_3_C_49_27
BEGIN_
