हंस सारस संघुष्टाम् वन्दे गोदावरीम् नदीम् |क्षिप्रम् रामाय शंस त्वम् सीताम् हरति रावणः || ३-४९-३१_END
BEGIN_
"I pray you who are with the bustle of swans and saarasa water birds, oh, River Godavari, you promptly 
tell Rama that Ravana is thieving Seetha. [3-49-31]_END

B_3_C_47_41
BEGIN_
अयो मुखानाम् शूलानाम् अग्रे चरितुम् इच्छसि |रामस्य सदृशीम् भार्याम् यो अधिगंतुम् त्वम् इच्छसि || 
३-४७-४४_END
BEGIN_
"You who wish to override the befitting and selfsame wife of Rama, are wishing to tread on the needle-sharp 
spikes of iron spears. [3-47-44b, c]_END

B_3_C_50_14
BEGIN_
सर्पम् आशीविषम् बद्ध्वा वस्त्र अन्ते न अवबुध्यसे |ग्रीवायाम् प्रतिमुक्तम् च काल पाशम् न पश्यसि || 
३-५०-१७_END
BEGIN_
"You are unconscious that you have presently bundled a lethally venomous serpent at the fringe of your 
attire, and you are equally unwary that the Terminator's lasso is presently loosened around your neck. 
[3-50-17]_END

B_3_C_49_28
BEGIN_
दैवतानि च यान्ति अस्मिन् वने विविध पादपे |नमस्करोमि अहम् तेभ्यो भर्तुः शंसत माम् हृताम् || ३-४९-३२_END
BEGIN_
"I also venerate you, the sylvan deities that travel in this forest with diverse trees or, those that 
abide on the treetops, you may please inform my husband that I am being stolen. [3-49-32]_END

B_3_C_47_42
BEGIN_
यद् अंतरम् सिंह शृगालयोः वनेयद् अंतरम् स्यन्दनिका समुद्रयोः |सुर अग्र्य सौवीरकयोः यद् अंतरम्
तद् अंतरम् दाशरथेः तव एव च || ३-४७-४५_END
BEGIN_
"Which odds are there between a lion and a fox in a given forest, which odds are there between a turbid-rivulet 
and an ocean, and which odds are there between a fine-wine and sour-gruel, likewise you are also at 
odds with the son of Dasharatha. [3-47-45]_END

B_3_C_50_15
BEGIN_
स भारः सौम्य भर्तव्यो यो नरम् न अवसादयेत् |तत् अन्नम् अपि भोक्तव्यम् जीर्यते यत् अनामयम् || ३-५०-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, cultured one, that weight alone is to be shouldered by which a man is not brought down, and that 
repast alone is to be consumed by which nothing upsets. [3-50-18]_END

B_3_C_49_29
BEGIN_
यानि कानिचित् अपि अत्र सत्त्वानि निवसन्ति उत |सर्वाणि शरणम् यामि मृग पक्षि गणान् अपि || ३-४९-३३_END
BEGIN_
"Or, over there, some few beings that are living over there on the ground below, I seek shelter of all 
the flocks of birds and hoards of animals, and I pray you to convey this news. [3-49-33]_END

B_3_C_47_43
BEGIN_
यद् अंतरम् कांचन सीस लोहयोःयद् अंतरम् चन्दन वारि पंकयोः |यद् अंतरम् हस्ति बिडालयोः वनेतद् 
अंतरम् दशरथेः तव एव च || ३-४७-४६_END
BEGIN_
"Which imparity is there among the metals of gold and lead, which imparity is there among the waters 
of sandalwood and sewage, which imparity is there between an elephant and a wildcat of forests, such 
an imparity exists between you and the son of Dasharatha. [3-47-46]_END

B_3_C_50_16
BEGIN_
यत् कृत्वा न भवेत् धर्मो न कीर्तिः न यशः ध्रुवम् |शरीरस्य भवेत् खेदः कः तत् कर्म समाचरेत् || ३-५०-१९_END
BEGIN_
"Who will undertake a deed that yields neither probity, nor deference, nor distinction but results in 
just physical drudgery? [3-50-19]_END

B_3_C_49_30
BEGIN_
ह्रियमाणाम् प्रियाम् भर्तुः प्राणेभ्यो अपि गरीयसीम् |विवश अपहृता सीता रावणेन इति शंसत || ३-४९-३४_END
BEGIN_
"Inform my husband about his dear and loftier wife than his lives, saying that, 'helpless Seetha is 
stolen by Ravana.' [3-49-34]_END

B_3_C_47_44
BEGIN_
यद् अंतरम् वायस वैनतेययोःयद् अंतरम् मद्गु मयूरयोः अपि |यद् अंतरम् हंस गृध्रयोः वनेतद् अंतरम् 
दाशरथेः तव एव च || ३-४७-४७_END
BEGIN_
"Which dissimilarity obtains betwixt a crow and an eagle, which dissimilarity obtains betwixt a waterfowl 
and a peacock, which dissimilarity obtains betwixt a swan and a falcon living in forest, such a dissimilarity 
obtains betwixt you and the son of Dasharatha. [3-47-47]_END

B_3_C_50_17
BEGIN_
षष्टि वर्ष सहस्राणि जातस्य मम रावण |पितृ पैतामहम् राज्यम् यथावत् अनुतिष्ठतः || ३-५०-२०_END
BEGIN_
"I have dedicated myself to the kingdom of my fathers and forefathers according to tradition, and sixty 
thousand years have elapsed since I was born. [3-50-20]_END

B_3_C_49_31
BEGIN_
विदित्वा माम् महाबाहुः अमुत्र अपि महाबलः |आनेष्यति पराक्रम्य वैवस्वत हृताम् अपि || ३-४९-३५_END
BEGIN_
"If that ambidextrous Rama comes to know about me, even if I am taken to heavens, or, even if I am impounded 
by Death, that great-mighty Rama brings me back, on aggressing against all of the gods in heaven, or, 
against Yama, the Death God." Thus, she appealed to one and all, but in vain. [3-49-35]_END

B_3_C_47_45
BEGIN_
तस्मिन् सहस्राक्ष सम प्रभावेरामे स्थिते कार्मुक बाण पाणौ |हृता अपि ते अहम् न जराम् गमिष्ये
वज्रम् यथा मक्षिकया अवगीर्णम् || ३-४७-४८_END
BEGIN_
"Even if you steal me away now, later when Indra similar Rama posits himself with his bow and arrows 
in hand on the battlefield, you cannot live on, and in the meanwhile you cannot digest me, as with a 
diamond swallowed along with a fly." Thus Seetha gave her vent to her disdainful feelings towards Ravana. 
[3-47-48]_END

B_3_C_50_18
BEGIN_
वृद्धो अहम् त्वम् युवा धन्वी स रथः कवची शरी |न च अपि आदाय कुशली वैदेहीम् न गमिष्यसि || ३-५०-२१_END
BEGIN_
"You are youngish whereas I am oldish, you are an armoured archer darting arrows from an air-chariot, 
whereas I am pensile bird in an open sky. Nevertheless, on taking Vaidehi you cannot abscond safely. 
[3-50-21]_END

B_3_C_49_32
BEGIN_
सा तदा करुणा वाचो विलपंती सुदुःखिता |वनस्पति गतम् ग्रिध्रम् ददर्श आयत लोचना || ३-४९-३६_END
BEGIN_
She that wide-eyed Seetha who is highly anguished and bewailing with pitiable words then with a wide-eyed 
expectancy saw the eagle Jatayu perching on a tree. [3-49-36]_END

B_3_C_47_46
BEGIN_
इति इव तत् वाक्यम् अदुष्ट भावासुदुष्टम् उक्त्वा रजनी चरम् तम् |गात्र प्रकंपात् व्यथिता बभूव
वात उद्धता सा कदली इव तन्वी || ३-४७-४९_END
BEGIN_
On speaking these sentences with high-strung words, with all her unsullied intentions to that highly 
sullied night-rambler Ravana, her fragile body trembled tormentedly as with a banana plant up-heaved 
by gust. [3-47-49]_END

B_3_C_49_33
BEGIN_
सा तम् उद् वीक्ष्य सुश्रोणी रावणस्य वशम् गता |समाक्रंदत् भयपरा दुःख उपहतया गिरा || ३-४९-३७_END
BEGIN_
She that well-waisted lady who has gone into the captivity of Ravana craned and stared at the eagle, 
and worsted by fear she shrieked squeakily with a stuttering voice that is walloped with anguish. [3-49-37]_END

B_3_C_50_19
BEGIN_
न शक्तः त्वम् बलात् हर्तुम् वैदेहीम् मम पश्यतः |हेतुभिः न्याय संयुक्तैः ध्रुवाम् वेद श्रुतीम् इव 
|| ३-५०-२२_END
BEGIN_
"It will be incapable of you to forcibly abduct Vaidehi when I keep an eye one her, as with the defilement 
of definitive Vedic scriptures by the logicians, dialecticians, materialists and suchlike non-believers, 
with their conjectural logic._END

B_3_C_47_47
BEGIN_
ताम् वेपमानाम् उपलक्ष्य सीताम्स रावणो मृत्यु सम प्रभावः |कुलम् बलम् नाम च कर्म च आत्मनःसमाचचक्षे 
भय कारण अर्थम् || ३-४७-५०_END
BEGIN_
On closely marking Seetha to be tremulous, he that Ravana whose impetus is Death similar, clearly informed 
her of his name, caste, competency, and capability as his purpose is to cause scare. [3-47-50]_END

B_3_C_49_34
BEGIN_
जटायो पश्य मम आर्य ह्रियमाणम् अनाथ वत् |अनेन राक्षसेद्रेण करुणम् पाप कर्मणा || ३-४९-३८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, fatherly Jatayu, see me, like an orphanized one I am pitiably abducted by this lord of demons with 
sinister deeds. [3-49-38]_END

B_3_C_50_20
BEGIN_
युध्यस्व यदि शूरो असि मुहूर्तम् तिष्ठ रावण |शयिष्यसे हतो भूमौ यथा पूर्वम् खरः तथा || ३-५०-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Stay for a moment, oh, Ravana, if you are valiant enough you can combat with Rama who will return right 
away, and at his hand you will be slain and sprawling on earth in the same way as Khara sprawled earlier. 
[3-50-23]_END

B_3_C_49_35
BEGIN_
न एष वारयितुम् शक्यः त्वया क्रूरो निशाचर |सत्त्ववान् जितकाशी च स आयुधः चैव दुर्मतिः || ३-४९-३९_END
BEGIN_
"It is impossible for you to forestall this merciless night-walker, for he is formidable, shining forth 
with cunning conquests, also thus this wicked minded one is with weaponry. [3-49-39]_END

B_3_C_50_21
BEGIN_
असकृत् संयुगे येन निहता दैत्य दानवाः |न चिरात् चीर वासाः त्वाम् रामो युधि वधिष्यति || ३-५०-२४_END
BEGIN_
"He who eliminated demons and ogres in combats time after time, that Rama though apparently attired 
in jute-cloths like a meek-saint, will become a towering-inferno in a given combat, and he eliminates 
you very soon. [3-50-24]_END

B_3_C_49_36
BEGIN_
रामाय तु यथा तत्त्वम् जटायो हरणम् मम |लक्ष्मणाय च तत् सर्वम् आख्यातव्यम् अशेषतः || ३-४९-४०_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Jatayu, everything about my abduction shall be narrated to Rama, or to Lakshmana, as it has happened 
in its entirety." Thus Seetha supplicated Jatayu. [3-49-40]_END

B_3_C_50_22
BEGIN_
किम् नु शक्यम् मया कर्तुम् गतौ दूरम् नृप आत्मजौ |क्षिप्रम् त्वम् नश्यसे नीच तयोः भीतो न संशयः || 
३-५०-२५_END
BEGIN_
"What can possibly be done by me when those princes have gone far-off! It is beyond the scope of my 
fetching them in time! You knave, you who are scared of them will now be lost to my blockade, without 
a doubt. [3-50-25]_END

B_3_C_50_23
BEGIN_
न हि मे जीवमानस्य नयिष्यसि शुभाम् इमाम् |सीताम् कमल पत्र अक्षीम् रामस्य महषीम् प्रियाम् || ३-५०-२६_END
BEGIN_
"When I am alive you cannot lead away this auspicious, lotus-leave-eyed Seetha, the dear queen of Rama. 
[3-50-26]_END

B_3_C_50_24
BEGIN_
अवश्यम् तु मया कार्यम् प्रियम् तस्य महात्मनः |जीवितेन अपि रामस्य तथा दशरथस्य च || ३-५०-२७_END
BEGIN_
"But I must definitely accomplish something to forestall you till they come, for I cannot willingly 
depart from here to fetch any of the two brothers, and that deed I needs must do shall be agreeable 
to the great-souled Rama, likewise even to Dasharatha, even at the stake of my life. [3-50-27]_END

B_3_C_50_25
BEGIN_
तिष्ठ तिष्ठ दशग्रीव मुहूर्तम् पश्य रावण |वृन्तात् इव फलम् त्वाम् तु पातयेयम् रथ उत्तमात् |युद्ध 
आतिथ्यम् प्रदास्यामि यथा प्राणम् निशा चर || ३-५०-२८_END
BEGIN_
"Stopoff! Stopoff! Oh, Decahedral Ravana, briefly learn of me as how I jettison you from your best air-chariot, 
as with the unloading of a burdensome fruit from its sepals. Oh, nightwalker, I will be giving guestship 
to you in a duel as long as I am alive. [3-50-28]_END

B_3_C_51_0
BEGIN_
इति उक्तः क्रोध ताम्राक्षः तप्त कांचन कुण्डलः |राक्षसेन्द्रो अभिदुद्राव पतगेन्द्रम् अमर्षणः || ३-५१-१_END
BEGIN_
When Ravana is spoken to by Jataayu with judicious words, Ravana's eyes reddened infuriately, and his 
burnished golden ear-knobs flickered injuriously, and that lord of demons dashed towards the lord of 
birds, intolerantly. [3-51-1]_END

B_3_C_51_1
BEGIN_
स संप्रहारः तुमुलः तयोः तस्मिन् महा मृधे |बभूव वात उद्धतयोः मेघयोः गगने यथा || ३-५१-२_END
BEGIN_
As with two gigantic clouds up-heaved by the tornadic gusts will be hard hitting each other tempestuously 
in sky, the combat between those two, Ravana and Jataayu, became tempestuous in the sky. [3-51-2]_END

B_3_C_51_2
BEGIN_
तत् बभूव अद्भुतम् युद्धम् गृध्र राक्षसयोः तदा |सपक्षयोः माल्यवतोः महा पर्वतयोः इव || ३-५१-३_END
BEGIN_
As with a startling combat between two gigantic and winged mountains, called Mt. Maalyavanta-s, that 
combat between the eagle and demon then became a startling one. [3-51-3]_END

B_3_C_51_3
BEGIN_
ततो नालीक नाराचैः तीक्ष्ण अग्रैः च विकर्णिभिः |अभ्यवर्षत् महाघोरैः गृध्र राजम् महाबलः || ३-५१-४_END
BEGIN_
Then the great-mighty Ravana incessantly stormed the lord of eagles Jataayu, with arrows that have excruciating 
and highly dreadful arrowheads, like tubular arrows, iron arrows, and with arrows that have crescentic 
arrowheads. [3-51-4]_END

B_3_C_51_4
BEGIN_
स तानि शर जालानि गृध्रः पत्ररथ ईश्वरः |जटायुः प्रतिजग्राह रावण अस्त्राणि संयुगे || ३-५१-५_END
BEGIN_
That eagle Jataayu who is the lord of winged-chariots, namely birds, in turn sustained those arrays 
of Ravana's arrows in that combat. [3-51-5]_END

B_3_C_51_5
BEGIN_
तस्य तीक्ष्ण नखाभ्याम् तु चरणाभ्याम् महाबलः |चकार बहुधा गात्रे व्रणान् पतग सत्तमः || ३-५१-६_END
BEGIN_
But that great-mighty Jataayu severally made gashes on the body of Ravana with his two feet that have 
gashing claws for that bird is with best stamina. [3-51-6]_END

B_3_C_52_0
BEGIN_
सा तु तारा अधिप मुखी रावणेन निरीक्ष्य तम् |गृध्र राजम् विनिहतम् विललाप सुदुःखिता || ३-५२-१_END
BEGIN_
Seetha whose visage is like a full moon wept on gazing the king of eagles Jataayu whom Ravana nearly 
killed. [3-52-1]_END

B_3_C_51_6
BEGIN_
अथ क्रोधात् दशग्रीवः जग्राह दश मार्गणान् |मृत्यु दण्ड निभान् घोरान् शत्रोर् निधन कान्क्षया || ३-५१-७_END
BEGIN_
Now the Decahedral demon Ravana infuriately took up ten deadly arrows that are similar in their shine 
to the Shafts of the Terminator, wishful of the elimination of his enemy. [3-51-7]_END

B_3_C_52_1
BEGIN_
निमित्तम् लक्षणम् स्वप्नम् शकुनि स्वर दर्शनम् |अवश्यम् सुख दुःखेषु नराणाम् परिदृश्यते || ३-५२-२_END
BEGIN_
"Humans definitely perceive either agony or ecstasy by its concomitant happenings, or by the characteristics 
of uncommon reflexes of their own body parts, or by the presages, or by conjecturable concomitants, 
or by cognising calls of birds. [3-52-2]_END

B_3_C_51_7
BEGIN_
स तैः बाणैः महावीर्यः पूर्ण मुक्तैः अजिह्म गैः |बिभेद निशितैः तीक्ष्णैः गृध्रम् घोरैः शिली मुखैः 
|| ३-५१-८_END
BEGIN_
That highly energetic Ravana released and impaled the eagle with straight shooting arrows on fully stretching 
the bowstring up to his ear, whose steel-pointed arrowheads are sharp, hurtful, and deadly. [3-51-8]_END

B_3_C_52_2
BEGIN_
न नूनम् राम जानासि महत् व्यसनम् आत्मनः |धावन्ति नूनम् काकुत्स्थ मत् अर्थम् मृग पक्षिणः || ३-५२-३_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama, for sure you are not able to know about big catastrophe called my kidnap is chancing on you, 
even though oh, Kakutstha, these animals and birds are running towards you surely for my sake, to tell 
about me. [3-52-3]_END

B_3_C_51_8
BEGIN_
स राक्षस रथे पश्यन् जानकीम् बाष्प लोचनाम् |अचिंतयित्वा बाणाम् तान् राक्षसम् समभिद्रवत् || ३-५१-९_END
BEGIN_
That Jataayu on seeing teary-eyed Jaanaki in the chariot of the demon forcefully lunged towards that 
demon heedless of arrows that are lunging at him. [3-51-9]_END

B_3_C_52_3
BEGIN_
अयम् हि कृपया राम माम् त्रातुम् इह संगतः |शेते विनिहतो भूमौ मम अभाग्यात् विहंगमः || ३-५२-४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama, this sky flier Jataayu who mercifully came here to save me is verily mangled on his encountering 
Ravana, and he is sprawling on earth, indeed by my ill luck." Thus Seetha wailed. [3-52-4]_END

B_3_C_51_9
BEGIN_
ततो अस्य सशरम् चापम् मुक्ता मणि विभूषितम् |चरणाभ्याम् महातेजा बभंज पतगोत्तमः || ३-५१-१०_END
BEGIN_
That unexcelled bird of high refulgence then shattered Ravana's bow which is decorated with pearls and 
gemstones, and on which an arrow is admitted targeting the eagle, just by the pair of his bare feet. 
[3-51-10] _END

B_3_C_52_4
BEGIN_
त्राहि माम् अद्य काकुत्स्थ लक्ष्मण इति वरांगना |सु संत्रस्ता समाक्रंदत् शृण्वताम् तु यथा अन्तिके 
|| ३-५२-५_END
BEGIN_
That best lady who is very highly panicked bawled noisily, "oh, Rama of Kakutstha... oh, Lakshmana... 
liberate me now..." as though the addressees are before her. [3-52-5]_END

B_3_C_51_10
BEGIN_
ततो अन्यत् धनुः आदाय रावणः क्रोध मूर्च्छितः |ववर्ष शर वर्षाणि शतशो अथ सहस्रशः || ३-५१-११_END
BEGIN_
Ravana convulsed in anger then took up another bow and stormed hundreds and thousands of arrow storms. 
[3-51-11]_END

B_3_C_52_5
BEGIN_
ताम् क्लिष्ट माल्य आभरणाम् विलपन्तीम् अनाथवत् |अभ्यधावत वैदेहीम् रावणो राक्षस अधिपः || ३-५२-६_END
BEGIN_
That sovereign of demons, Ravana, rushed towards Vaidehi whose garlands and jewellery are muddled up 
and who is bawling like an orphanized one. [3-52-6]_END

B_3_C_51_11
BEGIN_
शरैः आवारितः तस्य संयुगे पतगेश्वरः |कुलायम् अभिसंप्राप्तः पक्षिः इव बभौ तदा || ३-५१-१२_END
BEGIN_
Nested in the arrows shot by Ravana that lordly bird Jataayu then shone forth in that combat like a 
bird that obtains a readymade nest. [3-51-12]_END

B_3_C_52_6
BEGIN_
ताम् लताम् इव वेष्टन्तीम् आलिंगन्तीम् महाद्रुमान् |मुंच मुंच इति बहुशः प्रवदन् राक्षस अधिपः || ३-५२-७
क्रोशन्तीम् राम राम इति रामेण रहिताम् वने |जीवित अन्ताय केशेषु जग्राह अन्तक संनिभः || ३-५२-८_END
BEGIN_
Ravana, the lord of demons, has repeatedly and harshly taunted Seetha saying, 'leave it off, leave it 
off...' when Seetha devoid of Rama in that timberland is clinging and muffling a sturdy tree like a 
climber plant, and bawling, 'Rama, Rama,' and that demon whose shine is similar to the Death has clutched 
her hair loosened from her bun, as death loomed large on him. [3-52-7, 8]_END

B_3_C_51_12
BEGIN_
स तानि शर जालानि पक्षाभ्याम् तु विधूय ह |चरणाभ्याम् महातेजा बभंज अस्य महत् धनुः || ३-५१-१३_END
BEGIN_
On winnowing those arrays of arrows with both of his wings, he that highly refulgent Jataayu shattered 
the mighty bow of Ravana with both of his feet. [3-51-13]_END

B_3_C_52_7
BEGIN_
प्रधर्षितायाम् वैदेह्याम् बभूव स चरा अचरम् |जगत् सर्वम् अमर्यादम् तमसा अन्धेन संवृतम् || ३-५२-९
न वाति मारुतः तत्र निष् प्रभो अभूत् दिवाकरः |_END
BEGIN_
While Vaidehi is insulted thus, entire world together with its mobile or sessile beings became chaotic, 
and there chanced a blanketing of a blinding blackness, and waft-less is the Wind and shine-less is 
the Sun. [3-52-9]_END

B_3_C_51_13
BEGIN_
तत् च अग्नि सदृशम् दीप्तम् रावणस्य शरावरम् |पक्षाभ्याम् च महातेजा व्यधुनोत् पतगेश्वरः || ३-५१-१४_END
BEGIN_
That highly resplendent lord of birds also blasted off the armour of Ravana, which is glowing and flamelike 
in its flare, with both of his feet. [3-51-14]_END

B_3_C_52_8
BEGIN_
दृष्ट्वा सीताम् परा मृष्टाम् देवो दिव्येन चक्षुषा || ३-५२-१०कृतम् कार्यम् इति श्रीमान् व्याजहार 
पितामहः |प्रहृष्टा व्यथिताः च आसन् सर्वे ते परम ऋषयः || ३-५२-११_END
BEGIN_
On seeing Seetha's appropriation by an inappropriate being with His clairvoyant eyes, the illustrious 
Grandparent of Universe Brahma declared, "the deed is done..." but all of the supreme sages in Brahma's 
abode on seeing Seetha in such a condition became despondent, and yet delighted in foreseeing results. 
[3-52-10b, 11a]_END

B_3_C_51_14
BEGIN_
कांचन उरः छदान् दिव्यान् पिशाच वदनान् खरान् |तान् च अस्य जव संपन्नान् जघान समरे बली || ३-५१-१५_END
BEGIN_
Mighty Jataayu also knocked off the ghost-faced mules yoked to the chariot of Ravana which are covered 
in golden armours and tantivy in fastness. [3-51-15]_END

B_3_C_52_9
BEGIN_
दृष्ट्वा सीताम् परा मृष्टाम् दण्डकारण्य वासिनः |रावणस्य विनाशम् च प्राप्तम् बुद्ध्वा यदृच्छया || 
३-५२-१२_END
BEGIN_
On seeing Seetha's appropriation by an impropriate being, the dwellers in Dandaka forest cognised that 
Ravana's annihilation has chanced coincidentally. [3-52-12]_END

B_3_C_51_15
BEGIN_
अथ त्रिवेणु संपन्नम् कामगम् पावक अर्चिषम् |मणि सोपान चित्र अंगम् बभंज च महारथम् || ३-५१-१६_END
BEGIN_
Then that great-chariot which is flourishing with three bamboos from chassis to yoke, and which traverses 
just by its steersman's wish, and which is crafted fantastically with gem-studded body and stairs, or, 
whose wheels are crafted with gold and gemstones, and which in its flare is like a Ritual-fire, Jataayu 
splintered down even that chariot of Ravana. [3-51-16]_END

B_3_C_52_10
BEGIN_
स तु ताम् राम राम इति रुदन्तीम् लक्ष्मण इति च |जगाम आदाय च आकाशम् रावणो राक्षसेश्वर || ३-५२-१३_END
BEGIN_
Ravana, the lord of demons, on wresting Seetha who is bawling, "Rama... Rama..." also thus as, "Lakshmana..." 
took flight skyward. [3-52-13]_END

B_3_C_51_16
BEGIN_
पूर्ण चन्द्र प्रतीकाशम् छत्रम् च व्यजनैः सह |पातयामास वेगेन ग्राहिभी राक्षसैः सह || ३-५१-१७_END
BEGIN_
Jataayu swiftly collapsed the parasol of Ravana which in shine is mirroring the full moon, along with 
the regalia of white-royal-fur-fans, together with the demons handling them for fanning Ravana. [3-51-17]_END

B_3_C_52_11
BEGIN_
तप्त आभरण वर्ण अन्गी पीत कौशेय वासनी |रराज राज पुत्री तु विद्युत् सौदामनी यथा || ३-५२-१४_END
BEGIN_
That princess Seetha scintillated like the oblique flashes of lightning in a cloud, owing to her golden 
coloured body which is muffled up with jewellery of pure gold, and added with a golden coloured ocherish 
silky dress, while traversing in the sky. [3-52-14]_END

B_3_C_53_0
BEGIN_
खम् उत्पतन्तम् तम् दृष्ट्वा मैथिली जनक आत्मजा |
दुःखिता परम उद्विग्ना भये महति वर्तिनी || ३-५३-१_END
BEGIN_
Maithili, the daughter of Janaka, on seeing the skyward flight of Ravana taking her
along became highly frantic and remaining in highest dismay she is distraught. [3-53-1]_END

B_3_C_51_17
BEGIN_
सारथेः च अस्य वेगेन तुण्डेन च महत् शिरः |पुनः व्यपाहरत् श्रीमान् पक्षिराजो महाबलः || ३-५१-१८_END
BEGIN_
Again that highly energetic and imposing king of birds pecked off the robust head of the charioteer 
of Ravana with beak. [3-51-18]_END

B_3_C_52_12
BEGIN_
उद्धूतेन च वस्त्रेण तस्याः पीतेन रावणः |अधिकम् परिबभ्राज गिरिः दीप इव अग्निना || ३-५२-१५_END
BEGIN_
When her ochreish silk sari's upper fringe is upheaved by air onto to Ravana, Ravana looked blazing 
like a mountain set ablaze, muchly and overly. [3-52-15]_END

B_3_C_53_1
BEGIN_
रोष रोदन ताम्राक्षी भीमाक्षम् राक्षस अधिपम् |
रुदती करुणम् सीता ह्रियमाणा इदम् अब्रवीत् || ३-५३-२_END
BEGIN_
Seetha whose eyes turned coppery-red with tears and resentment, still outpouring
tears while being abducted she piteously poured this scorn on that gory-eyed demon's chief, Ravana.
[3-53-2]_END

B_3_C_51_18
BEGIN_
स भग्न धन्वा विरथो हत अश्वो हत सारथिः |अंकेन आदाय वैदेहीम् पपात भुवि रावणः || ३-५१-१९_END
BEGIN_
Now Ravana who is with his devastated bow, devoid of chariot, dispatched are his horses and departed 
is his charioteer, and such as he is, he on grabbing Vaidehi by her torso, or, placing her on the lower 
end of his torso, jumped to earth. [3-51-19]_END

B_3_C_52_13
BEGIN_
तस्याः परम कल्याण्याः ताम्राणि सुरभीणि च |पद्म पत्राणि वैदेह्या अभ्यकीर्यन्त रावणम् - यद्वा -
- च्युतानि पद्म पत्राणि रावणम् समावाकिरन् - || ३-५२-१६_END
BEGIN_
Reddish and scented lotus-petals adorning that highly auspicious Seetha have slithered, but again upheaved 
by air they are bestrewn on Ravana. [3-52-16]_END

B_3_C_53_2
BEGIN_
न व्यपत्रपसे नीच कर्मणा अनेन रावण |
ज्ञात्वा विरहिताम् यो माम् चोरयित्वा पलायसे || ३-५३-३_END
BEGIN_
"You knave Ravana, you are taking flight on thieving me after prowling about my
loneliness, such as you are, are you not ashamed in the least for this subterfuge. [3-53-3]_END

B_3_C_51_19
BEGIN_
दृष्ट्वा निपतितम् भूमौ रावणम् भग्न वाहनम् |साधु साधु इति भूतानि गृध्र राजम् अपूजयन् || ३-५१-२०_END
BEGIN_
On seeing Ravana who is foundered onto earth from his crumbled vehicle, all beings like sylvan deities, 
caarana-s, siddha-s and suchlike, reverenced that lordly eagle Jataayu. [3-51-20]_END

B_3_C_52_14
BEGIN_
तस्याः कौशेयम् उद्धूतम् आकाशे कनक प्रभम् |बभौ च आदित्य रागेण ताम्रम् अभ्रम् इव आतपे || ३-५२-१७_END
BEGIN_
Upper fringe of Seetha's silk sari with golden glitter is upheaved in the sky, and with the reddish 
hue of sun in red heat of midday it beamed forth like a reddish cloud. [3-52-17]_END

B_3_C_53_3
BEGIN_
त्वया एव नूनम् दुष्टात्मन् भीरुणा हर्तुम् इच्छता |
मम अपवाहितो भर्ता मृग रूपेण मायया || ३-५३-४_END
BEGIN_
"You black-hearted fiend, for sure, you alone sidelined my husband in a trickish
guise of Golden Deer wishful to abduct me as you are a coward. [3-53-4]_END

B_3_C_51_20
BEGIN_
परिश्रान्तम् तु तम् दृष्ट्वा जरया पक्षि यूथपम् |उत्पपात पुनर् हृष्टो मैथिलीम् गृह्य रावणः || ३-५१-२१_END
BEGIN_
But on seeing the commandant of birds Jataayu is fatigued owing to his senescence, Ravana is gladdened 
and he again rose up to skies taking Maithili. [3-51-21]_END

B_3_C_52_15
BEGIN_
तस्याः तत् विमलम् - सु नसम् - वक्त्रम् आकाशे रावण अंक गम् |न रराज विना रामम् विनालम् इव पंकजम् || 
३-५२-१८_END
BEGIN_
As with a stalk-less lotus the immaculate visage of Seetha is unbright in the sky when she is on the 
flank of Ravana as Rama is not in vicinage. [3-52-18]_END

B_3_C_53_4
BEGIN_
यो हि माम् उद्यतः त्रातुम् सो अपि अयम् विनिपातितः |
गृध्र राजः पुराणो असौ श्वशुरस्य सखा मम || ३-५३-५_END
BEGIN_
"Which king of eagles battled against you to bail me out, an old friend of my
father-in-law, such as he is he is also felled, indeed. [3-53-5]_END

B_3_C_51_21
BEGIN_
तम् प्रहृष्टम् निधाय अंके रावणम् जनक आत्मजाम् |गच्छंतम् खड्ग शेषम् च प्रणष्ट हत साधनम् || ३-५१-२२
गृध्र राजः समुत्पत्य रावणम् समभिद्रवत् |समावार्यम् महातेजा जटायुः इदम् अब्रवीत् || ३-५१-२३_END
BEGIN_
The highly resplendent king of eagles Jataayu swiftly rose to sky dashing practically to forestall Ravana, 
which demon's assault devices are all demolished by now save for a single sword, but who is cheerful 
to spirit away the daughter of Janaka, and actually spiriting away holding her onto his flank, and Jataayu 
spoke this to such Ravana. [3-51-22, 23]_END

B_3_C_52_16
BEGIN_
बभूव जलदम् नीलम् भित्त्वा चन्द्र इव उदितः |सु ललाटम् सु केश अंतम् पद्म गर्भ आभम् अव्रणम् || ३-५२-१९
शुक्लैः सु विमलैर् दन्तैः प्रभावद्भिः अलंकृतम् |तस्याः सु नयनम् वक्त्रम् आकाशे रावण अंक गम् || ३-५२-२०
रुदितम् व्यपमृष्ट अस्रम् चन्द्रवत् प्रिय दर्शनम् |सु नासम् चारु ताम्र ओष्ठम् आकाषे हाटक प्रभम् || 
३-५२-२१_END
BEGIN_
Her lotus pistil like un-pimply face is adorned with a pretty forehead on which prettyish curls are 
fluttering, and with teeth that are spick and span and sparkling, but tears dabbed on that face to sideways 
when she wept, yet it is pleasant like moon for a sight with shapely nose, pretty eyes, roseate lips, 
and shining with golden hue in sky. Nevertheless, when she has gone in the flank of Ravana on the sky 
such an immaculate face of Seetha turned like a palish moon that has just risen bursting a bluish cloud. 
[3-52-19, 20, 21]_END

B_3_C_53_5
BEGIN_
परमम् खलु ते वीर्यम् दृश्यते राक्षसाधम |
विश्राव्य नामधेयम् हि युद्धे न अस्मि जिता त्वया || ३-५३-६_END
BEGIN_
"Ah, truly what an audacious audacity is shown by you... you basely demon... by
ear-shattering your great name saying that 'I am Ravana...' I am conquered in a combat -
Really?_END

B_3_C_51_22
BEGIN_
वर्ज संस्पर्श बाणस्य भार्याम् रामस्य रावण |अल्प बुद्धे हरसि एनाम् वधाय खलु रक्षसाम् || ३-५१-२४_END
BEGIN_
"You mean-minded Ravana, you abduct her whose husband wields arrows that touch off like the Thunderbolt 
of Indra, and this spite of yours is definitely for the destruction of all the demons. [3-51-24]_END

B_3_C_52_17
BEGIN_
राक्षसेन्द्र समाधूतम् तस्याः तत् वदनम् शुभम् |शुशुभे न विना रामम् दिवा चन्द्र इव उदितः || ३-५२-२२_END
BEGIN_
Highly disconcerted by the king of demons that auspicious face of Seetha is unbright like the moon arisen 
in daytime with somewhat golden hue, owing to the absence of Rama. [3-52-22]_END

B_3_C_53_6
BEGIN_
ईदृशम् गर्हितम् कर्म कथम् कृत्वा न लज्जसे |
स्त्रियाः च हरणम् नीच रहिते च परस्य च || ३-५३-७_END
BEGIN_
"A woman, that too a lonely one, that too the other man's wife, that too an
abduction, but not winning or wooing her... you knave, on your undertaking such a kind of
deplorable deed, how unashamed are you? [3-53-7]_END

B_3_C_51_23
BEGIN_
स मित्र बन्धुः स अमात्यः स बलः स परिच्छदः |विष पानम् पिबसि एतत् पिपासित इव उदकम् || ३-५१-२५_END
BEGIN_
"As one thirsteth drinketh water, you drinketh venomous drink along with your friends, relatives, ministers, 
armies, and with your accomplices, as this abduction of Seetha itself is squirrelling away dangerous 
poison. [3-51-25]_END

B_3_C_52_18
BEGIN_
सा हेम वर्णा नील अंगम् मैथिली राक्षस अधिपम् |शुशुभे कांचनी कांची नीलम् मणिम् - गजम् - इव आश्रिता 
|| ३-५२-२३_END
BEGIN_
She that golden coloured Maithili who is moored by the blackish-bodied sovereign of demons shone forth 
like a sapphirine gemstone studded in a golden cincture. _END

B_3_C_53_7
BEGIN_
कथयिष्यन्ति लोकेषु पुरुषाः कर्म कुत्सितम् |
सुनृशंसम् अधर्मिष्ठम् तव शौण्डीर्य मानिनः || ३-५३-८_END
BEGIN_
"A self-glorifier as you are, this highly inhuman, iniquitous, imputable deed of
yours will be recounted by all men in all worlds. [3-53-8]_END

B_3_C_51_24
BEGIN_
अनुबंधम् अजानंतः कर्मणाम् अविचक्षणाः |शीघ्रम् एव विनश्यन्ति यथा त्वम् विनशिष्यसि || ३-५१-२६_END
BEGIN_
"As with the mindless adventurers quickly getting ruination for they undertake self-ruinous exploits, 
unknowing the backlashes thereof, so also you too will ruin that quickly with this mindless adventure. 
[3-51-26]_END

B_3_C_52_19
BEGIN_
सा पद्म पीता हेम आभा रावणम् जनक आत्मजा |विद्युत् घनम् इव आविश्य शुशुभे तप्त भूषणा || ३-५२-२४_END
BEGIN_
Seetha, the daughter of Janaka, with a complexion that is goldenly yellowish in the tinge of a lotus, 
moreover with her ornaments of purified gold, flashed like a lightning possessed in a dark-cloud, when 
that stonehearted Ravana possessed her. [3-52-24]_END

B_3_C_53_8
BEGIN_
धिक् ते शौर्यम् च सत्त्वम् च यत् त्वया कथितम् तदा |
कुल आक्रोशकरम् लोके धिक् ते चारित्रम् ईदृशम् || ३-५३-९_END
BEGIN_
"Damn with what you have said then about your might and mettle... damn with this
kind of your demeanour which is lamentable to whole of your clan in this world. [3-53-9]_END

B_3_C_51_25
BEGIN_
बद्धः त्वम् काल पाशेन क्व गतः तस्य मोक्ष्यसे |वधाय बडिशम् गृह्य स अमिषम् जलजो यथा || ३-५१-२७_END
BEGIN_
"You are tethered for termination with the lasso of the Terminator, as with a fish that can go nowhere 
on its biting fishhook with a piece of flesh. How do you untether yourself from that lasso of the Terminator, 
even if you go anywhere? [3-51-27]_END

B_3_C_52_20
BEGIN_
तस्या भूषण घोषेण वैदेह्या राक्षस अधिपः |बभूव विमलो नीलः सघोष इव तोयदः || ३-५२-२५_END
BEGIN_
With the rustles of Vaidehi's jewellery that lord of demons shone forth like a shipshape blue-black 
cloud with rumbles and undulating lightning. [3-52-25]_END

B_3_C_53_9
BEGIN_
किम् शक्यम् कर्तुम् एवम् हि यत् जवेन एव धावसि |
मुहूर्तम् अपि तिष्ठस्व न जीवन् प्रतियास्यसि || ३-५३-१०_END
BEGIN_
"What can be done possibly... why because you are fleeing very speedily in this
way... wait for a moment to ascertain whether you can go back in aliveness... [3-53-10]_END

B_3_C_51_26
BEGIN_
न हि जातु दुराधर्षौ काकुत्स्थौ तव रावण |धर्षणम् च आश्रमस्य अस्य क्षमिष्येते तु राघवौ || ३-५१-२८_END
BEGIN_
"But, oh Ravana, the unassailable Raghava-s of Kakutstha dynasty will nevermore condone your assailing 
this hermitage. [3-51-28]_END

B_3_C_52_21
BEGIN_
उत्तम अंग च्युता तस्याः पुष्प वृष्टिः समन्ततः |सीताया ह्रियमाणायाः पपात धरणी तले || ३-५२-२६_END
BEGIN_
Flowers gracing her best body on her head, in garlands on chest, and on armlets have fallen all-over 
the surface of earth like showers of flowers while she is being abducted. [3-52-26]_END

B_3_C_53_10
BEGIN_
न हि चक्षुः पथम् प्राप्य तयोः पार्थिव पुत्रयोः |
स सैन्यो अपि समर्थः त्वम् मुहूर्तम् अपि जीवितुम् || ३-५३-११_END
BEGIN_
"On your coming into the line of sight of those two princes, even if you are with
whole of your military, you will be incapacitated to live on, indeed even for a moment...
[3-53-11]_END

B_3_C_51_27
BEGIN_
यथा त्वया कृतम् कर्म भीरुणा लोक गर्हितम् |तस्कर आचरितो मार्गो न एष वीर निषेवितः || ३-५१-२९_END
BEGIN_
"Like a dastard you are committing a crime of thieving Seetha when none at home in the footsteps of 
thieves, this thieving is contemptible to society and condemnable by valiant ones. [3-51-29]_END

B_3_C_52_22
BEGIN_
सा तु रावण वेगेन पुष्प वृष्टिः समन्ततः |समाधूता दशग्रीवम् पुनः एव अभ्यवर्तत || ३-५२-२७_END
BEGIN_
Though that flower-shower has fallen all-over, it is windswept by the speed of Ravana, and fell again 
on that Decahedral demon. [3-52-27]_END

B_3_C_53_11
BEGIN_
न त्वम् तयोः शर स्पर्शम् सोढुम् शक्तः कथंचन |
वने प्रज्वलितस्य इव स्पर्शम् अग्नेः विहंगमः || ३-५३-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Anywise it will be incapable of you to endure the touch of their arrows, as with a
bird that cannot endure the overly flaring up wildfire in a forest. [3-53-12]_END

B_3_C_51_28
BEGIN_
युध्यस्व यदि शूरो असि मुहूर्तम् तिष्ठ रावण |शयिष्यसे हतो भूमौ यथा भ्राता खरः तथा || ३-५१-३०_END
BEGIN_
"Stay for a moment, oh, Ravana, if you are valiant enough you can combat with Rama who will return right 
away, and at his hand you will be slain and sprawling on earth in the same way as Khara sprawled earlier. 
[3-50-23]_END

B_3_C_52_23
BEGIN_
अभ्यवर्तत पुष्पाणाम् धारा वैश्रवण अनुजम् |नक्षत्र माला विमला मेरुम् नगम् इव उन्नतम् || ३-५२-२८_END
BEGIN_
Like the garland of pristine stars that circles round the loftiest Mt. Meru, that flower-shower circled 
Ravana, the brother of Kubera. [3-52-28]_END

B_3_C_53_12
BEGIN_
साधु कृत्वा आत्मनः पथ्यम् साधु माम् मुंच रावण |
मत् प्रधर्षण रुष्टो हि भ्रात्रा सह पतिः मम || ३-५३-१३
विधास्यति विनाशाय त्वम् माम् यदि न मुंचसि |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Ravana, positively contemplate in your soul and politely release me... and if
you do not release me, indeed by the rancour of insulting me, my husband along with his brother
devises your doom... [3-53-13, 14a]_END

B_3_C_51_29
BEGIN_
परेत काले पुरुषो यत् कर्म प्रतिपद्यते |विनाशाय आत्मनो अधर्म्यम् प्रतिपन्नो असि कर्म तत् || ३-५१-३१_END
BEGIN_
"A person undertakes such an unrighteous and fateful activity if only death looms large on him. You 
too have undertaken this unrighteous fateful activity only for your self-ruination. [3-51-31]_END

B_3_C_52_24
BEGIN_
चरणात् नूपुरम् भ्रष्टम् वैदेह्या रत्न भूषितम् |विद्युत् मण्डल संकाशम् पपात धरणी तले || ३-५२-२९_END
BEGIN_
Slid from the left foot of Vaidehi her anklet adorned with gems fell down onto the plane of earth like 
an electric annulus with its sparky sparkles. [3-52-29]_END

B_3_C_51_30
BEGIN_
पाप अनुबंधो वै यस्य कर्मणः को नु तत् पुमान् |कुर्वीत लोक अधिपतिः स्वयंभूः भगवान् अपि || ३-५१-३२_END
BEGIN_
"If sin is consequential to any given activity who will undertake it? Even if that person vies with 
the Self-Born God and Lord of the Universe, namely Brahma, will he undertake it?" Thus Jataayu advised 
Ravana. [3-51-32]_END

B_3_C_53_13
BEGIN_
येन त्वम् व्यवसायेन बलात् माम् हर्तुम् इच्छसि || ३-५३-१४
व्यवसायः तु ते नीच भविष्यति निरर्थकः |_END
BEGIN_
"You rogue! By which endeavour you are desirous of thieving me under duress, that
endeavour of yours behoves absurd. [3-53-14b, 15a]_END

B_3_C_52_25
BEGIN_
तरु प्रवाल रक्ता सा नील अंगम् राक्षस ईश्वरम् |प्राशोभयत वैदेही गजम् कक्ष्या इव कांचनी || ३-५२-३०_END
BEGIN_
She that Vaidehi who is so delicate like reddish leaflets of trees made that blackish bodied lord of 
demons, Ravana, well and truly lambent, herself becoming a golden girdle girded around the elephant 
like Ravana._END

B_3_C_54_0
BEGIN_
ह्रियमाणा तु वैदेही कंचित् नाथम् अपश्यती |
ददर्श गिरि शृंगस्थान् पंच वानर पुंगवान् || ३-५४-१_END
BEGIN_
Vaidehi has not seen any rescuer while she is abducted, but she has seen five
prominent vanara-s staying on a mountaintop. [3-54-1]_END

B_3_C_51_31
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्त्वा शुभम् वाक्यम् जटायुः तस्य रक्षसः |निपपात भृशम् पृष्ठे दशग्रीवस्य वीर्यवान् || ३-५१-३३_END
BEGIN_
Even on speaking those commonsensical words to Ravana, Jataayu found him carrying off Seetha heedlessly, 
then that valorous Jataayu descended on the hind-side of that Decahedral demon Ravana, devastatingly. 
[3-51-33]_END

B_3_C_53_14
BEGIN_
न हि अहम् तम् अपश्यन्ती भर्तारम् विबुध उपमम् || ३-५३-१५
उत्सहे शत्रु वशगा प्राणान् धारयितुम् चिरम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Though I am in aliveness now, but on my going under the control of an enemy and on
unseeing godlike husband of mine I am indeed unenthused to bear up my lives for a long.
[3-53-15]_END

B_3_C_54_1
BEGIN_
तेषाम् मध्ये विशालाक्षी कौशेयम् कनक प्रभम् |
उत्तरीयम् वरारोहा शुभानि आभरणानि च || ३-५४-२
मुमोच यदि रामाय शंसेयुः इति भामिनी |_END
BEGIN_
That broad-eyed and curvaceous lady with resentment Seetha, inwrapping her
auspicious ornaments in the upper-fringe of her sari, dropped in the midmost of those five Vanara-s
with a thinking that 'these creatures may perhaps indicate them to Rama.' [3-54-2, 3a]_END

B_3_C_52_26
BEGIN_
ताम् महा उल्काम् इव आकाशे दीप्यमानाम् स्व तेजसा |जहार आकाशम् आविश्य सीताम् वैश्रवण अनुजः || ३-५२-३१_END
BEGIN_
Ravana, the brother of Kubera, on invading the sky abducted that radiant Seetha who is radiating the 
sky by her own radiancy like a massive meteor. [3-52-31]_END

B_3_C_51_32
BEGIN_
तम् गृहीत्वा नखैः तीक्ष्णैः विददार समंततः |अधिरूढो गज आरोहो यथा स्यात् दुष्ट वारणम् || ३-५१-३४_END
BEGIN_
On clasping Ravana with incisive claws Jataayu lacerated deeply and rampantly, as a mahout, an elephant-trainer-controller, 
sitting astride on it will try to control an uncontrollable elephant that is running amok with an incisive 
goad. [3-51-34]_END

B_3_C_53_15
BEGIN_
न नूनम् च आत्मनः श्रेयः पथ्यम् वा समवेक्षसे || ३-५३-१६
मृत्यु काले यथा मर्त्यो विपरीतानि सेवते |_END
BEGIN_
"Definitely and completely unanticipated in your heart are either that which is
worthwhile or that which is beneficial to you, as mortals undertake a quirkily behaviour at the
time of their death..._END

B_3_C_54_2
BEGIN_
वस्त्रम् उत्सृज्य तन् मध्ये विनिक्षिप्तम् स भूषणम् || ३-५४-३
संभ्रमात् तु दशग्रीवः तत् कर्म न च बुद्ध्वान् |_END
BEGIN_
On his part that Decahedron Ravana has not noticed her action in whipping up her
silky upper-cloth and ornaments, their bundling and stowing away at five vanara-s, owing to his own
hurry. [3-54-3]_END

B_3_C_51_33
BEGIN_
विददार नखैः अस्य तुण्डम् पृष्ठे समर्पयन् |केशान् च उत्पाटयामास नख पक्ष मुख आयुधः || ३-५१-३५_END
BEGIN_
Weaponed only with his claws, wings, and beak, Jataayu not only tore the back of Ravana asunder applying 
his beak and claws, but started to tweeze even his hair. [3-51-35]_END

B_3_C_52_27
BEGIN_
तस्याः तानि अग्नि वर्णानि भूषणानि मही तले |स घोषाणि अवकीर्यन्त क्षीणाः तारा इव अंबरात् || ३-५२-३२_END
BEGIN_
Some of her ornaments which are lustrously flamy, for they are sparkling like the sparkles of fireworks, 
are strewn about on the plane of earth with much clatter like the stars pelted down from the sky. [3-52-32]_END

B_3_C_53_16
BEGIN_
मुमूर्षूणाम् तु सर्वेषाम् यत् पथ्यम् तत् न रोचते || ३-५३-१७
पश्यामि इव हि कण्ठे त्वाम् काल पाश अवपाशितम् |_END
BEGIN_
"But which is recuperative that is unpalatable to all of the death-rattlers, and
indeed, I behold you as one around whose throat the noose of Time is looped. [3-53-17b, 18a]_END

B_3_C_51_34
BEGIN_
स तथा गृध्र राजेन क्लिश्यमानो मुहुर् मुहुः |अमर्ष स्फुरित ओष्ठः सन् प्राकंपत स राक्षसः || ३-५१-३६_END
BEGIN_
His lips becoming intolerantly quivery when Ravana is exasperated by that king of eagles repetitiously, 
that demon staggered on to his right targeting the hovering eagle at his hind-side to fell it down. 
[3-51-36]_END

B_3_C_54_3
BEGIN_
पिंगाक्षाः ताम् विशालाक्षीम् नेत्रैः अनिमिषैः इव || ३-५४-४
विक्रोशन्तीम् तदा सीताम् ददृशुः वानर ऋषभाः |_END
BEGIN_
Those ochreish-eyed best Vanara-s with their unwinking eyes have observed the
broad-eyed Seetha, who at that time is verily wailing. [3-54-4b, 5a]_END

B_3_C_52_28
BEGIN_
तस्याः स्तन अन्तरात् भ्रष्टो हारः तारा अधिप द्युतिः |वैदेह्या निपतन् भाति गंगा इव गगनात् च्युता 
|| ३-५२-३३_END
BEGIN_
A multi-string pearl pendant, a rivi�re, that vies with the moonshine has glissaded from the medial 
of her breasts, and while glissading from sky it is sheeny like River Ganga while she glissaded from 
skies. [3-52-33]_END

B_3_C_53_17
BEGIN_
यथा च अस्मिन् भय स्थाने न बिभेषि दशानन || ३-५३-१८
व्यक्तम् हिरण्मयान् हि त्वम् संपश्यसि मही रुहान् |_END
BEGIN_
"As you are dauntless in this daunting situation as for yourself, oh, Decahedral
demon, indeed it is clear that you are clearly fantasising the ill-omened golden trees all around.
[3-53-18b, 19a]_END

B_3_C_51_35
BEGIN_
संपरिष्वज्य वैदेहीम् वामेन अंकेन रावणः |तलेन अभिजघान आर्तो जटायुम् क्रोध मूर्चितः || ३-५१-३७_END
BEGIN_
Ravana who is aggrieved and convulsed in fury hit back Jataayu with his palm while firmly clutching 
Vaidehi onto his left flank. [3-51-37]_END

B_3_C_52_29
BEGIN_
उत्पात वात अभिहता नाना द्विज गण आयुताः |मा भैः इति विधूत अग्रा व्याजह्रुः इव पादपाः || ३-५२-३४_END
BEGIN_
The trees on which diverse birds are perching have been stirred up with the wind blown and up-heaved 
by the gust of Ravana's flight, while the swaying motion of those treetops is as though waving hands 
to console Seetha saying, "fear not... fear not..." [3-52-34]_END

B_3_C_54_4
BEGIN_
स च पंपाम् अतिक्रम्य लंकाम् अभिमुखः पुरीम् || ३-५४-५
जगाम रुदतीम् गृह्य मैथिलीम् राक्षस ईश्वरः |_END
BEGIN_
The chief of demons Ravana captivating Maithili, who is still wailing, has crossed
the Pampa region down underneath and advanced facing the City of Lanka. [3-54-5b, 6a]_END

B_3_C_53_18
BEGIN_
नदीम् वैतरणीम् घोराम् रुधिर ओघ विवाहिनीम् || ३-५३-१९
खड्ग पत्र वनम् चैव भीमम् पश्यसि रावण |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Ravana, you will see the ghastly River Vaitarani which will be tumultuously
streaming with blood streams, also thus you will see the grisly sword-leaved-forests in hell.
[3-53-19b, 20a]_END

B_3_C_51_36
BEGIN_
जटायुः तम् अतिक्रम्य तुण्डेन अस्य खग अधिपः |वाम बाहून् दश तदा व्यपाहरत् अरिन्दमः || ३-५१-३८_END
BEGIN_
Jataayu, the lord of birds, being a vanquisher of enemies outstripped Ravana and ripped off ten left-arms 
of Ravana with his beak, with which left arms Ravana is clutching Vaidehi, in order to release her from 
his clutches. [3-51-38]_END

B_3_C_52_30
BEGIN_
नलिन्यो ध्वस्त कमलाः त्रस्त मीन जले चराः |सखीम् इव गत उत्साहाम् शोचन्ति इव स्म मैथिलीम् || ३-५२-३५_END
BEGIN_
With wilted lotuses and scared fishes and other beings moving in water the lotus lakes are unenthusiastically 
sorrowing for Maithili as though Seetha is their girlfriend._END

B_3_C_54_5
BEGIN_
ताम् जहार सुसंहृष्टो रावणो मृत्युम् आत्मनः || ३-५४-६
उत्संगेन एव भुजगीम् तीक्ष्ण दंष्ट्राम् महाविषाम् |_END
BEGIN_
Ravana is jubilantly happy in stealing his own death alias Seetha, as one would
carry a stingingly fanged and lethally venomous she-snake in his own lap. [3-54-6b, 7a]_END

B_3_C_53_19
BEGIN_
तप्त कांचन पुष्पाम् च वैदूर्य प्रवर च्छदाम् || ३-५३-२०
द्रक्ष्यसे शाल्मलीम् तीक्ष्णाम् आयसैः कण्टकैः चिताम् |_END
BEGIN_
"You will see silk-cotton trees flowered with molten gold, shrouded with lapis
gemlike melting leaves, and enshrouded with sharp irony thorns in hell. [3-53-20b, 21a]_END

B_3_C_51_37
BEGIN_
संच्छिन्न बाहोः सद्यो वै बाहवः सहसा अभवन् |विष ज्वालावली युक्ता वल्मीकत् इव पन्नगाः || ३-५१-३९_END
BEGIN_
Though his arms are mutilated thus, they instantaneously ricocheted from his body like snakes possessing 
a series of venomous blazes sprawling out from a snake pit. [3-51-39]_END

B_3_C_52_31
BEGIN_
समंतात् अभिसंपत्य सिंह व्याघ्र मृग द्विजाः |अन्वधावन् तदा रोषात् सीताम् छाया अनुगामिनः || ३-५२-३६_END
BEGIN_
All lions, tigers, animals and birds have then gathered in herds from all-over and ran rancorously and 
pursuantly shadowing the shadow of Seetha. [3-52-36]_END

B_3_C_54_6
BEGIN_
वनानि सरितः शैलान् सरांसि च विहायसा || ३-५४-७
स क्षिप्रम् समतीयाय शरः चापात् इव च्युतः |_END
BEGIN_
He bolted out in skyway up above the woodlands, waterways, pools, and mountains at
the double, as with an arrow bolting from a bow. [3-4-7b, 8a]_END

B_3_C_55_0
BEGIN_
संदिश्य राक्षसान् घोरान् रावणो अष्टौ महाबलान् |आत्मानम् बुद्धि वैक्लव्यात् कृत कृत्यम् अमन्यत || 
३-५५-१_END
BEGIN_
On directing those eight ghastly demons Ravana is amused in his heart of hearts that he has accomplished 
a great feat. [3-55-1]_END

B_3_C_53_20
BEGIN_
न हि त्वम् ईदृशम् कृत्वा तस्य अलीकम् महात्मनः || ३-५३-२१
धारितुम् शक्स्यसि चिरम् विषम् पीत्वा इव निर्घृणः |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, unmerciful one, on doing this kind of misdeed to that noble-souled Rama you are
incapable to bear up life for a long time like the one who quaffed venom. [3-53-21b, 22a]_END

B_3_C_51_38
BEGIN_
ततः क्रोद्धात् दशग्रीवः सीताम् उत्सृज्य वीर्यवान् |मुष्टिभ्याम् चरणाभ्याम् च गृध्र राजम् अपोथयत् 
|| ३-५१-४०_END
BEGIN_
The valorous Decahedron Ravana then threw off Seetha, and out of fury he scuffled with the king of eagles 
with fisticuffs and kicks, by both his feet and fists. [3-51-40]_END

B_3_C_54_7
BEGIN_
तिमि नक्र निकेतम् तु वरुण आलयम् अक्षयम् || ३-५४-८
सरिताम् शरणम् गत्वा समतीयाय सागरम् |_END
BEGIN_
On reaching the ocean, a housing for sharks, alligators, a home of Rain-god, a
never-draining deep and an ultimate course of the rivers, he hastily crossed it over. [3-54-8b,
9a]_END

B_3_C_55_1
BEGIN_
स चिंतयानो वैदेहीम् काम बाण संप्रपीडितः |प्रविवेश गृहम् रम्यम् सीताम् द्रष्टुम् अभित्वरन् || ३-५५-२_END
BEGIN_
On continually musing upon Vaidehi Ravana is tormented with the arrows of Love-god, thereby to lay eyes 
on Seetha he post-hastily entered the beautiful palace. [3-55-2]_END

B_3_C_52_32
BEGIN_
जल प्रपात अस्र मुखाः शृन्गैः उच्छ्रित बाहवः |सीतायाम् ह्रियमाणायाम् विक्रोशन्ति इव पर्वताः || ३-५२-३७_END
BEGIN_
The mountains appeared bewailing with their waterfalls as shedding tears and with their peaks as upraised 
arms, while Seetha is thus being abducted. [3-52-37]_END

B_3_C_53_21
BEGIN_
बद्धः त्वम् काल पाशेन दुर्निवारेण रावण || ३-५३-२२
क्व गतो लप्स्यसे शर्म भर्तुः मम महात्मनः |_END
BEGIN_
"You are bound by the unpreventable lasso of the Time, oh, Ravana, on going where
you will get complacency from that uncompromising husband of mine? [3-53-22b, 23a]_END

B_3_C_51_39
BEGIN_
ततो मुहूर्तम् संग्रामो बभूव अतुल वीर्ययोः |राक्षसानाम् च मुख्यस्य पक्षिणाम् प्रवरस्य च || ३-५१-४१_END
BEGIN_
Then there chanced an encounter for some time between those two valorous ones with mutually outweighing 
capabilities, namely the chieftain of demons and the chief of the birds. [3-51-41]_END

B_3_C_54_8
BEGIN_
संभ्रमात् परिवृत्त ऊर्मी रुद्ध मीन महोरगः || ३-५४-९
वैदेह्याम् ह्रियमाणायाम् बभूव वरुण आलयः |_END
BEGIN_
That ocean being the abode of Rain-god is highly flustered when Vaidehi is being
abducted over it, and its waves became topsy-turvy and its fishes and great marine-reptiles
remained shilly-shally. [3-54-9b, 10a]_END

B_3_C_55_2
BEGIN_
स प्रविश्य तु तत् वेश्म रावणो राक्षस अधिपः |अपश्यत् राक्षसी मध्ये सीताम् दुःख परायणम् || ३-५५-३_END
BEGIN_
On entering the palace-chamber that supremo of demons beheld Seetha overwhelmed with ruefulness amongst 
demonesses. [3-55-3]_END

B_3_C_52_33
BEGIN_
ह्रियमाणाम् तु वैदेहीम् दृष्ट्वा दीनो दिवाकरः |प्रविध्वस्त प्रभः श्रीमान् आसीत् पाण्डुर मण्डलः || 
३-५२-३८_END
BEGIN_
On seeing Vaidehi who is being abducted thus, magnificent Sun in firmament is saddened, and lowly weakened 
is his sunshine, palely whitened is his sun-disc, and faintly deadened is his solar constant. [3-52-38]_END

B_3_C_53_22
BEGIN_
निमेष अन्तर मात्रेण विना भ्रातरम् आहवे || ३-५३-२३
राक्षसा निहता येन सहस्राणि चतुर्दश |
कथम् स राघवो वीरः सर्व अस्त्र कुशलो बली || ३-५३-२४
न त्वाम् हन्यात् शरैः तीक्ष्णैः इष्ट भार्या अपहारिणम् |_END
BEGIN_
"By whom fourteen thousand demons are killed in war just within a minute,
single-handedly without any help from his brother, how then that brave and mighty Raghava, an
expert in all kinds of missiles, will not eliminate you, the stealer of his chosen wife, with his
mordant arrows?" Thus Seetha poured forth her ire at Ravana. [3-53-23b, 24, 25a]_END

B_3_C_51_40
BEGIN_
तस्य व्यायच्छमानस्य रामस्य अर्थे अथ रावणः |पक्षौ पादौ च पार्श्वौ च खड्गम् उद्धृत्य सो अच्छिनत् || 
३-५१-४२_END
BEGIN_
Ravana brandishing his sword at Jataayu, who is revolting for the sake of Rama, hewed off both of his 
wings, sides, and feet. [3-51-42]_END

B_3_C_54_9
BEGIN_
अन्तरिक्ष गता वाचः ससृजुः चारणाः तदा || ३-५४-१०
एतत् अन्तो दशग्रीव इति सिद्धाः तदा अब्रुवन् |_END
BEGIN_
Then the siddha-s and caarana-s available in airspace averred saying, "this alone is
the end of Decahedron Ravana." [3-54-10b, 11a]_END

B_3_C_55_3
BEGIN_
अश्रु पूर्ण मुखीम् दीनाम् शोक भार अवपीडिताम् |वायु वेगैः इव आक्रांताम् मज्जन्तीम् नावम् अर्णवे || 
३-५५-४मृग यूथ परिभ्रष्टाम् मृगीम् श्वभिः इव आवृताम् |अधोगत मुखीम् सीताम् ताम् अभ्येत्य निशाचरः 
|| ३-५५-५ताम् तु शोक वशात् दीनाम् अवशाम् राक्षस अधिपः |स बलात् दर्शयामास गृहम् देव गृह उपमम् 
|| ३-५५-६_END
BEGIN_
She whose visage is brimming over with tears, one browbeaten and downtrodden with the burden of bewail, 
one capsized like a boat that is about to capsize in an ocean spreadeagled with whirlwinds, and one 
alike an impala altogether swerved from its herd of impala yet hemmed in with dog-wolves, that nightwalker 
came nigh of such a Seetha whose face is downcast unwilling to see any, and to such a pitiable Seetha 
who is in the shackles of her sorrow, that supremo of demons compellingly started to show his palace 
which is similar to any paradisiacal palace. [3-55-4, 5, 6]_END

B_3_C_52_34
BEGIN_
न अस्ति धर्मः कुतः सत्यम् न आर्जवम् न अनृशंसता |यत्र रामस्य वैदेहीम् भार्याम् हरति रावणः || ३-५२-३९
इति भूतानि सर्वाणि गणशः पर्यदेवयन् |_END
BEGIN_
"When Ravana is abducting none other than the wife of Rama, then there is no probity. At such a juncture, 
how conscience can prevail? Unfounded are candour and compassion," thus the throngs of all beings overly 
regretted. [3-52-39, 40a]_END

B_3_C_53_23
BEGIN_
एतत् च अन्यत् च परुषम् वैदेही रावण अंक गा |
भय शोक समाविष्टा करुणम् विललाप ह || ३-५३-२५_END
BEGIN_
On saying this much and other exacting words, Vaidehi who has gone onto the flank of
Ravana, indeed lamented lamentably as her dismay is coalesced with her distress. [3-53-25b, c]_END

B_3_C_51_41
BEGIN_
स छिन्न पक्षः सहसा रक्षसा रौद्र कर्मणा |निपपात महा गृध्रो धरण्याम् अल्प जीवितः || ३-५१-४३_END
BEGIN_
When that demon of cruel actions has ruptured his wings that colossal eagle Jataayu immediately fell 
down to earth with a lessened life. [3-51-43]_END

B_3_C_54_10
BEGIN_
स तु सीताम् विचेष्टन्तीम् अंकेन आदाय रावणः || ३-५४-११
प्रविवेश पुरीम् लन्काम् रूपिणीम् मृत्युम् आत्मनः |_END
BEGIN_
Ravana entered the city of Lanka transporting Seetha, while she wriggling in his
flank, who appeared like the personified death of Ravana wriggling its way into his Lanka.
[3-54-11b, 12a]_END

B_3_C_55_4
BEGIN_
हर्म्य प्रासाद संबधम् स्त्री सहस्र निषेवितम् |नाना पक्षि गणैः जुष्टम् नाना रत्न समन्वितम् || ३-५५-७
दान्तकैः तापनीयैः च स्फाटिकै राजतैः तथा |वज्र वैदूर्य चित्रैः च स्तम्भैः दृष्टि मनोरमैः || ३-५५-८
दिव्य दुन्दुभि निर्घोषम् तप्त कांचन भूषणम् |_END
BEGIN_
That paradisiacal mansion house of Decahedral Ravana is congestive with innumerable cupolaed skyscrapers, 
adored with thousands of females, frequented by diverse bevies of birds, and it comprised of numerous 
gemstones. The pillars are amazingly gilded with engraving of ivory, gilt, quartz, silvern linocuts, 
and they are even embossed with diamonds and with lapis gems, which are heart-pleasing for a look. The 
drumbeats of divine drums are echoing in entire palace, and its archways are adorned with the gildings 
of pure gold. [3-55-7, 8, 9a]_END

B_3_C_52_35
BEGIN_
वित्रस्तका दीन मुखा रुरुदुः मृग पोतकाः || ३-५२-४०उद्वीक्ष्य उद्वीक्ष्य नयनैः अस्र पात आविल ईक्षणाः 
|_END
BEGIN_
Verily frightened are the fawns of deer, and their saddened faces are with tear shedding eyes with flustered 
looks, and they looked up and up at Seetha in sky and wept. [3-52-40b, 41a]_END

B_3_C_53_24
BEGIN_
तथा भृश आर्ताम् बहु चैव भाषिणीम्
विललाप पूर्वम् करुणम् च भामिनीम् |
जहार पापः तरुणीम् विवेष्टतीम्
नृपात्मजाम् आगत गात्र वेपथुम् || ३-५३-२६_END
BEGIN_
She who is highly agonised and weeping before talking, a ranter who ranted much, a
resentful lady who has come of age, and a pitiable whirler in the hands of demon whose whirligig
has transformed into spasmodic jerking of her body for deliverance from that sinner, and in that
way that sinner stole that princess Seetha. [3-53-26]_END

B_3_C_51_42
BEGIN_
तम् दृष्ट्वा पतितम् भूमौ क्षतज आर्द्रम् जटायुषम् |अभ्यधावत वैदेही स्व बंधुम् इव दुःखिता || ३-५१-४४_END
BEGIN_
On seeing Jataayu fallen on earth and dampened with blood Vaidehi fell into a fit of weeping and ran 
towards him as if he is her own relative. [3-51-44]_END

B_3_C_54_11
BEGIN_
सः अभिगम्य पुरीम् लंकाम् सुविभक्त महापथाम् || ३-५४-१२
संरूढ कक्ष्या बहुलम् स्वम् अंतः पुरम् आविशत् |_END
BEGIN_
On going towards the city Lanka that has well-symmetrized roadways, then he entered
his own palace-chambers which is with very many doors and chambers thronging with crowds._END

B_3_C_55_5
BEGIN_
सोपानम् कांचनम् चित्रम् आरुरोह तया सह || ३-५५-९दान्तका राजताः चैव गवाक्षाः प्रिय दर्शनाः |हेम 
जाला आवृताः च आसन् तत्र प्रासाद पंक्तयः || ३-५५-१०_END
BEGIN_
Ravana walked up the wonderful golden staircase along with Seetha, and the rows of skyscrapers with 
windows that are ivoried and silvered and with window-blinds are seen from the windows of the landing 
on that flight of stairs, which are also ivoried and silvered windows with window-blinds, and all are 
amusing for sight. [3-55-9b, 10]_END

B_3_C_52_36
BEGIN_
सुप्रवेपित गात्राः च बभूवुः वन देवताः || ३-५२-४१विक्रोशन्तीम् दृढम् सीताम् दृष्ट्वा दुःखम् तथा गताम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
On seeing Seetha who is undergoing anguish in that way the sylvan deities physically shuddered in a 
worst way. [3-52-41b, 42a]_END

B_3_C_56_0
BEGIN_
सा तथा उक्ता तु वैदेही निर्भया शोक कर्शिता |तृणम् अन्तरतः कृत्वा रावणम् प्रति अभाषत || ३-५६-१_END
BEGIN_
She that Vaidehi who is haggard by anguish boldly spoke to Ravana when he addressed her in that way, 
duly placing a blade of straw in between herself and Ravana. [3-56-1]_END

B_3_C_51_43
BEGIN_
तम् नील जीमूत निकाश कल्पम्सुपाण्डुर उरस्कम् उदार वीर्यम् |ददर्श लंका अधिपतिः पृथिव्याम्जटायुषम् 
शान्तम् इव अग्नि दावम् || ३-५१-४५_END
BEGIN_
Ravana, the monarch of Lanka, gazed at that worthily valorous Jataayu, who in his shine is like a blue-black 
cloud with a whitely white chest and who by now is like a quiescent fire-storm flattened onto ground. 
[3-51-45]_END

B_3_C_54_12
BEGIN_
तत्र ताम् असित अपांगाम् शोक मोह परायणाम् || ३-५४-१३
निदधे रावणः सीताम् मयो मायाम् इव आसुरीम् |_END
BEGIN_
Ravana placed down Seetha whose eyelashes are blackish and who is deep in
bewilderment caused by whimpering, therein his palace chambers, as demon Maya once kept his
lady-love, a nymphet called Hema, in a demonic Black Hole._END

B_3_C_55_6
BEGIN_
सुधा मणि विचित्राणि भूमि भागानि सर्वशः |दशग्रीवः स्व भवने प्रादर्शयत मैथिलीम् || ३-५५-११_END
BEGIN_
That Decahedral Ravana displayed the multiple stories of his own palace which is all over white-marbled 
and diamond encrusted to Maithili. [3-55-11]_END

B_3_C_52_37
BEGIN_
ताम् तु लक्ष्मण राम इति क्रोशन्तीम् मधुर स्वराम् || ३-५२-४२अवेक्षमाणाम् बहुशो वैदेहीम् धरणी तलम् 
|स ताम् आकुल केशान्ताम् विप्रमृष्ट विशेषकाम् |जहार आत्म विनाशाय दशग्रीवो मनस्विनाम् || ३-५२-४३_END
BEGIN_
She who is looking searchingly at the plane of earth for Rama or Lakshmana, and truly bawling in high-pitched 
but mellowly voice calling "Rama, Lakshmana", and whose hair-lengths are tousled, and whose felicitous 
vermilion mark on her forehead is smudged very untidily, that Decahedral demon abducted such an uncompromising 
husband-devout, Vaidehi, only for his self-ruination. [3-52-42a, 43]_END

B_3_C_56_1
BEGIN_
राजा दशरथो नाम धर्म सेतुः इव अचलः |सत्य सन्धः परिज्ञातो यस्य पुत्रः स राघवः || ३-५६-२_END
BEGIN_
"He whose son is Raghava, is a resolute king known as Dasharatha. That king is a kingly rampart for 
righteousness, a kingpin abiding in forthrightness and thereby his kingliness is well renowned in all 
worlds, and my husband Rama is such a king's son. [3-56-2]_END

B_3_C_51_44
BEGIN_
ततः तु तम् पत्ररथम् मही तलेनिपातितम् रावण वेग मर्दितम् |पुनः च संगृह्य शशि प्रभ आननारुरोद 
सीता जनक आत्मजा तदा || ३-५१-४३_END
BEGIN_
But then Seetha, the daughter of Janaka, whose face vies with moonshine hugged eagle Jataayu, whom Ravana 
has subjugated with his forcefulness and felled down onto the surface of earth, and she wept over incessantly. 
[3-51-46]_END

B_3_C_54_13
BEGIN_
अब्रवीत् च दशग्रीवः पिशाचीः घोर दर्शनाः || ३-५४-१४
यथा न एनाम् पुमान् स्त्री वा सीताम् पश्यति असम्मतः |_END
BEGIN_
That Decahedron Ravana also instructed the bogey-sightly bogeywomen, "your watch and
ward shall be in such a way that neither a female nor a male can see Seetha impermissibly."
[3-54-14b, 15a]_END

B_3_C_55_7
BEGIN_
दीर्घिकाः पुष्करिण्यः च नाना पुष्प समावृताः |रावणो दर्शयामास सीताम् शोक परायणाम् || ३-५५-१२_END
BEGIN_
Ravana continued to display the descendible wellsprings and leisure pools from which diverse flowers 
have sprung and overspread them, regardless of Seetha's languishing under her anguish. [3-55-12]_END

B_3_C_52_38
BEGIN_
ततः तु सा चारु दती शुचि स्मिताविना कृता बन्धु जनेन मैथिली |अपश्यती राघव लक्ष्मणाउ उभौविवर्ण 
वक्त्रा भय भार पीडिता || ३-५२-४४_END
BEGIN_
She who is already detracted from her kinsfolk in Mithila or in Ayodhya, that Maithili with pretty teeth 
and clean-cut smile is then distanced from the only two last kinsmen, for either Raghava or Lakshmana 
or both are unseen by her, and thus her face is paled for she is chastened by the cumber of consternation. 
[3-52-44]_END

B_3_C_56_2
BEGIN_
रामो नाम स धर्मात्मा त्रिषु लोकेषु विश्रुतः |दीर्घ बाहुः विशालाक्षो दैवतम् स पतिः मम || ३-५६-३_END
BEGIN_
"Such a Dasharatha's son who is virtue-souled one, who is highly renowned in all the three worlds for 
his ambidexterity and perspicacity, and who is known as Rama is my husband and a god to me. [3-56-3]_END

B_3_C_54_14
BEGIN_
मुक्ता मणि सुवर्णानि वस्त्राणि आभरणानि च || ३-५४-१५
यत् यत् इच्छेत् तत् एव अस्या देयम् मत् च्छंदतो यथा |_END
BEGIN_
"Whatever she wishes to have, gold, jewels, pearls, apparels or adornments, they all
be given to her as you would give me according to my whimsies. [3-54-15b, 16a]_END

B_3_C_55_8
BEGIN_
दर्शयित्वा तु वैदेहीम् कृत्स्नम् तत् भवन उत्तमम् |उवाच वाक्यम् पापात्मा सीताम् लोभितुम् इच्छया || 
३-५५-१३_END
BEGIN_
On flaunting his best palace in its entirety to Vaidehi that dirty-minded Ravana spoke this sentence 
to Seetha in order that she may be tempted on her own, lustily. [3-55-13]_END

B_3_C_56_3
BEGIN_
इक्ष्वाकूणाम् कुले जातः सिंह स्कन्धो महाद्युतिः |लक्ष्मणेन सह भ्रात्रा यः ते प्राणान् हरिष्यति || 
३-५६-४_END
BEGIN_
"He who took birth in Ikshvaku's dynasty is a great-resplendent one with his shoulders like those of 
a lion, and who comes here along with similarly lion-shouldered and nearly great-resplendent brother 
of his, namely Lakshmana, to take your lives away. Such Rama is my husband. [3-56-4]_END

B_3_C_55_9
BEGIN_
दश राक्षस कोट्यः च द्वाविंशतिः अथ अपराः |वर्जयित्वा जरा वृद्धान् बालान् च रजनीचरान् || ३-५५-१४
तेषाम् प्रभुः अहम् सीते सर्वेषाम् भीम कर्मणाम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Seetha, ten crores of first-rated demons are there, furthermore, twenty-two crores of demons of 
ghastly exploits are there, thus all put together, three hundred twenty millions of demons are there 
in Lanka, omitting the weakish, oldish, youngish demons. For all of them I am the lord." Thus Ravana 
started his self-eulogy. [3-55-14, 15a]_END

B_3_C_54_15
BEGIN_
या च वक्ष्यति वैदेहीम् वचनम् किंचित् अप्रियम् || ३-५४-१६
अज्ञानात् यदि वा ज्ञानान् न तस्या जीवितम् प्रियम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Whosoever speaks unpleasant words to Vaidehi in the least, either unknowingly or
knowingly, her life becomes unpleasant for herself." Thus Ravana ordered the chamber-demonesses.
[3-54-16b, 17a]_END

B_3_C_56_4
BEGIN_
प्रत्यक्षम् यदि अहम् तस्य त्वया स्याम् धर्षिता बलात् |शयिता त्वम् हतः संख्ये जनस्थाने यथा खरः || 
३-५६-५_END
BEGIN_
"Had I been forcibly humiliated by you in the presence of Rama, you too would have been killed by Rama 
in combat and by now you too would be sprawling on earth, as with Khara in Janasthaana, but you foxed 
him. However, such Rama is my husband. [3-56-5]_END

B_3_C_54_16
BEGIN_
तथा उक्त्वा राक्षसीः ताः तु राक्षसेन्द्रः प्रतापवान् || ३-५४-१७
निष्क्रम्य अन्तः पुरात् तस्मात् किम् कृत्यम् इति चिंतयन् |
ददर्श अष्टौ महावीर्यान् राक्षसान् पिशित अशनान् || ३-५४-१८_END
BEGIN_
On speaking to those demonesses thus that chief of demons exited from that palace
chamber, and giving a thought to what is to be done in sequel, then he gave audience to eight
highly vigorous demons, the feasters on raw-flesh. [3-54-17b, 18]_END

B_3_C_55_10
BEGIN_
सहस्रम् एकम् एकस्य मम कार्य पुरःसरम् || ३-५५-१५यत् इदम् राज्य तंत्रम् मे त्वयि सर्वम् प्रतिष्ठितम् 
|जीवितम् च विशालाक्षि त्वम् मे प्राणैः गरीयसी || ३-५५-१६_END
BEGIN_
"For every single work of mine a thousand servitors will rush in. Such as I am I pledge entire life 
of mine along with the suzerainty of this sovereign city-state Lanka to you, oh, broad-eyed lady, for 
you are loftier than my lives. [3-55-15b, 16]_END

B_3_C_56_5
BEGIN_
य एते राक्षसाः प्रोक्ता घोर रूपा महाबलाः |राघवे निर्विषाः सर्वे सुपर्णे पन्नगा यथा || ३-५६-६_END
BEGIN_
"Those demons who are spoken of you to be with ghastly forms and gruelling power, they all will become 
formless and powerless in face of Raghava, as with all snakes becoming non-poisonous earthworms in the 
face of Garuda, the Divine Eagle. Such Rama is my husband. [3-56-6]_END

B_3_C_54_17
BEGIN_
स तान् दृष्ट्वा महावीर्यो वर दानेन मोहितः |
उवाच तान् इदम् वाक्यम् प्रशस्य बल वीर्यतः || ३-५४-१९_END
BEGIN_
He who is egocentric by the boon awarded by Brahma for his invincibleness, that
Ravana on giving an audience to those eight demons spoke this sentence to them praiseful of their
might and valour. [3-54-19]_END

B_3_C_55_11
BEGIN_
बह्वीनाम् उत्तम स्त्रीणाम् मम यो असौ परिग्रहः |तासाम् त्वम् ईश्वरी सीते मम भार्या भव प्रिये || ३-५५-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Seetha, you will become an empress for all of the those countless females of finest fabric amassed 
by me, oh, dear, if only you marry me. [3-55-17]_END

B_3_C_56_6
BEGIN_
तस्य ज्या विप्रमुक्ताः ते शराः कांचन भूषणाः |शरीरम् विधमिष्यन्ति गंगा कूलम् इव ऊर्मयः || ३-५६-७_END
BEGIN_
"Those gilded arrows of Rama unloosened directly and unswervingly from his bowstring will utterly batter 
your body, as the waves of River Ganga will be battering that river's riverbanks. Such Rama is my husband. 
[3-56-7]_END

B_3_C_55_12
BEGIN_
साधु किम् ते अन्यया बुद्ध्या रोचयस्व वचो मम |भजस्व मा अभितप्तस्य प्रसादम् कर्तुम् अर्हसि || ३-५५-१८_END
BEGIN_
"You be keen on my amiable words and it will be apt of you to show compassion on me, for I have burning 
desire for you, and of what use is your thinking conversely about that long-lost Rama? [3-55-18]_END

B_3_C_54_18
BEGIN_
नाना प्रहरणाः क्षिप्रम् इतो गच्छत सत्वराः |
जनस्थानम् हत स्थानम् भूत पूर्वम् खर आलयम् || ३-५४-२०_END
BEGIN_
"You immediately take up multiple assaultive weaponry and begone from here to
Janasthaana speedily, a place now deadpanned for demons, which earlier was the placement of Khara.
[3-54-20]_END

B_3_C_56_7
BEGIN_
असुरैः वा सुरैः वा त्वम् यदि अवध्यो असि रावण |उत्पाद्य सुमहत् वैरम् जीवन् तस्य न मोक्ष्यसे || ३-५६-८_END
BEGIN_
"Even if you are unkillable either by gods or by demons, you Ravana, you will not be disenthralled by 
Rama while you are alive, for you hatched a very great animosity in him against you. [3-56-8]_END

B_3_C_55_13
BEGIN_
परिक्षिप्ता समुद्रेण लंका इयम् शत योजना |न इयम् धर्षयितुम् शक्या स इन्द्रैः अपि सुर असुरैः || ३-५५-१९_END
BEGIN_
"It is impossible to assail this Lanka even for Indra with all of the gods and demons, as an ocean roundly 
enshrouds this Lanka which is hundred-yojana-s witdthwise. [3-55-19]_END

B_3_C_54_19
BEGIN_
तत्र उष्यताम् जनस्थाने शून्ये निहत राक्षसे |
पौरुषम् बलम् आश्रित्य त्रासम् उत्सृज्य दूरतः || ३-५४-२१_END
BEGIN_
"Throwaway your fright faraway and you stay in that Janasthaana which fell void as
the demons are voided by someone called Rama, and there you shall stay self-assuredly and
self-confidently. [3-54-21]_END

B_3_C_55_14
BEGIN_
न देवेषु न यक्षेषु न गंधर्वेषु न ऋषिषु |अहम् पश्यामि लोकेषु यो मे वीर्य समो भवेत् || ३-५५-२०_END
BEGIN_
"I behold none matchable to my vitality is existent among gods; among yaksha-s - no; among gandharva-s 
- no; among sages - no, nor anyone in any world. [3-55-20]_END

B_3_C_56_8
BEGIN_
स ते जीवित शेषस्य राघवो अन्त करो बली |पशोः यूप गतस्य इव जीवितम् तव दुर्लभम् || ३-५६-९_END
BEGIN_
"That mighty Rama will become the terminator of the vestige of your life, and as with an animal fastened 
to the stake of sacrifice your life too will become irretrievable. [3-56-9]_END

B_3_C_54_20
BEGIN_
बहु सैन्यम् महावीर्यम् जनस्थाने निवेशितम् |
स दूषण खरम् युद्धे निहतम् राम सायकैः || ३-५४-२२_END
BEGIN_
"Though highly forceful forces are deployed in Janasthaana, Rama's arrows have
utterly destroyed them, together with Khara and Duushana. [3-54-22]_END

B_3_C_55_15
BEGIN_
राज्य भ्रष्टेन दीनेन तापसेन पदातिना |किम् करिष्यसि रामेण मानुषेण अल्प तेजसा || ३-५५-२१_END
BEGIN_
"What can you achieve with that dethroned, hapless, seer, vagrant Rama who is short-lived, for after 
all, he is a human with littlest vitality? [3-55-21]_END

B_3_C_56_9
BEGIN_
यदि पश्येत् स रामः त्वाम् रोष दीप्तेन चक्षुषा |रक्षः त्वम् अद्य निर्दग्धो यथा रुद्रेण मन्मधः || 
३-५६-१०_END
BEGIN_
"If he that Rama glances you with his rancour-torched eyes, you demon, you will be completely burnt 
down now itself, as with Love-god burnt down by Furious Shiva. [3-56-10]_END

B_3_C_54_21
BEGIN_
ततः क्रोधो मम अपूर्वो धैर्यस्य उपरि वर्धते |
वैरम् च सुमहत् जातम् रामम् प्रति सुदारुणम् || ३-५४-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Thereby an unprecedented fury is escalating over and above my courage, and an
unhindered and unforgivable animosity towards that Rama is evoked in me. [3-54-23]_END

B_3_C_55_16
BEGIN_
भजस्व सीते माम् एव भर्ता अहम् सदृशः तव |यौवनम् हि अध्रुवम् भीरु रमस्व इह मया सह || ३-५५-२२_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Seetha, you apotheosise me only for I am your seemliest husband, oh, jumpy lady, indeed, primeness 
has impermanence, thus here you be blithesome with me. [3-55-22]_END

B_3_C_57_0
BEGIN_
राक्षसम् मृग रूपेण चरन्तम् काम रूपिणम् |निहत्य रामो मारीचम् तूर्णम् पथि न्यवर्तत || ३-५७-१_END
BEGIN_
Rama on killing that demon Maareecha, who is a guise changer at his wish and who moved about in the 
guise of a deer, instantly started to return on the trail by which he trailed after that deer-demon. 
[3-57-1]_END

B_3_C_56_10
BEGIN_
यः चन्द्रम् नभसो भूमौ पातयेन् नाशयेत वा |सागरम् शोषयेत् वा अपि स सीताम् मोचयेत् इह || ३-५६-११_END
BEGIN_
"He that Rama who hurls down the moon from skies onto earth, or else extirpates it if need be, or even 
desiccates an ocean, he alone rescues Seetha from here. [3-56-11]_END

B_3_C_54_22
BEGIN_
निर्यातयितुम् इच्छामि तत् च वैरम् अहम् रिपोः |
न हि लप्स्यामि अहम् निद्राम् अहत्वा संयुगे रिपुम् || ३-५४-२४_END
BEGIN_
"I wish to cast out my begrudging against my enemy who bears a grudge against me,
and indeed, to me 'sleep' is not the word for it, until my enemy is undone in a war. [3-54-24]_END

B_3_C_55_17
BEGIN_
दर्शने मा कृथाः बुद्धिम् राघवस्य वरानने |का अस्य शक्तिः इह आगंतुम् अपि सीते मनोरथैः || ३-५५-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, beautifully visaged lady, it is needless to have half a mind to see that Raghava, oh, Seetha, even 
if his wits chariot him what is his calibre to come thither crossing an un-crossable ocean? [3-55-23]_END

B_3_C_57_1
BEGIN_
तस्य संत्वरमाणस्य द्रष्टु कामस्य मैथिलीम् |क्रूर स्वरो अथ गोमायुः विननाद अस्य पृष्ठतः || ३-५७-२_END
BEGIN_
While Rama is anxiously hurrying to see Maithili, then a brutish voiced jackal deafeningly howled at 
his behind. [3-57-2]_END

B_3_C_56_11
BEGIN_
गत आयुः त्वम् गत श्रीकः गत सत्त्वो गत इन्द्रियः |लंका वैधव्य संयुक्ता त्वत् कृतेन भविष्यति || ३-५६-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Gone is your liveability, gone is your prosperity, gone is your vivacity, and gone is your faculty. 
Thus Lanka is widowed by a single deed of yours. [3-56-12]_END

B_3_C_54_23
BEGIN_
तम् तु इदानीम् अहम् हत्वा खर दूषण घातिनम् |
रामम् शर्म उपलप्स्यामि धनम् लब्ध्वा इव निर्धनः || ३-५४-२५_END
BEGIN_
"I for myself will be comfortable only on eliminating him who has eliminated Khara
and Duushana as with a pauper acquiring riches. [3-54-25]_END

B_3_C_57_2
BEGIN_
स तस्य स्वरम् आज्ञाय दारुणम् रोम हर्षणम् |चिंतयामास गोमायोः स्वरेण परिशन्कितः || ३-५७-३_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that threatening and hair-raising howl of jackal Rama is overly threatened just by the tone 
of fox in which it is foreboding, inasmuch as the forbidding intoning of Maareecha. [3-57-3]_END

B_3_C_55_18
BEGIN_
न शक्यो वायुः आकाशे पाशैः बद्धम् महाजवः |दीप्यमानस्य वा अपि अग्नेः ग्रहीतुम् विमलाम् शिखाम् || ३-५५-२४_END
BEGIN_
"It is impossible to knot the currents of cyclonic gusts in mid air, more so, it is impracticable to 
lay hold on the tongues of radiately irradiant fire. [3-55-24]_END

B_3_C_56_12
BEGIN_
न ते पापम् इदम् कर्म सुख उदर्कम् भविष्यति |या अहम् नीता विना भावम् पति पार्श्वात् त्वया वनात् || 
३-५६-१३_END
BEGIN_
"In forest you have separated me from the propinquity of my husband, which diabolic deed of yours will 
not result in any ultimate happiness for you. [3-56-13]_END

B_3_C_54_24
BEGIN_
जनस्थाने वसद्भिः तु भवद्भिः रामम् आश्रिता |
प्रवृत्तिः उपनेतव्या किम् करोति इति तत्त्वतः || ३-५४-२६_END
BEGIN_
"While you remain in Janasthaana you have to accurately bring me the information
about Rama's activities and deportment. [3-54-26]_END

B_3_C_57_3
BEGIN_
अशुभम् बत मन्ये अहम् गोमायुः वाश्यते यथा |स्वस्ति स्यात् अपि वैदेह्या राक्षसैः भक्षणम् विना || ३-५७-४_END
BEGIN_
"Huh! As to how this jackal has howled I deem that as inauspicious. As yet undevoured by demons would 
Vaidehi be safe? [3-57-4]_END

B_3_C_55_19
BEGIN_
त्रयाणाम् अपि लोकानाम् न तम् पश्यामि शोभने |विक्रमेण नयेत् यः त्वाम् मत् बाहु परिपालिताम् || ३-५५-२५_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, benefactress of bliss, he who can lead you back with his valour, while you are being fended off 
by my mighty arms, him I do not envisage even in any one world of this threefold world. [3-55-25]_END

B_3_C_56_13
BEGIN_
स हि देवर - दैवत - संयुक्तो मम भर्ता महाद्युतिः |निर्भयो वीर्यम् आश्रित्य शून्ये वसति दण्डके || 
३-५६-१४_END
BEGIN_
"In fact, that great-resplendent husband of mine, Rama, is still residing in the eremitical Dandaka 
forest, bravely hinging on to his own valour, in tandem only with my brother-in-law. [3-56-14]_END

B_3_C_54_25
BEGIN_
अप्रमादात् च गंतव्यम् सर्वैः एव निशाचरैः |
कर्तव्यः च सदा यत्नो राघवस्य वधम् प्रति || ३-५४-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Do not go heedlessly, you all night-walkers, for that Rama appears to be too
dangerous, and on your going there heedfully, you have to continually try for the elimination of
that Raghava. [3-54-27]_END

B_3_C_55_20
BEGIN_
लंकायाम् सुमहत् राज्यम् इदम् त्वम् अनुपालय |त्वत् प्रेष्या मत् विधा चैव देवाः च अपि चर अचरम् || 
३-५५-२६_END
BEGIN_
"You rule over this very great empire of Lanka as an empress of Lanka, while me and mine, also thus 
all gods like me who hitherto are under my rule, and all mobile and sessile entities of whom I am the 
ruler, they too will hereafter make ourselves useful as your royal stewards, if you marry me. [3-55-26]_END

B_3_C_57_4
BEGIN_
मारीचेन तु विज्ञाय स्वरम् आलक्ष्य मामकम् |विक्रुष्टम् मृग रूपेण लक्ष्मणः शृणुयात् यदि || ३-५७-५
स सौमित्रिः स्वरम् श्रुत्वा ताम् च हित्वा अथ मैथिलीम् |तया एव प्रहितः क्षिप्रम् मत् सकाशम् इह एष्यति 
|| ३-५७-६_END
BEGIN_
"On knowing the nature of my voice Maareecha in the semblance of a deer yelled out mimicking my voice. 
If Lakshmana listens that voice, recognising it as my voice he will instantly rush to my near. Else 
if Maithili listens, she will hasten him to go over here and Soumitri instantly rushes here leaving 
her off. [3-57-5, 6]_END

B_3_C_56_14
BEGIN_
स ते वीर्यम् दर्पम् बलम् उत्सेकम् च तथा विधम् |अपनेष्यति गात्रेभ्यः शर वर्षेण संयुगे || ३-५६-१५_END
BEGIN_
"With storms of his arrows in a given combat my husband will dislodge arrogance, insolence, puissance, 
like that impudence from every limb of yours. [3-56-15]_END

B_3_C_54_26
BEGIN_
युष्माकम् तु बलम् ज्ञातम् बहुशो रण मूर्धनि |
अतः तु अस्मिन् जनस्थाने मया यूयम् नियोजिताः || ३-५४-२८_END
BEGIN_
"I am aware of your might in battle fronts for a number of times, as such I have
commissioned you all in that Janasthaana." Thus Ravana spoke to those eight demons. [3-54-28]_END

B_3_C_55_21
BEGIN_
अभिषेक उदक क्लिन्ना तुष्टा च रमयस्व माम् |दुष्कृतम् यत् पुरा कर्म वन वासेन तद् गतम् || ३-५५-२७
यत् च ते सुकृतो धर्मः तस्य इह फलम् आप्नुहि |_END
BEGIN_
"Wet with the waters of anointment you be elated and then delight me. By your damnable dwelling in forests 
bygone is your bad-luck that you misdealt in bygone times. And what dutiable good deed is to be done 
by you in marrying me, you do that now, and secure the fruits of that good deed here by marrying me. 
[3-55-27, 28a]_END

B_3_C_57_5
BEGIN_
राक्षसैः सहितैर् नूनम् सीताया ईप्सितो वधः |कांचनः च मृगो भूत्वा व्यपनीय आश्रमात् तु माम् || ३-५७-७
दूरम् नीत्वा अथ मारीचो राक्षसो अभूत् शर आहतः |हा लक्ष्मण हतो अस्मि इति यत् वाक्यम् व्यजहार ह || 
३-५७-८_END
BEGIN_
"As could be seen from Maareecha's becoming a Golden Deer only to sidetrack and take me away from hermitage, 
his becoming a demon when hit with an arrow, and his shouting words indeed like, 'ha, Lakshmana, ha, 
Seetha, I am killed,' the demons are collectively intending to do away with Seetha. It is certain. [3-57-7, 
8]_END

B_3_C_56_15
BEGIN_
यदा विनाशो भूतानाम् दृश्यते काल चोदितः |तदा कार्ये प्रमाद्यन्ति नराः काल वशम् गताः || ३-५६-१६_END
BEGIN_
"As and when ruination of created beings manifests actuated by Time, then all of them will place their 
behaviour in endangerment, as they have gone under the control of End-Time. [3-56-16]_END

B_3_C_54_27
BEGIN_
ततः प्रियम् वाक्यम् उपेत्य राक्षसा
महाअर्थम् अष्टौ अभिवाद्य रावणम् |
विहाय लंकाम् सहिताः प्रतस्थिरे
यतो जनस्थानम् अलक्ष्य दर्शनाः || ३-५४-२९_END
BEGIN_
Then on picking up those words amiable to all intents and purposes of Ravana, those
eight demons departed from Lanka on hailing Ravana, and they collectively journeyed in the
direction of Janasthaana with their imperceivable appearances. [3-54-29]_END

B_3_C_55_22
BEGIN_
इह सर्वाणि माल्यानि दिव्य गंधानि मैथिलि || ३-५५-२८भूषणानि च मुख्यानि तानि सेव मया सह |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Maithili, here all the garlands are divinely fragranced and the jewellery is topmost, you will 
dress up with them along with me should you become my wife. [3-55-28b]_END

B_3_C_57_6
BEGIN_
अपि स्वस्ति भवेत् द्वाभ्याम् रहिताभ्याम् मया वने |जनस्थान निमित्तम् हि कृत वैरो अस्मि राक्षसैः || 
३-५७-९निमित्तानि च घोराणि दृश्यन्ते अद्य बहूनि च |_END
BEGIN_
"Whether there will be safety in forest for those two in my absence, or not, is my doubt. Owing to my 
devastating Janasthaana I have become a harboured grudge for demons, am not I! As such, foretokens are 
appearing now, severely and severally." Thus Rama's thoughts have sprinted. [3-57-9, 10a]_END

B_3_C_56_16
BEGIN_
माम् प्रधृष्य स ते कालः प्राप्तो अयम् रक्षस अधम |आत्मनो राक्षसानाम् च वधाय अन्तः पुरस्य च || ३-५६-१७_END
BEGIN_
"This is that time which has bechanced on you owing to your molesting me, you basely demon, by which 
time-factor yourself, all of your demons, and even all of your queens in the Chambers of Queens will 
be devastated. [3-56-17]_END

B_3_C_54_28
BEGIN_
ततः तु सीताम् उपलभ्य रावणः
सुसंप्रहृष्टः परिगृह्य मैथिलीम् |
प्रसज्य रामेण च वैरम् उत्तमम्
बभूव मोहात् मुदितः स राक्षसः || ३-५४-३०_END
BEGIN_
Ravana is then highly gladdened well and truly on gaining over Seetha, and even for
holding sway over that Maithili, and equally for the well-wrought and archly animosity with Rama,
whereby that demon Ravana is hypocritically amused. [3-54-30]_END

B_3_C_55_23
BEGIN_
पुष्पकम् नाम सुश्रोणि भ्रातुः वैश्रवणस्य मे || ३-५५-२९विमानम् सूर्य संकाशम् तरसा निर्जितम् रणे |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, well-waisted lady, just by my might I notched up an aircraft known as Pushpaka from my brother 
Kubera in a war with him, which is similar sun in its shine. [3-55-29b. 30a]_END

B_3_C_58_0
BEGIN_
स दृष्ट्वा लक्ष्मणम् दीनम् शून्यम् दशरथ आत्मजः |पर्यपृच्छत धर्माअत्मा वैदेहीम् आगतम् विना || ३-५८-१_END
BEGIN_
On seeing dreary Lakshmana coming into the void of forest devoid of Vaidehi, then the virtue-souled 
Rama, the son of Dasharatha, has asked him impatiently. [3-58-1]_END

B_3_C_57_7
BEGIN_
इति एवम् चिंतयन् रामः श्रुत्वा गोमायु निःस्वनम् || ३-५७-१०निवर्तमानः त्वरितो जगाम आश्रमम् आत्मवान् 
|आत्मनः च अपनयनम् मृग रूपेण रक्षसा || ३-५७-११_END
BEGIN_
When that soulful Rama has heard the whistle of jackal while returning, he persistently thought in this 
way about his detour caused by demon in the disguise of a deer, thus he speedily advanced towards his 
hermitage. [3-57-10b, 11]_END

B_3_C_56_17
BEGIN_
न शक्या यज्ञ मध्यस्था वेदिः स्रुक् भाण्ड मण्डिता |द्विजाति मंत्र संपूता चण्डालेन अवमर्दितुम् || 
३-५६-१८_END
BEGIN_
"It is impossible for a profaner to heavily tread on the Altar of Fire amidst a Ritual Hall surrounded 
by oblational vessels, further sanctified by Vedic hymns. [3-56-18]_END

B_3_C_55_24
BEGIN_
विशालम् रमणीयम् च तत् विमानम् मनो जवम् || ३-५५-३०तत्र सीते मया सार्धम् विहरस्व यथा सुखम् |_END
BEGIN_
"That aircraft is expansive and exhilarating, also its speed is on par with intuition, oh, Seetha, in 
that you can cheerfully fly about along with me, should you marry me. [3-55-30b, 31a]_END

B_3_C_57_8
BEGIN_
आजगाम जनस्थानम् राघवः परिशन्कितः |तम् दीन मानसम् दीनम् आसेदुः मृग पक्षिणः || ३-५७-१२_END
BEGIN_
Raghava came to Janasthaana doubting overly, and the animals and birds of Janasthaana which look doleful 
have neared him whose heart has become doleful. [3-57-12]_END

B_3_C_58_1
BEGIN_
प्रस्थितम् दण्डक अरण्यम् या माम् अनुजगाम ह |क्व सा लक्ष्मण वैदेही याम् हित्वा त्वम् इह आगतः || ३-५८-२_END
BEGIN_
"She who has come in tow with me to Dandaka forest when I started for peregrination, whom you have now 
deserted and came here, oh, Lakshmana, she that Vaidehi, where is she? [3-58-2]_END

B_3_C_56_18
BEGIN_
तथा अहम् धर्म नित्यस्य धर्म पत्नी दृढ व्रता |त्वया संप्रष्टुम् न शक्या अहम् राक्षसाधम पापिना || 
३-५६-१९_END
BEGIN_
"Likewise, I am the solemnly pledged legitimate wife of one who steadied himself in righteousness, and 
such as I am, you basely demon, it is impossible for you trespasser to touch me even. [3-56-19]_END

B_3_C_55_25
BEGIN_
वदनम् पद्म संकाशम् विमलम् चारु दर्शनम् || ३-५५-३१शोक आर्तम् तु वरारोहे न भ्राजति वर आनने |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, lady with a comely countenance, your visage is lotus similar in its shine, besides being immaculate, 
fairish and eyeful, but oh, curvaceous lady, with such a mushily maudlin of such a face this palace 
of mine is unbright, thus marry me to brighten everything" Thus Ravana spoke to Seetha. [3-55-31b, 32a]_END

B_3_C_58_2
BEGIN_
राज्य भ्रष्टस्य दीनस्य दण्डकान् परिधावतः |क्व सा दुःख सहाया मे वैदेही तनु मध्यमा || ३-५८-३_END
BEGIN_
"When I have become forlorn with the forfeiture of my kingdom and when I was rushing for Dandaka forest 
she stood with me as a partaker in my woes. She that comely Vaidehi, where is she? [3-58-3]_END

B_3_C_57_9
BEGIN_
सव्यम् कृत्वा महात्मानम् घोराम् च ससृजुः स्वरान् |तानि दृष्ट्वा निमित्तानि महाघोराणि राघवः |
न्यवर्तत अथ त्वरितो जवेन आश्रमम् आत्मनः || ३-५७-१३_END
BEGIN_
Those doleful animals and birds moving in circumambulations from the left side to right of that noble-souled 
Rama they let off frightening shrieks, and then observing those highly forbidding foretokens Rama returned 
to his own hermitage hastily and hurriedly. [3-57-13]_END

B_3_C_56_19
BEGIN_
क्रीडन्ती राज हंसेन पद्म षँडेषु नित्यशः |हंसी सा तृण षण्डस्थम् कथम् द्रक्षेत मद्गुकम् || ३-५६-२०_END
BEGIN_
"How a she-swan ever frolicking with majestic swans in bunches of lotuses can leer at a water-crow sneaking 
in a bunch of grass? [3-56-20]_END

B_3_C_55_26
BEGIN_
एवम् वदति तस्मिन् सा वस्त्र अन्तेन वर अंगना || ३-५५-३२पिधाय इन्दु निभम् सीता मंदम् अश्रून् अवर्तयत् 
|_END
BEGIN_
While Ravana is speaking to her in this way that graceful lady Seetha veiled her moonier face with fringe 
of her sari, and stiflingly dispelled tears on that mooniest face behind her half-veil. [3-55-32b, 33a]_END

B_3_C_58_3
BEGIN_
याम् विना न उत्सहे वीर मुहूर्तम् अपि जीवितुम् |क्व सा प्राण सहाया मे सीता सुर सुत उपमा || ३-५८-४_END
BEGIN_
"Without whom I am disinclined to live even for a moment, oh, valiant one, such a Seetha who in simile 
is like the daughter of deities and who is my life-force, where is she? [3-58-4]_END

B_3_C_57_10
BEGIN_
ततो लक्षणम् आयान्तम् ददर्श विगत प्रभम् |ततो अविदूरे रामेण समीयाय स लक्ष्मणः || ३-५७-१४विषण्णः 
स विषण्णेन दुःखितो दुःख भागिना |_END
BEGIN_
Then Rama saw Lakshmana coming towards him with a lacklustre face, and then Lakshmana, who is melancholic 
and anguishing in his divergence from Seetha, met Rama not a long-way-off, where Rama is a similar partaker 
in melancholy and anguishing by way of his convergence upon ill-omens. [3-57-14, 15a]_END

B_3_C_56_20
BEGIN_
इदम् शरीरम् निःसंज्ञम् बन्ध वा घातयस्व वा |न इदम् शरीरम् रक्ष्यम् मे जीवितम् वा अपि राक्षस || ३-५६-२१
न तु शक्यामि उपक्रोशम् पृथिव्याम् धातुम् आत्मनः |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, demon, you may either trammel or vandalise this inertial body of mine. I claim neither this body 
nor life of mine as my own. But I am intolerant to bear with any disrepute on this earth." Thus Seetha 
castigated Ravana. [3-56-21, 22a]_END

B_3_C_55_27
BEGIN_
ध्यायन्तीम् ताम् इव अस्वस्थाम् सीताम् चिंता हत प्रभाम् || ३-५५-३३उवाच वचनम् वीरो रावणो रजनी चरः 
|_END
BEGIN_
