To her who is disconcerted and whose anguish marred her brilliance and who is appearing as though pondering 
over the question of her submittal to Ravana, or otherwise, although she is meditating, to such a Seetha 
Ravana the nightwalker said these words. [3-55-33b, 34a]_END

B_3_C_57_11
BEGIN_
संजगर्हे अथ तम् भ्राता दृष्टा लक्ष्मणम् आगतम् || ३-५७-१५विहाय सीताम् विजने वने राक्षस सेविते |_END
BEGIN_
On seeing Lakshmana who has arrived at this place leaving off Seetha in a forest that is desolate, more 
so an adorable forest for demons, Rama reproached him as his elder brother. [3-57-15b, 16a]_END

B_3_C_58_4
BEGIN_
पतित्वम् अमराणाम् वा पृथिव्याः च अपि लक्ष्मण |विना ताम् तपनीय आभाम् न इच्छेयम् जनक आत्मजाम् || ३-५८-५_END
BEGIN_
"I am unambitious for the rulership either on heavens or on the earth, oh, Lakshmana, without the daughter 
of Janaka whose aspect glisters like gold. [3-58-5]_END

B_3_C_56_21
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्त्वा तु वैदेही क्रोद्धात् सु परुषम् वचः || ३-५६-२२रावणम् मैथिली तत्र पुनः न उवाच किंचन |_END
BEGIN_
Vaidehi on speaking those highly caustic words angrily to Ravana in this way, she that Maithili spoke 
no more in that matter. [3-56-22b, 23a]_END

B_3_C_55_28
BEGIN_
अलम् व्रीडेन वैदेहि धर्म लोप कृतेन ते || ३-५५-३४आर्षो अयम् देवि निष्यन्दो यः त्वाम् अभिगमिष्यति 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Vaidehi, enough is this embarrassment of yours presuming that your consorting with me is detrimental 
to scriptural canons, oh, empress, what that is approaching you in the form of queen-hood is absolutely 
compatible with the tradition._END

B_3_C_57_12
BEGIN_
गृहीत्वा च करम् सव्यम् लक्ष्मणम् रघुनंदनः || ३-५७-१६उवाच मधुर उदर्कम् इदम् परुषम् आर्तवत् |_END
BEGIN_
Taking Lakshmana's left hand into his, Rama, the descendent of Raghu, alike a bewailer spoke this brusque 
speech that has a mellowly fruition in future. [3-57-16b, 17a]_END

B_3_C_58_5
BEGIN_
कच्चित् जीवति वैदेही प्राणैः प्रियतरा मम |कच्चित् प्रव्राजनम् वीर न मे मिथ्या भविष्यति || ३-५८-६_END
BEGIN_
"Vaidehi who is dearer to me than my lives, will she be alive somehow! Oh, valiant Lakshmana, this peregrination 
of mine, will it not become futile, someway! [3-58-6]_END

B_3_C_56_22
BEGIN_
सीताया वचनम् श्रुत्वा परुषम् रोम हर्षणम् || ३-५६-२३प्रति उवाच ततः सीताम् भय संदर्शनम् वचः |_END
BEGIN_
On hearing Seetha's scathing and hair-raising censures, then Ravana retorted with these intimidatory 
chides. [3-56-23b, 24a]_END

B_3_C_55_29
BEGIN_
एतौ पादौ मया स्निग्धौ शिरोभिः परिपीडितौ || ३-५५-३५प्रसादम् कुरु मे क्षिप्रम् वश्यो दासो अहम् अस्मि 
ते |_END
BEGIN_
"Let these two feet of yours be massaged by my ten heads, do me favour readily, for I am your subordinate 
and servant. [3-55-35b. 36a]_END

B_3_C_58_6
BEGIN_
सीता निमित्तम् सौमित्रे मृते मयि गते त्वयि |कच्चित् स कामा सुखिता कैकेयी सा भविष्यति || ३-५८-७_END
BEGIN_
"When I am dead for the sake of Seetha and when you get back to Ayodhya lonesomely, and when Kaikeyi's 
wishes are accomplished thus, oh, Soumitri, will she be comfortable, somewhat! [3-58-7]_END

B_3_C_57_13
BEGIN_
अहो लक्ष्मण गर्ह्यम् ते कृतम् यः त्वम् विहाय ताम् || ३-५७-१७सीताम् इह आगतः सौम्य कच्चित् स्वस्ति 
भवेत् इति |_END
BEGIN_
"You have done a deplorable deed in coming here forsaking Seetha. Now, oh, gentle Lakshmana, are we 
somewhat safe, or everything has already gone astray now itself, or what. [3-57-17b, 18a]_END

B_3_C_56_23
BEGIN_
शृणु मैथिलि मत् वाक्यम् मासान् द्वादश भामिनि || ३-५६-२४कालेन अनेन न अभ्येषि यदि माम् चारु हासिनि 
|ततः त्वाम् प्रातः आशा अर्थम् सूदाः छेत्स्यन्ति लेशशः || ३-५६-२५_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, angry lady Maithili, listen to my words. A period of twelve months is given to you. And oh, smiley 
smiler, if you do not come nigh of me within that period, then the cooks will slice you to pieces for 
the purpose of a morning meal." [3-56-24b, 25]_END

B_3_C_55_30
BEGIN_
इमाः शून्या मया वाचः शुष्यमाणेन भाषिताः || ३-५५-३६न च अपि रावणः कांचित् मूर्ध्ना स्त्रीम् प्रणमेत 
ह |_END
BEGIN_
"I with a lustful hollow-heart spoke all these hollow words that are unbefitting to my stature, indeed, 
Ravana will never supplicate headlong to whosoever woman. [3-55-36b, 36c]_END

B_3_C_58_7
BEGIN_
स पुत्र राज्याम् सिद्ध अर्थाम् मृत पुत्रा तपस्विनी |उपस्थास्यति कौसल्या कच्चित् सौम्येन - सौम्य 
न - कैकयीम् || ३-५८-८_END
BEGIN_
"Kaikeyi is with her son, with a kingdom, and further her 'purposes are achieved,' oh, gentle Lakshmana, 
and because of the death of her son will my austerely mother Kausalya humbly get into the servitude 
of Kaikeyi, anyhow! [3-58-8]_END

B_3_C_57_14
BEGIN_
न मे अस्ति संशयो वीर सर्वथा जनकात्मजा || ३-५७-१८विनष्टा भक्षिता वा अप राक्षसैः वन चारिभिः |अशुभानि 
एव भूयिष्ठम् यथा प्रादुर् भवन्ति मे || ३-५७-१९_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, brave one, according to these many inauspicious forebodings that have manifested themselves to 
me, we might have lost Janaka's daughter Seetha, or the forest ranging demons might have devoured her, 
or else they might have kidnapped her, I am doubtless about it. [3-57-18b, 19]_END

B_3_C_56_24
BEGIN_
इति उक्त्वा परुषम् वाक्यम् रावणः शत्रु रावणः |राक्षसीः च ततः क्रुद्ध इदम् वचनम् अब्रवीत् || ३-५६-२६_END
BEGIN_
Thus on saying those harsh words, Ravana, the one who makes his enemies to bewail, and who is now infuriated 
said this sentence to the guarding demonesses. [3-56-26]_END

B_3_C_55_31
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्त्वा दशग्रीवो मैथिलीम् जनक आत्मजाम् |कृत अन्त वशम् आपन्नो मम इयम् इति मन्यते || ३-५५-३७_END
BEGIN_
That Decahedral Ravana on speaking thus to Maithili, who is the daughter of Janaka, deemed that 'she 
is mine,' as he has gone under the sway of the Terminator. [3-55-37]_END

B_3_C_58_8
BEGIN_
यदि जीवति वैदेही गमिष्याम्य् आश्रमम् पुनः |सुवृत्ता यदि वृत्ता सा प्राणान् त्यक्ष्यामि लक्ष्मण || 
३-५८-९_END
BEGIN_
"I wish to get at the hermitage again if only that Vaidehi of good-conduct is alive in hermitage, else, 
oh, Lakshmana, if death has already conducted her out of hermitage I too will give up my lives here 
itself. [3-58-9]_END

B_3_C_57_15
BEGIN_
अपि लक्ष्मण सीतायाः सामग्र्यम् प्राप्नुयावहे |जीवन्त्याः पुरुषव्याघ्र सुताया जनक्स्य वै || ३-५७-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, tigerly-man Lakshmana, I wonder whether we can at least make out the daughter of Janaka Seetha 
in her intactness and aliveness. [3-57-20]_END

B_3_C_56_25
BEGIN_
शीघ्रम् एव हि राक्षस्यो विकृता घोर दर्शनाः |दर्पम् अस्या अपनेष्यन्तु मांस शोणित भोजनाः || ३-५६-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, gnarled demonesses of grisly mien and devourers of meat and blood, you have to indeed remove her 
pride immediately. [3-56-27]_END

B_3_C_59_0
BEGIN_
अथ आश्रमात् उपावृत्तम् अंतरा रघुनंदनः |परिपप्रच्छ सौमित्रिम् रामो दुःख अर्दितः पुनः || ३-५९-१_END
BEGIN_
Rama the descendent of Raghu, again asked Soumitri who strayed from the hermitage and whom his own anguish 
is distressing now, in the middle of path towards their hermitage. [3-59-1]_END

B_3_C_57_16
BEGIN_
यथा वै मृग संघाःअ गोमायुः च भैरवम् |वाश्यन्ते शकुनाः च अपि प्रदीप्ताम् अभितो दिशम् |अपि स्वस्ति 
भवेत् तस्या राज पुत्र्या महाबल || ३-५७-२१_END
BEGIN_
"On observing these mobs of deer, this jackal, also even these birds which are voicing noisily facing 
the direction lit by the sun, oh, great-mighty Lakshmana, can we presume that there will be safety to 
that princes Seetha? [3-57-21]_END

B_3_C_58_9
BEGIN_
यदि माम् आश्रम गतम् वैदेही न अभिभाषते |पुनः प्रहसिता सीता विनशिष्यामि लक्ष्मण || ३-५८-१०_END
BEGIN_
"If Seetha, the princess from Videha, does not chat with me as before smiling gleefully on my arrival 
at the hermitage, oh, Lakshmana, I really breath my last. [3-58-10]_END

B_3_C_56_26
BEGIN_
वचनात् एव ताः तस्य विकृता घोर दर्शनाः |कृत प्रांजलयो भूत्वा मैथिलीम् पर्यवारयन् || ३-५६-२८_END
BEGIN_
Just by that order of Ravana those demonesses of grotesque and ugly appearance have obediently made 
palm-fold to him and encircled Maithili. [3-56-28]_END

B_3_C_59_1
BEGIN_
तम् उवाच किम् अर्थम् त्वम् आगतो अपास्य मैथिलीम् |यदा सा तव विश्वासात् वने विहरिता मया || ३-५९-२_END
BEGIN_
Rama spoke to such Lakshmana, "when I left her in the forest, I left only on confiding in you. For what 
reason you came to me on abandoning Maithili? [3-59-2]_END

B_3_C_57_17
BEGIN_
इदम् हि रक्षो मृग संनिकाशम्प्रलोभ्य माम् दूरम् अनुप्रयातम् |हतम् कथंचित् महता श्रमेणस राक्षसो 
अभूत् म्रियमाण एव || ३-५७-२२_END
BEGIN_
"This very demon in his likeness to a deer led me on and led me off distantly as I was indeed following 
him, and by an intense effort somehow he was killed, and when dying he transfigured into a demon. [3-57-22]_END

B_3_C_58_10
BEGIN_
ब्रूहि लक्ष्मण वैदेही यदि जीवति वा न वा |त्वयि प्रमत्ते रक्षोभिः भक्षिता वा तपस्विनी || ३-५८-११_END
BEGIN_
"Say Lakshmana, whether that pietistic Vaidehi is alive or not? Or, on your becoming unmindful of your 
guard is she consumed by demons, either? [3-58-11]_END

B_3_C_56_27
BEGIN_
स ताः प्रोवाच राजा तु रावणो घोर दर्शनाः |प्रचाल्य चरण उत्कर्षैः दारयन् इव मेदिनीम् || ३-५६-२९_END
BEGIN_
That king Ravana paced in an earth-shattering manner as though to cleave it and clearly said this to 
those demonesses with ghastly look. [3-56-29]_END

B_3_C_59_2
BEGIN_
दृष्ट्वा एव अभ्यागतम् त्वाम् मे मैथिलीम् त्यज्य लक्ष्मण |शंकमानम् महत् पापम् यत् सत्यम् व्यथितम् 
मनः || ३-५९-३_END
BEGIN_
"What my heart had been doubting, rather a perilous evil, oh, Lakshmana, that has become a fact on seeing 
only you, coming to me leaving off Maithili. [3-59-3]_END

B_3_C_57_18
BEGIN_
मनः च मे दीनम् इह अप्रहृष्टम्चक्षुः च सव्यम् कुरुते विकारम् |असंशयम् लक्ष्मण न अस्ति सीता
हृता मृता वा पथि वर्तते वा || ३-५७-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Now even my heart is woeful and I am woebegone, my left eye is also fluttering erratically, oh, Lakshmana, 
no doubt Seetha is not there in hermitage, maybe she is whisked away, or, wiped out, or, wandering around 
on a wrong way. [3-57-23]_END

B_3_C_58_11
BEGIN_
सुकुमारी च बाला च नित्यम् च अदुःख दर्शिनी |मत् वियोगेन वैदेही व्यक्तम् शोचति दुर्मनाः || ३-५८-१२_END
BEGIN_
"She who is softish by her nature and youngish by her age has never noticed the despair of separation 
from me, and now by my dissociation she will be despairing brokenheartedly, so it seems. [3-58-12]_END

B_3_C_56_28
BEGIN_
अशोक वनिका मध्ये मैथिली नीयताम् इति |तत्र इयम् रक्ष्यताम् गूढम् युष्माभिः परिवारिता || ३-५६-३०_END
BEGIN_
"Let this Maithili be taken to the centre of Ashoka gardens, where you all shall blockade and guard 
her stealthily. [3-56-30]_END

B_3_C_59_3
BEGIN_
स्फुरते नयनम् सव्यम् बाहुः च हृदयम् च मे |दृष्ट्वा लक्ष्मण दूरे त्वाम् सीता विरहितम् पथि || ३-५९-४_END
BEGIN_
"Seeing your coming without Seetha on pathway at a distance my left eye and left shoulder have pulsated, 
and oh, Lakshmana, my heart too has fluttered." Thus Rama said to Lakshmana. [3-59-4]_END

B_3_C_58_12
BEGIN_
सर्वथा रक्षसा तेन जिह्मेन सुदुरात्मना |वदता लक्ष्मण इति उच्छैः तव अपि जनितम् भयम् || ३-५८-१३_END
BEGIN_
"That impostor and highly impudent demon Maareecha who shouted loudly as, 'oh, Lakshmana,' might have 
caused fear even in you in everyway. [3-58-13]_END

B_3_C_56_29
BEGIN_
तत्र एनाम् तर्जनैः घोरैः पुनः सांत्वैः च मैथिलीम् |आनयध्वम् वशम् सर्वा वन्याम् गज वधूम् इव || ३-५६-३१_END
BEGIN_
"You threaten her with dreadful admonitions and again speaking imploringly you all have to bring her 
under control, as a wild she-elephant of age will be brought under control. [3-56-31]_END

B_3_C_59_4
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु सौमित्रिः लक्ष्मणः शुभ लक्षणः |भूयो दुःख संआविष्टो दुःखितम् रामम् अब्रवी|| ३-५९-५_END
BEGIN_
When Sumitra's son Lakshmana, whose traits are blamelessly auspicious is addressed thus, anguish cast 
a double spell on him, one for the tongue-lashing of Seetha while the other for the reproach from Rama, 
and he replied Rama who is anguished in his own way. [3-59-5]_END

B_3_C_58_13
BEGIN_
श्रुतः च मन्ये वैदेह्या स स्वरः सदृशो मम |त्रस्तया प्रेषितः त्वम् च द्रष्टुम् माम् शीघ्रम् आगतः 
|| ३-५८-१४_END
BEGIN_
"I hope that Vaidehi has also heard that voice which is similar to that of mine, and I hope frightened 
as she is she might have also hastened you, and I hope you also have come to see me, that hastily! [3-58-14]_END

B_3_C_56_30
BEGIN_
इति प्रति समादिष्टा राक्षस्यो रावणेन ताः |अशोक वनिकाम् जग्मुः मैथिलीम् परिगृह्य तु || ३-५६-३२
सर्वकामफलैर्वृक्षैर्नानापुष्पफलैर्वृताम् - यद्वा -सर्व काम फलैः वृक्षैः नाना पुष्प फलैः वृताम् |
सर्व काल मदैः च अपि द्विजैः समुपसेविताम् || ३-५६-३३_END
BEGIN_
When Ravana has clearly ordered, those demonesses on their part took Maithili to Ashoka garden. That 
Ashoka gardens are surrounded with trees that yield fruits to every savour, and now they are diversely 
flowered and fruited. Further, those gardens are highly adored by all-time lusty birds. [3-56-32, 33]_END

B_3_C_59_5
BEGIN_
न स्वयम् काम कारेण ताम् त्यक्त्वा अहम् इह आगतः |प्रचोदितस्तयैवोग्रैत्वत्सकाशमिहाअगतः - यद्वा -
प्रचोदितः तया एव उग्रैः त्वत् सकाशम् इह आगतः || ३-५९-६_END
BEGIN_
"I have not come here leaving her off either independently or intentionally, I came here, to your proximity, 
virtually driven by her hurtful words." Thus Lakshmana is relying Rama. [3-59-6]_END

B_3_C_58_14
BEGIN_
सर्वथा तु कृतम् कष्टम् सीताम् उत्सृजता वने |प्रतिकर्तुम् नृशंसानाम् रक्षसाम् दत्तम् अन्तरम् || ३-५८-१५_END
BEGIN_
"In everyway you have caused hardship by leaving Seetha in isolation, and a leeway is given to the diabolical 
demons for a counterattack against us. [3-58-15]_END

B_3_C_56_31
BEGIN_
सा तु शोक परीत अंगी मैथिली जनकात्मजा |राक्षसी वशम् आपन्ना व्याघ्रीणाम् हरिणी यथा || ३-५६-३४_END
BEGIN_
But she that Janaka's daughter Maithili whose body is with a coverall of anguish, further on obtaining 
the control of demonesses, she is as good as a she-deer under the coverall of tigresses. [3-56-34]_END

B_3_C_59_6
BEGIN_
आर्येण एव परिक्रुष्टम् - पराक्रुष्टम् - हा सीते लक्ष्मण इति च |परित्राहि इति यत् वाक्यम् मैथिल्याः 
तत् श्रुतिम् गतम् || ३-५९-७_END
BEGIN_
"Maithili gave an ear to that message which is loudly shouted as if by your honour saying, 'ha, Seetha... 
ha, Lakshmana... save me immediately...' [3-59-7]_END

B_3_C_58_15
BEGIN_
दुःखिताः खर घातेन राक्षसाः पिशित अशनाः |तैः सीता निहता घोरैः भविष्यति न संशयः || ३-५८-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Raw-flesh eating demons are distraught as I have liquidated Khara, as a result those ghastly ones would 
have liquidated Seetha by now. There is no doubt about it. [3-58-16]_END

B_3_C_56_32
BEGIN_
शोकेन महता ग्रस्ता मैथिली जनकात्मजा |न शर्म लभते भीरुः पाश बद्धा मृगी यथा || ३-५६-३५_END
BEGIN_
Maithili, the daughter of Janaka, who is already consumed by utmost agony has not obtained any placidity 
now as with a she-deer bound by tether - where timorousness is common to both. [3-56-35]_END

B_3_C_58_16
BEGIN_
अहो अस्मि व्यसने मग्नः सर्वथा रिपु नाशन |किम् तु इदानीम् करिष्यामि शंके प्राप्तव्यम् ईदृशम् || ३-५८-१७_END
BEGIN_
"In everyway I am sunken in scourge, but oh, enemy-eliminator Lakshmana, what I can possibly do in present 
situation? Perchance, this sort of scourge is liable to chance upon me, alas!" Thus Rama gave vent to 
his feelings on his way to hermitage. [3-58-17]_END

B_3_C_56_33
BEGIN_
न विन्दते तत्र तु शर्म मैथिलीविरूप नेत्राभिः अतीव तर्जिता |पतिम् स्मरन्ती दयितम् च देवरम्
विचेतना अभूत् भय शोक पीडिता || ३-५६-३६_END
BEGIN_
Maithili knows no peace when the bizarre-eyed demonesses have highly intimidated her, and by shut-seeing 
those demonesses her reminiscences went over to her dear husband and about her brother-in-law Lakshmana 
too, and when she felt about the improbability of their coming here, she is distraught with alarm and 
anguish, and then she swooned. [3-56-36]_END

B_3_C_59_7
BEGIN_
सा तम् आर्त स्वरम् श्रुत्वा तव स्नेहेन मैथिली |गच्छ गच्छ इति माम् आह रुदन्ती भय - विक्लवा - विह्वला 
|| ३-५९-८_END
BEGIN_
"On hearing that grievous voice of yours and owing to her love for you she shuddered with fear and wept 
out to me 'hurry up...get going...' [3-59-8]_END

B_3_C_58_17
BEGIN_
इति सीताम् वरारोहाम् चिंतयन् एव राघवः |आजगाम जन स्थानम् त्वरया सह लक्ष्मणः || ३-५८-१८_END
BEGIN_
In this way while thinking emotively about that curvaceous Seetha, Raghava hurriedly returned to Janasthaana 
along with Lakshmana. [3-58-18]_END

B_3_C_59_8
BEGIN_
प्रचोद्यमानेन मया गच्छ इति बहुशः तया |प्रत्युक्ता मैथिली वाक्यम् इदम् तत् प्रत्यय अन्वितम् || ३-५९-९_END
BEGIN_
"When she frequently and insistingly compelled me to go, I have replied Maithili in this sentence which 
is expressive of my confidence in you. [3-59-9]_END

B_3_C_59_9
BEGIN_
न तत् पश्यामि अहम् रक्षो यत् अस्य भयम् आवहेत् |निर्वृता भव न अस्ति एतत् केन अपि एवम् उदाहृतम् || 
३-५९-१०_END
BEGIN_
" 'I do no think that there is a demon who can cause panic to Rama. All this is feigning. Someone might 
have typified his voice in this way, please control yourself. [3-59-10]_END

B_3_C_58_18
BEGIN_
विगर्हमाणो अनुजम् आर्त रूपम्क्षुधा श्रमेण एव पिपासया च |विनिःश्वसन् शुष्क मुखो विषण्णःप्रतिश्रयम् 
प्राप्य समीक्ष्य शून्यम् || ३-५८-१९स्वम् आश्रमम् स प्रविगाह्य वीरोविहार देशान् अनुसृत्य कांश्चित् 
|एतत् तत् इति एव निवास भूमौप्रहृष्ट रोमा व्यथितो बभूव || ३-५८-२०_END
BEGIN_
He that Rama who chastened his younger brother en route is worried in aspect and wizened is his mouth 
by hunger, by strain, and also thus by thirst, and suspiring heavily he arrived near at hermitage, and 
became dispirited when he beheld the hermitage in vacuity. That valiant Rama on quickly entering his 
own hermitage found it to be vacuous. Then he rushed out and went round a place of pastime of Seetha, 
saying 'yes, this is that place where she used to move round for plucking flowers.' And again he dashed 
in to hermitage only to find it as an empty cottage. Then he rushed out to some other place of playtime 
of Seetha yelling, 'yes, this is that place where she used play with deer, squirrels and birds.' And 
again came back to vacant hermitage, and again he dashed to some other prayer-time place exclaiming, 
'yes, this is that very place where she offered her daily prayers.' Finally on returning to the vacant 
hermitage he became one who is plunged into hair-raising throes of despair as that cottage is emptied 
of Seetha. [3-58-19, 20]_END

B_3_C_59_10
BEGIN_
विगर्हितम् च नीचम् च कथम् आर्यो अभिधास्यति |त्राहि इति वचनम् सीते यः त्रायेत् त्रिदशान् अपि || ३-५९-११_END
BEGIN_
" 'How can my esteemed brother who can safeguard even gods, oh, Seetha, will exclaim in saying, 'save 
me,' which is a highly disparaging and basely manner to call for the help of a lady to safeguard him 
in such circumstances. [3-59-11]_END

B_3_C_59_11
BEGIN_
किम् निमित्तम् तु केन अपि भ्रातुः आलंब्य मे स्वरम् |विस्वरम् व्याहृतम् वाक्यम् लक्ष्मण त्राहि माम् 
इति || ३-५९-१२_END
BEGIN_
" 'But, somehow, for some reason, someone mimicking my brother's voice discordantly shouted words saying, 
'Lakshmana save me.' [3-59-12]_END

B_3_C_59_12
BEGIN_
राक्षसेन ईरितम् वाक्यम् त्रसात् त्राहि इति शोभने |न भवत्या व्यथा कार्या कुनारी जन सेविता || ३-५९-१३_END
BEGIN_
" 'Oh, auspicious lady, it is unbefitting for you to panic, like lowly womenfolk who will be frivolously 
panicking for flimsy reasons, for the words like 'save me,' shouted by some demon, who may conceivably 
be Maareecha. [3-59-13]_END

B_3_C_59_13
BEGIN_
अलम् वैक्लवताम् गंतुम् स्वस्था भव निर् उत्सुका |न च अस्ति त्रिषु लोकेषु पुमान् यो राघवम् रणे || 
३-५९-१४जातो वा जायमानो वा संयुगे यः पराजयेत् |अजेयो राघवो युद्धे देवैः शक्र पुरोगमैः || ३-५९-१५_END
BEGIN_
" 'Enough is your slipping into consternation and you be undismayed. There is none in all the three 
worlds who took birth, or going to take birth, to defeat Raghava in any given battle of any terrible 
nature. Raghava is undefeatable even if all gods come battling along with Indra in their van.' This 
is what I said to Vaidehi" Thus Lakshmana is informing Rama. [3-59-14, 15]_END

B_3_C_59_14
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्ता तु वैदेही परिमोहित चेतना |उवाच अश्रूणि मुंचन्ती दारुणम् माम् इदम् वचः || ३-५९-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Though I said thus, while her volition is overly besotted for you, Vaidehi said this tartly word to 
me outpouring tears. [3-59-16]_END

B_3_C_59_15
BEGIN_
भावो मयि तव अत्यर्थम् पाप एव निवेशितः |विनष्टे भ्रातरि प्राप्तुम् न च त्वम् माम् अवाप्स्यसि || ३-५९-१७_END
BEGIN_
" 'In my respect you have harboured only an impure and nastily perspective to achieve me on the utter 
ruination of your brother, but I am unachievable to you. [3-59-17]_END

B_3_C_60_0
BEGIN_
भृशम् आव्रजमानस्य तस्य अधो वाम लोचनम् |प्रास्फुरत् च अस्खलत् रामो वेपथुः च अस्य जायते || ३-६०-१_END
BEGIN_
While Rama is coming towards hermitage his lower eyelid frequently fluttered, his gait faltered, and 
he missed his footing. [3-60-1]_END

B_3_C_59_16
BEGIN_
संकेतात् भरतेन त्वम् रामम् समनुगच्छसि |क्रोशन्तम् हि यथा अत्यर्थम् न एनम् अभ्यवपद्यसे || ३-५९-१८_END
BEGIN_
" 'As to why you are refraining to rush towards Rama even though he is inordinately yelling, it hints 
that Bharata made some arrangements with you, and that is the reason why you have closely followed Rama 
in exile. [3-59-18]_END

B_3_C_60_1
BEGIN_
उपालक्ष्य निमित्तानि सो अशुभानि मुहुर् मुहुः |अपि क्षेमम् तु सीताया इति वै व्याजहार ह || ३-६०-२_END
BEGIN_
On closely watching those inauspicious forebodings Rama indeed uttered oftentimes reflexly thus as, 
'would she be safe, in fact!' [3-60-2]_END

B_3_C_59_17
BEGIN_
रिपुः प्रच्छन्न चारी त्वम् मत् अर्थम् अनुगच्छसि |राघवस्य अन्तर प्रेप्सुः तथा एनम् न अभिपद्यसे || 
३-५९-१९_END
BEGIN_
" 'You are an adversary of Rama comporting yourself in disguise, following him because of me, and searching 
for a leeway from Rama. Thereby now you are not rushing to Rama. [3-59-19]_END

B_3_C_60_2
BEGIN_
त्वरमाणो जगाम अथ सीता दर्शन लालसः |शून्यम् आवसथम् दृष्ट्वा बभूव उद्विग्न मानसः || ३-६०-३_END
BEGIN_
He quickened himself and went with an ardency to see Seetha, and then on seeing an empty home his heart 
is distraught. [3-60-3]_END

B_3_C_59_18
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तो हि वैदेह्या संरब्धो रक्त लोचनः |क्रोधात् प्रस्फुरमाण ओष्ठ आश्रमात् अभिनिर्गतः || ३-५९-२०_END
BEGIN_
"When Vaidehi spoke to me thus I hurriedly came out of hermitage to you with anger reddening my eyes 
and trembling my lips. [3-59-20]_END

B_3_C_60_3
BEGIN_
उद् भ्रमन् इव वेगेन विक्षिपन् रघु नन्दनः |तत्र तत्र उटज स्थानम् अभिवीक्ष्य समंततः || ३-६०-४ददर्श 
पर्ण शालाम् च सीतया रहिताम् तदा |श्रिया विरहिताम् ध्वस्ताम् हेमन्ते पद्मिनीम् इव || ३-६०-५_END
BEGIN_
Raghava looked like a flying-flutterer as his speed jostled his arms and gait flutteringly, and on closely 
probing there and there, and all-over the places of that cottage, then he saw the lustreless house of 
straw devoid of Seetha, alike a befogged wintry lotus-lake without lustre. [3-60-4, 5]_END

B_3_C_59_19
BEGIN_
एवम् ब्रुवाणम् सौमित्रिम् रामः संताप मोहितः |अब्रवीत् दुष्कृतम् सौम्य ताम् विना यत् त्वम् आगतः || 
३-५९-२१_END
BEGIN_
Rama who is deluded by angst said to Soumitri who is speaking thus, that "your arrival without her is 
an improper deed, oh, gentle one. [3-59-21]_END

B_3_C_60_4
BEGIN_
रुदन्तम् इव वृक्षैः च ग्लान पुष्प मृग द्विजम् |श्रिया विहीनम् विध्वस्तम् संत्यक्त वन दैवतैः || ३-६०-६
विप्रकीर्ण अजिन कुशम् विप्रविद्ध बृसी कटम् |दृष्ट्वा शून्य उटज स्थानम् विललाप पुनः पुनः || ३-६०-७_END
BEGIN_
The trees of that woodland are seemingly weeping, as their flowers are witheringly weakening and their 
birds are weepingly warbling, and the animals are whingeingly weeping, and that woodland is charmless 
and utterly shattered, since its georgic deities have completely abandoned it. Rather utterly bestrewn 
are the deerskins and sacred grass blades, rather utterly battered are the tender-grass-seats and other 
mats in the compound of cottage, and he who ardently wanted to see Seetha, such a Rama, on seeing such 
an emptied locale and cottage, wept over, over and again. [3-60-6, 7]_END

B_3_C_59_20
BEGIN_
जानन् अपि समर्थम् माम् रक्षसाम् अपवारणे |अनेन क्रोध वाक्येन मैथिल्या निर्गतो भवान् || ३-५९-२२_END
BEGIN_
"You know that I am capable enough to foil the demons, even then you have come out by the angry words 
of Maithili? [3-59-22]_END

B_3_C_60_5
BEGIN_
हृता मृता वा नष्टा वा भक्षिता वा भविष्यति |निलीना अपि अथवा भीरुः अथवा वनम् आश्रिता || ३-६०-८_END
BEGIN_
"That bashful Seetha might be stolen by the grudging demons, or slain by the very same grisly demons, 
or savoured by some gruesome beasts, or else she strayed in this gauntly forest, and even she might 
have playfully shrouded herself in the grimly forest, or else she must be sheltering herself in this 
forest which will be gruelling to locate. [3-60-8]_END

B_3_C_59_21
BEGIN_
न हि ते परितुष्यामि त्यक्त्वा यत् यासि मैथिलीम् |क्रुद्धायाः परुषम् श्रुत्वा स्त्रिया यत् त्वम् 
इह आगतः || ३-५९-२३_END
BEGIN_
"On hearing bitter words of an angry lady you have came away on leaving her off, such as you are, I 
am not at all happy with you. [3-59-23]_END

B_3_C_60_6
BEGIN_
गता विचेतुम् पुष्पाणि फलानि अपि च वा पुनः |अथवा पद्मिनीम् याता जल अर्थम् वा नदीम् गता || ३-६०-९_END
BEGIN_
"Or else, she might have again gone to pick the flowers or fruits, or again gone to lotus-lake, or gone 
to the river for water." Thinking thus, Rama started his search for Seetha. [3-60-9]_END

B_3_C_59_22
BEGIN_
सर्वथा तु अपनीतम् ते सीतया यत् प्रचोदितः |क्रोधस्य वशम् आगम्य न अकरोः शासनम् मम || ३-५९-२४_END
BEGIN_
"That which action of yours is there in non-compliance of my directive to stand guard to Seetha, either 
compelled by Seetha, or coming under your own ire, it shows your dereliction in everyway. [3-59-24]_END

B_3_C_59_23
BEGIN_
असौ हि राक्षसः शेते शरेण अभिहतो मया |मृग रूपेण येन अहम् आश्रमात् अपवाहितः || ३-५९-२५_END
BEGIN_
"By whom I am detoured from hermitage in the form of a deer he is indeed a demon, and he fell flat when 
my arrow hit him down. [3-59-25]_END

B_3_C_60_7
BEGIN_
यत्नात् मृगयमाणः तु न आससाद वने प्रियाम् |शोक रक्त ईक्षणः श्रीमान् उन्मत्त इव लक्ष्यते || ३-६०-१०_END
BEGIN_
Though he searched effortfully for his dear Seetha he did not get her, and as his anguish is reddening 
his eyes the appearance of that glorious one seems to be that of a madman. [3-60-10]_END

B_3_C_61_0
BEGIN_
दृष्ट्वा आश्रम पदम् शून्यम् रामो दशरथ आत्मजः |रहिताम् पर्णशालाम् च प्रविद्धानि आसनानि च || ३-६१-१
अदृष्ट्वा तत्र वैदेहीम् संनिरीक्ष्य च सर्वशः |उवाच रामः प्राक्रुश्य प्रगृह्य रुचिरौ भुजौ || ३-६१-२_END
BEGIN_
On seeing the vacant threshold of the hermitage and empty cottage of straw, also at the leaf-mat-seats 
that are utterly shattered, and not finding Vaidehi even on watchfully eyeing everywhere Rama shrieked 
loudly, and then on clasping the winning shoulders of Lakshmana he said this to him. [3-61-1, 2]_END

B_3_C_59_24
BEGIN_
विकृष्य चापम् परिधाय सायकम्स लील बाणेन च ताडितो मया |मार्गीम् तनुम् त्यज्य च विक्लव स्वरो
बभूव केयूर धरः स राक्षसः || ३-५९-२६_END
BEGIN_
"When I effortlessly shot an arrow setting on bowstring and stretching the bow to full length, he hit 
by that arrow left deer's body to become a piteously bewailing demon wearing bracelets and the like 
ornaments. [3-59-26]_END

B_3_C_60_8
BEGIN_
वृक्षात् वृक्षम् प्रधावन् स गिरीम् च अपि नदी नदम् |बभ्राम विलपन् रामः शोक पंक अर्णव प्लुतः || ३-६०-११_END
BEGIN_
Rama ran speedily from tree to shrub, from hill to hillock, from river to rivulet, and revolving around 
them he wailed for Seetha, as he is inundated in a sludgy ocean of woes. [3-60-11]_END

B_3_C_61_1
BEGIN_
क्व नु लक्ष्मण वैदेही कम् वा देशम् इतो गता |केन आहृता वा सौमित्रे भक्षिता केन वा प्रिया || ३-६१-३_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Lakshmana, possibly where can be Vaidehi? Or, to which place she has gone from here? Or, Soumitri, 
who stole her away? Or, who has gorged up my ladylove? [3-61-3]_END

B_3_C_60_9
BEGIN_
अस्ति कच्चित् त्वया दृष्टा सा कदम्ब प्रिया प्रिया |कदम्ब यदि जानीषे शंस सीताम् शुभ आननाम् || ३-६०-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Kadamba tree, seest thou someone a lady who is lover of Kadamba flowers, one with a lovable face 
and a love of mine, thou tellest me if thou knowest. [3-60-12]_END

B_3_C_59_25
BEGIN_
शर आहतेन एव तदा आर्तया गिरास्वरम् मम आलंब्य सु दूर सु श्रवम् |उदाहृतम् तत् वचनम् सु दारुणम्
त्वम् आगतो येन विहाय मैथिलीम् || ३-५९-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Then hit down by arrow thus, he with an anguished voice that is clearly audible at a very remotely 
place and that which is mimicking my voice, uttered those highly gruesome words, whereby you have come 
here forsaking Maithili." Thus Rama said to Lakshmana on their way to their hermitage. [3-59-27]_END

B_3_C_61_2
BEGIN_
वृक्षेण आवार्य यदि माम् सीते हसितुम् इच्छसि |अलम् ते हसितेन अद्य माम् भजस्व सुदुःखितम् || ३-६१-४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Seetha, if you have concealed yourself under trees wishing to poke fun at me, enough is your fun 
and games, get in touch with me now, as I am highly anguished... [3-61-4]_END

B_3_C_60_10
BEGIN_
स्निग्ध पल्लव संकाशाम् पीत कौशेय वासिनीम् |शंसस्व यदि सा दृष्टा बिल्व बिल्व उपम स्तनी || ३-६०-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Bilva tree, if thou seest someone who is drest in yellowy-ochry silks, whose skin likens to the 
silkiness of thine leaflets, breasts to thine rotund and silky Bilva fruits, thou tellest me... [3-60-13]_END

B_3_C_61_3
BEGIN_
यैः सह क्रीडसे सीते विश्वस्तैः मृग पोतकैः |एते हीनाः त्वया सौम्ये ध्यायन्ति अस्र आविल ईक्षणाः || 
३-६१-५_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, meek Seetha, with which meekly young deer you were playing, all these are now broody with tearfully 
fluttery looks, without you... [3-61-5]_END

B_3_C_60_11
BEGIN_
अथवा अर्जुन शंस त्वम् प्रियाम् ताम् अर्जुन प्रियाम् |जनकस्य सुता तन्वी यदि जीवति वा न वा || ३-६०-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Otherwise, thou Arjuna tree, if thou knowest her who is a lover of thine Arjuna flowers and the ladylove 
of mine, thou telleth whether that slender-waisted daughter of Janaka liveth or otherwise... [3-60-14]_END

B_3_C_61_4
BEGIN_
सीताया रहितो अहम् वै न हि जीवामि लक्ष्मण |वृतम् शोकेन महता सीता हरणजेन माम् || ३-६१-६पर लोके 
महाराजो नूनम् द्रक्ष्यति मे पिता |_END
BEGIN_
"Really Lakshmana, I will not live long without Seetha, indeed I am enveloped in high anguish caused 
by the abduction of Seetha, and this alone will become a murderer, and on my going to other world when 
murdered by my own agony my father and that great king Dasharatha will definitely observe me in the 
other world... [3-61-6, 7a]_END

B_3_C_60_12
BEGIN_
ककुभः ककुभ ऊरुम् ताम् व्यक्तम् जानाति मैथिलीम् |लता पल्लव पुष्प आढ्यो भाति हि एष वनस्पतिः || ३-६०-१५_END
BEGIN_
"As to how this Kakubha tree shineth laden with creepy-creepers, foliole-foliage and flowery-flowers, 
this tree knowest Maithili whose thighs can be likened to the smoothish trunk of this very Kakubha tree... 
[3-60-15]_END

B_3_C_61_5
BEGIN_
कथम् प्रतिज्ञाम् संश्रुत्य मया त्वम् अभियोजितः || ३-६१-७अपूरयित्वा तम् कालम् मत् सकाशम् इह आगतः 
|काम वृत्तम् अनार्यम् माम् मृषा वादिनम् एव च || ३-६१-८धिक् त्वाम् इति परे लोके व्यक्तम् वक्ष्यति 
मे पिता |_END
BEGIN_
"When I go to other world after my death our father Dasharatha who is already staying there will deride 
me saying, 'when I have directed you for a fourteen year exile, and when you too have assuredly agreed 
and promised me for that term, how you have to my presence in this ultramundane world without completing 
that term of fourteen year exile, besides breaking your own word of honour... thus you have become a 
wilful disobedient, despicable and dishonest person, such as you are, fie on you...' [3-61-7b, 8, 9a]_END

B_3_C_60_13
BEGIN_
भ्रमरैर् उपगीतः च यथा द्रुम वरो हि असि |एष व्यक्तम् विजानाति तिलकः तिलक प्रियाम् || ३-६०-१६_END
BEGIN_
"As to how this best tree among all trees heareth the chorus of honeybees that singest around it, thereby 
this Tilaka tree clearly knowest Maithili, a lover of Tilaka trees, as this shouldst have heard her. 
[3-60-16]_END

B_3_C_61_6
BEGIN_
विवशम् शोक संतप्तम् दीनम् भग्न मनोरथम् || ३-६१-९माम् इह उत्सृज्य करुणम् कीर्तिः नरम् इव अन्ऋजुम् 
|क्व गच्चसि वरारोहे मा मोत्सृज्य - मा मा उत्सृज्य - सुमध्यमे || ३-६१-१०त्वया विरहितः च अहम् 
त्यक्ष्ये जीवितम् आत्मनः |_END
BEGIN_
"Anguish seared and bewildered me and I am woebegone with broken down buoyancy, and oh, beautiful lady, 
jilting such an woeful one as I am, where you are going now, as with prestige jilting a prevaricator? 
And if you shun me I will have to shun my life..." Thus Rama bewailed imaging her right in his front 
and running away. [3-61-9b, 10, 11a]_END

B_3_C_62_0
BEGIN_
सीताम् अपश्यन् धर्मात्मा शोक उपहत चेतनः |
विललाप महाबाहू रामः कमल लोचनः || ३-६२-१_END
BEGIN_
In not seeing Seetha that virtue-souled Rama's sagacity is marred by his anguish and
he bewailed with his lotus-like eyes that are reddening like a pair of lotuses, raising is long
arms. [3-62-1]_END

B_3_C_60_14
BEGIN_
अशोक शोक अपनुद शोक उपहत चेतनम् |त्वन् नामानम् कुरु क्षिप्रम् प्रिया संदर्शनेन माम् || ३-६०-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Ashoka tree, an alleviator of agony, that is thine name lingually... but practically and readily 
name me after thine, by showing my ladylove, as my agony has marred my empathy... [3-60-17]_END

B_3_C_61_7
BEGIN_
इति इव विलपन् रामः सीता दर्शन लालसः || ३-६१-११न ददर्श सुदुःख आर्तो राघवो जनक आत्मजाम् |_END
BEGIN_
Though that legatee of Raghu is desperate for seeing Seetha, though he is highly anguished and agonised, 
though he bewailed this way, that Rama has not found Janaka's daughter, Seetha. [3-61-10b, 11a]_END

B_3_C_62_1
BEGIN_
पश्यन् इव च ताम् सीताम् अपश्यन् मदन अर्दितः |
उवाच राघवो वाक्यम् विलाप आश्रय दुर्वचम् || ३-६२-२_END
BEGIN_
Even if Raghava is not able to see Seetha in his presence he started talking to her
in a kind of inarticulate wailing, as wailing pampered his articulacy because his speech took
shelter of wailing instinct, and as he is cowed down by Love-god, and thus he started to vent out
his heart in this way. [3-62-2]_END

B_3_C_60_15
BEGIN_
यदि ताल त्वया दृष्टा पक्व ताल फल स्तनी |कथयस्व वरारोहाम् कारुण्यम् यदि ते मयि || ३-६०-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Palm tree, if thou seest that lady breasted alike ripened-palm fruits of thine, and if thine mercy 
is mine, thou telleth of that shapely lady Seetha... [3-60-18]_END

B_3_C_61_8
BEGIN_
अनासादयमानम् तम् सीताम् शोकपरायणम् || ३-६१-१२पंकम् आसाद्य विपुलम् सीदन्तम् इव कुंजरम् |लक्ष्मणो 
रामम् अत्यर्थम् उवाच हित काम्यया || ३-६१-१३_END
BEGIN_
To him who is unable to find Seetha, and who is sinking in sadness as with an elephant sinking in a 
chasmal mud, Lakshmana spoke to such a Rama in a positive manner desiring his wellbeing. [3-61-11b, 
13]_END

B_3_C_62_2
BEGIN_
त्वम् अशोकस्य शाखाभिः पुष्प प्रिय तराअ प्रिये |
अवृणोषि शरीरम् ते मम शोक विवर्धिनी || ३-६२-३_END
BEGIN_
"Flowers fascinate you very much, my dear, hence you veil yourself with the full
bloomed branches of Ashoka tree, but that alone is amplifying my anguish because you both have
presently became tormentors. [3-62-3]_END

B_3_C_60_16
BEGIN_
यदि दृष्टा त्वया सीता जम्बो जांबूनद सम प्रभा |प्रियाम् यदि विजानासि निःशंक कथयस्व मे || ३-६०-१९_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rose-apple tree, if thou seest Seetha and thee knowest my ladylove with golden glitter, thou telleth 
me without hesitation..._END

B_3_C_61_9
BEGIN_
मा विषादम् महाबुद्धे कुरु यत्नम् मया सह |इदम् गिरि वरम् वीर बहु कन्दर शोभितम् || ३-६१-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, well-informed one, do not get into desperation, you make efforts along with me, and oh, brave one, 
this best mountain is beaming forth with many caves, she may be there somewhere. [3-61-14]_END

B_3_C_62_3
BEGIN_
कदली काण्ड सदृशौ कदल्या संवृता उभौ |
ऊरू पश्यामि ते देवि न असि शक्ता निगूहितुम् || ३-६२-४_END
BEGIN_
"Maybe, both your thighs liken to the stalks of banana plants, thinking so, now you
have lapped them in grovy banana plants, but I can distinguish which is which, thus now I caught
sight of them, oh, lady, you are inapt at least to cover them from me. [3-62-4]_END

B_3_C_61_10
BEGIN_
प्रिय कानन संचारा वन उन्मत्ता च मैथिली |सा वनम् वा प्रविष्टा स्यात् नलिनीम् वा सुपुष्पिताम् || ३-६१-१५
सरितम् वा अपि संप्राप्ता मीन वंजुल सेविताम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Maithili is a fascinated saunterer in woodlands so she might have entered the forest, she is even infatuated 
with waters, so she might have gone to the fully bloomed lotus-lake, or to the river that is adorned 
by fishes and cane-breaks. [3-61-15]_END

B_3_C_60_17
BEGIN_
अहो त्वम् कर्णिकार अद्य पुष्पितः शोभसे भृशम् |कर्णिकार प्रियाम् साध्वीम् शंस दृष्टा यदि प्रिया || 
३-६०-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Aha! Karnikaara tree, now thou art in full bloom and blooming magnificently, if thou seest that lover 
of Karnikaara-flowers and an immaculate ladylove of mine, thou telleth me... [3-60-20]_END

B_3_C_62_4
BEGIN_
कर्णिकार वनम् भद्रे हसंती देवि सेवसे |
अलम् ते परिहासेन मम बाधावहेन वै || ३-६२-५_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, lady, you are facetiously glorying in the boscage of fully bloomed Karnikaara
trees which is really wafting worry to me, rather than the fragrance of those flowers oh, glorious
lady, enough, enough is this facetiousness of yours. [3-62-5]_END

B_3_C_61_11
BEGIN_
वित्रासयितु कामा वा लीना स्यात् कानने क्वचित् || ३-६१-१६जिज्ञासमाना वैदेही त्वाम् माम् च पुरुषर्षभ 
|तस्या हि अन्वेषणे श्रीमन् क्षिप्रम् एव यतावहे || ३-६१-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Or, wishing to know our reaction when she scares us with her prank, Maithili might have squirreled 
away into forest. Oh, honourable brother, let us endeavour quickly to search her. [3-61-16]_END

B_3_C_60_18
BEGIN_
चूत नीप महा सालान् पनसान् कुरवान् धवान् |दाडिमान् अपि तान् गत्वा दृष्ट्वा रामो महायशाः || ३-६०-२१
बकुलान् अथ पुन्नागान् च चंदनान्केतकान् तथा |पृच्छन् रामो वने भ्रान्त उन्मत्त इव लक्ष्यते || ३-६०-२२_END
BEGIN_
Rama has gone on asking trees like mango, niipa, massive saala, jack-fruit, kuruva, dhava, and even 
around daaDima, bakula, punnaaga, sandalwood, ketaka trees, and when he is running around them that 
highly glorious Rama appeared like a madman. [3-60-21, 22]_END

B_3_C_62_5
BEGIN_
विशेषेण आश्रमस्थाने हासो अयम् न प्रशस्यते |
अवगच्छामि ते शीलम् परिहास प्रियम् प्रिये || ३-६२-६
आगच्छ त्वम् विशालाक्षी शून्यो अयम् उटजः तव |_END
BEGIN_
"I am aware of your humour, lady, and I know that you are jocose, but in a place
like hermitage unmerited is this sort of raillery, even if it is good-natured. Hence, you come
back, oh, wide-eyed one, your cottage is empty. [3-62-6, 7a]_END

B_3_C_61_12
BEGIN_
वनम् सर्वम् विचिनुवो यत्र सा जनक आत्मजा |मन्यसे यदि काकुत्स्थ मा स्म शोके मनः कृथाः || ३-६१-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama of Kakutstha, if you consider that we shall search the forest in its entirety to locate where 
she that Janaka's daughter might be, let us quickly do so. But do not engulf your heart in sadness." 
Thus Lakshmana advised Rama. [3-61-18]_END

B_3_C_60_19
BEGIN_
अथवा मृग शाब अक्षीम् मृग जानासि मैथिलीम् |मृग विप्रेक्षणी कांता मृगीभिः सहिता भवेत् || ३-६०-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Or else, oh, deer, dost thou know what bechanced to that fawn-eyed Maithili, one with quick-looks like 
thee deer? Or else, hast she herded herself into the herd of she-deer of yours... [3-60-23]_END

B_3_C_62_6
BEGIN_
सु व्यक्तम् राक्षैः सीता भक्षिता वा हृता अपि वा || ३-६२-७
न हि सा विलपंतम् माम् उपसम्प्रैति लक्ष्मण |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Lakshmana, very evidently demons have either gorged up Seetha, or perhaps
abducted her, because she is not returning to me who am whiny indeed for her. [3-62-7b, 8a]_END

B_3_C_61_13
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु सौहार्दात् लक्ष्मणेन समाहितः |सह सौमित्रिणा रामो विचेतुम् उपचक्रमे || ३-६१-१९_END
BEGIN_
When Lakshmana good-heartedly spoke this way, Rama self-collectedly made a headway for the search of 
Seetha along with Soumitri. [3-61-19]_END

B_3_C_60_20
BEGIN_
गज सा गज नासोरुः यदि दृष्टा त्वया भवेत् |ताम् मन्ये विदिताम् तुभ्यम् आख्याहि वर वारण || ३-६०-२४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, elephant, thou mightst beheld her whose thighs likens to your trunk at that problematic hour, thus 
methinks, and that Maithili is familiar to thee, and oh, best elephant, if thou beholdest her, thou 
tallest me... [3-60-24]_END

B_3_C_62_7
BEGIN_
एतानि मृग यूधानि स अश्रु नेत्राणि लक्ष्मण || ३-६२-८
शंशन्ति इव हि मे देवीम् भक्षिताम् रजनीचरैः |_END
BEGIN_
"Indeed these teary-eyed mobs of deer look as if to explain that nightwalkers have
gluttonised my lady. [3-62-8b, 9a]_END

B_3_C_61_14
BEGIN_
तौ वनानि गिरीन् चैव सरितः च सरांसि च |निखिलेन विचिन्वन्तौ सीताम् दशरथ आत्मजौ || ३-६१-२०_END
BEGIN_
Those two sons of Dasharatha have started a thorough search for Seetha in forests, on mountains, also 
thus at rivers and lakes. [3-61-20]_END

B_3_C_60_21
BEGIN_
शार्दूल यदि सा दृष्टा प्रिया चंद्र निभ आनना |मैथिली मम विस्रब्धम् कथयस्व न ते भयम् || ३-६०-२५_END
BEGIN_
"Fear not, oh, tiger, hast thou seen Maithili, the moonfaced ladylove of mine, if thou hast seen speak 
in good faith... [3-60-25]_END

B_3_C_62_8
BEGIN_
हा मम आर्ये क्व याता असि हा साध्वि वर वर्णिनि || ३-६२-९
हा स कामा अद्य कैकेयी देवि मे अद्य भविष्यति |_END
BEGIN_
"Ha! My graceful lady, to where you have strayed now... Ha! Chastely and best
complexioned lady, now the ambition of my queen mother Kaikeyi will be fulfilled, as I breath my
last owing to your straying... [3-62-8b, 9a]_END

B_3_C_61_15
BEGIN_
तस्य शैलस्य सानूनि शिलाः च शिखराणि च |निखिलेन विचिन्वन्तौ न एव ताम् अभिजग्मतुः || ३-६१-२१_END
BEGIN_
On searching whole of mountainsides of that Mt. Chitrakuta, where their hermitage is there, even in 
its caves, crags, and mountain peaks they have not found Seetha. [3-61-21]_END

B_3_C_60_22
BEGIN_
किम् धावसि प्रिये नूनम् दृष्टा असि कमल ईक्षणे |वृक्षेण आच्चाद्य च आत्मानम् किम् माम् न प्रतिभाषसे 
|| ३-६०-२६_END
BEGIN_
"Oh lotus-eyed lady, in fact I have seen you my dear, then why this running away and concealing yourself 
under trees, why do not you reply me... [3-60-26]_END

B_3_C_62_9
BEGIN_
सीताया सह निर्यातो विना सीताम् उपागतः || ३-६२-१०
कथम् नाम प्रवेक्ष्यामि शून्यम् अन्तः पुरम् मम |_END
BEGIN_
"I have come to forests with Seetha and have to go back to Ayodhya without Seetha.
How, in all but name, can I step into an oblivion called my palace-chambers? [3-62-9b, 10a]_END

B_3_C_61_16
BEGIN_
विचित्य सर्वतः शैलम् रामो लक्ष्मणम् अब्रवीत् |न इह पश्यामि सौमित्रे वैदेहीम् पर्वते शुभाम् || ३-६१-२२_END
BEGIN_
On exploring everywhere on that mountain Rama said to Lakshmana, "oh, Soumitri, here on this mountain 
I do not descry auspicious Vaidehi." [3-61-22]_END

B_3_C_63_0
BEGIN_
स राज पुत्र प्रिया विहीनःशोकेन मोहेन च पीड्यमानः |विषादयन् भ्रातरम् आर्त रूपोभूयो विषादम्प्रविवेश 
तीव्रम् || ३-६३-१_END
BEGIN_
That prince Rama whom agony and anguish are distressing has become anxious in his mien, and he again 
drifted into a dire desperation while despairing his brother Lakshmana. [3-63-1]_END

B_3_C_60_23
BEGIN_
तिष्ठ तिष्ठ वरारोहे न ते अस्ति करुणा मयि |न अत्यर्थम् हास्य शीला असि किम् अर्थम् माम् उपेक्षसे || 
३-६०-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Stay...stay... oh, best lady, don't you have mercy on me? You are not unacceptably tease-humoured! 
What for you ignore me? [3-60-27]_END

B_3_C_61_17
BEGIN_
ततो दुःख अभिसंतप्तो लक्ष्मणो वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् |विचरन् दण्डक अरण्यम् भ्रातरम् दीप्त तेजसम् || ३-६१-२३_END
BEGIN_
While roving searchingly in Dandaka forest Lakshmana who is tormented by anguish said a sentence to 
his greatly resplendent brother Rama. [3-61-23]_END

B_3_C_63_1
BEGIN_
स लक्ष्मणम् शोक वश अभिपन्नम्शोके निमग्नो विपुले तु रामः |उवाच वाक्यम् व्यसनानुरूपम्उष्णम् 
विनिःश्वस्य रुदन् स शोकम् || ३-६३-२_END
BEGIN_
Rama who is sunken in a chasmal sorrow spoke this sentence while wailing sorrowfully, suspiring severely 
and scorchingly, and which sentence is seemly to his sensitivity, to Lakshmana who is already under 
the sway of sorrow. [3-63-2]_END

B_3_C_62_10
BEGIN_
निर्वीर्य इति लोको माम् निर्दयः च इति वक्ष्यति || ३-६२-११
कातरत्वम् प्रकाशम् हि सीता अपनयनेन मे |_END
BEGIN_
"People will denounce me as a vigourless and pitiless person, and my ineptitude will
indeed be self-evident, for Seetha is led away from me by some tactical being... [3-62-10b,
11a]_END

B_3_C_60_24
BEGIN_
पीत कौशेयकेन असि सूचिता वर वर्णिनि |धावन्ति अपि मया दृष्टा तिष्ठ यदि अस्ति सौहृदम् || ३-६०-२८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, beautifully complexioned lady, even if you are running away your yellowy silk-sari betokens you, 
stay, if you have goodwill for me... [3-60-28]_END

B_3_C_63_2
BEGIN_
न मत् विधो दुष्कृत कर्म कारीमन्ये द्वितीयो अस्ति वसुंधरायाम् |शोक अनुशोको हि परंपरायामाम् 
एति भिन्दन् हृदयम् मनः च || ३-६३-३_END
BEGIN_
"I am second to none among the blameworthy wrongdoers on this earth, thus I deem, and indeed woe followed 
by woe are getting at me in seriation to burst my heart and mind... [3-63-3]_END

B_3_C_61_18
BEGIN_
प्राप्स्यसि त्वम् महाप्राज्ञ मैथिलीम् जनक आत्मजाम् |यथा विष्णुः महाबाहुः बलिम् बद्ध्वा महीम् इमाम् 
|| ३-६१-२४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, insightful brother, you will reacquire Janaka's daughter Maithili, as Vishnu once subjugated Emperor 
Bali and reacquired this earth." [3-61-24]_END

B_3_C_62_11
BEGIN_
निवृत्त वन वासः च जनकम् मिथिल अधिपम् || ३-६२-१२
कुशलम् परिपृच्छन्तम् कथम् शक्षे निरीक्षितुम् |_END
BEGIN_
"When the king of Mithila Janaka asks after the wellbeing of all the three of us
after the completion of forest living, how do I have the face to stand him? [3-62-11b, 12a]_END

B_3_C_60_25
BEGIN_
न एव सा नूनम् अथवा हिंसिता चारु हासिनी |कृच्छ्रम् प्राप्तम् न माम् नूनम् यथा उपेक्षितुम् अर्हति 
|| ३-६०-२९_END
BEGIN_
"Otherwise, she whom I have just seen me may not be Seetha, why because, it is unapt of her to avoid 
me who attained this wretched state, hence Seetha with cheery smiles is certainly murdered... [3-60-29]_END

B_3_C_63_3
BEGIN_
पूर्वम् मया नूनम् अभीप्सितानिपापानि कर्माणि असत्कृत् कृतानि |तत्र अयम् अद्य पतितो विपाको
दुःखेन दुःखम् यद् अहम् विशामि || ३-६३-४_END
BEGIN_
"I might have definitely, habitually, and desirably committed damnable deeds in my previous births, 
and now the result of those impious deeds is very much ripened and has fallen on me, whereby I am entering 
misery after misery... [3-63-4]_END

B_3_C_61_19
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु वीरेण लक्ष्मणेन स राघवः |उवाच दीनया वाचा दुःख अभिहत चेतनः || ३-६१-२५_END
BEGIN_
But when the valiant Lakshmana addressed him in that way, Raghava whose thinking is marred by poignance 
spoke these pathetic words. [3-61-25]_END

B_3_C_62_12
BEGIN_
विदेह रजो नूनम् माम् दृष्ट्वा विरहितम् तया || ३-६२-१३
सुता विनाश संतप्तो मोहस्य वशम् एष्यति |_END
BEGIN_
"On seeing me without Seetha the king of Videha will be distraught by the perishing
of his daughter, and he defiantly goes under the preponderance of perplexity... [3-62-12b, 13a]_END

B_3_C_60_26
BEGIN_
व्यक्तम् सा भक्षिता बाला राक्षसैः पिशित अशनैः |विभज्य अंगानि सर्वाणि मया विरहिता प्रिया || ३-६०-३०_END
BEGIN_
"Obviously the raw-flesh gorgers must have gorged that youngish lady on diving all her limbs in my absence 
from my dear one... [3-60-30]_END

B_3_C_61_20
BEGIN_
वनम् सुविचितम् सर्वम् पद्मिन्यः फुल्ल पंकजाः |गिरिः च अयम् महाप्राज्ञ बहु कन्दर निर्झरः |न हि 
पश्यामि वैदेहीम् प्राणेभ्यो अपि गरीयसीम् || ३-६१-२६_END
BEGIN_
"This forest in its entirety, these lotus-lakes with their blossomed lotuses, and this mountain with 
its many caves and mountain-rapids, all are evidently searched. But, oh, sensible brother, I do not 
descry Vaidehi who is loftier than my lives." [3-61-27]_END

B_3_C_63_4
BEGIN_
राज्य प्रणाशः स्व जनैः वियोगःपितुर् विनाशो जननी वियोगः |सर्वानि मे लक्ष्मण शोक वेगम्आपूरयन्ति 
प्रविचिन्तितानि || ३-६३-५_END
BEGIN_
"I am deprived of the kingdom, departed from my own people, mainly Seetha, my father departed and I 
am detached from my mother, and Lakshmana, when all these setbacks are very deeply thought over they 
are replenishing the haste of my agony... [3-63-5]_END

B_3_C_62_13
BEGIN_
अथवा न गमिष्यामि पुरीम् भरत पालितम् || ३-६२-१४
स्वर्गो अपि हि तया हीनः शून्य एव मतो मम |_END
BEGIN_
"Instead, I prefer not to go to the city Ayodhya that is ruled by Bharata, because
it must be comforting to one and all under his rulership, but not to me as Seetha will not be with
me... else if, that end of my life occurs now and if I were to go to heaven, even that heaven will
be a void to me without her... I believe so... [3-62-13b, 14a]_END

B_3_C_60_27
BEGIN_
नूनम् तत् शुभ दंत ओष्ठम् सुनासम् शुभ कुण्डलम् |पूर्ण चंद्र निभम् ग्रस्तम् मुखम् निष्प्रभताम् गतम् 
|| ३-६०-३१_END
BEGIN_
"Her face which is similar to a full-moon with pretty teeth, prettier lips, prettily nose and with prettyish 
earrings, might have obtained a blanched look when being devoured... [3-60-31]_END

B_3_C_61_21
BEGIN_
एवम् स विलपन् रामः सीता हरण कर्शितः |दीनः शोक समाविष्टो मुहूर्तम् विह्वलो अभवत् || ३-६१-२७_END
BEGIN_
Lamenting in this way Rama languished owing to the abduction of Seetha and became a pitiable one, and 
while sadness besieging him he is perturbed for a moment. [3-61-28]_END

B_3_C_63_5
BEGIN_
सर्वम् तु दुःखम् मम लक्ष्मण इदम्शान्तम् शरीरे वनम् एत्य क्लेशम् |सीता वियोगात् पुनर् अपि उदीर्णम्
काष्टैः इव अग्निः सहसा प्रदीप्तः || ३-६३-६_END
BEGIN_
"All this sadness of mine has silenced physically and there is some peace on coming to these desolate 
forests, in association of Seetha, but with the dissociation of Seetha misery is again upshot, as with 
fire which flares up in a flash when fuel is added... [3-63-6]_END

B_3_C_62_14
BEGIN_
तत् माम् उत्सृज्य हि वने गच्छ अयोध्या पुरीम् शुभाम् || ३-६२-१५
न तु अहम् ताम् विना सीताम् जीवेयम् हि कथंचन |_END
BEGIN_
"Hence, Lakshmana, you go back to that auspicious city Ayodhya forsaking me in
forests, because I have no existence without Seetha, isn't it! [3-62-14b, 15a]_END

B_3_C_60_28
BEGIN_
सा हि चंपक वर्ण आभा ग्रीवा ग्रैवेयक उचिता |कोमला विलपन्त्याः तु कान्ताया भक्षिता शुभा || ३-६०-३२_END
BEGIN_
"But that exquisite and beautiful neck of that lady which shines forth in the colour of Campaka flower, 
befitting for any neck ornament, indeed it might be glutted down while she is bewailing... [3-60-32]_END

B_3_C_61_22
BEGIN_
स विह्वलित सर्व अंगो गत बुद्धिः विचेतनः |निषसाद आतुरो दीनो निःश्वस्य अशीतम् आयतम् || ३-६१-२८_END
BEGIN_
All the limbs of Rama are fluttered, his faculty has become functionless, his fervour is frozen, he 
is forlorn and flustered, and such as he is he sank down suspiring swelteringly and lengthily. [3-61-29]_END

B_3_C_63_6
BEGIN_
सा नूनम् आर्या मम राक्षसेन हिअभ्याहृता खम् समुपेत्य भीरुः |अपस्वरम् सु स्वर विप्रलापाभयेन 
विक्रन्दितवति अभीक्ष्णम् || ३-६३-७_END
BEGIN_
"My noblewoman might be abducted by a demon, and on reaching the sky that lady who converses with a 
sweet voice might have wept a lot fearfully, and it is definite that she must have shouted a lot, untunefully... 
[3-63-7]_END

B_3_C_62_15
BEGIN_
गाढम् आश्लिष्य भरतो वाच्यो मत् वचनात् त्वया || ३-६२-१६
अनुज्ञातो असि रामेण पालय इति वसुंधराम् |_END
BEGIN_
"On tightly hugging Bharata you shall tell him these words as I have said, 'Rama
authorises you to reign the earth...' [3-62-16]_END

B_3_C_60_29
BEGIN_
नूनम् विक्षिप्यमाणौ तौ बाहू पल्लव कोमलौ |भक्षितौ वेपमान अग्रौ स हस्त आभरण अंगदौ || ३-६०-३३_END
BEGIN_
"Her two arms which are delicate like tender leaves, ornamented with bangles and bicep-lets might have 
been definitely nibbled while they are wriggling with quivering fingers... [3-60-33]_END

B_3_C_61_23
BEGIN_
बहुशः स तु निःश्वस्य रामो राजीव लोचनः |हा प्रिये ति विचुक्रोश बहुशो बाष्प गद्गदः || ३-६१-२९_END
BEGIN_
Suspiring repeatedly he that lotus-eyed Rama shrieked repeatedly and loudly thus as, 'ha, Seetha...' 
with tears stifling his throat. [3-61-30]_END

B_3_C_63_7
BEGIN_
तौ लोहितस्य प्रिय दर्शनस्यसदा उचितौ उत्तम चंदनस्य |वृत्तौ स्तनौ शोणित पंक दिग्धौनूनम् प्रियाया 
मम न अभिभात || ३-६३-८_END
BEGIN_
"Those two roundish bosoms of my ladylove which always deserved the application of pleasantly looking 
red-sandalwood's paste might definitely be unshiny, as they might be bedaubed with muddy blood when 
they are extricated from her body for devouring. [3-63-8]_END

B_3_C_62_16
BEGIN_
अंबा च मम कैकेयी सुमित्रा च त्वया विभो || ३-६२-१७
कौसल्या च यथा न्यायम् अभिवाद्या मम अज्ञया |
रक्षणीया प्रयत्नेन भवता सा उक्त कारिणा || ३-६२-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, efficacious Lakshmana, on revering my mothers Kaika, Sumitra, and Kausalya
justifiably you tell them my good bye, and you as the one who effectuates whatever is assigned to
you, you have to effortfully protect my mother Kausalya by doing whatever she says. [3-62-17b,
18]_END

B_3_C_60_30
BEGIN_
मया विरहिता बाला रक्षसाम् भक्षणाय वै |सार्थेन इव परित्यक्ता भक्षिता बहु बांधवा || ३-६०-३४_END
BEGIN_
"This is as though I have forsaken this youngish Seetha really as a feast for the demons in my absence, 
and though Seetha has many relatives she has become as worse as a lonesome woman who is completely forsaken 
by her caravan who is lonesomely ready for the feast of highwaymen, and demons have feasted on her. 
[3-60-34]_END

B_3_C_64_0
BEGIN_
स दीनो दीनया वाचा लक्ष्मणम् वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् |
शीघ्रम् लक्ष्मण जानीहि गत्वा गोदावरीम् नदीम् || ३-६४-१
अपि गोदावरीम् सीता पद्मानि आनयितुम् गता |_END
BEGIN_
A pitiable one, such as he is, he spoke to Lakshmana in a pitiable voice,
"Lakshmana, go quickly to River Godavari and find out whether Seetha has gone to Godavari to fetch
lotuses..." [3-64-1, 2a]_END

B_3_C_61_24
BEGIN_
तम् सान्त्वयामास ततो लक्ष्मणः प्रिय बान्धवम् |बहु प्रकारम् शोक आर्तः प्रश्रितः प्रश्रित अंजलिः || 
३-६१-३०_END
BEGIN_
Though Rama has many kinsfolk who hold him dear he is now left with a single one, namely Lakshmana, 
and that obedient brother Lakshmana who is already anguished for Rama's sadness, then adjoining his 
palms obediently started to pacify Rama with divers methods. [3-61-31]_END

B_3_C_63_8
BEGIN_
तत् श्लक्ष्ण सु व्यक्त मृदु प्रलापम्तस्या मुखम् कुंचित केश भारम् |रक्षो वशम् नूनम् उपगताया
न भ्राजते राहु मुखे यथा इंदुः || ३-६३-९_END
BEGIN_
"She has a sweet, softish, and very clear talkativeness on her lips. That visage with such lips is crowned 
with a hairdo with hair lumped together and plaited, such as her visage is, it must have become unshiny 
on her going into the repression of demon, as with an unshiny moon when repressed in the mouth of eclipsing 
planet Raahu, it is definite... [3-63-9]_END

B_3_C_62_17
BEGIN_
सीतायाः च विनाशो अयम् मम च अमित्र सूदन |
विस्तरेण जनन्या विनिवेद्य त्वया भवेत् || ३-६२-१९_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, the subjugator of unfriendly, Lakshmana... you shall clearly inform in detail
about this perish of Seetha, also that of mine, to our mothers. [3-62-19]_END

B_3_C_64_1
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु रामेण लक्ष्मणः पुनः एव हि || ३-६४-२
नदीम् गोदावरीम् रम्याम् जगाम लघु विक्रमः |_END
BEGIN_
When Rama said thus to him Lakshmana again went to the charming River Godavari
quickening his pace. [3-64-2b, 3a]_END

B_3_C_60_31
BEGIN_
हा लक्ष्मण महाबाहो पश्यसे त्वम् प्रियाम् क्वचित् |हा प्रिये क्व गता भद्रे हा सीते इति पुनः पुनः 
|| ३-६०-३५_END
BEGIN_
"Ha, Lakshmana... oh, dextrous one... have you seen my ladylove anywhere... ha, dear, where have you 
gone... oh, auspicious lady... ha, Seetha..." thus Rama lamented again and again in his search. [3-60-35]_END

B_3_C_63_9
BEGIN_
ताम् हार पाशस्य सदा उचित अंतम्ग्रीवाम् प्रियाया मम सु व्रताया |रक्षांसि नूनम् परिपीतवन्ति
शून्ये हि भित्वा रुधिर अशनानि || ३-६३-१०_END
BEGIN_
"The contours of the neck of that strait-laced ladylove of mine are always worthy for necklaces and 
chain-wears. The bloodthirsty demons would have indeed mangled that neck in a secluded place and they 
might have drunk her blood, it is definite... [3-63-10]_END

B_3_C_61_25
BEGIN_
अनादृत्य तु तत् वाक्यम् लक्ष्मण ओष्ठ पुट च्युतम् |अपश्यन् ताम् प्रियाम् सीताम् प्राक्रोशत् स पुनः 
पुनः || ३-६१-३१_END
BEGIN_
But disavowing the word of advice that fell out from the cupped lips of Lakshmana, Rama stridently yelled 
again and again when his dear Seetha has become unseeable. [3-61-32]_END

B_3_C_62_18
BEGIN_
इति विलपति राघवो तु दीनो
वनम् उपगम्य तया विना सु केश्या |
भय विकल मुखः तु लक्ष्मणो अपि
व्यथित मना भृशम् आतुरो बभूव || ३-६२-२०_END
BEGIN_
Thus Raghava, the dejected, neared every corner of the forest in his search, and
bewailed because that lady with best plaits, Seetha, is not found and missing from him. Even
Lakshmana became whey-faced, frantic-hearted, highly overwrought, by the fear of uncertainty
looming large on them. [3-62-20]_END

B_3_C_64_2
BEGIN_
ताम् लक्ष्मणः तीर्थवतीम् विचित्वा रामम् अब्रवीत् || ३-६४-३
नैनाम् पश्यामि तीर्थेषु क्रोशतो न शृणोति मे |_END
BEGIN_
Searching at many declivities which River Godavari has on its banks Lakshmana said
to Rama, "I do not espy her at ghats, declivities of riverbanks, and she is not replying though I
shouted for her. [3-64-3b, 4a]_END

B_3_C_60_32
BEGIN_
इति एवम् विलपन् रामः परिधावन् वनात् वनम् |क्वचित् उद् भ्रमते वेगात् क्वचित् विभ्रमते बलात् || ३-६०-३६
क्वचित् मत्त इव आभाति कांता अन्वेषण तत्परः |_END
BEGIN_
On bewailing in this way and on overly rushing from wood to wood, somewhere Rama has become highly delusional 
by the forcefulness of delusion and spots forest stuff as Seetha, though none of them have any resemblance 
to Seetha, and somewhere else, marking creepers, plants or slender shrubs and suchlike delicacies as 
Seetha he has become really alluded by the powerfulness of allusion, and elsewhere, he is not discriminating 
paths or pathless routes for his trekking as an impassioned one in the search of his ladylove, and thus 
he is nitid like a madman. [3-60-36, 37a]_END

B_3_C_63_10
BEGIN_
मया विहीना विजने वने यारक्षोभिः आहृत्य विकृष्यमाणा |नूनम् विनादम् कुररि इव दीनासा मुक्तवती 
आयत कान्त नेत्रा || ३-६३-११_END
BEGIN_
"While I was away from her in this uninhibited forest demons would have forcibly hauled her up when 
they are abducting that lady with broad-bright eyes, and she would have discordantly shrieked out like 
a piteous she-dove, it is definite... [3-63-11]_END

B_3_C_64_3
BEGIN_
कम् नु सा देशम् आपन्ना वैदेही क्लेश नाशिनी || ३-६४-४
न हि तम् वेद्मि वै राम यत्र सा तनु मध्यमा |_END
BEGIN_
"In fact, oh, Rama, to which place she that neutraliser of nervousness, namely
Vaidehi, has got round to, or where that frailty is, that place is really incomprehensible to me...
[3-64-4b, 5a]_END

B_3_C_60_33
BEGIN_
स वनानि नदीः शैलान् गिरि प्रस्रवणानि च |काननानि च वेगेन भ्रमति अपरिसंस्थितः || ३-६०-३७_END
BEGIN_
Rama is on the rove around woods, rivers, hills, mountain-rapids and thicketed forests, speedily and 
restlessly. [3-60-37]_END

B_3_C_63_11
BEGIN_
अस्मिन् मया सार्थम् उदार शीलाशिला तले पूर्वम् उपोपविष्टा |कान्त स्मिता लक्ष्मण जात हासात्वाम् 
आह सीता बहु वाक्य जातम् || ३-६३-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Sitting very close to me on this stone's surface, oh, Lakshmana, she that well-mannered Seetha with 
bright smiles was speaking to you verbosely with all smiles... [3-63-12]_END

B_3_C_64_4
BEGIN_
लक्ष्मणस्य वचः श्रुत्वा दीनः संताप मोहितः || ३-६४-५
रामः समभिचक्राम स्वयम् गोदावरीम् नदीम् |
स ताम् उपस्थितो रामः क्व सीते इति एवम् अब्रवीत् || ३-६४-६_END
BEGIN_
Rama who is already stupefied by anguish is now despaired on listening Lakshmana's
words and he personally went straight to River Godavari, and staying nearby that river Rama shouted
in this way, "Seetha... where are you?" [3-64-5b, 6]_END

B_3_C_60_34
BEGIN_
तदा स गत्वा विपुलम् महत् वनम्परीत्य सर्वम् तु अथ मैथिलीम् प्रति |अनिष्ठित आशः स चकार मार्गणे
पुनः प्रियायाः परमम् परिश्रमम् || ३-६०-३८_END
BEGIN_
On going round the vast of great forest in that way and on searching for Maithili, his hope became intangible, 
but again he undertook the search for his ladylove, over-strenuously. [3-60-38]_END

B_3_C_63_12
BEGIN_
गोदावरी इयाम् सरिताम् वरिष्टाप्रिया प्रियाया मम नित्य कालम् |अपि अत्र गच्छेत् इति चिंतयामि
न एकाकिनी याति हि सा कदाचित् || ३-६३-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Among rivers this Godavari is the best and it is an all the time cherished river to my ladylove, and 
I think she would have gone thereunto. But, at anytime she did not go there, singly... [3-63-13]_END

B_3_C_64_5
BEGIN_
भूतानि राक्षसेन्द्रेण वध अर्हेण हृताम् अपि |
न ताम् शशंसू रामाय तथा गोदावरी नदी || ३-६४-७_END
BEGIN_
The forest creatures which were asked earlier have not said to Rama that a
deservedly destructible demagogue of demons has divested him of Seetha, likewise now River Godavari
which is now being asked has not informed Rama about Seetha. [3-64-7]_END

B_3_C_63_13
BEGIN_
पद्म आनना पद्म पलाश नेत्रापद्मानि वा आनेतुम् अभिप्रयाता |तत् अपि अयुक्तम् न हि सा कद्दचित्
मया विना गच्छति पंकजानि || ३-६३-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Or, that lotus-faced, lotus-petal eyed Seetha has gone straight to bring lotuses! Nay, that idea itself 
is incongruous, for she never goes to get lotuses, indeed without me... [3-63-14]_END

B_3_C_64_6
BEGIN_
ततः प्रचोदिता भूतैः शंस च अस्मै प्रियाम् इति |
न च सा हि अवदत् सीताम् पृष्टा रामेण शोचता || ३-६४-८_END
BEGIN_
Though the woeful Rama has asked her, and even though all the georgic beings
impelled her to inform Rama the fact about his ladylove, River Godavari then remained mouthless
about Seetha. [3-64-8]_END

B_3_C_63_14
BEGIN_
कामम् तु इदम् पुष्पित वृक्ष सण्डम्नाना विधैः पक्षि गणैः उपेतम् |वनम् प्रयाता नु तत् अपि अयुक्तम्
एकाकिनी सा अति बिभेति भीरुः || ३-६३-१५_END
BEGIN_
"But has she really gone to this stand of thicket which is with flowered trees and with birds of divers 
kind! Nay, that thought also is incongruent, because she as a timid one is much scared of solitude... 
[3-63-15]_END

B_3_C_65_0
BEGIN_
तप्यमानम् तथा रामम् सीता हरण कर्शितम् |
लोकानाम् अभवे युक्तम् सांवर्तकम् इव अनलम् || ३-६५-१
वीक्षमाणम् धनुः सज्यम् निःश्वसंतम् पुनः पुनः |
दग्धु कामम् जगत् सर्वम् युग अन्ते च यथा हरम् || ३-६५-२
अदृष्ट पूर्वम् संक्रुद्धम् दृष्ट्वा रामम् स लक्ष्मणः |
अब्रवीत् प्रांजलिः वाक्यम् मुखेन परिशुष्यता || ३-६५-३_END
BEGIN_
Lakshmana on seeing Rama who is searing and careworn owing to the abduction of
Seetha, blazing like the doomsday inferno, twinned with the notion of rendering the worlds into
nonentity, kenning at his stringed bow, keen to blaze away entire universe, suspiring again and
again, and who is alike Rudra at the end of era, and whose highly infuriated persona Lakshmana has
not seen previously, became pale-faced and spoke to Rama with folded palms. [3-65-1]_END

B_3_C_64_7
BEGIN_
रावणस्य च तत् रूपम् कर्माणि च दुरात्मनः |
ध्यात्वा भयात् तु वैदेहीम् सा नदी न शशंस ह || ३-६४-९_END
BEGIN_
She that River Godavari has not informed Rama about Vaidehi just out of fear on
recalling the mien and manoeuvres of malefic-minded Ravana, lest Ravana may drain her away.
[3-64-9]_END

B_3_C_63_15
BEGIN_
आदित्य भो लोक क्रृत अकृत ज्ञःलोकस्य सत्य अनृत कर्म साक्षिन् |मम प्रिया सा क्व गता हृता वा
शंसव मे शोक हतस्य सर्वम् || ३-६३-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Sun, you are the knower of performed and unperformed deeds in the world, a wittnesser of good and 
bad deeds in the world, tell me, who am woefully writhing, to where my ladylove strolled, or is she 
stolen... [3-63-16]_END

B_3_C_65_1
BEGIN_
पुरा भूत्वा मृदुः दांतः सर्व भूत हिते रतः |
न क्रोध वशम् आपन्नः प्रकृतिम् हातुम् अर्हसि || ३-६५-४_END
BEGIN_
"Previously, you were self-collected and self-controlled and delighted in the
wellbeing of all the beings. But presently, slipping into fury you are discarding your own
disposition, which is unapt of you... [3-65-4]_END

B_3_C_64_8
BEGIN_
निराशः तु तया नद्या सीताया दर्शने कृतः |
उवाच रामः सौमित्रिम् सीता दर्शन कर्शितः || ३-६४-१०_END
BEGIN_
Rama who is already in a rundown condition owing to the non-appearance of Seetha, is
further rendered as a hopeless being by River Godavari in the matter of his catching a glimpse of
Seetha, and such a Rama spoke to Saumitri. [3-64-10]_END

B_3_C_63_16
BEGIN_
लोकेषु सर्वेषु न नास्ति किंचित्यत् ते न नित्यम् विदितम् भवेत् तत् |शंसस्व वयोः कुल शालिनीम् 
ताम्मृता हृता वा पथि वर्तते वा || ३-६३-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Air, whatsoever is there in the world, wheresoever it might be, or whensoever it might have happened, 
and whichsoever it might be, and whencesoever it might exist, that cannot possibly be unknown to you. 
Hence, tell me of the lady from noble heritage... is she stolen, or slain, or strayed her steps..." 
Thus Rama begged of the Eternals for locating Seetha. [3-63-17]_END

B_3_C_65_2
BEGIN_
चन्द्रे लक्ष्मीः प्रभा सूर्ये गतिः वायौ भुवि क्षमा |
एतत् च नियतम् सर्वम् त्वयि च अनुत्तमम् यशः || ३-६५-५_END
BEGIN_
"Grandeur in moon, splendour in sun, motion in wind, and composure in earth are
perpetual and all this perpetuity is available in you, besides an unexcelled honour... [3-65-5]_END

B_3_C_64_9
BEGIN_
एषा गोदावरी सौम्य किंचन् न प्रतिभाषते |
किम् नु लक्ष्मण वक्ष्यामि समेत्य जनकम् वचः || ३-६४-११
मातरम् चैव वैदेह्या विना ताम् अहम् अप्रियम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, kind Lakshmana, this Godavari is talking to me anything but a reply. In the
absence of Vaidehi, oh Lakshmana, really what is that unpleasant word I have to say to Vaidehi's
father king Janaka, also thus to Vaidehi's mother-in-law and my mother Kausalya, when I meet them!
[3-64-11, 12a]_END

B_3_C_63_17
BEGIN_
इति इव तम् शोक विधेय देहम्रामम् विसंज्ञम् विलपंतम् एव |उवाच सौमित्रिःअदीन सत्त्वःन्याये 
स्थितः काल युतम् च वाक्यम् || ३-६३-१८_END
BEGIN_
To such a Rama whose physique is routed by his anguish in this way and who is insensately bewailing 
in that way, Soumitri whose courage is un-dispirited gave a justifiable and timely suggestion. [3-63-18]_END

B_3_C_65_3
BEGIN_
एकस्य न अपराधेन लोकान् हन्तुम् त्वम् अर्हसि |
न तु जानामि कस्य अयम् भग्नः सांग्रामिको रथः || ३-६५-६
केन वा कस्य वा हेतोः स आयुधः स परिच्छदः |_END
BEGIN_
"It will be unapt of you to vandalise worlds for a single-soul's felony. It is
unclear as to whose combat-chariot is this, or by whom, or by what reason it is shattered with its
weaponry and paraphernalia... [3-65-6, 7a]_END

B_3_C_64_10
BEGIN_
या मे राज्य विहीनस्य वने वन्येन जीवतः || ३-६४-१२
सर्वम् व्यपनयत् शोकम् वैदेही क्व नु सा गता |_END
BEGIN_
"Which Vaidehi is the remover of all my sadness who am a destitute of kingdom and
surviving in forests on forest produce, such as she is, where has she gone, really! [3-64-12b,
13a]_END

B_3_C_63_18
BEGIN_
शोकम् विमुंच आर्य धृतिम् भजस्वसह उत्साहता च अस्तु विमार्गणे अस्याः |उत्साहवन्तो हि नरा न लोके
सीदन्ति कर्मसु अति दुष्करेषु || ३-६३-१९_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, noble brother, banish that anguish and brace yourself with fortitude, and let you be with spiritedness 
in her searching... indeed, there is no backsliding for spirited men in their enterprises in this world, 
even though the enterprises are highly impracticable..." [3-63-19]_END

B_3_C_65_4
BEGIN_
खुर नेमि क्षतः च अयम् सिक्तो रुधिर बिन्दुभिः || ३-६५-७
देशो निवृत्त संग्रामः सु घोरः पार्थिव आत्मज |_END
BEGIN_
"This has become a very ghastly place since it is grooved by the hooves of ungulates
and by the felloies of chariot-wheels, and it is wetted with drops of blood, oh, prince, thereby a
combat is fought and stalled at this place... [3-65-7b, 8a]_END

B_3_C_64_11
BEGIN_
ज्ञाति वर्ग विहीनस्य राज पुत्रीम् अपश्यतः || ३-६४-१३
मन्ये दीर्घा भविष्यन्ति रात्रयो मम जाग्रतः |_END
BEGIN_
"Though I am distanced from my relatives I deemed that princess Seetha alone would
be an evermore relative of mine. But now when that princess alone is unseen I deem that my
sleepless nights would be lengthy. [3-64-13b, 14a]_END

B_3_C_63_19
BEGIN_
इति इव सौमित्रिम् उदग्र पौरुषम्ब्रुवन्तम् आर्तो रघु वंश वर्धनः |न चिंतयामास धृतिम् विमुक्तवान्
पुनः च दुःखम् महत् अभ्युपागमत् || ३-६३-२०_END
BEGIN_
When Soumitri of towering bravery is speaking this way, Rama, the enhancer of Raghu's lineage, gave 
no heed to it, and since he castaway his fortitude he again encountered an inexplicable anguish. [3-63-20]_END

B_3_C_65_5
BEGIN_
एकस्य तु विमर्दो अयम् न द्वयोः वदताम् वर || ३-६५-८
न हि वृत्तम् हि पश्यामि बलस्य महतः पदम् |_END
BEGIN_
"This is just a solo-combatant's combat but not among duo, oh, best articulator one
among best articulators, I indeed observe that no huge army is eventuated here, nor its stamp...
[3-65-8b, 9a]_END

B_3_C_64_12
BEGIN_
मंदाकिनीम् जनस्थानम् इमम् प्रस्रवणम् गिरिम् || ३-६४-१४
सर्वाणि अनुचरिष्यामि यदि सीता हि लभ्यते |_END
BEGIN_
"I will search all these places of Godavari, Janasthaana and this mountain with many
rapids, perhaps Seetha may be available somewhere. [3-64-14b, 15a]_END

B_3_C_65_6
BEGIN_
न एकस्य तु कृते लोकान् विनाशयितुम् अर्हसि || ३-६५-९
युक्त दण्डा हि मृदवः प्रशान्ता वसुधा अधिपाः |_END
BEGIN_
"It will be inapt of you to wish for wrecking a havoc upon all worlds for an
individual's wrongdoing. Why because, the good-hearted, good-natured kings are they who impose
tenable punishment... [3-65-9b, 10a]_END

B_3_C_64_13
BEGIN_
एते महा मृगा वीर माम् ईक्षन्ते पुनः पुनः || ३-६४-१५
वक्तु कामा इह हि मे इंगितानि अनुपलक्षये |_END
BEGIN_
"Now all these burly animals are repeatedly looking at me as though to speak to me,
oh, brave Lakshmana, this I reckon with their body language as it were. [3-64-15b, 16a]_END

B_3_C_66_0
BEGIN_
तम् तथा शोक संतप्तम् विलपंतम् अनाथवत् |
मोहेन महता आविष्टम् परिद्यूनम् अचेतनम् || ४-६६-१
ततः सौमित्रिः आश्वास्य मुहूर्तात् इव लक्ष्मणः |
रामम् संबोधयामास चरणौ च अभिपीडयन् || ४-६६-२_END
BEGIN_
While Rama is bewailing like a forlorn as his anguish is scorching him, rendered
impoverished with an inanimate heart as a high passion possessed him, Lakshmana, the son of
Sumitra, suppliantly gripped his feet and started to address him. [4-66-1, 2]_END

B_3_C_65_7
BEGIN_
सदा त्वम् सर्व भूतानाम् शरण्यः परमा गतिः || ३-६५-१०
को नु दार प्रणाशम् ते साधु मन्येत राघव |_END
BEGIN_
"You are always the shelterer for all beings, for you're above all the good-natured
and good-hearted ordinary kings, and who can really deem the ravagement of you wife as an act of
grace... [3-65-10b, 11a]_END

B_3_C_64_14
BEGIN_
तान् तु दृष्ट्वा नरव्याघ्र राघवः प्रत्युवाच ह || ३-६४-१६
क्व सीत इति निरीक्षन् वै बाष्प संरुद्धया गिरा |_END
BEGIN_
But on seeing them pryingly that tigerly-man Raghava has indeed asked them at once
with a voice stifled with tears, "where is Seetha?" [3-64-16b, 17a]_END

B_3_C_66_1
BEGIN_
महता तपसा राम महता च अपि कर्मणा |
राज्ञा दशरथेन असि लब्धो अमृतम् इव अमरैः || ४-६६-३_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama, as gods have reaped ambrosia after a prolonged churning of Milky Ocean,
you are a reap of King Dasharatha's superlative ascesis and even by his superior acts...
[4-66-3]_END

B_3_C_65_8
BEGIN_
सरितः सागराः शैला देव गन्धर्व दानवाः || ३-६५-११
न अलम् ते विप्रियम् कर्तुम् दीक्षितस्य इव साधवः |_END
BEGIN_
"As no altruist can evoke indignation in a hallowed person who is performing
Vedic-ritual, honestly, these rivers, oceans, mountains, gods, celestials, and cacodemons too
cannot evoke indignation in you, because they are always gentle to you... isn't so... [3-65-10b,
11a]_END

B_3_C_64_15
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्ता नरेन्द्रेण ते मृगाः सहसा उत्थिता || ३-६४-१७
दक्षिण अभिमुखाः सर्वे दर्शयन्तो नभः स्थलम् |
मैथिली ह्रियमाणा सा दिशम् याम् अभ्यपद्यत || ३-६४-१८
तेन मार्गेण गच्छन्तो निरीक्षन्तो नराधिपम् |_END
BEGIN_
When that best king has asked, those animals rose to their feet in a trice and
facing themselves southward showed skyward with their snouts. And while running in the direction in
which Maithili is taken away they are stopping to look back at that lord of people, Rama. Thus they
are repeatedly running, stopping and staring at Rama. [3-64-17b, 18, 19a]_END

B_3_C_66_2
BEGIN_
तव चैव गुणैः बद्धः त्वत् वियोगात् महिपतिः |
राजा देवत्वम् आपन्नो भरतस्य यथा श्रुतम् || ४-६६-४_END
BEGIN_
"Our father was an enlivener of all the subjects and that king was beholden only to
your rosy endowments, but he obtained godhood by your separation... this is what we heard from
Bharata... [4-66-4]_END

B_3_C_65_9
BEGIN_
येन राजन् हृता सीता तम् अन्वेषितुम् अर्हसि || ३-६५-१२
मद् द्वितीयो धनुष् पाणिः सहायैः परम ऋषिभिः |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, king, it will be apt of you to wield your bow and search for him who abducted
Seetha, along with me as your squire and standby, and with the help of sublime sages available in
this forest... [3-65-12b, 13a]_END

B_3_C_64_16
BEGIN_
येन मार्गम् च भूमिम् च निरीक्षन्ते स्म ते मृगाः || ३-६४-१९
पुनः नदन्तो गच्छन्ति लक्ष्मणेन उपलक्षिताः |_END
BEGIN_
By which reason those animals are going in a southerly course on a southerly
terrain, and stopping to peer at Rama, and again clamorously adopting the very same southerly
course, Lakshmana ascertained that reason. [3-64-19b, 20a]_END

B_3_C_66_3
BEGIN_
यदि दुःखम् इदम् प्राप्तम् काकुत्स्थ न सहिष्यसे |
प्राकृतः च अल्प सत्त्वः च इतरः कः सहिष्यति || ४-६६-५_END
BEGIN_
"If you are unable to withstand this anguish chanced on you, oh, Kakutstha, then how
a simpleton and whose boldness is meagre can withstand it... [4-66-5]_END

B_3_C_65_10
BEGIN_
समुद्रम् च विचेष्यामः पर्वतान् च वनानि च || ३-६५-१३
गुहाः च विविधा घोरा पद्मिन्यो विविधाः थथा |_END
BEGIN_
"Let us search the oceans, rivers and forests, and even divers dreadful caves and
different lotus-lakes... [3-65-13b, 14a]_END

B_3_C_64_17
BEGIN_
तेषाम् वचन सर्वस्वम् लक्षयामास च इन्गितम् || ३-६४-२०
उवाच लक्ष्मणो धीमान् ज्येष्ठम् भ्रातरम् आर्तवत् |_END
BEGIN_
On noticing the lingua franca and even the lingua persona of those animals, that
imaginative Lakshmana spoke to his elder brother, alike a striver striving hard for some
information. [3-64-20b, 21a]_END

B_3_C_66_4
BEGIN_
आश्वसिहि नरश्रेष्ठ प्राणिनः कस्य न आपद |
संस्पृशन्ति अग्निवत् राजन् क्षणेन व्यपयान्ति च || ४-६६-६_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, first and foremost man, tell me who is uncaught by mischance, which mischance
will be catchy like fire-catch, and oh, king, even that, that lets up momently... [4-66-6]_END

B_3_C_65_11
BEGIN_
देव गन्धर्व लोकान् च विचेष्यामः समाहिताः || ३-६५-१४
यावत् न अधिगमिष्यामः तव भार्या अपहारिणम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Let us intently search the worlds of gods and celestials as long as the abductor of
your wife is unapprehended... [3-65-14b, 15a]_END

B_3_C_64_18
BEGIN_
क्व सीत इति त्वया पृष्टा यथा इमे सहसा उथिताः || ३-६४-२१
दर्शयन्ति क्षितिम् चैव दक्षिणाम् च दिशम् मृगाः |
सधु गच्छावहे देव दिशम् एताम् च नैर्ऋतीम् || ३-६४-२२
यदि तस्य आगमः कश्चित् आर्या वा सा अथ लक्ष्यते |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, godly brother, when you have asked these animals, 'where is Seetha,' they
quickly rose to their feet, and as to how they are showing the track on the ground and the southern
direction as well, thereby we may, for sure, go south-westward to know whether there is some
information about her, or else, even that noble lady herself may be available there..." [3-64-21a,
22, 23a]_END

B_3_C_66_5
BEGIN_
दुःखितो हि भवान् लोकान् तेजसा यदि धक्ष्यते |
आर्ताः प्रजा नर व्याघ्र क्व नु यास्यन्ति निर्वृतिम् || ४-६६-७_END
BEGIN_
"If you are going to blaze away worlds with your radiance in your ruefulness, to
where the ordinary people in rue shall go for solace, really... [4-66-7]_END

B_3_C_65_12
BEGIN_
न चेत् साम्ना प्रदास्यन्ति पत्नीम् ते त्रिदश ईश्वराः |
कोसल इन्द्र ततः पश्चात् प्राप्त कालम् करिष्यसि || ३-६५-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Lord of Kosala kingdom, if the heavenly lords are not going bestow your wife
propitiously, rather after our humanly effort, then you may do whatever you want, seasonably...
[3-65-15b, c]_END

B_3_C_64_19
BEGIN_
बाढम् इति एव काकुत्स्थः प्रस्थितो दक्षिणाम् दिशम् || ३-६४-२३
लक्ष्मण अनुगत श्रीमान् वीक्ष्यमाणो वसुन्धराम् |_END
BEGIN_
On saying "Yes!" to Lakshmana that illustrious Rama of Kakutstha sallied forth to
southern direction followed by Lakshmana, scrutinising the earth on his walkway. [3-64-23b,
24a]_END

B_3_C_65_13
BEGIN_
शीलेन साम्ना विनयेन सीताम्
नयेन न प्राप्स्यसि चेत् नरेन्द्र |
ततः समुत्सादय हेम पुंखैः
महेन्द्र वज्र प्रतिमैः शर ओघैः || ३-६५-१६_END
BEGIN_
"If, oh, king, you with your traits of sincerity, solidarity, simplicity, and
scrupulosity are not going to get back Seetha, then you may you may put whole of the universe to
turmoil with the torrents of your arrows which have swift egress as they are with golden-handles
which are stuffed with eagle feathers, and which mirror up the Thunderbolts of Mahendra in their
trajectories..." Thus Lakshmana appealed to ireful Rama. [3-65-16]_END

B_3_C_66_6
BEGIN_
लोक स्वभाव एव एष ययातिः नहुष आत्मजः |
गतः शक्रेण सालोक्यम् अनयः तम् समस्पृशत् || ४-६६-८_END
BEGIN_
"World's disposition is this way only, even if Nahusha, the son Yayaati, has become
an egalitarian with Indra, writhe touched him off... [4-66-8]_END

B_3_C_64_20
BEGIN_
एवम् संभाषमाणौ तौ अन्योन्यम् भ्रातरौ उभौ || ३-६४-२४
वसुन्धरायाम् पतित पुष्प मार्गम् अपश्यताम् |_END
BEGIN_
Those two brothers who are proceeding while discussing among themselves have seen
the walkway bestrewn with flowers fallen from a person. [3-64-24b, 25a]_END

B_3_C_66_7
BEGIN_
महाऋषि यः वसिष्ठः तु यः पितुः नः पुरोहितः |
अह्ना पुत्र शतम् जज्ञे तथैव अस्य पुनर् हतम् || ४-६६-९_END
BEGIN_
"Which great sage Vashishta is there, who is also the priest of our father, he
parented a hundred sons in one day and like that they are all eliminated in one day by Vishvamitra,
for which Vashishta also lamented, but not for a long... [4-66-9]_END

B_3_C_64_21
BEGIN_
पुष्प वृष्टिम् निपतिताम् दृष्ट्वा रामो मही तले || ३-६४-२५
उवाच लक्ष्मणम् वीरो दुःखितो दुःखितम् वचः |_END
BEGIN_
That valiant Rama who is anguished to see the drizzle of flowers fallen on the
surface of earth spoke this word to Lakshmana who is equally anguished. [3-64-25b, 26a]_END

B_3_C_66_8
BEGIN_
या च इयम् जगतो माता सर्व लोक नमस्कृता |
अस्याः च चलनम् भूमेः दृश्यते कोसलेश्वर || ४-६६-१०_END
BEGIN_
"This Mother Earth who is the mother of worlds and venerated by all animate and
inanimate, or even celestial beings, oh, king of Kosala kingdom, even she undergoes tremors and
earthquakes... [4-66-10]_END

B_3_C_64_22
BEGIN_
अभिजानामि पुष्पाणि तानि इमानि इह लक्ष्मण || ३-६४-२६
अपिनद्धानि वैदेह्या मया दत्तानि कानने |_END
BEGIN_
"I recognise these flowers that are fallen here, oh, Lakshmana. In forest I gave
them to Vaidehi and she tucked these very flowers in her bun. [3-64-26b, 27a]_END

B_3_C_66_9
BEGIN_
यौ धर्मौ जगताम् नेत्रे यत्र सर्वम् प्रतिष्ठितम् |
आदित्य चन्द्रौ ग्रहणम् अभ्युपेतौ महाबलौ || ४-६६-११_END
BEGIN_
"Which duteous pair is the pair of eyes of the world in whom all the systems of
world are peremptory, though that pair of Sun and Moon are doughtily influential in this solar
system, eclipse draws nigh of them... [4-66-11]_END

B_3_C_64_23
BEGIN_
मन्ये सूर्यः च वायुः च मेदिनी च यशशिविनि || ३-६४-२७
अभिरक्षन्ति पुष्पाणि प्रकुर्वन्तो मम प्रियम् |_END
BEGIN_
"These flowers are carefully safeguarded by the sun, as they are unwithered yet, by
air as they are unswept by it, and by the glorious earth, as they are unspoilt by that, thus I deem
that these naturals, sun, air, and earth are really proffering a helping hand to me. [3-64-27b,
28a]_END

B_3_C_66_10
BEGIN_
सुमहान्ति अपि भूतानि देवाः च पुरुष ऋषभ |
न दैवस्य प्रमुंचन्ति सर्व भूतानि देहिनः || ४-६६-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Even very great incorporates like earth and suchlike planets, oh, bullish man, or
even the gods, or even all corporeal beings, cannot get release from the predestine of Supreme
Being... [4-66-12]_END

B_3_C_64_24
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्त्वा महाबाहुः लक्ष्मणम् पुरुषर्षभम् || ३-६४-२८
उवाच रामो धर्मात्मा गिरिम् प्रसवण आकुलम् |_END
BEGIN_
On saying thus to best one among men Lakshmana, that virtue-souled and dextrous Rama
asked the mountain that is uproarious with rapids. [3-64-28b, 29a]_END

B_3_C_66_11
BEGIN_
शक्र आदिषु अपि देवेषु वर्तमानौ नय अनयौ |
श्रूयेते नर शार्दूल न त्वम् व्यथितुम् अर्हसि || ४-६६-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, tigerly-man, we hear that whether gods like Indra et al., are ethical and/or
unethical, yet they too have the resultant agonies and ecstasies... hence, it is inapt of you to
fret thyself... [4-66-13]_END

B_3_C_64_25
BEGIN_
कच्चित् क्षिति भृताम् नाथ दृष्टा सर्वांग सुंदरीम् || ३-६४-२९
रामा रम्ये वनोद् देशे मया विरहिता त्वया |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, lord among the earth-bolstered mountains, have you somehow seen a beauty by all
her limbs, foregone by me in beautiful woodlands?" [3-64-29b, 30a]_END

B_3_C_66_12
BEGIN_
हृतायाम् अपि वैदेह्याम् नष्टायाम् अपि राघव |
शोचितुम् न अर्हसे वीर यथा अन्यः प्राकृतः तथा || ४-६६-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Whether Vaidehi is stolen or slain, oh, brave one, it will be inapt of you sadden
like this as with any other commoner without tracking her whereabouts... [4-66-14]_END

B_3_C_64_26
BEGIN_
क्रुद्धो अब्रवीत् गिरिम् तत्र सिंहः क्षुद्र मृगम् यथा || ३-६४-३०
ताम् हेम वर्णाम् हेम अंगीम् सीताम् दर्शय पर्वत |
यावत् सानूनि सर्वाणि न ते विध्वंसयामि अहम् || ३-६४-३१_END
BEGIN_
Because his question is unanswered he is enraged as with a lion enraging at a puny
animal, and then he spoke to the mountain, "show me that golden tinged, golden limbed Seetha, oh,
mountain, no sooner than I devastate all your apices, apiece..." [3-64-30b, 31]_END

B_3_C_66_13
BEGIN_
त्वत् विधा नहि शोचन्ति सततम् सर्व दर्शिनः |
सुमहत्सु अपि कृच्छ्रेषु राम अनिर्विण्ण दर्शनाः || ४-६६-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Persons of your like who are always equable in their outlook, oh, Rama, they will
remain non-dispirited even if they are undergoing desperate straits, and they will not just sadden
like this... [4-66-15]_END

B_3_C_64_27
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु रामेण पर्वतो मैथिलीम् प्रति |
दर्शयन् इव ताम् सीताम् न दर्शयत राघवे || ३-६४-३२_END
BEGIN_
