When Rama spoke to the mountain in this way, that mountain echoed as if it is
revealing Seetha, but actually it has not revealed Seetha to Raghava. [3-64-32]_END

B_3_C_66_14
BEGIN_
तत्त्वतो हि नरश्रेष्ठ बुद्ध्या समनुचिंतय |
बुद्ध्या युक्ता महाप्राज्ञा विजानन्ति शुभ अशुभे || ४-६६-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, foremost man among men, you ratiocinate in subtle pursuit, objectively and
brainily, and great brains will comprehend good and bad in subtlety with their braininess...
[4-66-16]_END

B_3_C_64_28
BEGIN_
ततो दाशरथी राम उवाच शिलोच्चयम् |
मम बाण अग्नि निर्दग्धो भस्मी भूतो भविष्यसि || ३-६४-३३
असेव्यः सततम् चैव निस्तृण द्रुम पल्लवः |_END
BEGIN_
Then Rama of Dasharatha said to the hefty mountain, "When the infernos of my arrows
will burn you down completely and when you will be pared down ashes, you shall be grassless,
treeless and tender-leafless, and thus you become a meritless mountain... hence, show Seetha before
becoming so... [3-64-33, 34a]_END

B_3_C_66_15
BEGIN_
अदृष्ट गुण दोषाणाम् अधृवाणाम् च कर्मणाम् |
न अंतरेण क्रियाम् तेषाम् फलम् इष्टम् च वर्तते || ४-६६-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Indiscernible are the rights and wrongs of actions, and indefinite are the
cherished fruits of those actions, and without performing any action, fruits also will be
nonexistent... [4-66-17]_END

B_3_C_64_29
BEGIN_
इमाम् वा सरितम् च अद्य शोषयिष्यामि लक्ष्मण || ३-६४-३४
यदि न आख्याति मे सीताम् अद्य चन्द्र निभ आननाम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Lakshmana, if this River Godavari is not going to tell me immediately about that
moonshine-faced Seetha, now I will dry her up... [3-64-34b, 35a]_END

B_3_C_64_30
BEGIN_
एवम् प्ररुषितो रामो दिधक्षन् इव चक्षुषा || ३-६४-३५
ददर्श भूमौ निष्क्रांतम् राक्षसस्य पदम् महत् |
त्रस्तया राम काङ्क्षिण्याः प्रधावन्त्या इतः ततः || ३-६४-३६
राक्षसेन अनुवृत्तया वैदेह्या च पादानि तु |_END
BEGIN_
This way when Rama is highly infuriated and who appeared to burn down anything just
with his eyes, then he has seen on the ground gigantic footprints of a demon, and the footprints of
Vaidehi, who appeared to have run fearfully here and there in a helter-skelter manner expecting the
arrival of Rama, and which footprints are heavily trodden by a demon who followed her. [3-64-35b,
36, 37a]_END

B_3_C_66_16
BEGIN_
माम् एवम् हि पुरा वीर त्वम् एव बहुशो उक्तवान् |
अनुशिष्यात् हि को नु त्वाम् अपि साक्षात् बृहस्पतिः || ४-६६-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh valiant one, indeed you alone have said this way to me previously and
repeatedly, who really can profess you even he were to be professedly the Jupiter... [4-66-18]_END

B_3_C_64_31
BEGIN_
स समीक्ष्य परिक्रान्तम् सीताया राक्षसस्य च || ३-६४-३७
भंगम् धनुः च तूणी च विकीर्णाम् बहुधा रथम् |
संभ्रांत हृदयो रामः शशंस भ्रातरम् प्रियम् || ३-६४-३८_END
BEGIN_
On scrutinising the overly trodden footprints of Seetha and the demon, and a broken
bow, broken quiver, and broken and variously bestrewn chariot also, then Rama became baffle-hearted
and said to his dear brother Lakshmana. [3-64-37b, 38]_END

B_3_C_66_17
BEGIN_
बुद्धिः च ते महाप्राज्ञ देवैः अपि दुर्अन्वया |
शोकेन अभिप्रसुप्तम् ते ज्ञानम् सम्बोधयामि अहम् || ४-६६-१९_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, great discerner, your thinking process is non-explicatory even to gods, but now
that thinking process is obliquely and utterly slumberous owing to your sadness, hence I am
addressing your percipience and this is no schoolteaching... [4-66-19]_END

B_3_C_64_32
BEGIN_
पश्य लक्ष्मण वैदेह्याः कीर्णाम् कनक बिन्दवः |
भूषणानाम् हि सौमित्रे माल्यानि विविधानि च || ३-६४-३९_END
BEGIN_
"See Lakshmana, many beads of jewellery and many bits of garlands of Vaidehi have
indeed fallen down, and oh, Soumitri, they are strewn around... [3-64-39]_END

B_3_C_66_18
BEGIN_
दिव्यम् च मानुषम् च एवम् आत्मनः च पराक्रमम् |
इक्ष्वाकु वृषभ अवेक्ष्य यतस्व द्विषताम् वधे || ४-६६-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, foremost one among Ikshvaku, oh, Rama, contemplate the divineness of those
immortals and their pure being in maintaining world order, also consider the humanness of these
mortals and their helpless susceptibility to pain, also count on your own valour that which can
annihilate the whole of anything... and then come to conclusion whether or not to annihilate
everything... but, before that try hard to eliminate the abuser, lest he may abuse many others...
[4-66-20]_END

B_3_C_64_33
BEGIN_
तप्त बिन्दु निकाशैः च चित्रैः क्षतज बिन्दुभिः |
आवृतम् पश्य सौमित्रे सर्वतो धरणी तलम् || ३-६४-४०_END
BEGIN_
"Also the surface of the earth is everywhere interspersed with big and small blood
drops that are akin to golden droplets, you see them Saumitri... [3-64-40]_END

B_3_C_66_19
BEGIN_
किम् ते सर्व विनाशेन कृतेन पुरुष ऋषभ |
तम् एव तु रिपुम् पापम् विज्ञाय उद्धर्तुम् अर्हसि || ४-६६-२१_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, best one among men, what is it you gain on performing a complete annihilation
owing to a single soul's malefaction, hence, mark him... that malefactor and a malevolent of yours,
and it will be apt of you to uproot him... him alone... [4-66-21]_END

B_3_C_64_34
BEGIN_
मन्ये लक्ष्मण वैदेही राक्षसैः काम रूपिभिः |
भित्त्वा भित्त्वा विभक्ता वा भक्षिता वा भविष्यति || ३-६४-४१_END
BEGIN_
"I think Lakshmana, guise changing demons would have ripped and rived Vaidehi, or
divided her into pieces, or they might have gluttonised her. [3-64-41]_END

B_3_C_67_0
BEGIN_
पूर्वजो अपि उक्त मात्रः तु लक्ष्मणेन सुभाषितम् |
सार ग्राही महासारम् प्रतिजग्राह राघवः || ३-६७-१_END
BEGIN_
Even though Rama is elder to Lakshmana he gleaned the ultimate tenor of Lakshmana's
words when Lakshmana just said them expediently because Raghava is a best gleaner of the gist of
advises. [3-67-1]_END

B_3_C_64_35
BEGIN_
तस्या निमित्तम् वैदेह्या द्वयोः विवदमानयोः |
बभूव युद्धम् सौमित्रे घोरम् राक्षसयोः इह || ३-६४-४२_END
BEGIN_
"A deadly clash has occurred here, Soumitri, while two demons were clashing between
themselves on account of Vaidehi... [3-64-42]_END

B_3_C_67_1
BEGIN_
स निगृह्य महाबाहुः प्रवृद्धम् रोषम् आत्मनः |
अवष्टभ्य धनुः चित्रम् रामो लक्ष्मणम् अब्रवीत् || ३-६७-२_END
BEGIN_
Such as he is that dextrous Rama on controlling his highly heightening fury,
propping against his bedazzling bow spoke this to Lakshmana. [3-67-2]_END

B_3_C_64_36
BEGIN_
मुक्ता मणि चितम् च इदम् तपनीय विभूषितम् |
धरण्याम् पतितम् सौम्य कस्य भग्नम् महत् धनुः || ३-६४-४३
राक्षसानाम् इदम् वस्त सुराणाम् अधवा अपि |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, gentle Lakshmana, studded with pearls and gems this great bow of someone is
beautifully decorated, but it is fragmented and fallen to earth. Oh, dear boy, Lakshmana, this bow
may perhaps belong to demons, or else to gods... [3-64-43, 44a]_END

B_3_C_67_2
BEGIN_
किम् करिष्यावहे वत्स क्व वा गच्छाव लक्ष्मण |
केन उपायेन पश्येयम् सीताम् इह विचिन्तय || ३-६७-३_END
BEGIN_
"What is to be done by us, oh, dear boy... or, whereto we might go, or, by which
device Seetha is discernable... Lakshmana, now you think of it, clearly... [3-67-3]_END

B_3_C_64_37
BEGIN_
तरुण आदित्य संकाशम् वैदूर्य गुलिका चितम् || ३-६४-४४
विशीर्णम् पतितम् भूमौ कवचम् कस्य कांचनम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Studded with lapis gem beads this golden armour of someone is similar to the rising
sun in its shine, but it is splintered and fallen to earth... [3-64-44b, 45a]_END

B_3_C_67_3
BEGIN_
तम् तथा परिताप आर्तम् लक्ष्मणो रामम् अब्रवीत् |
इदम् एव जनस्थानम् त्वम् अन्वेषितुम् अर्हसि || ३-६७-४
राक्षसैः बहुभिः कीर्णम् नाना द्रुम लता आयुतम् |_END
BEGIN_
To such a Rama who is tormented by anguish, Lakshmana said, "it will be apt of you
to search this Janasthaana alone which is rife with many demons, and replete with manifold trees
and climber-plants... [3-67-4]_END

B_3_C_64_38
BEGIN_
छत्रम् शत शलाकम् च दिव्य माल्य उपशोभितम् || ३-६४-४५
भग्न दण्डम् इदम् कस्य भूमौ सौम्य निपातितम् |_END
BEGIN_
"This hundred-spoked regal-parasol of someone is embellished with divine festoons,
but oh, gentle Lakshmana, its central-shaft is wrecked and it is felled to earth... [3-64-45b,
46a]_END

B_3_C_67_4
BEGIN_
सन्ति इह गिरि दुर्गाणि निर्दराः कंदराणि च || ३-६७-५
गुहाः च विविधा घोरा नाना मृग गण आकुलाः |
आवासाः किन्नराणाम् च गन्धर्व भवनानि च || ३-६७-६_END
BEGIN_
"Here there are unclimbable mountains, glens and glyphs as well. There are divers
and pernicious caverns tumultuous with diverse packs of predators, and here are the mansions of
kinnaraa-s and palaces of gandharva-s, as well... [3-67-5b, 6]_END

B_3_C_64_39
BEGIN_
कान्चन उरः छदाः च इमे पिशाच वदनाः खराः || ३-६४-४६
भीम रूपा महाकायाः कस्य वा निहता रणे |_END
BEGIN_
"These ghost-faced mules with golden breastplates are macabre in form and massive in
frame, but they are hewed down in war, whose are they, either... [3-64-46b, 47a]_END

B_3_C_67_5
BEGIN_
तानि युक्तो मया सार्धम् समन्वेषितुम् अर्हसि |
त्वत् विधा बुद्धि संपन्ना माहात्मानो नरर्षभ || ३-६७-७
आपत्सु न प्रकंपन्ते वायु वेगैः इव अचलाः |_END
BEGIN_
"It will be apt of you to steadfastly search in them along with me, and oh, best one
among men, your sort of literati and clever-souls will be unfluctuating in calamities like the
mountains unfluctuating in windstorms..." Lakshmana said so Rama. [3-67-6, 7, 8a]_END

B_3_C_64_40
BEGIN_
दीप्त पावक संकाशो द्युतिमान् समर ध्वजः || ३-६४-४७
अपविद्धः च भग्नः च कस्य सांग्रामिको रथः |_END
BEGIN_
"Somebody's combat-chariot is irradiant and similar in shine to the flaring fire
with a war-pennon, but it is broken and battered down, as well... [3-64-47b, 48a]_END

B_3_C_67_6
BEGIN_
इति उक्तः तत् वनम् सर्वम् विचचार स लक्ष्मणः || ३-६७-८
क्रुद्धो रामः शरम् घोरम् संधाय धनुषि क्षुरम् |_END
BEGIN_
When Lakshmana said in this way to that ireful Rama, he roved entire forest along
with Lakshmana readying a crescent-shaped razor-sharp deadly arrow on his bow. [3-67-8b, 9a]_END

B_3_C_64_41
BEGIN_
रथ अक्ष मात्रा विशिखाः तपनीय विभूषणाः || ३-६४-४८
कस्य इमे निहता बाणाः प्रकीर्णा घोर दर्शनः |_END
BEGIN_
"These frightful looking arrows of somebody are gilded and they are as much as a
chariot's axle in their thickness, but their arrowheads are shred and they are manifoldly shredded
and strewn around... [3-64-48, 49a]_END

B_3_C_67_7
BEGIN_
ततः पर्वत कूट आभम् महा भागम् द्विज उत्तमम् || ३-६७-९
ददर्श पतितम् भूमौ क्षतज आर्द्रम् जटायुषम् |_END
BEGIN_
Then Rama beheld Jataayu who is akin to a mountaintop in his gleam, and a best
beatific brave bird among all the birds, but bloodstained and buckling on earth. [3-67-9b, 10a]_END

B_3_C_64_42
BEGIN_
शरावरौ शरैः पूर्णौ विध्वस्तौ पश्य लक्ष्मण || ३-६४-४९
प्रतोद अभीशु हस्तो अयम् कस्य वा सारथिः हतः |_END
BEGIN_
"Lakshmana, you see these two quivers packed with arrows are completely shattered,
and the charioteer is drop dead with whip and bridles still in his hands... whose charioteer he
might be! [3-64-49b, 50a]_END

B_3_C_67_8
BEGIN_
तम् दृष्ट्वा गिरि शृंग आभम् रामो लक्ष्मणम् अब्रवीत् || ३-६७-१०
अनेन सीता वैदेही भक्षिता न अत्र संशयः |_END
BEGIN_
On beholding him who is like a mountaintop in his gleam, Rama said to Lakshmana,
"This one has gluttonised Seetha, the princess from Vaidehi, there is no doubt about it...
[3-67-10b, 11a]_END

B_3_C_64_43
BEGIN_
पदवी पुरुषस्य एषा व्यक्तम् कस्य अपि राक्षसः || ३-६४-५०
वैरम् शत गुणम् पश्य मम तैः जीवित अंतकम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Evidently this is the modus operandi of someone who is a male demon, and you see
how my animosity has become hundredfold to eradicate them... [3-64-50b, 51a]_END

B_3_C_67_9
BEGIN_
गृध्र रूपम् इदम् व्यक्तम् रक्षो भ्रमति काननम् || ३-६७-११
भक्षयित्वा विशालाक्षीम् आस्ते सीताम् यथा सुखम् |
एनम् वधिष्ये दीप्त अग्रैः घोरैः बाणैः अजिह्मगैः || ३-६७-१२_END
BEGIN_
"It is apparent that this demon skulks in the forest in the semblance of an eagle,
and having gluttonised that wide-eyed Seetha he is now reposing comfortably. I will eliminate him
with deadly arrows, whose arrowheads blaze away and which shoot off straightly..." Thus Rama
declared. [3-67-11b, 12]_END

B_3_C_64_44
BEGIN_
सुघोर हृदयैः सौम्य राक्षसैः काम रूपिभिः || ३-६४-५१
हृता मृता वा सीता हि भक्षिता वा तपस्विनी |
न धर्मः त्रायते सीताम् ह्रियमाणाम् महावने || ३-६४-५२_END
BEGIN_
"The highly stony-hearted demons that are guise-changers by their wish have either
abducted, or killed or gluttonised saintly Seetha... but, they say that rectitude saves such
saintly persons... yet that rectitude has not saved Seetha while she is being abducted in great
forest... [3-64-51b, 52]_END

B_3_C_67_10
BEGIN_
इति उक्त्वा अभ्यपतत् गृध्रम् सन्धाय धनुषि क्षुरम् |
क्रुद्धो रामः समुद्र अन्ताम् चालयन् इव मेदिनीम् || ३-६७-१३_END
BEGIN_
On saying thus and on readying a crescent-shaped razor-sharp deadly arrow on his
bow, that ireful Rama rushed towards the eagle, as though to a-tremble the whole of the earth that
which is within the perimeter of oceans. [3-67-13]_END

B_3_C_64_45
BEGIN_
भक्षितायाम् हि वैदेह्याम् हृतायाम् अपि लक्ष्मण |
के हि लोके प्रियम् कर्तुम् शक्ताः सौम्य मम ईश्वराः || ३-६४-५३_END
BEGIN_
"Whether Vaidehi is taken away or taken in by some unknown being, oh, gentle
Lakshmana, then who are the gods who can possibly be benignant to me in this world... [3-64-53]_END

B_3_C_67_11
BEGIN_
तम् दीन दीनया वाचा स फेनम् रुधिरम् वमन् |
अभ्यभाषत पक्षी तु रामम् दशरथ आत्मजम् || ३-६७-१४_END
BEGIN_
But that bird spewing up frothy blood pathetically appealed to such an ireful son of
Dasharatha, namely Rama, in a pathetic tone. [3-67-14]_END

B_3_C_64_46
BEGIN_
कर्तारम् अपि लोकानाम् शूरम् करुण वेदिनम् |
अज्ञानात् अवमन्येरन् सर्व भूतानि लक्ष्मण || ३-६४-५४_END
BEGIN_
"Lakshmana, someone, even if He were a Creator of Worlds, or an Omnipotent, if He
were to be lenient at heart or in His actions, He will be disrespected by all beings, owing to the
unenlightenment of those beings... [3-64-54]_END

B_3_C_68_0
BEGIN_
रामः प्रेक्ष्य तु तम् गृध्रम् भुवि रौद्रेण पातितम् |सौमित्रिम् मित्र संपन्नम् इदम् वचनम् अब्रवीत् 
|| ३-६८-१_END
BEGIN_
Rama on seeing that eagle felled to ground by the atrocious Ravana, said this sentence to Soumitri who 
is an asset for good companionability. [3-68-1]_END

B_3_C_67_12
BEGIN_
याम् ओषधिम् इव आयुष्मन् अन्वेषसि महा वने |
सा देवी मम च प्राणा रावणेन उभयम् हृतम् || ३-६७-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, boy Rama, blest is your eternality, for whom you are searching as with the
search of a rejuvenescent herb in the vast of forest, Ravana stole that lady and my lives, too...
[3-67-15]_END

B_3_C_64_47
BEGIN_
मृदुम् लोक हिते युक्तम् दांतम् करुण वेदिनम् |
निर्वीर्य इति मन्यन्ते नूनम् माम् त्रिदश ईश्वराः || ३-६४-५५_END
BEGIN_
"I who am mellowly, magnanimous, merciful and yoked only to the wellbeing of all
worlds, such as I am, all of the heavenly gods deem me as non-Omnipotent... it is definite...
[3-64-55]_END

B_3_C_68_1
BEGIN_
मम अयम् नूनम् अर्थेषु यतमानो विहंगमः |राक्षसेन हतः संख्ये प्राणान् त्यजति मत् कृते || ३-६८-२_END
BEGIN_
"While this bird is venturing in my concern the demon felled him in combat and he is leaving off his 
lives owing to me, definitely... [3-68-2]_END

B_3_C_67_13
BEGIN_
त्वया विरहिता देवी लक्ष्मणेन च राघव |
ह्रियमाणा मया दृष्टा रावणेन बलीयसा || ३-६७-१६_END
BEGIN_
"I have seen that lady while being stolen by brute-forced Ravana when you and even
Lakshmana absented from her... [3-67-16]_END

B_3_C_64_48
BEGIN_
माम् प्राप्य हि गुणो दोषः संवृत्तः पश्य लक्ष्मण |
अद्य एव सर्व भूतानाम् रक्षसाम् अभवाय च || ३-६४-५६
संहृत्य एव शशि ज्योत्स्नाम् महान् सूर्य इव उदितः |
संहृत्य एव गुणान् सर्वान् मम तेजः प्रकाश्ते || ३-६४-५७_END
BEGIN_
"Have you seen Lakshmana how merits like mercifulness, magnanimity and the like are
inverted to become demerits on getting at me, thus I am unmerited in forgoing Seetha. As such, as
with the sizzle of sun uprisen quelling all the moonshine, now you may see as to how my irradiance
radiates quelling all the merits like softness and fairness for the nonentity of all beings
proactive to demons, inclusive of demons. [3-64-56, 57]_END

B_3_C_68_2
BEGIN_
अति खिन्नः शरीरे अस्मिन् प्राणो लक्ष्मण विद्यते |तथा स्वर विहीनो अयम् विक्लवम् समुदीक्षते || ३-६८-३_END
BEGIN_
"Obviously, lives in his body are very feeble, oh, Lakshmana, it is natural, isn't it, and he looks 
highly anguished with a dulled voice..." Thus on saying to Lakshmana, Rama then spoke to Jataayu. [3-68-3]_END

B_3_C_64_49
BEGIN_
न एव यक्षा न गंधर्वा न पिशाचा न राक्षसाः |
किन्नरा वा मनुष्या वा सुखम् प्राप्स्यन्ति लक्ष्मण || ३-६४-५८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Lakshmana, will the yaksha-s be comfortable now, no; gandharva-s - no; monsters
- no; demons - no; either kinnaraa-s or humans - no, none can be comfortable henceforth...
[3-64-58]_END

B_3_C_67_14
BEGIN_
सीताम् अभ्यवपन्नो अहम् रावणः च रणे मया |
विध्वंसित रथः च अत्र पातितो धरणी तले || ३-६७-१७_END
BEGIN_
"I outreached to rescue Seetha... and in a combat Ravana is rendered as one with
utterly battered chariot... and I felled him and that chariot there... onto earth's surface...
[3-67-17]_END

B_3_C_68_3
BEGIN_
जटायो यदि शक्नोषि वाक्यम् व्याहरितुम् पुनः |सीताम् आख्याहि भद्रम् ते वधम् आख्याहि च आत्मनः || ३-६८-४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Jataayu, if you are in fine fettle to further reiterate words, relate about Seetha, let safe betide 
you, and recount how you are murdered, too... [3-68-4]_END

B_3_C_64_50
BEGIN_
मम अस्त्र बाण संपूर्णम् आकाशम् पश्य लक्ष्मण |
असंपातम् करिष्यामि हि अद्य त्रैलोक्य चारिणाम् || ३-६४-५९_END
BEGIN_
"Now the welkin will be packed with my arrows and missiles, and I will render it as
an impassable sphere for the treaders in the triad of worlds... [3-64-59]_END

B_3_C_67_15
BEGIN_
एतत् अस्य धनुः भग्नम् एतत् अस्य शरावरम् |
अयम् अस्य रणे राम भग्नः सांग्रामिको रथः || ३-६७-१८_END
BEGIN_
"This one is his fragmented bow and this is his fragmented armour... oh, Rama, this
is his combat-chariot... which, in combat shattered by me... [3-67-18]_END

B_3_C_68_4
BEGIN_
किम् निमित्तो जहार आर्याम् रावणः तस्य किम् मया |अपराधम् तु यम् दृष्ट्वा रावणेन हृता प्रिया || ३-६८-५_END
BEGIN_
"What is the reason for Ravana in stealing that noblewoman, and even what is the wrong I have committed 
in his respect, keeping which in view that Ravana stole my ladylove... [3-68-5]_END

B_3_C_64_51
BEGIN_
संनिरुद्धग्रहगणमावारितनिशाकरम् |
विप्रनष्टानलमरुद्भास्करद्युतिसंवृतम् || - यद्व -
संनिरुद्ध ग्रह गणम् आवारित निशा करम् |
विप्रनष्ट अनल मरुत् भास्कर द्युति संवृतम् || ३-६४-६०
विनिर्मथितशैलाग्रम्शुष्यमाणजलाअशयम् |
ध्वस्तद्रुमलतागुल्मम्विप्रणाशितसागरम् || - यद्वा -
विनिर्मथित शैल अग्रम् शुष्यमाण जल आशयम् |
ध्वस्त द्रुम लता गुल्मम् विप्रणाशित सागरम् || ३-६४-६१
त्रै लोक्यम् तु करिष्यामि संयुक्तम् काल कर्मणा |_END
BEGIN_
"I will make the triad of worlds quiescent by completely blockading all the
planetary bodies. The night-maker moon will be barricaded, aurae of fire, air and sun will be
devastated, and then everything will be overcast with darkness. Mountaintops will be completely
pulverised, water receptacles will be dried out, and trees, creeping-plants and shrubberies will be
destroyed, and oceans depleted, thus I will bring the triad of the worlds to nought, relative to
the task of Time in extinguishing an era... [3-64-60, 61, 62a]_END

B_3_C_67_16
BEGIN_
अयम् तु सारथिः तस्य मत् पक्ष निहतो भुविः |
परिश्रान्तस्य मे पक्षौ छित्त्वा खड्गेन रावणः || ३-६७-१९
सीताम् आदाय वैदेहीम् उत्पपात विहायसम् |
रक्षसा निहतम् पूर्वम् न माम् हन्तुम् त्वम् अर्हसि || ३-६७-२०_END
BEGIN_
"This is his charioteer drop dead onto earth by my wings... when I am overtired
Ravana gashed my wings and flew skyward taking Seetha of Videha kingdom with him, and it will be
inapt of you to kill me who am already killed by the demon..." Thus Jataayu appealed to Rama.
[3-67-19, 20]_END

B_3_C_68_5
BEGIN_
कथम् तत् चन्द्र संकाशम् मुखम् आसीत् मनोहरम् |सीतया कानि च उक्तानि तस्मिन् काले द्विजोत्तम || ३-६८-६_END
BEGIN_
"How was that moon similar heart-stealing face of hers at that time of abduction, oh, best bird, and 
even what are the words she uttered when being abducted... [3-68-6]_END

B_3_C_64_52
BEGIN_
न ते कुशलिनीम् सीताम् प्रदास्यन्ति मम ईश्वराः || ३-६४-६२
अस्मिन् मुहूर्ते सौमित्रे मम द्रक्ष्यन्ति विक्रमम् |_END
BEGIN_
"If the gods are not going to safely restore Seetha to me, oh, Soumitri, they can
see what my blitzkrieg is, at this very moment... [3-64-62b, 63a]_END

B_3_C_67_17
BEGIN_
रामः तस्य तु विज्ञाय सीता सक्ताम् प्रियाम् कथाम् |
गृध्र राजम् परिष्वज्य परित्यज्य महत् धनुः || ३-६७-२१_END
BEGIN_
Rama jettisoned his forceful bow when he heard the much desired news about Seetha
while hugging that kingly eagle Jataayu. [3-67-21]_END

B_3_C_68_6
BEGIN_
कथम् वीर्यः कथम् रूपः किम् कर्मा स च राक्षसः |क्व च अस्य भवनम् तात ब्रूहि मे परिपृच्छतः || ३-६८-७_END
BEGIN_
"What is his stamina of that demon? What is his form? And what are his strategies? And where is his 
stronghold? Oh, sire, tell me while I ask you inquisitively..." Rama urged Jataayu thus for information. 
[3-68-7]_END

B_3_C_64_53
BEGIN_
न आकाशम् उत्पतिष्यन्ति सर्व भूतानि लक्ष्मण || ३-६४-६३
मम चाप गुण उन्मुक्तैः बाण जालैः निरंतरम् |_END
BEGIN_
"All beings cannot fly high in the sky, oh, Lakshmana, as there will be a labyrinth
of my arrows released from my bowstring, minus an intercolumniation... [3-64-63b, 64a]_END

B_3_C_67_18
BEGIN_
निपपात अवशो भूमौ रुरोद सह लक्ष्मण |
द्विगुणीकृत ताप आर्तो रामो धीरतरो अपि सन् || ३-६७-२२_END
BEGIN_
Even though Rama is comparatively a bold person he involuntarily fell down to
ground, as the onefold scorch of anguish for Seetha is doubled by this predicament of Jataayu, and
he wept over Jataayu. [3-67-22]_END

B_3_C_68_7
BEGIN_
तम् उद्वीक्ष्य सः धर्मात्मा विलपन्तम् अनाथवत् |वाचा विक्लवया रामम् इदम् वचनम् अब्रवीत् || ३-६८-८_END
BEGIN_
Then that warm-hearted Jataayu with his eyes rolling upwards saw Rama and with a fluttery voice said 
this sentence to Rama who is wailing like an orphan. [3-68-8]_END

B_3_C_64_54
BEGIN_
मर्दितम् मम नाराचैः ध्वस्त भ्रांत मृग द्विजम् || ३-६४-६४
समाकुलम् अमर्यादम् जगत् पश्य अद्य लक्ष्मण |_END
BEGIN_
"Bombarded with my iron-shafts this world will be put to disorderliness, Lakshmana,
you may now witness how the animals and birds will be dazed and devastated... [3-64-64b, 65a]_END

B_3_C_67_19
BEGIN_
एकम् एक अयने कृच्छ्रे निःश्वसन्तम् मुहुर् मुहुः |
समीक्ष्य दुःखितो रामः सौमित्रिम् इदम् अब्रवीत् || ३-६७-२३_END
BEGIN_
Jataayu is supine on a single-strait passable for a single-person and he is
suspiring for several times, and on seeing such Jataayu Rama became anguished and spoke this to
Soumitri. [3-67-23]_END

B_3_C_68_8
BEGIN_
सा हृता राक्षसेन्द्रेण रावणेन दुरात्मना |मायाम् आस्थाय विपुलाम् वात दुर्दिन संकुलाम् || ३-६८-९_END
BEGIN_
"Resorting to his illusionistic devices like creating an immense and tumultuous windstorm and cloud-cover, 
the flagitious chief of demons Ravana abducted Seetha... [3-68-9]_END

B_3_C_64_55
BEGIN_
आकर्णपूर्णैरिषुभिर्जीवलोकंदुरावरैः || - यद्वा -
आकर्ण पूर्णैर् इषुभिर् जीव लोकम् दुरावरैः || ३-६४-६५
करिष्ये मैथिली हेतोः अपिशाचम् अराक्षसम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Because of Maithili I will render this mortal world de-demonical, de-phantasmal by
force-stretching my unstoppable arrows up to my ears to release them forcefully... [3-64-65b,
66a]_END

B_3_C_67_20
BEGIN_
राज्यम् भ्रष्टम् वने वासः सीता नष्टा मृते द्विजः |
ईदृशी इयम् मम अलक्ष्मीः दहेत् अपि पावकम् || ३-६७-२४_END
BEGIN_
"Mislaid is my kingdom and I am mislocated into forests, Seetha is misplaced and now
this mischance of death on this bird... this kind of misfortune of mine incinerates even Agni, the
Divine-Incinerator... [3-67-24]_END

B_3_C_68_9
BEGIN_
परिक्लांतस्य मे तात पक्षौ चित्त्वा निशाचरः |सीताम् आदाय वैदेहीम् प्रयातो दक्षिणा मुखः || ३-६८-१०_END
BEGIN_
"That night walker hacked both my wings when I was overtired, and went southward taking the princess 
of Videha, Seetha, along with him... [3-68-10]_END

B_3_C_64_56
BEGIN_
मम रोष प्रयुक्तानाम् विशिखानाम् बलम् सुराः || ३-६४-६६
द्रक्ष्यन्ति अद्य विमुक्तानाम् अमर्षात् दूर गामिनाम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Let the gods witness now the impact of the blaze-crested, thoroughgoing arrows of
mine, projected by my wrath and released by my irascibility... [3-64-66b, 67a]_END

B_3_C_67_21
BEGIN_
संपूर्णम् अपि चेत् अद्य प्रतरेयम् महोदधिम् |
सो अपि नूनम् मम अलक्ष्म्या विशुष्येत् सरिताम् पतिः || ३-६७-२५_END
BEGIN_
"Even if it were to be a plethoric and limitless ocean, and now if I were to enter
it, or take a swim to the other shore of blissfulness, even that Lord of Rivers runs completely
dry, owing to my misfortune, it is definite... [3-67-25]_END

B_3_C_68_10
BEGIN_
उपरुध्यन्ति मे प्राणा दृष्टिर् भ्रमति राघव |पश्यामि वृक्षान् सौवर्णान् उशीर कृत मूर्धजान् || ३-६८-११_END
BEGIN_
"My sight is spinning and my lives are stifled, oh, Raghava, I am now seeing golden trees with cuscus 
grass as their treetops... [3-68-11]_END

B_3_C_64_57
BEGIN_
न एव देवा न दैतेया न पिशाचा न राक्षसाः || ३-६४-६७
भविष्यन्ति मम क्रोधात् त्रैलोक्ये विप्रणाशिते |_END
BEGIN_
"That being so, when the triad of worlds is completely ruined by my anger will there
be gods, no; demons - no; phantoms - no, none can survive... [3-64-67b, 68a]_END

B_3_C_67_22
BEGIN_
न अस्ति अभाग्यतरो लोके मत्तो अस्मिन् स चराचरे |
येन इयम् महती प्राप्ता मया व्यसन वागुरा || ३-६७-२६_END
BEGIN_
"There will not be any greater unfortunate being in this world than me, even if all
the sessile and mobile beings are put together, by whom such a complicated catastrophic enmeshment
as this is derived... [3-67-26]_END

B_3_C_69_0
BEGIN_
कृत्वा एवम् उदकम् तस्मै प्रस्थितौ राघवौ तदा |अवेक्षन्तौ वने सीताम् जग्मतुः पश्चिमाम् दिशम् || ३-६९-१_END
BEGIN_
In this way, Raghava-s on offering water oblations to Jataayu went southwestward in the forest and proceeded 
looking around for Seetha. [3-69-1]_END

B_3_C_64_58
BEGIN_
देव दानव यक्षाणाम् लोका ये रक्षसाम् अपि || ३-६४-६८
बहुधानिपतिष्यन्तिबाणोघैश्शकलीकृताः | - यद्वा -
बहुधा नि पतिष्यन्ति बाण ओघैः शकली कृताः |_END
BEGIN_
"Whatever worlds of gods, or monsters, or even those of demons are there, they will
be splintered and falling down apiece by the fusillades of my arrows... [3-64-68b, 69a]_END

B_3_C_68_11
BEGIN_
येन याति मुहूर्तेन सीताम् आदाय रावणः |विप्रनष्टम् धनम् क्षिप्रम् तत् स्वामि प्रतिपद्यते || ३-६८-१२
विन्दो नाम मुहूर्तो असौ स च काकुत्स्थ न अबुधत् |_END
BEGIN_
"In which spell of time Ravana has gone taking away Seetha, that spell is named as Vinda... if any riches 
are lost during that spell, the original possessor of those riches will repossess them very quickly... 
oh, Kakutstha, he that Ravana is unmindful of that fact and stole Seetha only to loose her... [3-68-12, 
13a]_END

B_3_C_67_23
BEGIN_
अयम् पितृ वयस्यो मे गृध्र राजो जरा अन्वितः |
शेते विनिहतो भूमौ मम भाग्य विपर्ययात् || ३-६७-२७_END
BEGIN_
"This decrepit kingly eagle is the friend of my father who is terminally gashed and
recumbent on the floor owing only to the backlash of my fortune..." So lamented Rama for the
wounded eagle Jataayu. [3-67-27]_END

B_3_C_69_1
BEGIN_
ताम् दिशम् दक्षिणाम् गत्वा शर चाप असि धारिणौ |अविप्रहतम् ऐक्ष्वाकौ पन्थानम् प्रतिपेदतुः || ३-६९-२_END
BEGIN_
On going in southwest direction, both the Ikshvaku-s wielding bows, arrows, and swords, have come about 
a pathway which is an off the beaten track. [3-69-2]_END

B_3_C_64_59
BEGIN_
निर्मर्यादानिमाँल्लोकान्करिष्याम्यद्यसायकैः || - यद्वा -
निर् मर्यादान् इमान् लोकान् करिष्यामि अद्य सायकैः || ३-६४-६९
हृताम् मृताम् वा सौमित्रे न दास्यन्ति मम ईश्वराः |_END
BEGIN_
"Whether she is abducted, or even if she is killed, oh, Soumitri, if the gods are
not going to give back my Seetha I will now jeopardise these worlds with my arrows... [3-64-69b,
70a]_END

B_3_C_68_12
BEGIN_
त्वत् प्रियाम् जानकीम् हृत्वा रावणो राक्षसेश्वर |झषवत् बडिशम् गृह्य क्षिप्रम् एव विनश्यति || ३-६८-१३_END
BEGIN_
"On stealing your ladylove Janaki, that chief of demons, Ravana, will ruin himself, as with a fish which 
swallows a baited fishhook... [3-68-13b, c]_END

B_3_C_67_24
BEGIN_
इति एवम् उक्त्वा बहुशो राघवः सह लक्ष्मणः |
जटायुषम् च पस्पर्श पितृ स्नेहम् निदर्शयन् || ३-६७-२८_END
BEGIN_
Thus, lamenting in that way for many times Raghava patted the body of Jataayu along
with Lakshmana instancing his parental regard. [3-67-28]_END

B_3_C_69_2
BEGIN_
गुल्मैः वृक्षैः च बहुभिः लताभिः च प्रवेष्टितम् |आवृतम् सर्वतो दुर्गम् गहनम् घोर दर्शनम् || ३-६९-३_END
BEGIN_
That pathway is thickly wrapped in and penned up with numerous trees, climber plants, and hedgerows 
from all over, thus that is jammed, blocked and horrid in its appearance. [3-69-3]_END

B_3_C_68_13
BEGIN_
न च त्वया व्यथा कार्या जनकस्य सुताम् प्रति |वैदेह्या रंस्यसे क्षिप्रम् हत्वा तम् रणमूर्धनि || ३-६८-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Impractical is your anguishing for the daughter of Janaka, as you will delight yourself with Vaidehi 
in no time, on killing that Ravana in the vanguard of a war..." Thus saying Jataayu paused for a while. 
[3-68-14]_END

B_3_C_64_60
BEGIN_
तथा रूपम् हि वैदेहीम् न दास्यन्ति यदि प्रियाम् || ३-६४-७०
नाशयामि जगत् सर्वम् त्रैलोक्यम् स चर अचरम् |
यावत् दर्शनम् अस्या वै तापयामि च सायकैः || ३-६४-७१_END
BEGIN_
"If my ladylove is not returned indeed in a fine fettle as she was before my running
after Golden Deer, I will be annihilating the triad of world in its entirety, together with its
mobile and sessile beings, and I will be sweltering the entire universe with my arrows as long as I
am not going to get a glimpse of her." Thus Rama gave a vent to his feelings. [3-64-70b, 71a]_END

B_3_C_67_25
BEGIN_
निकृत्त पक्षम् रुधिर अवसिक्तम्
तम् गृध्र राजम् परिरभ्य रामः |
क्व मैथिलि प्राण समा मम इति
विमुच्य वाचम् निपपात भूमौ || ३-६७-२९_END
BEGIN_
On hugging that kingly eagle whose wings are hacked off and who is bloodstained, and
on uttering this much, "she who is identical with my lives,... where is that Maithili..." Rama
collapsed to earth. [3-67-29]_END

B_3_C_69_3
BEGIN_
व्यतिक्रम्य तु वेगेन गृहीत्वा दक्षिणाम् दिशम् |सु भीमम् तन् महाअरण्यम् व्यतियातौ महाबलौ || ३-६९-४_END
BEGIN_
On taking up the southern direction, and on crossing over that highly horrendous and thick of the forest, 
both those spryly energetic brothers moved ahead, speedily. [3-69-4]_END

B_3_C_68_14
BEGIN_
असंमूढस्य गृध्रस्य रामम् प्रति अनुभाषतः |आस्यात् सुस्राव रुधिरम् म्रियमाणस्य स अमिषम् || ३-६८-१५_END
BEGIN_
Though Jataayu is speaking on to Rama with an alert mind, blood freely flowed from his mouth with shreds 
of flesh as death verged on him, even then he struggled to say. [3-68-15]_END

B_3_C_64_61
BEGIN_
इति उक्त्वा क्रोध ताम्र अक्षः स्फुरमाण ओष्ट संपुटः |
वल्कल अजिनम् आबद्ध्य जटा भारम् बन्धयत् || ३-६४-७२_END
BEGIN_
Rama on saying thus with his eyes reddening in fury, his lappet-fold of lips jerking
spasmodically, he girded up his jute-cloths and deerskin and twined up the mass of his matted-hair.
[3-64-72]_END

B_3_C_69_4
BEGIN_
ततः परम् जनस्थानात् त्रि क्रोशम् गम्य राघवौ |क्रौंच अरण्यम् विविशतुः गहनम् तौ महौजसौ || ३-६९-५_END
BEGIN_
Thereafter, both the highly vigorous Raghava-s have entered the impassable Kraunca forest, on going 
three krosa-s from Janasthaana. [3-69-5]_END

B_3_C_68_15
BEGIN_
पुत्रो विश्रवसः साक्षात् भ्राता वैश्रवणस्य च |इति उक्त्वा दुर्लभान् प्राणान् मुमोच पतगेश्वरः || 
३-६८-१६_END
BEGIN_
"That demon is the son of Vishravasa... literally... the brother of Kubera..." on saying thus, that 
lord of birds released his lives, which are unobtainable for oneself. [3-68-16]_END

B_3_C_64_62
BEGIN_
तस्य क्रुद्धस्य रामस्य तथा अभूतस्य धीमतः |
त्रि पुरम् जग्नुषः पूर्वम् रुद्रस्य इव बभौ तनुः || ३-६४-७३_END
BEGIN_
When the disposition of that venturesome and infuriated Rama has become in that way
holocaustic, it is like that of Rudra, the All-Inflamer god, when He became like this in earlier
times, intending to inflame the Triple-Cities. [3-64-73]_END

B_3_C_69_5
BEGIN_
नाना मेघ घन प्रख्यम् प्रहृष्टम् इव सर्वतः |नाना वर्णैः शुभैः पुष्पैः मृग पक्षि गणैः युतम् || ३-६९-६
दिदृक्षमाणौ वैदेहीम् तत् वनम् तौ विचिक्यतुः |तत्र तत्र अवतिष्ठन्तौ सीता हरण दुःखितौ || ३-६९-७_END
BEGIN_
Those two brothers who are disquieted by the abduction of Seetha are now agog to find her, and they 
intently explored that forest temporising there and there. That forest is evocative of a congeries of 
many a black-cloud, and it embodies numerous flowers on many a flowered tree, numerous flights of birds 
flitting over them, and numerous animals sprawling under them, and with them that forest is as though 
highly rejoiced everywhere. [3-69-6, 7]_END

B_3_C_68_16
BEGIN_
ब्रूहि ब्रूहि इति रामस्य ब्रुवाणस्य कृतांजलेः |त्यक्त्वा शरीरम् गृध्रस्य जग्मुः प्राणा विहायसम् 
|| ३-६८-१७_END
BEGIN_
But the lives of Jataayu departing from his body went into thin air before the very eyes of Rama who 
is still speaking to him with folded-palms, "tell... tell more..." [3-68-17]_END

B_3_C_64_63
BEGIN_
लक्ष्मणात् अथ च आदाय रामो निष्पीड्य कार्मुकम् |
शरम् आदाय संदीप्तम् घोरम् अशी विष उपमम् || ३-६४-७४
संदधे धनुषि श्रीमान् रामः पर पुरंजयः |
युग अन्त अग्निः इव क्रुद्धः इदम् वचनम् अब्रवीत् || ३-६४-७५_END
BEGIN_
On saying so that illustrious Rama, the delighter of world, grabbed his bow from
Lakshmana and gripped it tightly, unholstered a deadly and dazzling arrow from his quiver which is
like a poisonous serpent, and readying it on the bowstring of his bow, that Rama, the vanquisher of
enemies fastnesses, who looked like the Ear-End-Fire, spoke this sentence. [3-64-74, 75]_END

B_3_C_69_6
BEGIN_
ततः पूर्वेण तौ गत्वा त्रि क्रोसम् भ्रातरु तदा |क्रौंचारण्यम् अतिक्रम्य मातंग आश्रम अंतरा || ३-६९-८
दृष्टा तु तद् वनम् घोरम् बहु भीम मृग द्विजम् |नाना वृक्ष समाकीर्णम् सर्वम् गहन पादपम् || ३-६९-९
ददृशाः ते गिरौ तत्र दरीम् डशरथ आत्मजौ |पाताल सम गम्भीराम् तमसा नित्य संवृताम् || ३-६९-१०_END
BEGIN_
Then, both the brothers on passing over that Kraunca forest and on going from there eastwardly on a 
three-krosha route, those sons of Dasharatha have seen a horrendous forest in between Kraunca forest 
and Matanga hermitage, which is overspread with various thicketed and impassable trees, and over-sprawled 
by numerous gigantic predators and vulturine birds, and on scrutinising such a forest everywhere, there 
they saw a cave in a mountain, which is abyssal, equal to infernal region, and ever enshrouded by gloom. 
[3-69-8. 9, 10]_END

B_3_C_70_0
BEGIN_
तौ तु तत्र स्थितौ दृष्ट्वा भ्रातरौ राम लक्ष्मणौ |बाहु पाश परिक्षिप्तौ कबन्धो वाक्यम् अब्रवीत् || 
३-७०-१_END
BEGIN_
On prying at those two brothers, Rama and Lakshmana, who are completely stowed in the hangman's halter-like 
arms of the demon, and who are enduring within it, Kabandha said this sentence to them. [3-70-1]_END

B_3_C_68_17
BEGIN_
स निक्षिप्य शिरो भूमौ प्रसार्य चरणौ तदा |विक्षिप्य च शरीरम् स्वम् पपात धरणी तले || ३-६८-१८_END
BEGIN_
Jataayu flopped his head on earth, sprawled his feet on ground, and then his body collapsed onto the 
surface of earth writhing jerkily. [3-68-18]_END

B_3_C_64_64
BEGIN_
यथा जरा यथा मृत्युः यथा कालो यथा विधिः |
नित्यम् न प्रतिहन्यन्ते सर्व भूतेषु लक्ष्मण |
तथा अहम् क्रोध संयुक्तो न निवार्यो अस्मि असंशयम् || ३-६४-७६_END
BEGIN_
"As to how all the created beings cannot counteract the ageing, dying, fate and the
Time at anytime, likewise I too am non-countervailed, when I am coalesced with fury, no doubt about
it..." [3-64-76]_END

B_3_C_69_7
BEGIN_
आसाद्य च नरव्याघ्रौ दर्याः तस्या अविदूरतः |ददर्श तु महारूपाम् रक्षसीम् विकृत आननाम् || ३-६९-११_END
BEGIN_
On getting at that cave those manly-tigers have seen a demoness nearby that cave, who is massive in 
shape and misshapen in her face. [3-69-11]_END

B_3_C_70_1
BEGIN_
तिष्ठतः किम् नु माम् दृष्ट्वा क्षुधा आर्तम् क्षत्रिय ऋषभौ |आहार अर्थम् तु सन्दिष्टौ दैवेन गत चेतसौ 
|| ३-७०-२_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, excellent Kshatriya-s, on seeing me who am miserably famished, really what for you stay cool? You 
are the godsend gobs of mine, and hence now you are almost dead..." So said Kabandha to brothers. [3-70-2]_END

B_3_C_68_18
BEGIN_
तम् गृध्रम् प्रेक्ष्य ताम्र अक्षम् गत असुम् अचलोपमम् |रामः सु बहुभिः दुह्खैः दीनः सौमित्रिम् अब्रवीत् 
|| ३-६८-१९_END
BEGIN_
He who is worsened by very many mishaps that Rama, on seeing the mountainous eagle whose eyes are bloodshot 
and whose lives have gone, said this way to Soumitri... [3-68-19]_END

B_3_C_64_65
BEGIN_
पुरा इव मे चारु दतीम् अनिन्दिताम्
दिशन्ति सीताम् यदि न अद्य मैथिलीम् |
सदेव गन्धर्व मनुष्य पन्नगम्
जगत् स शैलम् परिवर्तयामि अहम् || ३-६४-७७_END
BEGIN_
"If that princess of Mithila, who has suavely and toothy smiles and who causes
irreproachability to my character if only I can have a glimpse of her, is not returned to me in
fine fettle as she was when she was with me, then I will countermove whole of this universe
together with its gods, immortals, humans, florae and faunas, mountains and waters... and
whatnot... [3-64-77]_END

B_3_C_69_8
BEGIN_
भयदाम् अल्प सत्त्वानाम् भीभत्साम् रौद्र दर्शनाम् |लंबोदरीम् तीक्ष्ण दंष्ट्राम् करालीम् परुष त्वचम् 
|| ३-६९-१२भक्षयन्तीम् मृगान् भीमान् विकटाम् मुक्त मूर्धजाम् |अवैक्षताम् तु तौ तत्र भ्रातरौ राम 
लक्ष्मणौ || ३-६९-१३_END
BEGIN_
Both the brothers, Rama and Lakshmana, have seen a demoness there, who is an inducer of horror to the 
dunderheaded dullards, traumatic in her acts and truculent in her appearance, pot-bellied, pierce-fanged, 
overblown, pachydermatous, head hair shaggy, body shape lumpy-bumpy, and she is going on eating massive 
beasts. [3-69-12, 13]_END

B_3_C_70_2
BEGIN_
तत् श्रुत्वा लक्ष्मणो वाक्यम् प्राप्त कालम् हितम् तदा |उवाच आर्तिम् समापन्नो विक्रमे कृत निश्चयः 
|| ३-७०-३_END
BEGIN_
Lakshmana who is possessed by anguish, and who is determined to wreck revenge on that demon, said these 
expedient and advisable words to Rama on hearing that demon's word. [3-70-3]_END

B_3_C_68_19
BEGIN_
बहूनि रक्षसाम् वासे वर्षाणि वसता सुखम् |अनेन दण्डकारण्ये विशीर्णम् इह पक्षिणा || ३-६८-२०_END
BEGIN_
"This bird which for years together lived fearlessly in Dandaka forest, a habitat of demons, that bird 
wilted to death, because of me... [3-68-20]_END

B_3_C_69_9
BEGIN_
सा समासाद्य तौ वीरौ व्रजन्तम् भ्रातुः अग्रतः |एहि रंस्यावहे इति उक्त्वा समालंबत लक्ष्मणम् || ३-६९-१४_END
BEGIN_
Drawing nigh of those valorous brothers who are journeying on their way, that demoness actually clung 
onto Lakshmana who is going ahead of his elder brother, saying, "come... let's romance..." [3-69-14]_END

B_3_C_70_3
BEGIN_
त्वाम् च माम् च पुरा तूर्णम् आदत्ते राक्षस अधमः |तस्मात् असिभ्याम् अस्य आशु बाहू चिन्दावहे गुरू 
|| ३-७०-४_END
BEGIN_
"This scurrilous demon quickly hauled in you and me to his face level, and he will quickly take us in, 
therefore, we will have to swiftly hack off his lengthy arms at his shoulder level... [3-70-4]_END

B_3_C_68_20
BEGIN_
अनेक वार्षिको यः तु चिर काल समुत्थितः |सो अयम् अद्य हतः शेते कालो हि दुर्अतिक्रमः || ३-६८-२१_END
BEGIN_
"He who has longevity over many years, who actively strived for a long for rectitude, he is now killed 
and prostrating before the Time, because of me... alas... it is indeed impossible to infringe the Time... 
[3-68-21]_END

B_3_C_69_10
BEGIN_
उवाच च एनम् वचनम् सौमित्रिम् उपगुह्य सा |अहम् तु अयोमुखी नाम लाभः ते त्वम् असि प्रियः || ३-६९-१५
नाथ पर्वत दुर्गेषु नदीनाम् पुलिनेषु च |आयुः चिरम् इदम् वीर त्वम् मया सह रंस्यसे || ३-६९-१६_END
BEGIN_
Closeting Soumitri in her embrace she told him this sentence, "I am Ayomukhi, by my name... you won 
me by your heroic personality, by that way, none can win me over... thus, you alone are my lover... 
oh, hero, oh, my husband... you will romance with me on mountaintops, in rivers, and on sandy isles, 
till the end of this life..." So is the love prattle of that demoness Ayomukhi. [3-69-15, 16]_END

B_3_C_70_4
BEGIN_
भिषणो अयम् महाकायो राक्षसो भुज विक्रमः |लोकम् हि अति जितम् कृत्वा हि अवाम् हन्तुम् इह इच्छति || 
३-७०-५_END
BEGIN_
"Gruesome is this gargantuan bodied demon, and triumphing over just with his arms he has utterly devastated 
this province, and he now wishes to end us... [3-70-5]_END

B_3_C_68_21
BEGIN_
पश्य लक्ष्मण गृध्रो अयम् उपकारी हतः च मे |सीताम् अभ्यवपन्नो हि रावणेन बलीयसा || ३-६८-२२_END
BEGIN_
"Lakshmana, this eagle which has dashed to rescue Seetha in order to render help to me is slain by that 
brute-forced Ravana, only because of me, you see... [3-68-22]_END

B_3_C_69_11
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु कुपितः खडगम् उद्धृत्य लक्ष्मणः |कर्ण नास स्तनम् तस्या निचकर्ता अरिसूदनः || ३-६९-१७_END
BEGIN_
When said that way that enemy-suppressor Lakshmana became furious, and upraising his sword he sheared 
off her nose, one ear, and one of her breasts. [3-69-17]_END

B_3_C_70_5
BEGIN_
निश्चेष्टानाम् वधो राजन् कुत्स्तितो जगती पतेः |क्रतु मध्य उपनीतानाम् पशूनाम् इव राघव || ३-७०-६_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, king Raghava, killing the non-aggressive is tantamount to the killing of animals that are led into 
Vedic-ritual in its midst is despicable to the kings... [3-70-6]_END

B_3_C_68_22
BEGIN_
गृध्र राज्यम् परित्यज्य पितृ पैतामहम् महत् |मम हेतोः अयम् प्राणान् मुमोच पतगेश्वरः || ३-६८-२३_END
BEGIN_
"On abandoning great empire of eagles belonging to his father and forefathers this lord of bird has 
now abandoned his lives too, only for my sake... [3-68-23]_END

B_3_C_69_12
BEGIN_
कर्ण नासे निकृत्ते तु विस्वरम् विननाद सा |यथा आगतम् प्रदुद्राव राक्षसी घोर दर्शना || ३-६९-१८_END
BEGIN_
When her nose and ear are cut off that demoness of hideous mien yelled highly in a high voice, and she 
rushed off as she had rushed in at Lakshmana. [3-69-18]_END

B_3_C_70_6
BEGIN_
एतत् संजल्पितम् श्रुत्वा तयोः क्रुद्धः तु राक्षसः |विदार्य आस्यम् ततो रौद्रम् तौ भक्षयितुम् आरभत् 
|| ३-७०-७_END
BEGIN_
On hearing all of their conversation that demon is infuriated, and then widely opening his ferocious 
mouth he started to wolf down both of them. [3-70-7]_END

B_3_C_68_23
BEGIN_
सर्वत्र खलु दृश्यन्ते साधवो धर्म चारिणः |शूराः शरण्याः सौमित्रे तिर्यक् योनि गतेषु अपि || ३-६८-२४_END
BEGIN_
"Universally noticeable are the protective, prepotent, principled ones that are the followers of probity, 
oh, Soumitri, even though their births are avian or bestial... [3-68-24]_END

B_3_C_69_13
BEGIN_
तस्याम् गतायाम् गहनम् व्रजन्तौ वनम् ओजसा |आसेदतुः अरि मित्र घ्नौ भ्रातरौ राम लक्ष्मणौ || ३-६९-१९_END
BEGIN_
When she fled those two brothers who are the eliminators of the friends of their enemies, have travelled 
further into the forest and entered a dense area of that forest, with their spiritedness as their guiding 
force. [3-69-19]_END

B_3_C_70_7
BEGIN_
ततः तौ देश कालज्ञौ खड्गाभ्याम् एव राघवौ |अच्छिन्दताम् सुसंहृष्टौ बाहू तस्य अंस देशतः || ३-७०-८_END
BEGIN_
Then both the Raghava-s are very highly gladdened as the demon is hauling them towards his eye at shoulder 
level, and as they are the brothers with circumspection, they instantly mutilated his arms right at 
their shoulder joints only with two swords. [3-70-8]_END

B_3_C_68_24
BEGIN_
सीता हरणजं दुःखम् न मे सौम्य तथा गतम् |यथा विनाशो गृध्रस्य मत् कृते च परंतप || ३-६८-२५_END
BEGIN_
"To me, oh, enemy-inflamer, oh, gentle Lakshmana, anguish caused by Seetha's abduction is not that much, 
when compared with the anguish caused by the perish of this eagle, that too, because of me... [3-68-25]_END

B_3_C_69_14
BEGIN_
लक्ष्मणः तु महातेजाः सत्त्ववान् शीलवान् शुचिः |अब्रवीत् प्रांजलिः वाक्यम् भ्रातरम् दीप्त तेजसम् 
|| ३-६९-२०_END
BEGIN_
Though Lakshmana is the one with preparedness, properness, and pureness and thus a highly fulgent one 
by his persona, he prayfully said this sentence to his brother Rama whose anima is radiantly fulgorous. 
[3-69-20]_END

B_3_C_70_8
BEGIN_
दक्षिणो दक्षिणम् बाहुम् असक्तम् असिना ततः |चिच्छेद रामो वेगेन सव्यम् वीरः तु लक्ष्मणः || ३-७०-९_END
BEGIN_
Then that dextrous Rama with an unrestrained speed hacked off the right arm, and valiant Lakshmana on 
his part hewed down the left arm that speedily. [3-70-9]_END

B_3_C_68_25
BEGIN_
राजा दशरथः श्रीमान् यथा मम मया यशाः |पूजनीयः च मान्यः च तथा अयम् पतगेश्वरः || ३-६८-२६_END
BEGIN_
"As to how the celebrated and highly renowned king Dasharatha is venerable and honourable for me, likewise 
this lord of birds is also a venerable and honourable one to me... [3-68-26]_END

B_3_C_69_15
BEGIN_
स्पंदन्ते मे दृढम् बाहुः उद्विग्नम् इव मे मनः |प्रायशः च अपि अनिष्टानि निमित्तानि उपलक्षये || ३-६९-२१_END
BEGIN_
"My left arm is strongly shuddering and my heart is as though distraught... and even undesirable forebodings 
are also bidding fair... [3-69-21]_END

B_3_C_70_9
BEGIN_
स पपात महाबाहुः चिन्न बाहुः महा स्वनः |खम् च गाम् च दिशः चैव नादयन् जलदो यथा || ३-७०-१०_END
BEGIN_
He that overlong-armed Kabandha fell down with mangled arms, reverberated the sky, earth, and all of 
the ten points of horizon with a cacophonous voice, like a black-thunderous-cloud. [3-70-10]_END

B_3_C_68_26
BEGIN_
सौमित्रे हर काष्ठानि निर्मथिष्यामि पावकम् |गृध्र राजम् दिधक्षामि मत् कृते निधनम् गतम् || ३-६८-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Soumitri, get the firewood and I will produce fire by friction of two sticks, as I wish to cremate 
this lord of birds who expired because of me... [3-68-27]_END

B_3_C_69_16
BEGIN_
तस्मात् सज्जी भव आर्य त्वम् कुरुष्व वचनम् हितम् |मम एव हि निमित्तानि सद्यः शंसन्ति संभ्रमम् || ३-६९-२२_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, exalted brother, thereby you be at the ready by paying attention to my expedient words... these 
forebodings are indeed portending to me as if some hazard is immediately ensuing... [3-69-22]_END

B_3_C_71_0
BEGIN_
पुरा राम महाबाहो महाबल पराक्रम |रूपम् आसीत् मम अचिंत्यम् त्रिषु लोकेषु विश्रुतम् || ३-७१-१यथा 
सूर्यस्य सोमस्य शक्रस्य च यथा वपुः |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, great dextrous Rama with great daring and dashing, as to how the physique of sun, moon, and even 
that of Indra is there now, my physique was also like that earlier, an unbelievable mien and renowned 
in all the three worlds... [3-71-1, 2a]_END

B_3_C_70_10
BEGIN_
स निकृत्तौ भुजौ दृष्ट्वा शोणित ओघ परिप्लुतः |दीनः पप्रच्छ तौ वीरौ कौ युवाम् इति दानवः || ३-७०-११_END
BEGIN_
That demon on seeing at his dissevered shoulders on which the gushes of blood are overflowing, he self-piteously 
asked those two bold ones thus as, "who are you..." [3-70-11]_END

B_3_C_68_27
BEGIN_
नाथम् पतग लोकस्य चिताम् आरोपयामि अहम् |इमम् धक्ष्यामि सौमित्रे हतम् रौद्रेण रक्षसा || ३-६८-२८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Soumitri, I will mount this lord of realm of birds onto the pyre and cremate him who is killed 
by a feral demon..." Thus saying to Lakshmana, Rama said this to dead eagle Jataayu. [3-68-28]_END

B_3_C_69_17
BEGIN_
एष वंजुलको नाम पक्षी परम दारुणः |आवयोः विजयम् युद्धे शंसन् इव विनर्दति || ३-६९-२३_END
BEGIN_
"This eerily dreadful bird known to be Vanjulaka is loudly ululating as though presaging our triumph 
in any given conflict that may ensue..." So said Lakshmana to Rama. [3-69-23]_END

B_3_C_71_1
BEGIN_
सो अहम् रूपम् इदम् कृत्वा लोक वित्रासनम् महत् || ३-७१-२ऋषीन् वन गतान् राम त्रासयामि ततः ततः |_END
BEGIN_
"Such as I was with an admirable body, disguising myself in this kind of horrendous form which is utterly 
dreadful to the world, I was scaring the forest living sages, there and there... [3-71-2]_END

B_3_C_70_11
BEGIN_
इति तस्य ब्रुवाणस्य लक्ष्मणः शुभ लक्षणः |शशंस तस्य काकुत्स्थम् कबंधस्य महाबलः || ३-७०-१२_END
BEGIN_
When that great mighty Kabandha is asking thus, Lakshmana who has prosperous characteristics has informed 
him about Rama of Kakutstha, an unremitting dynasty. [3-70-12]_END

B_3_C_68_28
BEGIN_
या गतिः यज्ञ शीलानाम् आहित अग्नेः च या गतिः |अ पर आवर्तिनाम् या च या च भूमि प्रदायिनाम् || ३-६८-२९
मया त्वम् समनुज्ञातो गच्छ लोकान् अनुत्तमान् |गृध्र राज महा सत्त्व संस्कृतः च मया व्रज || ३-६८-३०_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, greatly mighty king of eagles, by me cremated ritually and by me aptly consented to, you depart 
to the unexcelled heavenly worlds... you depart to those worlds that are destined for the virtuosos 
of Vedic-rituals, and to those worlds that are destined for the practisers of ascesis amid Five-Ritual-fires, 
and to those that are destined for un-retreating combatants, and to those worlds that destined for the 
donors of lands..." So said Rama to the departed Jataayu. [3-68-29, 30]_END

B_3_C_69_18
BEGIN_
तयोः अन्वेषतोः एवम् सर्वम् तत् वनम् ओजसा |संजज्ञे विपुलः शब्दः प्रभंजन् इव तत् वनम् || ३-६९-२४_END
BEGIN_
When those two brothers are searching entire forest for Seetha in that way, they heard a boisterous 
brouhaha emanated as though to completely shatter down that forest. [3-69-24]_END

B_3_C_71_2
BEGIN_
ततः स्थूलशिरा नाम महर्षिः कोपितो मया || ३-७१-३संचिन्वन् विविधम् वन्यम् रूपेण अनेन धर्षितः |_END
BEGIN_
"On one day, when a great sage named Sthuulashira was collecting divers forest produce for his Vedic-ritual, 
I scared him with this ugly form and I even exasperated him... [3-71-3b, 4a]_END

B_3_C_68_29
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्त्वा चिताम् दीप्ताम् आरोप्य पतगेश्वरम् |ददाह रामो धर्मात्मा स्व बन्धुम् इव दुःखितः || ३-६८-३१_END
BEGIN_
On saying that way, that ethical-souled Rama mounted that lord of birds onto the pyre and he sorrowfully 
incinerated that eagle in a flaring fire of pyre, as he would do in respect of his own deceased relative. 
[3-68-31]_END

B_3_C_70_12
BEGIN_
अयम् इक्ष्वाकु दायादो रामो नाम जनैः श्रुतः |तस्य एव अवरजम् विद्धि भ्रातरम् माम् च लक्ष्मणम् || ३-७०-१३_END
BEGIN_
"He is known to people by the name of Rama, the legatee of Ikshvaku dynasty, and you know me as his 
younger brother, Lakshmana, by my name... [3-70-13]_END

B_3_C_69_19
BEGIN_
संवेष्टितम् इव अत्यर्थम् गहनम् मातरिश्वना |वनस्य तस्य शब्दो अभूत् दिवम् आपूरयन् इव || ३-६९-२५_END
BEGIN_
As though an unbearable windstorm muffles up the forest, that forest's cacophony appeared to be unbearably 
filling up that forest._END

B_3_C_71_3
BEGIN_
तेन अहम् उक्तः प्रेक्ष्य एवम् घोर शाप अभिधायिना || ३-७१-४एतत् एव नृशंसम् ते रूपम् अस्तु विगर्हितम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
"On seeing me that sage who is an enforcer of deadly curse cursed me in this way, 'that which is presently 
diabolic and despicable form of yours, hereinafter you will abide in this form alone...' [3-71-4b, 5a]_END

B_3_C_68_30
BEGIN_
रामो अथ सह सौमित्रिः वनम् यात्वा स वीर्यवान् |स्थूलान् हत्वा महा रोहीन् अनु तस्तार तम् द्विजम् || 
३-६८-३२_END
BEGIN_
Then that resolute Rama on going into forest along with Soumitri hunted a robust-bodied, big Rohi animal, 
or, Kesari animal, and then he spread sacred grass on ground to place that offering to the deceased 
soul of that bird. [3-68-32]_END

B_3_C_70_13
BEGIN_
मात्रा प्रतिहतो राज्ये रामः प्रवाजितो वनम् |मया सह चरति एष भार्यया च महत् वनम् || ३-७०-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Countervailed from kingdom by mother this Rama is bluntly sent to forests, and he is on the rove in 
great forests along with me ad his wife... [3-70-14]_END

B_3_C_69_20
BEGIN_
तम् शब्दम् कांक्षमाणः तु रामः खड्गी सह अनुजः |ददर्श सु महा कायम् राक्षसम् विपुल उरसम् || ३-६९-२६_END
BEGIN_
But desiring to know the source of that noise that sword-wielder Rama has seen a gigantically giant-bodied 
and gigantesque-chested demon in a section of brushwood along with his younger brother Lakshmana. [3-69-26]_END

B_3_C_71_4
BEGIN_
स मया याचितः क्रुद्धः शापस्य अन्तो भवेत् इति || ३-७१-५अभिशाप कृतस्य इति तेन इदम् भाषितम् वचः |_END
BEGIN_
"When I begged that enraged sage as, 'even if I have committed this blasphemy owing to my blasphemous 
fate, will there be an end to this blasphemed form of mine, or not...' and then he spoke this word to 
me... [3-71-5b, 6a]_END

B_3_C_68_31
BEGIN_
रोहि मांसानि च उद्धृत्य पेशी कृत्वा महायशाः |शकुनाय ददौ रामो रम्ये हरित शाद्वले || ३-६८-३३_END
BEGIN_
On drawing up the flesh of that Rohi animal and lumping it to gobbets, that highly observant Rama placed 
those gobbets on pleasant greenish pasturelands as obsequial offerings in respect of that bird Jataayu. 
[3-68-33]_END

B_3_C_70_14
BEGIN_
अस्य देव प्रभावस्य वसतो विजने वने |रक्षसा अपहृता भार्या याम् इच्छन्तौ इह आगतौ || ३-७०-१५_END
BEGIN_
"A demon stole his wife while he whose leverage is like that of god is living in the unpopulated forest... 
and wishing to retrieve her we came here... [3-70-15]_END

B_3_C_69_21
BEGIN_
आसेदतुः च तत् रक्षः तौ उभौ प्रमुखे स्थितम् |विवृद्धम् अ-शिरो ग्रीवम् कबंधम् उदरे मुखम् || ३-६९-२७_END
BEGIN_
Then they both had to drew nigh of a waylaying demon Kabandha, who is situated frontally with an overgrown 
body, which is neckless, ergo headless, ergo mouth in paunch. [3-69-27]_END

B_3_C_71_5
BEGIN_
यदा छित्त्वा भुजौ रामः त्वाम् दहेत् विजने वने || ३-७१-६तदा त्वम् प्राप्स्यसे रूपम् स्वम् एव विपुलम् 
शुभम् |_END
BEGIN_
" 'When Rama incinerates you in an uninhibited forest on chopping off your shoulders, then you will 
regain your own grand and auspicious form...' So said the sage to me... [3-71-6b, 7a]_END

B_3_C_68_32
BEGIN_
यत् तत् प्रेतस्य मर्त्यस्य कथयन्ति द्विजातयः |तत् स्वर्ग गमनम् पित्र्यम् क्षिप्रम् रामो जजाप ह || 
३-६८-३४_END
BEGIN_
Rama immediately chanted Vedic hymns that are employed in such funerals of one's own paternal people, 
as Brahmans say that those hymns are employable in such rites as they lead the soul of the departed 
to heaven. [3-68-34]_END

B_3_C_70_15
BEGIN_
त्वम् तु को वा किम् अर्थम् वा कबन्ध सदृशो वने |आस्येन उरसि दीप्तेन भग्न जन्घो विचेष्टसे || ३-७०-१६_END
BEGIN_
"But who are you? Your legs are broken, and your mouth is infernal, yet it is on your chest, and alike 
a topless, rootless tree trunk you are sprawling in the forest, how so, or, for what reason?" Lakshmana 
asked the demon thus. [3-70-16]_END

B_3_C_71_6
BEGIN_
श्रिया विराजितम् पुत्रम् दनोः त्वम् विद्धि लक्ष्मण || ३-७१-७इन्द्र कोपात् इदम् रूपम् प्राप्तम् एवम् 
रण आजिरे |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Lakshmana, you may know as the most handsome son of Danu, and this misshapen form has chanced on 
me owing the ire of Indra in battlefield... [3-71-7b, 8a]_END

B_3_C_69_22
BEGIN_
रोमभिर्निश्चितैस्तीक्ष्णैर्महागिरिमिवोच्छ्रितम् - यद्वा -रोमभिः निचितैः तीक्ष्णैः महागिरिम् इव उच्छ्रितम् 
|नील मेघ निभम् रौद्रम् मेघ स्तनित निःस्वनम् || ३-६९-२८_END
BEGIN_
That diabolical demon is peaking like a huge mountain, his hair is horripilate and thickset, and his 
gleam is like a dark cloud, and his sounding is like a thunder. [3-69-28]_END

B_3_C_70_16
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः कबंधः तु लक्ष्मणेन उत्तरम् वचः |उवाच परम प्रीतः तत् इन्द्र वचनम् स्मरन् || ३-७०-१७_END
BEGIN_
But Kabandha is highly delighted when Lakshmana spoke that way, as the words of Indra came to his memory, 
and he said these words in reply. [3-70-17]_END

B_3_C_68_33
BEGIN_
ततो गोदावरीम् गत्वा नदीम् नर वर आत्मजौ |उदकम् चक्रतुः तस्मै गृध्र राजाय तौ उभौ || ३-६८-३५_END
BEGIN_
Then both the sons of that notable man, namely Dasharatha, on going to River Godavari they have oblated 
waters for that king of eagles, Jataayu. [3-68-35]_END

B_3_C_71_7
BEGIN_
अहम् हि तपसा उग्रेण पितामहम् अतोषयम् || ३-७१-८दीर्घम् आयुः स मे प्रादात् ततो माम् विभ्रमो अस्पृशत् 
|_END
BEGIN_
"I have gladdened Grandparent Braham with severe ascesis and He granted longevity to me, and then a 
kind of recalcitrance touched off in my mind... [3-71-8b, 9a]_END

B_3_C_69_23
BEGIN_
अग्नि ज्वाल निकाशेन ललाटस्थेन दीप्यता |महापक्षेण पिंगेन विपुलेन आयतेन च || ३-६९-२९एकेन उरसि 
घोरेण नयनेन आशु दर्शिना |महा दंष्ट्र उपपन्नम् तम् लेलिहानम् महा मुखम् || ३-६९-३०_END
BEGIN_
Only one ochry eye blazing like the tongue of an inferno is there on his forehead, which forehead situated 
on his chest. That single eye with incisive and sharp-sight is broad beaming and wide angling, on which 
there are winglike eyelids. That monster is now licking his giant mouth that is stuffed with spearhead 
like fangs, as he has just finished a gobble, and the brothers had to drew nigh of such a demon. [3-69-29, 
30]_END

B_3_C_70_17
BEGIN_
स्वागतम् वाम् नरव्याघ्रौ दिष्ट्या पश्यामि वाम् अहम् |दिष्ट्या च इमौ निकृत्तौ मे युवाभ्याम् बाहु 
बन्धनौ || ३-७०-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, manly tigers, by my providence you are revealed to me... welcome to you... and providentially sheared 
are these shackles, called my two arms, by you... [3-70-18]_END

B_3_C_71_8
BEGIN_
दीर्घम् आयुः मया प्राप्तम् किम् मे शक्रः करिष्यति || ३-७१-९इति एवम् बुद्धिम् आस्थाय रणे शक्रम् अधर्षयम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
" 'When longevity is acquired by me what Indra can do to me...' thus relying upon that kind of certitude, 
I jousted with Indra in a bout... [3-71-9b, 10a]_END

B_3_C_68_34
BEGIN_
शास्त्र दृष्टेन विधिना जले गृधाय राघवौ |स्नात्वा तौ गृध्र राजाय उदकम् चक्रुः तदा || ३-६८-३६_END
BEGIN_
Both of the Raghava-s took funeral baths in the waters of River Godavari and then made water oblations 
to the king of eagles. [3-68-36]_END

B_3_C_69_24
BEGIN_
भक्षयंतम् महा घोरान् ऋक्ष सिम्ह मृग द्विपान् |घोरौ भुजौ विकुर्वाणम् उभौ योजनम् आयतौ || ३-६९-३१_END
BEGIN_
He is eating the highly brutal bears, lions, predators, and elephants, and he is outstretching both 
of his deadly arms, each of which is stretchable to a yojana distance, and the bothers neared such a 
demon. [3-69-31]_END

B_3_C_70_18
BEGIN_
विरूपम् यत् च मे रूपम् प्राप्तम् हि अविनयात् यथा |तत् मे शृणु नरव्याघ्र तत्त्वतः शंसतः तव || ३-७०-१९_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, manly tiger, actually how this form of mine is disfigured, of course owing to my distrustful behaviour, 
that you may listen while I narrate it to you. [3-70-19]_END

B_3_C_71_9
BEGIN_
तस्य बाहु प्रमुक्तेन वज्रेण शत पर्वणा || ३-७१-१०सक्थिनी च शिरः चैव शरीरे संप्रवेशितम् |_END
BEGIN_
"But the Thunderbolt that has a hundred cutting edges and that which is launched from Indra's hand has 
rammed by head and thighs into my body... [3-71-10b, 11a]_END

B_3_C_68_35
BEGIN_
स गृध्र राजः कृतवान् यशस्करम्सु दुष्करम् कर्म रणे निपातितः |महर्षि कल्पेन च संस्कृतः तदा
जगाम पुण्याम् गतिम् आत्मनः शुभाम् || ३-६८-३७_END
BEGIN_
That king of eagle Jataayu, who has performed a creditworthy deed of stalling and combating Ravana, 
but who is felled by that Ravana, went away to the merited and auspicious heavenly realms of his own, 
as and when consecrated by sublime sage like Rama. [3-68-37]_END

B_3_C_69_25
BEGIN_
कराभ्याम् विविधान् गृह्य ऋक्षान् पक्षि गणान् मृगान् |आकर्षन्तम् विकर्षन्तम् अनेकान् मृग यूथपान् 
|| ३-६९-३२स्थितम् आवृत्य पन्थानम् तयोः भ्रात्रोः प्रपन्नयोः |_END
BEGIN_
That demon stayed waylaying the pathway of both the brothers who chanced there, while he is catching 
bears, divers flights of birds, and numerous choicest animals of those and those herds, gripping them 
with both of his long-reaching hands and hauling towards his mouth at his paunch, or dropping them off 
if they are unpalatable, and the brothers reached nearby of such a demon. [3-69-32, 33a]_END

B_3_C_71_10
BEGIN_
स मया याच्यमानः सन् न आनयत् यम सादनम् || ३-७१-११पितामह वचः सत्यम् तत् अस्ति इति मम अब्रवीत् |_END
BEGIN_
"When I begged of him saying, 'lead me to the hell of Yama, rather than making me to live this hell 
of a body...' Then Indra said this to me, 'Let the Grandparent Brahma's word about your longevity come 
true...' Thus Indra spared me to me... [3-71-11b, 12a]_END

B_3_C_68_36
BEGIN_
कृतोदकौ तौ अपि पक्षि सत्तमेस्थिराम् च बुद्धिम् प्रणिधाय जग्मुतुः |प्रवेश्य सीता अधिगमने ततो 
मनोवनम् सुरेन्द्रौ इव विष्णु वासवौ || ३-६८-३८_END
BEGIN_
Even those two, Rama and Lakshmana, on performing water oblations in respect of that best bird Jataayu, 
and on assertively giving thought to the information given by Jataayu, they like the chiefs of gods, 
namely Vishnu and Indra, went to southerly woods when their mind is set to search for Seetha. [3-68-38]_END

B_3_C_69_26
BEGIN_
अथ तम् समतिक्रम्य क्रोश मात्रम् ददर्शतुः || ३-६९-३३महान्तम् दारुणम् भीमम् कबंधम् भुज संवृतम् |
कबंधम् इव संस्थानत् अति घोर प्रदशनम् || ३-६९-३४_END
BEGIN_
On travelling just a krosha distance, then they have seen Kabandha, whose body is colossal, and who 
is heinous and hideous, and who is like living trunk fenced by its shoulders and arms, and who by his 
physique is very deadly in appearance. [3-69-33b, 34]_END

B_3_C_69_27
BEGIN_
स महा बाहुः अत्यर्थम् प्रसार्य विपुलौ भुजौ |जग्राह सहितौ एव राघवौ पीडयन् बलात् || ३-६९-३५_END
BEGIN_
He that overlong-armed Kabandha outstretching his overlong arms snatched both of the Raghava-s, keeping 
them side-by-side in his fists, and wringing them with his might. [3-69-35]_END

B_3_C_71_11
BEGIN_
अनाहारः कथम् शक्तो भग्न सक्थि शिरो मुखः || ३-७१-१२वज्रेण अभिहतः कालम् सु दीर्घम् अपि जीवितुम् |_END
BEGIN_
" 'By the impaction of Thunderbolt disarranged are my thighs and head, thereby my mouth went into my 
stomach... and without thighs how can I prowl, without arms how can I scrabble, and without a mouth 
how can I guzzle... and how am I capable to live on, and even that living too, is destined for too long 
a time...' [3-71-12b, 13a]_END

B_3_C_71_12
BEGIN_
स एवम् उक्तः मे शक्रो बाहू योजनम् आयतौ || ३-७१-१३तदा च आस्यम् च मे कुक्षौ तीक्ष्ण दंष्ट्रम् अकल्पयत् 
|_END
BEGIN_
"When I said to Indra this way, Indra devised for me yojana long arms, also that way a rapier-fanged 
mouth in my paunch... [3-71-13b, 14a]_END

B_3_C_69_28
BEGIN_
खड्गिनौ दृढ धन्वानौ तिग्म तेजौ महा भुजौ |भ्रातरौ विवशम् प्राप्तौ कृष्यमाणौ महा बलौ || ३-६९-३६_END
BEGIN_
Though they are the grapplers with swords and brandishers of unerring bows, and though outblazing is 
their pneuma and outstanding is their dexterity, both of those great mighty brothers lost control and 
had to yield themselves to that demon when he captured and dragged them. [3-69-36]_END

B_3_C_71_13
BEGIN_
सो अहम् भुजाभ्याम् दीर्घाभ्याम् संकृष्य अस्मिन् वने चरान् || ३-७१-१४सिंह द्विपि मृग व्याघ्रान् भक्षयामि 
समंततः |_END
BEGIN_
"Such as I am, I have been eating the lions, elephants, animals, and tigers that are on the move in 
this forest, hauling them in with both of my overlong arms... [3-71-14b, 15a]_END

B_3_C_69_29
BEGIN_
तत्र धैर्यात् च शूराः तु राघवो न एव विव्यधे |बाल्यात् अनाश्रयत्वात् च एव लक्ष्मणः तु अतिविव्यधे 
|| ३-६९-३७उवाच च विषण्णम् सन् राघवम् राघव अनुजः |_END
BEGIN_
In that situation, that valiant Rama, the legatee of Raghava-s, is not verily anguished owing to his 
courage, but Lakshmana is very much anguished, as if he is callow and in an unsheltered state, and he 
that younger brother of Raghava, namely Lakshmana, also dejectedly said this to Rama, the legatee of 
Raghava-s. [3-69-37, 38a]_END

B_3_C_71_14
BEGIN_
स तु माम् अब्रवीत् इन्द्रो यदा रामः स लक्ष्मणः || ३-७१-१५छेत्स्यते समरे बाहू तदा स्वर्गम् गमिष्यसि 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Indra has also said to me, 'as and when Rama hacks off your arms along with Lakshmana in a conflict, 
then you can go to heaven...' Thus Indra said to me and vanished. [3-71-15b, 16a]_END

B_3_C_69_30
BEGIN_
पश्य माम् विवशम् वीर राक्षसस्य वशम् गतम् || ३-६९-३८मया एकन तु निर्युक्तः परिमुच्यस्व राघव |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, valiant brother, see me, who am out of control on my inner-self, and gone into the control of the 
demon... oh, Raghava, you leave me and get yourself released from the grip of the demon... [3-69-38b, 
39a]_END

B_3_C_71_15
BEGIN_
अनेन वपुषा तात वने अस्मिन् राजसत्तम || ३-७१-१६यत् यत् पश्यामि सर्वस्य ग्रहणम् साधु रोचये |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, sire, I am grabbing whatever I see in this forest while living with this body... oh, powerful king, 
as I feel it meetly and a must for me... [3-71-16b, 17a]_END

B_3_C_69_31
BEGIN_
माम् हि भूत बलिम् दत्त्वा पलास्व यथा सुखम् || ३-६९-३९अधिगंता असि वैदेहीम् अचिरेण इति मे मतिः |_END
BEGIN_
"Indeed offer me as an offering to this quiddity, and you seek safety at your pleasure... and you will 
reach Vaidehi shortly... this is my belief... [3-69-39b, 40a]_END

B_3_C_71_16
BEGIN_
अवश्यम् ग्रहणम् रामो मन्ये अहम् समुपैष्यति || ३-७१-१७इमाम् बुद्धिम् पुरस्कृत्य देह न्यास कृत श्रमः 
|_END
BEGIN_
"I believed that Rama will certainly come nigh of my captivity, and confiding myself in this kind of 
determination, presaged by sage Sthuulashira, as well... I have been toiling to dislodge this body... 
[3-71-17b, 18a]_END

B_3_C_69_32
BEGIN_
प्रति लभ्य च काकुत्स्थ पितॄ पैतामहम् महीम् || ३-६९-४०तत्र माम् राम राज्यस्थः स्मर्तुम् अर्हसि सर्वदा 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Kakutstha, on regaining the kingdom of our father and forefathers, and when enthroned, oh, Rama, 
it will be apt of you to reminisce me always..." So said Lakshmana to Rama. [3-69-40b, 41a]_END

B_3_C_71_17
BEGIN_
स त्वम् रामो असि भद्रम् ते न अहम् अन्येन राघव || ३-७१-१८शक्यो हन्तुम् यथा तत्त्वम् एवम् उक्तम् महर्षिणा 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Raghava, as to how this has happened in this way according to the sum and substance told by the 
sage Sthulashira, you alone are that Rama, let safe betide you, and none other than you is capable to 
mangle me... [3-71-18b, 19a]_END

B_3_C_69_33
BEGIN_
लक्ष्मणेन एवम् उक्तः तु रामः सौमित्रिम् अब्रवीत् || ३-६९-४१मा स्म त्रासम् वृथा वीर न हि त्वा दृक् 
विषीदति |_END
BEGIN_
But when Lakshmana said that way, Rama said to Soumitri, "Fret not thyself, futilely... oh, brave one, 
your king of persons will not get dismayed, futilely... [3-69-41b, 42a]_END

B_3_C_71_18
BEGIN_
अहम् हि मति साचिव्यम् करिष्यामि नर ऋषभ || ३-७१-१९मित्रम् चैव उपदेक्ष्यामि युवाभ्याम् संस्कृतो अग्निना 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, impetuous man Rama, if I were to be beatified by you two by incinerating me in Fire, I will advice 
you about the next course of your action... I will further advise you about your prospective friend..." 
So said Kabandha to Rama. [3-71-19b, 20a]_END

B_3_C_69_34
BEGIN_
एतस्मिन् अन्तरे क्रूरो भ्रातरौ राम लक्ष्मणौ || ३-६९-४२तौ उवाच महाबाहुः कबन्धो दानव उत्तमः |_END
BEGIN_
In the meantime, that ruthless, log-armed, fiercest demon Kabandha thunderously asked those brothers, 
Rama and Lakshmana. [3-69-42b, 43a]_END

B_3_C_71_19
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु धर्मात्मा दनुना तेन राघवः || ३-७१-२०इदम् जगाद वचनम् लक्ष्मणस्य उपशृण्वतः |_END
BEGIN_
When Raghava is said thus by that Kabandha, the heir of Danu, that duty-minded Rama said this word to 
Kabandha while Lakshmana is hearing. [3-71-20b, 21a]_END

B_3_C_69_35
BEGIN_
कौ युवाम् वृषभ स्कन्धौ महा खड्ग धनुर् धरौ || ३-६९-४३घोरम् देशम् इमम् प्राप्तौ दैवेन मम चाक्षुषौ 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Who are you two? Your shoulders are akin to the bull-humps, and you are shouldering longbows and brandishing 
broad swords, how have you come about this province? For god's sake, I come across my most dainty morsel... 
[3-69-43b, 44a]_END

B_3_C_71_20
BEGIN_
रावणेन हृता सीता मम भार्या यशस्विनी || ३-७१-२१निष्क्रांतस्य जनस्थानात् सह भ्रात्रा यथा सुखम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Ravana conveniently stole my illustrious wife when myself and my brother exited from Janasthaana... 
[3-71-21b, 22a]_END

B_3_C_69_36
BEGIN_
वदतम् कार्यम् इह वाम् किम् अर्थम् च आगतौ युवाम् || ३-६९-४४इमम् देशम् अनुप्राप्तौ क्षुधा आर्तस्य 
इह तिष्ठतः |_END
BEGIN_
"What business you have here, and for which reason you have come here... you chanced for me who am sitting 
here and painfully ravenous... [3-69-44b, 45a]_END

B_3_C_71_21
BEGIN_
नाम मात्रम् तु जानामि न रूपम् तस्य रक्षसः || ३-७१-२२निवासम् वा प्रभावम् वा वयम् तस्य न विद्महे |_END
BEGIN_
"I only know his name but not the form of that demon... and we are unaware either of his stronghold 
or of his staying power... [3-71-22b, 23a]_END

B_3_C_71_22
BEGIN_
शोक आर्तानाम् अनाथानाम् एवम् विपरिधावताम् || ३-७१-२३कारुण्यम् सदृशम् कर्तुम् उपकारे च वर्तताम् |_END
BEGIN_
"It will be apt of you to show befitting mercy on us who are anguished by agony, running all over helter-skelter 
like unsheltered ones, and we who will be compliant for your restitution... [3-71-23b, 24a]_END

B_3_C_69_37
BEGIN_
स बाण चाप खड्गौ च तीक्ष्ण शृंगौ इव ऋषभौ || ३-६९-४५मम तूर्णम् उपसंप्राप्तौ दुर्लभम् जीवितम् वाम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Though you are with arrows, bows and swords, and though you are like bulls with sharp horns ready to 
gore... but they are all a waste, as your life has readily become ungainful on reaching nigh of my sight 
and arms..." So said Kabandha, in his arrogant tone. [3-69-45b, 46a]_END

B_3_C_69_38
BEGIN_
तस्य तत् वचनम् श्रुत्वा कबंधस्य दुरात्मनः || ३-६९-४६उवाच लक्ष्मणम् रामो मुखेन परिशुष्यता |_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that sentence of that vile-souled Kabandha, Rama said this to Lakshmana with a wilted face. 
[3-69-46b, 47a]_END

B_3_C_71_23
BEGIN_
काष्ठानि आनीय भग्नानि काले शुष्काणि कुंजरैः || ३-७१-२४धक्ष्यामः त्वाम् वयम् वीर श्वभ्रे महति कल्पिते 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, brave Kabandha, on bringing dried up firewood that was rent at times by elephants, and on digging 
a large trench, we will incinerate you in it... [3-71-24b, 25a]_END

B_3_C_71_24
BEGIN_
स त्वम् सीताम् समाचक्ष्व येन वा यत्र वा हृता || ३-७१-२५कुरु कल्याणम् अत्यर्थम् यदि जानासि तत्त्वतः 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Such as you are, if you actually know who stole Seetha, or whereto she is stolen, either... you clearly 
inform of her when incinerated, thus you will be rendering a most gracious deed to me, and to all concerned..." 
Thus Rama made clear of his case. [3-71-25b, 26a]_END

B_3_C_69_39
BEGIN_
कृच्छ्रात् कृच्छ्रतरम् प्राप्य दारुणम् सत्य विक्रम || ३-६९-४७व्यसनम् जीवित अन्ताय प्राप्तम् अप्राप्य 
ताम् प्रियाम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, truth-valiant Lakshmana, now coming to pass is a worst catastrophe, after a worse catastrophe, 
after a catastrophe...namely, the expiration at the hands of this demon presently, and the expropriation 
of Seetha previously, and the expulsion from kingship, still previously... nonetheless, without coming 
across that ladylove, this disastrous despair of ending our lives is coming about... [3-69-47b, 48a]_END

B_3_C_71_25
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः तु रामेण वाक्यम् दनुः अनुत्तमम् || ३-७१-२६प्रोवाच कुशलो वक्तुम् वक्तारम् अपि राघवम् |_END
BEGIN_
When he is said thus that expert articulator Kabandha replied Rama, who is also an expert enunciator, 
with expedient words. [3-71-26b, 27a]_END

B_3_C_69_40
BEGIN_
कालस्य सुमहत् वीर्यम् सर्व भूतेषु लक्ष्मण || ३-६९-४८त्वाम् च माम् च नरव्याघ्र व्यसनैः पश्य मोहितौ 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Lakshmana, the efficacy of Time is preponderant and proportional among all beings... oh, manly-tiger, 
why generalisation... see, as to how yourself and even myself are entangled in the tangles of life, 
even though we assert ourselves to be brave and best... [3-69-48b, 49a]_END

B_3_C_71_26
BEGIN_
दिव्यम् अस्ति न मे ज्ञानम् न अभिजानामि मैथिलीम् || ३-७१-२७यः ताम् ज्ञास्यति तम् वक्ष्ये दग्धः स्वम् 
रूपम् आस्थितः |_END
BEGIN_
"There is no divine knowledge to me as of now... nor I can identify Maithili... but when I am burnt 
I assume my own original divine form, and then I will be able tell about him, who will find her out... 
[3-71-27b, 28a]_END

B_3_C_69_41
BEGIN_
न हि भारो अस्ति दैवस्य सर्व भुतेषु लक्ष्मण || ३-६९-४९शूराः च बलवंतः च कृत अस्त्राः च रण आजिरे |
काल अभिपन्नाः सीदन्ति यथा वालुक सेतवः || ३-६९-५०_END
BEGIN_
Oh, Lakshmana, to show its impact on each and every being Time, or God is unencumbered and unremitting... 
may he be a brave one or a brawny one... or, may they be those that have perfected their missilery... 
when Time chances their nigh, they have to founder... as with a sandy levee... [3-69-49b, 50]_END

B_3_C_69_42
BEGIN_
इति ब्रुवाणो दृढ सत्य विक्रमोमहायशा दाशरथिः प्रतापवान् |अवेक्ष्य सौमित्रिम् उदग्र विक्रमम्
स्थिराम् तदा स्वाम् मतिम् आत्मना अकरोत् || ३-६९-५१_END
BEGIN_
Rama being the son of Dasharatha is an indomitable one, besides, a firmly and factually valorous one, 
by which he earned a great renown, and he on telling thus, and on looking over that recalcitrantly vengeful 
Soumitri, then Rama readied himself by his own steadied thinking. [3-69-51]_END

B_3_C_71_27
BEGIN_
यो अभिजानाति तद् रक्षः तद् वक्ष्ये राम तत् परम् || ३-७१-२८अदग्धस्य हि विज्ञातुम् शक्तिः अस्ति न 
मे प्रभो |राक्षसम् तम् महावीर्यम् सीता येन हृता तव || ३-७१-२९_END
BEGIN_
"With this unburnt body, oh, Rama, I indeed have no ability to discern anything, hence oh, lord, I will 
be able to speak about him who can familiarise you with that great mighty demon, by whom your Seetha 
is stolen, only after that incineration... [3-71-28b, 29]_END

B_3_C_71_28
BEGIN_
विज्ञानम् हि महत् भ्रष्टम् शाप दोषेण राघव |स्वकृतेन मया प्राप्तम् रूपम् लोक विगर्हितम् || ३-७१-३०_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Raghava, utterly distorted is my acumen, indeed, by the blemish of curse... and this form which 
is despicable to world has bechanced only because of my own antics... [3-71-30]_END

B_3_C_71_29
BEGIN_
किम् तु यावत् न याति अस्तम् सविता श्रान्त वाहनः |तावत् माम् अवटे क्षिप्त्वा दह राम यथा विधि || ३-७१-३१_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama, soon you have to toss me into trench to burn me customarily, sooner than the Sun's going 
to Mt. Dusk when his horses are fatigued... [3-71-31]_END

B_3_C_71_30
BEGIN_
दग्धः त्वया अहम् अवटे न्यायेन रघुनंदन |वक्ष्यामि तम् महावीर यः तम् वेत्स्यति राक्षसम् || ३-७१-३२_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama, the legatee of Raghu, when I am scripturally burnt by you in a trench, oh, great valiant 
Rama, for sure, I will tell of him, who can quiet fathom that demon... [3-71-32]_END

B_3_C_71_31
BEGIN_
तेन सख्यम् च कर्तव्यम् न्याय्य वृत्तेन राघव |कल्पयिष्यति ते प्रीतः साहाय्यम् लघु विक्रमः || ३-७१-३३_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Raghava, you have to befriend him with an amicable comportment... and that valiantly alacritous 
one will be gladdened by the sequel of your friendship, and he will evolve a succour to you... [3-71-33]_END

B_3_C_71_32
BEGIN_
न हि तस्य अस्ति अविज्ञातम् त्रिषु लोकेषु राघव |सर्वान् परिवृतो लोकान् पुरा वै कारण अन्तरे || ३-७१-३४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Raghava, nothing is there in all the three worlds that is unfamiliar to him, for he circumnavigated 
all worlds once, in a different context... [3-71-34]_END

B_3_C_72_0
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तौ तु तौ वीरौ कबन्धेन नर ईश्वरौ |गिरि प्रदरम् आसाद्य पावकम् विससर्जतुः || ३-७२-१_END
BEGIN_
When Kabandha said that way, both those brave men and lords of people, on throwing the body of Kabandha 
into a mountain cleft and then embedded it with firewood. [3-72-1]_END

B_3_C_72_1
BEGIN_
लक्ष्मणः तु महा उल्काभिः ज्वलिताभिः समन्ततः |चिताम् आदीपयामास सा प्रजज्वाल सर्वतः || ३-७२-२_END
BEGIN_
On his part Lakshmana started to torch that pyre with highly sparkling torches from all over, and even 
that pyre too suddenly blazed with blazes from all over. [3-72-2]_END

B_3_C_72_2
BEGIN_
तत् शरीरम् कबन्धस्य घृत पिण्ड उपमम् महत् |मेदसा पच्यमानस्य मन्दम् दहति पावकः || ३-७२-३_END
BEGIN_
That massy body of Kabandha is full with fat and while it is being cooked, it is in simile with a massy 
gob of ghee. But the Fire had to stew that body tardily, though that stewed meat is Fire's favourite 
dish, because of that body's massiveness. [3-72-3]_END

B_3_C_72_3
BEGIN_
स विधूय चिताम् आशु विधूमो अग्निर् इव उत्थितः |अरजे वाससी बिभ्रत् मालाम् दिव्याम् महाबलः || ३-७२-४_END
BEGIN_
In a trice that highly dynamic Kabandha zoomed up shoving off that pyre, and he is now attired in lily-white 
vestments and angelic garlands, and appeared like a fumeless fire. [3-72-4]_END

B_3_C_72_4
BEGIN_
ततः चिताया वेगेन भास्वरो विरज अंबरः |उत्पपात आशु संहृष्टः सर्व प्रत्यंग भूषणः || ३-७२-५_END
BEGIN_
Then highly gladdened Kabandha jumped up onto sky from the pyre, and there he is irradiant with unsullied 
clothing, and fineries decorated on every limb. [3-72-5]_END

B_3_C_72_5
BEGIN_
विमाने भास्वरे तिष्ठन् हंस युक्ते यशस् करे |प्रभया च महातेजा दिशो दश विराजयन् || ३-७२-६सो अन्तरिक्ष 
गतो वाक्यम् कबन्धो रामम् अब्रवीत् |_END
BEGIN_
On going to firmament Kabandha is now seated in a dazzling celestial aircraft yoked with swans, which 
endows renown because it takes the occupants to the realms of Brahma, and sitting in that celestial 
aircraft he said this sentence to Rama, while his own great glimmer and glitter beamed forth in all 
ten quarters. [3-72-6, 7]_END

B_3_C_72_6
BEGIN_
शृणु राघव तत्त्वेन यथा सीमाम् अवाप्स्यसि || ३-७२-७राम षड् युक्तयो लोके याभिः सर्वम् विमृश्यते |
परिमृष्टो दश अन्तेन दश आभागेन सेव्यते || ३-७२-८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Raghava, how you will regain Seetha, that you listen from me in its essence... oh, Rama, by which 
and which analyses everything will be analysed, six of such ideations are available in this world... 
and when a person is touched down by a spell of nemeses, he shall adore one who is equally in such spell 
of nemesis... [3-72-7b, 8]_END

B_3_C_72_7
BEGIN_
दश आभाग गतो हीनः त्वम् राम सह लक्ष्मणः |यत् कृते व्यसनम् प्राप्तम् त्वया दार प्रधर्षणम् || ३-७२-९_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama, you along with Lakshmana went into a spell of nemesis, and thus you have become an underprivileged 
one, and that spell alone has obtained you this dire straits, in the form of abducting your wife... 
[3-72-9]_END

B_3_C_72_8
BEGIN_
तत् अवश्यम् त्वया कार्यः स सुहृत् सुहृदाम् वर |अकृत्वा न हि ते सिद्धिम् अहम् पश्यामि चिन्तयन् || 
३-७२-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, best among kind-hearted ones, thereby you have to certainly befriend such a soul in similar dire 
straits... however deeply I may think, I am not able to perceive your accomplishment if you do not befriended 
with such a soul... [3-72-10]_END

B_3_C_72_9
BEGIN_
श्रूयताम् राम वक्ष्यामि सुग्रीवो नाम वानरः |भ्रात्रा निरस्तः क्रुद्धेन वालिना शक्र सूनुना || ३-७२-११_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama, listen what I tell... a vanara is there by name Sugreeva, who is vengefully reneged by his 
brother Vali, the son of Indra... [3-72-11]_END

B_3_C_72_10
BEGIN_
ऋष्यमूके गिरि वरे पंपा पर्यन्त शोभिते |निवसति आत्मवान् वीरः चतुर्भिः सह वानरैः || ३-७२-१२_END
BEGIN_
"That self-respectful valiant Sugreeva is living on the Mt. Rishyamuka, a best mountain available in 
the lambent fringes of Pampa Lake, along with four other vanara-s. [3-72-12]_END

B_3_C_72_11
BEGIN_
वानरेन्द्रो महावीर्यः तेजोवान् अमित प्रभः |सत्य संधो विनीतः च धृतिमान् मतिमान् महान् || ३-७२-१३_END
BEGIN_
"He that Sugreeva is a masterful one among vanara-s, highly mettlesome, self-resplendent, and illimitable 
is his self-radiance... and he is also truth-bound and culture-bound... a mastermind, master-hand and 
a taskmaster... [3-72-13]_END

B_3_C_72_12
BEGIN_
दक्षः प्रगल्भो द्युतिमान् महा बल पराक्रमः |भ्राता विवासितो वीर राज्य हेतो महात्मना || ३-७२-१४_END
BEGIN_
"He is a capable adventurer, a courageous exploiter and incomparable one in intrepidity and a brave 
one in incursions, and his personality will be coruscating ever and anon, for he is the son of Sun-god... 
but he is banished by his self-conceited brother owing to the reasons of kingdom... [3-72-14]_END

B_3_C_72_13
BEGIN_
स ते सहायो मित्रम् च सीतायाः परिमार्गणे |भविष्यति हि ते राम मा च शोके मनः कृधाः || ३-७२-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama, he will be your associate and an aid in searching for Seetha, and he conducts himself in 
your wellbeing, hence let not your heart yield to agony... [3-72-15]_END

B_3_C_72_14
BEGIN_
भवितव्यम् हि यत् च अपि न तत् शक्यम् इह अन्यथा |कर्तुम् इक्ष्वाकु शार्दूल कालो हि दुर्रक्रमः ||३-७२-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, tigerly Ikshvaaku, further nothing can be countermanded in this world which is indeed ineluctable, 
and it is impossible to countervail against Time, isn't it... [3-72-16]_END

B_3_C_72_15
BEGIN_
गच्छ शीघ्रम् इतो वीर सुग्रीवम् तम् महाबलम् |वयस्यम् तम् कुरु क्षिप्रम् इतो गत्वा अद्य राघव || ३-७२-१७
अद्रोहाय समागम्य दीप्यमाने विभावसौ |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, bold one, you go straight from here to that great mighty Sugreeva, and oh, Raghava, on going from 
here now and promptly you fraternise with Sugreeva... and to not to bode any ill of unfriendliness among 
you two, you make him a friend before blazing Fire, making that Fire as an Attestor of your friendship... 
[3-72-17, 18a]_END

B_3_C_72_16
BEGIN_
न च ते सो अवमन्तव्यः सुग्रीवो वानर अधिपः || ३-७२-१८कृतज्ञः काम रूपी च सहाय अर्थी च वीर्यवान् |_END
BEGIN_
"You shall not look down on that lord of monkeys taking him as a lowly simian, why because that Sugreeva 
is a valiant one, a guise changing wizard and presently he is in the need of a bolsterer, and if you 
render help he will be obligated to you for ever... [3-72-18b, 19]_END

B_3_C_72_17
BEGIN_
शक्तौ हि अद्य युवाम् कर्तुम् कार्यम् तस्य चिकीर्षितम् || ३-७२-१९कृतार्थो वा अकृतार्थो वा तव कृत्यम् 
करिष्यति |_END
BEGIN_
"Now you two are capable enough to effectuate the desired task of Sugreeva, isn't it... whether his 
own purpose is achieved through you or not, he will effectuate your task... [3-72-19b, 20a]_END

B_3_C_72_18
BEGIN_
स ऋक्षरजसः पुत्रः पंपाम् अटति शन्कितः || ३-७२-२०भास्करस्य औरसः पुत्रो वालिना कृत किल्बिषः |_END
BEGIN_
"Sugreeva is the son of Riksharaja, and the direct son of the Sun, but Vali trespassed against him. 
Wary of Vali's onslaughts Sugreeva is wandering around Pampa... [3-72-20b, 21a]_END

B_3_C_72_19
BEGIN_
संनिधाय आयुधम् क्षिप्रम् ऋष्यमूक आलयम् कपिम् || ३-७२-२१कुरु राघव सत्येन वयस्यम् वन चारिणम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Raghava, right away and candidly you make that monkey Sugreeva, a wanderer in the forest, sheltering 
himself on Mt. Rishyamuka, as a friend of yours taking an oath on your weapon besides the Fire-witness... 
[3-72-21b, 22a]_END

B_3_C_72_20
BEGIN_
स हि स्थानानि सर्वाणि कार्त्स्न्येन कपि कुंजरः || ३-७२-२२नर मांस अशिनाम् लोके नैपुण्यात् अधिगच्छति 
|_END
BEGIN_
"With his expertise that straightforward monkey Sugreeva is indeed conversant with all of the strongholds 
of anthropophagite demons in the world in their entirety... [3-72-22b, 23a]_END

B_3_C_72_21
BEGIN_
न तस्य अविदितम् लोके किंचित् अस्ति हि राघव || ३-७२-२३यावत् सूर्यः प्रतपति सहस्रांशुः अरिन्दम |_END
BEGIN_
