"Oh, enemy-subjugator Rama, as far as the thousand rayed sun manifestly irradiates the world, oh, Raghava, 
thus far, nothing in the least is unfamiliar to him, isn't it... [3-72-23b, 24a]_END

B_3_C_72_22
BEGIN_
स नदीः विपुलान् शैलान् गिरि दुर्गाणि कंदरान् || ३-७२-२४अन्विष्य वानरैः सार्धम् पत्नीम् ते अधिगमिष्यति 
|_END
BEGIN_
"He makes the monkeys to purposefully rake over the expansive rivers, extensive mountains and their 
impassable cliffs and caves in locating your wife... [3-72-24b, 25a]_END

B_3_C_72_23
BEGIN_
वानरान् च महाकायान् प्रेषयिष्यति राघव || ३-७२-२५दिशो विचेतुम् ताम् सीताम् त्वत् वियोगेन शोचयतीम् 
|अन्वेष्यति वरारोहाम् मैथिलीम् रावण आलये || ३-७२-२६_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Raghava, he expedites giant bodied monkeys in all directions to search for her, who is agonised 
by your parting, and he quests after the residence of Ravana for that comely lady Maithili... [3-72-25b, 
26]_END

B_3_C_72_24
BEGIN_
स मेरु शृंग अग्र गताम् अनिंदिताम्प्रविश्य पाताल तले अपि वा आश्रिताम् |प्लवंगमानाम् ऋषभः तव प्रियाम्
निहत्य रक्षांसि पुनः प्रदास्यति || ३-७२-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Whether that unreprovable ladylove of yours, Seetha, is located on the tops of Mt. Meru's peaks, or 
abiding on the planes of nadir of the earth, he that defiant one among fly-jumpers, Sugreeva, on entering 
there and annihilating the demons, he again bestows Seetha to you..." So Kabandha continued his advise 
to Rama regarding Sugreeva. [3-72-27]_END

B_3_C_73_0
BEGIN_
दर्शयित्वा रामाय सीतायाः प्रैमार्गने |वाक्यम् अन्वर्थम् अर्थज्ञः कबंधः पुनः अब्रवीत् || ३-७३-१_END
BEGIN_
On showing a concept for questing after Seetha that context-sensitive Kabandha further spoke this sentence 
which is inclusive of right concept to Rama. [3-73-1]_END

B_3_C_73_1
BEGIN_
एष राम शिवः पंथा यत्र एते पुष्पिता द्रुमाः |प्रतीचीम् दिशम् आश्रित्य प्रकाशन्ते मनो रमाः || ३-७३-२
जंबू प्रियाल पनसाः प्लक्ष न्यग्रोध तिंदुकाः |अश्वत्थाः कर्णिकाराः च चूताः च अन्ये च पादपाः || ३-७३-३
धन्वना नाग वृक्षा तिलका नक्तमालकाः |नील अशोक कदंबाः च करवीराः च पुष्पिताः || ३-७३-४अग्निमुखा 
अशोकाः च सुरक्ताः परिभद्रकाः |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama, have a recourse to westward, and where the trees of Rose-apple, Priyaala, Jackfruit, Plaksha, 
Banyan, Tinduka, Pipal, Karnikara, Mango, and others... and even trees like Dhanva, Naaga, Tilaka, Naktamaala, 
blue Ashoka, Kadamba, Karaviira, Agnimukha, Ashoka, red-sandalwood trees and Neem trees will be heart-pleasingly 
shining forth in full blossom, that alone is an optimistic course for you. [3-73-2, 3, 4, 5a]_END

B_3_C_73_2
BEGIN_
तान् आरुह्य अथवा भूमौ पातयित्वा च तान् बलात् || ३-७३-५फलानि अमृत कल्पानि भक्षयित्वा गमिष्यथः |_END
BEGIN_
"On shinning up those trees, or else, even on forcefully pelting those fruits down onto ground, then 
you may pelt over, devouring those ambrosial fruits... [3-73-5b, 6a]_END

B_3_C_73_3
BEGIN_
तत् अतिक्रम्य काकुत्स्थ वनम् पुषित पादपम् || ३-७३-६नंदन प्रतिमम् तु अन्यत् कुरवः उत्तरा इव |_END
BEGIN_
"On crossing over that parkland, oh, Kakutstha, another parkland with blossomy flowers is there, which 
replicates the heavenly Nandana gardens, and a replica of North-Kuru, an all-endowing province... [3-73-6b, 
7a]_END

B_3_C_73_4
BEGIN_
सर्व काल फला यत्र पादपा मधुर स्रवाः || ३-७३-७सर्वे च ऋतवः तत्र वने चैत्ररथे यथा |_END
BEGIN_
"Wherein the trees fruit all-season fruits that transude nectar, why fruits alone, in that parkland 
all seasons are coeval, as they will be in Caitraratha, the celestial gardens of Kubera... [3-73-7b, 
8a]_END

B_3_C_73_5
BEGIN_
फल भार नताः तत्र महा विटप धारिणः || ३-७३-८शोबन्ते सर्वतः तत्र मेघ पर्वत संनिभाः |_END
BEGIN_
"In there, the trees bear enormous branches which will be crouching under the weight of their own fruits, 
and everywhere such trees will be shining forth like shiny clouds and shining mountains... [3-73-8b, 
9a]_END

B_3_C_73_6
BEGIN_
तान् आरुह्य अथवा भूमौ पातैत्वा यथा सुखम् || ३-७३-९फलानि अमृत कल्पानि लक्षमणः ते प्रदास्यति |_END
BEGIN_
"Let Lakshmana present those ambrosial fruits to you either by climbing up those trees to pluck them, 
or else by pelting them to ground, according to his convenience... [3-73-9b-10a]_END

B_3_C_73_7
BEGIN_
चङ्क्रमंतौ वरान् शैलान् शैलात् शैलम् वनात् वनम् || ३-७३-१०ततः पुष्करिणीम् वीरौ पंपाम् नाम गमिष्यथः 
|_END
BEGIN_
"Peregrinating finest places by trekking from mountain to mountain, from forest to forest, oh, valorous 
ones, you will trek to an auspicious lotus-lake, called Pampa... [3-73-10b, 11a]_END

B_3_C_73_8
BEGIN_
अशर्कराम् अविभ्रंशाम् सम तीर्थम् अशैवलाम् || ३-७३-११राम संजात वालूकाम् कमल उत्पल शोभिताम् |_END
BEGIN_
"It is un-pebbly, un-slippery, un-weedy thereabouts, oh, Rama, equal are its quaysides and emersed are 
its sandbanks, red and blue lotuses beautify that Pampa Lake... [3-73-11b, 12a]_END

B_3_C_73_9
BEGIN_
तत्र हंसाः प्लवाः क्रौङ्चाः कुरराः चैव राघव || ३-७३-१२वल्गु स्वरा निकूजन्ति पंपा सलिल गोचराः |_END
BEGIN_

will be letting out peeps in tuneful voice... [3-73-12a, 13b]_END

B_3_C_73_10
BEGIN_
न उद्विजन्ते नरान् दृष्ट्वा वधस्य अकोविदाः शुभाः || ३-७३-१३घृत पिण्ड उपमान् स्थूलान् तान् द्विजान् 
भक्षयिष्यथः |_END
BEGIN_
"Thereabout birds will be unflustered on seeing humans, because they are artless to avoid hunting, because 
none kills them, and you may savour them because those birds will be best and burley, similar to ghee-gobs... 
[3-73-13b, 14a]_END

B_3_C_73_11
BEGIN_
रोहितान् वक्र तुण्डान् च नल मीनान् च राघव || ३-७३-१४पंपायाम् इषुभिः मत्स्यान् तत्र राम वरान् हतान् 
|निस्त्वक्पक्षानयसतप्तानकृशान्नैककण्टकान् - यद्वा -निः त्वक् पक्षान् अयस तप्तान् अकृशान् न अनेक 
कण्टकान् || ३-७३-१५तव भक्त्या समायुक्तो लक्ष्मणः संप्रदास्यति |भृशम् तान् खादतो मत्स्यान् पंपायाः 
पुष्प संचये || ३-७३-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama in that Pampa Lake there are best fishes, red-carps, and blunt-snouted small porpoises, and 
a sort of sprats, which are neither scraggy, nor with many fish-bones. Lakshmana will reverentially 
offer them to you on skewering them with arrow, and on broiling them on iron rod of arrow after descaling 
and de-finning them. [3-73-14b, 15, 16a]_END

B_3_C_73_12
BEGIN_
पद्म गन्धि शिवम् वारि सुख शीतम् अनामयम् |उद्धृत्य स तदा अक्लिष्टम् रूप्य स्फटिक सन्निभम् || ३-७३-१७
अथ पुष्कर पर्णेन लक्ष्मणः पाययिष्यति |_END
BEGIN_
"While you eat those fishes to satiety, Lakshmana will offer you the water of Pampa Lake, which will 
be in the bunches of flowers of that lake, and which will be lotus-scented, pellucid, comfortably cool, 
shiny like silver and crystal, uncontaminated and that way pristine, by lifting it up that water with 
lotus leaf, making that leaf a stoup-like basin... [3-73-16b, 17, 18a]_END

B_3_C_73_13
BEGIN_
स्थूलान् गिरि गुहा शय्यान् वानरान् वन चारिणः || ३-७३-१८साय आह्ने विचरन् राम दर्शयिष्यति लक्ष्मणः 
|अपाम् लोभात उपावृत्तान् वृषभान् इव नर्दतः || ३-७३-१९रूप अन्वितान् च पंपायाम् द्रक्ष्यसि त्वम् 
नरोत्तम |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, best one among men Rama, at Pampa you will see best shaped Vanara-s who have their bunk bed in 
mountain caves, and who will be coming nearby the lake, greedy as they are for water, and those forest 
movers will be moving about in evening time of the day, bellowing like bulls... oh, Rama, Lakshmana 
will show them to you... [3-73-18b, 19, 20a]_END

B_3_C_73_14
BEGIN_
साय अह्ने विचरन् राम विटपीन् माल्य धारिणः || ३-७३-२०शिव उदकम् च पंपायाम् दृष्ट्वा शोकम् विहास्यसि 
|_END
BEGIN_
"While roving in the evenings, oh, Rama, should you see the serenely water of Pampa, with her trees 
garlanded with their own blooms and twigs, you will discard your own dolour... [3-73-20b, 21a]_END

B_3_C_73_15
BEGIN_
सु मनोभिः चितान् तत्र तिलकान् नक्त मालकान् || ३-७३-२१उत्पलानि च फुल्लानि पंकजानि च राघव |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Raghava, there you will see highly delightful and wide-ranging trees like Tilaka and Naktamaala, 
and fully bloomed red and blue lotuses, as well... [3-73-21b, 22a]_END

B_3_C_73_16
BEGIN_
न तानि कश्चित् माल्यानि तत्र आरोपयिता नरः || ३-७३-२२न च वै म्लानताम् यान्ति न च शीर्यन्ति राघव |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Raghava, there is none someone to inwreathe the garlands of those flowers, and indeed, they neither 
dry up, nor drop down... [3-73-22b, 23a]_END

B_3_C_73_17
BEGIN_
मतंग शिष्याः तत्र आसन् ऋषयः सुसमाहितः || ३-७३-२३तेषाम् भार अभितप्तानाम् वन्यम् आहरताम् गुरोः |
ये प्रपेतुः महीम् तूर्णम् शरीरात् स्वेद बिन्दवः || ३-७३-२४तानि माल्यानि जातानि मुनीनाम् तपसा तदा 
|स्वेद बिन्दु समुत्थानि न विनश्यन्ति राघव || ३-७३-२५_END
BEGIN_
"Erst there were self-collected sages, the disciples of Sage Matanga, and at one time while they were 
bringing the forest produce as ritual paraphernalia, they were much wearied by its weight and they were 
sweating... and all of those earthbound strings of sweat-drops that quickly dropped from their bodies 
were wafted by air onto trees, and on them they reoccurred as strings of flowers, by the merit of the 
ascesis of those sages... oh, Raghava, since those flowers have emerged from sweat-drops, they are imperishable, 
indeed... [3-73-23b, 24, 25]_END

B_3_C_73_18
BEGIN_
तेषाम् गतानाम् अद्य अपि दृश्यते परिचारिणी |श्रमणी शबरी नाम काकुत्स्थ चिर जीविनी || ३-७३-२६_END
BEGIN_

a long-lived one and an anchoress, named Shabari, can be seen there, even today... [3-73-26]_END

B_3_C_73_19
BEGIN_
त्वाम् तु धर्मे स्थिता नित्यम् सर्व भूत नमस्कृतम् |दृष्ट्वा देव उपमम् राम स्वर्ग लोकम् गमिष्यति 
|| ३-७३-२७_END

"Oh, Rama, she who always stands by probity will depart to the sphere of heaven, on attending to you, 
for you are the referent to god, and a reverent for one and all... [3-73-27]_END

B_3_C_73_20

"Oh, Rama, thereafter on your taking course to that western bank of Pampa Lake, oh, Kakutstha, there

B_3_C_73_21
BEGIN_

B_3_C_73_22

मातंग वनम् इति एव विश्रुतम् रघुनंदन |तस्मिन् नंदन संकाशे देव अरण्य उपमे वने || ३-७३-३०नाना विहग 
संकीर्णे रंस्यसे राम निर्वृतः |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, the legatee of Raghu, that woodland which in simile is like a godly forest, similar to the heavenly 
Nandana gardens, overspread with divers birds is renowned as 'Matanga woodland', and oh, Rama, you will

B_3_C_73_23
BEGIN_
ऋष्यमूकः तु पंपायाः पुरस्तात् पुष्पित द्रुमः || ३-७३-३१सु दुःख आरोहणः च एव शिशु नाग अभिरक्षितः |
उदारो ब्रह्मणा चैव पूर्व काले विनिर्मितः || ३-७३-३२_END
BEGIN_
"In front of Pampa there is a bountiful but an unclimbable mountain is there with trees in full blossom, 
which is well-protected by baby elephants, and which in earlier times was purposefully created by Brahma, 
and that alone is Mt. Rishyamuka... [3-73-31b, 32]_END

B_3_C_73_24
BEGIN_
शयानः पुरुषो राम तस्य शैलस्य मूर्धनि |यत् स्वप्ने लभते वित्तम् तत् प्रबुद्धो अधिगच्छति || ३-७३-३३_END
BEGIN_
"And should a man sleep on the heights of that mountain, and should he dream of gaining some riches 
in that sleep, he gains that much when he wakes up... [3-73-33]_END

B_3_C_73_25
BEGIN_
यः तु एनम् विषम आचारः पाप कर्मा अधिरोहति |तत्र एव प्रहरन्ति एनम् सुप्तम् आदाय राक्षसाः || ३-७३-३४_END
BEGIN_
"But he who is diabolic in his deportment and devilish in comportment, climbs that and hopes to sleep

B_3_C_73_26
BEGIN_

"Oh, Rama, there the blaring trumpet-blasts of baby elephants that amuse themselves at Lake Pampa, and 
of those that are the indwellers of Matanga hermitage, even there on Mt. Rishyamuka are audible... [3-73-35]_END

B_3_C_74_0
BEGIN_
तौ कबन्धेन तम् मार्गम् पम्पाया दर्शितम् वने |आतस्थतुः दिशम् गृह्य प्रतीचीम् नृ वर आत्मजौ || ३-७४-१_END
BEGIN_
Both the sons of that best king Dasharatha, on taking up westerly path in that forest travelled on the 
passage to Pampa as shown by Kabandha. [3-74-1]_END

B_3_C_73_27
BEGIN_
सिक्ता रुधिर धाराभिः संहत्य परम द्विपाः |प्रचरन्ति पृथक् कीर्णा मेघ वर्णाः तरस्विनः || ३-७३-३६_END
BEGIN_
"The mighty and massy dark-cloud coloured elephants will be hitting head-on, and with dripping blood 
streams on their jumbo heads and temples, they disperse and move about separately, only to come together 
for yet another round of head-to-head collision... [3-73-36]_END

B_3_C_74_1
BEGIN_
तौ शैलेषु आचित अनेकान् क्षौद्र कल्प फल द्रुमान् |वीक्षन्तौ जग्मतुः द्रष्टुम् सुग्रीवम् राम लक्ष्मणौ 
|| ३-७४-२_END
BEGIN_
Those two, Rama and Lakshmana, while seeing several of the ticketed trees on mountains which have nectarous 
fruits on them moved forward to see Sugreeva. [3-74-2]_END

B_3_C_73_28
BEGIN_
ते तत्र पीत्वा पानीयम् विमलम् चारु शोभनम् |अत्यन्त सुख संस्पर्शम् सर्व गन्ध समन्वितम् || ३-७३-३७
निवृत्ताः सम्विगाहन्ते वनानि वन गोचराः |_END
BEGIN_
"There the elephants are quenched on drinking water of Pampa Lake, that is daintily clean, and neatly 
clear, springlike for touch, and in which all scents of flowers of that lake are included, and then 
they will be collectively re-entering the forests, for they are forest ranging elephants... [3-73-37, 
38a]_END

B_3_C_74_2
BEGIN_
कृत्वा च शैल पृष्ठे तु तौ वासम् रघु नन्दनौ |पंपायाः पश्चिमम् तीरम् राघवौ उपतस्थतुः || ३-७४-३_END
BEGIN_
Those two legatees of Raghu on making a sojourn on the mountaintop, they the Raghava-s drew nigh of 
the moorland on the westward of Pampa Lake. [3-74-3]_END

B_3_C_73_29
BEGIN_
ऋक्षाम् च द्विपिनः चैव नील कोमलक प्रभान् || ३-७३-३८रुरून् अपेता अपजयान् दृष्ट्वा शोकम् प्रहास्यसि 
|_END
BEGIN_
"On your seeing the bears, also thus the tigers and even the exultant sapphire-blue Rurus with black 
stripes there, you will discard your distress... [3-73-38b, 39a]_END

B_3_C_74_3
BEGIN_
तौ पुष्करिण्याः पंपायाः तीरम् आसाद्य पश्चिमम् |अपश्यताम् ततः तत्र शबर्या रम्यम् आश्रमम् || ३-७४-४_END
BEGIN_
Then on getting at the westward moorland of that lotus-lake Pampa, there those two have spotted the 
idyllic hermitage of Shabari. [3-74-4]_END

B_3_C_74_4
BEGIN_
तौ तम् आश्रमम् आसाद्य द्रुमैः बहुभिः आवृतम् |सु रम्यम् अभिवीक्षन्तौ शबरीम् अभ्युपेयतुः || ३-७४-५_END
BEGIN_
On getting at that hermitage and on perusing at that picturesque environ that is wreathed round with 
several picturesque trees, those two came nigh of Shabari. [3-74-5]_END

B_3_C_73_30
BEGIN_
राम तस्य तु शैलस्य महती शोभते गुहा || ३-७३-३९शिला पिधाना काकुत्स्थ दुःखम् च अस्याः प्रवेशनम् |_END
BEGIN_
"But oh, Rama, a cavernous cave lidded with a boulder stone outshines on that mountain, and oh, Kakutstha, 
problematic is an entry into it... [3-73-39b, 40a]_END

B_3_C_74_5
BEGIN_
तौ दृष्ट्वा तु तदा सिद्धा समुत्थाय कृतांजलिः |पादौ जग्राह रामस्य लक्ष्मणस्य च धीमतः || ३-७४-६_END
BEGIN_
On seeing them that sublimated yogi Shabari instinctively made palm-fold, got up imperatively, and then 
she braced the feet of Rama, and even that of sagacious Lakshmana, impressively. [3-74-6]_END

B_3_C_73_31
BEGIN_
तस्या गुहायाः प्राक् द्वारे महान् शीत उदको ह्रदः || ३-७३-४०बहु मूल फलो रम्यो नाना नग समाकुलः |_END
BEGIN_
"On its right at its eastern opening a delightful lake with highly coolant waters is there, fringed 
with divers trees and fraught with numerous tubers and fruits... [3-73-40b, 41a]_END

B_3_C_74_6
BEGIN_
पाद्यम् आचमनीयम् च सर्वम् प्रददात् यथा विधि |ताम् उवाच ततो रामः श्रमणीम् धर्म संस्थिताम् || ३-७४-७_END
BEGIN_
She gave them water for feet-wash and mouthwash, and other viands customarily affordable to visitants, 
and then Rama asked after that anchoress who is unflinchingly abiding in her duty. [3-74-7]_END

B_3_C_73_32
BEGIN_
तस्याम् वसति सुग्रीवः चतुर्भिः सह वानरैः || ३-७३-४१कदाचित् शिखरे तस्य पर्वतस्य अपि तिष्ठते |_END
BEGIN_
"Sugreeva dwells in that cave along with four other monkeys, and at times he will be available on the 
peaks of that mountain, even on its bluffs and cliffs, for he is a terrified monkey..." Thus Kabandha 
informed them. [3-73-41b, 42a]_END

B_3_C_74_7
BEGIN_
कच्चित् ते निर्जिता विघ्नाः कच्चित् ते वर्धते तपः |कच्चित् ते नियतः कोप आहारः च तपोधने || ३-७४-८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, ascetically wealthy lady, perchance your deterrents in ascesis are completely overcome, somehow... 
your ascetic practises culminating, someway... your annoyances and ailments are adjusted, somewhat... 
isn't it! [3-74-8]_END

B_3_C_73_33
BEGIN_
कबंधः तु अनुशास्य एवम् तौ उभौ राम लक्ष्मणौ || ३-७३-४२स्रग्वी भास्कर वर्ण आभः खे व्यरोचत वीर्यवान् 
|_END
BEGIN_
That impressive Kabandha adorned with divine garlands and abiding in sky scintillating with the grandeur 
of the dazzle of the sun has bidden both the brothers, Rama and Lakshmana thus, awaited a bid adieu 
from them. [3-73-42b, 43a]_END

B_3_C_74_8
BEGIN_
कच्चित् ते नियमाः प्राप्ताः कच्चित् ते मनसः सुखम् |कच्चित् ते गुरु शुश्रूषा सफला चारु भाषिणि || 
३-७४-९_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, suave speaker, mayhap your sacred commitments are achieved, anywise... appeased is your self, anyway... 
and your subservience to your mentors brought to fruition, perchance... isn't it!" Thus Rama enquired 
with Shabari. [3-74-9]_END

B_3_C_73_34
BEGIN_
तम् तु ख स्थम् महाभागम् कबंधम् राम लक्ष्मणौ || ३-७३-४३प्रस्थितौ त्वम् व्रजस्व इति वाक्यम् ऊचतुः 
अन्तिके |_END
BEGIN_
Rama and Lakshmana who started off on their peregrination said this sentence to that highly providential 
Kabandha, who is temporising in the sky in their vicinity, thus as "you may proceed..." [3-73-43b, 44a]_END

B_3_C_73_35
BEGIN_
गम्यताम् कार्य सिद्धि अर्थम् इति तौ अब्रवीत् च सः || ३-७३-४४सुप्रीतौ तौ अनुज्ञाप्य कबंधः प्रस्थितः 
तदा || ३-७३-४५_END
BEGIN_
On getting the orders for departure from those two brothers who are highly gladdened at the information 
given by Kabandha, he that Kabandha who is ready to exit, he further said to them thus, "proceed for 
the purpose of achieving your task..." [3-73-44b, 45]_END

B_3_C_74_9
BEGIN_
रामेण तापसी पृष्ठा सा सिद्धा सिद्ध सम्मता |शशंस शबरी वृद्धा रामाय प्रति अवस्थिता || ३-७४-१०_END
BEGIN_
When Rama asked her in this way she that Shabari who is a senescent anchoress, sublimated yogin and 
an adherent to the sublimated yogis of higher rank, informed Rama remaining in his vis-�-vis. [3-74-10]_END

B_3_C_73_36
BEGIN_
स तत् कबंधः प्रतिपद्य रूपम्वृतः श्रिया भास्कर सर्व देहः |निदर्शयन् रामम् अवेक्ष्य ख स्थः
सख्यम् कुरुष्व इति तदा अभ्युवाच || ३-७३-४६_END
BEGIN_
Kabandha who redeemed his divine form has now got an aureole around him, and while irradiance is tamping 
whole of his mien, he moved further up on sky and reappeared. And staying in the sky he pointed out 
at the side of Mt. Rishyamuka, and then he reiterated, "you befriend Sugreeva..."and then he vanished. 
[3-73-46]_END

B_3_C_74_10
BEGIN_
अद्य प्राप्ता तपः सिद्धिः तव संदर्शनात् मया |अद्य मे सफलम् जन्म गुरवः च सुपूजिताः || ३-७४-११_END
BEGIN_
"Just now, on your pleasing manifestation before me my ascesis is accomplished, and now only my birth 
is fructified, and now only my subservience to my mentors is well hallowed... [3-74-11]_END

B_3_C_74_11
BEGIN_
अद्य मे सफलम् तप्तम् स्वर्गः चैव भविष्यति |त्वयि देव वरे राम पूजिते पुरुषर्षभ || ३-७४-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, best one among men, now all my ascesis is fructified when I personally worshiped you, who are none 
other than the best god among gods, thus the heaven will also be there for me... [3-74-12]_END

B_3_C_74_12
BEGIN_
तव अहम् चक्षुषा सौम्य पूता सौम्येन मानद |गमिष्याम्यक्षयांलोकांस्वत्प्रसादादरिन्दम - यद्वा -गमिष्यामि 
अक्षयान् लोकान् त्वत् प्रसादात् अरिंदम || ३-७४-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, kind one, your blessed sight has sanctified me... and oh, endower of respect, by your beneficence 
I wish to go to those returnless worlds because I have subjugated those enemies of yours, viz.,
ari SaD varga-s in me, and I think my prayer to you is justified because 
you are a subjugator of such enemies... [3-74-13]_END

B_3_C_74_13
BEGIN_
चित्रकूटम् त्वयि प्राप्ते विमानैः अतुल प्रभैः |इतः ते दिवम् आरूढा यान् अहम् पर्यचारिषम् || ३-७४-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Divine aircrafts of unequalled refulgence have lifted those disciples of Sage Matanga in whose tendance 
I was, to welkin on your arriving at Chitrakuta... [3-74-14]_END

B_3_C_74_14
BEGIN_
तैः च अहम् उक्ता धर्म ज्ञैः महाभागैः महर्षिभिः |आगमिष्यति ते रामः सु पुण्यम् इमम् आश्रमम् || ३-७४-१५
स ते प्रतिग्रहीतव्यः सौमित्रि सहितो अतिथिः |तम् च दृष्ट्वा वरान् लोकान् अक्षयान् त्वम् गमिष्यसि 
|| ३-७४-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Those knowers of probity, highly providential, and eminent-saints have told me, 'Rama will come to 
this highly blest hermitage of yours along with Soumitri... and you have to cordially welcome them as 
your guests, and on your seeing him you will go to best worlds, where merit remains undiminished...' 
[3-74-15, 16]_END

B_3_C_74_15
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्ता महाभागैः तदा अहम् पुरुषर्षभ |मया तु विविधम् वन्यम् संचितम् पुरुषर्षभ || ३-७४-१७तव 
अर्थे पुरुषव्याघ्र पम्पायाः तीर संभवम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, best one among men Rama, thus I was told by those highly providential sages, oh, best one among 
men, oh, manly tiger, and I have gleaned various forest fruits and eatables that occur on the moorlands 
of Pampa Lake for your sake..." So said Shabari to Rama. [3-74-17]_END

B_3_C_74_16
BEGIN_
एवम् उक्तः स धर्मात्मा शबर्या शबरीम् इदम् || ३-७४-१८राघवः प्राह विज्ञाने ताम् नित्यम् अबहिष्कृताम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
When that graceful souled Rama is addressed thus by Shabari, he that Raghava enquiringly said this to 
that Shabari who is never ever debarred from esoteric knowledge and gnosis. [3-74-18b, 19a]_END

B_3_C_74_17
BEGIN_
दनोः सकाशात् तत्त्वेन प्रभावम् ते महात्मनः || ३-७४-१९श्रुतम् प्रत्यक्षम् इच्छामि संद्रष्टुम् यदि 
मन्यसे |_END
BEGIN_
"Your and your preceptors' effectiveness is heard in effect from the wraith of the great souled Danu's 
son, Kabandha, and if you feel showing it like I wish to clearly see it, personally..." Thus Rama asked 
her to show hermitage. [3-74-19b, 20a]_END

B_3_C_74_18
BEGIN_
एतत् तु वचनम् श्रुत्वा राम वक्त्रात् विनिःसृतम् || ३-७४-२०शबरी दर्शयामास तौ उभौ तत् वनम् महत् |_END
BEGIN_
On hearing those words voiced by Rama, Shabari started to show that unique woodland to both of them. 
[3-74-20]_END

B_3_C_74_19
BEGIN_
पश्य मेघ घन प्रख्यम् मृग पक्षि समाकुलम् || ३-७४-२१मतंग वनम् इति एव विश्रुतम् रघुनंदन |इह ते 
भावित आत्मानो गुरवो मे महाद्युते |जुहवान् चक्रिरे नीडम् मंत्रवत् मंत्र पूजितम् || ३-७४-२२_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama the delight of Raghu's lineage... this one comparable to a crammed cloud that would be ever 
ready to yield much cherished cloudbursts, and compacted with animals and birds that are ever ready 
to enjoy seasonable rains, is that hermitage to which you have come, that way this woodland is well 
known as Matanga, meaning a cloud, or an elephant, or an elephantine cloud that showers blessings on 
all... and oh, highly resplendent Rama, you may see this nest, snuggery, where those contemplative souls, 
my teachers, used to conduct oblations into the Ritual-fires, orienting and worshipping them with Vedic 
hymns... [3-74-21b, 22]_END

B_3_C_74_20
BEGIN_
इयम् प्रत्यक् स्थली वेदी यत्र ते मे सुसत्कृताः |पुष्प उपहारम् कुर्वन्ति श्रमात् उद् वेपिभिः करैः 
|| ३-७४-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Where those great sages that are highly revered by me used to offer flowers with their extremely doddery 
hands in the worship the Altar of Fire, this alone is that Altar of Fire raised at western end... [3-74-23]_END

B_3_C_74_21
BEGIN_
तेषाम् तपः प्रभावेन पश्य अद्य अपि रघूत्तम |द्योतयन्ति दिशः सर्वाः श्रिया वेद्यः अतुल प्रभाः || ३-७४-२४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, best one from Raghu-s, by the efficacy of the ascesis of my teachers these Altars of Fire are with 
incomparable irradiance, and even now they are irradiating all of the directions with solemnity... see 
them... [3-74-24]_END

B_3_C_74_22
BEGIN_
अशक्नुवद्भिस्तैर्गन्तुमुपवासश्रमालसैः - यद्वा -अशक्नुवद्भिः तैः गन्तुम् उपवास श्रम आलसैः |चिन्तिते 
अभ्यागतान् पश्य समेतान् सप्त सागरान् || ३-७४-२५_END
BEGIN_
"Enervated by dieting and straining they were incapable to go for sea bathing, and just at their thought 
process all the seven seas came close by, in coalescence... see them... [3-74-25]_END

B_3_C_74_23
BEGIN_
कृत अभिषेकैः तैः न्यस्ता वल्कलाः पादपेषु इह |अद्य अपि न विशुष्यन्ति प्रदेशे रघुनंदन || ३-७४-२६_END
BEGIN_
"On performing holy baths those sages have spread their jute cloths on those trees with their own doddering 
hands here at this place and oh, Raghu's legatee, those cloths did not dry even now by the touch of 
their hands... [3-74-26]_END

B_3_C_74_24
BEGIN_
देव कार्याणि कुर्वद्भिः यानि इमानि कृतानि वै |पुष्पैः कुवलयैः सार्थम् म्लानत्वम् न तु यान्ति वै 
|| ३-७४-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Which garlands they have knotted together with black-lotuses and other flowers while they were worshiping 
gods, these are really those garlands, and indeed there is no discolouration to them... [3-74-27]_END

B_3_C_74_25
BEGIN_
कृत्स्नम् वनम् इदम् दृष्टम् श्रोतव्यम् च श्रुतम् त्वया |तत् इच्छामि अभ्यनुज्ञाता त्यक्ष्यामि एतत् 
कलेवरम् || ३-७४-२८_END
BEGIN_
"You have seen what is seeable and you have listened what is listenable of this woodland in its entirety... 
thereby I wish to become a permittee, where you alone are my permitter, as I wish to castaway this sheathe 
of soul, called my body... to make that soul to move nigh of my teachers feet... [3-74-28]_END

B_3_C_74_26
BEGIN_
तेषाम् इच्छामि अहम् गन्तुम् समीपम् भावित आत्मनाम् |मुनीनाम् आश्रमो येषाम् अहम् च परिचारिणी || ३-७४-२९_END
BEGIN_
"Of which sages this hermitage is, and of which sages I am also a maidservant, I soulfully go the proximity 
of those contemplative souls..." Thus, she appealed to Rama. [3-74-29]_END

B_3_C_74_27
BEGIN_
धर्मिष्ठम् तु वचः श्रुत्वा राघवः सह लक्ष्मणः |प्रहर्सम् अतुलम् लेभे आश्चर्यम् इदम् च अब्रवीत् || 
३-७४-३०_END
BEGIN_
Rama on hearing those duty-congruous words of Shabari along with Lakshmana, obtained a uniquely high 
rejoice and he also said, "astonishing is this..." [3-74-30]_END

B_3_C_74_28
BEGIN_
ताम् उवाच ततो रामः शबरी संश्रित व्रताम् |अर्चितो अहम् त्वया भद्रे गच्छ कामम् यथा सुखम् || ३-७४-३१_END
BEGIN_
Then Rama spoke to that Shabari who is firmed up in her faith towards her masters, "oh, saintly lady, 
you treated me with deference... thus may go to your cherished worlds, where you can solace yourself 
with your masters... [3-74-31]_END

B_3_C_74_29
BEGIN_
इति एवम् उक्ता जटिला चीर कृष्ण अजिन अंबरा |अनुज्ञाता तु रामेण हुत्वा आत्मानम् हुत अशने || ३-७४-३२
ज्वलत् पावक संकाशा स्वर्गम् एव जगाम सा |_END
BEGIN_
Thus that way said by Rama in consent, she who is wearing tufty-matted hair, jute-cloths, and deerskin 
as her clothing, she offered herself as an oblation into Ritual-fire, and then like a flaring fire, 
she went to heaven alone. [3-74-32, 33a]_END

B_3_C_74_30
BEGIN_
दिव्यम् आभरण संयुक्ता दिव्य माल्य अनुलेपना || ३-७४-३३दिव्य अंबर धरा तत्र बभूव प्रिय दर्शन |विराजयन्ती 
तम् देशम् विद्युत् सौदामिनी यथा || ३-७४-३४_END
BEGIN_
Now she appeared as an angle bejewelled with angelic ornaments, wearing angle's wraparound and angelical 
flowery tassels, and bedaubed with suchlike cosmetics, and as with the scintillations of electric sparks 
she scintillated that province. [3-74-33b, 34]_END

B_3_C_74_31
BEGIN_
यत्र ते सुकृत आत्मानो विहरन्ति महर्षयः |तत् पुण्यम् शबरी स्थानम् जगाम आत्म समाधिना || ३-७४-३५_END
BEGIN_
Shabari who is a perfect yogin with perfected meditative concentration, now went to that sanctum locus 
where the blest souls of those sublime sages, namely her masters, saunter. [3-74-35]_END

B_3_C_75_0
BEGIN_
दिवम् तु तस्याम् यातायाम् शबर्याम् स्वेन तेजसा |लक्ष्मणेन सह भ्रात्रा चिन्तयामास राघवः || ३-७५-१_END
BEGIN_
While Shabari ascended to heaven with her own divine self-resplendence, Raghava who is with Lakshmana 
started to cogitate over the magnificence of Matanga disciples. [3-75-1]_END

B_3_C_75_1
BEGIN_
चिंतयित्वा तु धर्मात्मा प्रभावम् तम् महात्मनाम् |हित कारिणम् एक अग्रम् लक्ष्मणम् राघवो अब्रवीत् 
|| ३-७५-२_END
BEGIN_
That noble-souled Raghava on thinking about the efficacy of the disciples of Matanga, said to Lakshmana, 
who is the maintainer of Rama's well being, and who is thinking single-mindedly. [3-75-2]_END

B_3_C_75_2
BEGIN_
दृष्टो मया आश्रमः सौम्य बहु आश्चर्यः कृत आत्मनाम् |विश्वस्त मृग शार्दूलो नाना विहग सेवितः || ३-७५-३_END
BEGIN_
"I have seen a highly astounding hermitage of self-controlled sages, oh, gentle Lakshmana, in which 
the deer and tigers are at home, and which is adored by divers birds... [3-75-3]_END

B_3_C_75_3
BEGIN_
सप्तानाम् च समुद्राणाम् तेषाम् तीर्थेषु लक्ष्मण |उपस्पृष्टम् च विधिवत् पितरः च अपि तर्पिताः || ३-७५-४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Lakshmana, holy is our taking a bath in this holy Pampa Lake, for it is formed by the waters of 
seven seas, and even holier is our oblation of this holy waters to manes... [3-75-4]_END

B_3_C_75_4
BEGIN_
प्रणष्टम् अशुभम् यत् नः कल्याणम् समुपस्थितम् |तेन तु एतत् प्रहृष्टम् मे मनो लक्ष्मण संप्रति || ३-७५-५
हृदये हि नर व्याघ्र शुभम् आविर्भविष्यति |_END
BEGIN_
"What that was unpropitious for us is completely abated by our holy bath and holy oblations, oh, Lakshmana, 
propitiousness is standing en face us, thereby presently this heart of mine is highly gladdening... 
oh, lion-like man, indeed, heart alone hatches hope... [3-75-5, 6a]_END

B_3_C_75_5
BEGIN_
तत् आगच्छ गमिष्यावः पंपाम् ताम् प्रिय दर्शनाम् || ३-७५-६ऋष्यमूको गिरिः यत्र न अति दूरे प्रकाशते 
|यस्मिन् वसति धर्मात्मा सुग्रीवो अंशुमतः सुतः || ३-७५-७नित्यम् वालि भयात् त्रस्तः चतुर्भिः सह 
वानरैः |_END
BEGIN_
"Thereby, where Mt. Rishyamuka is beaming forth at its nearby, on which that right minded son of the 
Sun, Sugreeva, is living along with four other vanara-s, always frightened by the fear from Vali, we 
will go to her, to that spectacular Lake Pampa, come on, Lakshmana... [3-75-6b, 7, 8a]_END

B_3_C_75_6
BEGIN_
अहम् त्वरे च तम् द्रष्टुम् सुग्रीवम् वानरर्षभम् || ३-७५-८तत् अधीनम् हि मे कार्यम् सीतायाः परिमार्गणम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
"I am also hasty to see that best one among vanara-s, Sugreeva, for my enterprise called search for 
Seetha is under his aegis, isn't it... [3-75-8b, 9a]_END

B_3_C_75_7
BEGIN_
इति ब्रुवाणम् तम् वीरम् सौमित्रिः इदम् अब्रवीत् || ३-७५-९गच्छावः त्वरितम् तत्र मम अपि त्वरते मनः 
|_END
BEGIN_
To that brave Rama who is speaking thus, Soumitri said this, " my heart too is hastening me, let us 
go there promptly..." [3-75-9b, 10a]_END

B_3_C_75_8
BEGIN_
आश्रमात् तु ततः तस्मात् निष्क्रम्य स विशाम् पतिः || ३-७५-१०आजगाम ततः पंपाम् लक्ष्मणेन सहप्रभुः |_END
BEGIN_
Then that Lord of People and Lord of Nature on exiting from that hermitage, he then came nigh of Lake 
Pampa along with Lakshmana. [3-75-10b, 11a]_END

B_3_C_75_9
BEGIN_
समीक्षमाणः पुष्प आढ्यम् सर्वतो विपुल द्रुमम् || ३-७५-११कोयष्टिभिः च अर्जुनकैः शत पत्रैः च कीरकैः 
|एतैः च अन्यैः च बहुभिः नादितम् तत् वनम् महत् || ३-७५-१२स रामो विविधान् वृक्षान् सरांसि विविधानि 
च |पश्यन् काम अभिसंतप्तो जगाम परमम् ह्रदम् || ३-७५-१३_END
BEGIN_
Rama on scrutinising that rosy woodland in which everywhere there are outsized and diverse trees that 
are thickset with flowers, and different lakes loaded with the trilling birds like plovers, peacocks, 
waterfowls and suchlike, with which that woodland itself is trilling in much ado, became impassioned 
as he is instantly rendered thus by Love-god, and thus that Rama went towards that lovely Lake Pampa. 
[3-75-11b, 12, 13]_END

B_3_C_75_10
BEGIN_
स ताम् आसाद्य वै रामो दूरात् पानीय वाहिनीम् |मतंग सरसम् नाम ह्रदम् समवगाहत || ३-७५-१४_END
BEGIN_
Rama spotted Pampa Lake from a distance which is plethoric with water, but entered into a lake called 
Matanga Lake on his way to Pampa... [3-75-14]_END

B_3_C_75_11
BEGIN_
तत्र जग्मतुः अव्यग्रौ राघवौ हि समाहितौ |स तु शोक समाविष्टो रामो दशरथात्मजः || ३-७५-१५_END
BEGIN_
Though both Raghava-s came there composedly and dispassionately, but Rama, the son of Dasharatha, is 
ensorcelled by anguish on seeing a ladylike lake Pampa. [3-75-15]_END

B_3_C_75_12
BEGIN_
विवेश नलिनीम् रम्याम् पंकजैः च समावृताम् |तिलकाशोकपुंनागबकुलोद्दालकाशिनीम् - यद्वा -तिलक अशोक 
पुन्नाग बकुल उद्दाल काशिनीम् || ३-७५-१६_END
BEGIN_
Rama entered the area of that beautiful lake which is beaming forth with lotuses hemming in from inside, 
and trees like Tilaka, Ashoka, Punnaga, Bakula, Uddala, are hemming it from outside. [3-75-16]_END

B_3_C_75_13
BEGIN_
रम्य उपवन संबाधाम् पद्म संपीडित उदकाम् |स्फटिक उपम तोय आढ्याम् श्लक्ष्ण वालुक संतताम् || ३-७५-१७_END
BEGIN_
That lake is huddled with delightful fringe lands and lotuses squeeze it from within, and its water 
is plethoric and crystalline, and its sand is softish all over. [3-75-17]_END

B_3_C_75_14
BEGIN_
मत्स्य कच्छप संबाधाम् तीरस्थ द्रुम शोभिताम् |सखीभिः इव संयुक्ताम् लताभिः अनुवेष्टिताम् || ३-७५-१८_END
BEGIN_
That lake is beautified with packs of fishes and tortoises, and packs of trees on its banks, on which 
climber plants are wraparound like the ladyloves of those trees. [3-75-18]_END

B_3_C_75_15
BEGIN_
किंनरोरगगन्धर्वयक्षराक्षससेविताम् -यद्वा - |किन्नर उरग गन्धर्व यक्ष राक्षस सेविताम् |नाना द्रुम 
लता आकीर्णाम् शीत वारि निधिम् शुभाम् || ३-७५-१९_END
BEGIN_
And that is adored by the beings like sylvan, reptilian, celestial, georgic, and elfish beings, and 
it is overcrowded with trees and tendrils, and it is a trove for fairish and clodish water. [3-75-19]_END

B_3_C_75_16
BEGIN_
पद्म सौगन्धिकैः ताम्राम् शुक्लाम् कुमुद मण्डलैः |नीलाम् कुवलय उद् घाटैः बहु वर्णाम् कुथाम् इव || 
३-७५-२०अरविन्द उत्पलवतीम् पद्म सौगन्धिक आयुताम् |पुष्पित आम्र वणोपेताम् बर्हिण उद् घुष्ट नादिताम् 
|| ३-७५-२१_END
BEGIN_
The lotuses of the lake are rich in their fragrance, and with the heaps of clusters of reddish, whitish, 
and blackish lotuses, and with such pinkish, whitish, and reddish lotuses the sheet of water is like 
a picturesquely painted canvas and it is surrounded by the orchards of flowered mango trees and sounded 
much by the screams of peacocks. [3-75-20, 21]_END

B_3_C_75_17
BEGIN_
स ताम् दृष्ट्वा ततः पंपाम् रामः सौमित्रिणा सह |विललाप च तेजस्वी कामात् दशरथात्मजः || ३-७५-२२_END
BEGIN_
Then Rama along with Lakshmana on seeing at that Pampa Lake, that self-refulgent son of Dasharatha whimpered 
over, owing to his passionate recollection of Seetha. [3-75-22]_END

B_3_C_75_18
BEGIN_
तिलकैः बीज पूरैः च वटैः शुक्ल द्रुमैः तथा |पुष्पितैः करवीरैः च पुन्नागैः च सु पुष्पितैः || ३-७५-२३
मालती कुंद गुल्मैः च भण्डीरैः निचुलैः तथा |अशोकैः सप्त पर्णैः च केतकैः अतिमुक्तकैः || ३-७५-२४
अन्यैः च विविधैः वृक्षैः प्रमदा इव उपशोभिताम् |_END
BEGIN_
That Pampa Lake is wraparound with the trees of Tilaka, Citron-fruits, Banyan, White-trees, likewise 
flowered are flowery trees like Red oleanders, Punnaaga, shrubs of Maalati and Kunda, likewise flowered 
are the trees of Madder, Nicula, Ashoka, and Seven-leaved banana plants, and plants of Mogra and climbers 
of Maadhavii Lata are also flowered, and with them she that Ladylike Pampa shone forth like a pulchritudinous 
lady. [3-75-23, 24]_END

B_3_C_75_19
BEGIN_
अस्याः तीरे तु पूर्व उक्तः पर्वतो धातु मण्डितः || ३-७५-२५ऋश्यमूक इति ख्यातः चित्र पुष्पित पादपः 
|_END
BEGIN_
The aforesaid mountain renowned as Rishyamuka which is abounding with colourful ores and amazingly flowered 
trees is there on the bank of Pampa Lake. [3-75-25b, 26a]_END

B_3_C_75_20
BEGIN_
हरेः ऋक्षरजो नाम्नः पुत्रः तस्य महात्मनः || ३-७५-२६अध्यास्ते तु महावीर्यः सुग्रीव इति विश्रुतः |_END
BEGIN_
A noble soul by his name Risharaja was there and that monkey's son is the highly valiant Sugreeva, thus 
he is renowned, and he presides over that mountain. [3-75-26b, 27b]_END

B_3_C_75_21
BEGIN_
सुग्रीवम् अभिगच्छ त्वम् वानरेन्द्रम् नरर्षभ || ३-७५-२७इति उवाच पुनः वाक्यम् लक्ष्मणम् सत्य विक्रमम् 
|कथम् मया विना सीताम् शक्यम् लक्ष्मण जीवितुम् || ३-७५-२८_END
BEGIN_
That best one among men Rama, said this way, "oh, Lakshmana, you make a headway for that chief of monkeys, 
Sugreeva..." and further said this to Lakshmana whose valiance is truthfulness alone, "how can I possibly 
live without Seetha..." [3-75-27b, 28]_END

B_3_C_75_22
BEGIN_
इति एवम् उक्त्वा मदन अभिपीडितःस लक्ष्मणम् वाक्यम् अनन्य चेतनः |विवेश पंपाम् नलिनी मनो रमाम्
तम् उत्तमम् शोकम् उदीरयाणः || ३-७५-२९_END
BEGIN_
Such as he is whose thinking is applying itself to Seetha alone, and who is vocalising his anguish for 
her, to whom aa stymie is laid by the Love-god just at the appearance that lake, that Rama on saying 
that sentence in that way to Lakshmana neared that superb and heart delighting lotus Lake Pampa. [3-75-29]_END

B_3_C_75_23
BEGIN_
क्रमेण गत्वा प्रविलोकयन् वनम्ददर्श पंपाम् शुभ दर्श काननाम् |अनेक नाना विध पक्षि संकुलाम्
विवेश रामः सह लक्ष्मणेन || ३-७५-३०_END
BEGIN_
On going step by step, and on going on seeing ardently and intently at that forest which has picturesque 
visuals of forestry, and which is with hurly-burly birds, not one, but numerous and divers are they, 
and then Rama along with Lakshmana on entering the area of that lake, has seen that Lake Pampa. [3-75-30]_END
